MAT - Pangu
Maatiyu
Maat
Maatiyu
Mazama nama zumaa nama Yeesu kuta̱taga nata̱ Maatiyu
Mazama nama zumaa nama Yeesu kuta̱taga nata̱
Maatiyu
Iri na ta̱yansun na yigo
Butu naa ta̱gi takaada na̱nna taa shi Maatiyu, buka̱ kaꞌupwa na ree ana Yeesu be̱ tazwara. Butasha Buyaahudiya.
Mazama nama zumaa kuta̱taga nata̱ Maatiyu ta̱bisa̱gi ta̱hyan, Yeesu ta shi buyata naa Hwe̱n bwa tanda ala̱ka̱wa̱ri ndaabwa ta na̱ mꞌmagwashe̱ kawyatu ndaabwa ta̱hyan unii káji. Ayaahudiya aba ta sha̱a̱ sume̱ ta̱hyan biwuci. Mana̱nna mazama nama zumaa matashici kuꞌnꞌnama Ayaahudiya, ama nama hyo̱ awyatu na sa̱ra̱ri yana.
Una̱nna takaada na Maatiyu upa̱shi na̱ mazama nama ta̱ma̱ncin nata̱ Yeesu na̱ baba̱tiisa̱ma nde̱e̱be̱ na̱ nꞌta̱maanwyana ta̱nde̱e̱be̱. Bwa gura̱a̱ shapa ta̱bisa̱ga̱ mazama nama zumaa, na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana, na̱ nꞌta̱kuda̱gahinaa awyatu na̱ Gaalili. Mahwarapi takaada na̱nna bwa duwa̱ni ta̱cita̱ga̱ ala̱ka̱wa̱ri na Hwe̱n bwa tandaakaka awyatu ta na̱ mꞌmagwashe̱, na̱ haruwa na Yeesu be̱ ciga̱hinii wyan. Una̱nna takaada gura̱a̱ ta̱bisa̱ ki ta̱hyan Yeesu shi biwya̱ra̱mii naa o̱to̱, binaa mazama mande̱e̱be̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ ta̱ba mꞌbaa ta̱kai nata̱ huri nata̱ Muusa.
Na̱ takaada na̱nna asha̱a̱gi ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ Yeesu zhagu mata. Na hin hiin, bwa shi ta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ na̱ undu na o̱to̱ nata̱ haruwa na ujabagu una awyatu na jwarigi Hwe̱n bwa naa (sura 5 zhagu 7). Na hin reenu, ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ ana be̱ tazwara aꞌupwa na ree na̱ haruwa na abaa naa nda tuma ndaaba (sura 10). Taatu, ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ mazama na̱ nꞌta̱kun nama ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ kuta̱ba shi (sura 13). Na̱nshin, ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ iri na ahari ana shi butu naa jwarigi buꞌmꞌbaa (sura 18), na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ ta̱huwa̱ nata̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana na̱ zhagu na ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ na wuci (sura 24 zhagu 25).
Iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱
Bikorogo naa Yeesu na̱ nꞌta̱ma̱ncin ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ :1--2:23Mazama ta̱bisa̱ga̱ nama Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma :1-12Baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ nꞌta̱maanwyana nata̱ Yeesu :13--4:11Tuma na Yeesu be̱ ndagi na̱ Gaalili :12--18:35Ukuswa na Yeesu na̱ Gaalili zhagu Hurushaliima :1--20:34Utuma na Yeesu na ta̱makwaakaa na̱ Hurushaliima :1--27:66Ta̱hiika̱ nata̱ Yeesu na̱ nꞌta̱bisa̱a̱ hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱ :1-20
Bikorogo naa Ala̱masiihu Yeesu
Luka 3:23-38
Utakaada naa korogo naa Ala̱masiihu Yeesu binaa báni kii korogo naa Dawuda na̱ Ibiraahin:
Ibiraahin tata mantan Isiyaaku,
Isiyaaku bwa ma̱ncin Yaakubu,
Yaakubu bwa ma̱ncin Yaahuda na̱ aya̱na̱ba.
Yaahuda bwa ma̱ncin Peruzu na̱ Zera. Aya̱na̱ ndaaba aba shi Tamaru.
Peruzu bwa ma̱ncin He̱zuro,
He̱zuro bwa ma̱ncin Aramu,
Aramu bwa ma̱ncin Amiinada,
Amiinada bwa ma̱ncin Nasho,
Nasho bwa ma̱ncin Salumu,
Salumu bwa ma̱ncin Bowaazu. Aya̱na̱ aba shi Rahaba̱.
Bowaazu bwa ma̱ncin Obedi. Aya̱na̱ aba shi Ruta.
Obedi bwa ma̱ncin Yeese,
Yeese bwa ma̱ncin Dawuda.
Bugwama Dawuda bwa ma̱ncin Suleemaanu. Aya̱na̱ aba tasha Bata̱sheeba, bunaa tasha aꞌa̱yo Uriya.
Suleemaanu bwa ma̱ncin Rahobowama,
Rahobowama bwa ma̱ncin Abiija,
Abiija bwa ma̱ncin Asa,
Asa bwa ma̱ncin Yahoshafata,
Yahoshafata bwa ma̱ncin Yorama,
Yorama bwa ma̱ncin Uziya,
Uziya bwa ma̱ncin Yotama,
Yotama bwa ma̱ncin Ahaza,
Ahaza bwa ma̱ncin Hezekiya,
Hezekiya bwa ma̱ncin Manaase,
Manaase bwa ma̱ncin Amonu,
Amonu bwa ma̱ncin Yosiya,
Yosiya bwa ma̱ncin Yekoniya na̱a̱ ya̱na̱ ha̱ni na aba sha̱pi Ayaahudiya ta̱gyama kuce̱nye̱n nata̱ Baabila.
Na aba ꞌye̱e̱ wyan Baabila, Yekoniya bwa ma̱ncin Sheyalitiyali,
Sheyalitiyali bwa ma̱ncin Zerubaabili,
Zerubaabili bwa ma̱ncin Abihudu,
Abihudu bwa ma̱ncin Eliyakimi,
Eliyakimi bwa ma̱ncin Azoru,
Azoru bwa ma̱ncin Zaduku,
Zaduku bwa ma̱ncin Akimu,
Akimu bwa ma̱ncin Eliyudu,
Eliyudu bwa ma̱ncin Eleyazara,
Eleyazara bwa ma̱ncin Matana,
Matana bwa ma̱ncin Yaakubu,
Yaakubu bwa ma̱ncin Yusufu awya̱rugo na Maariyamu,
Maariyamu be̱ ma̱ncin Yeesu bunaa aba ta hyan Ala̱masiihu.
Hyo̱ aya̱nu aha̱ni upwa na̱ na̱nshin aba tasha bike̱nye̱n naa Ibiraahin zhagu Dawuda. Ayaan aha̱ni upwa na̱ na̱nshin aba ta sha zhagu bike̱nye̱n naa Dawuda hara̱ ta̱shapa wyan ta̱gyama zhagu Baabila. Ta ha̱ni ya̱nu bwa wuce kiike̱nye̱n naa Ala̱masiihu, ubwa gura̱a̱ sha aha̱ni upwa na̱ na̱nshin.
Ta̱ma̱ncin nata̱ Ala̱masiihu
Luka 2:1-7
Nde̱e̱ haruwa na ta̱ma̱ncin nata̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu ta̱ba shi na. Maariyamu ada̱a̱da̱ na Yeesu be̱ na̱ nꞌta̱be̱e̱ biꞌa̱ binaa aba tahoo pana Yusufu xbinaa zhaa. Ta aba njiwo ta̱wya̱ri, be̱ ta mꞌbaa huba̱ na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n.
Sa̱mba̱ri nde̱e̱be̱ bwa shi butu naa bina̱, bwa ribici ta̱pa buu nꞌkogi kawyatu da̱shi, bwa hoo sha̱a̱ ta̱hyan bunii gaa buu ta̱zhaa kunta wau.
Bwa nꞌta̱maga̱gaaga, kuutuma naa Hwe̱n bwa jaa, bwa nje̱ mazama nii bwa na̱ ara̱rabi, bwa hin buu, <<Yusufu buyoo Dawuda, ta-ha̱nga rukwanyan naru ta̱zhaa Maariyamu bishi buꞌa̱ ndaabi, wana huba̱ na be̱ mꞌbaa ashi na báni ta kii-Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n.
Binii mantan be̱e̱ biwya̱ri, gaa nii pa buu ruzha̱a̱ Yeesu, na̱ wana be̱ ta nii biha̱na̱ wyatu nde̱e̱be̱ kupinsan ndaaba.>>
Hyo̱ iri ya̱nu tanda na̱ wana aciga̱hini ta̱cita̱ nata̱ Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n nata̱ bwa tacita̱ kuucita̱a̱ga̱ wuun mazama,
<<Nde̱e̱ be̱e̱ biꞌa̱ na binaa ta yancin butu wya̱ri binii ciga̱ huba̱, bima̱ncin be̱e̱ biwya̱ri, aba nii nꞌgana buu Imaanuwa̱i.>> Ane̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan, <<Uhwe̱n ne̱e̱ huku na̱ ga̱tu.>>
Na Yusufu bwa zhe̱mbe̱ kara̱rabi, bwa jwarigi iri na butuma naa Hwe̱n bwa tabishi bwa, bwa ra̱ga̱ni Maariyamu be̱ shi a̱yo.
Hyo̱ na̱ kunnu, bwa tayancin buu buꞌa̱ kiike̱nye̱n naa be̱ ma̱ncin be̱e̱ binde̱e̱be̱ naa yigo naa wya̱ri, bwa pa̱ buu ruzha̱a̱ Yeesu.

Wyatu ana mꞌbaa ta̱yansun nata̱ nꞌgwasu aba báni hwe̱n ta̱bani
Atamantan Yeesu na̱ Baitalaami na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya na̱ ha̱ni na bugwama Hirudu. Na̱ bwa ha̱ni ana mꞌbaa ta̱yansun nata̱ nꞌgwasu aba báni hwe̱n ta̱bani, aba jaa Hurushaliima, abaa hantaana awyatu ma hyaan,
<<Pe̱kata aba ma̱ncin bugwama naa fo naa Ayaahudiya? Ta̱ndái bigwasu ndaabwa ma báni hwe̱n ta̱bani, ta ga̱tu jwárige̱ buu wana xta̱pa̱ buu hunrun.>>
Naa gwama Hirudu bwa hange̱ kunnu, bigata ndaabwa be̱ ha̱nsha̱nha̱ni ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, hyo̱ na̱ awyatu na Hurushaliima.
Bwa wuna̱ni hyo̱ apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa, bwa ha̱nta̱ni wyan, <<Pe̱kata aba nii mantan Ala̱masiihu?>>
Aba hin bwa, <<Na̱ bicice̱pe̱ naa Baitalaami na ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Ayaahudiya ta. Kunnu ta buyaan bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama bwa ta taga, ta̱hyan,
<< <Gaa bicice̱pe̱ naa Baitalaami na Yaahudiya,
bushici njeke kana ha̱mba̱a̱gi ta̱gwama nata̱ Yaahudiya.
Wakaa kata buyaan bunaa nii ha̱mba̱ga̱ ta̱gwama bwaa báni,
bunaa nii naa na̱ iyo̱ na awyatu nimi na Isiraaꞌila.> >>
Hirudu bwa nꞌgani aba wyatu ana mꞌbaa ta̱yansun nata̱ nꞌgwasu wana xbuyansun ki ha̱ni na bigwasu be̱ tabáni.
Bwa ka̱ji wyan zhagu Baitalaami, bwa hin, <<Jaga ma, iwya̱nzhin be̱e̱ bibe̱e̱ ki. Kiindái buu, ijaa iꞌmꞌbishi wana ga̱n taa ma jaga ma pé̱e̱ buu hunrun taa.>>
Na aba hange̱ mazama nama bugwama hyo̱, aba huri ta̱hani ta̱ndaaba. Bigwasu ya̱nu naa aba tajwárige̱ be̱ ne̱e̱ iyeebe ndaaba, aba jwarigi buu, be̱ e̱she̱ paakii be̱e̱ bibe̱e̱.
Na aba nda̱i bibe̱e̱ gwasu aba hange̱ gama ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Aba ta̱ni ina, aba nda̱i be̱e̱ na̱ aya̱na̱ Maariyamu, aba ta̱a̱gi buu runrun, aba pa̱ buu hunrun. Sa̱i aba rigijigi ꞌwaa ndaaba aba pa̱ga̱ni buu zinaari na̱ turaare na lubana na̱ mariga̱ nama muru.
Na aba hiin hura̱, aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱ ce̱nye̱n ta̱ndaaba kuyaan yo̱n goo, wana Hwe̱n kooci wyan na̱ ara̱rabi xata kusa paa Hirudu.
Yusufu na̱ Maariyamu gidigi zhagu Masa
Na wyatu ana mꞌbaa ta̱yansun nata̱ nꞌgwasu aba huri, buyaan butuma naa Hwe̱n bwa mabisa̱a̱ paaku Yusufu na̱ ara̱rabi, bwa hin buu, <<Hiika̱ na̱ be̱e̱ na̱ aya̱na̱ nde̱e̱be̱, u-gidigi zhagu ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Masa. Hunrana ma piree sa̱i kimii hin ma kushiika ma, bugwama Hirudu nii naa wyanzan be̱e̱ bibe̱e̱ na hyan bukwane̱ buu.>>
Yusufu bwa hiiki bwa sha̱pi be̱e̱ na̱ aya̱na̱ na̱ gita, aba huri ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Masa,
bwa ne̱e̱ kaun kiike̱nye̱n naa Hirudu bwa ꞌwi. Ana nda kunnu wana aciga̱hini mazama nama Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n bwa tacita̱ kuucita̱a̱ga̱ wuun mazama ta̱hyan, <<Ta na̱ Masa ta ga̱n báhine̱ Baa buniimi.>>
Akwane̱ mꞌmwaan njeke na̱ Yaahudiya
Na Hirudu bwa nda̱i ta̱hyan ana mꞌbaa ta̱yansun nata̱ nꞌgwasu andaaki be̱ maka̱ri, bwa gware̱ me̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱. Bwa shaani xakunai mꞌmwaan wya̱ri hyo̱ na̱ Baitalaami, na̱ mꞌbiin ndaabwa, na nꞌnje̱ nꞌyo̱ nꞌreeko na ciin kunrin, re̱ nii ke̱nye̱n naa ana mꞌbaa ta̱yansun nata̱ nꞌgwasu aba na bisa̱ bwa mazama.
Na̱ kunnu ta aba taciga̱hina̱ mazama nama bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Iriminyan, ta̱hyan,
<<Ahange̱ ta̱ꞌungwa na̱ Raama,
nꞌungwa na nꞌame̱ ta̱gura ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Ahange̱ Rahiila nii nꞌgaga na̱ wana mꞌmwaan nꞌnde̱e̱be̱,
be̱ ga̱a̱ akuri na abaa apaga buu,
wana nꞌhoo ꞌwa̱ga̱.>>
Kushiikwa ndaaba Masa zhagu Naazare
Na Hirudu bwa ꞌwi, buyaan butuma naa Hwe̱n bwa gura̱a̱ mabisa̱a̱ ku-Yusufu na̱ ara̱rabi na̱ Masa, bwa hin,
<<Hiika̱, u-sha̱pi bibibe̱e̱ na̱ aya̱na̱, u-huri ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Isiraaꞌila, wana ana ribi buu ta̱kuna aꞌwa̱gi.>>
Bwa hiiki, bwa sha̱pi be̱e̱ bibe̱e̱ na̱ aya̱na̱, aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱ ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Isiraaꞌila.
Na bwa hange̱ ta̱hyan Ara̱kilayasu buyoo Hirudu ka̱ta̱ni ta̱gwama nata̱ ashin na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya, bwa hange̱ rukwanyan naru ta̱wuta̱ kaun. Ama Hwe̱n bwa kooci bwa na̱ ara̱rabi, sa̱i bwa huri taha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Gaalili,
bwa hunrani na̱ yaan ce̱pe̱ na aba ta nꞌgana Naazare. Na̱ kunnu ta aba taciga̱hina̱ ta̱cita̱ hiku nata̱ acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ta̱hyan, <<Anii nꞌgana buu Bunaazare.>>

Mazama nama Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma
Marukusu 1:1-8; Luka 3:1-18; Yoohana 1:19-28
Na̱ nꞌhwe̱n ya̱nu, buyaan butu naa ba ta nꞌgana Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma bwa ja̱a̱ ahira̱ ceeku na Yaahudiya. Sa̱i bwaa bisa̱ga̱ awyatu mazama,
bwaa hyaan, <<Pana ma pinsan baa, ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱goki.>>
Buna̱nna taa shi bunaa bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Ishaaya, bwa tanda mazama mandaabwa, bwa hin,
<<Ta̱ꞌnꞌga ma nꞌga na̱ ahira̱ ma hyaan,
<A̱sa̱ga̱a̱ga̱ ma Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n yo̱n,
ika̱mbiga̱gi ayo̱n na bwaa jwára̱gani.> >>
Yoohana bwa ta taana uda̱bi na aba tano̱o̱ nꞌta̱hinje nata̱ raakumi. Bwa ka̱da̱gi ambi ndaabwa na̱ kapa na tutuu. Ma̱ni nama swain na̱ aꞌyo̱n ta tasha shami ndaabwa.
Awyatu hwarapi na Hurushaliima na̱ ana mꞌbiin na n-Yaahudiya na̱ hyo̱ mꞌbiin na nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Rwaga na Joodan, abaa jábagi waabwa.
Ana nii cita̱ga̱ apinsan ndaaba, Yoohana bwaa ndaga wyan baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ ame̱ na Rwaga na Joodan.
Na Yoohana bwa nda̱i Afaraasiya na̱ Asaduukiya hwarapi ma jábagi waabwa wana xandagi wyan baba̱tiisa̱ma, bwa hin wyan, <<Ga̱hin bigudu naa suhwaa nasu we̱! Iyaa ta bisa̱gi ma ta̱hyan gida̱ga̱na̱ ma ta̱suuga̱ nasu wuci?
Nda ma iri na hyan ibisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan ipa̱ni pinsan baa.
Ta-naa ma nꞌta̱hyan, <Ibiraahin ta shi adaada na adaadoo nda̱tu.> Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, Hwe̱n nii ara ta̱ndaaka Ibiraahin mꞌmwaan katari na̱nna.
Ahoo sha̱a̱ aca̱gu paaku kunrun kunrun na ꞌwe̱e̱. Hyo̱ ꞌwe̱e̱ na nje̱ce̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ bina̱, aꞌya̱pa̱gi wuun, abwagi na̱ ra.
<<Ga̱n na̱maa ndaga ma baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ ma̱ni na hyan ibisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan ipa̱ni pinsan baa, ama buyaan bunaa nꞌhuri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ wuci ta̱baa ta̱niimi, bunaa ga̱n jwaci ma antana akandaga ndaabwa. Bwa taa ja̱maa ndaga ma baba̱tiisa̱ma nii Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n na̱ ra.
Bwa shi haku butu naa ha̱mba̱gi ukada ndaabwa na pyashi, na bwaa pyasa shami ndaabwa. Buwuna̱a̱ni hyo̱ shami, buzooga̱ni na̱ nꞌndukwa nꞌndaabwa. Ama buhuunha̱ni nꞌshasu kura na za ta̱kuna.>>
Anje̱ Yeesu baba̱tiisa̱ma
Marukusu 1:9-11; Luka 3:21-22
Nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu ta Yeesu be̱ tabáni kuta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Gaalili, be̱ ja̱a̱ Rwaga na Joodan paa Yoohana wana xbunje̱ buu baba̱tiisa̱ma.
Yoohana bwa ribi ta̱yansan buu, bwa hin buu, <<Ga̱n ta nꞌshi na hyan u-nꞌnje̱ baba̱tiisa̱ma, ta gaa jaa wa̱ka̱mi?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni bwa be̱ hin, <<xMashi kunnu niina, uhuri gama ta̱ciga̱hini hyo̱ iri na ta̱to̱n ina Hwe̱n bwa ribi.>> Naazhin Yoohana bwa ra̱ni ta̱nda buu baba̱tiisa̱ma.
Na bwa nje̱ Yeesu baba̱tiisa̱ma, be̱e̱ báni na̱ ame̱ na ma̱ni, ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱ba gunii, be̱ nda̱i Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n ma cíin haku mꞌpirwa na nꞌhuunruun, be̱ za̱ta̱ni nii be̱.
Aba hange̱ kuta̱yaan ta̱ꞌnꞌga ta̱báni nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ma hyaan, <<Buna̱nna taa shi Baa buniimi bunaa ga̱n hura̱gi ta̱ruba̱, ga̱n mashiragi na̱a̱ bwa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.>>

Bupira̱ bwa ma̱a̱nwya̱ni Yeesu
Marukusu 1:12-13; Luka 4:1-13
Sa̱i Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ ra̱ga̱ni Yeesu ahira̱ ceeku wana xBupira̱ ma̱a̱nwya̱ni buu.
Yeesu be̱ nje̱ ruꞌure̱ nꞌhwe̱n handa gita na̱ hwe̱n, sa̱i be̱ hange̱ rumunro̱n ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Sa̱i Bupira̱ bwa jaa, bwa hin buu, <<Kuu-shi Buyoo Hwe̱n, shana atari na̱nna ashi buroodi.>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni bwa be̱ hin, <<Ata̱gi na̱ takaada na Hwe̱n, <Shii kini shami ta butu bwa ta nda bina̱, ama na̱ koya̱ mazama nama báni paaku nu na Hwe̱n ta bwa ta nda bina̱.> >>
Bupira̱ bwa ra̱ga̱ni buu zhagu Hurushaliima ce̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ na Hwe̱n, bwa ꞌye̱e̱ buu bwa za̱ta̱a̱ buu nii cira̱ naa hura̱gi za̱ka̱ na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n na Ayaahudiya.
Bwa hin buu, <<Kuu-shi Buyoo Hwe̱n, guba̱ u-ke̱ne̱ na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n, wana ata̱gi ta̱hyan,
<< <Uhwe̱n nii shana atuma ndaabwa aasa̱a̱ki.
Ana̱maa raa na̱ nꞌara nꞌndaaba,
na̱ wana gaa jaa basana mꞌbuna nꞌndaabi na̱ paga.> >>
Yeesu be̱ hin bwa, <<Agura̱a̱ taga ta̱hyan, <Ta-maanwyana Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n ndaa.> >>
Sa̱i Bupira̱ bwa gura̱a̱ iya buu kuyaan undu na za̱ka̱ri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, bwa bisa̱a̱gi buu hyo̱ ta̱gwama nata̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌo̱to̱ nata̱ ta̱ba.
Bwa gura̱a̱ hyan buu, <<Na̱nna hyo̱ nꞌna̱maa pana tuun, kuu-she̱nshe̱n na uba̱ nimi gaa mꞌpa̱ hunrun.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin bwa, <<Hura̱ pata, gaa Bupira̱! Ata̱gi ta̱hyan, <Pa Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n ndaa hunrun, kuubwa ta gaa nii naa ndaaka tuma.> >>
Ha̱ni ya̱nu Bupira̱ bwa mahooshi nii be̱. Katuma na Hwe̱n aba he̱e̱n buza̱a̱, aba jaa abaa ndaaka buu tuma.
Yeesu be̱ pa̱shi tuma na̱ Gaalili
Marukusu 1:14-15; Luka 4:14-15
Ha̱ni na Yeesu be̱ hange̱ ta̱hyan azwa̱ga̱ni Yoohana na̱ zhaaro, be̱ hiiki, be̱ kwashe̱e̱ke̱ ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Gaalili.
Na be̱ ga̱a̱ Naazare, be̱ huri ce̱pe̱ na Kapanahu na ne̱e̱ do̱ko̱ na̱ Rwaga na O̱to̱ na Gaalili na ne̱e̱ na̱ ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ ta̱ꞌyapa nata̱ Zabuluna na̱ Nafitali.
Na̱nna ta shi ta̱ciga̱hini nata̱ iri na bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Ishaaya bwa tacita̱ ta̱hyan,
<<Ta̱ꞌyapa nata̱ Zabuluna na̱ nata̱ Nafitali,
na ne̱e̱ na̱ yo̱n na ja̱a̱ dabu na ne̱e̱ hira̱ree na Rwaga na Joodan,
na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Gaalili paaku ta̱ꞌyapa nata̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya,
awyatu ninhin ana tahunrana kaun na̱ nꞌta̱yincincin,
aba anda̱i ta̱gwaan ta̱ꞌo̱to̱,
ana tahunrana na̱ hunrun na ta̱ꞌwa̱ taa maa,
ta̱gwaan ta̱ba tára̱kani wyan.>>
Ta na̱ ha̱ni ya̱nu, Yeesu be̱ pa̱shi ta̱naa bisa̱ga̱ wyatu mazama, be̱e̱ hyaan, <<Pana ma pinsan baa, ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱goki.>>
Yeesu nꞌgani ana kota̱ga̱ni na nꞌjooshiipa na̱nshin
Marukusu 1:16-20; Luka 5:1-11
Yaan hwe̱n na Yeesu be̱ ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hani na̱ inza̱n na Rwaga na O̱to̱ na Gaalili, be̱ nda̱i buyaan butu na̱a̱ ya̱na̱ aba ree, Siima bunaa aba ta hyan Biituru na̱a̱ ya̱na̱ Andaraawa. Na ta̱hyan ashi awyatu na kota̱ga̱ni na nꞌjooshiipa, abaa bwaga ataaro na̱ ame̱ na ma̱ni.
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Jaa ma inꞌjwárige̱ nꞌna̱maa ga̱gaagana ma haruwa na ta̱naa dúubagi awyatu.>>
Aba ta̱cii ke̱nye̱n du, aba ga̱a̱ ꞌwaa ndaaba, aba jwarigi buu.
Na be̱ ta̱ ta̱hura̱ nꞌta̱hani, be̱ nda̱i ayaan wyatu reeko, butu na̱a̱ ya̱na̱, Yaakubu buyoo Zabadi na̱a̱ ya̱na̱ Yoohana. Aba ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ na hantun na ma̱ni huku na̱a̱ shiiba Zabadi, aba ma a̱sa̱a̱ga̱na̱ ataaro ndaaba. Sa̱i be̱ nꞌgani wyan taa.
Aba ta̱cii ke̱nye̱n du, aba ga̱a̱ hantun hyo̱ na̱a̱ shiiba, aba jwarigi buu.
Yeesu kuda̱gahinai wyatu hwarapi
Luka 6:17-19
Yeesu be̱ waro̱be̱ne̱ kope na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Gaalili, ma ga̱gaagana wyatu na̱ aka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya, ma bisa̱ga̱ wyan mazama nama zumaa nama ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱. Be̱e̱ kuda̱gahinaa awyatu na ha̱ngagici sa̱ na̱ koya̱ iri na suguma.
Be̱e̱ nda kunnu, mazama mande̱e̱be̱ mꞌba mawya̱shi kope na̱ ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Suuriya. Abaa iyaagagi buu hyo̱ wyatu na ha̱ngagici sa̱, na̱ ana suguma koya̱ iri, na̱ ana nii swa ta̱guma o̱to̱, na̱ ana nꞌhwaanwun na nꞌwe̱, na̱ ana suguma nasu nꞌrabi, na̱ ana ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ba swa̱. Hyo̱ ndaaba be̱ kuda̱gahinai wyan.
Nꞌgudu nꞌhwarapi na nꞌwyatu mꞌba jwarigi buu, ana Gaalili na̱ ana ta̱ꞌyapa nata̱ Ace̱pe̱ Upwa, na̱ Hurushaliima, na̱ mꞌbiin na n-Yaahudiya, hara̱ na̱ ana hira̱ree na Rwaga na Joodan.

Ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ Yeesu nii undu
Ha̱ni na Yeesu be̱ nda̱i nꞌgudu na nꞌwyatu, be̱ ka̱ta̱ni undu, be̱ hunrani. Ana jwarigi buu aba wuce waabe̱,
be̱ pa̱shi ta̱naa ga̱gaagana wyan.
Ana rubara̱ka ta
Luka 6:20-23
Be̱ hin,
<<Awyatu na e̱nshe̱n ta̱hyan aribi ndaya Hwe̱n,
ashi ana Hwe̱n bwa ndaaki rubara̱ka,
ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱shi ta̱ndaaba.
Awyatu na ne̱e̱ na̱ yama na̱ nꞌungwa,
ashi ana Hwe̱n bwa ndaaki rubara̱ka,
uja̱a̱ uuhina̱a̱ wyan.
Awyatu na sha̱pici hyuhyu ndaaba ashi yaanyini,
ashi ana Hwe̱n bwa ndaaki rubara̱ka,
aja̱a̱ hya̱su sa̱ra̱ri yana.
Awyatu na mayanshin ta̱ha̱nga mansuunran aba ne̱e̱ mꞌmagawa nama hyan anje̱ ta̱suuga̱ nata̱ ta̱to̱n,
ashi ana Hwe̱n bwa ndaaki rubara̱ka,
aja̱a̱ nda ta̱ga̱da̱ri.
Awyatu na mꞌbaa ambishiri,
ashi ana Hwe̱n bwa ndaaki rubara̱ka,
aja̱a̱ ndaaka wyan ambishiri.
Awyatu na mꞌbaa nꞌgata na nꞌtande̱,
ashi ana Hwe̱n bwa ndaaki rubara̱ka,
aja̱a̱ ndaya Hwe̱n.
Awyatu na ta shana hunranhunran na ta̱gumunu,
ashi ana Hwe̱n bwa ndaaki rubara̱ka,
aja̱a̱ nꞌgana wyan mꞌmwaan na n-Hwe̱n.
Awyatu na aba yanshin ta̱mataa wana anii ndaga ri na ta̱to̱n,
ashi ana Hwe̱n bwa ndaaki rubara̱ka,
ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱ndaaba ta̱ta.
<<Ishi ana Hwe̱n bwa ndaaki rubara̱ka ha̱ni na awyatu abaa cwaagaga ma, abaa yanshin ma ta̱mataa, abaa ndaakaka ma ta̱be̱, abaa hyaan ma iri hwarapi na we̱ wana iꞌnꞌjwarigi.
Nda ma ta̱ga̱da̱ri inaa guba̱ga̱, wana ufuna̱ ninhin ja̱a̱ naa o̱to̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱. Kunta ta aba tandaakaka acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ana yigo.
Ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ wun na̱ mꞌmaza̱ki
Marukusu 9:50; Luka 14:34-35
<<Ga̱hin taa shi haku wun na sa̱ra̱ri yana. Koya̱ wun na hwii masuunran mandaabwa, uza kuta̱ꞌa̱sa̱ga̱na̱. Uza yaan ri na baa nda na̱ bwa, kuta̱munsan, abaa munsan wuun, awyatu fundaci.
<<Ga̱hin taa shi haku ta̱gwaan nata̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana haku ce̱pe̱ na aba ma̱ da̱ nii undu uꞌa̱cii naa ta̱swee.
Aꞌa̱cii pantaan pitila aꞌubi wuun bigwaga, sa̱i da̱i aca̱guda̱ni wuun nii ꞌwa̱ruꞌwa̱ru wana uta̱ra̱ka̱ni ina naa gwaan.
Kunnu taa ga̱hin, gaa ma maza̱ki maniinhin xmata̱ra̱ka̱ni kaꞌuba̱ na wyatu, wana hyan anda̱i tuma ninhin na zumaa, wana hyan aya̱ba̱ni Ada ninhin na ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
Ta̱ga̱gaagana Nꞌgira̱nshin
<<Ta-sha̱a̱ ma ta̱hyan ga̱n jaa wana ma kuna Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n bwa tapana Muusa na̱ atakaada na acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, sa̱i da̱i ma ciga̱hina̱ muu.
Mahanda ga̱n maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n ta̱ja̱a̱ huwa̱, koo ta̱ta ta̱ka̱ nata̱ njeke nata̱ nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa ta̱jaa foga̱, sa̱i ki ri cigi hyo̱.
Koo buya̱ naa ga̱a̱ bigira̱nshin naa hura̱gi ta̱ge̱, bwa gura̱a̱ ga̱gaagana awyatu xaga̱a̱ buu, kunta Hwe̱n bwa nii nꞌgana be̱ bunaa hura̱gi ta̱ge̱ kuta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱. Bunaa gura̱a̱ jwara̱ga nꞌgira̱nshin na̱nna, bwa gura̱a̱ ga̱gaagana awyatu muu, kunta Hwe̱n bwa nii nꞌgana be̱ bunaa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ kuta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
<<Ga̱n nii gura̱a̱ maa tuuta̱a̱ga̱ ma, kuta̱jwara̱ga Nꞌgira̱nshin niinhin ta̱hurici nata̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na̱ Afaraasiya, ijaa da̱ba ta̱ta̱na̱ kuta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ mahwa.
Ta̱ga̱gaagana wana ame̱ ta̱gura
Luka 12:57-59
<<Ihoo ha̱nga atabisa̱ adaadoo nda̱tu na yigo ta̱hyan, <Ta-kuna butu. Kuu-kwane̱ butu, ana̱maa iya kuta̱suuga̱.>
Ama ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma ta̱hyan, koo ta̱gura me̱ na̱ ayami gaa gware̱, ana̱maa iya kuta̱suuga̱. Kuu-nꞌgani ayami butu naa uwa̱, ana̱maa ndaaka ta̱suuga̱ hiku. Kuu-hiin yaan, <Guzha̱ni,> bi-ne̱e̱ na̱ yo̱n na ra na za ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱.
<<Wana kunnu, koo iri gaa ne̱e̱ na̱ zhagu ta̱pana na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n, pita pita gaa mata̱ma̱nriin ta̱hyan ayami mꞌbaa mazama na̱ gaa,
sha̱a̱ kwan wuun paa kiizhe̱nke̱n, u-ja̱a̱, u-maꞌá̱sa̱ga̱ni na̱ ayami ya̱nu, naazhin u-sha̱pi ri yata u-pa̱ni Hwe̱n.
<<Kuuyaan buuꞌye̱e̱ kuta̱suuga̱, na̱ ha̱ni maga̱ga̱a̱gi na̱a̱ bwa butu ta ga̱hin na̱ yo̱n. Kuu-nje̱ce̱ kunnu, bwaa ꞌye̱e̱ kubutu naa ta̱suuga̱, butu naa ta̱suuga̱ buuꞌye̱e̱ kubutu naa kapa, aazwa̱ga̱ni na̱ zhaaro.
Mahanda ga̱n mꞌmaa bisa̱ga̱ ma, bi-jaa bana kaun sa̱i kuu-pa̱ga̱ni hyo̱ ta̱re̱ga ta̱ndaabi, za iri na nii bwa.
Ta̱ga̱gaagana wana ta̱wya̱ri
Maatiyu 19:9; Marukusu 10:11-12; Luka 16:18
<<Ihoo ha̱nga ta̱hyan, <Ta-nda banshaun na̱ aꞌa̱yoo yaan.>
Ama ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma ta̱hyan, koo buya̱ gwatani buꞌa̱ agwataga na ta̱ruba̱, buhoo nda ta banshaun na̱a̱ bwa nii gata nꞌndaabwa.
Kuyishe ndaa na̱maa shaana u-nje̱ pinsan, cwakara̱ka wuun, u-mo̱nshe̱n. Uhuri gama gaa jaa mꞌbaa ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabi ta̱ka̱, na hyan aamunsani hyo̱ ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabi paaku ra na za ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱.
Kunnu taa, kuꞌara ndaa na kataga na̱maa shaana u-nje̱ pinsan, ꞌyapa wuun, u-mo̱nshe̱n. Uhuri gama gaa jaa mꞌbaa ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabi ta̱ka̱, na hyan u-ta̱ni hyo̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabi paaku ra na za ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱.
<<Ihoo ha̱nga ta̱hyan, <Bunaa ta̱zhiga̱ni aꞌa̱yo, mashi ga̱ga̱ga̱ bupa̱ni wyan takaada na ta̱kuna ta̱wya̱ri.>
Ama ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma ta̱hyan, butu naa ta̱zhiga̱ni aꞌa̱yo ubwa shici wana wyanzun na wyatu wya̱ri bwaa nda, bushaani be̱ ta banshaun. Bunaa zha̱a̱ buꞌa̱ naa awya̱rugo aba ta̱zhiga̱ni, bunii nda ta banshaun na̱a̱ bwaa a̱.
Ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ sa̱nsan
<<Mayaan ihoo ha̱nga atabisa̱ adaadoo nda̱tu na yigo ta̱hyan, <Ta-kunsa̱n sa̱nsan na gaa tasha̱pi, shapa wuun kiike̱nye̱n naa gaa ta hin Hwe̱n bi-nii wuciha̱na̱.>
Ama ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma ta̱hyan, ta-taa ma sa̱nsan mahwa. Ta-nda kunnu na̱ nꞌruzha̱a̱ naru ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, wana ta̱ba ta ta̱shi bizhe̱nke̱n naa ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n.
Ta-nda kunnu koo na̱ nꞌruzha̱a̱ naru nꞌce̱nye̱n, wana mꞌbata nꞌshi paaku bwa ta cagudana mꞌbuna nꞌndaabwa. Ta-nda kunnu koo na̱ nꞌruzha̱a̱ naru Hurushaliima wana bwa ta shi ce̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ unaa gwama naa o̱to̱ Hwe̱n.
Ta-taa sa̱nsan na̱ hyuhyu ndaa, wana bi-jaa ara koo ta̱hinje ta̱ka̱ ta̱gigiriga̱hina̱ ta̱shi ta̱tande̱ koo ta̱shiri.
Hyo̱ iri na ga̱hin hiin cita̱ xiꞌisa kuna̱, <Kunnu> koo <Shici kunnu>. Kihuri kunnu, ishi ta ina Bupira̱.
Ta̱ga̱gaagana wana wyaan ta̱kuna
Luka 6:29-30
<<Ihoo ha̱nga ta̱hyan, <Wyaan na yishe ta̱kuna shi taa kuyishe, kunnu taa wyaan na ruya̱n rushi taa kuruya̱n.>
Ama ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma ta̱hyan, iri na we̱ na butu bwaa ndaaki ma ta-kuna ma wyaan. Kuuyaan buupa̱shi na̱ gawa na kataga, gura̱a̱ kicihinana be̱ gawa na kagura̱.
Kuuyaan buuꞌye̱e̱ kuta̱suuga̱ wana hyan buura̱a̱ da̱bi ndaa, gaaga be̱ hyo̱ zuzu ndaa na rocu.
Kuuyaan butu naa ta̱gwama buushaani ta̱hani nata̱ mame̱ma nama kiloomita ka̱, too, nda ma ta̱hani nata̱ kiloomita reeko huku.
Kuuyaan buuro̱pe̱ ri, u-pa̱ni bwa. Ta-gaa ta̱pana kana jaa wyanzun na ta̱ꞌwapa wakaa.
Ta̱ga̱gaagana wana anaa ribici
Luka 6:27-28,32-36
<<Ihoo ha̱nga ta̱hyan, <Ruba̱ butu naa nꞌharu ndaabi,> u-ga̱a̱ buna buuribici.
Ama ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma ta̱hyan, ruba̱ ma anaa ribici ma, indaaki ana taa kaka ma ro̱pe̱,
wana ubisa̱a̱ ishi mꞌmwaan na Buushiinhin naa ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱. Bunaa ta shaana uhwe̱n báni utára̱kani hyo̱ paaka awyatu na mꞌbaa ambyau na̱ ana bure, ugura̱a̱ shana ashira̱ ke̱ne̱ paaka awyatu na bina̱ na̱ ana a̱cii naa nda ri na bina̱.
Kiiribi kawyatu naa ribi baa ka̱, uya̱ funa̱ ga̱hin da̱ba? Ka̱i, koo awyatu na ta naa raaga ga̱ndu kunta aba ta naa ndaga.
Kushi kawyatu ninhin baa ka̱ ga̱hin tanaa zumaana, iba̱ ga̱hin nje̱ ina ne̱e̱ goo na̱ ayaan? Koo ana tanaa paga gumaka hunrun maa kunta ta aba ta naa ndaga.
Wana kunnu, sha ma ana ta̱hiku hakuu Shiinhin naa ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ bwa shii naa ta̱hiku.

Ta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱pana wana ana za
Yeesu be̱ re̱ iyeebe mꞌmazama ma hyaan,<<Nda ma ha̱nka̱ri, utuma ninhin na bina̱ na ga̱hin nda xuta sha wana awyatu wuma nda̱i. Kiinje̱ kunnu, ijaa da̱ba funa̱ paakuu Shiinhin naa ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
Ha̱ni na gaa hiin pana buyaan bunaa za ri iri, ta-naa taa nu wana awyatu wuma hange̱. Kunnu awyatu na za mahanda aba ta naa nda da̱shi, wana awyatu nda̱i na hyan aya̱ba̱ni wyan. Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, funa̱ ndaaba ta aba hoo raa huwa̱.
Ama gaa, ha̱ni na gaa hiin pana bunaa za ri iri, xuꞌara kagura̱ ndaa ta yansun iri na ara kataga bwaa pana.
xIri na gaa pana shi ta̱swee, Ashibo na nda̱i iri na gaa nje̱ ta̱swee ta na̱maa funa̱.
Ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ ro̱pe̱
Luka 11:2-4
<<Kunnu mayaan, ha̱ni na ga̱hin hiin nda ro̱pe̱, ta-naa nda ma haka wyatu na za mahanda aba ta naa nda, wana ahuri ta̱ruba̱ ta̱naa nda isa isa na̱ paaka aka̱ta̱ku na̱ masa̱ci nama ayo̱n, wana awyatu nda̱i anii nda ro̱pe̱. Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, funa̱ ndaaba ta aba hoo raa huwa̱.
Ama gaa ha̱ni na gaa hiin nda ro̱pe̱, ta̱na̱ dura̱ ndaa, u-guna̱ni wuun, u-nje̱ ro̱pe̱ ndaa ta̱swee ku-Hwe̱n. Ashibo na nda̱i iri na gaa nje̱ ta̱swee ta na̱maa funa̱.
Ha̱ni na ga̱hin hiin nda ro̱pe̱, ta-naa gida̱ba kiri ka̱ haku ana nii paga gumaka hunrun aba ta naa ndaga, wana ta̱hyan ta̱ndaaba ta̱naa gida̱ba ma̱ ta Hwe̱n bwaa rana wyan.
Ta-naa nda ma haka ba, wana Bushiinhin hoo yansun hyo̱ ri na ga̱hin ribi ta ga̱hin rupwa bwa.
Nda ma ro̱pe̱ kunna,
<< <Ada nda̱tu na ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱,
xapa̱ ruzha̱a̱ rundaabi naru ne̱e̱ sabu hunrun.
Shaana ta̱gwama ta̱ndaabi ta̱wuce pina.
Iri na gaa ribi xinje̱ pina na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana,
haruwa na aba ta naa nda wuun nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
U-ta̱pa̱ ba̱re shami na rwaru.
Ta-ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ pinsan nda̱tu nii gata ndaabi,
haruwa na ga̱tu ha̱mba̱ga̱ncin ana ta̱ndaaki pinsan.
Ta-ta̱ꞌiya paaku ta̱maanwyana,
ama u-ta̱ pe̱e̱n kuunaa we̱.>+ :13 Ta̱yaan ta̱taga ta̱ka̱ ta̱hin: Na ta̱hyan ta̱gwama na̱ nꞌta̱kai na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ta̱shi ta̱ndaabi na̱ mꞌmahwa.<<Kiiha̱mba̱ga̱ncin ayaan pinsan na abaa ndaaki ma nii gata niinhin, Bushiinhin taa na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ bujamaa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ ma pinsan ninhin.
Ama kiiha̱mba̱ga̱ni ayaan pinsan na abaa ndaaki ma nii gata niinhin, Bushiinhin taa buna̱maa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ ma pinsan ninhin.
Ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ ruꞌure̱ ta̱nda
<<Ha̱ni na ga̱hin nda ruꞌure̱, ta-ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ ma apusa̱ka ninhin haka wyatu na za mahanda aba ta naa ndaga, na hyan abisa̱a̱ wyatu ane̱e̱ nꞌruꞌure̱. Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, funa̱ ndaaba ta aba hoo raa huwa̱.
Ha̱ni na gaa ne̱e̱ nꞌruꞌure̱, ha̱mbara u-a̱sa̱ga̱ni hyuhyu ndaa,
na hyan xbuyaan buta yansun ta̱hyan bi-ne̱e̱ nꞌruꞌure̱. Sa̱i Ashibo ana aba nda̱ci, tanii ndaya iri na gaa nda ta̱swee, aapa̱ni funa̱.
Ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ ta̱sha̱a̱ ri na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱
Luka 12:33-34
<<Ta-masha̱a̱ga̱ ma ꞌwaa na yuwa na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana, paaku are̱e̱ aba nii re̱, ta̱kura ta̱kota̱ni wyan, azumba̱ ta̱ni asha̱pi wyan.
Masha̱a̱gi ma ꞌwaa nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ paaku are̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱kura ta̱ba jaa kota̱na̱ wyan, azumba̱ aba jaa ta̱na̱ asha̱pi.
Na̱ wana ta̱hyan, paa ꞌwaa ninhin be̱ ne̱e̱, kabata bigata ninhin be̱e̱ naa.
Ta̱gwaan nata̱ ta̱ꞌwaba
Luka 11:34-36
<<Ayishe ta shi ta̱gwaan nata̱ ta̱ꞌwaba. Kayishe ndaa ne̱e̱ gumunu, hyo̱ ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabi ta̱ba nii naa gwaan.
Kayishe ndaa za ta̱gwaan, hyo̱ ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabi ta̱ba nii sha ta̱yincincin. Kuta̱gwaan nata̱ ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabi hyo̱ ta̱shi ta̱yincincin, ta̱yincincin ta̱ya̱nu ta̱yaburi.
<<Butu za naa nii ara ta̱sha bugyama naa awyatu reeko. Koo buga̱a̱ buka̱, buribi ka̱, koo bundaaki ka̱ iri na bina̱, buhwashe̱ ka̱. Majaa nda na hyan ijwara̱ga Hwe̱n, igura̱a̱ sha̱a̱ nꞌgata kayuwa ha̱ni ka̱.
Ta-makaka ma
Luka 12:22-31
<<Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, na̱ wana kunnu, ta-makaka ma na̱ hyuhyu ninhin wana shami na ga̱hin nii naa re̱, na̱ iri na ga̱hin nii naa swa, koo aꞌwana na ga̱hin nii naa taagana na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwaba ta̱niinhin. Ka̱i, hyuhyu ninhin hurici shami bina̱? Ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱niinhin ta̱hurici ꞌwana bina̱?
Gwatana ma ano̱no̱. Aꞌa̱cii bira, aba a̱cii guba̱, aba a̱cii sha̱a̱ga̱ na̱ nꞌndukwa, ama Bushiinhin nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ taa nii biga wyan. Ga̱hin hurici ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa bina̱ waabwa?
Iyaa ta suga̱hin ne̱e̱ pina na ga̱hin makaki, bunii ara ta̱duwa̱na̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa koo ge̱ nꞌhwe̱n na nꞌta̱ꞌwa̱?
<<Wana ba̱ ga̱hin makaki na̱ aꞌwana na ta̱taana? Gwatana ma kuharuwa na ta̱sumu nata̱ aga ta̱ba ta mawaana. Ta̱ba a̱cii nda tuma, ta̱ba a̱cii mandaaka ꞌwana na ta̱taana.
Ama nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma koo bugwama Suleemaanu hyo̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ta̱ndaabwa, buta nda ruzhanna rundaabwa ruba jaa wuta̱ gama na ta̱sumu.
Too, ku-Hwe̱n nii ara ta̱ndaaka awyamu na aga kunnu, awyamu na ta hyaan kane̱e̱ ba̱re na̱ bunwan ahuni ra, kuga̱hin? Ka̱i ma, ipa̱ni nꞌgata kuge̱ ku-Hwe̱n!
<<Wana kunnu, ta-makaka ma, inaa hyaan, <Iba̱ ga̱tu nii naa re̱?> koo, <Iba̱ ga̱tu nii naa swa?> koo, <Iba̱ ga̱tu nii naa taagana?>
Awyatu na nii paga gumaaka hunrun atanaa wyanzan hyo̱ ri ya̱nu, Bushiinhin naa ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ hoo yansun iribi ri ya̱nu hyo̱.
Pana ma kwan suhyu suniinhin Hwe̱n shi bugwama na nꞌgata nꞌninhin na̱ nꞌta̱naa nda ri na bina̱ kuꞌaꞌuba̱ ndaabi, buna̱maa pana ma hyo̱ taa iri ya̱nu.
Wana kunnu, ta-makaka ma ta̱hyan bunwan paan, bunwan una Hwe̱n ta bwa shi. Ungwan na koya̱ hwe̱n gii ma.>>

Ta-ndaaka ayaan ta̱suuga̱
Luka 6:37-38,41-42
Yeesu be̱ re̱ iyeebe mꞌmazama ma hyaan, <<Ta-ndaaka ma ayaan ta̱suuga̱, ga̱hin taa maa Hwe̱n bwa jamaa ndaaka ma ta̱suuga̱.
Ruꞌwana naru ga̱hin ma̱a̱nyin ayaan nꞌruba, ruba ta bwa na̱maa maanwyan ma taa.
<<Ka̱i! Wana ba̱ gaa nda̱i bishashabi binaa ne̱e̱ na̱ ayishe na yami, ama gaa nda̱ci uguguji na ne̱e̱ na̱ andaa yishe?
Na gaa nii hyan ayami, <xIiya̱a̱cigi bishashabi binaa ne̱e̱ na̱ ayishe ndaa,> gaa na̱ guguji taa na̱ andaa yishe?
Gaa butu naa za mahanda, yaaciga kwan uguguji na̱ ayishe ndaa, naazhin u-a̱ri ta̱yaaciga bishashabi binaa ne̱e̱ na̱ ayishe na ayami.
<<Ta-pana ma ꞌwaa na yuwa ina ta̱sabu paaku awyatu na we̱. Kiinje̱ kunnu ushi haku naa bwaagi sudo̱ nasu ina atari naru shama sukwashe̱ sufo̱nje̱ce̱ wyan na̱ ada̱daba, koo haku naa pa̱ni aba tari kusuwa nasu mꞌpe̱re̱, sukúshe̱, suuga̱ba̱gi.
Rupa ma, wyanzan ma, gba̱a̱nta̱a̱na̱ ma
Luka 11:9-13
<<Naa rupa ma ji, ana̱maa pana ma iri na ga̱hin rupani. Naa wyanzan ma ji, inii da̱ba. Naa gba̱a̱nta̱a̱na̱ ma ji, ana̱maa guna̱a̱nwya̱n ma adubo.
Koo buya̱ naa rupani, anii pana be̱. Koo buya̱ naa wya̱nzhin, bunii da̱ba. Koo buya̱ naa rupani, anii guna̱a̱nwya̱n be̱ adubo.
<<Iyaa ta suga̱hin ne̱e̱ pina kuuyoo rupani be̱ buroodi, bupa̱ni buu tari?
Koo kuurupani be̱ bijooshiipa, bupa̱ni buu hwaa na wuma? Majaa nda!
Kuga̱hin naa shi awyatu na we̱, iyan ri na gama na ga̱hin nii pana mꞌmwaan nꞌniinhin, kuu-Shiinhin naa ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, bunaa nii pana ri na gama kana rupani bwa?
<<Kunnu taa, ndaaka ma awyatu iri na ga̱hin ribi aandaaki ma taa. Ya̱nu ta shi ta̱ꞌyapaga mazama nama Nꞌgira̱nshin na̱ nꞌta̱taga nata̱ acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama hyo̱.
Adubo na ta̱suswee
Luka 13:24
<<Ta̱na̱ ma ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ paaka adubo na ta̱suswee, wana adubo na ha̱a̱n ana huri ta paaku ta̱ꞌwa̱ mahwa, awyatu hwarapi ta ta ta̱na̱ kaun.
Ama adubo na huri paaku bina̱ na mahwa suswee aba ne̱e̱, yo̱n ndaabwa da̱a̱rici, awyatu ha̱hamba ata ara wuun ta̱jwara̱ga.
Ata insan ꞌwe̱e̱ // paaku ta̱ꞌwa̱ri ta̱ndaabwa
Luka 6:43-44
<<Nda ma ha̱nka̱ri na̱ acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ana ta̱be̱. Anii jaa haka na za mayaan haki ka̱ra̱bi, ama na̱ nꞌgata ndaaba akura̱na̱ ta aba shi ana magawa.
Inii insan wyan paaku tuma ndaaba. Anii ara ta̱gwasa ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ uriga̱ paaku sunrun? Koo ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ waanwan paaku sa̱pi?
Kunta taa, ꞌwe̱e̱ na bina̱ ita ꞌwara ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ bina̱. Uꞌwe̱e̱ na zumaancin, kuta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ zumaancin bwa ta ꞌwara.
Za haruwa na ꞌwe̱e̱ na zumaancin bwa nii ꞌwara ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ zumaa. Kunta taa, ꞌwe̱e̱ na zumaa ujaa ꞌwara ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ zumaancin.
Koya̱ ꞌwe̱e̱ na ꞌwa̱rici ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ zumaa xaꞌya̱pi wuun, amunsani wuun kura.
Kunnunu, ga̱hin nii insan wyan paaku tuma ndaaba.
Ana jwarigi ana ta̱be̱ na̱ ana mahanda
Luka 13:25-27
<<Shii koo buya̱ bunaa nii nꞌhyaan, <Butu O̱to̱, Butu O̱to̱,> bwa taa nii ta̱na̱ paaku ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, kuunaa nje̱ iri na Ada nimi na ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ aba ribi.
Awyatu hwarapi nii nꞌhyan na̱ hwe̱n ya̱nu, <Butu O̱to̱! Ga̱tu naa tacita̱a̱ga̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama na̱ nꞌta̱kai ta̱ndaabi, ga̱tu ba̱ha̱nai nꞌhwaanwun na nꞌwe̱ na̱ nꞌta̱kai ta̱ndaabi, ga̱tu ndagi iri hwarapi na ta̱jikita̱na̱ na̱ nꞌta̱kai ta̱ndaabi.>
Sa̱i ga̱n ma hyan wyan, <Ga̱mii yancin ma. Hiika̱ ma na uba̱ nimi ga̱hin naa tagaa ta̱jwara̱ga yo̱n na Hwe̱n.>
Awyatu reeko ana ta̱ma
Luka 6:47-49
<<Kwayaa na hange̱ ta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱ya̱nu ta̱niimi bwa jwarigi tuun, bushi haku butu naa be̱te̱re̱ge̱ naa ma̱ ina ndaabwa hiku da̱da̱da̱ na atari.
Ashira̱ aba ke̱ne̱, rwaga bwa ba̱ni ma̱ni o̱to̱, pyara bwa puuki wuun, ibe̱ huzhici, wana buma̱ wuun hiku da̱da̱da̱ na atari.
Kwayaa na hange̱ ta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱ya̱nu ta̱niimi, bwa jwarigici tuun, bushi haki guzha̱ni na butu, bunaa ma̱ ina ndaabwa paaka ange̱nshe̱n.
Ashira̱ aba ke̱ne̱, rwaga bwa ba̱ni ma̱ni o̱to̱, pyara bwa puuki wuun, ibe̱ huzhi, ye̱ge̱ye̱ge̱.>>
Na Yeesu be̱ hwii ri ya̱nu ta̱bisa̱ga̱ wyan, nꞌgudu na nꞌwyatu hyo̱ be̱ jikita̱ni nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱nde̱e̱be̱,
wana binii nda ta̱ga̱gaagana hakuu naa mꞌbaa ta̱kai, shii haku nꞌwya̱ra̱mi ndaaba nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa.

Yeesu kuda̱gahini butu naa suguma nasu tutuu
Marukusu 1:40-45; Luka 5:12-16
Na Yeesu be̱ cíin kuꞌundu, nꞌgudu na nꞌawyatu hwarapi mꞌba jwárige̱ buu.
Kuuyaan butu ta bunaa suguma nasu tutuu bwa jaa paa Yeesu, bwa ta̱ runrun, bwa hin buu, <<Butu o̱to̱, kuu-ribi, bu-nii ara u-nꞌkuda̱gahini nꞌsuguma suniimi ma naa sabu.>>
Yeesu be̱ cikaa ara nde̱e̱be̱, be̱ a̱nta̱ni bwa ma hyaan, <<Nꞌribi, kuda̱ga, u-naa sabu!>> Kupita suguma nasu tutuu suba kwade̱ge̱.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin bwa, <<Ta-bisa̱ kwan buyaan, sa̱i kuu-ja̱a̱ paaku pirisiti ubwaa nda̱i. U-pa̱ni ri na Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa mꞌba hin xapa̱ni, na hyan awyatu yansun ta̱hyan bu-ne̱e̱ sabu.>>
Yeesu kuda̱gahini bugyama naa sooja na o̱to̱ na Rooma
Luka 7:1-10
Na Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni Kapanahu, kuuyaan sooja na o̱to̱ kasooja na ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Rooma bwa jaa waabe̱, bwa ro̱pe̱ buu, bwa hin,
<<Butu o̱to̱, bugyama niimi taa na̱ ina buꞌa̱rici ta̱hiika̱, ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ꞌwa̱ni bwa, bune̱e̱ nꞌta̱guma ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin bwa, <<Nꞌnii jaga ma kuda̱gahina bwa.>>
Ubwa sooja bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Ga̱n jwaci na hyan u-ta̱ni ina nimi. Ama cita̱ kumazama, bugyama niimi nii kuda̱ga.
Na̱ wana ga̱mi hyuhyu nimi nꞌne̱e̱ taa kunrin naa yaan, ayaan asooja aba ne̱e̱ taa kunrin nimi. Ga̱n ta hyan buka̱, <Jaga,> buja̱a̱, ma hyan buyaan, <Jaa,> bujaa. Ma hyan bugyama niimi, <Nda kunna,> bunje̱ wuun.>>
Na Yeesu be̱ hange̱ maya̱nu, be̱ jikita̱ni, be̱ hin ana jwarigi buu, <<Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, nꞌtade̱be̱ce̱ koo buka̱ na̱ Isiraaꞌila bunaa pa̱nii gata hakuu na̱nna.
Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma wyatu hwarapi ana shici Ayaahudiya aja̱a̱ báni hakuu na̱nna kope na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana, ahunraana shami ta̱re̱ na̱ Ibiraahin na̱ Isiyaaku na̱ Yaakubu na̱ ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
Ama Aꞌisiraaꞌila hwarapi ana shi na hyan ajaa hya̱su ta̱ba ta̱gwama, Hwe̱n ja̱a̱ bwa wyan na̱ ame̱ na ta̱yincincin paaku ta̱ꞌnꞌgaaga na̱ mꞌmbwa ta̱re̱ mꞌba ne̱e̱.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin ubwa sooja, <<Hura̱, manii nda haruwa na gaa pa̱nii gata.>> Nii be̱ ke̱nye̱n bugyama ndaabwa bwa kwade̱ge̱.
Yeesu kuda̱gahini awyatu hwarapi
Marukusu 1:29-39; Luka 4:38-41
Na Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni ina na Biituru, be̱ nda̱i aya̱na̱wan na Biituru na a̱, ataa na̱ wyansun mꞌmamboo.
Yeesu be̱ a̱nta̱ni ara ndaaba, aba kwade̱ge̱ na̱ mꞌmamboo, kabata aba hiiki aba ndaaki buu shami.
Na shurugo bwa nje̱, aba iyaagagi buu awyatu hwarapi ana wyatu na hira̱ ba jwarigi, be̱ bishi wyan mazama aba ba̱nii kawyatu. Be̱ kuda̱gahinai hyo̱ ana ha̱ngagici sa̱.
Ya̱nu tanda na hyan mazama nama bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Ishaaya macigi ta̱hyan,
<<Be̱ sha̱pi suguma sunda̱a̱tu,
be̱ ya̱a̱cigi ta̱hange̱ce̱ sa̱ ta̱nda̱a̱tu.>>
Ta̱guma nata̱ ta̱jwara̱ga Yeesu
Luka 9:57-62
Na Yeesu be̱ nda̱i bigudu riini buu, be̱ hin ana jwarigi buu xaka̱a̱ci hira̱ree na rwaga na o̱to̱.
Sa̱i biyaan biwya̱ra̱mi naa Nꞌgira̱nshin be̱ jaa waabe̱, be̱ hin, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, nꞌna̱maa jwara̱ga hyo̱ paa gaa ja̱a̱.>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Suwa nasu aga suꞌmꞌbaa aꞌibwa na ta̱naa, nꞌno̱no̱ mꞌba mꞌbaa ta̱hurugo nata̱ rocu, ama Buyoo Butu bwaa za ina na hyuhyu ndaabwa.>>
Buyaan bunaa jwarigi buu bwa hin buu, <<Butu O̱̱to̱, xnꞌgii kwan ina ma wuma̱ni ada nimi.>>
Ama Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Nꞌjwárige̱, hakata ana ꞌwa̱gi xawuma̱a̱ni ana ꞌwa̱gi.>>
Yeesu shaani ma̱ni na̱ pyara aba nje̱ fo̱n
Marukusu 4:35-41; Luka 8:22-25
Sa̱i be̱ ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni, ana jwarigi buu aba jwarigi.
kupita sa̱i uyaan pyara na yaburi bwa punshin na̱ rwaga, ma̱ni nama nii rokuuco mꞌbaa ta̱na̱a̱ hantun. Ama Yeesu be̱ ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌrabi.
Ana jwarigi buu aba hiika̱hini buu ma hyaan, <<Butu O̱to̱, ta̱mbiha̱ni! Ta̱na̱manhuwa̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱!>>
Be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Iꞌmꞌbaa bigata ta̱pana kuge̱, iba̱ shaani ga̱hin ne̱e̱ na̱ rukwanyan kunna?>> Kabata be̱ he̱e̱n kaki be̱ yinzha̱nkani pyara na̱ ma̱ni, komba̱ri ibe̱ nje̱ fo̱n.
Ana jwarigi buu aba nje̱ kuma̱, aba ha̱nta̱ni, <<Imba̱ iri na butu ta na̱nna? Bunaa pyara na̱ ma̱ni mꞌba cina̱ni bwa!>>
Yeesu kuda̱gahini wyatu ree ana awyatu na hira̱ ba jwarigi
Marukusu 5:1-20; Luka 8:26-39
Na be̱ ka̱a̱ci hira̱ree naa biin bina ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Agarasa̱na, awyatu ree ana awyatu na hira̱ ba jwarigi aba báni kaꞌabotubotu na paga na aba ta naa wuma̱a̱na̱ wyatu. Ashi ri na rukwanyan na ta̱hyan buza naa nii ara ta̱jwara̱gana ubwa yo̱n.
Aba ta̱a̱ni nu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, aba hin, <<Iba̱a̱ ta̱ gbi na̱ ga̱tu, gaa Buyoo Hwe̱n? Bu-jaa u-ta̱ pa̱ ngwan taa ke̱nye̱n be̱ wuco?>>
Biyaan bigudu naa yaburi naa sudo̱n nasu ina sutanaa kaun ma re̱ ta̱re̱e̱ do̱ko̱ nii be̱e̱ ko.
Aba wyatu naa hira̱ aba ro̱pe̱ Yeesu ta̱hyan, <<Kuu-ta̱ba̱ha̱ni, u-ta̱ ga̱a̱ ta̱ta̱ni ame̱ naa gudu naa sudo̱n.>>
Be̱ hin wyan, <<Hura̱ ma!>> Kupita aba ba̱ni na̱ ame̱ na aba wyatu, aba ta̱ni kiigudu naa sudo̱n. Suba sudo̱n suba hiiki na̱ nꞌsumo̱, suba huri cuun, suba mazooni na̱ ame̱ na dabu na o̱to̱, suba ꞌwa̱gi hyo̱ na̱ ma̱ni.
Aba aꞌiyo̱ na sudo̱n aba gida̱ga̱gi, aba ta̱ni me̱ na ce̱pe̱, aba bisa̱gi wyatu komba̱ri na nje̱, na̱ ri na nje̱ na̱ awyatu ree ana wyatu na hira̱ ba tajwara̱ga.
Kabata hyo̱ ubwa ce̱pe̱ bwa ba̱ni na hyan aꞌura̱ku na̱ Yeesu. Na ba nda̱i buu, aba ro̱pe̱ buu ta̱hyan xbiga̱a̱ ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ ta̱ndaaba.

Yeesu kuda̱gahini butu naa ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ba so
Marukusu 2:1-12; Luka 5:17-26
Na Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni, be̱ huri kaaco̱ zhagu ce̱pe̱ nde̱e̱be̱, Kapanahu.
Ayaan wyatu ba iyaagi buu buyaan butu naa ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ba so, bwa taa taa na̱ aco̱ko̱. Na Yeesu be̱ nda̱i bigata ta̱pana ndaaba, be̱ hin na̱a̱ bwa butu, <<Yaari, nda kii gata, iiha̱mba̱ga̱ncin pinsan ndaa.>>
Nꞌyaan wya̱ra̱mi nami nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa, mꞌbaa mahyaan, <<Buna̱nna butu buhwashe̱ Hwe̱n!>>
Yeesu be̱ e̱nshe̱n ri na abaa makicihinaa na̱ sume̱ sundaaba, be̱ hin, <<Iba̱ shaani ga̱hin nii makicihinaa mazama maya̱nu nama we̱ na̱ nꞌgata nꞌniinhin?
Ya̱ ta huri ta̱yoo ahin, <Iiha̱mba̱ga̱ncin pinsan ndaa,> koo ahin, <Hiika̱, u-huri ta̱hani>?
Ama nꞌribi na hyan iyansun ta̱hyan, Buyoo Butu mꞌbaa ta̱kai na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana nata̱ ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ncin butu pinsan.>> Kabata be̱ hin butu naa ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ba so, <<Hiika̱, u-sha̱pi aco̱ko̱ ndaa, u-huri giyo.>>
Kabata bwa butu bwa hiiki, bwa huri giyo.
Na bigudu naa wyatu be̱ nda̱i kunta, rukwanyan ruba humuni wyan, aba ya̱ba̱ni Hwe̱n, bunaa shi naa pa̱ni ta̱ba ta̱kai kubutu.
Yeesu nꞌgani Maatiyu
Marukusu 2:13-17; Luka 5:27-32
Na Yeesu be̱ re̱ iyeebe nꞌta̱hani, be̱ nda̱i butu naa aba ta nꞌgana Maatiyu, bwa hunrani paaku tuma na ga̱ndu ta̱raaga. Be̱ hin bwa, <<Nꞌjwárige̱.>> Maatiyu bwa hiiki, bwa jwarigi buu.
Na Yeesu be̱e̱ re̱ shami na̱ ina na Maatiyu, awyatu hwarapi ana ga̱ndu ta̱raaga na̱ ana pinsan, aba jaa, aba re̱ shami huku nii be̱ na̱ ana jwarigi buu.
Na Afaraasiya aba nda̱i kunta, aba ha̱nta̱ni ana jwarigi buu, <<Iba̱ shani biwya̱ra̱mi niinhin be̱e̱ re̱ shami na̱ wyatu na ga̱ndu ta̱raaga na̱ ana ga̱a̱ci pinsan?>>
Na Yeesu be̱ hange̱ maya̱nu, be̱ hin, <<Awyatu na ne̱e̱ kami, uza na nii shana wyan amakaka na̱ butu naa njibi, kana ha̱ngagici sa̱.
Ama jaga ma iꞌe̱nshe̱n mana̱nna mazama kwan, <Ambishiri ga̱n ribi wunhin, shii ta̱ꞌmꞌpana bikico̱.> Wana nꞌja̱a̱ci ma nꞌgana awyatu na bina̱, kana ga̱a̱ci pinsan.>>
Mazama nama ruꞌure̱
Marukusu 2:18-22; 5:33-39
Awyatu na jwarigi Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma aba jaa waabe̱, aba ha̱nta̱ni buu, <<Iba̱ shani ga̱tu na̱ Afaraasiya ga̱tu ta naa ndaga ruꞌure̱, ama anaa jwarigi aba a̱cii nda ruꞌure̱?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, <<Ine̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan, inii ara ta̱yansan ta̱shika nata̱ ne̱e̱ da̱nda̱ na̱ butu naa zha̱a̱ buꞌa̱ ta̱re̱ shami na̱ hwe̱n na buki. Ke̱nye̱n wuci naa aba ja̱a̱ shapana wyan be̱, ha̱ni ya̱nu ta aba ja̱a̱ naa ndaga ruꞌure̱.
Buza naa nii dabana da̱bi na gwashe̱ na̱ bisumma naa fo. Kuunje̱ kunnu, bisumma naa fo nii handa ubwa da̱bi, uhuri ta̱ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ kubwa tane̱e̱ na̱ ayigo.
Buza naa nii zooga̱na̱ ma̱ni nama nꞌko̱ro̱ nama fo na̱ nꞌsoso na nꞌta̱sha̱a̱ ma̱ni nama nꞌko̱ro̱ nama gwashe̱. Kuunje̱ kunnu, ma̱ni nama nꞌko̱ro̱ nama fo manii punsa̱n nꞌsoso mawya̱shiki, nꞌsoso na nꞌta̱sha̱a̱ ma̱ni nꞌkuni. xAzooga̱ni ma̱ni nama nꞌko̱ro̱ nama fo na̱ nꞌsoso na nꞌfo taa.>>
Be̱e̱ binaa ꞌwi na̱a̱ a̱ naa nii zoo mahin
Marukusu 5:21-43; Luka 8:40-56
Na be̱e̱ cita̱ga̱ maya̱nu, kuyaan butu o̱to̱ naa ka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya bwa jaa, bwa ta̱ runrun na uba̱ nde̱e̱be̱, bwa hin, <<Be̱e̱ biniimi naa a̱ biꞌwi niina. Ama jaa u-sha̱a̱gi buu nꞌara, binii kúshe̱e̱ wuma.>>
Yeesu na̱ ana jwarigi buu aba hiiki, aba jwarigi bwa butu.
Kuyaan buꞌa̱ naa pa̱ nꞌyo̱ nꞌupwa na̱ nꞌree bwa mazoo mahiin, bwa gii nꞌta̱baa nata̱ Yeesu, bwa a̱nta̱ni biin binaa da̱bi na Yeesu.
Bwa mahin, <<Huwo kunꞌa̱nta̱ni biin binaa da̱bi nde̱e̱be̱, nꞌnii kuda̱ga.>>
Yeesu be̱ ke̱ce̱e̱ke̱, be̱ nda̱i bwa. Be̱ hin, <<Da̱du, nda kiigata ta̱pana gata ndaabi kuga̱mi ta̱a̱ kuda̱gahini.>> Bubwa a̱ bwa kwade̱ge̱ nii be̱ ke̱nye̱n.
Na Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni ina na butu o̱to̱ naa ka̱ta̱ku, kabata be̱ nda̱i bigudu naa wyatu na suruuge na̱ wyatu na nii hurupa̱ga̱ nꞌhuro na nꞌta̱ꞌwa̱.
Be̱ hin, <<Hura̱ ma pata. Bibe̱ be̱e̱ biꞌwici, biroci nꞌrabi.>> Kabata aba ke̱ne̱ buu nꞌratu ta̱ꞌwa̱.
Na aba ba̱ha̱na̱i aba wyatu, be̱ ta̱ni, be̱ kota̱ni be̱ be̱e̱ ara, kabata be̱ híike.
Mazama maya̱nu mꞌba ga̱ta̱a̱gi kope na̱ ame̱ na ta̱ba ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱.
Yeesu kuda̱gahini aruba̱ ree
Na Yeesu be̱ ga̱a̱ kaba pa̱ri, ayaan ruba̱ ree aba jwarigi buu, ma nꞌga, <<Ta̱ndaaki mbishiri, Buyoo Dawuda!>>
Na be̱ ta̱ni yaan ina, aba ruba̱ ba jaa waabe̱, kabata be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan, <<Ipa̱ni nꞌgata ta̱hyan ga̱n nii ara ta̱a̱kuda̱gahina ma?>>
Sa̱i be̱ a̱nta̱ni ayishe ndaaba be̱ hin, <<Kuga̱hin pa̱ni nꞌgata xmaashaagi ma kunnu.>>
Kabata ayishe ndaaba aba huwa̱gi. Yeesu be̱ kooci wyan ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ta̱hyan, <<Ta-bisa̱ ma koo buyaan maba mazama.>>
Hyo̱ na̱ kunnu na aba ba̱ni, aba ke̱ne̱ ta̱naa wyasa maba mazama mande̱e̱be̱ hyo̱ na̱ ame̱ na ta̱ba ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱.
Yeesu kuda̱gahini butu naa a̱rici mazama ta̱cita̱
Na baa bana, kabata aba iyaagi Yeesu butu naa a̱rici mazama ta̱cita̱, wana wyatu na hira̱ jwarigi bwa.
Na ba ba̱ha̱ni wyatu na hira̱, butu naa nu bwa taguna̱ni bwa cici mazama. Bigudu naa wyatu be̱ nje̱ ma̱, abaa hyaan, <<Buza naa tahoo ndaya iri na ne̱e̱ kunna na̱ Isiraaꞌila.>>
Ama Afaraasiya baa hyaan, <<Na̱ ta̱kai nata̱ Bupira̱ ta̱ta, bugwama naa wyatu na hira̱, be̱e̱ ba̱ha̱na̱a̱ wyatu na hira̱.>>
Awyatu na tuma hwaani
Yeesu be̱e̱ wura̱binaa na̱ ace̱pe̱ na̱ nꞌcice̱pe̱ na nꞌne̱e̱ kaun, ma ga̱gaagana awyatu na̱ aka̱ta̱ku ndaaba, ma cita̱ga̱ mazama nama zumaa nama ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, ma kuda̱gahinaa koya̱ iri na suguma na̱ nꞌta̱hange̱ce̱ sa̱.
Na be̱ nda̱i awyatu hwarapi na ne̱e̱ kaun, be̱ hange̱ mbishiri ndaaba, na̱ wana anii swa ngwan, aba za naa gwatani wyan, haki ka̱ra̱bi na zaa iyo̱.
Kabata be̱ hin ana jwarigi buu, <<Uguba̱ jwa o̱to̱ ama awyatu na tuma ba hwaani.
Na̱ wana kunnu, rupa ma butu o̱to̱ naa guba̱, xbukáji atumashini kubwa guba̱.>>

Yeesu ka̱ji aꞌupwa na ree
Marukusu 3:13-19; Luka 6:12-16
Yeesu be̱ nꞌgani ana jwarigi buu aꞌupwa na ree, be̱ pa̱ni wyan ta̱kai nata̱ ta̱ba̱ha̱na̱a̱ nꞌhwaanwun na nꞌwe̱ na̱ nꞌta̱kuda̱gahinaa koya̱ iri na suguma na̱ nꞌta̱hange̱ce̱ sa̱.
Na̱nna tashi azha̱a̱zha̱a̱ na atumashini upwa na ree: bunaa yigo, Siima, bunaa aba ta nꞌgana Biituru, na̱a̱ ya̱na̱ Andaraawa, na̱ Yaakubu buyoo Zabadi, na̱a̱ ya̱na̱ Yoohana,
Filibu na̱ Baatalomi, Toma na̱ Maatiyu butu naa ga̱ndu ta̱raaga, Yaakubu buyoo Hala̱fa, na̱ Tadaawusu,
na̱ Siima, bunaa aba ta hyan butahura̱ ta̱ꞌisa hiku na̱ ce̱nye̱n ta̱ndaabwa, na̱ Yaahuda Isikariyo̱ti bunaa ja̱a̱ pana buu.
Yeesu ka̱ji aꞌupwa na ree
Marukusu 6:7-13; Luka 9:1-6
Na Yeesu be̱e̱ kada aba upwa na ree, be̱ hin wyan, <<Ta-ta̱na̱ ma paaka wyatu na shici Ayaahudiya, koo ita̱ni yaan ce̱pe̱ na Asamaariya.
Haru jaga ma kika̱ra̱bi na fogi ina ina na Isiraaꞌila.
Jaga, bisa̱ ma wyan ta̱hyan, <Ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱goki.>
Kuda̱gahinaa ma ana za kami, ihiika̱hini ana ꞌwa̱gi, ikuda̱gahinai ana mꞌbaa suguma nasu tutuu, iba̱ha̱na̱i wyatu na hira̱. ꞌYe̱n ga̱hin ra̱a̱, ꞌye̱n ga̱hin pana taa.
<<Ta-shapa ma ayuwa na zinaari, koo ana azurufa, koo aniinii na̱ nꞌruzupi.
Ta-shapa ma paaku na̱ ta̱hani ta̱niinhin koo uyaan da̱bi na hin reenu, koo kandaga, koo angwo, wana butu naa tuma uzumaa na hyan bura̱a̱ funa̱ ndaabwa.
Koya̱ ce̱pe̱ koo bicice̱pe̱ naa ga̱hin ta̱ni, wyanzan ma butu naa bina̱, inaa na̱ ina ndaabwa zhagu kiike̱nye̱n naa ga̱hin gaa bwa ce̱pe̱.
Kiinii ta̱na̱ ubwa ina, ihin, <xUhunranhunran na ta̱gumunu naa na̱ ga̱hin.>
Kubwa ina shi na bina̱, ta̱gumunu ta̱niinhin ta̱nii naa na̱ aba, kubwa shi na uwa̱, ta̱gumunu ta̱niinhin ta̱na̱maa kúshitani ma.
Hyo̱ buna buu ra̱a̱ci ma koo bwa shiragici mazama maniinhin, bana ma na̱ bwa ina koo ce̱pe̱, ibukuta̱gi aputu na mꞌbuna nꞌniinhin.
Mahanda ga̱n na̱ maa bisa̱ga̱ ma anii hura̱ ta̱ ha̱nga mbishiri na So̱do̱m na̱ Gomora hwe̱n na ta̱suuga̱ na̱ awyatu na bwa ce̱pe̱.
Mamboo nama wuci
Marukusu 13:9-13; Luka 21:12-17
<<Nde̱e̱ ga̱n ta ga̱n na̱maa kada ma haki ka̱ra̱bi na̱ ame̱ na akura̱na̱. Na̱ wana kunnu mꞌbaa ma mahunre̱n haku yimaga̱ru, inaa na za maꞌwe̱n haku huunruun.
Iya ma shukuu na̱ awyatu wana ana̱maa iya ma kuta̱gwama, aazuragi ma nꞌdunduun na̱ aka̱ta̱ku ndaaba.
Aba na̱ maa iya ma kawyatu na ta̱suuga̱ na̱ nꞌgwama wana iꞌnꞌjwarigi. Ubwa nii sha ha̱ni na hyan ibisa̱gi wyan na̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya mazama maniimi.
Ama kaakota̱ni ma ta-makaka ma na̱ ri na ga̱hin gura̱ha̱na̱, koo iba̱ ga̱hin bisa̱ wyan. Nii be̱e̱ ke̱nye̱n Hwe̱n na̱maa pana ma ri na ga̱hin cita̱,
na̱ wana shii ga̱hin taa nii cita̱, ama Bihwaanwun na Buushiinhin taa na̱maa bisa̱ ma iri na hyan icici.
<<Butu ja̱a̱ panaa ya̱na̱ akwane̱ bwa, ashin na be̱e̱ aba ja̱a̱ pana buyoo. Mꞌmwaan mꞌba ja̱a̱ci cina̱na̱ sushoo, nꞌshani anaa kunaa wyan.
Koo buya̱ ja̱a̱ maa gaa ma na̱ wana nimi, ama bunaa e̱she̱ hiku hara̱ ubwa hwe̱n, buja̱a̱ bina̱.
Kaakaki ma na̱ ce̱pe̱ na̱nna imape̱e̱n kuyaan ce̱pe̱. Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, ta ga̱hin huwa̱ ta̱riin ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Isiraaꞌila, ga̱n Buyoo Butu ja̱a̱ kúshe̱.
<<Bunaa abaa ga̱gaagana buhurici biwya̱ra̱mii ndaabwa, bugyama bwa hurici butu naa ina ndaabwa.
xAna baa ga̱gaagana naa haku nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nꞌndaaba, agyama taa haka wyatu na nꞌina ndaaba. Kaꞌnꞌgani ga̱n, butu naa ina, bugwama naa awyatu na hira̱, too, na aba nii nꞌgana ga̱hin, wyatu na ina nimi?
Bunaa abaa wasa
Luka 12:2-9,51-53; 14:26-27
<<Ta-wasa ma wyatu anaa kaki ma. Za iri na guna̱ni na jaa guna̱a̱, ibe̱ za iri na ne̱e̱ ta̱swee na aba jaa yansun.
Ri na ga̱mii bishi ma ta̱swee taana ma nu icici wuun ba̱da̱. Ri na abaa bishi ma wau wau na̱ dura̱, katana ma sa̱ku icici wuun.
Ta-wasa ma ana nii ara ta̱kuna ta̱ꞌwaba, ama aba jaa ara ta̱kuna bihwaanwun. Ama wasa ma Hwe̱n na nii ara ta̱kuna ta̱ꞌwaba nii hwaanwun kura na za ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱.
Shii nꞌsweeswee nꞌree na nꞌnjeke nꞌta aba ta sa̱a̱nha̱na̱ aniinii ree? Ama bizaa naa nii kina na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n Bushiinhin bwa jaa yansun.
Hyo̱ ta̱hinje nata̱ hyuhyu niinhin uro̱be̱ tuun.
Na̱ wana kunnu ta-ha̱nga ma rukwanyan, ihuri nꞌsweeswee bina̱ ku-Hwe̱n mahwa.
<<Koo buya̱ naa cici ta̱hyan buꞌnꞌribi na̱ aꞌuba̱ na awyatu, ga̱n ja̱a̱ cita̱ ta̱hyan ga̱n ribi be̱ taa na̱ aꞌuba̱ na Ada nimi na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
Koo buya̱ naa hin bwaa nꞌyancin na̱ aꞌuba̱ na awyatu, nꞌja̱a̱ci yansun be̱ taa na̱ uba̱ na Ada nimi na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
<<Ta-hyan ma nꞌjaa ta ma íye̱ hunranhunran na ta̱gumunu na̱ sa̱ra̱ri. Aaꞌa, nꞌja̱a̱ci ma íye̱ hunranhunran na ta̱gumunu ama ugagu.
Na̱ wana nꞌjaa ta ma shana ta̱maꞌunso̱ncin
<< <Kubaa na̱ ashin,
be̱e̱ binaa a̱ na̱ aya̱na̱,
a̱yo yoo na̱ aꞌuugo.
Awyatu na ina na butu, aba ja̱a̱ci ruba̱ be̱.>
<<Kwayaa na huri ta̱ruba̱ ashin koo aya̱na̱ na̱ ga̱mi, bushici na hyan bushi buniimi. Kwayaa na huri ta̱ruba̱ baa koo be̱e̱ bindaabwa binaa a̱, bushici na hyan bushi buniimi.
Kwayaa na sha̱pici guguji ndaabwa bwa nꞌjwarigi, bushici na hyan bushi buniimi.
Kwayaa naa ribi hyuhyu ndaabwa, buja̱a̱cii da̱ba wuun, ama bunaa ga̱a̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa na̱ wana ga̱mi, buja̱a̱ da̱ba wuun.
<<Buna buura̱a̱ ma, buꞌnꞌra̱a̱ ta ga̱mi. Buna buꞌnꞌra̱a̱ ga̱mi, bura̱a̱ ta buna buꞌnꞌkáji.
Bunaa ra̱a̱ bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama na̱ wana bushi bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, bunii raa funa̱ naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama. Mayaan, bunaa ra̱a̱ butu naa bina̱ na̱ wana bushi butu naa bina̱, buja̱a̱ raa funa̱ na butu naa bina̱.
Bunaa pa̱ koo bijogoo ka̱ naa ma̱ni kuuka̱ naa shi naa njeke kana̱nna na nꞌjwarigi, mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, buja̱a̱ da̱ba funa̱ ndaabwa.>>

Yeesu na̱ Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma
Luka 7:18-35
Na Yeesu be̱ hwii ta̱bisa̱ga̱ ana jwarigi buu upwa na ree ri na hyan anje̱, sa̱i be̱ hiiki, be̱ huri, be̱e̱ ga̱gaagana na̱ nꞌcice̱pe̱ ndaaba na nꞌne̱e̱ na̱ Gaalili.
Na Yoohana na ne̱e̱ na̱ zhaaro bwa hange̱ tuma na Ala̱masiihu be̱e̱ ndaga, sa̱i bwa ka̱ji ana jwarigi bwa
xahántani buu ta̱hyan, <<Gaa taa shi Ala̱masiihu bunaa ga̱tu ha̱mbagi bunii jaa, Koo ta̱ha̱mbaga buyaan?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Kushiika ma, ibishi Yoohana iri na ga̱hin hange̱ na̱ iri na ga̱hin nda̱i.
Aruba̱ huwa̱gi, agurubi ba nje̱ ta̱hani, awyatu na suguma nasu tutuu aba kuda̱gagi, awo̱nro̱n ba tibi, ana ꞌwa̱gi ba hiika̱ki, abaa gura̱a̱ bisa̱ga̱ aꞌwa̱ta̱gi mazama nama zumaa.
Hwe̱n ndaaki butu naa za maree maree na̱ ga̱mi rubara̱ka.>>
Ha̱ni na ana jwarigi Yoohana aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱, Yeesu be̱ pa̱shi ta̱naa nda mazama nama Yoohana na̱ bigudu naa awyatu. Be̱ hin, <<Iyaa ta ga̱hin tabana ta̱ndái na̱ hira̱ ceeku? Bunaa ne̱e̱ haka awyamu na nge̱nshe̱n na pyara bwaa puuka̱ koya̱a̱ biin?
Too, iyaa ta ga̱hin taja̱a̱ ta̱ndái? Bunaa ta̱a̱ni aꞌwana na yuwa? Nde̱e̱! Ana ta̱a̱ni aꞌwana na yuwa, ane̱e̱ paaku ta̱gwama. Shii na̱ aga.
Iyaa ta ga̱hin taja̱a̱ ta̱ndái? Butu naa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama? Too, ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, buna̱nna buhuri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ butu naa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama.
Yoohana ta shi bunaa utakaada na Hwe̱n aba tacita̱ ta̱hyan,
<< <Nde̱e̱! Ga̱n nii káji butuma niimi iyeebe ndaa,
bunaa na̱maa a̱sa̱ga̱a̱ga̱ yo̱n ta gaa wuco.>
Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, buza butu wuma naa wuci Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma. Ama bunaa shi njeke njeke na̱ bina̱ ta̱za paaku ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, buhuri bwa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Taa ke̱nye̱n naa Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma zhagu ba̱re ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱ba tanaa swa ta̱guma nata̱ aha̱nka̱ri ta̱hiika̱hina̱, awyatu na we̱ aba ribi ta̱wugujigaga tuun na̱ kai.
Na̱ wana ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ Muusa na̱ atakaada ana acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama hyo̱ acita̱gi mazama nama ta̱ba ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ bwa wuce kuwuco na Yoohana.
Kiinii rana na̱ ri na abaa bisa̱gi ma, Yoohana ta shi butu naa acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ba tanda mazama mandaabwa ha̱ni na aba hin Iliya nii jaa.
Hyo̱ bunaa mꞌbaa ce̱be̱ na tuba̱ xbutibi.
<<Haki ba̱ ga̱n nii kuta̱a̱ awyatu naa ke̱nye̱n yana na̱ be̱? Ashi hakii gudu na mꞌmwaan na nꞌne̱e̱ paaku pa̱ri naka umuntun, mꞌbaa nꞌga aya̱na̱ba ndaaba na umuntun, abaa hyaan,
<< <Ga̱tuu hurupa̱a̱ga̱ga̱ ma suru,
ga̱hin ga̱a̱ ta̱hibwa.
Ga̱tuu zhinyaana ma zha̱a̱ na ta̱ꞌwa̱,
ga̱hin ga̱a̱ ta̱naa nꞌgaaga!>
Ha̱ni na Yoohana bwa tajaa, bwa ma̱a̱ncin ta̱naa re̱ shami, bwa ma̱a̱ncin ta̱naa swa, ga̱hin hin, <Wyatu na hira̱ jwarigi bwa.>
Buyoo Butu bwa wuce, bwaa re̱ga, bwaa swaga. Hyo̱ mꞌmaya̱nu ga̱hin hyaan, <Nde̱e̱! Bumama̱a̱ ta̱re̱e̱ bwa shi sowa̱, bwa shi ta̱shika nata̱ awyatu na ta naa raaga ga̱ndu na̱ awyatu na ga̱a̱ci pinsan.> Hyo̱ na̱ kunnu ata insan ta̱bita̱riga nata̱ Hwe̱n paaku tuma nata̱ ba.>>
Ace̱pe̱ na ga̱a̱ ta̱pana pinsan baa
Luka 10:13-15
Yeesu be̱ ke̱ne̱ ta̱naa pagana ace̱pe̱ ana be̱ tandaga tuma na yaburagi na̱ ame̱ ndaaba nu na̱ wana aga̱a̱ ta̱pana pinsan baa.
<<Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma, ga̱hin awyatu na Koraasi! Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma, ga̱hin awyatu na Batasaida! Ri na rukwanyan na ga̱n ndagi wunhin, ibe̱ shi, be̱ ta ga̱n ndagi na̱ Taaya na̱ Sidon, kahoo pana pinsan baa hasaa. Kata̱a̱ga̱ni ta̱wuzuwuzu, kahunraani ana mazooga̱na̱ nꞌto̱n na̱ hyuhyu, na hyan abisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan apa̱ni pinsan baa.
Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, ama uhwe̱n na ta̱suuga̱, anii hura̱ ta̱ndaaka awyatu na Taaya na̱ Sidon akuri na̱ ga̱hin na ga̱a̱ ta̱gaa pinsan.
Ga̱hin maa, awyatu na Kapanahu, inda̱i ta̱hyan ija̱a̱ hura̱ koo buya̱ ta̱raa ku-Hwe̱n na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱? Too, ija̱a̱cii hura̱. Uja̱maa bwé̱e̱ ma kunrin, kupa̱ri naka awyatu na ꞌwa̱gi. xBwa shi tuma na ta̱jikita̱na̱ na ga̱mii ndaakaki ma ta ga̱n ndagi na̱ So̱do̱m, katane̱e̱ zhagu ba̱re.
Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, ama uhwe̱n na ta̱suuga̱, anii hura̱ ta̱ndaaka awyatu na So̱do̱m akuri na̱ ga̱hin na ga̱a̱ ta̱gaa pinsan.>>
Jaa ma wa̱ka̱mi hyan ide̱be̱ ha̱nka̱na̱
Luka 10:21-22
Nii be̱e̱ ke̱nye̱n Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Ada, Butu O̱to̱ naa hya̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, iigooji wana ta̱hyan bi-soo iri na̱nna kawyatu na be̱te̱re̱ge̱ na̱ mꞌmahunre̱n, gaa bisa̱a̱ wuun kana be̱te̱re̱ge̱ce̱ haku mꞌmwaan.
Ada, kunta ta gaa huri ta̱ruba̱ unje̱.
<<Ada nimi mꞌpa̱ni hyo̱ iri. Bwa za naa yan, koo iyaa ta Buyoo bubwa shi, kaba Shin. Bwa za naa yan, koo iyaa ta Ada aba shi, kuubwaa Yoo na̱a̱ naa Buyoo bubwa ribi xbuyansun.
<<Jaa ma wa̱ka̱mi hyo̱ ninhin ga̱hin awyatu na mꞌbaa ꞌwaa na ca̱ma̱ncin ubwaa kwane̱ ma, nꞌna̱maa ha̱nka̱a̱n ma.
Pana ma hyuhyu ninhin kutuma nimi na ga̱mii ta̱ ma, ijwara̱ga mazama maniimi. Wana ga̱n, nꞌshi naa za mayaan, ga̱n za hyuhyu ta̱guma, bigata niinhin be̱e̱ taa fo̱n.
Na̱ wana tuma niimi ma̱a̱ncin ngwan, iꞌwaa nimi be̱ cima̱ncincin.>>

Ta̱hantana nata̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya
Marukusu 2:23-28--3:1-6; Luka 6:11
Uyaan hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya, Yeesu na̱ ana jwarigi buu, na abaa hura̱, abaa raan cima na shami. Sa̱i abaa hwara̱pigaga mꞌmansan na nꞌshami, abaa re̱ga na aba ha̱ngagi rumunro̱n.
Na Afaraasiya aba nda̱i kunta, aba hin Yeesu, <<Nde̱e̱ iri na anaa jwarigi baa nda ina nꞌgira̱nshin nda̱a̱tu mꞌba yanshin na̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Ka̱i! Icita̱gici iri na Dawuda bwa tanda ha̱ni na bwa na̱ awyatu ndaabwa aba hange̱ rumunro̱n?
Bwa ta̱ni Ina na Hwe̱n paa aba tasha̱a̱ buroodi, una shi kapirisiti baa ka̱ abaa ara ta̱re̱, bwa re̱, bwa na̱ awyatu ndaabwa.
Koo, icita̱gici na̱ ame̱ na takaada na Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa, kuꞌapirisiti ana shi anje̱ tuma na̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ abaa ara ta̱nda tuma ubwaa jaa sha anje̱ pinsan?
Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma tahyan, nde̱e̱ bunaa huri Ina na Hwe̱n na pina.
Ama xga̱hin e̱nshe̱n iri na mazama mana̱nna mꞌba hin, ta̱hyan, <Ambishiri ga̱n ribi wunhin, shii ta̱ꞌmꞌpana bikico̱,> itajaa hyan, awyatu nimi na za pinsan aꞌmꞌbaa pinsan.
Na̱ wana ta̱hyan Buyoo Butu taa shi Butu O̱to̱ naa hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱.>>
Na be̱ ga̱a̱ bibe̱e̱ ko, sa̱i be̱ ta̱ni ka̱ta̱ku ndaaba na Ayaahudiya.
Buyaan butu tanaa kaun bunaa ura bwa swa̱. Wana Afaraasiya nii wyanzan ri na hyan ahin binje̱ pinsan, sa̱i aba ha̱nta̱ni buu, <<Unje̱ to̱n na̱ Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa na hyan akuda̱gahini butu hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱?>>
Be̱ hin wyan, <<Kuuyaan kuga̱hin ne̱e̱ pina buꞌmꞌbaa bika̱ra̱bi, be̱ mazoga̱ni na̱ ibwa na̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱, bujaa jaga buyáacige̱ buu nuu?
Ai, butu buhuri bika̱ra̱bi bina̱! Na̱ wana kunnu une̱e̱ to̱n na hyan butu nje̱ ri na bina̱ na̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱.>>
Be̱ hin bwa butu naa ara ka̱ ubwa so, <<Cikaa ara ndaa.>> Bwa cikaa ubwa ara na so. Kabata ubwa ara bwa kwade̱ge̱, ubwa ne̱e̱ haku na̱nnda̱ree ara.
Ama Afaraasiya aba maꞌnꞌgani na hyan xamaga̱ga̱a̱gi haruwa na hyan akwane̱ Yeesu.
Yeesu bugyama naa Hwe̱n bwa ka̱shi
Na Yeesu be̱ e̱nshe̱n ri na abaa maga̱gaaga, kabata be̱ hiiki, be̱ huri. Bigudu naa wyatu be̱ jwarigi buu, sa̱i be̱ kuda̱gahini hyo̱ ana ha̱ngagici sa̱.
Be̱ kooci wyan ta̱hyan xata bisa̱ koo butu iri na be̱ nje̱.
Ya̱nu tanda wana hyan ta̱cita̱ nata̱ bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Ishaaya ta̱cigi ta̱hyan,
<<Nde̱e̱ bugyama niimi ta bunaa ga̱n ka̱shi,
bunaa ga̱n ribi, bunaa nꞌce̱e̱n na̱ ame̱.
Nꞌnii sha̱a̱ Bihwaanwun niimi na̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa,
bunii bisa̱ awyatu wuma ta̱suuga̱ nata̱ mahanda.
Bujaa naa nda kuda̱ga na̱ awyatu koo iga̱gashi na mazama ma̱,
buzaa naa nii ha̱nga nu ndaabwa na̱ yo̱n.
Usaan na nguncin na nii nda na̱ nꞌta̱kusa bujaa wanyan wuun,
mayaan pitila na goki ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱ bujaa ꞌwa̱ga̱hina̱ wuun,
sa̱i bushaani suuga̱ nasu mahanda ta̱ba e̱she̱ na̱ sa̱ra̱ri.
Wyatu wuma ba nii sha̱a̱ nꞌgata nꞌndaaba na̱a̱ bwa.>>
Yeesu na̱a̱ gwama naa wyatu na hira̱
Marukusu 3:20-30; Luka 11:14-23
Kabata aba íyaagi buu butu naa awyatu na hira̱ ba jwarigi, bunaa shi buruba̱ bwa a̱rici ta̱naa cita̱ga̱ mazama. Yeesu be̱ kuda̱gahini bwa, bwa a̱ri ta̱huwa̱ga̱ na̱ ta̱cita̱ mazama.
Hyo̱ awyatu aba nje̱ kuma̱, aba hin, <<Shii buna̱nna taa shi buyoo Dawuda?>>
Na Afaraasiya aba hange̱ ri na nje̱, sa̱i aba hin, <<Ai, binii paga awyatu na hira̱ sumo̱ na̱ ta̱kai nata̱ Baꞌala̱zabu bugwama naa wyatu na hira̱.>>
Yeesu be̱ e̱nshe̱n sume̱ sundaaba, be̱ hin wyan, <<Hyo̱ ta̱gwama nata̱ mahoosa̱ga̱gi ta̱nii gataaga. Mayaan koya̱ ce̱pe̱ koo ina na mahoosa̱ga̱gi unii huza̱.
Ku-Shatan nii paga awyatu na hira̱ sumo̱, bunii nda ta gagu na̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa, ta̱gwama ta̱ndaabwa ta̱baa jaa isa.
Ama kuga̱n nii paga awyatu na hira̱ sumo̱ na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ bugwama naa awyatu na hira̱, too, awyatu ninhin naa jwarigi ma haan? Aba taamaa anii paga awyatu na hira̱ sumo̱, nꞌta̱kai nata̱ iyaa abaa nda? Aba maa ana̱maa ndaaka ma suuga̱ na̱ iri na ga̱hin cici.
Kushi na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n ta̱ta ga̱n paga awyatu na hira̱ sumo̱, too, ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱wuce wunhin.
<<Ajaa ara ta̱ta̱na̱ ina na butu naa mꞌbaa kai anje̱ zumba̱ na ꞌwaa na ina ndaabwa, sa̱i aka̱da̱a̱gi bwa kwan, naazhin asha̱pa̱gi ꞌwaa ndaabwa.
<<Koo buya̱ butu naa jaa nda huku na̱ ga̱mi, bunaa nꞌga̱a̱ buta bwa shi. Bunaa nꞌnguncin ta̱wuna̱a̱na̱, bunii gata ta.
Na̱ wana kunnu nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma ta̱hyan koya̱ iri na pinsan na̱ hwashe̱ na butu bwa nje̱ ajaa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ bwa, ama koya̱ mazama nama hwashe̱ kii-Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n anii ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ bwa.
Koo buya̱ bucici mazama nama hwashe̱ kuu-Yoo Butu ajaa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ bwa pinsan ndaabwa. Ama koo buya̱ bucici mazama nama hwashe̱ kii-Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n, anii ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ bwa pinsan ndaabwa niina ko nii ke̱nye̱n naa wuci.
Uꞌwe̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwa̱ri ta̱ndaabwa
Luka 6:43-45
<<Ata insan ꞌwe̱e̱ paaku ta̱ꞌwa̱ri ta̱ndaabwa. Kuꞌwe̱e̱ shi una zumaa, ta̱ꞌwa̱ri ta̱ndaabwa ta̱nii zumaa. Kuꞌwe̱e̱ shi una zumaancin, ta̱ꞌwa̱ri ta̱ndaabwa ta̱jaa zumaa.
Ga̱hin bigudu naa suhwaa nasu we̱! Na ta ga̱hin nii ara ta̱cita̱ iri na zumaa tana ga̱hin shi awyatu na uwa̱? Ai, iri na ne̱e̱ nii gata ta tanaa bánai na̱ nu.
Butu naa bina̱ buta cita̱ ri na bina̱ na ne̱e̱ nii gata ndaabwa naa bina̱, butu naa uwa̱ bwa ta cita̱ ri na uwa̱ na ne̱e̱ nii gata naa uwa̱ ndaabwa.
Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, na̱ hwe̱n na ta̱suuga̱ Hwe̱n nii ndaaka koo buya̱ ta̱suuga̱ na̱ koya̱ mazama nama uwa̱ nama bwa tacita̱ga̱.
Na̱ wana mazama nama gaa cita̱ga̱ maba ta ma na̱maa kadaga koo maa ha̱mba̱ri.>>
Wyanzun na ri na ta̱jikita̱na̱
Marukusu 8:11-12; Luka 11:29-32
Uyaan hwe̱n Afaraasiya na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa mꞌba hin Yeesu, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, ta̱ribi ta̱nda̱i ri na ta̱jikita̱na̱ wakaa.>>
Be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Awyatu na we̱ ana ga̱a̱ Hwe̱n anaa ke̱nye̱n yana aribi ta̱ndaya ri na ta̱jikita̱na̱! Ama uza na ga̱n nii bisa̱a̱ wyan, kuna bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Yunuusa.
Haruwa na Yunuusa bwa tanaa na̱ ame̱ na ta̱mba̱ra̱ na ta̱a̱jooshiipa naa yaburi nꞌhwe̱n nꞌtaatu gita na̱ hwe̱n, kunta taa Buyoo Butu bwa ja̱a̱ naa nꞌhwe̱n nꞌtaatu gita na̱ hwe̱n na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n.
Hwe̱n na ta̱suuga̱, awyatu na Nineba anii hiika̱ kunnu taa, aꞌisaga huku na̱ awyatu naa ke̱nye̱n yana, abishi awyatu naa ke̱nye̱n yana anje̱ pinsan na̱ wana aba pa̱ni pinsan baa wana mazama nama Yunuusa be̱ tabisa̱ga̱ wyan. Niina, butu naa huri Yunuusa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ bwa na na̱ aba.
Hwe̱n na ta̱suuga̱, Bisorooniya naa Sheeba nii hiika̱, biꞌisa, bibishi awyatu naa ke̱nye̱n yana ta̱hyan anje̱ pinsan, na̱ wana bitabáni ce̱nye̱n nata̱ me̱mi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, be̱ shiragi mazama nama maca̱ma̱nta̱n nama ta̱yansun nata̱ Bugwama Suleemaanu. Niina butu naa huri Suleemaanu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ bwa na na̱ aba.
Kuswa naa hwaanwun naa we̱
Luka 11:24-26
<<Kiihwaanwun naa we̱ ba̱ni kubutu, bita naa riinshina̱ paaka za wyanfo̱n na̱ wana xbide̱be̱ kuta̱ha̱nka̱na̱. Kiide̱be̱ce̱,
bihin, <Nꞌnii kushiika kubutu naa ga̱n tabáni waabwa.> Jaa kiiwuce, be̱ wuta̱ni ina ne̱e̱ ha̱nda̱, ibe̱ ha̱riki, ibe̱ ne̱e̱ sabu,
bikwashe̱e̱ke̱, bijaa na̱ nꞌyaan nꞌhwaanwun nꞌta̱nda̱ra̱ na nꞌhuri na nꞌyigo ta̱we̱, nꞌta̱ni kubutu yata mayaan. Haruwa na butu bwaa naa uhuri na yigo ta̱we̱. Kunnu ubwaa shaaga awyatu naa ke̱nye̱n yana naa we̱.>>
Ada̱a̱da̱ na Yeesu na̱ aya̱na̱ba
Marukusu 3:31-35; Luka 8:19-21
Yeesu mꞌmazama na̱ awyatu, ada̱a̱da̱ nde̱e̱be̱ na̱ aya̱na̱ba aba wuce, aba isagi na̱ sa̱ra̱ri, aba ribi ta̱nda mazama nii be̱.
Sa̱i buyaan bwa bishi buu ta̱hyan, <<Ada̱a̱da̱ ndaa na̱ ayamboo ree na̱ hwa aꞌisagi, aribi ta̱nda mazama na̱ gaa.>>
Be̱ hin, <<Ayaa ta shi da̱a̱da̱ nimi? Abwaa ba shi aya̱too?>>
Be̱ cikaa ara kana jwarigi buu, be̱ hin, <<Nde̱e̱ ada̱a̱da̱ nimi na na̱ aya̱too nimi.
Wana koo buya̱ naa nje̱ ri na Ada nimi ana ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ aba hin xanje̱, bwa taa shi buya̱tu naa wya̱ri na̱a̱ naa a̱ na̱ ada̱a̱da̱ nimi.>>

Ta̱kun nata̱ butu naa ta̱bira
Marukusu 4:1-12; Luka 8:4-10
Na̱ bwa hwe̱n ya̱nu Yeesu be̱ ba̱ni na̱ bwa ina, be̱ ja̱a̱, be̱ hunrani nii biin binaa Rwaga na O̱to̱ na Gaalili.
Bigudu naa wyatu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ be̱ riini buu, sa̱i na be̱ ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni, be̱ hunrani, awyatu aba isagi na̱ inza̱n.
Be̱ bisa̱gi wyan mazama ma hwarapi na̱ nꞌta̱kun, be̱ hin, <<Buyaan buhwaanyan tabana ta̱wyasa kaasu na̱ cima ndaabwa.
Na bwaa wyasa ikaasu, ika̱ be̱ kinai na̱ yo̱n, nꞌno̱no̱ mꞌba ta̱in wuun.
Iyaan ibe̱ kinai paaku atari kaba za ce̱nye̱n du. Sa̱i ibe̱ báni kunrun wana be̱e̱ ko za ce̱nye̱n du.
Na hwe̱n bwa báni ibe̱ hoogi zaga na̱ wana anga̱nga̱nda̱ irici na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n.
Iyaan kaasu ibe̱ kinai kasa̱pi. Na asa̱pi ba mawaani, aba hwii hyo̱ be̱ kaasu ta̱tuba̱ga̱.
Iyaan ibe̱ kinai kupa̱ri naka mawundu, ibe̱ báni, ibe̱ ꞌwa̱ruba̱ni ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nꞌyina̱ nꞌka̱a̱ nꞌka̱a̱, ika̱ kuje cininhin cininhin, ika̱ kuje taatu taatu na ri na aba tabira.
Hyo̱ bunaa mꞌbaa ce̱be̱ na ta̱tuba̱ xbutibi.>>
Sa̱i ana jwarigi buu aba jaa, aba ha̱nta̱ni buu, <<Iba̱ shani gaa nda ta̱ga̱gaagana nꞌta̱kun?>>
Be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Ga̱hin aapa̱ni ma na hyan iyansun ashe̱re̱ na ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, ama aba, apa̱ncin wyan.
Kuꞌana nꞌshiragi ta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱niimi, Hwe̱n nii duwa̱na̱ wyan ta̱yansun, ayansun ta̱ꞌo̱to̱. Ama kuꞌana nꞌshiraagici, koo una aba yan ge̱, Hwe̱n nii yaaciga ta̱yansun, uga̱a̱ wyan kunta.
Ri na shani na ga̱n ga̱gaagana wyan na̱ nꞌta̱kun,
<<Anii gwataaga aba jaa ndaya,
ashiraaga aba jaa yansun iri na cici.
Mahanda ta̱cita̱ nata̱ bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Ishaaya ta̱cigi waaba ta̱hyan,
<< <Ta̱ha̱nga inii ha̱nga, ama ga̱hin jaa yansun iri na aba hin mahwa,
ta̱ndaya inii ndaya, ama ga̱hin jaa huwa̱ga̱ iri na aba nje̱ mahwa.
Na̱ wana nꞌgata na nꞌawyatu na̱nna shirigi,
aba bukakani suce̱be̱ sundaaba,
aba guna̱a̱ni suyishe sundaaba,
na̱ wana hyan xata ndaya nꞌsuyishe sundaaba,
xata ha̱nga nꞌsuce̱be̱ sundaaba,
xata insan na̱ nꞌgata nꞌndaaba iri na ne̱e̱,
na hyan ayimirike wa̱ka̱mi ma kuda̱gahina wyan.>
Hwe̱n ndaaki ma rubara̱ka wana suyishe suniinhin suhuwa̱gi, na̱ suce̱be̱ suniinhin suba hange̱.
Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, awyatu na ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama na̱ awyatu na bina̱ ataruba̱ ta̱ndaya iri na ga̱hin nda̱i, aba nda̱ci wuun. Ataruba̱ ta̱ha̱nga iri na ga̱hin hange̱, aba hange̱ce̱ wuun.
Iri na ta̱kun nata̱ hwaanyan ta̱ba shi
Marukusu 4:13-20; Luka 8:11-15
<<Shiraaga ma ri na mazama nama ta̱kun nata̱ hwaanyan ta̱ba shi na:
Ikaasu na kinai na̱ yo̱n ibe̱ ta shi haka awyatu na hange̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n ama aba e̱nshe̱nshe̱n muu. Bupira̱ bwa wuce, bwa ya̱a̱cigi muu na̱ nꞌgata nꞌndaaba.
Ikaasu na kinai na̱ apaga ibe̱ ta shi haka awyatu na hange̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n, aba ra̱a̱ muu kunrun nꞌara nꞌree.
Ama mꞌba irici na̱ nꞌgata nꞌndaaba wana ashi haki shami na e̱she̱ be̱ za anga̱nga̱nda̱ na iri na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n. Kungwan wuce wana apa̱ni nꞌgata kumazama nama Hwe̱n ape̱e̱n muu nii inro̱n.
Ikaasu na kinai kuꞌasa̱pi ibe̱ ta shi haka awyatu ana hange̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n. Ama wana ta̱makaka na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana, na̱ wyanzun na ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa iri ma̱ na riini muu ma re̱ muu, ushaani muu aba jaa nda kaasu.
Ama ikaasu ina kinai nii koo naa mawundu, ibe̱ ta shi haka awyatu na hange̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n, aba e̱nshe̱n muu, sa̱i mꞌba maꞌwa̱ruba̱ga̱ni, ika̱ nꞌyina̱ nꞌka̱a̱ ka̱a̱, ika̱ kuje cininhin cininhin, ika̱ kuje taatu taatu, na ri na aba tabira.>>
Ta̱kun nata̱ awyababa na̱ ame̱ na ahyu
Yeesu be̱ gura̱a̱ bisa̱ wyan ta̱yaan ta̱kun, be̱ hin, <<Ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ne̱e̱ haku butu naa be̱re̱ ikaasu na zumaa na̱ cima ndaabwa.
Ama na koo buya̱a̱ bwa taa nꞌrabi na̱ gita, butu naa ribici bwa, bwa wuce, bwa be̱re̱ awyababa na̱ me̱ na ahyu, bwa huri ta̱hani ta̱ndaabwa.
Na ahyu ba mawaani, aba nje̱ suyishe, awyababa ba mawaani taa huku.
<<Sa̱i agyama na butu naa hya̱ cima aba wuce, ba hin bwa butu, <Butu naa ina, shii ikaasu na bina̱ ta gaa tabira na̱ cima ndaa? Na ikaasu na awyababa ba báni?>
<<Bwa hin wyan, <Butu naa nꞌribici taa tabe̱re̱.>
<<Agyama ndaabwa ba ha̱nta̱ni bwa, <xTa̱ja̱a̱ ta̱muunyin?>
<<Bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <Aaꞌa, xuta jaa shi ha̱ni na ga̱hin muunwya̱n awyababa ija mata̱ ahyu.
Hakata ma wyan huku amawaani da̱nda̱, kiike̱nye̱n naa guba̱. Ha̱ni na guba̱, nꞌja̱a̱ bisa̱ awyatu na tuma aya̱a̱cigi kwan awyababa, awuna̱a̱ni wyan, aka̱da̱a̱gi wyan, ahuunhuni wyan. Ama ahyu azooga̱ni na̱ nꞌndukwa.> >>
Ta̱kun nata̱a̱ kaasu naa masa̱ta
Marukusu 4:30-32; Luka 13:18-21
Yeesu be̱ gura̱a̱ bisa̱ wyan ta̱yaan ta̱kun, be̱ hin, <<Ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱shi hakii kaasu naa masa̱ta, binaa butu bwa be̱re̱ na̱ cima ndaabwa.
Be̱ taa shi naa hura̱gi mawuzhira̱ kikaasu hyo̱, ama jaa kiinje̱ o̱to̱ bihura̱gi hyo̱ koya̱ iri na ꞌwaa na shiipa na aba be̱re̱ na̱ cima, biba̱ni ꞌwe̱e̱, nꞌno̱no̱ ndagi ta̱hurugo na̱ aruun na bwa ꞌwe̱e̱.>>
Ta̱kun nata̱a̱ kaasu naa yisiti
Be̱ gura̱a̱ bisa̱ wyan ta̱yaan ta̱kun, <<Ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱shi haku nꞌhyun na nꞌyisiti, na mꞌbuꞌa̱ bwa ye̱be̱ na̱ nꞌhyun o̱to̱ ubwa hange̱ hyo̱ na̱ mꞌba nꞌhyun mꞌba she̱ke̱re̱ke̱.>>
Yeesu tanaa bisa̱ga̱ awyatu hyo̱ mazama mande̱e̱be̱ na̱ nꞌta̱kun, biza iri na be̱ tabishi sa̱ wyan na shici nꞌta̱kun.
Una̱nna shi ta̱ciga̱hina̱ nata̱ mazama nama bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Ishaaya bwa tanda,
<<Nꞌnii cita̱ga̱ mazama nꞌta̱kun.
Iri na tanaa ta̱swee ta nꞌta̱nda nata̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana, nꞌnii banrinyan wuun.>>
Iri na ta̱kun nata̱ awyababa na̱ ame̱ na ahyu ta̱ba shi na
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ga̱a̱ bibe̱e̱ gudu, be̱ ta̱ni ina. Ana jwarigi buu aba wuce, ba ha̱nta̱ni buu ta̱hyan, <<Ta̱bishi iri na ta̱kun nata̱ awyababa na̱ ame̱ na ahyu ta̱ba shi.>>
Be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Buyoo Butu taa shi buhwaanyan naa nii wyasa ikaasu na gama.
Ucima ta shi sa̱ra̱ri yana, ikaasu na gama ibe̱ ta shi mꞌmwaan na nꞌta̱ba ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱. Aba awyababa ta shi mꞌmwaan na mꞌbutu naa we̱.
Butu naa ribici buhwaanyan naa be̱re̱ awyababa bwa taa shi Shatan. Ha̱ni guba̱ bwa shi ta̱huwo nata̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana. Awyatu na guba̱ ba shi atuma na Hwe̱n.
<<Haruwa na aba wuna̱ni awyababa, ahuunhuni wyan na̱ ra, kunta ubwa ja̱a̱ sha kuta̱huwa̱ nata̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana.
Buyoo Butu ja̱a̱ káji atuma na Hwe̱n ndaabwa, amuunyin hyo̱ iri na ta shaana awyatu naa ndaga pinsan na̱ hyo̱ ana tanaa ndaga iri na we̱, aba̱ha̱ni wyan kuta̱gwama ta̱ndaabwa.
Anii bwa wyan kura na hura̱gi mamboo, kaba aba nii nda nꞌungwa na̱ mꞌmbwa ta̱re̱.
Awyatu na bina̱ ba nii tara̱kana ta̱gwaan ta̱ndaaba haku hwe̱n paaku ta̱gwama nata̱a̱ Shiiba. Hyo̱ bunaa mꞌbaa ce̱be̱ nata̱ tuba̱ xbutibi.
Ta̱kun nata̱ iri na hura̱gi yuwa
<<Ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱shi haku iri na hura̱gi yuwa ina wuma̱ni na̱ cima. Na butu bwa nda̱i wuun, bwa gura̱a̱ wuma̱na̱ wuun. Wana bune̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱da̱ri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, bwa ja̱a̱, bwa sáanhinai hyo̱ iri ndaabwa, bwa gura̱a̱ san bwa cima.
<<Ji da̱i mayaan, ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱shi, haku butu naa nii wyanzan zinaari na hyan busa̱n.
Na bwa de̱be̱ uzinaari ka̱ na hura̱gi yuwa ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa, bwa ja̱a̱, bwa sáanhinai hyo̱ iri ndaabwa, bwa gura̱a̱ san wuun.
Ta̱kun nata̱ ataaro ana kota̱ga̱ni na nꞌjooshiipa
<<Ji da̱i mayaan, ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱shi haka ataaro ana kota̱ga̱ni na nꞌjooshiipa ana aba bwe̱ na̱ dabu, aba kota̱ga̱ni nꞌjooshiipa zwaan mahwarapi.
Na ataaro ba cigi, sa̱i aba máni wyan inza̱n, aba tura̱ni nꞌjooshiipa, aba ta̱in na nꞌgama, na nꞌzumaancin aba bwe̱ muu pata.
Kunnu ubwa nii sha kuta̱huwa̱ nata̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana ta̱wuce. Atuma na Hwe̱n nii jaa, ahooshi ana suhari nata̱ bina̱ kuꞌana we̱.
Anii bwa ana we̱ kura na hura̱gi mamboo, kaba aba nii nda nꞌungwa na̱ mꞌmbwa ta̱re̱.
<<Iꞌe̱nshe̱n hyo̱ iri ya̱nu?>>
Aba ra̱ni, aba hin, <<Ee.>>
Sa̱i be̱ hin wyan, <<Na̱ wana kunnu, hyo̱ biwya̱ra̱mi naa Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa binaa shi naa nꞌjwarigi na̱ nꞌta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, bishi haku butu naa ina, bunaa díbe̱ iri ndaabwa díbe̱ iri na fo na̱ na gwashe̱ paaku bwa sha̱a̱gi ꞌwaa ndaabwa.>>
Aga̱a̱ Yeesu na̱ Naazare
Marukusu 6:1-6; Luka 4:16-30
Na Yeesu be̱ hwii ta̱bisa̱ga̱ wyan mazama nꞌta̱kun hyo̱, be̱ ga̱a̱ bwa ce̱pe̱.
Na be̱ jaa ce̱pe̱ nde̱e̱be̱, sa̱i be̱ ke̱ne̱ ta̱naa ga̱gaagana awyatu na̱ aka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya, aba ndagi kuma̱, aba hin, <<Pe̱kata butu na̱nna bwa díbe̱ ta̱yansun kunna na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ ta̱naa ndaga iri na ta̱jikita̱na̱?
Buna̱nna shii buyoo buusha̱bi yata ta? Aya̱na̱ aba shi Maariyamu? Aya̱na̱ba ba shi Yaakubu na̱ Yusufu na̱ Samiinu na̱ Yaahuda?
Aya̱na̱ba na a̱ shii aba na hyo̱ na̱ ga̱tu? Too, pe̱kata butu na̱nna bwa díbe̱ hyo̱ ina̱nna ri?>>
Sa̱i abaa fukaa gata nii be̱.
Ama Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Ata pa bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama hunrun kope ama shii na̱ ce̱pe̱ ndaabwa na̱ ina ndaabwa.>>
Be̱ ndagici iri na ta̱jikita̱na̱ hwarapi wana ta̱pa̱ncin nꞌgata ndaaba.

Ta̱ꞌwa̱ nata̱ Yoohana na baba̱tiisa̱ma
Marukusu 6:14-29; Luka 9:7-9
Na̱ bwa ha̱ni ya̱nu na Hirudu Antipasi bwa hange̱ iri na Yeesu be̱e̱ ndaga,
sa̱i bwa hin awyatu na tuma ndaabwa, <<Ai, ya̱nu unii sha Yoohana na baba̱tiisa̱ma nu, buhiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱, ta shani bwa mꞌbaa ta̱kai ta̱ya̱nu nata̱ ta̱naa ndaga ri na ta̱jikita̱na̱.>>
Na̱ wana Hirudu tahoo shana aba kota̱ni Yoohana, aba zwa̱ga̱ni bwa na̱ zhaaro, wana aꞌa̱yoo ya̱na̱ Hiruudiya. Buta sha aꞌa̱yo Filibu buya̱na̱ naa o̱to̱.
Na ta̱hyan Yoohana tanaa sa̱ bisa̱ga̱ Hirudu ta̱hyan, <<Kuꞌnꞌgira̱nshin mꞌba hin, uzumaancin na hyan u-zha̱a̱ bwa.>>
Koo na ta̱hyan Hirudu taruba̱ ta̱kuna Yoohana, ama bwa hange̱ rukwanyan, wana awyatu sha̱pi ta̱hyan Yoohana shi bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama.
Ama na hwe̱n na ta̱matamanrinyan ta̱ma̱ncin nata̱ Hirudu bwa riini, sa̱i buyoo Hiruudiya naa a̱ be̱ nje̱ ta̱hibwa nata̱ caanhini Hirudu bigata na̱ agai ndaabwa na jaa buki.
Hyo̱ na̱ nꞌta̱taa sa̱nsan bunii pana buu hyo̱ iri na be̱ rupani bwa.
Ama na aya̱na̱ ba hurupa̱ga̱ni buu ce̱be̱, sa̱i be̱ hin, <<Mꞌpa̱ni hyuhyu na Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma u-cágudani wuun na̱ kada.>>
Bugwama bwa hange̱ce̱ gama mahwa, wana butahoo taa sa̱nsan na̱ aꞌuba̱ na agai ndaabwa, sa̱i bwa pa̱ni nu xapa̱ni buu iri na be̱ ha̱nta̱ni.
Bwa ka̱ji, aba ja̱a̱, ba ꞌyápi hyuhyu na Yoohana na̱ zhaaro.
Aba shápi hyuhyu na Yoohana na aba cágudani na̱ kada, aba cikaa be̱e̱ bibe̱e̱, be̱ ja̱a̱, be̱ cikaa aya̱na̱.
Na aba hwii, ana jwarigi Yoohana aba jaa, ba wuma̱ni bwa. Aba huri, ba bishi Yeesu.
Yeesu pa̱ awyatu dubu ta shami
Marukusu 6:30-44; Luka 9:10-17; Yoohana 6:1-14
Na Yeesu be̱ hange̱ kunnu, sa̱i be̱ ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni, be̱ huri paaka za koo butu na hyan binaa be̱e̱ ka̱. Ama na bigudu naa awyatu be̱ hange̱ paa be̱ huri, aba bánai kuꞌace̱pe̱, aba jwarigi buu na̱ mꞌbuna.
Na be̱e̱ naa ca̱a̱n na̱ inza̱n, sa̱i be̱ wuta̱ni bigudu naa wyatu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱. Ambishiri ba kota̱ni buu, be̱ kuda̱gahinai ana ha̱ngagici sa̱.
Na shurugo bwaa naa nda, sa̱i ana jwarigi buu aba wuce waabe̱, aba hin buu, <<Pa̱ri kayana kaza koo butu, uhwe̱n ta bwa ke̱ne̱ ta̱ꞌira̱. Cipana awyatu, wana hyan ata̱ni kuꞌnꞌcice̱pe̱, amasáanwyain shami.>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni wyan, <<Ushici ga̱ga̱ga̱ ahuri. Ga̱hin pa ma wyan shami xare̱.>>
Aba hin buu, <<Mꞌburoodi nꞌta na̱ nꞌjooshiipa nꞌree ga̱tu mꞌbaa hina huwa̱.>> Bread and fish|hk00155c.tif|col|14:13-21||Mꞌburoodi na̱ nꞌjooshiipa|14:17Be̱ hin wyan, <<Nꞌiyaagi ma paan.>>
Sa̱i be̱ hin xawyatu hunraana na̱ awyamu. Na be̱ sha̱pi aba buroodi ta na̱ nꞌjooshiipa nꞌree, sa̱i be̱ ka̱cihini hyuhyu da̱da̱da̱, be̱ gooji Hwe̱n, be̱ ya̱biza̱gi, be̱e̱ pagana ana jwarigi buu, aba baa pagana awyatu.
Koo buya̱ bwa re̱, bwa cigi haruwa na gii bwa. Ana jwarigi buu aba wuna̱a̱ni na bwe̱ nꞌtumunsun nꞌupwa na̱ nꞌree.
Awyatu na tare̱ atanda awyatu dubu ta, aba ta shiici aꞌa̱ na̱ mꞌmwaan.
Yeesu nje̱ ta̱hani da̱da̱da̱ na ma̱ni
Marukusu 6:45-56; Yoohana 6:15-21
xAnaa huwa̱, sa̱i be̱ hin ana jwarigi buu xanaa hura̱na̱ buu zhagu hira̱ree, be̱ ma cipana awyatu.
Na be̱ hwii wyan ta̱cipana, sa̱i be̱ ka̱ta̱ni undu be̱e̱ ka̱ wana hyan xbinje̱ ro̱pe̱. Kugita bwa nje̱, be̱ ma naa kaun be̱e̱ ka̱.
Na̱ bwa ha̱ni uhantun tahoo naa wyantancin na ma̱ni, ata na ma̱ni ma basagana wuun, upyara bwaa mana wuun.
Utanaa nda do̱ko̱ kasu na shiri, sa̱i Yeesu be̱e̱ hure ta̱hani da̱da̱da̱ na ma̱ni zhagu kana jwarigi buu.
Na ana jwarigi buu aba nda̱i buu ma nda ta̱hani da̱da̱da̱ na ma̱ni, sa̱i aba hange̱ rukwanyan. Aba ta̱ ta̱ꞌungwa nata̱ rukwanyan, aba hin, <<Upataruwa ta!>>
Sa̱i be̱ bishi wyan mazama na̱ ha̱ni, <<Ta ma kiishita̱. Ga̱n ta. Ta-ha̱nga ma rukwanyan.>>
Sa̱i Biituru bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Kushi gaa ta, Butu O̱to̱, too, hyan nꞌjaa wakaa na̱ nꞌta̱hani da̱da̱da̱ na ma̱ni.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin bwa, <<Jaa ka̱i.>>
Sa̱i Biituru bwa ba̱ni na̱ hantun, bwa ke̱ne̱ ta̱hani da̱da̱da̱ na ma̱ni zhagu paaku Yeesu.
Ama na bwa nda̱i upyara ma̱a̱ kai, sa̱i bwa hange̱ rukwanyan, bwa ke̱ne̱ ta̱ꞌira̱, bwa ta̱ ta̱ꞌungwa, <<Butu O̱to̱, mꞌbiha̱ni.>>
Kunrun na̱ ha̱ni Yeesu be̱ cikaa ara, be̱ kota̱ni bwa. Be̱ hin, <<Gaa naa pa̱ni gata kuge̱. Wana ba̱ gaa ta̱zhiga̱ncin gata?>>
Na aba ta̱ni hantun, upyara bwa taa fo̱n.
Ana ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ na hantun, aba pa̱ buu hunrun, aba hin, <<Mahanda, gaa Buyoo Hwe̱n ta gaa shi.>>
Na aba ka̱a̱ci bwa rwaga na o̱to̱, aba ciin na̱ Janiisarata.
Na awyatu na ta̱ba ce̱nye̱n aba e̱nshe̱n ta̱hyan Yeesu ta, sa̱i mazama mꞌba wuci kope kuta̱ba ce̱nye̱n, aba iyaagagi buu hyo̱ ana ha̱ngagici sa̱.
Aba ro̱pe̱ buu ta̱hyan ana ha̱ngagici sa̱ xaꞌa̱nta̱a̱ni koo bibiin binaa da̱bi nde̱e̱be̱. Hyo̱ ana a̱nta̱a̱ni aba kuda̱gagi.

Nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌawyatu o̱to̱
Marukusu 7:1-23
Ayaan Afaraasiya na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin ana báni Hurushaliima aba wuce paa Yeesu, aba ha̱nta̱ni buu,
<<Iba̱ shani anaa jwarigi aba jwarigici nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌawyatu o̱to̱, na abaa re̱ shami na shikita̱gici nꞌara sabu?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Wana ba̱ ga̱hin jwarigici nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n, kuꞌnꞌniinhin?
Wana Hwe̱n hin, <Cina̱na̱ abaaba ndaa na̱ ada̱a̱da̱ ndaa.> Bwa gura̱a̱ hyan, <Hyo̱ bunaa cwaagani ashin koo aya̱na̱ ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ akwane̱ be̱.>
Ama ga̱hin hin uzumaa butu hin aya̱na̱ koo ashin, <Re̱ kuri, hyo̱ iri na gaa tahiin da̱ba wa̱ka̱mi nꞌhoo pe̱e̱n wuun na hyan ma pana Hwe̱n.>
Na̱ kunnu inii hyaan nu, xata cina̱na̱ ashin koo aya̱na̱. Ama wana nꞌgira̱nshin nꞌniinhin nꞌta nꞌshani ga̱hin ga̱a̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n.
Ga̱hin awyatu na za mahanda, to̱n ta Ishaaya be̱ tacita̱ wana ninhin na be̱ tahyan,
<< <Awyatu na̱nna ana̱maꞌmꞌpaga hunrun kuna̱ nu,
ama nꞌgata nꞌndaaba nꞌne̱e̱ tutu na̱ ga̱mi.
ꞌYe̱n ta abaa mꞌpaga hunrun.
Anii ga̱gaagana awyatu nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌwyatu wuma,
ta̱hyan anii ga̱gaagana Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n.> >>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ nꞌgani bigudu xahange̱. Sa̱i be̱ hin, <<Shiraga ma iꞌe̱nshe̱n ki.
Shii iri na ta̱ni na̱ nu na butu ta nii ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ bwa, ama ri na báni na̱ nu ndaabwa ta nii ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ bwa.>>
Sa̱i ana jwarigi buu aba ja̱a̱ waabe̱, aba ha̱nta̱ni buu, aba hin, <<Bi-yan ta̱hyan Afaraasiya gware̱ sume̱ na aba hange̱ iri na gaa cici?>>
Be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Koya̱ ta̱bira nata̱ shici Abaaba nimi na ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta be̱re̱, anii muu tuun.
Hakata ma wyan. Aruba̱ ta ana tanaa mana aruba̱ ango. Kushi buruba̱ taa nii mana buruba̱ ango, hyo̱ ndaaba aba ja̱a̱ mamunsana na̱ ibwa.>>
Biituru bwa hin buu, <<Ta̱bisa̱gi iri na ta̱kun ta̱ya̱nu ta̱ba hin ki.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Ka̱i, ita e̱nshe̱nshe̱n mahwa?
Ga̱n ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan hyo̱ iri na butu bwa re̱, na yigo inii ta̱na̱ nu ndaabwa, zhagu ta̱mba̱ra̱, ijaa gura̱a̱ bana nꞌta̱ꞌwaba.
Ama iri na nii bánai paaku nu na butu, nii gata ndaabwa ta ibe̱e̱ báni. Ibe̱ ta shi na ta ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ butu ku-Hwe̱n.
Na ta̱hyan, nii gata ta iri na zumaancin ibe̱ ta naa bánai. Haku ta̱kuna butu, na̱ wyanzun na a̱ na ta̱wya̱ri na̱ banshaun, na̱ zumba̱, ta̱hyan ri na shici mahanda ishi mahanda, na̱ tahanshinhina butu ruzha̱a̱.
Iri ya̱nu ta taha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ butu ku-Hwe̱n, ama ta̱re̱ shami na shikici ara a̱cii ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ butu ku-Hwe̱n.>>
Buyaan buꞌa̱ naa pa̱nii gata
Marukusu 7:24-30
Yeesu be̱ ga̱a̱ kaun, be̱ huri ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Taaya na̱ Sidon,
sa̱i kuyaan buꞌa̱ naa ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Kaꞌaana bwa jaa waabe̱, bwa ta̱a̱ni nu, bwa hin, <<Ha̱nga ambishiri nimi Butu O̱to̱, Buyoo Dawuda. Buyaan butu naa hira̱ naa we̱ taa nii pa be̱e̱ biniimi ngwan ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.>>
Yeesu be̱ hincin be̱ koori. Sa̱i ana jwarigi buu aba jaa waabe̱ aba ro̱pe̱ buu, aba hin, <<Pa be̱ sumo̱, wana buta̱jwárige̱, bwaa ta̱sha̱a̱ na̱ ta̱ꞌungwa.>>
Be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Hwe̱n nꞌkáji wana ka̱ra̱bi na Isiraaꞌila na fogi, shii wana iyaan.>>
Ama bwaa a̱ bwa ta̱ runrun na̱ aꞌuba̱ nde̱e̱be̱, bwa hin, <<Butu O̱to̱, nꞌguni ga̱mi.>>
Be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Uzumaancin asha̱pi shami na mꞌmwaan abwaagagi suwa.>>
Bwaa a̱ bwa hin, <<Kunnunu Butu O̱to̱, koo suwa suta taan nꞌwuzu na nꞌnii kinaa paaku ta̱re̱ shami na butu naa ina.>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Buꞌa̱, ta̱panaa gata ndaabi ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa kai, iri na gaa ribi nje̱ kunnu.>> Na̱ ha̱ni bwa, be̱e̱ bindaabwa naa a̱ be̱ kwade̱ge̱.
Yeesu kuda̱gahinai awyatu hwarapi
Maya̱nu mꞌba hwii, sa̱i Yeesu be̱ huri bibiin naa Rwaga na O̱to̱ na Gaalili, be̱ ka̱ta̱ni biꞌundu, be̱ hunrani.
Awyatu hwarapi aba jaa waabe̱ ma íyagi agurubi, na̱ aruba̱, na̱ awyatu na nꞌara mꞌba swa̱, na̱ ana a̱rici ta̱naa cita̱ga̱ mazama, na̱ ayaan wyatu hwarapi, aba shii wyan na uba̱ nde̱e̱be̱. Be̱ kuda̱gahinai wyan.
Awyatu abaa jikita̱ga̱ na aba nda̱i ana a̱rici ta̱cita̱ mazama nii cita̱ga̱ mazama, ana nꞌara mꞌba swa̱ kuda̱gagi, agurubi aba ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hani, aruba̱ aba huwa̱gi. Hyo̱ ndaaba abaa yaba Hwe̱n na Isiraaꞌila.
Yeesu pa̱ awyatu dubu na̱nshin shami
Marukusu 8:1-10
Ha̱ni ya̱nu, Yeesu be̱ nꞌgani ana jwarigi buu, be̱ hin, <<Ga̱n hange̱ ambishiri naa gudu na̱nna, ba̱re nꞌhwe̱n ndaaba nꞌtaatu aba huku na̱ ga̱mi, aba za shami na ta̱re̱. Ga̱n ribici ma cipana wyan nꞌrumunro̱n, xata jaa kinai na̱ yo̱n wana rumunro̱n.>>
Ana jwarigi buu, aba hin, <<Pina na̱ aga yana, pee ga̱tu nii díbe̱ shami na nii jwasu bigudu na̱nna?>>
Yeesu be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, << Mꞌburoodi hamba ga̱hin mꞌbaa?>>
Aba hin buu, <<Nꞌta̱nda̱ra̱ na̱ nꞌjooshiipa na njeke ge̱.>>
Yeesu be̱ shaani awyatu xahunraana na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n.
Be̱ sha̱pi mꞌba mꞌburoodi ta̱nda̱ra̱, na̱ mꞌba nꞌjooshiipa. Na be̱ hwii Hwe̱n ta̱gooda̱, be̱ ya̱biza̱gi muu, be̱ pa̱ni ana jwarigi buu, ana jwarigi buu aba pa̱ga̱ni wyatu.
