Koo buya̱ bwa re̱, bwa cigi. Ana jwarigi buu aba wuna̱ni shami na bwe̱ nꞌtumunsun nꞌta̱nda̱ra̱ na nꞌo̱to̱.
Hwarapi na wyatu ana tare̱ shami, awyatu wya̱ri na nda adubu na̱nshin, aba na shiici aꞌa̱ na̱ mꞌmwaan.
Ha̱ni na be̱ cipani bigudu naa awyatu, sa̱i be̱ ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni na̱ ana jwarigi buu zhagu bibiin binaa Magadan.

Wyanzun na iri na ta̱jikita̱na̱
Marukusu 8:11-13; Luka 12:54-56
Afaraasiya na̱ Asaduukiya aba jaa paa Yeesu wana xama̱a̱nwya̱ni buu, aba ro̱pe̱ buu ta̱hyan xbibisa̱a̱ wyan iri na ta̱jikita̱na̱ na hyan ayansun ta̱hyan Hwe̱n ne̱e̱ nii be̱.
Be̱ ra̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Kushurugo nje̱, ga̱hin nda̱i ta̱ra ta̱she̱e̱n, ihin, <Na̱ bunwan ashira̱ ja̱a̱cii kina.>
Ga̱hin ta gura̱a̱ hyan na̱ bunwan maza, ga̱hin nda̱i ta̱ra ta̱she̱e̱n, ta̱ba ne̱e̱ go̱no̱o̱, ihin, <Ba̱re ashira̱ ja̱a̱ kina.> Inii ara ta̱ꞌinsan haruwa na ta̱ra ta̱ba ne̱e̱, ga̱hin jaa ara ta̱ꞌinsan ri na nii nda nii ke̱nye̱n yana.
Awyatu na we̱ ana ga̱a̱ Hwe̱n anaa ke̱nye̱n yana aribi ta̱ndaya ri na ta̱jikita̱na̱! Ama uza na ga̱n nii bisa̱a̱ wyan, kuna bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Yunuusa.>> Be̱ ga̱a̱ wyan, be̱ huri.
Afaraasiya na̱ Asaduukiya shi ayisiti
Marukusu 8:14-21
Na aba ka̱ciga̱ni hira̱ree na Rwaga na O̱to̱ na Gaalili, ana jwarigi buu aba e̱nshe̱n ta̱hyan asha̱pici buroodi.
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Iya ma shukuu, imahooshi na̱ yisiti na Afaraasiya na̱ na Asaduukiya.>>
Kaba kaba abaa mahyaan, <<Bihin kunnu wana ta̱manpa̱ci buroodi ta.>>
Na Yeesu be̱ nda̱i kunnu, be̱ hin, <<Ga̱hin awyatu na pa̱ni nꞌgata ge̱ ku-Hwe̱n, iba̱ shani ga̱hin hyaan imapa̱ci buroodi ta?
Hara̱ niina ita e̱nshe̱nshe̱n? Iri ha̱a̱sa̱ni ma nii ke̱nye̱n naa ga̱n ta pa awyatu adubu ta na̱ mꞌburoodi nꞌta? Nꞌtumunsun nꞌhamba ga̱hin tawuna̱na̱?
Koo na ga̱n ta pa awyatu adubu na̱nshin na̱ mꞌburoodi nꞌta̱nda̱ra̱? Nꞌtumunsun nꞌhamba ga̱hin tawuna̱na̱?
Wana ba̱ ga̱hin a̱rici ta̱ꞌinsan, shii mꞌburoodi nꞌnu ga̱n nda mazama mandaabwa? Ga̱n hin, imahooshi na̱ yisiti na Afaraasiya na̱ na Asaduukiya.>>
Naazhin ana jwarigi buu aba e̱nshe̱n shici yisiti na aba ta zoona̱ na̱ mꞌburoodi nu be̱e̱ nda mazama mandaaba, ama bine̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ zumaancin nata̱ Afaraasiya na̱ nata̱ Asaduukiya.
Biituru cici Yeesu shi Ala̱masiihu
Marukusu 8:27-30; Luka 9:18-21
Ha̱ni na Yeesu be̱ wuce ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Kaisariya Filibi, be̱ ha̱nta̱ni ana jwarigi buu, be̱ hin, <<Iyaa ta awyatu aba ta hyan Buyoo Butu shi?>>
Aba hin, <<Awyatu ka̱ nii hyaan Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma, aka̱ aba nii hyaan Iliya, ayaan aba nii hyaan Iriminyan, aka̱ aba nii gura̱a̱ hyaan gaa taa shi buyaan kuuka̱ kacita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama.>>
Be̱ gura̱a̱ hantana wyan, <<Ga̱hin paan, iyaa ta ga̱hin hyaan nꞌshi?>>
Sa̱i Siima Biituru bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Gaa taa shi Ala̱masiihu, Buyoo Hwe̱n na ne̱e̱ buwuma.>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Siima buyoo Yunuusa, gaa bunaa Hwe̱n bwa ndaaki rubara̱ka ta gaa shi! Shici butu wuma ta buu bishi na̱nna ri, ama Ada nimi na ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ taa bishi.
Ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ gaa, gaa taa shi Biituru (ane̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan utari) una ga̱n nii ciba̱ awyatu na pa̱ni nꞌgata na̱ ga̱n, ana ikai na ta̱ꞌwa̱ ta̱ba jaa ha̱mba̱ga̱.
Ga̱n na̱maa pana ta̱kai nata̱ ta̱gwama nata̱ awyatu na pa̱ni gata ku-Hwe̱n. Hyo̱ ri na gaa ka̱da̱gi pina na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n, inii sha ina ka̱da̱gi nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, hyo̱ ri na gaa rigijigi pina na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n, inii sha ina rigijigi nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.>>
Yeesu be̱ kooci ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ana jwarigi buu ta̱hyan xata bisa̱ ayaan ta̱hyan be̱ taa shi Ala̱masiihu.
Yeesu cici haruwa na be̱e̱ ꞌwa̱
Marukusu 8:31--9:1; Luka 9:22-27
Ta na̱ ha̱ni ya̱nu, Yeesu be̱e̱ bisa̱ga̱ ana jwarigi buu ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ bija̱a̱ Hurushaliima, biswa̱ ta̱guma goo goo kawyatu o̱to̱ ndaaba, kawyatu o̱to̱ na apirisiti, na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami nꞌgira̱nshin, agura̱a̱ kuna buu, na̱ hwe̱n na hin taatu bihiiki kuꞌuya̱.
Nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu, Biituru bwa ra̱ga̱ni buu biyaan bibiin goo, bwa hin buu hana, ma hyaan, <<Butu O̱to̱, majaa nda! xUhwe̱n ta shaana manje̱ kunnu na̱ gaa.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ke̱ce̱e̱ke̱, be̱ hin Biituru, <<Mahooshi na̱ ga̱mi, gaa Bupira̱! Bu-shi ri na kina wa̱ka̱mi, bi-nii ga̱gaaga kina shi na butu wuma, shii na Hwe̱n.>>
Ha̱ni ya̱nu, Yeesu be̱ hin ana jwarigi buu, <<Koo buya̱ naa nꞌribi ta̱ꞌnꞌjwara̱ga xbuga̱a̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa busha̱pi guguji ndaabwa na ta̱ꞌwa̱, buꞌnꞌjwara̱ga.
Bunaa ribi ta̱wungumana hyuhyu ndaabwa, buja̱a̱ci da̱ba wuun. Bunaa ga̱a̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa na̱ wana nimi, buja̱a̱ da̱ba wuun.
Uya̱ funa̱ ta butu bwaa da̱ba, bwa de̱be̱ hyo̱ ri na sa̱ra̱ri yana? Koo iba̱ butu bwaa ara ta̱pana Hwe̱n wana hyan xbude̱be̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa?
Buyoo Butu ja̱a̱ jaa na̱ atuma ndaabwa na̱ nꞌta̱ shapaciga nata̱ Ashin, ha̱ni ya̱nu ta bwa ja̱a̱ ndupa koo buya̱ funa̱ na tuma ndaabwa.
Mahanda ga̱n maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, aka̱ ne̱e̱ na isagi pina, ana jaa ꞌwa̱ga̱ sa̱i kanda̱i kushiikwa naa Yoo Butu nꞌta̱gwama ta̱ndaabwa.>>

Yeesu he̱re̱ge̱ mꞌpirwa
Marukusu 9:2-13; Luka 9:28-36
Na nꞌhwe̱n cininhin mꞌba huri, Yeesu be̱ sha̱pi Biituru na̱ Yaakubu na̱ Yoohana, buya̱na̱ naa Yaakubu, be̱ ꞌye̱e̱ wyan paaku yaan undu na za̱ka̱ri aba ne̱e̱ kaun baa ka̱.
Be̱ he̱re̱ge̱ mꞌpirwa na̱ aꞌuba̱ ndaaba. Aꞌwana nde̱e̱be̱ na be̱ taani aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱ tande̱ paawu haku hwe̱n.
Bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Muusa, na̱ bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Iliya aba manra̱ncinye̱n buza̱a̱ waaba ma nda mazama na̱ Yeesu.
Sa̱i Biituru bwa hin Yeesu, <<Butu O̱to̱, uhuri gama na ga̱tu ne̱e̱ pina. Kuu-ribi ga̱n nii ta nꞌdura̱ nꞌtaatu, bika̱ bindaabi, bika̱ binaa Muusa, bika̱ binaa Iliya.>>
Biituru manda mazama, kuyaan rara na tande̱ bwa guna̱ni wyan, aba gura̱a̱ ha̱nga mazama na̱ ame̱ na rara mꞌba hin, <<Buna̱nna taa shi Baa buniimi, bunaa ga̱n hura̱gi ta̱ruba̱, ga̱n mashiragi na̱a̱ bwa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱. Shiraga ma be̱.>>
Ana jwarigi buu na aba hange̱ kunnu, aba hange̱ rukwanyan ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ hara̱ aba kinai na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ja̱a̱, be̱ a̱nta̱a̱ni wyan ma hyaan, <<Hiika̱ka̱ ma. Ta-ha̱nga ma rukwanyan.>>
Na koo buya̱ bwa ka̱cihini hyuhyu, aba nda̱ci koo butu ki-Yeesu be̱e̱ ka̱.
Na abaa cíin undu, Yeesu be̱ kooci wyan, be̱ hin, <<Ta-bisa̱ ma koo butu iri na ga̱hin nda̱i, kuhwe̱n na Buyoo Butu bwa hiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱.>>
Ana jwarigi buu aba ha̱nta̱ni buu, <<Too, wana ba̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami nꞌgira̱nshin mꞌba ta hyan, ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Iliya bwa taa nii gira ta̱jaa?>>
Be̱ ra̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Mahanda manu, Iliya taa nii jaa, biꞌa̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni iri hyo̱.
Ama ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma Iliya hoo jaa aba e̱nshe̱nshe̱n buu, aba ndaaki buu ri na zumaancin na ba ribi. Kunta taa Buyoo Butu bwa ja̱a̱ swa ngwan na̱ nꞌara ndaaba.>>
Sa̱i ana jwarigi buu aba e̱nshe̱n ta̱hyan mazama nama Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma manu be̱e̱ nda.
Yeesu kuda̱gahini be̱e̱ binaa mꞌbaa butu naa hira̱
Marukusu 9:14-29; Luka 9:37-43
Na aba wuce paaki gudu naa awyatu, kuuyaan butu bwa jaa paa Yeesu, bwa she̱nshe̱n na̱ aꞌuba̱ nde̱e̱be̱, bwa hin,
<<Butu O̱to̱, ha̱nga ambishiri na be̱e̱ bina̱nna niimi, binii swa ngwan na̱ nꞌsuguma nasu nꞌrabi, mahwarapi be̱ kinai na̱ ame̱ na ra na̱ ame̱ na ma̱ni.
Ga̱n ꞌye̱e̱ buu paaka anaa jwarigi ama aba a̱rici buu ta̱kuda̱gahina.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Ga̱hin awyatu na ha̱ni yana iza nꞌgata ta̱pana, iꞌmꞌbaa suhari nasu we̱. Ya̱ ha̱ni ga̱n naa na̱ ga̱hin ga̱n jaa rukuta̱? ꞌWaan ma be̱ be̱e̱ paan.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ yinzha̱nkani butu naa hira̱, bwa mahooshi na̱ be̱e̱. Ha̱ni ya̱nu be̱e̱ bibe̱ kwade̱ge̱.
Ana jwarigi buu aba ha̱nta̱ni Yeesu ta̱swee, aba hin buu, <<Na̱ wana ba̱ ga̱tu ta a̱rici butu naa hira̱ ta̱pa sumo̱?>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Wana ipa̱ni nꞌgata kuge̱. Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, kiigata niinhin ta̱pana ta̱ne̱e̱ koo ge̱ hakii kaasu naa masa̱ta inii ara ta̱hyan uꞌundu na̱nna, <Hiika̱ pina, u-huri pa̱ree> uhiiki. Iri za na na̱maa ngazana ma.
Iri haki na̱nna a̱cii bana sa̱i kuna̱ ro̱pe̱ na̱ nꞌruꞌure̱.>>+ :21 Ta̱yaan ta̱taga ta̱ka̱ nata̱ yigo ta̱za aaya na̱nna.Yeesu gura̱a̱ cita̱ haruwa na be̱e̱ ꞌwa̱
Marukusu 9:30-32; Luka 9:43-45
Na ana jwarigi buu aba mawuna̱ni na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Gaalili, Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Anii pana Buyoo Butu kuꞌnꞌara nꞌna̱ nꞌwyatu ana ribici be̱.
Aba nii kuna be̱. Hwe̱n na hin taatu bihiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱.>> Sa̱i ana jwarigi buu aba makaki ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Ta̱pana ga̱ndu na Ina na Hwe̱n
Na Yeesu na̱ ana jwarigi buu aba wuci ce̱pe̱ na Kapanahu, awyatu na ta naa raaga ga̱ndu wana Ina na Hwe̱n aba jaa, aba hin Biituru, <<Biwya̱ra̱mii niinhin a̱cii pana ga̱ndu na Ina na Hwe̱n ke̱e̱n?>>
Bwa hin, <<Bita pana.>>
Na Biituru bwa kúshiike̱ ina, Yeesu be̱ re̱ge̱ bwa ta̱bisa̱ mazama, be̱ hin, <<Biituru, imbata gaa nda̱i nꞌta̱hantana ta̱na̱nna? Paa abwaa nꞌgwama mꞌba ta naa raaga ga̱ndu? Paaku mꞌmwaan ndaaba, koo paaka yaan wyatu?>>
Na Biituru bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Paaka yaan,>> sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Suta̱hyan, mꞌmwaan ndaaba nꞌa̱cii naa pagana.
Wana xawyatu ta gura me̱ na̱ wana nda̱tu, jaga dabu, jwabana kurigiya na̱ ma̱ni, u-gunii nu naa jooshiipa naa yigo naa gaa kota̱ni, bi-nii ndaya uꞌazurufa una nii jwasu, ja̱a̱ u-pa̱ni ga̱ndu ndaa na̱ nimi.>>

Iyaa ta nii sha o̱to̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱
Marukusu 9:33-37; Luka 9:46-48
Nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu, ana jwarigi aba jaa paa Yeesu, aba ha̱nta̱ni buu, aba hin, <<Iyaa ta nii hura̱ga̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ hyo̱ nꞌta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱?>>
Sa̱i be̱ nꞌgani biyaan be̱e̱ binaa njeke, be̱ isaa buu na̱ wyantancin ndaaba,
be̱ hin, <<Mahanda ga̱n maa bisa̱ga̱ ma kiihe̱re̱ge̱ce̱, ga̱hin shi haku mꞌmwaan nꞌnjeke, ijaa ta̱na̱ ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ mahwa.
Hyo̱ bunaa mahusani bwa ne̱e̱ hakii bibe̱e̱ bina̱nna naa njeke, bwa taa shii naa hura̱gi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ nꞌta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
<<Hyo̱ bunaa ra̱a̱ be̱e̱ binaa njeke hakii na̱nna nꞌara ree na̱ wana ga̱mi, ga̱n ta bwa nꞌra̱a̱.
Iri na ta shana dukuta
Marukusu 9:42-48; Luka 17:1-2
<<Inii sha ri na ambishiri bunaa shaani buka̱ kuꞌmꞌmwaan na̱nna na mꞌpa̱ni nꞌgata wa̱ka̱mi nꞌnje̱ pinsan. Huri gama aka̱da̱gi be̱ hyoo na nama na o̱to̱ na̱ ruru, amunsani be̱ kurwaga na iri.
Sa̱ra̱ri yana ja̱a̱ swa ta̱guma wana ishaani wyatu dukuta! Ga̱ga̱ga̱ iri na ta shaana wyatu dukuta wuce, ama bunaa shaani wuun ja̱a̱ swa ta̱guma ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Kushi ara koo buna ndaa taa shaana dukuta, ꞌyapa wuun u-mo̱nshe̱n. Uhuri gama u-ta̱ni paaku bina̱ na mahwa kuna̱ ara ka̱ koo buna ka̱, na hyan aamunsani na̱ ra na za ta̱kuna na̱ nꞌara nꞌreeko koo mꞌbuna nꞌreeko.
Kushi yishe ndaa ta taa shaana dukuta, cwakara̱ka wuun, u-mo̱nshe̱n. Uhuri gama u-ta̱ni paaku bina̱ na mahwa kuna̱ yishe ka̱, na hyan aamunsani na̱ ra na za ta̱kuna na̱ ayishe reeko.
Ta̱kun nata̱ bika̱ra̱bi naa fogi
Luka 15:3-7
<<Yansun ma, ta-husana ma koo bika̱ kuꞌmꞌmwaan na̱nna na nꞌnjeke. Ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, atuma na Hwe̱n ndaaba nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ anaawan koya̱ ha̱ni na̱ Ada nimi nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱. + :10 Ta̱taga ta̱ka̱ ta̱duwa̱ni aaya na̱nna: Na̱ wana ga̱n Buyoo Butu nꞌjaa ma wyanzan ana fogi hakuu na̱nna xma biha̱na̱ wyan.<<Iba̱ ga̱hin nda̱i? Kubutu naa ta ha̱mba bikico̱ mꞌbaa ka̱ra̱bi biyina̱ ka̱, bika̱ be̱ fogi, bujaa gaa nuu kuje tundushi na̱ tundushi na̱ nꞌundu ma re̱ ta̱re̱e̱, buja̱a̱ wyanzun naa ka̱ naa fogi?
Mahanda ga̱n maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, kuundái buu, bunii hura̱ ta̱ha̱nga gama nii ka̱ yata na̱ kuje tundushi na̱ tundushi ina tafogici.
Kunta ta, Shiinhin nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ buribici koo bika̱ kuꞌmꞌmwaan na̱nna na nꞌnjeke, bifogi.
Ayami nje̱ pinsan
<<Kayamii ndaaki pinsan,+ :15 Ta̱taga ta̱ka̱ ta̱hin: Kayami nje̱ pinsanjaga u-bishi wyan pinsan na abaa ndaaki, gaa na̱a̱ bwa huwa̱. Kaashiragi, bi-kúshihine̱ ta yami.
Ama kubuushiragici, gura̱a̱ jaga waabwa, gaa na̱a̱ yaan koo ayaan reeko, wana ata nda sheeda na mazama kaꞌawyatu reeko koo ataatu.
Kaba yami shiragici wyan, u-bishi awyatu na pa̱ni nꞌgata. Kaba yami gura̱a̱ci shiraga wyan, sa̱i u-sha̱pi be̱ haku butu naa yancin Hwe̱n, koo butu naa ga̱a̱ ta̱pana pinsan baa.
<<Mahanda ga̱n maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, hyo̱ ri na ga̱hin ka̱da̱gi pina na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n, inii sha ina ka̱da̱gi nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱. Hyo̱ ri na ga̱hin rigijigi pina na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n, inii sha ina rigijigi nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
<<Mahanda ga̱n nii gura̱a̱ maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, paaka wyatu reeko haku ga̱hin pina na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n, aba shii mazama maka̱ na ta̱rupa yaanyini, Ada nimi na ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ na̱maa ndaaka ma wuun.
Na ta̱hyan, hyo̱ paa wyatu reeko koo taatu aba mawuna̱ni wana ga̱mi, nꞌne̱e̱ huku na̱ aba.>>
Ta̱kun nata̱ butu naa za mbishiri
Aba na̱ kunnu, sa̱i Biituru bwa jaa, bwa hin Yeesu, <<Butu O̱to̱, kuuya̱tu na̱ma nꞌndaakaka pinsan, mahamba ga̱n jaa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ bwa nii gata niimi? Hara̱ mata̱nda̱ra̱?>>
Yeesu be̱ hin be̱, <<Shii mata̱nda̱ra̱, ama mata̱nda̱ra̱ kuje ta̱nda̱ra̱.+ :22 Koo kuje ta̱nda̱ra̱ mata̱nda̱ra̱,uza haru nu.<<Wana kunnu, anii hyan ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱shi haku yaan bugwama naa ribi ta̱raaga wyaan na agyama ndaabwa aba ha̱mba̱a̱gi.
Naa bwaa gwama bwa pa̱shi ta̱raaga, sa̱i aba iyaagi bwa buyaan butu naa bwa jwarigi wyaan na azurufa na bwa butu bwa jaa ara ta̱ndupa mahwa.
Na bwa a̱rici ta̱ndupa, sa̱i bugwama bwa shaani xasa̱a̱nha̱ni be̱ na̱ aꞌa̱yo na̱ mꞌmwaan ndaabwa na̱ hyo̱ iri na bwa mꞌbaa wana ando̱pe̱ aba wyaan.
<<Bwaa gyama bwa she̱nshe̱n na uba̱ naa gwama ma rupa bwa ma hyaan, <Nꞌre̱e̱gi kuri, nꞌna̱maa ndupa wuun hyo̱.>
Sa̱i bubwaa gwama bwa hange̱ mbishiri naa bwaa gyama, bwa ta̱zhiga̱ni be̱, bwa ga̱a̱gi be̱ bwa wyaan.
<<Ama bwaa gyama nꞌta̱naa bana, sa̱i bwa wuta̱ni butu naa bwaa nda tuma da̱nda̱, bunaa bwa jwarigi wyaan na azurufa na wucici ndaabwa o̱to̱. Bwa kota̱ni be̱ ruru ma hyaan, <Mꞌpa̱ni ri na ga̱mii jwarigi.>
<<Bushikaa ndaabwa kutuma bwa she̱nshe̱n, bwa ro̱pe̱ bwa, bwa hin, <Nꞌre̱e̱gi kuri, nꞌnii ndupa.>
<<Bwaa gyama bwa ga̱a̱, bwa shaani aba zwa̱ga̱ni be̱ na̱ zhaaro, sa̱i kuukwane̱ bwa wyaan hyo̱.
Na ta̱shika ta̱ndaaba kutuma aba hange̱ ri na nje̱, nꞌgata mꞌba pa̱ncin wyan mahwa. Aba hiiki, aba ja̱a̱, aba bishi bwaa gwama hyo̱ ri na nje̱.
<<Bubwaa gwama bwa nꞌgani bwaa gyama, bwa hin be̱, <Gaa bugyama naa we̱ ta gaa shi. Iiga̱a̱gi hyo̱ bwa wyaan wana bi-nꞌro̱pe̱.
Ka̱i, hurici gama gaa u-hange̱ mbishiri na bushikaa naa tuma ndaa haruwa na ga̱n tahange̱ mbishiri ndaa?>
Bwaa gwama bwa gware̱ me̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, bwa pa̱ni be̱ kawyatu na ta ha̱mba zhaaro xapa̱ be̱ ngwan ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, sa̱i kuukwane̱ bwa wyaan hyo̱.
<<Kunta taa Ada nimi nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ aba ja̱a̱ ndaaka koo buya̱a̱ niinhin naa ha̱mba̱gi pinsan naa buya̱na̱ nii gata ndaabwa.>>

Ta̱tazhigana buꞌa̱
Marukusu 10:1-12
Ha̱ni na Yeesu be̱ hwii ta̱cita̱ga̱ ri ya̱nu, be̱ ga̱a̱ Gaalili, be̱ ta̱ni ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya na ne̱e̱ hira̱ree na Rwaga na Joodan.
Awyatu hwarapi aba jwarigi buu, be̱ kuda̱gahinai ana suguma kaun.
Afaraasiya aba jaa waabe̱ wana xama̱a̱nwya̱ni buu, aba hin buu, <<Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa mꞌba hin, ma shi to̱n butu ta̱zhiga̱ni aꞌa̱yo wana koya̱ ri na bwa nje̱?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Ka̱i, icita̱gici ta̱hyan, ta na Hwe̱n bwa nje̱ wyan, <Utanda wyan butu wya̱ri na̱a̱ a̱.> Bwa gura̱a̱ hyan,
<Na̱ wana kunnu, butu nii ara ta̱gaa ashin na̱ aya̱na̱, bumaꞌunpin na̱ a̱yo, aba reeko ashi ri ka̱.>
Iyeebe hina aba jaa sha aba reeko, sa̱i da̱i ashi ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ka̱. Na̱ wana kunnu, ri na Hwe̱n bwa wa̱ta̱ku, xbuyaan buta hoosa̱.>>
Sa̱i aba hin buu, <<Kushi kunnu, wana ba̱ bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Muusa bwa na sha̱a̱ ta̱hyan ga̱ga̱ga̱ apa̱ni a̱ takaada na ta̱tazhigana, agura̱a̱ cipanaa bwaa a̱?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Wana nꞌgata nꞌniinhin na nꞌwe̱ nꞌta Muusa bwa tapana nu ta̱hyan xubutu pa̱ni aꞌa̱yo takaada na ta̱kuna ta̱wya̱ri, ama na yigo una shici kunnu.
Ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, koo buya̱a̱ naa ta̱zhiga̱ni a̱yo kushici nꞌta̱hyan bunii wyanzan wyatu wya̱ri, bwa gura̱a̱ zhaa buyaan, bunii nda ta banshaun na̱a̱ bwaa a̱.>>
Ana jwarigi aba hin buu, <<Kumashi kunnu paaku a̱ na̱ butu wya̱ri, ma huri gama butu ta zhaa mahwa.>>
Ama be̱ hin wyan, <<Shii koo buya̱ nii ara ta̱ shapa mazama maya̱nu sa̱i kana Hwe̱n bwa pa̱ni ta̱kai nata̱ ta̱raa muu.
Ane̱e̱ ana jaa ara ta̱ zhaa a̱ wana ama̱ncin kunta. Aba ne̱e̱ ana jaa ara ta̱zhaa a̱ wana wyatu shani wyan kunta. Aba ne̱e̱ ana zha̱a̱gici aꞌa̱ na̱ wana ta̱ruba̱ nata̱ ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱. Hyo̱ bunaa nii ara ta̱raa muu xbura̱a̱ muu.>>
Yeesu sha̱a̱gi mꞌmwaan nꞌnjeke rubara̱ka
Marukusu 10:13-16; Luka 18:15-17
Ha̱ni ya̱nu, aba iyaagagi buu mꞌmwaan nꞌnjeke wana xbica̱guda̱a̱ga̱gi muu nꞌara, bindaaki muu ro̱pe̱, ama ana jwarigi buu abaa hyaan wyan hana.
Ama Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Hakata ma mꞌmwaan nꞌjaa wa̱ka̱mi, ta-yansan ma muu, na̱ wana ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱shi nata̱ ana ne̱e̱ haku mꞌmwaan na̱nna.>>
Na be̱ ca̱guda̱a̱ga̱gi muu nꞌara na nꞌrubara̱ka, be̱ huri.
Butu naa mꞌbaa ri ma̱
Marukusu 10:17-31; Luka 18:18-30
Aba na̱ kunnu, kuyaan butu naa mꞌbaa ri ma̱ bwa wuce paa Yeesu, bwa hin, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, ya̱ ri na bina̱ na shi na ga̱n nda na hyan ma da̱ba bina̱ na mahwa?>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin be̱, <<Wana ba̱ gaa nꞌha̱nta̱ni ina bina̱? Hwe̱n ta shi bunaa bina̱ bwaa ka̱. Kuu-ribi ta̱da̱ba bina̱ na mahwa, sa̱i u-jwara̱ga Nꞌgira̱nshin.>>
Sa̱i bwa hin Yeesu, <<Nꞌya̱ nꞌgira̱nshin?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Ta-kuna butu. Ta-nda banshaun. Ta-nda zumba̱. Ta-hyan ri na shi mahanda shi ta̱be̱.
Cina̱na̱ abaaba ndaa na̱ ada̱a̱da̱ ndaa. U-ribi butu naa nꞌharu ndaabi haruwa na gaa ribi hyuhyu ndaa.>>
Sa̱i bwa butu bwa hin, <<Nꞌhoo jwara̱ga hyo̱ iri ya̱nu, iba̱ mꞌbwa̱ta̱ni?>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin be̱, <<Kuu-ribi sha naa ta̱hiku, jaga, sáanhinai hyo̱ ri na gaa mꞌbaa, u-pa̱ga̱ni aꞌwa̱ta̱gi aba yuwa, bi-nii masha̱a̱ga̱ iri ma̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱. Naazhin u-jaa u-nꞌjwara̱ga.>>
Na bwa baa bubwa hange̱ kunnu, bwa huri na̱ ame̱ ta̱ gura, wana buꞌmꞌbaa ri ma̱.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin ana jwarigi buu, <<Mahanda ga̱n maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, ma jaa da̱a̱ra̱ ana mꞌbaa ri ma̱ ata̱ni ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
Ga̱n nii gura̱a̱ maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, manii hura̱ ta̱yoo uraakumi uta̱ni na̱ riyishe na zhimbira, na hyan butu naa mꞌbaa iri ma̱ buta̱ni kuta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.>>
Na ana jwarigi buu aba hange̱ kunnu, aba nje̱ kuma̱, aba hin, <<Kushi kunnu, iyaa nu nii bina̱na̱?>>
Ama Yeesu be̱ gwatani wyan, be̱ hin, <<Iri na nga̱za̱ni butu wuma, a̱cii ngazana Hwe̱n ta̱nda.>>
Sa̱i Biituru bwa hin, <<Ga̱tu na ga̱tu hoo gáa hyo̱ iri nda̱tu ga̱tuu jwarigi. Kushi kunnu, iba̱ ga̱tuu da̱ba?>>
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Mahanda ga̱n maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, ha̱ni na wuci naa Yoo Butu bwa ja̱a̱ hunrana nii zhe̱nke̱n naa ta̱gwama ta̱ndaabwa, ga̱hin na nꞌjwarigi ta ja̱a̱ hunrana paaku nꞌzhe̱nke̱n nꞌupwa na̱ nꞌree na nꞌta̱gwama, inaa ndaaka nꞌkorogo nꞌupwa na̱ nꞌreeko na n-Isiraaꞌila suuga̱.
Hyo̱ ana gáa nꞌina, koo aya̱na̱ba na wya̱ri koo na a̱, koo ashoo koo aya̱ndoo koo mꞌmwaan, koo nꞌcima, wana niimi, anii da̱ba na huri yata na aba gaa biyina̱ ka̱, agura̱a̱ hya̱su bina̱ na mahwa.
Awyatu hwarapi ana ta sha wyatu o̱to̱ na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana, aja̱a̱ sha ana njeke kuꞌaꞌuba̱ na Hwe̱n. Ana njeke na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana aba ja̱a̱ sha awyatu o̱to̱ kuꞌaꞌuba̱ na Hwe̱n.>>

Awyatu na tuma na̱ cima na iinabi
<<Ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱shi hakuu yaan buhwaanyan naa báni na̱ bunwan maza, bwaa wyanzan awyatu na nii ndaaka bwa tuma na̱ cima ndaabwa na ꞌwe̱e̱ na iinabi.
Aba maga̱ga̱a̱gi na̱ awyatu ta̱hyan bunii pana wyan ayuwa na aba ta pana butu na̱ rwaru. Bwa ka̱ji wyan zhagu cima ndaabwa.
<<Bwa ba̱ni ha̱ni na ta̱ruma ta̱tundushi, sa̱i bwa nda̱i ayaan mahunraanyin ꞌye̱n nii biin naa kasuwa,
bwa hin wyan, <Ga̱hin taa maa jaga ma cima nimi, nꞌja̱maa pagana ma ri na nje̱ to̱n.>
Sa̱i aba huri.
<<Na bwa butu naa ina bwa gura̱a̱ bana na̱ hwe̱n da̱, bwa gura̱a̱ bana na̱ nꞌta̱ruma ta̱taatu, bwa gura̱a̱ shapaga awyatu na tuma.
Ji kunnu, bwa gura̱a̱ bana na̱ nꞌta̱ruma ta̱ta na̱ shurugo, bwa nda̱i ayaan isagi na jaa nda koori, bwa hin wyan, <Wana ba̱ ga̱hin mahunraanyin ꞌye̱n rwaru na munrun?>
<<Aba hin bwa, <Ga̱tu de̱be̱ce̱ naa ta̱pa̱ tuma na ta̱nda.>
<<Sa̱i bwa hin wyan, <Ga̱hin taa maa jaga ma cima nimi.>
<<Na shurugo bwa nje̱, sa̱i bwa hin butu naa taguna̱ be̱ ta̱gwatana wyatu na nii hwana be̱ cima, <Nꞌgana wyatu na tuma sa̱i u-pa̱ga̱ni wyan yuwa ndaaba. Pasa kana ta̱hakana u-jaa wuci kana yigo.>
<<Ana taja̱a̱ bike̱nye̱n naa ta̱ruma ta̱ta ba jaa, koo buya̱ bwa ra̱a̱ haruwa na hyan bura̱a̱ na̱ rwaru.
Ana tare̱ge̱ ta̱jaga ba wuce aba shii ta̱hyan anii pagana wyan ana huri ndaaba, ama aba taa maa koo buya̱ bwa ra̱a̱ haruwa na hyan bura̱a̱ na̱ rwaru.
Na aba ra̱a̱gi aba ndaakaki bwa hwaanyan nꞌduunrin,
abaa hyaan, <Ana tawuce ta̱hakana, tuma naa ke̱nye̱n ka̱ aba nje̱, ta gaa pa̱ni wyan nge̱n na̱ ga̱tu, ga̱tu naa rwaa manda tuma, gaa hwe̱n na ga̱tu swa̱.>
<<Sa̱i bwa ra̱ni buka̱ ndaaba, bwa hin, <Bushikaa niimi, ga̱mii pirici ma. Ta̱tashiici ta̱hyan nꞌja̱maa ndupa haruwa na ba ta pana na̱ rwaru nuu?
Raa ri na shi ndaa u-huri. Ga̱n taꞌnꞌribi ta̱pana ana tawuce ta̱hakana nge̱n haruwa na ga̱mii pa̱ni.
Nꞌza ta̱kai nuu na hyan manda ri na ga̱n ribi na̱ ri nimi? Koo bi-ribici ayami mꞌbaa wana nꞌshii naa ndaaki hyo̱ awyatu ri na bina̱?>
<<Kunta ta ana ta sha wyatu o̱to̱ na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana, aja̱a̱ sha ana njeke kuꞌaꞌuba̱ na Hwe̱n. Ana njeke na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana aba ja̱a̱ sha awyatu o̱to̱ kuꞌaꞌuba̱ na Hwe̱n.>>
Yeesu gura̱a̱ cita̱ haruwa na be̱e̱ ꞌwa̱
Marukusu 10:32-34; Luka 18:31-34
Na Yeesu na̱ ana be̱ tazwara upwa na ree abaa katana zhagu Hurushaliima, sa̱i be̱ pe̱e̱n wyan nii biin naa yo̱n, be̱ hin,
<<Ga̱tu na ga̱tu hura̱ katanu Hurushaliima. Anii pana Buyoo Butu kapirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin. Anii ndaaka buu ta̱suuga̱ nata̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱.
Apa̱ni buu kana shici Ayaahudiya, andaaki buu umuntun na uwa̱, azware̱ buu nꞌdunduun, aka̱bi buu na̱ guguji. Ama na̱ hwe̱n na hin taatu bihiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱.>>
Ro̱pe̱ na da̱a̱da̱ na Yaakubu na̱ Yoohana
Marukusu 10:35-45
Aba na̱ kunnu, ada̱a̱da̱ na mꞌmwaan na n-Zabadi ba jaa paa Yeesu na̱ ayoo, aba she̱nshe̱n na̱ aꞌuba̱ nde̱e̱be̱, aba ha̱nta̱ni buu yaan ri.
Be̱ hin, <<Iba̱ gaa ribi?>>
Bwaa a̱ bwa hin, <<Shana mꞌmwaan na̱nna niimi nꞌree nꞌhunraana, bika̱ nꞌkataga kandaabi, bika̱ nꞌkagura̱ kandaabi paaku ta̱gwama ta̱ndaabi.>>
Ama Yeesu be̱ hin mꞌba mꞌmwaan, <<Iyancin ri na ga̱hin rupa! Inii ara ta̱swa nii koopi naa ngwan naa ga̱n swa?>>
Aba hin buu, <<Ta̱nii ara.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Kunnu inii ara ta̱swa nii koopi naa ngwan niimi, ama ta̱hunrana nꞌkataga koo kagura̱ kaniimi, shici ga̱n ta nꞌnii pana. Abaaba nimi tahoo a̱sa̱ga̱na̱ kaba pa̱ri kana ba ka̱shi.>>
Na aba upwa na bwa̱ci ba hange̱ kunnu, aba gware̱ sume̱ na̱ areeko.
Ama Yeesu be̱ nꞌgani hyo̱ ndaaba, be̱ hin, <<Iyan haruwa na nꞌgwama na nꞌana shici Ayaahudiya ba ta bisa̱a̱ ta̱kai kawyatu ndaaba, wyatu o̱to̱ ndaaba taa aba ta zhintaana wyatu ndaaba.
Ama shii kunnu mꞌba nii sha wunhin. Na hyan ma shi kunnu, hyo̱ bunaa ribi bushi butu o̱to̱ niinhin, xbushi bugyama naa aya̱na̱ba.
Bunaa ribi bushii o̱to̱, xbushi bugyama niinhin.
Kuharuwa na ga̱n Buyoo Butu nꞌjaa, shii na̱ wana hyan anaa nꞌndaaka tuma, ama wana masha bugyama, ma gura̱a̱ pana hyuhyu nimi wana xawyatu hwarapi bini.>>
Aruba̱ reeko huwa̱gi
Marukusu 10:46-52; Luka 18:35-43
Ha̱ni na Yeesu na̱ ana jwarigi buu baa bana Yeriiko, awyatu hwarapi ba jwarigi buu.
Ayaan ruba̱ reeko ba hunraani nii biin naa yo̱n. Na aba hange̱ Yeesu nu nii hura̱, aba ta̱a̱ni sunu sundaaba, ma hyaan, <<Butu O̱to̱, Buyoo Dawuda! Ha̱nga ambishiri nda̱tu!>>
Ayaan hwarapi ba yinzha̱nkani wyan, xanaa wau. Sa̱i aba duwa̱ni kusu nu ta̱taana, ma hyaan, <<Butu O̱to̱, Buyoo Dawuda! Ha̱nga ambishiri nda̱tu!>>
Yeesu be̱ e̱she̱, be̱ nꞌgani wyan, be̱ hin, <<Iba̱ ga̱hin ribi maa ndaaka ma?>>
Aba hin buu, <<Butu O̱to̱, xta̱ꞌa̱ri pa̱ri ta̱ndaya.>>
Wana ambishiri ndaaba, Yeesu be̱ a̱nta̱ni yishe ndaaba. Pita pita aba pa̱shi ta̱ndaya pa̱ri, aba jwarigi buu.

Yeesu ta̱ni Hurushaliima
Marukusu 11:15-19; Luka 19:45-48; Yoohana 2:13-22
Yeesu na̱ ana jwarigi abaa naa wuce Hurushaliima, kiyaan bicice̱pe̱ Batafaji naa ne̱e̱ na̱ Biꞌundu naa Iꞌwe̱e̱ na Zaitu. Yeesu be̱ ka̱ji areeko kuꞌana jwarigi buu,
be̱ hin wyan, <<Jaga ma bicice̱pe̱ naa ne̱e̱ iyeebe ninhin, kuta̱naa ta̱na̱, inii wuta̱na̱ uzhe̱nke̱n ufuni na̱a̱ yoo. Sa̱i irígijige, iꞌíye̱ wyan wa̱ka̱mi.
Kuuyaan buuhin ma yaanyini, ibishi be̱ ta̱hyan, <Butu O̱to̱ taa ribi wyan. Bunii kúshihine̱ wyan kunrun.> >>
Iri ya̱nu na nda wana mazama nama acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama macigi,
<<Bisa̱ ma awyatu ana ne̱e̱ na̱ Hurushaliima,
<Nde̱e̱ bugwama niinhin taa wuci wunhin.
Bumasha̱pici bushi yaanyini, buwuci da̱da̱da̱ na zhe̱nke̱n,
da̱da̱da̱ na buyoo zhe̱nke̱n ta bwa wuci.> >>
Ana jwarigi buu aba huri, aba nje̱ haruwa na Yeesu be̱ ta hin wyan xanje̱.
Aba shápi uzhe̱nke̱n na̱a̱ yoo, aba ba̱ra̱gi ada̱bi ndaaba na o̱to̱ na̱a̱ yoo zhe̱nke̱n, Yeesu be̱ ka̱ta̱ni, be̱ hura̱ni.
Awyatu hwarapi aba ba̱ra̱gi ada̱bi ndaaba na o̱to̱ na̱ yo̱n, aka̱ aba kúsagi aruun na ꞌwe̱e̱, aba ba̱ra̱gi na̱ yo̱n.
Bigudu naa wyatu ana ne̱e̱ iyeebe na̱ ana ta̱baa, abaa ta ta̱ꞌungwa, ma hyaan,
<<Hoosaana+ :9 Hoosaana Na̱ n-Ta̱ꞌibiraaniya ane̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan, ta̱biha̱na̱Aba kwashe̱he̱ne̱ wuun kala̱ma na ta̱naa yaba.kuu-Yoo Dawuda.>>
<<Rubara̱ka naru Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n ruba ne̱e̱ hiku kuunaa jaa nꞌta̱kai ta̱ndaabwa.>>
<<Hoosaana kuunaa hura̱gi hyo̱ o̱to̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.>>
Ha̱ni na Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni Hurushaliima, ce̱pe̱ hyo̱ bwa nje̱ ma̱, aba ha̱nta̱ni, <<Iyaa ta na̱nna?>>
Bigudu be̱ ra̱ni, <<Buna̱nna taa shi Yeesu, bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama naa báni Naazare na Gaalili.>>
Yeesu na̱ ame̱ na Ina na Hwe̱n
Marukusu 11:15-19; Luka 19:45-48; Yoohana 2:13-22
Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n, be̱ ga̱ci wyatu na nii saan na̱ ana nii sa̱a̱nha̱na̱a̱ ri kaun. Be̱ gura̱a̱ taacigaga ateeburu na wyatu na nii hira̱gaga yuwa na̱ nꞌzhe̱nke̱n na wyatu na nii sa̱a̱nha̱na̱a̱ nꞌhuunruun na nꞌina.
Be̱ hin wyan, << Ata̱gi na̱ takaada na Hwe̱n ta̱hyan,
<< <Anii hyan Ina nimi shi
Ina na ro̱pe̱ na wyatu hyo̱.>
Ta ga̱hin ba̱ha̱ni wuun <paaka azumba̱ aba ta masoo.> >>
Aruba̱ na̱ agurubi aba jaa waabe̱ paa be̱ ne̱e̱ na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n, be̱ kuda̱gahinai wyan hyo̱.
Ha̱ni ya̱nu, na apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa aba nda̱i ri na ta̱jikita̱na̱ na be̱ nje̱, na̱ mꞌmwaan na̱ nꞌnii taga ta̱ꞌungwa bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n wana ta̱ga̱da̱ri ma hyaan, <<Hoosaana paaku Buyoo Dawuda.>> Aba gware̱ sume̱.
Aba ha̱nta̱ni buu, aba hin, <<Bi-hange̱ ri na mꞌmwaan mꞌbaa hyaan?>>
Be̱ ra̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Ga̱n hange̱. Itacita̱gici na̱ takaada na Hwe̱n ta̱hyan,
<< <Paaku sunu nasu mꞌmwaan na̱ mꞌmwaan na nꞌaba hwii kuta̱mantaan ta
ta̱yaba ta̱ndaabi ta̱ba báni?> >>
Be̱ ga̱a̱ wyan, be̱ ba̱ni ce̱pe̱ zhagu Be̱tani, be̱ roci kaun.
Yeesu pa̱ni ꞌwe̱e̱ na waanwan nu
Na̱ bunwan maza, be̱ ma kushiika ce̱pe̱, be̱ hange̱ rumunro̱n.
Be̱ nda̱i yaan waanwan na ne̱e̱ nii biin binaa yo̱n, be̱ ja̱a̱ xbide̱be̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱ri, ama be̱ wuta̱ni kaba̱ba. Sa̱i be̱ hin wuun, <<Ta-gura̱a̱ ꞌwara ta̱ꞌwa̱ri mahwa.>> Bike̱nye̱n be̱ ta̱ci, ubwa hoogi.
Na ana jwarigi buu ba nda̱i kuꞌwe̱e̱ bwa nje̱, aba jikita̱ni. Aba hin, <<Na waanwan na̱nna bwa hoogi kunrun kunrun?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, <<Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, kubutu za maree maree bwa pa̱nii gata, bunii ara ta̱hyan undu na̱nna, <Hiika̱, u-mamunsani na̱ rwaga na o̱to̱,> Hwe̱n nii ndaaka be̱ wuun.
Kiipa̱ni nꞌgata, inii da̱ba hyo̱ ri na ga̱hin ha̱nta̱ni Hwe̱n na̱ ro̱pe̱.>>
Aha̱nta̱ni paaku ta̱kai nata̱ Yeesu ta̱ba báni
Na Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n, be̱ ma ga̱gaagana wyan, sa̱i apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na wyatu, aba jaa waabe̱. Aba hin buu, <<Nꞌta̱ya̱ ta̱kai ta̱ta gaa ndaga ri na̱nna, iyaa ta pa̱ni ta̱ba ta̱kai?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Ga̱n nꞌna̱maa hantana ma taa mayaan mazama ma ka̱. Kiiꞌnꞌra̱ni muu, ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ ma taa koo nꞌta̱kai nata̱ iyaa ta ga̱n ndaga ri na̱nna.
Ta̱kai nata̱ Yoohana bwa ta naa ndaga baba̱tiisa̱ma ta̱shi nata̱ ba̱ni pee? Paaku Hwe̱n koo paaku butu wuma?>>
Abaa maga̱ga̱a̱gi kaba kaba, <<Kuta̱hin, <Ta̱báni paa ku-Hwe̱n,> binii ta̱hyan, <Iba̱ shani ga̱hin pa̱ncin gata na̱a̱ bwa?>
Ama kuta̱hin, <Ta̱báni kubutu wuma,> ta̱hange̱ rukwanyan ri na wyatu baa ta̱ndaaka, wana ahoo shapa Yoohana bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ta bwa shi.>>
Sa̱i aba ra̱ni buu, aba hin, <<Ga̱tu yancin.>>
Sa̱i be̱ hin wyan, <<Ga̱n taa maa ga̱n jamaa bisa̱ ma koo nꞌta̱kai nata̱ iyaa ga̱n ndaga ri na̱nna.
Ta̱kun nata̱ mꞌmwaan nꞌwya̱ri nꞌree
<<Iba̱ ga̱hin nda̱i? Buyaan butu ne̱e̱ bwa mꞌbaa mꞌmwaan ree na nꞌwya̱ri. Bwa ja̱a̱ paakii naa yigo, bwa hin buu, <Baa buniimi, ba̱re ipa̱ cima na iinabi.>
<<Bwa baa bubwa hin, <Ga̱n jaa ipa̱,> sa̱i bike̱nye̱n ge̱, bwa he̱re̱ge̱ gata, bwa ipi.
<<Sa̱i abaaba ndaaba aba ja̱a̱ paaku naa hin reenu, aba bishi be̱ kuharuwa na aba ta bishi naa yigo. Bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <Ga̱n nii ipa̱, Baaba,> Ama bwa ipici.
<<Aba reeko ya̱nu iyaa ta nje̱ ri na abaaba ndaaba ba ribi?>>
Sa̱i aba hin, <<Bunaa yigo.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Mahanda ga̱n maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, wyatu na ta naa raaga ga̱ndu na̱ aꞌa̱ na uwa̱ ana̱maa gira ma ta̱ta̱na̱ kuta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
Yoohana jaa wana xbuubisa̱a̱ ma yo̱n na ta̱to̱n, ga̱hin pa̱ncin nꞌgata kuubwa. Ama awyatu na ta naa raaga ga̱ndu na̱ aꞌa̱ na uwa̱ aba pa̱ni nꞌgata. Hyo̱ na ga̱hin nda̱i kunnu, ga̱hin pa̱ncin pinsan baa, ga̱hin ga̱a̱ ta̱pana gata na̱a̱ bwa.
Ta̱kun nata̱ ahwaanyan na we̱
<<Too, shiraga ma ta̱yaan ta̱kun. Ana nda buyaan butu bunaa na mꞌbaa cima na ꞌwe̱e̱ na iinabi, bwa riini wuun na̱ nꞌta̱ma, bwa nje̱ paaku ta̱naa pinra̱a̱n ma̱ni nama ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ ꞌwe̱e̱ na iinabi kaun, bwa ta̱ bizhe̱nke̱n naa butu naa iyo̱. Bwa pa̱ni wuun unda kayaan hwaanyan, bwa ja̱a̱ ta̱yaan ce̱nye̱n.
Na ha̱ni na gwashi na ta̱ꞌwa̱ri bwa nje̱, bwa ka̱ji agyama ndaabwa xaja̱a̱ aráagi bwa ta̱taa ta̱ndaabwa nata̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱ri.
<<Ana taꞌunda cima, aba kota̱ga̱ni agyama, aba pa̱a̱ ka̱ dibi, aba kwane̱ ka̱, aba ta̱gi ka̱ tari.
Bwa gura̱a̱ kada ayaan gyama, ana huri na yigo. Ana taꞌunda bwa cima aba gura̱a̱ ndaaka wyan haka na yigo.
Ta̱hakana, butu naa cima bwa ka̱ji buyoo waaba, bwa shii nii gata ta̱hyan, <Kanda̱i be̱e̱ biniimi, anii cina̱na̱ be̱.>
<<Ama na ana taꞌunda cima aba nda̱i buyoo, aba mahin, <Manje̱ to̱n. Nde̱e̱ bunaa ja̱a̱ hya̱su ree ubwa cima. xTa̱kwane̱ be̱, ubwa cima shi nda̱tu!>
Aba kota̱ni be̱, aba bwe̱ be̱ na̱ ꞌyafu na ubwa cima, aba kwane̱ be̱.
<<Jaa kubutu naa cima jaa bwa wuce, na bwa ja̱a̱ nda na̱ awyatu na taꞌunda bwa cima?>>
<<Bunii kunaa wyatu ba na we̱, bupa̱ni ubwa cima unda kana nii naa pagana be̱ ꞌwaa na cima na shi ndaabwa.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Ka̱i, itacita̱gici ta̱taga nata̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n, ta̱hyan,
<< <Utari na awyatu na ta̱ma aba hwashe̱ ta̱hyan uza bina̱,
ubwa ta shi na hura̱gi hyo̱ bina̱ kuta̱ma.
Uya̱nu shi ta̱nda nata̱ Hwe̱n,
ubwa shi iri na yaburi nꞌsuyishe sunda̱a̱tu.>
<<Wana kunnu ga̱n na̱ maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, Hwe̱n nii raa ta̱gwama ta̱ndaabwa wunhin, upa̱ni ayaan na nii nda ri na bina̱.
Koo buya̱ na kinai na̱ ubwa tari bunii magumahinaa, bunaa ubwa tari bwa zhintani ubwa nii nama be̱ munta̱ ye̱ge̱ye̱ge̱.>>
Na apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ Afaraasiya aba hange̱ ta̱ya̱nu ta̱kun nata̱ be̱ bishi wyan, sa̱i aba shii ta̱hyan na̱ aba nu be̱e̱ nda.
Abaa wyanzan haruwa na hyan xakota̱ni buu, ama aba hange̱ rukwanyan naru bigudu naa awyatu, wana awyatu sha̱pi buu ta̱hyan bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ta be̱ shi.

Ta̱kun nata̱ buki na ta̱wya̱ri
Luka 14:15-24
Yeesu be̱ gura̱a̱ bisa̱ga̱ wyan ta̱yaan ta̱kun, be̱ hin,
<<Anii kuta̱a̱ ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ hakuu yaan bugwama naa ribi ta̱ndaaka buyoo buki na ta̱wya̱ri.
Bwa ka̱ji agyama ndaabwa xaꞌnꞌgani awyatu ana aba tabísa̱gi buki bwa, ama ana aba tabísa̱gi aba ga̱a̱ ta̱jábagi.
<<Bwa gura̱a̱ kada ayaan gyama, bwa hin, <Bisa̱gi ma awyatu na aba tabísa̱gi ta̱hyan, <<Ga̱n na ga̱n hoo huwa̱ shiri, ahoo shinraan inaa ina byabu na̱ iyo wana bwa buki. Ahoo sha̱a̱ hyo̱ ri. Jaa ma bwa buki ka̱i.>> >
<<Ama aba ta̱ci mꞌba mazama unfuun. Aba huri ri ndaaba. Buka̱ bwa huri cima ndaabwa, buka̱ bwa huri ciripe̱ na kasuwa.
Ana bwe̱ aba kota̱ga̱ni aba gyama, aba pa̱gi wyan dibi hara̱ aba kunai wyan.
Bugwama bwa gware̱ me̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱. Bwa ka̱ji asooja ndaabwa aba kúnai aba wyatu ana takúnai aba gyama ndaabwa, aba huunhuna̱i ce̱pe̱ ndaaba bo̱do̱.
<<Sa̱i bwa hin agyama ndaabwa, <Ahoo huwa̱ hyo̱ ri ta̱nda na bwa buki, ama ana aba tabísa̱gi aba magiici na̱ bwa buki.
Wana kunnu, jaga ma yo̱n yo̱n yo̱n, ihin hyo̱ ana ga̱hin nda̱i xajábagi bwa buki.>
Aba gyama aba jwara̱gagani yo̱n yo̱n yo̱n, aba rágagani hyo̱ awyatu na aba ndái, ana bina̱ na̱ ana we̱. Hyo̱ pa̱ri kaba cigi na̱ agai.
<<Naa bwaa gwama bwa ta̱ni wana xbunda̱i agai, bwa nda̱i buyaan bunaa ta̱a̱nici ꞌwana na buki.
Bwa hin bwa butu, <Bushika niimi, na gaa ta̱ni pina na ta̱a̱nici ꞌwaa na buki?> Butu bwa za ri na bwa cici.
<<Sa̱i bugwama bwa hin ana nii ndaaka bwa tuma, <Kadaga ma bwa buna na̱ nꞌara, imunsani be̱ paaka hura̱gi ta̱yincincin paaku nꞌungwa na̱ mꞌmbwa ta̱re̱.>
<<Aꞌnꞌgani wyatu hwarapi, ama ahamba aba ka̱shi.>>
Ga̱ndu ta̱pana ku-Kaisa
Marukusu 12:13-17; Luka 20:20-26
Aba na̱ kunnu, Afaraasiya aba ja̱a̱, aba maga̱ga̱a̱gi haruwa na aba nii karaaga buu ta̱ruma ade̱be̱ azha̱a̱ buu na̱ iri na be̱ nii cita̱.
Aba káji ana jwarigi wyan huku na wyatu na bugwama Hirudu aba hin, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, ta̱yan gaa bu-shi bunaa mahanda, gaa ta naa gura̱a̱ ga̱gaagana yo̱n na Hwe̱n to̱n na̱ mꞌmahanda. Wakaa, awyatu ashi iri ka̱, gaa a̱cii bisa̱a̱ ta̱hura̱ kuuyaan.
Ta̱bishi, bi-nda̱i ta̱hyan unje̱ to̱n ta̱pa̱ni ga̱ndu paaku Kaisa Bugwama naa Rooma koo na?>>
Wana Yeesu hoo insan ta̱ribici buu nata̱ ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌgata ndaaba, be̱ hin wyan, <<Ga̱hin wyatu na za mahanda, wana ba̱ ga̱hin mꞌmaanwyana?
Mꞌbisa̱a̱ ma aba yuwa na azurufa na ga̱hin ta naa pagana ga̱ndu na̱ aba.>> Aba sháapi buu azurufa ka̱.
Be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan, <<Mꞌpirwa na̱ nꞌruzha̱a̱ naru iyaa ta runa̱nna?>>
Aba ra̱ni, aba hin, <<Na Kaisa ta.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Too, pana ma iri na shi na Kaisa ku-Kaisa, ipa̱ni iri na shi na Hwe̱n ku-Hwe̱n.>>
Na aba hange̱ kiibe̱ ra̱ni, aba nje̱ kuma̱, aba hakaci buu, aba huri.
Ta̱hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱ na̱ nꞌta̱wya̱ri
Marukusu 12:18-27; Luka 20:27-40
Na̱ bwa hwe̱n, ayaan Asaduukiya aba jaa paa Yeesu xaha̱nta̱ni mꞌba mazama. Ana ta naa hyaan ta̱hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱ ta̱za.
Aba hin, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, Muusa hin, <Kubutu ꞌwi bwa ga̱a̱ aꞌa̱yo na za mꞌmwaan, xbuya̱na̱ sha̱pi aꞌa̱yo, buma̱nta̱a̱ni bwa mꞌmwaan.>
Too, atanda ayaan wyatu nda̱tu aba ta̱nda̱ra̱. Bunaa yigo bwa zha̱a̱ buꞌa̱, bwa ꞌwi, bwa ma̱ncincin na̱a̱ bwa a̱, bwa ga̱a̱gi buya̱na̱ buꞌa̱.
Kunnu bunaa hin reenu, na̱a̱ naa hin taatu, ubwa wuci kuunaa hin ta̱nda̱ra̱.
Jaa bubwa a̱ bwa ꞌwi.
Too, hwe̱n na ta̱hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱, aꞌa̱yo iyaa bwa ja̱a̱ sha, na ta̱hyan hyo̱ ata̱nda̱ra̱ ya̱nu azha̱a̱gi bwa?>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Haruwa na ga̱hin shii nꞌgata za to̱n, na ta̱hyan iyancin ta̱taga nata̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n, ga̱hin yancin ta̱kai nata̱ Hwe̱n.
Too, kuta̱hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱, wyatu wya̱ri ja̱a̱cii zhaaga a̱, aꞌa̱ ba ja̱a̱cii giya̱ga̱ ta̱wya̱ri, aja̱a̱ naa haka tuma na Hwe̱n nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
Na̱ mꞌmazama nama ta̱hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱, icita̱gici ri na Hwe̱n bwaa bisa̱gi ma? Uta̱gi ta̱hyan,
<Ga̱n ta nꞌshi Hwe̱n na Ibiraahin, Hwe̱n na Isiyaaku, Hwe̱n na Yaakubu.> Ubwa ta shi Uhwe̱n na awyatu na wuma, shici na wyatu na ꞌwa̱gi.>>
Na awyatu ba hange̱ kunnu, aba kota̱ni sunu ma jikita̱ga̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱nde̱e̱be̱.
Nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌhura̱gi hyo̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱
Marukusu 12:28-34; Luka 10:25-28
Na Afaraasiya ba hange̱ bire̱e̱hini Asaduukiya, aba mawuna̱ni.
Biyaan biwya̱ra̱mi naa yan Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa ki, be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wana xbima̱a̱nwya̱ni buu.
<<Biwya̱ra̱mi, biya̱a̱ gira̱nshin na Hwe̱n bwa tapana Muusa naa shi naa hura̱gi hyo̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱?>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, << <Ruba̱ Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n ndaa, nii gata ndaabi hyo̱, na̱ wuma ndaa hyo̱, na̱ ahari ndaa hyo̱.>
Na̱nna ta shi bigira̱nshin naa yigo naa hura̱gi hyo̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Binaa hin reenu, <Ruba̱ butu naa nꞌharu ndaabi haruwa na gaa ribi hyuhyu ndaa.>
Hyo̱ Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa na̱ atakaada na ana ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, abáni kuꞌnꞌgira̱nshin ya̱nu nꞌreeko.>>
Buyoo iyaa Ala̱masiihu be̱ shi
Marukusu 12:35-37; Luka 20:41-44
Na Afaraasiya aba mawuna̱ni, sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan, be̱ hin,
<<Mbata ga̱hin shii na̱ nꞌgata Ala̱masiihu shi? Buyoo iyaa be̱ shi?>>
Sa̱i aba hin buu, <<Buyoo Dawuda ta.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Na ta Dawuda na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱a̱ Hwaanwun na Hwe̱n be̱ tahyan buu <Butu O̱to̱>? Wana Dawuda hin,
<< <Butu O̱to̱ tahyan Butu O̱to̱ niimi,
<<Hunrana nꞌkataga kaniimi,
sa̱i kunshaani awyatu naa ribici
gaa fo̱nje̱ wyan na̱ kokobi na buna ndaa.>> >
Ku-Dawuda taꞌnꞌgana Ala̱masiihu <Butu O̱to̱>, na Ala̱masiihu be̱ shi buyoo?>>
Buza naa na ara buu ta̱rana. Ta hwe̱n ya̱nu buza na nje̱ gata xbugura̱a̱ hantana buu yaanyini.

Yeesu ba̱nra̱nyin ashe̱re̱ na nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na̱ Afaraasiya
Marukusu 12:38-39; Luka 11:43,46; 20:45-46
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin bigudu naa wyatu na̱ ana jwarigi buu,
<<Nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na̱ Afaraasiya, aba ta aba ta pana ta̱kai nata̱ xaga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni wyatu Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n bwa ta pana Muusa.
Na̱ wana kunnu, nda ma hyo̱ ri na abaa bishi ma, igura̱a̱ jwara̱ga, ama ta-nda ma haruwa na baa nda, wana ajaa nda iri na abaa ga̱gaagana ma.
Ata kadaga ꞌwaa na da̱a̱rici ta̱shapa, asha̱a̱gi wuun wyatu nii tutu, ama aba nꞌsuhyu sundaaba aba jaa guna̱ wyan ta̱ta̱ndana koo nii bwaa ka̱.
Atanaa nda ri ndaaba hyo̱ wana awyatu nda̱ya̱gi wyan, aba ta kadaaga atunu ndaaba aꞌunshin pain na mꞌbaa aꞌaaya na mazama nama Hwe̱n, aba ta sha̱a̱ga̱ nꞌhwa̱ na nꞌnge̱nshe̱n kuꞌmꞌbiin na ada̱bi ndaaba na o̱to̱. The pharisee with knot on forehead|hk00274.jpg|col|MAT 23:1-5||Bufaraasiya na̱ uꞌunshin na̱ tunu|23:5<<Ata hura̱ ta̱ruba̱ apa̱ni wyan paaka hunranhunran naka wyatu o̱to̱ paaka buki, na̱ pa̱ri paaka hura̱gi gama na hunranhunran kuꞌaka̱ta̱ku ndaaba,
aba ta ruba̱ azumanu na maca̱ma̱nta̱n na̱ kasuwa, koo buya̱ bwa ta ruba̱ anaa nꞌga bwa <Biwya̱ra̱mi.>
<<Ama ga̱hin, xataa nꞌgana ma <Biwya̱ra̱mi> wana biwya̱ra̱mi niinhin ka̱ ga̱hin mꞌbaa, hyo̱ ninhin nge̱n ga̱hin ne̱e̱ awyatu na ya̱na̱ba.
Ta-nꞌgana ma koo buya̱ butu na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana <Ada>, wana Ada ninhin aka̱ aba ne̱e̱, bwa taa shii naa ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
xAtaa nꞌgana ma <Butu o̱to̱>, wana butu o̱to̱ ka̱ ga̱hin mꞌbaa, be̱ taa shi Ala̱masiihu.
Bunaa shi butu o̱to̱ niinhin, bwa taa nii sha gyamaa niinhin.
Bunaa mapa̱ zha̱munkun, anii husana be̱, bunaa mahusani, anii pa be̱ zha̱munkun.
<<Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma, ga̱hin nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na̱ Afaraasiya, awyatu na za mahanda! Ita guna̱na̱ inco̱n na hyan awyatu ta̱nii kuta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱. Ga̱hin nꞌsuhyu suniinhin ga̱hin ta̱ncin, ga̱hin gura̱a̱ yansan ana ribi ta̱ta̱na̱ tunu.
Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma, ga̱hin nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na̱ Afaraasiya, awyatu na uwa̱! Ita re̱ ꞌwaa na aꞌa̱ na suwya̱rugooba suba ꞌwa̱gi, ga̱hin za mꞌpirwa na̱ ro̱pe̱ ngiswan kawyatu ba ne̱e̱. Wana kunnu, aja̱maa pa ma ngwan na hura̱gi mamboo.
<<Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma, ga̱hin nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na̱ Afaraasiya, wyatu na za mahanda! Ita kacigana rwaga na o̱to̱, iwuci ce̱nye̱n nata̱ me̱mi wana wyanzun na bunaa nii pana gata buka̱. Kiide̱be̱, sa̱i ishaani be̱ bushi baa bunaa paaku ra na za ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱, ma maree suga̱hin ne̱e̱.
<<Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma, ga̱hin aruba̱ na tanaa mana aya̱na̱nhin! Ga̱hin ta hyan, <Hyo̱ bunaa ta̱a̱ sa̱nsan na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n, koori za, ama hyo̱ bunaa ta̱a̱ sa̱nsan na̱ zinaari na Ina na Hwe̱n, ga̱ga̱ga̱ bunje̱ ri na shani bwa ta̱a̱ sa̱nsan.>
Ga̱hin nꞌguzha̱ni na̱ aruba̱! Ya̱ ta huri o̱to̱, zinaari koo Ina na Hwe̱n una shani zinaari bwa shi na ta̱sabu na bina̱?
Ga̱hin ta gura̱a̱ hyan, <Hyo̱ bunaa ta̱a̱ sa̱nsan nii zhe̱nke̱n naa Ina na Hwe̱n koori za, ama hyo̱ bunaa ta̱a̱sa̱nsan na̱ iri na aba íye̱ na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n, ga̱ga̱ga̱ bunje̱ ri na shani bwa ta̱a̱ sa̱nsan.>
Ga̱hin aruba̱! Ya̱ ta huri o̱to̱, iri na aba íye̱ koo bizhe̱nke̱n naa shani iri na aba íye̱ bwa shi na ta̱sabu na bina̱?
Na̱ wana kunnu, hyo̱ bunaa she̱nshe̱n nii zhe̱nke̱n naa Ina na Hwe̱n, bushe̱nshe̱n ta na̱ ri na ne̱e̱ nii be̱ ta.
Koo buya̱ naa she̱nshe̱n na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n, bushe̱nshe̱n ta na̱ bwa Hwe̱n una hunrani na̱ ame̱ ndaabwa.
Hyo̱ koo buya̱ naa she̱nshe̱n nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, bushe̱nshe̱n ta nii zhe̱nke̱n naa ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ na̱a̱ naa hunrani nii be̱e̱ zhe̱nke̱n naa ta̱gwama.
<<Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma, ga̱hin nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na̱ Afaraasiya, awyatu na za mahanda! Ita pana ta̱taa ta̱ka̱ kuta̱taa ta̱ꞌupwa nata̱ ꞌwaa na mꞌmbwaga, ama ga̱hin hakaci ri ka̱ ina hura̱gi bina̱ kuꞌnꞌgira̱nshin, be̱ ta shi, ta̱naa nda ri to̱n na̱ ambishiri, nꞌta̱ sha butu hiku. Ya̱nu ta shi na hyan iha̱mba̱ga̱ shii na hyan iga̱a̱ ika̱.
Ga̱hin aruba̱ ana ta naa mana aya̱na̱nhin, ita zaantan bikuta̱ma̱ naa njeke wana ga̱hin jaa cwara buu, ama ga̱hin ta cwara raakumi!
<<Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma, nꞌwya̱ra̱mi na nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ Muusa na̱ Afaraasiya, awyatu na za mahanda! Ita ha̱mbara abaa na nꞌjogo na̱ nꞌgwaga ki, ama iga̱a̱ ame̱ ninhin na̱ nꞌta̱shiri na̱ mꞌmaꞌwe̱n na̱ nꞌta̱maa ta̱ruba̱ hyuhyu.
Gaa buruba̱ na Bufaraasiya! Ha̱mbara kwan ame̱ na nꞌjogo na̱ nꞌgwaga naazhin abaa ndaaba naa sabu.
<<Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma, ga̱hin nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na̱ Afaraasiya, ana za mahanda! Ishi haku suꞌuya̱ nasu abaa shanaa wyan penti na tande̱, una ta zumaa ta̱ndaya na̱ sa̱ra̱ri, ama ame̱ ndaaba kuta̱shiri na̱ aꞌunfuun.
Kunta ta ga̱hin ne̱e̱, awyatu taa ndaya ma na̱ sa̱ra̱ri haka wyatu na bina̱, ama ame̱ ninhin da̱ aba cigi na̱ ri na uwa̱ na̱ mꞌmaꞌwe̱n.
<<Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma, ga̱hin nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na̱ Afaraasiya, wyatu na za mahanda! Ida̱ba̱a̱ga̱ni awyatu na ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama na yigo suꞌuya̱ sabu. Igura̱a̱ ndaaka suꞌuya̱ nasu wyatu na bina̱ ruzhanna.
Ita hyan, <xBwa shi ga̱tu na naa ha̱ni na adaadoo nda̱tu, kuta̱tanguncin wyan mahiin ta̱wyashika nama acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama.>
Ri na shani ta ga̱hin na bisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan ga̱hin taa shi mꞌmwaan na nꞌadaadoo ndaaba ba na kunaa acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama.
Wana kunu, sa̱i wanyin ta̱ciga̱hina̱ tuma na we̱ na adaadoo ninhin ba tapasa!
<<Ga̱hin suhwaa, ga̱hin bigudu suhwaa nasu we̱! Na ga̱hin nii ara igida̱ga̱ni ngwan na paaku ra na za ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱?
Na̱ wana kunnu, ga̱n na̱maa kádaagi ma acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama na̱ awyatu na mꞌbaa ta̱yansun na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin. Inii kunaa aka̱, ika̱ba̱gi aka̱ na̱ guguji, izuragi aka̱ nꞌdunduun na̱ ame̱ na aka̱ta̱ku ninhin, ijwara̱gagani wyan nꞌcice̱pe̱ nꞌcice̱pe̱ ma kaka wyan.
Ga̱n nii káji wyatu ya̱nu wana ruhaki naru mahiin nama awyatu na bina̱ hyo̱ rushi runiinhin, ta na̱ Habiila hara̱ zhagu Zakariya buyoo Bereekiya, bunaa ga̱hin na kuna wyantancin na udura̱ na bure na Ina na Hwe̱n na̱ bizhe̱nke̱n naa bikico̱ ta̱huunha̱na̱.
Mahanda ga̱n maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, iri ya̱nu nii nda hyo̱ na̱ wyatu naa ke̱nye̱n yana.
Yeesu ꞌyantani Hurushaliima
Luka 13:34-35
<<Ka̱i, awyatu na Hurushaliima! Ka̱i, awyatu na Hurushaliima! Ga̱hin naa nii kunaa ana nii cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ma gyasa tari kana Hwe̱n bwa káji wunhin! Mahwarapi ga̱n ribi ta̱a̱wuna̱a̱na̱ ma haku kuya bwa ta hyaan uwuna̱a̱ni ayoo na̱ apyami ndaabwa, ama ga̱hin ga̱a̱.
Nde̱e̱, aga̱a̱ ma pata, uce̱pe̱ ninhin ha̱nda̱!
Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, ijaa gura̱a̱ ma nꞌndaya, sa̱i kuhwe̱n na ga̱hin hin, <Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n ndaaki rubara̱ka, bunaa wuce na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ Hwe̱n.> >>

Ta̱huwa̱ nata̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana
Marukusu 13:1-2; Luka 21:5-6
Na Yeesu be̱ ba̱ni na̱ ame̱ na Ina na Hwe̱n, ma hura̱ ta̱hani, ana jwarigi buu abaa bisa̱a̱ga̱ buu ta̱ma goo goo nata̱ Ina na Hwe̱n.
Be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Inda̱i ta̱ma goo goo ta̱na̱nna? Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ ma, za tari na aba nii gaa ucagudana na̱a̱ ya̱na̱. Hyo̱ aba nii huza̱a̱ga̱ wyan.>>
Ungwan na yigo
Marukusu 13:3-13; Luka 21:7-19
Yeesu ma hunrana nii Undu naa Iꞌwe̱e̱ na Zaitu, sa̱i ana jwarigi buu aba jaa waabe̱ baa ka̱, sa̱i aba hin buu, <<Ta̱bishi, ya̱ ha̱ni nu iri ya̱nu be̱ ja̱a̱ nda? Imbata shi iri na ga̱tu ja̱a̱ ndaya ha̱ni na kushiikwa ndaa na̱ ta̱huwa̱ nata̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana?>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Sha̱a̱ ma suha̱nka̱ri suniinhin ki, xbuyaan butaa pira̱ ma.
Awyatu hwarapi ja̱a̱ jaa nꞌruzha̱a̱ runiimi, ahin, <Ga̱n ta nꞌshi Ala̱masiihu,> anii pira̱ awyatu hwarapi.
Ga̱hin nii ha̱nga anii ndaga gyasa nꞌko nꞌhwarapi, na̱ ayaan aza̱zama hwarapi ndaaba, xutaa ta maa gata buga̱, wana ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ inje̱, shii ta̱huwa̱ nata̱ bwa sa̱ra̱ri yana ta̱nu ta̱hoo wuce.
Ce̱nye̱n na̱ ce̱nye̱n ta̱ja̱a̱ naa nda gagu, ta̱gwama na̱ nꞌta̱gwama ta̱ba ja̱a̱ naa nda gyasa. Ce̱nye̱n ta̱ba ja̱a̱ zha̱a̱nta̱na̱, rumunro̱n ruba ja̱a̱ nda pa̱ri goo goo.
Ama hyo̱ ya̱nu ubwa shici kwan ubwa ngwan, ushi haku ta̱raan wunsa̱n na gaa hiin hwan cima.
<<Ha̱ni ya̱nu aba nii iya ma paaku ngwan, aakunai ma. Wyatu na sa̱ra̱ri hyo̱ ba nii gaa ma wana iꞌnꞌjwarigi.
Ha̱ni ya̱nu awyatu hwarapi aba nii ruma̱a̱ paakii gata ndaaba ta̱pana kuga̱mi, apa̱ni ayaan akunai wyan, aba jaa maꞌunso̱n.
Acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ana ta̱be̱ ba nii báni hwarapi, apiri wyatu hwarapi.
Na̱ wana maꞌwe̱n nama nii duwa̱na̱ kawyatu, ta̱maruba̱ nata̱ awyatu aba mꞌbaa ta̱rumii.
Ama bunaa e̱she̱ hiku hara̱ ubwa hwe̱n, buja̱a̱ bina̱.
Aba nii bisa̱ga̱ awyatu mazama nama zumaa nama ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ kuhyo̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana, wana hyan koo buya̱ hange̱ muu, naazhin ta̱huwa̱ nata̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana ta̱wuce.
Ngwan na zumaancin
Marukusu 13:14-23; Luka 21:20-24
<<Ija̱a̱ ndaya iri na yinzhin na we̱ na ja̱a̱ ꞌwaan ta̱huza̱a̱ga̱, hakuu cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Daaniyan bwa tacita̱, iꞌe̱she̱ kupa̱ri naka ta̱sabu. (Butu naa nii cita̱ga̱ xbuꞌe̱nshe̱n ki!)
Too, sa̱i ana ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya uja̱a̱ sha ga̱ga̱ga̱ agida̱ga̱gi paaki undu.
Bunaa zaci na̱ asa̱ku na dura̱ xbuta ciin buhin xbuta̱ni ina bushápi yaanyini na ne̱e̱ na̱ ina.
Bunaa tane̱e̱ na̱ cima xbuta hyan xbugiye bushápi zuzu ndaabwa.
Iiyirigani ma aꞌa̱ na suhuba̱ na̱ aꞌa̱ na hyaabu na̱ bwa ha̱ni ya̱nu!
Nda ma ro̱pe̱ asumo̱ ya̱nu xata wuce ha̱ni na robi koo hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ ninhin.
Na̱ ha̱ni bwa, aja̱a̱ nda ngwan na hura̱gi mamboo ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, una aba tanje̱ce̱ iri ndaabwa ta ha̱ni na aba nje̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana hara̱ niina. Aba jaa gura̱a̱ duwa̱na̱ wuun ta̱nda mahwa.
Bwa shici Hwe̱n bwa ha̱sa̱a̱ mꞌba hwe̱n o̱to̱, kuza butu wuma naa tanii bina̱. Ama wana ambishiri na ana Hwe̱n bwa takasa, sa̱i bwa ha̱sa̱a̱ ngiswan na mꞌba nꞌhwe̱n.
<<Na̱ ha̱ni bwa, koo buyaan buuhin ma, <Gwatana ma, nde̱e̱ Ala̱masiihu na paa> koo, <Nde̱e̱ beree piree!> ta-pana ma gata na̱a̱ bwa.
Na̱ ha̱ni bwa, aꞌala̱masiihu na̱ acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ana ta̱be̱ aja̱a̱ wuce, andagi iri na ta̱jikita̱na̱ na̱ iri na ta̱pa rukwanyan wana hyan anaa pira̱ ana Hwe̱n bwa takasa aba nii ara.
Too, ga̱n ta ga̱mii bishi ma kunrun.
<<Na̱ wana kunnu, koo buyaan buuhin ma, <Gwatana ma, beree na̱ aga,> ta-bana ma. Kuuyaan bugura̱ maa hyan ma, <Be̱ ree na̱ ame̱ na dura̱, be̱ masoo,> ta-pana maa gata na̱a̱ bwa.
Haruwa na ta̱manyan manyan ta̱ba ta tara̱kana hwe̱n ta̱bani zhagu hwe̱n ta̱ꞌira̱, kunta kushiikwa naa Yoo Butu bwa ja̱a̱ sha.
Paaku ruꞌwa̱ ruba ne̱e̱, kabata ada̱ma̱a̱ aba ta mawuna̱na̱.
Kushiikwa naa Yoo Butu
Marukusu 13:24-27; Luka 21:25-28
<<Na̱ nꞌta̱naa huwo nꞌhwe̱n ya̱nu na nꞌngwan,
<< <Uhwe̱n nii ta̱na̱ ta̱yincincin,
ta̱gwaan nata̱ pyanda ta̱ba jaa naa,
nꞌgwasu mꞌba ja̱a̱ kínai nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱,
iri na yaburagi ina ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ nii zha̱a̱nta̱na̱.>
<<Ha̱ni ya̱nu ta nii bisa̱a̱ Buyoo Butu da̱shi nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱. Nꞌkorogo na nꞌsa̱ra̱ri yana nꞌnii naa nꞌgaaga wana rukwanyan. Anii ndaya Buyoo Butu wuci na̱ ame̱ na arara na̱ nꞌta̱gwama na̱ nꞌta̱kai o̱to̱.
Bunii káji atuma ndaabwa ahurupa̱ni bihyo̱nhyo̱n ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, buwuna̱a̱ni ana bwa takasa kiibiin naa hwe̱n ta̱bani na̱ hwe̱n ta̱ꞌira̱ na̱ ruꞌwa na̱ zuba, Unii sha paa sa̱ra̱ri yana bwa swe̱n na̱ paaku ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱ba swe̱n.
Ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ uꞌwe̱e̱ na waanwan
Marukusu 13:28-31; Luka 21:29-33
<<Insan ma yaanyini kuꞌwe̱e̱ na waanwan. Kiinda̱i aba̱ba ndaabwa ana ange̱ nii kina ana fo aba ke̱ne̱ ta̱tansan, iyan ta̱hyan shuyo ta goki.
Kunnu mꞌba ja̱a̱ sha, ha̱ni na ga̱hin nda̱i hyo̱ iri ya̱nu na ga̱mii bisa̱gi ma inii ndaga, yansun ma bwa ha̱ni ta goki, bwa ta do̱ko̱ na̱ adubo.
Mahanda ga̱n maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, awyatu naa ke̱nye̱n yana ajaa huwa̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱, sa̱i hyo̱ kiri ya̱nu nje̱.
Ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n ta̱ja̱a̱ huwa̱ ta̱foga̱, ama mazama maniimi maza nama ja̱a̱ foga̱ mahwa.
Buza naa yan hwe̱n koo ha̱ni na kuswa na Ala̱masiihu
Marukusu 13:32-37; Luka 17:26-30-36
<<Ama buza naa yan ubwa hwe̱n koo ha̱ni na iri ya̱nu be̱e̱ nda, koo atuma na Hwe̱n ana ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, koo Buyoo, kaba Shin ta yan baa ka̱.
Haku haruwa na aba na nda bike̱nye̱n naa Nuhu, kunta mꞌba ja̱a̱ sha ha̱ni naa Yoo Butu bwa ja̱a̱ kúshiike̱.
Kunta taa, na̱ ha̱ni na uro̱be̱ bwa tawucici, awyatu baa re̱, abaa swaga, abaa zhaaga aꞌa̱, aꞌa̱ baa giya̱ga̱ ta̱wya̱ri, bwa wuci kuha̱ni na Nuhu na̱ awyatu ndaabwa aba ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni na o̱to̱.
Aba wyatu tayancin ri na hiin nda, aba nda̱i kuro̱be̱ wuce, bwa ushigi wyan hyo̱. Kunta taa kushiikwa naa Yoo Butu bwa ja̱a̱ sha.
Nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu, awyatu reeko nii naa na̱ cima, asha̱pi buka̱, aga̱a̱ buka̱.
Aꞌa̱ ree anii naa na̱ nama, asha̱pi buka̱, aga̱a̱ buka̱.
<<Wana kunu, naa ma ga̱ri, wana ijaa yansun hwe̱n na Butu O̱to̱ niinhin bwaa kúshiike̱.
Ama yansun ma, bwa xshi butu naa ina bwaa yansun ta̱hyan buzumba̱ ja̱a̱ jaa na̱ gita, bujaa taana nꞌrabi, bwa jaa gura̱a̱ hakata xbuta̱ni ina.
Na̱ wana kunnu, ga̱hin maa naa ma ga̱ri, wana ha̱ni na ga̱hin yancin ta Buyoo Butu bwa ja̱a̱ jaa.
Bugyama naa bina̱ koo bunaa za bina̱
Luka 12:41-48
<<Iyaa ta shi bugyama yata naa bina̱, bunaa maka̱ri, bunaa butu naa ina bwa hin be̱ xbugwataga ina ndaabwa, bunaa gura̱a̱ paga aya̱na̱ba gyama shami nii ke̱nye̱n to̱n?
Bugyama naa rubara̱ka ta, bunaa butu naa ina bwa wuce, bwa wuta̱na̱ bwa ma nda tuma ndaabwa.
Mahanda ga̱n maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, bunii pana be̱ xbuha̱mbana hyo̱ ꞌwaa ndaabwa.
Ama kuubwaa gyama shii naa we̱, bunii mahyan, <Butu naa ina jaa gíye na̱ ha̱ni,>
sa̱i buke̱ne̱ ta̱da̱ba̱ga̱ aya̱na̱ba gyama, ma re̱, ma swa huku na̱ asowa̱.
Kuunii nda kunnu ji, butu naa ina ja̱a̱ kúshiike̱ ha̱ni na bwa ja̱a̱cii yansun.
Butu naa ina bwa ja̱a̱ pa be̱ dibi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, bugura̱a̱ yibaku be̱ huku na̱ ana za mahanda paaku nꞌungwa na̱ mꞌmbwa ta̱re̱.>>

Ta̱kun nata̱ mꞌmwaan a̱ nꞌupwa
<<Na̱ ha̱ni ya̱nu, ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱nii sha haku nꞌyaan mꞌmwaan a̱ nꞌupwa na sha̱pi apitila ndaaba, aba gubi bunaa nii zhaa buꞌa̱.
Nꞌta mꞌba shi nꞌguzha̱ni, nꞌta mꞌba shi na mꞌmaka̱ri.
Nꞌta na nꞌshi nꞌguzha̱ni, mꞌba sha̱pi apitila ndaaba mꞌba mapa̱ci mariga̱ wana ta̱duwa̱na̱.
Nꞌna mꞌmaka̱ri mꞌba sha̱pi apitila ndaaba huku na̱ mayaan mariga̱ wana ta̱duwa̱na̱.
Bunaa nii zhaa buꞌa̱ bwa wucici na̱ ha̱ni, hyo̱ ndaaba aba hange̱ nꞌrabi, nꞌrabi mꞌba sha̱pi muu.
<<Tapata na̱ gita ꞌya̱piga̱su aba hange̱ ta̱ꞌungwa, <Bunaa nii zhaa buꞌa̱ ree. Báni ma iꞌura̱ku na̱a̱ bwa.>
<<Sa̱i mꞌba mꞌmwaan a̱ nꞌupwa mꞌba hiika̱ki nꞌrabi, mꞌbaa a̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni apitila ndaaba.
Mꞌba nꞌta na nꞌshi nꞌguzha̱ni, mꞌba hin na maka̱ri, <Ta̱pa̱gi ma ge̱e̱ge̱e̱ mariga̱ maniinhin ka̱i, apitila nda̱tu nii ꞌwa̱ga̱ga̱.>
<<Ama na mꞌbaa maka̱ri mꞌba hin muu, <Majaa nda, wana majaa ta̱jwasu ga̱hin na̱ nꞌga̱tu. Hura̱ ma ija̱a̱ paaka wyatu na nii sa̱a̱nha̱na̱a̱ imasáanwyain maniinhin.>
<<Na aba huri xamasáanwyain mandaaba, bunaa nii zhaa buꞌa̱ bwa hoo wuce. Nꞌna nꞌtanje̱ shiri mꞌba ta̱na̱a̱nwun paaku buki na ta̱wya̱ri huku, aba guna̱ni adubo.
<<Ta̱hakana na nꞌtabwe̱ mꞌba wuce, mꞌba hin, <Butu O̱to̱, Butu O̱to̱, ta̱gunii!>
Ama bunaa nii zha̱a̱ buꞌa̱ bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin muu, <Mahanda ga̱n maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, iiyancin ma.>
<<Wana kunnu sa̱i inaa ga̱ri, wana iyancin hwe̱n koo ha̱ni na kuswa nimi.>>
Ta̱ga̱gaagana wana ta̱sha butu naa munrun
Luka 19:11-27
Be̱ gura̱a̱ hyan mayaan, <<Ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱nii sha haku butu naa hiin jaga ta̱hani kayaan. Sa̱i bwa nꞌgani agyama ndaabwa, bwa pa̱ni wyan ri na bwa mꞌbaa ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱.
Bwa pa̱ni buka̱ azinaari nꞌguma nꞌta, buyaan azinaari nꞌguma nꞌree, buyaan azinaari uguma ka̱, kwayaa haruwa na kai ndaabwa. Sa̱i bwa huri ta̱hani ta̱ndaabwa.
Bunaa tara̱a̱ azinaari nꞌguma nꞌta, bike̱nye̱n be̱ ta̱ci du, bwa nje̱ ciripe̱ na̱ aba, bwa de̱be̱ nꞌguma nꞌta mayaan.
Kunta taa, bunaa tara̱a̱ azinaari nꞌguma nꞌree, bwa nje̱ ciripe̱, bwa de̱be̱ nꞌguma nꞌree mayaan.
Bunaa tara̱a̱ azinaari uguma ka̱, bwa ja̱a̱, bwa kinji ibwa, bwa wuma̱ni azinaari na butu naa ina ndaabwa.
<<Na aba ta̱a̱ ke̱nye̱n ge̱, sa̱i butu naa ina naa aba gyama bwa kúshiike̱ xbuga̱ga̱a̱gi ayuwa ndaabwa.
Sa̱i bunaa taraa azinaari nꞌguma nꞌta, bwa wuce iyeebe ndaabwa, bwa hin, <Butu o̱to̱, bi-taꞌmꞌpana azinaari nꞌguma nꞌta. Na ga̱n nje̱ ciripe̱ ta aba duwa̱ni nꞌyaan nꞌguma nꞌta.>
<<Sa̱i butu na ina ndaabwa bwa hin be̱, <Ha̱nnu, bugyama naa zumaa, bunaa bina̱! Bi-nje̱ ki na̱ iri na njeke. Ga̱n na̱maa pana tuma na huri o̱to̱. Hure, xta̱nje̱ ta̱ga̱da̱ri.>
<<Sa̱i bunaa taraa azinaari nꞌguma nꞌree bwa wuce iyeebe ndaabwa, bwa hin, <Butu o̱to̱, bi-taꞌmꞌpana azinaari nꞌguma nꞌree. Na ga̱n nje̱ ciripe̱ ta aba duwa̱ni nꞌyaan nꞌguma nꞌree.>
<<Sa̱i butu na ina ndaabwa bwa hin be̱, <Ha̱nnu, bugyama naa zumaa, bunaa bina̱! Bi-nje̱ ki na̱ iri na njeke. Ga̱n na̱maa pana tuma na huri o̱to̱. Hure, xta̱nje̱ ta̱ga̱da̱ri.>
<<Sa̱i bunaa taraa azinaari guma ka̱, bwa wuce iyeebe ndaabwa, bwa hin, <Butu o̱to̱, ga̱n yan, bu-shi butu naa da̱a̱rici. Bi-ta guba̱ paa gaa tabe̱re̱ce̱, u-wuna̱ni paa gaa tahwe̱nce̱n.
Bwa ta shani ga̱n taha̱nga rukwanyan, ga̱n ja̱a̱, ga̱n kinji ibwa, ga̱n wuma̱ni azinaari ndaa. Raa iri ndaa na.>
<<Sa̱i butu naa ina bwa ra̱ni be̱, bwa hin, <Ka̱i, gaa bugyama naa we̱, burinda. Bi-yan ga̱n ta guba̱ paa ga̱n tabe̱re̱ce̱, ma wuna̱a̱na̱ paa ga̱n tahwe̱nce̱n.
Bi-shi kuu-tasha̱a̱ ayuwa nimi paaka ba nii duwa̱na̱ o̱to̱, ha̱ni na ga̱n kúshiike̱ ma raa ayuwa nimi huku na̱ riba.
<< <Wana kunnu, raa ma ubwa guma waabwa, iduwa̱ni bunaa mꞌbaa upwa.
Wana kunnu, hyo̱ bunaa mꞌbaa iri anii duwa̱na̱ be̱, buꞌmꞌbaa hwarapi. Bunaa za ri, koo ge̱ na bwa mꞌbaa, anii raa wuun waabwa.
Igura̱a̱ bwa bwaa gyama naa uwa̱ kuta̱yincincin nata̱ shiri, paaku nꞌungwa na̱ mꞌmbwa ta̱re̱ mꞌba ne̱e̱.>
Ika̱ra̱bi na̱ iyo
<<Ha̱ni naa Buyoo Butu bwa ja̱a̱ jaa nꞌta̱gwama ta̱ndaabwa, huku na̱ atumashini hyo̱, ha̱ni ya̱nu ta bwa ja̱a̱ hunrana paakii zhe̱nke̱n naa ta̱gwama ta̱ndaabwa.
Hyo̱ awyatu kope na̱ sa̱ra̱ri aba nii mawuna̱a̱na̱ kaꞌuba̱ ndaabwa, bunii hoosa̱ga̱ga̱ wyan goo goo, hakuu iyo̱ naa bikico̱ bwa ta hoosa̱ga̱ga̱ ika̱ra̱bi goo na̱ iyo goo.
Bunii sha̱a̱ ika̱ra̱bi ara kataga ndaabwa, iyo ara kagura̱ ndaabwa.
<<Sa̱i Bugwama hin ana ne̱e̱ nꞌkataga, <Jaa ma, ga̱hin ana Baaba nimi baa ndaaki ma rubara̱ka. Raa ma ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ bwa naa sha̱a̱ga̱ ma ta nꞌta̱pasa nata̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana.
Wana ha̱ni na ga̱n hange̱ rumunro̱n ga̱hin mꞌpa̱ shami. Na ga̱n hange̱ ruꞌure̱, ga̱hin mꞌpa̱ ma̱ni, ga̱n so. Ga̱n shii gai, ga̱hin nꞌra̱a̱.
Ga̱n ne̱e̱ wa̱ra̱, ga̱hin mꞌpa̱ni da̱bi. Ga̱n hange̱ce̱ sa̱, ga̱hin nꞌgwatani. Ga̱n ne̱e̱ na̱ zhaaro, ga̱hin jaa wa̱ka̱mi.>
<<Sa̱i aya̱nu na bina̱ ara̱ni bwa, ahin, <Butu O̱to̱, ya̱ ha̱ni ga̱tu naa ndaya nꞌrumunro̱n, ga̱tuu pa̱ shami? Koo ga̱tuu pa̱ ma̱ni na gaa hange̱ ruꞌure̱, gaa so?
Koo ya̱ ha̱ni ga̱tuu naa ndaya bugai, ga̱tuu ra̱a̱? Koo ga̱tu naa ndaya wa̱ra̱, ga̱tuu pa̱ni da̱bi?
Koo ya̱ ha̱ni ga̱tuu naa ndaya bi-hange̱ce̱ sa̱, koo gaa ne̱e̱ na̱ zhaaro, ga̱tu jaa wakaa?>
<<Sa̱i bugwama ra̱ni wyan, buhin, <Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, ta na ga̱hin ndaaki buka̱ kaya̱too nimi ana̱nna ana hura̱gi ta̱ge̱, ga̱n ta ga̱hin nꞌndaaki.>
<<Sa̱i buhin ana ne̱e̱ nꞌkagura̱ kandaabwa, <Mahooshi ma na̱ ga̱n, ga̱hin ana Hwe̱n bwa pa̱ni nu, ta̱na̱ ma paaku ra na za ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱ mahwa, una Hwe̱n bwa sha̱a̱gi Bupira̱ na̱ atuma ndaabwa.
Ha̱ni na ga̱n hange̱ rumunro̱n, ga̱hin mꞌpa̱ci shami ma re̱. Ga̱n hange̱ ruꞌure̱, ga̱hin mꞌpa̱ci ma̱ni ga̱n swa̱.
Ga̱n shii gai, ga̱hin nꞌra̱a̱ci na̱ ina ninhin. Ga̱n na naa wa̱ra̱, ga̱hin mꞌpa̱ncin da̱bi. Ga̱n na hange̱ce̱ sa̱, ga̱n gura̱a̱ naa na̱ zhaaro, ga̱hin ja̱a̱ci wa̱ka̱mi.>
<<Sa̱i ara̱ni, ahin, <Butu O̱to̱, ya̱ ha̱ni nu ga̱tu naa ndaya nꞌrumunro̱n, koo nꞌruꞌure̱, koo bugai, koo gaa ne̱e̱ wa̱ra̱, koo gaa hange̱ce̱ sa̱, koo gaa ne̱e̱ na̱ zhaaro, ga̱tuu gwatancin?>
<<Sa̱i bura̱ni wyan buhin, <Mahanda ga̱n na̱ maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, ta na ga̱hin ndaakici buka̱ kaya̱too na̱nna ana hura̱gi ta̱ge̱, ga̱n ta ga̱hin nꞌndaakici.>
<<Aya̱nu ta nii ta̱na̱ paaku ngwan na za kuta̱huwa̱, ama ana shi ana bina̱, ata̱ni paaku bina̱ na mahwa.>>

Awyatu o̱to̱ maga̱ga̱a̱gi ta̱kuna Yeesu
Marukusu 14:1-2; Luka 22:1-2; Yoohana 11:45-53
Na Yeesu be̱ hwii ta̱cita̱ga̱ ri ya̱nu hyo̱, sa̱i be̱ hin ana jwarigi buu,
<<Iyan Ta̱mawuna̱na̱ nata̱ Ta̱matamanrinyan Ta̱hanrinyan Nꞌina ta̱goki, ba̱re nꞌhwe̱n ree mꞌbwa̱ci, anii pana Buyoo Butu, aka̱bi be̱ na̱ guguji.>>
Sa̱i apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya aba mawuna̱ni na̱ ina na butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti na aba ta nꞌgana Kayaapa.
Aba maga̱ga̱a̱gi haruwa na abaa kota̱na̱ buu ta̱swee akwane̱ buu.
Sa̱i aba hin, <<Shici na̱ hwe̱n na bwa buki na̱ wana xawyatu ta hiika̱hina̱ gagu.>>
Buꞌa̱ shani Yeesu mariga̱ na̱ Be̱tani
Marukusu 14:3-9; Yoohana 12:1-8
Na Yeesu be̱ ta̱naa na̱ Be̱tani na̱ ina na Siima, bunaa taꞌmꞌbaa suguma nasu tutuu,
sa̱i buyaan buꞌa̱ bwa wuce na̱ mꞌmariga̱ nama nꞌshima nama mꞌbaa yuwa o̱to̱, da̱ nii ndaashi naa aba nje̱ na̱ atari na rushama. Ha̱ni na be̱e̱ re̱ shami, sa̱i bwa zooni buu na̱ hyuhyu.
Na ana jwarigi buu aba nda̱i kunta, aba gware̱ sume̱, abaa mahyaan, <<Iba̱ shani aba kuha̱ni mariga̱ ma na̱nna kunta?
Ashi kasa̱a̱nha̱ni mꞌba mariga̱ na̱ ayuwa o̱to̱ apa̱ga̱ni aꞌwa̱ta̱gi, uhurici?>>
Tana ta̱hyan Yeesu yan ri na abaa cita̱ga̱, sa̱i be̱ hin wyan, <<Iba̱ shani ga̱hin kaki buꞌa̱ na̱nna? Ai, iri na zumaa ta bwa nꞌndaaki.
Aꞌwa̱ta̱gi tanaa koya̱ hwe̱n na̱ ga̱hin, ama ga̱n shii koya̱ hwe̱n ga̱n naa na̱ ga̱hin.
Mariga̱ nama bwa nꞌzooni, buꞌnꞌa̱sa̱ga̱ni ta wana ta̱wuma̱na̱ ta̱niimi nata̱ wuci.
Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, hyo̱ paa abaa bisa̱ga̱ awyatu mazama nama zumaa na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana anii naa cita̱ga̱ iri na bwa nje̱, wana hyan xanaa tamanrinyaan bwa.>>
Yaahuda ra̱ni bunii pana Yeesu
Marukusu 14:10-11; Luka 22:3-6
Sa̱i Yaahuda Isikariyo̱ti buka̱ kaꞌupwa na ree ana be̱ tazwara, bwa ja̱a̱ paaka apirisiti na o̱to̱,
bwa hin, <<Hamba ga̱hin mꞌpana, ga̱mii pa̱ni ma buu?>> Aba pa̱ni be̱ ayuwa na azurufa kuje taatu.
Ta ha̱ni ya̱nu, bwaa wyanzan haruwa na hyan bupa̱ni wyan buu.
Yeesu re̱ shami na ta̱makwaakaa na̱ ana jwarigi buu
Marukusu 14:12-26; Luka 22:7-23; Yoohana 13:21-30; 1 Akoronti 11:23-25
Na̱ hwe̱n na yigo na Buki na Buroodi na za Yisiti, sa̱i ana jwarigi aba ha̱nta̱ni Yeesu, <<Pee gaa ribi ta̱ja̱a̱ ta̱ꞌá̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni pa̱ri naka ta̱re̱ shami na Ta̱matamanrinyan Ta̱hanrinyan Nꞌina?>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Ta̱na̱ ma ce̱pe̱, inii ndaya buyaan butu, ihin be̱, <Biwya̱ra̱mi hin, bike̱nye̱n nde̱e̱be̱ goki, binii re̱ shami na Ubuki na Ta̱matamanrinyan na̱ ina ndaa huku na̱ ana jwarigi buu.> >>
Ana jwarigi buu aba nje̱ haruwa na Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, aba nje̱ shami na Ta̱mawuna̱na̱ nata̱ Ta̱matamanrinyan Ta̱hanrinyan Nꞌina kaun.
Na shurugo bwa nje̱, sa̱i Yeesu be̱e̱ re̱ shami na̱ aꞌupwa na ree na jwarigi buu.
Aba ma re̱ shami, sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, buka̱ na̱ ame̱ ninhin pina buna̱ma mꞌpana kana nꞌribici.>>
Aba gware̱ sume̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, abaa hantaana buu wyatu ka̱a̱ ka̱a̱, <<Koo ga̱n nu suu, Butu O̱to̱?>>
Be̱ ra̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Bunaa ga̱n re̱ shami bigwaga ka̱ na̱a̱ bwa, bwa ta nii mꞌpana.
Ga̱n Buyoo Butu nii ꞌwa̱ haruwa na aba tataga paaku mazama nama Hwe̱n wana nimi. Ama ta̱guma ta̱ne̱e̱ kubutu naa nii mꞌpana, manii hura̱a̱ga̱ bwa katama̱ncincin bwa!>>
Sa̱i Yaahuda bunaa ja̱a̱ pana buu, bwa hin, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, koo ga̱n nu suu?>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin be̱, <<Kunnunu, gaa bu-cici taa.>>
Aba ma re̱ shami, sa̱i Yeesu be̱ sha̱pi buroodi, be̱ gooji Hwe̱n, be̱ ya̱biza̱gi bwa buroodi, be̱ pa̱ga̱ni ana jwarigi buu, ma hyaan, <<Raa ma, ire̱, ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱niimi ta̱ta.>>
Be̱ gura̱a̱ shapa bikoopi naa ma̱ni nama iinabi. Na be̱ hwii Hwe̱n ta̱gooda̱, be̱ pa̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Swa ma hyo̱ ninhin.
Na̱nna ta shi mahiin maniimi nama ta̱masha̱a̱ga̱ nama ga̱n nii wyashika na̱ wana wyatu hwarapi, na hyan Hwe̱n bwa jaa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ wyan pinsan ndaaba.
Ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, ga̱n jaa gura̱a̱ swa ma̱ni nama iinabi mana̱nna sa̱i kuhwe̱n na ga̱n gura̱a̱ swa nama fo huku na̱ ga̱hin nꞌta̱gwama nata̱ Ada nimi.>>
Na Yeesu na̱ ana jwarigi buu aba zhe̱nye̱n zha̱a̱, aba ba̱ni zhagu Biꞌundu naa Iꞌwe̱e̱ na Zaitu.
Biituru nii hyan buyancin Yeesu
Marukusu 14:27-31; Luka 22:31-34; Yoohana 13:36-38
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Na̱ gita yana hyo̱ ninhin ga̱hin gida̱ga̱ga̱, iꞌnꞌga̱a̱, wana iri na na̱ma nꞌda̱ba, haruwa na aba ta̱gi na̱ takaada na Hwe̱n ta̱hyan,
<< <Ga̱n nii kuna buꞌiyo̱,
ika̱ra̱bi ga̱ta̱a̱gi.>
Ama bike̱nye̱n na ga̱n hiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱, nꞌja̱maa gira ma zhagu Gaalili.>>
Sa̱i Biituru bwa hin, <<Koo hyo̱ ndaaba agida̱ga̱gi wana ri na ja̱maa da̱ba, ga̱n jamaa gaa.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni <<Mahanda ga̱n maa bisa̱ga̱, na̱ gita na̱nna, ta uka̱nrin bwa ta̱wo ungwa, bu-nii cita̱ ta̱hyan bu-nꞌyancin mataatu.>>
Biituru bwa hin, <<Koo ana̱ma nꞌkuna da̱nda̱ na̱ gaa, nꞌjaa hyan iiyancin.>> Kunnu taa hyo̱ ndaaba.
Yeesu nje̱ ro̱pe̱ na̱ cima na Gata̱samaani
Marukusu 14:32-42; Luka 22:39-46
Sa̱i Yeesu na̱ na jwarigi buu aba huri paaki cima na aba ta hyan Gata̱samaani, be̱ hin wyan, <<Hunraana ma pina. Ga̱n nii jaga piree ma njé̱e̱ ro̱pe̱.>>
Be̱ sha̱pi Biituru na̱ Yaakubu na̱ Yoohana, mꞌmwaan na n-Zabadi, aba huri. Nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu be̱ makaki ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ ngwan na wuci.
Be̱ hin wyan, <<Ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱niimi ta̱shiragi ta̱guma haku ta̱hyan nꞌnii ꞌwa̱. Hunrana ma pina, inaa ga̱ri.>>
Na be̱ huri iyeebe ge̱, be̱ gii pwan, ma gwataga nꞌce̱nye̱n ma nda ro̱pe̱, <<Ada nimi, kumanii nda, nꞌya̱a̱cigi na̱ ngwan na̱nna. Hyo̱ mꞌmaya̱nu, shii maniimi gaa jwara̱ga, kiri na gaa hin.>>
Be̱ kúshiike̱ paaka aba taatu, be̱ wuta̱ni wyan na̱ nꞌrabi. Be̱ hin Biituru, << Ka̱i, ijaa ara ta̱naa ga̱ri koo na ha̱ni ge̱?
Naa ma ga̱ri, inaa nda ro̱pe̱ na̱ wana ga̱hin jaa mamunsana kuta̱maanwyana. Mahanda bigata taa ribi, ama ta ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ba ga̱a̱.>>
Be̱ gura̱a̱ kushiika mareenu, be̱ nje̱ ro̱pe̱, be̱ hin, <<Ada, kumajaa nda bwa shi ga̱ga̱ga̱ sa̱i kunswa̱ ta̱guma ta̱na̱nna, too, xiri na gaa ribi nje̱.>>
Na be̱ kúshiike̱ mayaan, be̱ wuta̱ni wyan na̱ nꞌrabi, na̱ wana ayishe ndaaba cigi na̱ nꞌrabi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Be̱ gura̱a̱ kúshiike̱ mataatu, be̱ nje̱ ro̱pe̱ ma cita̱ga̱ kiri ka̱ na be̱ tahoo cita̱ga̱.
Be̱ kúshiike̱ kana jwarigi buu, be̱ hin <<Ita ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌrabi ga̱hiin ha̱nka̱nka̱na̱? Gwatana ma, bike̱nye̱n nje̱ na aba nii pana Buyoo Butu kuꞌnꞌara na nꞌawyatu na pinsan.
Hiika̱ ma, xta̱nhuri. Nde̱e̱, buna nii mꞌpana taa wuce.>>
Akota̱ni Yeesu
Marukusu 14:43-50; Luka 22:47-53; Yoohana 18:3-12
Yeesu ma nda mazama na̱ aba, sa̱i Yaahuda buka̱ kaba upwa na ree, bwa jaa na̱ awyatu hwarapi, aba há̱mba̱a̱gi nꞌsa̱nka̱ri na̱ nꞌsungo. Apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na awyatu aba káji wyan.
Yaahuda na nii pana wyan Yeesu, bwa hoo macíta̱gi na̱ aba ta̱hyan, <<Bunaa ga̱n nii hwaamana bwa taa shi Yeesu. Kota̱na̱ ma be̱, ihuri, iha̱mba̱ga̱ be̱ ki.>>
Kunta̱wuta̱ nata̱ Yaahuda, bwa ta̱ ta̱hura̱ paa Yeesu, bwa hin buu, <<Ha̱nnu da̱i, biwya̱ra̱mi,>> Sa̱i bwa hwaamani buu.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin be̱, <<Bushikaa niimi, nda ri naa íye̱.>>
Sa̱i awyatu aba wuce, aba kota̱ni Yeesu, aba ha̱mbagi buu.
Na aba nda̱i kunta, sa̱i buka̱ kana naawan nii be̱, bwa cwáanrinye̱n bisa̱nka̱ri, bwa ꞌya̱pi bugyama naa butu o̱to̱ naa pirisiti ce̱be̱.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin be̱, <<Kushihina bisa̱nka̱ri ndaabi ta̱zwagana, hyo̱ bunaa shápi bisa̱nka̱ri, bisa̱nka̱ri taa nii kuna be̱.
Ga̱hin ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan nꞌza ta̱kai nata̱ hyan mawyanzan ta̱guna̱ paa Baaba nimi, kunrun kunrun aꞌnꞌkádaagi bigudu naa atuma ndaabwa binaa huri nꞌgudu na nꞌyaburi na nꞌasooja upwa na ree?
Too, na aba nii ciga̱hina̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n nama ta̱gi ta̱hyan ga̱ga̱ga̱ na̱nna ri nii nda?>>
Ha̱ni ya̱nu sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin aba awyatu, <<Nꞌshi butu naa nii hiika̱hina̱a̱ gagu nuu, na ga̱hin báni na̱ nꞌsa̱nka̱ri na̱ nꞌsungo na hyan iꞌnꞌkota̱ni? Koya̱ hwe̱n nꞌta hunrana na̱ bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n manaa nda ta̱ga̱gaagana ga̱hin nꞌkota̱ncin.
Ama hyo̱ iri ya̱nu nje̱ ta wana hyan iri na acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama aba na taga icigi.>> Kuta̱naa ha̱nga mazama maya̱nu, ana jwarigi buu, aba gida̱ga̱gi, aba ga̱a̱ buu be̱e̱ ka̱.
Yeesu kawyatu na taꞌyapa mazama
Marukusu 14:53-65; Luka 22:54-55,63-71; Yoohana 18:13-14,19-24
Sa̱i ana takota̱na̱ Yeesu aba ꞌye̱e̱ buu kuꞌina na Kayaapa, butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti. Nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya aba mawuna̱ni kaun hyo̱.
Biituru bwa jwarigi Yeesu ta̱baa ta̱hakana. Bwa jwarigi buu ji hara̱ bambanu na ina na butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti. Bwa hunrani huku na̱ awyatu na ta ha̱mba ina xbunda̱i kaba nda.
Apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ hyo̱ awyatu na ta ꞌyapa mazama, abaa wyanzan awyatu na nii nda ta̱be̱ acici yaan ri na bisa̱a̱ Yeesu nje̱ pinsan, akwane̱ buu.
Awyatu hwarapi aba cita̱gi ta̱be̱ nata̱ iri na aba hin Yeesu nje̱, ama ana ta ꞌyapa mazama aba de̱be̱ce̱ na shi mahanda.
Ta̱hakana, ayaan ree aba gura̱a̱ cita̱ ta̱be̱ hiku, aba hin,
<<Ta̱hange̱ bihin, <Ga̱n nii huza̱a̱ga̱ Ina na Hwe̱n yana, ma ma yaan na̱ nꞌhwe̱n taatu.> >>
Na butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti bwa hange̱ kunnu, bwa hiiki, bwa ha̱nta̱ni Yeesu, bwa hin, <<Bi-za ri na gaa gura̱ha̱na̱? Iri na aba cici na̱ wana ndaa paa?>>
Ama Yeesu be̱ ne̱e̱ wau. Sa̱i butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti bwa hin buu, <<Ga̱mii ro̱pe̱ na̱ wana Hwe̱n na ne̱e̱ buwuma, mꞌbishi koo gaa taa shi Ala̱masiihu, Buyoo Hwe̱n.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin be̱, <<Kunnunu kugaa hin. Ama hyo̱ ninhin ga̱mii hin ma, ha̱ni na wuci, ija̱a̱ ndaya Buyoo Butu hunrani nꞌkataga naka Hwe̱n na Hura̱gi Ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, ma cíin na̱ arara nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.>>
Sa̱i butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti bwa ha̱nji da̱bi ndaabwa wana ame̱ ta̱gura. Bwa hin, <<Bunje̱ mazama nama hwashe̱ ku-Hwe̱n! Uya̱ sheeda ga̱tun wyanzan? Ihange̱ bunje̱ mazama nama hwashe̱ ku-Hwe̱n.
Imbata ga̱hin hin?>>
Aba hin, <<Bigii ta̱kuna.>>
Aka̱ aba ke̱ne̱ ta̱busa̱ga̱ buu macimi na yishe, aba imi buu ri. Aka̱ baa pasaga buu hanpin,
ma hyaan buu, <<Sugaa hin bi-shi Ala̱masiihu, ta̱bishi, iyaa taa ba̱sa̱ni?>>
Biituru hin buyancin Yeesu
Marukusu 14:66-72; Luka 22:56-62; Yoohana 18:15-18,25-27
Nii be̱e̱ ke̱nye̱n, Biituru bwa hunrani bambanu na ina bwa, kiiyaan be̱e̱ biꞌa̱ binaa nii nda tuma na̱ bwa ina be̱ jaa kaun, be̱ hin be̱, <<Kai, gaa maa huku gaa naawan na̱ Yeesu na Gaalili.>>
Ama na uba̱ na wyatu hyo̱ Biituru bwa hin buyancin Yeesu, bwa gura̱a̱ hyan, <<Ga̱n maa, nꞌyancin iri na gaa cita̱ga̱ mahwa.>>
Na bwa báni kuka̱ta̱ku, biyaan be̱e̱ biꞌa̱ naa nii nda tuma na̱ bwa ina be̱ nda̱i bwa, sa̱i be̱ bishi awyatu na isagi kaun, be̱ hin, <<Buna̱nna, bunaawan huku na̱ Yeesu Bunaazare.>>
Biituru bwa gura̱a̱ hyan buyancin hara̱ na̱ sa̱nsan, bwa hin, <<Ga̱n maa, ga̱n yancin bwa butu.>>
Naa ke̱nye̱n be̱ huri ge̱, ana taꞌisaga do̱ko̱ na̱ Biituru aba hin bwa, <<Mahanda, gaa maa huku gaa ne̱e̱ na̱ aba. Haruwa na gaa cita̱ga̱ mazama ta bisa̱a̱.>>
Ama Biituru bwaa mapagana nu, ma taaga sa̱nsan na̱ aꞌuba̱ ndaaba, bwa hin, <<Ga̱n yancin bwa butu.>>
Bike̱nye̱n be̱ ta̱ci uka̱nrin bwa ta ungwa.
Sa̱i Biituru bwa mata̱ma̱nriin mazama nama Yeesu be̱ tabisa̱ bwa ta̱hyan, <<Ta uka̱nrin bwa ta̱ ungwa, bu-nii cita̱ ta̱hyan bu-nꞌyancin mataatu.>> Bwa ba̱ni sa̱ra̱ri, bwaa nꞌgaga ungwan namii gata ta̱guma.

Aꞌye̱e̱ Yeesu kugwamina Bilaatu
Marukusu 15:1; Luka 23:1-2; Yoohana 18:28-32
Ta na̱ bunwan maza apirisiti na o̱to̱, huku na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya aba maga̱ga̱a̱gi na hyan akwane̱ Yeesu.
Sa̱i aba ka̱da̱gi Yeesu, aba ꞌye̱e̱ buu ku-Bilaatu na Arooma aba tasha̱a̱ bwa shi gwamina.
Yaahuda maswa̱ta̱ni
Tuma 1:18-19
Ha̱ni na Yaahuda, bunaa tapana Yeesu, bwa nda̱i aꞌya̱a̱pi buu suuga̱ nasu ta̱kuna buu, iri be̱ ta̱ be̱ gbi nii gata, bwa kwashe̱he̱ne̱ aba azurufa kuje taatu paaka apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ wyatu o̱to̱.
Bwa hin, <<Ga̱n nje̱ pinsan na ga̱n pa̱ni butu naa za pinsan xakwane̱ be̱.>>
Ama aba ra̱ni bwa, aba hin, <<Iba̱ ta̱ta̱ gbi na̱ mꞌmaya̱nu? Gaa nu mꞌbaa kaki.>>
Sa̱i bwa mo̱nshe̱n aba yuwa na azurufa na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n, bwa ba̱ni, bwa maswa̱ta̱ni.
Sa̱i apirisiti na o̱to̱ aba ushigi aba yuwa, aba hin, <<Manje̱ce̱ ashii wyan paaka yuwa na Ina na Hwe̱n, wana ashi ayuwa na aba kwane̱ butu ta.>>
Aba maga̱ga̱a̱gi aba sa̱n pa̱ri naka ce̱nye̱n nata̱ nꞌga̱ga̱ri ta̱maa na̱ aba yuwa, wana hyan kashi paaka ta̱naa wuma̱a̱na̱ agai kubutu ꞌwi.
Na̱ wana kunnu, ta aba tanaa nꞌga kaun zhagu ba̱re, <<Pa̱ri naka mahiin.>>
Na̱ kunnu ta aba ciga̱hini ri na bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Iriminyan bwa tahyan, <<Aba sha̱pi ayuwa azurufa kuje taatu, ayuwa na awyatu na Isiraaꞌila aba taruba̱ xasa̱n buu.
Na̱ aba yuwa aba sa̱n pa̱ri naka ce̱nye̱n nata̱ nꞌga̱ga̱ri ta̱maa haruwa na Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n bwa mꞌpa̱ni nu.>>
Yeesu na̱ aꞌuba̱ na Bilaatu
Marukusu 15:2-5; Luka 23:3-5; Yoohana 18:33-38
Yeesu ma naa na̱ aꞌuba̱ na Bilaatu gwamina, sa̱i bwa ha̱nta̱ni buu <<Gaa taa shi bugwama naa Ayaahudiya?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Kunnunu kugaa hin.>>
Na awyatu o̱to̱ na apirisiti na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya aba shani buu mazama, be̱ hincin koo ri.
Bilaatu bwa ha̱nta̱ni buu, <<Bi-tibici suu iri na aba cita̱gi na aba hin bi-nje̱?>>
Ama Yeesu be̱ gura̱nha̱ncin bwa koo ri ka̱ hara̱ ugwamina bwa nje̱ ma̱.
Aꞌya̱a̱pi Yeesu suuga̱ nata̱ ta̱kuna buu
Marukusu 15:6-15; Luka 23:13-25; Yoohana 18:39--19:16
Too, aya̱wa̱ni ha̱ni na ubuki na Ta̱hanrinyan Nꞌina ugwamina ta he̱e̱n uta̱zhiga̱a̱gi wyan butu ka̱ naa zhaaro koya̱ yo̱.
Na̱ bwa yo̱ buyaan butu bunaa kukoya̱ bwa yan bunaa aba taꞌnꞌgana Baraba bwa ne̱e̱ na̱ zhaaro.
Na Ayaahudiya aba mawuna̱ni sa̱i Bilaatu bwa ha̱nta̱ni wyan, <<Buya̱ ga̱hin ribi iitázhigaagi ma? Baraba koo da̱i Yeesu naa aba tahyan Ala̱masiihu?>>
Wana buyan ta̱hyan aribici Yeesu ta shaani aba kóta̱ni buu.
Ha̱ni na Bilaatu bwa hunrani nii zhe̱nke̱n naa ta̱suuga̱, aꞌa̱yo ba kádaagi bwa tuma na̱nna, <<Hakata butu yata naa za pinsan, wana ba̱re mꞌmapa̱ dibi na ra̱rabi na̱ wana ndaabwa.>>
Apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ wyatu o̱to̱ na wyatu aba zwage̱ awyatu xahin xata̱zhiga̱ni Baraba, akwane̱ Yeesu.
Ugwamina bwa ha̱nta̱ni wyan mayaan, <<Buya̱ ta ga̱hin ribi maa tazhigaaga ma?>>
Bigudu be̱ ra̱ni, <<Baraba.>>
Bilaatu bwa hin wyan, <<Too, iba̱ ga̱hin ribi xnꞌnje̱ na̱ Yeesu bunaa aba taꞌnꞌgana Ala̱masiihu?>>
Aba ra̱ni, <<xAka̱bi buu na̱ guguji!>>
Bilaatu bwa ha̱nta̱ni, <<Wana ba̱? Uya̱ pinsan be̱ nje̱?>>
Ama aba duwa̱ni sunu ta̱taana ma hyaan, <<xAka̱bi buu!>>
Na Bilaatu bwa nda̱i iri za na bwaa ara ta̱nda, aba ribi ta̱hiika̱hina̱ suha̱nka̱ri, bwa sha̱pi ma̱ni, bwa ha̱mba̱ri nꞌara ndaabwa na uba̱ na wyatu, bwa hin, <<Nꞌza ruwa na̱ ruhaki naru mahiin nama butu na̱nna, bunaa za pinsan. Ga̱hin taa hya̱ ruhaki!>>
Hyo̱ awyatu aba ra̱ni ma hyaan, <<Mahiin mandaabwa xmanaa na̱ hyuhyu nda̱tu na̱ mꞌmwaan nda̱tu!>>
Bwa ta̱zhiga̱a̱gi wyan Baraba ama Yeesu bwa shani aba zware̱ buu nꞌdunduun, bwa pa̱ni buu kasooja xaka̱bi buu.
Asooja ndaaki Yeesu umuntun
Marukusu 15:16-20; Yoohana 19:2-3
Kabata asooja na gwamina aba sha̱pi Yeesu, aba ꞌye̱e̱ buu kuka̱ta̱ku na gwamina, aba wuna̱a̱nyin Yeesu hyo̱ asooja.
Aba ta̱a̱ciga̱gi buu aꞌwana nde̱e̱be̱, aba ta̱a̱ni buu uda̱bi naa shenje haku na nꞌgwama.
Aba ta̱ci bigita̱ na sa̱pi haku tagiya na ta̱gwama, aba huuta̱ni buu na̱ hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱. Aba pa̱ni buu angwo nata̱ gwama na̱ ara nde̱e̱be̱ na kataga. Aba ta̱gi runrun na̱ aꞌuba̱ nde̱e̱be̱ ma ndaga buu umuntun ma hyaan, <<xNꞌhwe̱n nꞌndaabi nꞌduwa̱ni hwarapi, bugwama naa Ayaahudiya.>>
Abaa busa̱ga̱ buu macimi, aba ra̱a̱ buu angwo, abaa basagana buu na̱ hyuhyu.
Na aba hwii ta̱ndaaka buu umuntun, aba ta̱a̱cigi buu da̱bi na shenje, aba ta̱a̱ni buu ꞌwana nde̱e̱be̱. Naazhin aba ba̱ha̱ni buu ha na hyan aka̱bi buu na̱ guguji.
Ta̱kaba nata̱ Yeesu na̱ guguji
Marukusu 15:21-32; Luka 23:26-43; Yoohana 19:17-27
Na aba ne̱e̱ na̱ banu, aba ura̱ku na̱ Siima, butu naa Kuraane, asooja aba shaani bwa ga̱ga̱ga̱ xbusha̱pi uguguji na Yeesu.
Aba wuce kayaan pa̱ri naka aba tahyan Gola̱gota ane̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan, <<Pa̱ri naka Ka̱a̱ta̱ra̱ na Hyuhyu.>>
Aba pa̱ni buu ma̱ni nama iinabi wa̱ta̱ku na̱ ma̱ni nama gagu ama na be̱ hunkuntani, be̱ ga̱a̱ ta̱ swa.
Na aba ka̱bi buu, aba hoosa̱ga̱gi ꞌwana nde̱e̱be̱, aba nje̱ umuntun na ta̱kasa.
Aba hunraani, aba hambe̱ buu kaun.
Da̱da̱da̱ na̱ hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱ aba ta̱gi iri na aba hin binje̱, <<BUNA̱NNA̱ TAA SHI YEESU BUGWAMA NAA AYAAHUDIYA.>>
Aba ka̱bi buu huku na̱ azumba̱ reeko, buka̱ na̱ nꞌkataga, buka̱ na̱ nꞌkagura̱.
Ana nii hura̱ga̱ abaa zuga buu aza̱zama na hwashe̱, abaa cwaagaga buu,
ma hyaan, <<Gaa naa tahyan bu-nii huza̱a̱ga̱ Ina na Hwe̱n, u-gura̱a̱ ma wuun na̱ nꞌhwe̱n nꞌtaatu, mabiha̱ni! Kuu-shi Buyoo Hwe̱n cíin kuguguji yata!>>
Kunnu taa apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na awyatu abaa gisa buu aza̱zama na we̱.
Abaa hyaan, <<Bibiha̱ni ayaan, ama ta be̱ a̱rici ta̱biha̱na̱ hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱! Kuushi bugwama naa Isiraaꞌila xbucíin kubwa guguji yata, naazhin ta̱mpa̱ni nꞌgata nii be̱.
Bipa̱nii gata ku-Hwe̱n, too, xubiha̱ni buu mana ubwa ribi buu! Na̱ wana bitahyan, <Ga̱n shi Buyoo Hwe̱n.> >>
Kunnu taa azumba̱ ana aba takaba buu huku na̱ aba, abaa zuga buu aza̱zama na we̱.
Ta̱ꞌwa̱ na̱ta̱ Yeesu
Marukusu 15:33-41; Luka 23:44-49; Yoohana 19:28-30
Na̱ hwe̱n da̱, ta̱yincincin ta̱ba guna̱ni hyo̱ ta̱ba ce̱nye̱n zhagu ke̱nye̱n naa ta̱ruma ta̱taatu nata̱ hwe̱n.
Biin binaa ta̱ruma ta̱taatu nata̱ hwe̱n Yeesu be̱ ta̱a̱ni nu ta̱ o̱to̱ be̱ hin, <<E̱lai, E̱lai, lama sabaka̱taani?>> Ane̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan, <<Uhwe̱n nimi, Uhwe̱n nimi, iba̱ shani gaa mꞌmo̱nshe̱n?>>
Na ana isagi do̱ko̱ nii be̱e̱ ko, aba hange̱ nuunu, aba hin, <<Be̱ nu ma nꞌga bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Iliya.>>
Buyaan na̱ ame̱ ndaaba bwa gidigi na̱ ha̱ni, bwa jwábani sooso na̱ ma̱ni nama sa̱mbi nama ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ iinabi, bwa tutuba̱ni na̱ angwo, bwa cikaa buu xbiswa̱.
Ama ayaan ana tanaa kaun aba hin, <<Isa ma, xta̱ngwataaga ta̱nnda̱i koo Iliya nii cíin, buciinha̱ni buu kaun.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ gura̱a̱ taana nu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, naazhin be̱ ta̱zhiga̱ni bihwaanwun nde̱e̱be̱, be̱ ꞌwi.
Nii be̱e̱ ke̱nye̱n Uzuzu na ta naa na̱ ame̱ na Ina na Hwe̱n bwa maha̱nda̱ga̱su maree ta da̱da̱da̱ bwa ciin kunrin, nꞌce̱nye̱n mꞌba zha̱a̱nta̱ni, apaga aba maburagi.
Suꞌuya̱ suba guna̱a̱nyin, awyatu na Hwe̱n ana ꞌwa̱gi hwarapi aba hiika̱ki wuma.
Aba bánai kusuꞌuya̱ ha̱ni na Yeesu be̱ hiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱, aba huri ce̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ na ta̱sabu Hurushaliima, aba mabisa̱a̱ kawyatu hwarapi.
Ha̱ni na usooja na o̱to̱ na̱ asooja ana taha̱mba Yeesu aba nda̱i nꞌce̱nye̱n nꞌzha̱a̱nta̱ni na̱ hyo̱ ri na nje̱, aba hange̱ rukwanyan, aba hin, <<Mahanda butu na̱nna buyoo Hwe̱n ta!>>
Ayaan a̱ aba tanaa, ana taꞌisaga katakii, aba gwataagi ana tajwárige̱ Yeesu ta na̱ ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Gaalili ma guna̱a̱ buu na̱ tuma.
Na̱ ame̱ ndaaba, Maariyamu Magadalina, na̱ Maariyamu ada̱a̱da̱ na Yaakubu na̱ Yusufu, na̱ ada̱a̱da̱ na mꞌmwaan na n-Zabadi ana tanaa.
Ta̱wuma̱na̱ nata̱ Yeesu
Marukusu 15:42-47; Luka 23:50-56; Yoohana 19:38-42
Na shurugo bwa nje̱ buyaan butu naa ruzha̱a̱ Yusufu na Arimatiya bunaa yuwa bwa jaa, bwa taa bwa shi naa jwarigi Yeesu.
Bwa ja̱a̱ paa Bilaatu, bwa ha̱nta̱ni xbupa̱ni bwa ruꞌwa̱ naru ta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ Yeesu, Bilaatu bwa pa̱ni nu ta̱hyan xaja̱a̱, apa̱ni bwa tuun.
Yusufu bwa sha̱pi ruꞌwa̱ naru ta̱ꞌwaba bwa rigi tuun na̱ zuzu na ruꞌwa̱ una liilin na ne̱e̱ sabu.
Bwa zwa̱ga̱ni na̱ uya̱ ndaabwa na fo una aba takinda̱ na̱ apaga, bwa riinhini tari na yaburi, bwa guna̱ni nu na uya̱, bwa huri.
Maariyamu na Magadalina na̱ na̱nnda̱ree Maariyamu aba ta hunraana do̱ko̱ na̱ paaku uya̱.
Awyatu na iyo na uya̱
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n hwe̱n na shiri na hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya, apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ Afaraasiya ba ja̱a̱ paa Bilaatu.
Sa̱i aba hin, <<Ta̱mata̱ma̱nriin ri na bupira̱ yata bwa tahyan ha̱ni na bwa ne̱e̱ na̱ wuma ndaabwa, <Kuꞌnꞌhwe̱n taatu nꞌhuri nꞌnii hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱.>
Na̱ wana kunnu pana nu xaha̱mba uya̱ zhagu nꞌhwe̱n taatu na̱ wana xana tajwara̱ga buu xata jaa ja̱a̱ asha̱pi buu zumba̱, ajaa hin bihiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱. Ta̱be̱ nata̱ ta̱hakana ta̱jaa huri nata̱ yigo o̱to̱.>>
Bilaatu bwa hin wyan, <<Tara ma awyatu na iyo̱, ija̱a̱, iha̱mba uya̱ haruwa na ga̱hin ara.>>
Aba huri, aba hambe̱ uya̱, aba duwa̱ni ta̱bukakana ki aba ta̱ aꞌiyo̱, aba hambe̱.

Ta̱hiika̱ nata̱ Yeesu kuta̱ꞌwa̱
Marukusu 16:1-10; Luka 24:1-12; Yoohana 20:1-10
Na hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya bwa huri, na̱ bunwan maza na hwe̱n na yigo na maako, Maariyamu Magadalina na̱ Maariyamu na̱nnda̱ree aba ja̱a̱ ta̱ndái uya̱.
Sa̱i nꞌce̱nye̱n mꞌba zha̱a̱nta̱ni ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ wana buyaan butuma naa Hwe̱n bwa cíin ta nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, bwa ngirinhini tari na uya̱, bwa hunrani da̱da̱da̱ ndaabwa.
Mꞌpirwa ndaabwa na̱ maza̱ki haku ta̱manyan manyan nata̱ shira̱, aꞌwana ndaabwa katande̱ haku ta̱zhin.
Na aꞌiyo̱ aba nda̱i bwa aba wa̱shi, abaa jikita̱ga̱, aba nje̱ sa ꞌwa̱gi.
Sa̱i butuma naa Hwe̱n bwa hin aba a̱, <<Ta-ha̱nga ma rukwanyan, nꞌyan inii wyanzan ta Yeesu, bunaa aba takaba na̱ guguji.
Biza pina, bihiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱ kiibe̱ taa hyan ma, jaa ma inda̱i paaka aba tataahini buu.
Hura̱ ma na̱ ha̱ni, jaa bisa̱ ma ana jwarigi buu bihiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱, bina̱maa gira ma wuco Gaalili. Piree kata ga̱hin ndaya buu. Ta-haasana ma iri na ga̱mii bishi ma.>>
Sa̱i aba hiiki na sumo̱ kuꞌuya̱ huku na̱ rukwanyan na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱da̱ri, aba ja̱a̱ ta̱bisa̱ ana jwarigi buu.
Yeesu be̱ he̱e̱n buza̱a̱ be̱ ura̱ku na̱ aba, be̱ hin wyan, <<Hunranhunran na̱ nꞌta̱gumunu xta̱naa huku na̱ ga̱hin!>> Aba jaa do̱ko̱ nii be̱, aba wunfunrani mꞌbuna nde̱e̱be̱, aba ta̱a̱ga̱gi buu runrun.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Ta-ha̱nga ma rukwanyan. Hura̱ ma ibishi aya̱too xahuri Gaalili piree kata aba na̱ma nꞌndaya.>>
Ta̱cita̱ nata̱ aꞌiyo̱
Na aba a̱ aba ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱hani, sa̱i aꞌiyo̱ aba ta̱ni ce̱pe̱, aba bisa̱gi apirisiti na o̱to̱ hyo̱ ri na nje̱.
Na apirisiti na o̱to̱ aba ura̱ku na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya, sa̱i aba maga̱ga̱a̱gi, aba pa̱ni asooja na iyo̱ ayuwa o̱to̱.
Aba hin wyan, <<Hyan ma, <Ana jwarigi buu ta tajaa na̱ gita, aba sha̱pi buu zumba̱ ga̱tu na̱ nꞌrabi.>
Kumana̱nna mazama mawuci ce̱be̱ na gwamina, ta̱na̱maa isaaga ma ga̱hin jaa ta̱na̱ mamboo.>>
Sa̱i aba aꞌiyo̱ ba ra̱a̱ yuwa, aba nje̱ kuꞌaba ga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni wyan. Mana̱nna mazama hara̱ ba̱re na̱ ame̱ na Ayaahudiya abaa wyasa muu.
Tuma na Yeesu be̱ ga̱a̱gi ana jwarigi buu
Marukusu 16:14-18; Luka 24:36-49; Yoohana 20:19-23; Tuma 1:6-8
Sa̱i ana jwarigi Yeesu aꞌupwa na̱ ka̱ aba huri Gaalili paa undu na be̱ tabisa̱ wyan xaja̱a̱.
Na aba nda̱i buu, aba pa̱ buu hunrun, ama aka̱ abaa hoosa̱ga̱ga̱ nꞌgata.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ wuce waaba, be̱ hin, <<Hyo̱ ta̱gwama nata̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ aꞌmꞌpa̱ni.
Wana kunnu jaga ma iga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni hyo̱ awyatu na sa̱ra̱ri yana aꞌnꞌjwara̱ga, indaakaki wyan baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ ta̱kai nata̱ Ada na̱ nata̱ Buyoo na̱ nata̱ Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n,
iga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni wyan xajwara̱ga hyo̱ nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌga̱mii pa̱ni ma. Ga̱n nii naawan huku na̱ ga̱hin, hara̱ ta̱huwo nata̱ ha̱ni yana mꞌmahwa.>>
MRK - Pangu
Marukusu
Mar
Marukusu
Mazama nama zumaa nama Yeesu kuta̱taga nata̱ Marukusu
Mazama nama zumaa nama Yeesu kuta̱taga nata̱
Marukusu
Iri na ta̱yansun na yigo
Bunaa shi naa ta̱gi takaada na̱nna na mazama nama zumaa bwa taa shi Marukusu, bunaa ruzha̱a̱ rundaabwa naru ta̱hiku ruba shi Yoohana Marukusu. Bwaa tasha bushikaa naa ta̱hiku naa Biituru butuma. Atataga takaada na̱nna ta aba huzo Hurushaliima na̱ yo̱ na 70 na̱ nꞌta̱mantan nata̱ Yeesu. Piree na̱ ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Rooma, atataga muu ta aba ta̱go atakaada taatu ana mazama nama zumaa nama Yeesu.
Na̱nna takaada tapasa na̱ nꞌta̱hyan, <<Na̱nna ta shi mazama nama zumaa nama Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, Buyoo Hwe̱n.>> Mꞌba mazama mata̱bisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan Yeesu shi bunaa Hwe̱n bwa káji naa ta̱hiku, huku na̱ nꞌta̱kai. Atandaya ta̱kai ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ paaku ta̱ga̱gaagana, na̱ nꞌta̱kai ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ paaka awyatu na hira̱ ta̱ba̱ha̱na̱a̱, na̱ nꞌta̱kai ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ paaku ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ncin awyatu pinsan. Yeesu tagura̱a̱ nda mazama nama hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱ ta̱hyan, be̱ taa shi Buyoo Hwe̱n, bunaa jaa na hyan bupa̱ni hyuhyu ndaabwa, bubiha̱ni awyatu. Una̱nna takaada huri ta̱nda mazama nama iri na Yeesu be̱ ndagi, uma̱a̱ncin ta̱nda mazama mande̱e̱be̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana. Aꞌaaya ana ta̱hakana anje̱ mazama nama utuma na Yeesu una maako na ta̱makwaakaa na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana ta be̱ uwa̱ na̱ nꞌta̱hiika̱ ta̱nde̱e̱be̱.
Iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱
