Ushiri na tuma na Yeesu :1-13Tuma na Yeesu na̱ Gaalili :14--9:50Ta̱hani nata̱ Yeesu na̱ Gaalili zhagu Hurushaliima :1-52Maako na ta̱makwaakaa na Yeesu :1--15:47 Hiiko na Yeesu kuta̱ꞌwa̱ :1-20
Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma bisa̱gi wyatu mazama
Maatiyu 3:1-12; Luka 3:1-18; Yoohana 1:19-28
Na̱nna ta shi mazama nama zumaa nama Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, Buyoo Hwe̱n. Ta ba ma̱nta̱n buu,
bunaa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Ishaaya tahoo taga ta̱hyan,
<<Nde̱e̱! Ga̱n nii káji butuma niimi iyeebe ndaa,
bunaa na̱maa a̱sa̱a̱ga̱ga̱ yo̱n ta gaa wuco.
Ta̱ꞌnꞌga ma nꞌga na̱ ahira̱ ma hyaan,
<A̱sa̱ga̱a̱ga̱ ma Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n yo̱n,
ika̱mbiga̱gi ayo̱n na bwaa jwára̱gani.> >>
Bwaa tuma tasha Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma. Bunaa tanaa na̱ ahira̱ ceeku, ma bisa̱ga̱ awyatu ta̱hyan xapa̱ni pinsan baa, ajaa, andagi wyan baba̱tiisa̱ma, wana hyan abisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan apa̱ni pinsan baa, Hwe̱n bwa jaa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ wyan pinsan ndaaba nii gata ndaabwa.
Awyatu hwarapi ana ne̱e̱ kope na̱ nꞌinro̱n na nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya na̱ awyatu na Hurushaliima, abaa jábagi waabwa na hyan anda̱i bwa ahange̱. Abaa cita̱ga̱ apinsan ndaaba, ma panaa apinsan baa. Bwaa ndaga wyan baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ Rwaga na Joodan.
Uda̱bi na Yoohana aba tano̱o̱ wuun na̱ nꞌta̱hinje nata̱ raakumi, na̱ kapa ndaabwa na tutuu. Ishami ndaabwa ibe̱ tasha iꞌyo̱n na̱ ma̱ni nama swain.
Bwaa nda mazama ma hyaan, <<Buyaan buwuci ta̱baa ta̱niimi, bunaa nꞌhuri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, ga̱n jwaci koo uhwa̱ na akandaga ndaabwa ma zha̱ma̱nra̱a̱n ta̱riijiga̱.
Ga̱n, iindagi ma baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ ma̱ni, ama bubwa buja̱maa ndaga ma nii Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n.>>
Anje̱ Yeesu baba̱tiisa̱ma
Maatiyu 3:13-17; Luka 3:21-22
Uyaan hwe̱n, aba na̱ mꞌmaba, Yeesu be̱ jaa, be̱ tabáni ce̱pe̱ na Naazare na ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Gaalili, Yoohana bwa nje̱ buu baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ Rwaga na Joodan.
Na Yeesu be̱e̱ báni na̱ ame̱ na ma̱ni, be̱ nda̱i ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱ba hin gwaan, Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ cíin na̱ hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱ na̱ mꞌpirwa na nꞌhuunruun.
Aba hange̱ ta̱ꞌnꞌga na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ma hyaan, <<Gaa taa shi Baa buniimi, bunaa ga̱n huri ta̱ruba̱, ga̱n mashiragi na̱ gaa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.>>
Bupira̱ ma̱a̱nwya̱ni Yeesu
Maatiyu 4:1-11; Luka 4:1-13
Kupita kunrun, Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ ma̱ni Yeesu zhagu hira̱ ceeku.
Be̱ hunrani na̱ ahira̱ nꞌhwe̱n handa, Bupira̱ bwa ma̱a̱nwya̱ni buu. Yeesu tanaa huku na̱ akuta̱ma̱ na gagu na̱ aga, ama atuma na Hwe̱n abaa ndaaka buu tuma.
Yeesu pa̱shi tuma nde̱e̱be̱ na̱ Gaalili
Maatiyu 4:12-22; Luka 4:14-15; 5:1-11
Na bugwama Hirudu Antipasi bwa zwa̱ga̱ni Yoohana na̱ zhaaro, na nꞌhwe̱n mꞌba pa̱gi, Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni Gaalili, be̱e̱ nda mazama nama zumaa nama báni ku-Hwe̱n.
Be̱e̱ hyaan, <<Uha̱ni wuce! Ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱goki. Pana ma pinsan baa, ipa̱ni nꞌgata nꞌniinhin na̱ mꞌmazama mana̱nna nama zumaa.>>
Yaan hwe̱n na Yeesu be̱e̱ hura̱ na̱ inza̱n na Rwaga na O̱to̱ na Gaalili, sa̱i be̱ nda̱i Siima na̱a̱ ya̱na̱ Andaraawa, ma bwaga ataaro na̱ ma̱ni, wana ashi awyatu ana ta naa kota̱ga̱na̱ nꞌjooshiipa.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ nꞌgani wyan, <<Jaa ma, iꞌnꞌjwara̱ga, nꞌna̱maa kushihina ma ana nii naa nꞌdúubagi wyatu shii nꞌjooshiipa.>>
Kupita aba ga̱a̱ hyo̱ ꞌwaa ndaaba na kota̱ga̱ni na nꞌjooshiipa, aba jwarigi buu.
Na be̱ huri iyeebe ge̱ na bwa inza̱n, sa̱i be̱ nda̱i Yaakubu buyoo Zabadi na̱a̱ ya̱na̱ Yoohana na̱ ame̱ na hantun ndaaba na ma̱ni ma a̱sa̱a̱ga̱na̱ ataaro ndaaba.
Kupita be̱ nꞌgani wyan, aba ga̱a̱ bushiiba na̱ bwa hantun na̱ awyatu na ta naa ndaaka wyan tuma, aba jwarigi buu.
Yeesu pa̱a̱ hwaanwun naa we̱ sumo̱
Luka 4:31-37
Na aba ta̱ni ce̱pe̱ na Kapanahu, uhwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya bwa wuce, Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni ka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya, be̱ ke̱ne̱ ta̱ga̱gaagana wyan.
Awyatu aba jikita̱ni na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱nde̱e̱be̱, na̱ wana binii nda ta̱ga̱gaagana hakuu naa mꞌbaa ta̱kai, shii haku nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa.
Kupita, kuuyaan butu ta na bihwaanwun naa we̱ be̱ jwarigi na̱ ame̱ na ka̱ta̱ku ma ta ta̱ꞌungwa,
ma hyaan, <<Ka̱i! Yeesu na Naazare nꞌnda̱i ruwa ndaa na̱ ga̱tu? Bi-jaa ta u-ta̱ga̱ci? Ga̱n yan iyaa ta gaa shi, gaa taa shi Buyata naa ne̱e̱ Sabu bunaa Hwe̱n!>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ yinzha̱nkani bubwa butu naa hira̱, ta̱hyan, <<Nda wau! Bana na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ butu yata!>>
Sa̱i bibe̱e̱ hwaanwun naa we̱ be̱ shani bwa bwa ta̱ ta̱ꞌungwa, be̱ zha̱a̱nta̱ni bwa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, be̱ ba̱ni na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabwa.
Hyo̱ awyatu aba nje̱ kuma̱, ma mahantaana, <<Ka̱i! Imba̱ iri na iri na kunna? Kai! Ta̱na̱nna ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ fo na̱ nꞌta̱kai kunna, nata̱ nꞌhwaanwun na nꞌwe̱ mꞌba nje̱ iri na bwa hin xnꞌnje̱!>>
Mꞌba mazama mꞌba mawya̱shi kope na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Gaalili.
Yeesu kuda̱gahini awyatu hwarapi
Maatiyu 8:14-17; Luka 4:38-41
Na aba ba̱ni ka̱ta̱ku aba huri da̱nda̱ na̱ Yaakubu na̱ Yoohana, aba ta̱ni ina na Siima Biituru na̱ Andaraawa.
Aya̱na̱wan na Siima na a̱ aba taa mamboo. Yeesu nꞌta̱naa ta̱na̱, aba bishi buu.
Sa̱i be̱ ja̱a̱ paa aba taa, be̱ kota̱ni ara ndaaba, be̱ sha̱pa̱cigi wyan aba hiiki, ta̱ꞌwaba mamboo ta̱ba hwii. Aba ya̱na̱wan na Siima aba hiiki, aba pa̱ wyan shami.
Na shurugo bwa nje̱, hwe̱n bwa iri, awyatu abaa sháapagi Yeesu hyo̱ ana ha̱ngagici sa̱ na̱ ana nꞌhwaanwun na nꞌwe̱ mꞌba jwarigi.
Awyatu hwarapi na ubwa ce̱pe̱ aba mawuna̱ni na̱ adubo na ubwa ina, aba gwataagi.
Yeesu be̱ kuda̱gahinii awyatu hwarapi na suguma goo goo, be̱ gura̱a̱ paga awyatu na hira̱ ma̱ sumo̱. Be̱ yanshin aba awyatu na hira̱ ta̱nda mazama na̱ wana ayan iyaa ta be̱ shi.
Yeesu ja̱a̱ ro̱pe̱ ta̱nda paaka za koo butu
Luka 4:42-44
Na̱ kasu na shiri ta iri be̱ hin gwaan, Yeesu be̱ hiiki, be̱ huri paaka za koo butu, paa be̱ tanaa nda ro̱pe̱.
Sa̱i Siima na̱ ana be̱ tanaawan na̱ aba, aba ja̱a̱ wyanzun nde̱e̱be̱.
Na aba nda̱i buu, aba hin buu, <<Hyo̱ awyatu aba tana̱maa wyanzan.>>
Ama Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni wyan, <<Ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ ta̱ja̱ba̱gi kwan kuꞌnꞌcice̱pe̱ na nꞌne̱e̱ iyeebe ma bisa̱ga̱ wyan mazama, na̱ wana kunnu ta ga̱n jaa.>>
Sa̱i be̱ jwara̱gagani kuꞌnꞌcice̱pe̱ na nꞌne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Gaalili, ma bisa̱ga̱ wyatu mazama na̱ aka̱ta̱ku, ma paga awyatu na hira̱ sumo̱.
Yeesu kuda̱gahini butu naa za mꞌmbwa
Maatiyu 8:1-4; Luka 5:12-16
Buyaan butu naa suguma nasu tutuu bwa jaa paa Yeesu bwa ta̱ runrun, ma rupa buu ta̱hyan, <<Kuu-ribi, bi-nii ara u-nꞌkuda̱gahini nꞌsuguma suniimi ma naa sabu.>>
Be̱ hange̱ ambishiri ndaabwa, be̱ cikaa ara, be̱ a̱nta̱ni bwa ma hyaan, <<Nꞌribi, kuda̱ga, u-naa sabu.>>
Kupita, suguma sundaabwa nasu tutuu suba fogi, bwa butu bwa kwade̱ge̱.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ cipani bwa, ma koota̱ bwa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ta̱hyan,
<<Shiraga ki, ta-bisa̱ kwan buyaan, sa̱i kuu-ja̱a̱ paa upirisiti ubwaa nda̱i. Naazhin u-bisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan bi-kwade̱ge̱ na̱ nꞌsuguma sundaabi. U-pa̱ni iri haruwa na Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa mꞌba hin xapa̱ni, butu bwa bwa̱cigi ta̱shiri nata̱ suguma nata̱ tutuu. Ta̱nda kunnu awyatu nii yansun ta̱hyan bi-ne̱e̱ sabu.>>
Ama bwa butu bwa huri ma taa nu, ma bisa̱ga̱ koo buya̱ iri na nje̱. Na̱ wana kunnu ubwa shani awyatu aba riini Yeesu kope, be̱ a̱rici ta̱ta̱na̱ yaan ce̱pe̱ da̱shi, be̱e̱ hunraana na̱ hwa paa kaza koo butu. Hyo̱ na̱ kunnu awyatu baa jábagi ji waabe̱ kiikoya̱ biin.

Yeesu kuda̱gahini butu naa ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ba so
Maatiyu 9:1-8; Luka 5:17-26
Na nꞌhwe̱n mꞌba hura̱gi na Yeesu be̱ kwashe̱e̱ke̱ Kapanahu, sa̱i mazama mꞌba mawya̱shi kunrun ta̱hyan bikúshe̱ ina.
Awyatu aba mawuna̱ni kope hyo̱ na̱ ina, pa̱ri kaba za naka bwa̱ci hyo̱ na̱ bambanu. Ha̱ni na be̱ tanaa bisa̱ga̱ wyan mazama nama zumaa,
ayaan wyatu aba wuce, aba na̱nshin ma sha̱pa̱go na̱ butu naa nꞌara na̱ mꞌbuna mꞌba so.
Na aba nda̱i ajaa ara ta̱ta̱na̱ paa Yeesu be̱ ne̱e̱, sa̱i aba be̱ ibwa da̱da̱da̱ na ta̱biyana nata̱ aba ba̱ri kuta̱bara re̱ paa Yeesu be̱ ne̱e̱. Sa̱i aba ciinha̱ni bwa butu huku na̱ aco̱ko̱ ndaabwa.
Na Yeesu be̱ nda̱i ta̱panaa gata ndaaba, sa̱i be̱ hin butu naa nꞌara na̱ mꞌbuna mꞌba so, <<Be̱e̱ biniimi, iiha̱mba̱ga̱ncin pinsan ndaa.>>
Too, nꞌyaan nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa mꞌba tanaa kaun, ma mahuwo ta̱makicihinaa muu na̱ nꞌsume̱ sundaaba,
abaa hyaan, <<Iba̱ shani butu na̱nna bwaa nda mazama kunnu? Uhwashe̱ ta ku-Hwe̱n! Buza naa nii ara ta̱yaaciga butu pinsan sa̱i ku-Hwe̱n bwaa ka̱.>>
Yeesu be̱ hoo insan kunrun iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌgata nꞌndaaba, be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan ta̱hyan, <<Wana ba̱ ga̱hin makicihinaa mazama maya̱nu na̱ nꞌgata nꞌniinhin?
Ya̱ ta huri ta̱yoo ahin butu na̱nna naa mꞌbuna na̱ nꞌara mꞌba so ta̱hyan, <Iiha̱mba̱ga̱ncin pinsan ndaa,> koo <Hiika̱, u-sha̱pi ba̱ra̱shina̱ ndaa, u-huri>?
Too, nꞌribi ta̱hyan iyansun, Buyoo Butu mꞌbaa ta̱kai na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana nata̱ ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ncin butu pinsan.>> Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ke̱ce̱e̱ke̱ kuubwa butu naa hange̱ce̱ sa̱ be̱ hin bwa,
<<Iihin, hiika̱, u-sha̱pi aco̱ko̱ ndaa, u-huri giyo.>>
Bwa hin kaki, bwa sha̱pi aco̱ko̱ ndaabwa, bwa ba̱ni. Hyo̱ awyatu aba zooni bwa suyishe, aba nje̱ kuma̱, abaa yaba Hwe̱n ma hyaan, <<Ta̱tannda̱ci iri na ina̱nna ri.>>
Yeesu nꞌgani Laawi
Maatiyu 9:9-13; Luka 5:27-32
Na Yeesu be̱ gura̱a̱ jaga inza̱n na Rwaga na O̱to̱ na Gaalili, awyatu aba mawuna̱ni riinhina̱ kiibe̱ ne̱e̱, be̱e̱ ga̱gaagana wyan.
Be̱ ma hura̱, sa̱i be̱ nda̱i Laawi buyoo Hala̱fa, bwa ma hunrana paa tuma ndaabwa na ga̱ndu ta̱raaga. Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin bwa, <<Nꞌjwárige̱.>> Bwa hiiki, bwa jwarigi buu.
Uyaan ha̱ni na Yeesu na̱ ana jwarigi buu abaa re̱ shami na̱ ina na Laawi, ayaan ana ta naa raaga ga̱ndu taa na̱ ana ga̱a̱ci pinsan, abaa re̱ shami huku na̱ aba, na̱ wana awyatu hwarapi iri na aya̱nu ta jwárige̱ Yeesu.
Na nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin ana shi Afaraasiya, aba nda̱i ta̱hyan binii re̱ shami na̱ ana ta naa raaga ga̱ndu na̱ ana ga̱a̱ci pinsan, sa̱i aba ha̱nta̱ni ana jwarigi buu, aba hin, <<Iba̱ shani be̱e̱ re̱ shami na̱ iri na awyatu na̱nna ana ga̱a̱ci pinsan?>>
Na Yeesu be̱ hange̱, be̱ hin wyan, <<Awyatu na ne̱e̱ kami, uza na nii shana wyan amakaka na̱ butu naa njibi, kana ha̱ngagici sa̱. Nꞌja̱a̱ci ma nꞌgana awyatu na bina̱, kana ga̱a̱ci pinsan.>>
Aha̱nta̱ni Yeesu ruꞌure̱ ta̱nda
Maatiyu 9:14-17; Luka 5:33-39
Too, na ana tajwara̱ga Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ ana jwarigi Afaraasiya abaa nda ruꞌure̱, sa̱i ayaan aba jaa paa Yeesu aba ha̱nta̱ni buu, <<Iba̱ shani ana jwarigi Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ Afaraasiya aba ta nda ruꞌure̱, andaa aba jaa nda?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Ta̱shika nata̱ ne̱e̱ da̱nda̱ na̱ butu naa zha̱a̱ buꞌa̱ ta̱ta nda ruꞌure̱ aba na̱ buki? Ajaa nda na̱ ha̱ni na bwa ne̱e̱ huku na̱ aba.
Ama yaan hwe̱n anii shapa bubwa butu naa zha̱a̱ buꞌa̱, uha̱ni ya̱nu ta abaa naa ndaga ruꞌure̱.
<<Buzaa naa nii dabana da̱bi na gwashe̱ na̱ bisumma naa fo. Kuunje̱ kunnu, bisumma naa fo nii handa ubwa da̱bi, uhuri ta̱ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ kubwa tane̱e̱ na̱ ayigo.
Buza naa nii zooga̱na̱ ma̱ni nama nꞌko̱ro̱ nama fo na̱ nꞌsoso na nꞌta̱sha̱a̱ ma̱ni nama gwashe̱. Kuunje̱ kunnu, ma̱ni nama nꞌko̱ro̱ nama fo manii punsa̱n nꞌsoso, abwe̱ be̱e̱ soso na̱ mꞌba ma̱ni. Ai, ma̱ni nama nꞌko̱ro̱ nama fo, kuꞌnꞌsoso na nꞌfo taa.>>
Ta̱hantana nata̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya
Maatiyu 12:1-8; Luka 6:1-5
Uyaan hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya, Yeesu na̱ ana jwarigi buu abaa hura̱ ma raan cima na shami. Aba na̱ nꞌta̱hani sa̱i ana jwarigi buu baa hwara̱pigaga mꞌmansan na nꞌshami na hyan are̱.
Sa̱i Afaraasiya aba hin Yeesu, <<Nde̱e̱ iri na anaa jwarigi baa nda. Iba̱ shani abaa nda guba̱ na̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Nꞌgira̱nshin nda̱a̱tu mꞌba yanshin?>>
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Icita̱gici iri na Dawuda bwa tanda ha̱ni na bwa na̱ awyatu na ta̱hani ndaabwa aba hange̱ rumunro̱n?
Uha̱ni na Abiyatara bwa tasha butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti, Dawuda bwa tata̱na̱ ina na Hwe̱n paa aba tasha̱a̱ buroodi, una shi kapirisiti baa ka̱ abaa ara ta̱re̱, bwa re̱, bwa gura̱a̱ pagana awyatu ndaabwa ana ta̱hani.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Anje̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na̱ wana butu, anje̱ce̱ butu na̱ wana hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱.
Na̱ wana kunnu, Buyoo Butu taa shi Butu O̱to̱ naa hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱.>>

Yeesu kuda̱gahini butu na̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱
Maatiyu 12:9-14; Luka 6:6-11
Na Yeesu be̱ gura̱a̱ kushiika ta̱ta̱na̱ ka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya, sa̱i be̱ nda̱i kuuyaan butu naa nꞌara mꞌba so na̱ ame̱.
Ayaan ana taruba̱ xanda̱i Yeesu nje̱ pinsan, akota̱ni buu, aba zooni buu suyishe koo binii kuda̱gahina butu naa nꞌara mꞌba so na̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin butu naa nꞌara mꞌba so, <<Jaa, u-isa na̱ aꞌuba̱ na awyatu hyo̱.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Imbata nꞌgira̱nshin nda̱a̱tu mꞌba hin xta̱nnje̱ na̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱? Ta̱nda iri na zumaa koo ina we̱? Ta̱biha̱na̱ koo ta̱kuna?>> Hyo̱ ndaaba aba naanyin wau wau.
Yeesu be̱ gwatani wyan na̱ ame̱ ta̱gura na̱ wana atibici mazama na̱ nꞌgata nꞌndaaba. Sa̱i be̱ hin bwa butu, <<Cikaa ara ndaa.>> Butu bwa cikaa ara, ubwa kwade̱ge̱.
Na̱ nꞌta̱ndaya kunta, kunrun Afaraasiya aba ba̱nii ha, aba mawa̱ta̱ku na̱ awyatu na bugwama Hirudu, abaa nda haruwa na hyan akwane̱ Yeesu.
Bigudu naa awyatu jwarigi Yeesu
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ba̱ni na̱ ana jwarigi buu, zhagu inza̱n na Rwaga na O̱to̱ na Gaalili. Awyatu hwarapi aba jwarigi buu, ana Gaalili, na̱ ana Yaahudiya,
na̱ ana Hurushaliima, na̱ ana ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Idumiya, na̱ ana hira̱ree na Rwaga na Joodan, na̱ ana ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Taaya na̱ Sidon. Awyatu hwarapi aba jábagi na̱ wana xahange̱ ri na be̱e̱ ndaga.
Na̱ wana xawyatu ta maa buu ta̱kaka, be̱ bishi ana jwarigi buu xaꞌwaanyin buu hantun na ma̱ni na njeke ka̱.
Binje̱ kunnu wana bihoo kuda̱gahinaa awyatu hwarapi, ubwa wuci na ta̱hyan ana ha̱ngagici sa̱, abaa matutumaa wyan na hyan aja̱a̱ do̱ko̱ nii be̱ xaꞌa̱nta̱a̱ni buu.
Hyo̱ koya̱ ha̱ni awyatu na hira̱ na we̱ aba nda̱i buu, koo buya̱ bukinai na̱ aꞌuba̱ nde̱e̱be̱, ma hyaan, <<Gaa Buyoo Hwe̱n ta gaa shi.>>
Ama be̱e̱ koota̱ga̱ wyan ta̱hyan xata bisa̱ koo buyaan iyaa ta be̱ shi.
Yeesu zwa̱ri atumashini upwa na ree
Maatiyu 10:1-4; Luka 6:12-16
Aba na̱ kunnu, Yeesu be̱ ka̱ta̱ni undu, be̱ nꞌgani ana be̱ ribi, aba ja̱a̱ waabe̱.
Sa̱i be̱ ka̱shi aꞌupwa na ree xanaa nii be̱, ana be̱ taꞌnꞌgana atumashini nde̱e̱be̱, na hyan binaa kadaga wyan anaa bisa̱ga̱ awyatu mazama,
be̱ pa̱ni wyan ta̱kai nata̱ ta̱ba̱ha̱na̱a̱ awyatu na hira̱.
Nde̱e̱ aba upwa na ree na be̱ takasa na:
Siima, bunaa Yeesu be̱ tapa ruzha̱a̱ Biituru,
Yaakubu be̱e̱ binaa Zabadi na̱a̱ ya̱na̱ Yoohana, ana be̱ tapa <<Buwara̱najisa̱,>> ane̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan, <<Mꞌmwaan na Nꞌta̱,>>
na̱ Andaraawa,
na̱ Filibu,
na̱ Baatalomi,
na̱ Maatiyu,
na̱ Toma,
na̱ Yaakubu buyoo Hala̱fa,
na̱ Tadaawusu,
na̱ Siima, bunaa aba ta hyan butahura̱ ta̱ꞌisa hiku na̱ ce̱nye̱n ta̱ndaabwa,
na̱ Yaahuda Isikariyo̱ti bunaa ja̱a̱ pana akota̱ni Yeesu.
Yeesu na̱ Shatan
Maatiyu 12:22-32; Luka 11:14-23; 12:10
Na Yeesu be̱ kwashe̱e̱ke̱ ina na be̱ tanaa na̱ bwa, awyatu aba gura̱a̱ ciga̱ da̱, ubwa shani bibe̱ na̱ ana jwarigi buu aba de̱be̱ce̱ ha̱ni na shami ta̱re̱.
Na aya̱na̱ba aba hange̱ kunnu, aba ribi xakota̱ni buu, ahuri giyo nii be̱ ta̱hyan, <<Ai, bindagi mꞌpe̱re̱!>>
Nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌtabáni Hurushaliima aba hin, <<Ai, Baꞌala̱zabu bugwama naa awyatu na hira̱ ta kota̱ni buu, na̱ wana binii ba̱ha̱na̱a̱ awyatu na hira̱ na̱ nꞌta̱kai ta̱ndaabwa.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ nꞌgani wyan, be̱ bishi wyan mazama na̱ nꞌta̱kun ta̱hyan, <<Shatan nii ba̱ha̱na̱ Shatan nuu?
Ai, kuta̱gwama ta̱mahooshi maree, biin bika̱ be̱ maꞌunso̱ncin nii ka̱, ta̱gwama ta̱yata ta̱jaa isa mahwa.
Kunnu taa, kiꞌina mahooshi maree, biin bika̱ be̱ maꞌunso̱ncin nii biin bika̱, iꞌina yata jaa isa mahwa.
Ku-Shatan nii nda gagu na̱ nꞌsuhyu sundaabwa, aba mahooshi maree, ta̱jaa isa mahwa, uhuwo ndaaba nu wuce.
<<Kunnunu, buza naa nii ta̱na̱ ina na butu na mꞌbaa kai xbusha̱pi ꞌwaa ndaabwa, sa̱i kuuhuri be̱ kwan kai na ta̱kota̱na̱ be̱, bwa ka̱da̱a̱gi be̱, naazhin busha̱pa̱gi iꞌwaa na ina ndaabwa.
<<Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma mahanda, Hwe̱n jaa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ butu koya̱ pinsan na bwa nje̱ hyo̱ na̱ aza̱zama na hwashe̱ ku-Hwe̱n.
Ama butu naa nje̱ mazama nama hwashe̱ kii-Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n, Hwe̱n nii ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ bwa pinsan ndaabwa mahwa, buyata bunje̱ pinsan na mahwa.>>
Yeesu cici kunnu wana anii hyaan, <<Butu naa hira̱ naa we̱ ta kota̱ni buu.>>
Aya̱na̱ Yeesu na̱ aya̱na̱ba
Maatiyu 12:46-50; Luka 8:19-21
Aya̱na̱ Yeesu na̱ aya̱na̱ba aba jaa paa be̱e̱ nda mazama, aba e̱she̱ na̱ ha, aba ka̱ji xbijaa anje̱ mazama nii be̱.
Awyatu hwarapi ba tahunraana riinha̱nu nii be̱, aba hin buu, <<Nde̱e̱, ada̱a̱da̱ ndaa na̱ ayamboo ree maa wyanzan na̱ ha.>>
Sa̱i be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan be̱ hin, <<Abwaa nu shi ada̱a̱da̱ nimi na̱ aya̱too nimi?>>
Sa̱i be̱ gwatani ana hunrani riinha̱nu huku nii be̱, be̱ hin, <<Nde̱e̱ ada̱a̱da̱ na! Nde̱e̱ aya̱too na!
Hyo̱ bunaa nje̱ iri na Hwe̱n bwa ribi, bwa taa shi buya̱tu naa wya̱ri, bwa shi buya̱tu naa a̱, bwa shi ada̱a̱da̱ nimi.>>

Ta̱kun nata̱ buhwaanyan naa nii wyasa kaasu
Maatiyu 13:1-9; Luka 8:4-8
Yeesu be̱ gura̱a̱ kina ta̱ga̱gaagana awyatu na̱ inza̱n na Rwaga na O̱to̱ na Gaalili. Bigudu naa awyatu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ be̱ mawuna̱ni riinha̱nu nii be̱. Sa̱i na be̱ ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni, bigudu naa awyatu be̱ hunraani na̱ bwa inza̱n.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ke̱ne̱ ta̱ga̱gaagana wyatu mazama mahwarapi nꞌta̱kun, be̱ hin wyan,
<<Shiraaga ma! Buyaan buhwaanyan tabana ta̱wyasa kaasu na̱ cima ndaabwa.
Bwa ma wyasa ibe̱ kaasu, sa̱i ika̱ ibe̱ kinai na̱ yo̱n, nꞌno̱no̱ mꞌba ja̱a̱, mꞌba ta̱in wuun.
Iyaan ibe̱ kinai paaku atari kaba za ce̱nye̱n du. Sa̱i ibe̱ báni kunrun wana be̱e̱ ko za ce̱nye̱n du.
Na hwe̱n bwa báni ibe̱ hoogi zaga, wana anga̱nga̱nda̱ irici na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n.
Iyaan kaasu ibe̱ kinai kuꞌasa̱pi. Na asa̱pi aba mawaani, aba hwii hyo̱ be̱ kaasu ta̱tuba̱ga̱, aba yanshin wuun ta̱mawaana na hyan inje̱ bina̱.
Iyaan ibe̱ kinai kupa̱ri naka mawundu. Ibe̱ báni, ibe̱ nje̱ o̱to̱, ika̱ be̱ ꞌwa̱ruba̱ni kuje taatu taatu, ika̱ kuje cininhin cininhin, ika̱ nꞌyina̱ nꞌka̱a̱ ka̱a̱.>>
Sa̱i be̱ hin, <<Hyo̱ bunaa mꞌbaa ce̱be̱ na ta̱tuba̱ xbutibi.>>
Iri na ta̱ba ta̱kun ta̱ba hin na
Maatiyu 13:10-17; Luka 8:11-15
Ha̱ni na Yeesu be̱ tanaa be̱e̱ ka̱, sa̱i aꞌupwa na ree na be̱ tazwara na̱ ayaan ana tajwara̱ga buu kaun, aba ro̱pe̱ Yeesu xbibishi wyan iri na ta̱ba ta̱kun ta̱ya̱nu ta̱hwarapi ta̱ba hin na.
Be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Ga̱hin, aapa̱ni ma na hyan iyansun ushe̱re̱ na ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n kuta̱ba ne̱e̱. Ama ana za na̱ ga̱hin, nꞌta naa ndaakaka wyan hyo̱ mazama kuꞌnꞌta̱kun,
na̱ wana hyan,
<< <Kanda̱i iri na ga̱n nje̱, aba jaa yansun.
Kahange̱ iri na ga̱n cita̱, aba jaa insan.
Wana hyan xata insan akíciike̱ wa̱ka̱mi,
Hwe̱n bwa jaa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ wyan pinsan ndaaba.> >>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Kiiꞌe̱nshe̱nshe̱n iri na ta̱kun ta̱na̱nna ta̱ba hin, na ga̱hin nii ara ta̱ꞌinsan ta̱yaan?
Bunaa nii wyasa kaasu bwa taa shi naa nii wyasa mazama nama Hwe̱n kuꞌayaan.
Ikaasu ina kinai na̱ yo̱n, ta shi haka wyatu na hange̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n, Bupira̱ wuce kunrun, buya̱a̱cigi muu na̱ nꞌgata nꞌndaaba.
Ikaasu na ke̱ne̱ paaka atari ta shi haku ana hange̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n, aba ra̱a̱ muu kunrun na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱da̱ri.
Ama wana aza nga̱nga̱nda̱ na iri, aba jaa taa ke̱nye̱n mꞌmaba. Ha̱ni na ngwan bwa wuce koo iyaan ri na kaki wyan na̱ wana mꞌba mazama, aba jaa isa hiku ji, sa̱i ama̱ni ta̱baa.
Ikaasu na ke̱ne̱ kasa̱pi ta shi haka wyatu na hange̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n,
ama wana ta̱makaka na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana, wyanzun na ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa iri ma̱, na̱ nꞌta̱ruba̱ nata̱ iyaan iri na sa̱ra̱ri yana, mariini muu ma re̱ muu, u-nda̱i ma aꞌa̱rici ta̱nda yaan kaasu.
Ikaasu na ke̱ne̱ na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n na mꞌmawundu, ibe̱ ta shi haka wyatu na hange̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n, aba ra̱a̱ muu nꞌara nꞌree, mꞌba maꞌwa̱ruba̱ga̱ni, ika̱ kuje taatu taatu, ika̱ kuje cininhin cininhin, ika̱ nꞌyina̱ nꞌka̱a̱ ka̱a̱.>>
Ta̱kun nata̱ maza̱ki nama ra
Luka 8:16-18
Yeesu be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan, <<Buyaan bune̱e̱ bunaa nii pantaan pitila buꞌuuta̱ni wuun nii tumunsun, koo busoo wuun na̱ kunrin na wyansun? Shii ita cagudana ta wuun nii ꞌwa̱ruꞌwa̱ru wana ta̱hyan agwataga maza̱ki?
Hyo̱ iri na ne̱e̱ ta̱swee, anii bara̱nwyan wuun na̱ sa̱ra̱ri. Iri na guna̱a̱ni, anii guna̱a̱ wuun inaa hoo.
Hyo̱ bunaa mꞌbaa ce̱be̱ na ta̱tuba̱ xbutibi.>>
Be̱ gura̱a̱ hyan wyan, <<Shiraga ma ki iri na ga̱hin hange̱. Haruwa na ga̱hin shiraagi ki, kunta Hwe̱n bwa na̱maa pana ma ta̱yansun, hyo̱ nꞌta̱duwa̱na̱ maa mayaan.
Kuꞌana nꞌshiragi ta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱niimi, Hwe̱n nii duwa̱na̱ wyan ta̱yansun. Ama kuꞌana nꞌshiraagici, koo una aba yan ge̱, Hwe̱n nii yaaciga ta̱yansun, uga̱a̱ wyan kunta.>>
Ta̱kun nata̱a̱ kaasu naa báni
Yeesu be̱ gura̱a̱ hyan, <<Ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ne̱e̱ haku hwaanyan naa wya̱shi ikaasu na̱ cima ndaabwa.
Nꞌhwe̱n na̱ hwe̱n ma hura̱ga̱ na̱ gita na̱ hwe̱n, ikaasu be̱ báni, ibe̱ mawaani, ama bwa yancin kiꞌibe̱ nje̱ o̱to̱.
Nꞌce̱nye̱n kuꞌmꞌba nꞌtapa shami na cima, na̱ ayigo ita nda saan, naazhin inje̱ bwasu, ubwasu nje̱ ikaasu.
Ha̱ni na ibe̱ nje̱ ta̱guba̱, bushápi ipa̱, bugubi na̱ wana ta̱hyan ha̱ni na guba̱ nje̱.>>
Ta̱kun nata̱a̱ kaasu naa masa̱ta
Maatiyu 13:31-34; Luka 13:18-19
Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Na̱ iba̱ ga̱tun kuta̱a̱ ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n? Koo na̱ nꞌta̱ya̱ ta̱kun ga̱tun cita̱ na hyan ta̱bisa̱a̱ kuta̱ba ne̱e̱?
Ta̱shi hakii kaasu naa masa̱ta binaa aba be̱re̱ na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n. Be̱ taa hura̱gi mawuzhira̱ hyo̱ na̱ kaasu.
Hyo̱ na̱ kunnu, kabe̱re̱ buu, bita mawaana, bihuri hyo̱ koya̱ iri na ꞌwaa na shiipa na aba be̱re̱ na̱ cima. Bita nda aruun na o̱to̱, ana nꞌno̱no̱ mꞌba ta naa ndaga ta̱hurogo nꞌnaa ha̱nka̱nka̱na̱ na̱ ahunrun ndaaba.>>
Na̱ nꞌta̱kun ta̱hwarapi na̱ta̱ mazama Yeesu be̱ bisa̱gi wyan mazama nama Hwe̱n, na nje̱ to̱n na̱ nꞌta̱yansun ta̱ndaaba.
Be̱ a̱cii bisa̱ wyan mazama sa̱i kiinje̱ tuma nꞌta̱kun, kubwa hwarapi na tamawuna̱na̱. Ama ha̱ni na be̱ ne̱e̱ be̱e̱ ka̱ na̱ ana jwarigi buu, biguna̱a̱nyin wyan hyo̱ komba̱ri gwaan.
Yeesu yinzha̱nkani upyara na̱ ma̱ni
Maatiyu 8:23-27; Luka 8:22-25
Na hwe̱n bwaa nda nꞌta̱ꞌira̱, Yeesu be̱ hin ana jwarigi buu, <<xTa̱ka̱a̱ci ma hira̱ree na rwaga na o̱to̱.>>
Aba ga̱a̱ bigudu naa awyatu pita, aba sha̱pi Yeesu paa be̱ tanaa na̱ hantun, ayaan hantun aba tajwárige̱ wyan.
Sa̱i ururo bwa híike ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ pyara na kai, ma shapacigaga ama̱ma̱ni na dabu ma basagana uhantun. Ma̱ni mꞌbaa ta̱na̱a̱ na̱ ame̱ na hantun, ubwa ribi ta̱ciga̱ na̱ ma̱ni.
Yeesu be̱ tanaa ta̱baa na̱ta̱ hantun na̱ nꞌrabi, hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱ ma cagudana na̱ mataashi nꞌkai. Ana jwarigi aba hiika̱hini buu, aba hin buu, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, ta̱na̱manhuwa̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱, uukakici gaa suu?>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ zhe̱mbe̱, be̱ yinzha̱nkani pyara, be̱ hin ama̱ma̱ni na rwaga na nii rokuuco, <<U-naa wau! Nda fo̱n!>> Sa̱i upyara bwa nje̱ taa wau, kope kaba nje̱ fo̱n.
Sa̱i be̱ hin ana jwarigi buu, <<Iba̱ shani ga̱hin jikita̱ni? Hyo̱ niina ipa̱ncin nꞌgata niinhin na̱ ga̱mi?>>
Aba hange̱ rukwanyan ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, abaa mahyaan, <<Iyaa na na̱nna kunna? Bunaa upyara na̱ ata na ma̱ni aba cina̱ni bwa kunta!>>

Yeesu kuda̱gahini butu naa mꞌbaa awyatu na hira̱ na we̱
Maatiyu 8:28-34; Luka 8:26-39
Yeesu na̱ ana jwarigi buu aba ka̱ciga̱ni hira̱ree na rwaga na o̱to̱ na shi ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Agarasa̱na.
Na Yeesu be̱e̱ naa ca̱a̱n na̱ hantun na ma̱ni, kuuyaan butu ta naa mꞌbaa bihwaanwun naa we̱ bwa báni paa aba ta naa wuma̱a̱na̱ awyatu, bwa ꞌya̱pa̱a̱ buu.
Bubwa butu butanaa rota̱ga̱ paa abotubotu na aba ta naa wuma̱a̱na̱ wyatu. Bwa za naa nii gura̱a̱ ara ta̱kadaga bwa, koo na̱ akaca,
na̱ wana mahwarapi aba ka̱da̱a̱gi bwa nꞌara na̱ mꞌbuna na̱ akaca na̱ nꞌta̱ruma buhwii wyan ta̱ka̱kasa. Bwa za naa nii ara ta̱swa hyuhyu ndaabwa mayaan.
Koya̱ hwe̱n na̱ gita bunaa riinshina̱ paaku suꞌuya̱ na̱ paaku nꞌundu na nꞌtari, ma taga ta̱ꞌungwa, ma mahuwa̱ ta̱maꞌyapaga ta̱ꞌwaba na̱ atari.
Na bwa bwé̱e̱ yishe, bwa nda̱i Yeesu be̱ tutu, sa̱i bwa hiiki na̱ asumo̱, bwa ja̱a̱, bwa ta̱ runrun na̱ aꞌuba̱ nde̱e̱be̱.
Bwa butu bwa ta̱ ta̱ꞌungwa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ kai, <<Yeesu Buyoo Hwe̱n na Hura̱gi Ta̱ꞌo̱to̱! Nꞌnda̱i ruwa ndaa na̱ ga̱mi? Iiro̱pe̱ na̱ nꞌruzha̱a̱ naru Hwe̱n, ta-mꞌpa ngwan.>>
Bucici kunnu na̱ wana Yeesu hoo hyan bwa, <<Gaa bihwaanwun naa we̱, mahooshi na̱ butu yata!>>
Yeesu be̱ ha̱nta̱ni be̱, <<Imbata shi ruzha̱a̱ rundaabi?>>
Sa̱i bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Ruzha̱a̱ runiimi Bigudu na̱ wana ga̱tu hwarapi ta ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ na butu na̱nna.>>
Sa̱i bwaa rupa Yeesu ji, xbita pa wyan sumo̱ na̱ mꞌba nꞌguwa.
Do̱ko̱ nꞌkaba, suyaan sudo̱n nasu ina suhwarapi sutanaa kaun ma re̱ ta̱re̱e̱ nii biin binaa undu.
Mꞌba hwaanwun na nꞌwe̱, mꞌba ro̱pe̱ Yeesu, <<xTa̱ga̱a̱ ta̱ja̱a̱ paaku sudo̱n nasu ina, ta̱ta̱ni suun.>>
Yeesu be̱ pa̱ni muu nu, nꞌhwaanwun na nꞌwe̱ mꞌba ba̱ni kuubwa butu, mꞌba ta̱ni sudo̱n. Suba sudo̱n suba tanaa adubu ree, suba hiiki na̱ nꞌsumo̱, suba huri cuun kusha̱ru na undu suba mazooni na̱ rwaga na o̱to̱, suba gura̱kakani ma̱ni, suba hwii ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱.
Na ana tahambe̱ sudo̱n nasu ina ba nda̱i kunta, aba gida̱ga̱gi, aba ja̱a̱ aba bísa̱gi awyatu na ce̱pe̱ ndaaba na̱ ana mꞌbiin na nꞌce̱pe̱. Awyatu aba bánai xanda̱i iri na nje̱.
Na aba jaa paa Yeesu, aba nda̱i butu naa bigudu naa awyatu na hira̱ aba tajwara̱ga bwa taa hunrani na̱ aha̱nka̱ri ndaabwa ka̱, bwa taani da̱bi. Hyo̱ ndaaba aba hange̱ rukwanyan.
Too, ana ba tanda nꞌsuyishe sundaaba, abaa bisa̱ga̱ awyatu haruwa na iri na nje̱ na̱ butu naa taꞌmꞌbaa awyatu na hira̱, na̱ iri na nje̱ na̱ nꞌsudo̱n nasu ina.
Sa̱i aba wyatu aba ke̱ne̱ ta̱naa rupa Yeesu ta̱hyan xbiga̱a̱gi wyan pa̱ri kandaaba.
Na Yeesu be̱e̱ ta̱na̱ hantun na ma̱ni, sa̱i butu naa taꞌmꞌbaa awyatu na hira̱ bwa ro̱pe̱ Yeesu ta̱hyan xahurogo da̱nda̱ na̱a̱ bwa.
Ama Yeesu be̱ ga̱a̱, be̱ hin bwa, <<Hura̱ giyo ina kawyatu ndaa na̱ adiindiin ndaa, u-bishi wyan iri na o̱to̱ na Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n bwaa ndaaki na̱ kuubwa hange̱ mbishiri ndaa.>>
Sa̱i bwa butu bwa huri, bwa ke̱ne̱ ta̱bisa̱ga̱ awyatu kuta̱ꞌyapa nata̱ Ace̱pe̱ Upwa hyo̱ iri na Yeesu be̱ ndaaki bwa. Hyo̱ awyatu aba jikita̱ni.
Buyoo Yaarisu na̱a̱ a̱ naa a̱nta̱ni da̱bi na Yeesu
Maatiyu 9:18-26; Luka 8:40-56
Na Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni, be̱ kwashe̱e̱ke̱ ta̱kacigana hira̱ree na rwaga na o̱to̱. Bigudu naa awyatu hwarapi aba mawuna̱ni waabe̱ na̱ inza̱n na rwaga.
Sa̱i buyaan butu o̱to̱ naa ka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya, ruzha̱a̱ rundaabwa Yaarisu, bwa jaa kaun. Na bwa nda̱i Yeesu, bwa mata̱ pa̱m do̱ko̱ na̱ mꞌbuna nꞌnde̱e̱be̱,
bwaa rupa buu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ma hyaan, <<Be̱e̱ biniimi naa a̱ naa njeke nii nda na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwa̱. Kusu jaa, u-sha̱a̱gi buu nꞌara, u-kuda̱gahini buu, bikúshe̱e̱ wuma.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ huri na̱a̱ bwa, bigudu naa awyatu be̱ jwarigi buu ma masuka.
Buyaan buꞌa̱ tanaa naa tanda nꞌyo̱ nꞌupwa na̱ ree ma zoo mahiin.
Bwa taswa ngwan ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ majabaga paa kawyatu na njibi hwarapi, bwa hwii ri ndaabwa tawyashika paa wyanzun na njibi. Bwa kwade̱ge̱ce̱ nꞌsuguma, subaa duwa̱na̱ kuta̱duwa̱na̱.
Butahoo ha̱nga mazama nama Yeesu, na̱ wana kunnu, sa̱i bwa gii nꞌta̱baa nata̱ Yeesu na̱ ame̱ naa gudu naa awyatu, bwa a̱nta̱ni da̱bi nde̱e̱be̱,
bwa maga̱gaaga nii gata ndaabwa ta̱hyan, <<Koo uda̱bi nde̱e̱be̱ ga̱n a̱nta̱ni, nꞌnii kuda̱ga.>>
Kupita mahiin maba ꞌya̱pi ta̱naa zoo, bwaa a̱ bwa hange̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabwa bukwade̱ge̱.
Yeesu be̱ hange̱ kunrun ta̱kai nata̱ ta̱kuda̱gahina ta̱ba̱ni ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱nde̱e̱be̱, sa̱i be̱ ke̱ce̱e̱ke̱ kiigudu naa wyatu, be̱ hin, <<Iyaa ta a̱nta̱ni da̱bi nimi?>>
Ana jwarigi buu, aba hin, <<Gwatana u-nda̱i bina̱nna gudu naa nii masuka ma mafundata, gaa uhin, <Iyaa ta nꞌa̱nta̱ni?> >>
Ama Yeesu be̱e̱ gwataagana ji xbinda̱i bunaa nje̱ be̱ ri.
Too, bubwaa a̱ yan iri na nje̱ na̱a̱ bwa. Bwa báni na̱ nꞌrukwanyan ma jikita̱, bwa mata̱ pa̱m na̱ aꞌuba̱ nde̱e̱be̱, bwa bishi buu iri na bwa ndagi hyo̱.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin bwaa a̱, <<Be̱e̱ biniimi, ta̱panaa gata ndaabi kuga̱mi ta̱a̱biha̱ni. Hura̱ gumunu, bi-kwade̱ge̱ na̱ nꞌsuguma sundaabi.>>
Bitaꞌuuta̱ncin nu na̱a̱ bwaa a̱, katuma aba wuce kuꞌina na Yaarisu, aba hin, <<Ta-maa biwya̱ra̱mi ngwan ꞌye̱n, da̱du ndaa hoo ꞌwa̱.>>
Ama Yeesu be̱ gwatancin iri na aba cici, sa̱i be̱ hin Yaarisu, <<Ta-ha̱nga rukwanyan, sha̱a̱ kiigata.>>
Be̱ hakacici koo buyaan bujwara̱ga buu, sa̱i ku-Biituru na̱ Yaakubu na̱ Yoohana buya̱na̱ naa Yaakubu.
Na aba wuci ina na Yaarisu, Yeesu be̱ nda̱i awyatu yimo̱ yimo̱ na̱ nꞌungwa ma taagana sunu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Be̱ ta̱ni me̱ na ina, be̱ hin awyatu, <<Iba̱ shani ga̱hin nꞌgaaga ma taagana nu kunnu? Ai, be̱e̱ biꞌwici, nꞌrabi nꞌta be̱ taa.>>
Hyo̱ bibe̱e̱ gudu be̱e̱ ꞌwa̱ buu ratu na nꞌhwashe̱. Sa̱i be̱ sha̱pi ashin na̱ aya̱na̱ na be̱e̱, na̱ ana jwarigi buu taatu, be̱ ta̱ni paakii bibe̱e̱ bibe̱ taa.
Be̱ kota̱ni ara na be̱e̱, be̱ hin buu, <<Taliita kumi,>> ane̱e̱ ta̱hyan, <<Be̱e̱ binaa njeke, hiika̱.>>
Kupita be̱e̱ bibe̱ hiiki, be̱e̱ hura̱ ta̱hani. Nꞌyo̱ nꞌnde̱e̱be̱ nꞌupwa na̱ nꞌree. Ubwa ri bwa shani wyan aba jikita̱ni ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ aba nje̱ kuma̱.
Yeesu be̱ kooci wyan ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ta̱hyan xbuyaan buta ha̱nga ri na nje̱. Sa̱i be̱ hin xapa̱ buu shami.

Aga̱a̱ Yeesu na̱ Naazare
Maatiyu 13:53-58; Luka 4:16-30
Yeesu be̱ ga̱a̱ kaun, be̱ huri ce̱pe̱ nde̱e̱be̱ Naazare huku na̱ ana jwarigi.
Na hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya bwa wuce, be̱ ke̱ne̱ ta̱naa ga̱gaagana na̱ ka̱ta̱ku ndaaba, hyo̱ ana shiraagi buu awyatu hwarapi aba hin baka na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ ma hantaana, <<Pe̱kata butu na̱nna bwa díbe̱ ina̱nna ri? Ya̱ ta̱yansun ta̱nu aba pa̱ni buu nuunu, na be̱e̱ ndaga iri na ta̱jikita̱na̱ kunnu?
Shii be̱ taa shi busha̱bi yata, buyoo Maariyamu, buya̱na̱a̱ba naa Yaakubu, na̱ Yusufu, na̱ Yaahuda, na̱ Siima? Kuꞌaya̱na̱ba na a̱ na huku na̱ ga̱tu?>> Abaa fukaa gata nii be̱.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Ata pa bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama hunrun kope, ama shii na̱ ce̱pe̱ ndaabwa na̱ adiin ndaabwa.>>
Na̱ wana ta̱pa̱ncin nꞌgata ndaaba, Yeesu be̱ a̱rici ta̱nda yaan ri na ta̱jikita̱na̱ kaun hwarapi, sa̱i be̱ ca̱guda̱a̱ga̱gi kawyatu hamba nꞌara ana ha̱ngagici sa̱, be̱ kuda̱gahini wyan.
Be̱ jikita̱ni na̱ wana ta̱pa̱ncin nꞌgata ndaaba.
Yeesu ka̱ji upwa na ree ana be̱ tazwara
Maatiyu 10:5-15; Luka 9:1-6
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ jwara̱gagani nꞌcice̱pe̱ na nꞌnjeke ma ga̱gaagana wyatu.
Sa̱i be̱ nꞌgani aꞌupwa na ree ana be̱ tazwara, be̱ ka̱da̱gi wyan tuma aba ree ree, be̱ pa̱ga̱ni wyan ta̱kai nata̱ ta̱ba̱ha̱na̱ nꞌhwaanwun na nꞌwe̱.
Be̱ bishi wyan, <<Ta-shapa ma iyaan ri na̱ wana ta̱ba ta̱hani, koo ka̱fu koo shami koo ayuwa nꞌruzupi, sa̱i kangwo na ta̱hani.
Ama ibwa̱ta̱ni akandaga, ta-shapa ma uyaan da̱bi nata̱ hiriga, haruwa kuna ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwaba ta̱niinhin.
Hyo̱ paa ga̱hin ja̱a̱, ta-hiriga ma ina na ga̱hin te̱ne̱, kuha̱ni na ga̱hin bana ubwa ce̱pe̱.
Ama hyo̱ paa abaa ga̱a̱ ma koo abaa shiragici ma, kiinii bana kaun, ibukuta̱gi aputu na mꞌbuna niinhin, ta shi ibisa̱a̱ wyan ta̱hyan aꞌmꞌbaa suuga̱ ku-Hwe̱n.>>
Kunnu aba hura̱gi ma bisa̱ga̱ awyatu ta̱hyan xapa̱ni pinsan baa.
Abaa ba̱ha̱na̱a̱ nꞌhwaanwun na nꞌwe̱ nꞌhwarapi, abaa shanaa ana ha̱ngagici sa̱ mariga̱ na̱ hyuhyu, aba kuda̱gahinai wyan.
Ta̱ꞌwa̱ nata̱ Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma
Maatiyu 14:1-12; Luka 9:7-9
Bugwama Hirudu Antipasi bwa hange̱ mazama nama Yeesu, na̱ wana kope kanii cita̱ga̱ mazama mande̱e̱be̱, aka̱ abaa hyaan, <<Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma tahíike kuta̱ꞌwa̱, ta shani bwaa ndaga iri nata̱ jikita̱na̱.>>
Aka̱ abaa hyaan, <<Bunaa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Iliya ta.>> Ama aka̱ baa hyaan, <<Aaꞌa, buyaan bunaa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ta naa hasaa.>>
Na Hirudu bwa hange̱ mazama nama Yeesu, bwa hin, <<Yoohana na ga̱n tahoo ꞌyapa hyuhyu nu híike kuta̱ꞌwa̱.>>
Na ta̱hyan Hirudu tapana nu xakota̱ni Yoohana, azwa̱ga̱ni bwa na̱ zhaaro. Butanda kunnu na̱ wana xbucaanhini Hiruudiya me̱, bunaa Hirudu bwa tazhaa. Butasha aꞌa̱yoo ya̱na̱ naa o̱to̱ Filibu.
Yoohana tanaa bisa̱ga̱ Hirudu ta̱hyan, <<Uzumaancin u-zha̱a̱ aꞌa̱yo yami ku-Nꞌgira̱nshin nda̱a̱tu mꞌba hin.>>
Bibe̱ Hiruudiya tanaa fukaa gata na̱ Yoohana, be̱ ribi xbikwane̱ bwa, ama be̱ de̱be̱ce̱ ha̱ba̱,
na̱ wana Hirudu shiragi rukwanyan naru Yoohana, bwa yan ta̱hyan bushi butu naa bina̱, bunaa ta̱sabu. Uya̱nu bwa shani Hirudu bwa ha̱mba̱gi Yoohana ki. Utakaka be̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ hyo̱ ha̱ni na Yoohana bwaa nda mazama na̱a̱ bwa, ama hyo̱ na̱ kunnu butaha̱nga masuunran nama ta̱shiraga mazama mandaabwa.
Hiruudiya tada̱ba ha̱ba̱ na̱ hwe̱n na ta̱matamanrinyan ta̱ma̱ncin nata̱ Hirudu, na bwa tanda buki na̱ wana nꞌgwama na nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ ta̱ndaabwa na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na asooja na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na Gaalili.
Be̱e̱ binaa Hiruudiya naa a̱ be̱ nje̱ ta̱hibwa, Hirudu na̱ agai ndaabwa aba hange̱ gama ta̱ꞌo̱to̱. Sa̱i bugwama bwa hin be̱e̱ bibe̱e̱, <<Iba̱ gaa ribi? Hyo̱ iri na gaa ribi nꞌha̱nta̱ni wuun, iipa̱ni.>>
Hyo̱ na̱ nꞌta̱taa sa̱nsan, ta̱hyan, <<Hyo̱ iri na gaa ribi nꞌha̱nta̱ni, nꞌna̱maa pana wuun, koo ushi ta̱bware̱ nata̱ ta̱gwama ta̱niimi.>>
Sa̱i be̱ huri be̱ hin aya̱na̱, <<Iba̱ ga̱n hantana?>>
Aya̱na̱ aba hin, <<Uhyuhyu na Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma.>>
Be̱ he̱e̱n kwashe̱e̱kwa kunrun paakuu gwama be̱ hin, <<Nꞌribi niina niina mꞌpa̱ni uhyuhyu na Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma, u-cágudani wuun na̱ kada.>>
Na bugwama bwa hange̱ kunnu bwa hange̱ce̱ gama mahwa, ama wana usa̱nsan na bwa tahoo taa na̱ aꞌuba̱ na agai ndaabwa bwa ribici buu ta̱yansan.
Sa̱i kunrun pita bwa ka̱ji usooja xbuja̱a̱ buꞌwaan hyuhyu na Yoohana. Bwa sooja bwa ja̱a̱ bwa ꞌyápi hyuhyu na Yoohana na̱ zhaaro,
bwa ꞌwaan wuun na̱ kada, bwa cikaa be̱e̱ bibe̱e̱, be̱ sha̱pi, be̱ ja̱a̱ aya̱na̱.
Na ana jwarigi Yoohana aba hange̱ iri na nje̱, aba jaa, aba sha̱pi ruꞌwa̱ rundaabwa, aba wuma̱ni.
Yeesu pa̱ awyatu dubu ta shami
Maatiyu 14:13-21; Luka 9:10-17; Yoohana 6:1-14
Atumashini upwa na ree ana Yeesu be̱ takadaga tuma aba kúshe̱ waabe̱, aba bisa̱gi buu hyo̱ iri na aba ndági na̱ iri na aba gá̱gaagani wyatu.
Na ta̱hyan awyatu nii suruta̱ka̱ku, aka̱ ma jábagi, aka̱ ma kushiikaka, ubwa shani aba de̱be̱ce̱ ha̱ni na hyan are̱ shami, sa̱i be̱ hin wyan, <<xTa̱huri ma paa kaza koo buyaan wana hyan iha̱nka̱ni.>>
Sa̱i aba ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni, aba huri paa kaza koo butu kaba baa ka̱.
Ama awyatu hwarapi ana tandaya wyan ma hura̱ aba e̱nshe̱n paa aba huri, aba bánai kuꞌnꞌcice̱pe̱ ma raan inza̱n na rwaga na o̱to̱ na̱ nꞌsumo̱, aba re̱ge̱ wyan ta̱wuta̱.
Yeesu ma ca̱a̱n na̱ inza̱n, be̱ nda̱i awyatu hyamu aba hoo mawuna̱na̱, sa̱i be̱ hange̱ ambishiri ndaaba na̱ wana ane̱e̱ haki ka̱ra̱bi na zaa iyo̱. Sa̱i be̱ ke̱ne̱ wyan ta̱ga̱gaagana iri hwarapi.
Na̱ uha̱ni na hwe̱n bwa goki ta̱ꞌira̱ sa̱i ana jwarigi aba jaa waabe̱, aba hin buu, <<Pina kashi mbaa paaka za butu, uhwe̱n ta ubwa ke̱ne̱ ta̱ꞌira̱.
Cipana wyatu xaja̱ba̱gi paaku nꞌcice̱pe̱ na̱ nꞌina na nꞌnaanyin pina do̱ko̱ amasáanwyain shami na hyan are̱gi.>>
Ama Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Ga̱hin pa ma wyan shami na xare̱.>>
Aba hin buu, <<Uya̱nu nii nda urwaru na tuma nꞌhwe̱n nꞌyina̱ nꞌree. Bi-ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan, ta̱sha̱pi ayuwa ya̱nu o̱to̱ ta̱kúne̱ wyan na̱ ishami na hyan ta̱pa̱ awyatu are̱?>>
Be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan, <<Aburoodi hamba ga̱hin mꞌbaa? Jaga gwátani ma.>>
Na aba gwátani, aba hin buu, <<Mꞌburoodi nꞌta na̱ nꞌjooshiipa nꞌree.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin ana jwarigi buu, xahin awyatu xamata̱gi nꞌgudu nꞌgudu ahunraana na̱ awyamu na ye̱nce̱n.
Sa̱i aba hunraani nꞌgudu nꞌgudu, aka̱ nꞌyina̱ nꞌka̱a̱ ka̱a̱, aka̱ kuje ta ta ta.
Yeesu be̱ sha̱pi mꞌba mꞌburoodi nꞌta na̱ nꞌjooshiipa nꞌree, be̱ ka̱cihini ayishe da̱da̱da̱, be̱ gooji Hwe̱n, be̱ ya̱biza̱gi, be̱e̱ pagana ana jwarigi buu xahoosa̱ga̱ni awyatu. Be̱ gura̱a̱ hoosa̱ga̱ga̱ hyo̱ mꞌba nꞌjooshiipa nꞌree kaba wyatu.
Hyo̱ koo buya̱ bwa re̱, bwa cigi haruwa na gii bwa.
Na aba hwii, ana jwarigi aba wuna̱a̱ni aburoodi na̱ nꞌjooshiipa na mꞌbwe̱ nꞌtumunsun nꞌupwa na̱ nꞌree da̱a̱da̱a̱.
Uhwarapi na ana tare̱ bwa shami, awyatu wya̱ri kaba, adubu ta.
Yeesu nje̱ ta̱hani na̱ da̱da̱da̱ na ma̱ni
Maatiyu 14:22-33; Yoohana 6:15-21
Kunrun na̱ bwa ha̱ni Yeesu be̱ shani ana jwarigi buu aba ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni xanaa hura̱na̱ buu kacigana zhagu Batasaida, be̱ ma cipana awyatu.
Na be̱ hwii wyan ta̱cipana, sa̱i be̱ ka̱ta̱ni yaan undu na hyan xbinje̱ ro̱pe̱.
Na hwe̱n bwa iri, uhantun bwa ne̱e̱ na̱ awyantancin na ma̱ni, Yeesu be̱ tane̱e̱ na̱ undu be̱e̱ ka̱.
Be̱ nda̱i anii mapa dibi na̱ nꞌta̱naa mana hantun na̱ wana upyara yanshin wyan ta̱hura̱. Uha̱ni na ta̱ruma ta̱taatu nata̱ gita, be̱e̱ njé̱e̱ ta̱hani da̱da̱da̱ na ma̱ni nama rwaga na o̱to̱ zhagu waaba, be̱ nje̱ kiihiin ta ta̱hura̱ iyeebe ndaaba.
Ama na aba nda̱i buu ma hura̱ da̱da̱da̱ na ma̱ni, aba ta̱ ta̱ꞌungwa nata̱ rukwanyan ta̱hyan koo upataruwa ta.
Hyo̱ aba tanaa jikita̱ga̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na aba nda̱i buu.
Sa̱i be̱ nje̱ mazama na̱ bwa ha̱ni, be̱ hin wyan, <<Ta ma kiishita̱. Ga̱n ta. Ta-ha̱nga ma rukwanyan.>>
Too, sa̱i be̱ ta̱ni hantun, upyara bwa nje̱ fo̱n. Sa̱i aba nje̱ ma̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱,
na̱ wana ayancin koo imbata shi ta̱pa awyatu dubu ta shami ibe̱ bisa̱a̱. Nꞌgata nꞌndaaba nꞌne̱e̱ nꞌta̱yincincin.
Yeesu kuda̱gahini awyatu na ha̱ngagici sa̱ na̱ Janiisarata
Maatiyu 14:34-36
Na Yeesu na̱ ana jwarigi buu aba hwii ta̱kaata rwaga na o̱to̱, aba ciin na̱ Janiisarata, aba ka̱da̱gi hantun na̱ inza̱n na rwaga na o̱to̱.
Kuta̱naa bana ta̱ndaaba na̱ hantun na ma̱ni, sa̱i awyatu ba e̱nshe̱n ta̱hyan Yeesu ta.
Aba ke̱ne̱ nꞌsumo̱ ma shápagi awyatu ana ha̱ngagici sa̱ na̱ iri na taa taa ndaaba hyo̱ na̱ o̱to̱ na ta̱ba ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱, paa aba hange̱ Yeesu ne̱e̱.
Hyo̱ paa be̱ huri, ace̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ na̱ nꞌcice̱pe̱ na nꞌnjeke koo mꞌbiin na nꞌce̱pe̱, ma rota̱a̱ga̱ awyatu na ha̱ngagici sa̱ paaku awyatu aba ta mawuna̱ni, aro̱pe̱ buu na̱ wana hyan ana ha̱ngagici sa̱ xaꞌa̱nta̱a̱ni koo bibiin binaa da̱bi nde̱e̱be̱ na o̱to̱. Hyo̱ ana a̱nta̱a̱ni aba kuda̱gagi.

Nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌawyatu o̱to̱
Maatiyu 15:1-9
Uyaan hwe̱n ree na nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na̱ Afaraasiya aba jaa Hurushaliima na hyan anda̱i Yeesu.
Sa̱i aba shii aha̱nka̱ri ki, aba nda̱i ta̱hyan aka̱ ana jwarigi Yeesu aga̱a̱ ta̱jwara̱ga nꞌgira̱nshin ndaaba, wana ta̱hyan ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ u-shikici ara gaa hiin re̱ shami.
Na ta̱hyan Afaraasiya na̱ ayaan Ayaahudiya aꞌa̱cii re̱ shami sa̱i kubutu shikici ara sabu kuꞌnꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌawyatu o̱to̱ ndaaba mꞌba hin.
Kagiya̱gi kasuwa ajaa re̱ kwan shami sa̱i kamaha̱mba̱ra̱gi. Aba gura̱a̱ mꞌbaa nꞌyaan nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌaba sha̱pi, haku ha̱mbaragi na nꞌjogo na̱ agwara na̱ nꞌga̱ga̱ri.
Sa̱i Afaraasiya na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin aba ha̱nta̱ni Yeesu ta̱hyan, <<Iba̱ shani anaa jwarigi aba jwarigici nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌawyatu o̱to̱, na abaa re̱ shami na shikita̱gici nꞌara sabu?>>
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<To̱n ta kuga̱hin awyatu na za mahanda, Ishaaya bwa tanda tuma na ta̱cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, kuubwa ta̱gi muu ta̱hyan, Uhwe̱n hin,
<< <Awyatu na̱nna ana̱maꞌmꞌpaga hunrun kuna̱ nu,
ama nꞌgata nꞌndaaba nꞌne̱e̱ tutu na̱ ga̱mi.
ꞌYe̱n ta abaa mꞌpaga hunrun.
Anii ga̱gaagana awyatu nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌwyatu wuma,
ta̱hyan anii ga̱gaagana Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n.>
Iga̱a̱ iri na Hwe̱n bwa hin xinje̱, ta ga̱hin jwarigi nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌwyatu wuma.>>
Sa̱i be̱ hin wyan, <<Inda̱i ta̱hyan iꞌa̱ri ta̱munsan Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n, na̱ wana hyan ide̱be̱ ha̱ba̱ nata̱ jwara̱ga nꞌniinhin.
Suta̱hyan ku-Muusa bwa tahyan, <Cina̱na̱ abaaba ndaa na̱ ada̱a̱da̱ ndaa,> be̱ gura̱a̱ hyan, <Hyo̱ bunaa cwaagani ashin koo aya̱na̱ ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ akwane̱ be̱.>
Ama ga̱hin hin uzumaa butu hin aya̱na̱ koo ashin, <Re̱ kuri, hyo̱ iri na gaa tahiin da̱ba wa̱ka̱mi nꞌhoo pe̱e̱n wuun na hyan ma pana Hwe̱n.>
Na̱ kunnu iyanshin wyan ta̱pana ana ma̱ncin wyan iri na abaa wyanzan.
Na̱ kunnu ta ga̱hin tahe̱e̱n iga̱a̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n, na̱ wana nꞌgira̱nshin nꞌniinhin na nꞌga̱hin ga̱gaagana mꞌmwaan nꞌniinhin. Kunta ta ga̱hin gura̱a̱ ndaga iri hwarapi.>>
Iri na nii ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ butu kaꞌuba̱ na Hwe̱n
Maatiyu 15:10-20
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ gura̱a̱ nꞌgana awyatu, be̱ hin wyan, <<Nꞌshiraga ma hyo̱ ninhin, iꞌe̱nshe̱n ki.
Shii iri na ta̱ni na̱ ame̱ na butu ina sa̱ra̱ri tanii ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ bwa na̱ aꞌuba̱ na Hwe̱n, sa̱i kina báni na̱ ame̱ na butu tanii ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ bwa.>>+ :15 Ta̱taga ta̱ka̱ nata̱ yigo ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa aaya na 16 kunna: Hyo̱ bunaa mꞌbaa ce̱be̱ na ta̱tuba̱ xbutibi.Na Yeesu be̱ ga̱a̱ bibe̱e̱ gudu, be̱ ta̱ni ina, ana jwarigi buu aba ha̱nta̱ni buu iri na ta̱ba ta̱kun ta̱ba shi.
Be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Ga̱hin taa iꞌe̱nshe̱nshe̱n? Iyancin ta̱hyan iri na ta̱ni ame̱ na butu ina sa̱ra̱ri iꞌa̱cii ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ butu ku-Hwe̱n?
Ishami a̱cii ta̱na̱ nii gata naa butu, ita ta̱na̱ kuta̱mba̱ra̱, ijaa ba̱ni na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabwa.>> (Na̱ nꞌta̱cita̱ kunnu, Yeesu be̱ bisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan koya̱ shami ishi iri na ta̱sabu kaꞌuba̱ na Hwe̱n.)
Be̱ re̱ iyeebe macita̱ga̱ ta̱hyan, <<Iri na nii bánai na̱ ame̱ na butu, ibe̱ ta shi na ta ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ butu.
Na̱ wana ta̱hyan nii gata naa butu ta iri ibe̱ tanaa bánai suta̱hyan, mazama nama we̱, na̱ wyanzun na aꞌa̱ na ta̱wya̱ri, na̱ zumba̱, na̱ nꞌta̱kunaa yaan, na̱ banshaun,
na̱ nꞌta̱ruba̱ ri ma̱, na̱ nꞌta̱sha butu naa we̱, na̱ nꞌta̱sha bupunsun, na̱ banshaun da̱shi, na̱ nꞌta̱ribici ayami mꞌbaa, na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ buyaan ruzha̱a̱, na̱ nꞌta̱mashapaciga, na̱ nꞌta̱sha guzha̱ni.
Hyo̱ iri ya̱nu na we̱, ita naa bánai nii gata, ibe̱ ta ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ butu.>>
Ta̱panaa gata nata̱a̱ yaan buꞌa̱ bunaa shici Buyaahudiya
Maatiyu 15:21-28
Na̱ nꞌkaba Yeesu be̱ hiiki, be̱ ga̱a̱ Gaalili, be̱ huri zuba na ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Taaya. Bitaribici xbuyaan buyansun ina na be̱ ne̱e̱ na̱ bwa, hyo̱ na̱ kunnu ubwa nje̱ce̱.
-26 Buyaan buꞌa̱ bwa jaa waabe̱. Bwaa a̱ tashici Buyaahudiya. Ata mantan bwa na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Finikiya na̱ ame̱ na ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Suuriya. Be̱e̱ bindaabwa naa njeke naa a̱, butu naa hira̱ naa we̱ bwa jwarigi buu. Na bwa hange̱ mazama nama Yeesu, kupita bwa jaa bwa ta̱ runrun kuuhiin mata pa̱m kuꞌmꞌbuna nꞌnde̱e̱be̱. Sa̱i bwa ro̱pe̱ Yeesu xbiba̱ha̱ni bubwa butu naa hira̱ naa we̱ kiibe̱e̱ bibe̱e̱.
Yeesu be̱ hin bwaa a̱, <<xMꞌmwaan nꞌre̱gi kwan nꞌciga̱gi, uzumaancin asha̱pi shami na mꞌmwaan abwaagagi suwa+ :27 suwa: Hyo̱ bunaa shici Buyaahudiya, Ayaahudiya asha̱pi be̱ bushi haka wa.mꞌmwaan mꞌba taciga̱gici.>>
Ama bwaa a̱ bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, kunnu mꞌba shi, ama suwa suta taan nꞌwuzu na nꞌnii kinaa paaku mꞌmwaan mꞌbaa re̱ shami.>>
Sa̱i be̱ hin bwaa a̱, <<Na̱ wana bi-ra̱ni kunnu, giya̱ ina. Butu naa hira̱ mahooshi na̱ aya̱bi.>>
Na bwa kwashe̱e̱ke̱ ina, bwa wuta̱ni be̱e̱ bindaabwa taa na̱ wyansun wau, butu naa hira̱ bwa hoo bana.
Yeesu kuda̱gahini wo̱nro̱n
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ba̱ni kuta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Taaya, be̱ jwara̱gani Sidon, be̱ ja̱a̱ Rwaga na O̱to̱ na Gaalili. Na̱ bwa yo̱n be̱ wuce ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ ta̱yaan ce̱nye̱n nata̱ aba ta nꞌgana Ace̱pe̱ Upwa.
Ayaan wyatu aba iyaagi buu buyaan butu bunaa shi wo̱nro̱n, bwa ta cita̱ mazama dike̱, aba ro̱pe̱ Yeesu xbisha̱a̱ta̱a̱gi bwa nꞌara, bikuda̱gahini bwa.
Yeesu be̱ ma̱ni wo̱nro̱n nii inro̱n bwaa ka̱, be̱ cikaa mꞌmbwa nꞌnde̱e̱be̱ na ce̱be̱ ndaabwa, be̱ tupa̱ni macimi nii mbwa nde̱e̱be̱, be̱ ta̱a̱ni bwa na̱ re̱ntun ndaabwa.
Sa̱i be̱ ka̱cihini hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, be̱ ciinha̱ni nꞌhunjo̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, be̱ hin bwa, <<Ipata!>> Bine̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan, <<Guna̱a̱!>>
Kupita bwa wo̱nro̱n bwa tibi mazama, iri na taha̱mba̱ga̱ re̱ntun ndaabwa ibe̱ ta̱zhiga̱ni, bwa a̱ri ta̱naa cita̱ga̱ mazama ki.
Yeesu be̱ kooci bigudu ta̱hyan xata bisa̱ koo buyaan, ama be̱ ma yansaan wyan, aba ma duwa̱na̱ kuta̱naa wyasa mꞌba mazama.
Awyatu aba jikita̱ni, abaa hyaan ji, <<Kai, binje̱ komba̱ri to̱n, na be̱ shani ana ta tibici mazama na̱ ayigo ta aba tibi, ana taꞌa̱rici mazama na̱ ayigo ta aba a̱ri ta̱naa cita̱ga̱.>>

Yeesu pa̱ wyatu dubu na̱nshin shami
Maatiyu 15:32-39
Bike̱nye̱n be̱ ta̱ci du, bigudu naa awyatu hwarapi be̱ gura̱a̱ mawuna̱na̱. Wana ta̱hyan iri na ta̱re̱ za, Yeesu be̱ nꞌgani ana jwarigi buu waabe̱, be̱ hin wyan,
<<Ga̱n hange̱ ambishiri na wyatu na̱nna na̱ wana nꞌhwe̱n nꞌtaatu na aba ne̱e̱ na̱ ga̱mi, aba za iri na bwe̱ na hyan are̱.
Kunhin wyan xahuri giyo kunta nꞌrumunro̱n, nꞌnje̱ce̱ to̱n, xata jaa kinai na̱ yo̱n wana aka̱ abáni paaka me̱mi.>>
Ana jwarigi aba ra̱ni, aba hin, <<Pee shami be̱ nii da̱ba na̱ ahira̱ yana ina nii jwasu wyatu na̱nna?>>
Yeesu be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Mꞌburoodi hamba ga̱hin mꞌbaa?>>
Aba hin, <<Nꞌta̱nda̱ra̱.>>
Be̱ bishi bigudu naa awyatu xahunraana na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n. Na be̱ sha̱pi mꞌba mꞌburoodi ta̱nda̱ra̱, be̱ gooji Hwe̱n, be̱ ya̱biza̱gi muu, be̱ pa̱ga̱ni ana jwarigi buu xahoosa̱ga̱ni wyatu, aba nje̱ kunnu.
Aba gura̱a̱ mꞌbaa nꞌjooshiipa nꞌhamba na nꞌnjeke. Be̱ gooji Hwe̱n, be̱ pa̱ga̱ni ana jwarigi buu xahoosa̱ga̱ni wyan.
Awyatu aba re̱, aba ciga̱gi, naazhin ana jwarigi buu aba wuna̱ni na bwa̱ci nꞌtumunsun na nꞌo̱to̱ nꞌta̱nda̱ra̱.
Hwarapi na wyatu na tare̱, atanda adubu na̱nshin. Naazhin Yeesu be̱ cipani wyan.
Kunrun kunrun be̱ ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni, huku na̱ ana jwarigi buu, be̱ ka̱a̱ci zhagu ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Dalamanuta.
Wyanzun na iri na ta̱jikita̱na̱
Maatiyu 12:38-42; 16:1-4
Na Afaraasiya aba hange̱ Yeesu wuce, aba jaa aba pa̱shi ta̱nda kuda̱ga nii be̱. Aba ma̱a̱nwya̱ni Yeesu, aba ro̱pe̱ buu xbibisa̱a̱ wyan iri na ta̱jikita̱na̱ na hyan ayansun ta̱hyan Hwe̱n ne̱e̱ nii be̱.
Na be̱ hange̱ kunnu, be̱ hundani nꞌhunjo̱ na nꞌyaburi, be̱ hin, <<Na̱ wana ba̱ ga̱hin awyatu naa ke̱nye̱n yana ga̱hiin wyanzan ta̱ndaya iri na ta̱bisa̱a̱? Mahanda mata ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, iyaan iri za na aba na̱maa bisa̱a̱ ma.>>
Ha̱ni ya̱nu be̱ ga̱a̱ wyan kwan, be̱ ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni, be̱ ka̱ciga̱ni hira̱ree na rwaga na o̱to̱.
Ana jwarigi Yeesu e̱nshe̱nshe̱n mazama mande̱e̱be̱
Maatiyu 16:5-12
Ana jwarigi Yeesu aba háasani ta̱mapé̱e̱ buroodi, ama kuka̱ hwii aba taha̱mba̱gi paaku hantun na ma̱ni.
Yeesu be̱ kooci wyan, be̱ hin wyan, <<Mahooshi ma na̱ ayisiti na Afaraasiya na̱ ana Hirudu.>>
Ana jwarigi baa maga̱gaaga kaba kaba, abaa hyaan, <<Koo na̱ wana ta̱nza buroodi ta shani be̱ hin kunnu?>>
Yeesu be̱ e̱nshe̱n mazama nama abaa hyaan, be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan, <<Iba̱ shani ga̱hiin nda mazama ta̱hyan iza buroodi? Ka̱i! Ita e̱nshe̱nshe̱n? Ga̱hin ta yancin? Nꞌgata nꞌniinhin nꞌne̱e̱ nꞌta̱yincincin?
Iꞌmꞌbaa ayishe, ga̱hin nda̱ci? Ga̱hin mꞌbaa ace̱be̱, ga̱hin tibici? Ga̱hin mata̱ma̱nriincin
ha̱ni na mꞌburoodi nꞌta nꞌyata na ga̱n tahoosa̱ga̱na̱ awyatu adubu ta paa? Nꞌtumunsun nꞌhamba ga̱hin tawuna̱a̱na̱ ana tabwata?>>
Aba ra̱ni aba hin, <<Upwa na̱ nꞌreeko.>>
<<Mꞌburoodi nꞌta̱nda̱ra̱ yata na ga̱n tahoosa̱ga̱na̱ awyatu adubu na̱nshin, nꞌtumunsun nꞌhamba na nꞌo̱to̱ ga̱hin tawuna̱a̱ni ana tabwe̱?>>
Aba hin, <<Nꞌta̱nda̱ra̱.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Ita e̱nshe̱nshe̱n ji mazama maniimi?>>
Yeesu kuda̱gahini buruba̱ na̱ Batasaida
Aba wuce Batasaida, ayaan awyatu aba sháapi Yeesu buruba̱, aba ro̱pe̱ buu xbiꞌa̱nta̱ni bwaa ruba̱.
Be̱ kota̱ni ara ndaabwa, be̱ ra̱ga̱ni be̱, be̱ ba̱ha̱ni be̱ ta̱baa nata̱a̱ cice̱pe̱. Na be̱ ta̱a̱ni bwaa ruba̱ macimi na̱ ayishe, be̱ sha̱a̱gi be̱ nꞌara wana xbukwade̱ge̱. Be̱ ha̱nta̱ni be̱, be̱ hin, <<Bi-a̱ri ta̱ndaya yaanyini?>>
Bubwaa ruba̱ bwa ka̱cihini hyuhyu, bwa hin, <<Nꞌnii ndayaga awyatu ka̱i, ane̱e̱ haki ꞌwe̱e̱ abaa hura̱ga̱.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ gura̱a̱ sha̱a̱ga̱ be̱ nꞌara na̱ ayishe ndaabwa. Butu bwa gura̱a̱ fwara̱ga ayishe, ayishe ndaabwa aba kwade̱ge̱, bwa nda̱ya̱gi hyo̱ iri ki.
Yeesu be̱ cipani be̱ xbuhuri giyo ina, be̱ hin be̱, <<Kuu-huri giyo ta-ta̱na̱ bibe̱e̱ cice̱pe̱.>>
Biituru cici Yeesu shi Ala̱masiihu
Maatiyu 16:13-20; Luka 9:22-27
Yeesu na̱ ana jwarigi buu aba ga̱a̱ kaun, aba ta̱ni nꞌcice̱pe̱ na n-Kaisariya Filibi. Aba na̱ yo̱n, be̱ ha̱nta̱ni ana jwarigi buu, be̱ hin, <<Iyaa awyatu aba nii hyaan nꞌshi?>>
Aba ra̱ni buu, aba hin, <<Aka̱ nii hyaan gaa taa shi Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma, aka̱ aba nii hyaan gaa taa shi Iliya bunaa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, aka̱ aba nii gura̱a̱ hyaan gaa taa shi buyaan kacita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama.>>
Be̱ gura̱a̱ hantana wyan, be̱ hin, <<Ga̱hin paan? Iyaa ta ga̱hin hyaan nꞌshi?>>
Biituru bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Gaa taa shi Ala̱masiihu.>>
Yeesu be̱ kooci wyan xata bisa̱ koo buyaan ta̱hyan iyaa ta be̱ shi.
Yeesu cici haruwa na be̱e̱ ꞌwa̱
Maatiyu 16:21-28; Luka 9:22-27
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ pa̱shi ta̱bisa̱ga̱ wyan ta̱hyan ga̱ga̱ga̱ bwa Buyoo Butu bwaa swa ta̱guma koo ta̱ya̱, awyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya, na̱ apirisiti na o̱to̱, na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin, anii gaa buu. Ga̱ga̱ga̱ abaa kuna buu biꞌwi, na̱ hwe̱n na hin taatu bihiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱.
Na be̱ cita̱gi kunnu da̱shi kana jwarigi buu, Biituru bwa ra̱ga̱ni buu nii biin, bwaa hyaan buu hana xmata sha kunnu.
Yeesu be̱ ke̱ce̱e̱ke̱ kana jwarigi buu be̱ gwatani wyan, be̱ hin Biituru hana, <<Mahooshi na̱ ga̱mi, gaa Bupira̱! Gaa bu-nii ga̱gaaga kina shi na butu wuma, shii na Hwe̱n.>>
Na be̱ hin kunnu, sa̱i be̱ nꞌgani bigudu naa wyatu na̱ ana jwarigi buu do̱ko̱ waabe̱, be̱ hin wyan, <<Koo buya̱ naa nꞌribi ta̱ꞌnꞌjwara̱ga xbuga̱a̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa busha̱pi guguji ndaabwa na ta̱ꞌwa̱, buꞌnꞌjwara̱ga.
Bunaa ribi ta̱wungumana hyuhyu ndaabwa, buja̱a̱ci da̱ba wuun. Bunaa ga̱a̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa na̱ wana nimi na̱ wana mazama nama zumaa, buja̱a̱ da̱ba wuun.
Uya̱ funa̱ butu bwaa da̱ba, bwa de̱be̱ hyo̱ iri na sa̱ra̱ri yana, bwa jaa da̱ba ta̱nda bina̱ na mahwa?
Iba̱ butu bwaa ara ta̱pana Hwe̱n na hyan xbude̱be̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa?
Hyo̱ bunaa hange̱ nꞌkogi nꞌniimi, na̱ nꞌkogi na mꞌmazama maniimi, nii yana ke̱nye̱n naa za mꞌpirwa na̱ pinsan na̱ nꞌta̱gaa Hwe̱n, Buyoo Butu taa buja̱a̱ ha̱nga nꞌkogi nꞌndaabwa ha̱ni na bwaa wuce na̱ nꞌta̱shapaciga nata̱ Ashin Hwe̱n huku na̱ atuma ndaabwa ana ne̱e̱ sabu.>>

Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, aka̱ ne̱e̱ na isagi pina, ana jaa ꞌwa̱ga̱ sa̱i kanda̱i ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱wuce nꞌta̱kai!>>
Yeesu he̱re̱ge̱ mꞌpirwa
Maatiyu 17:1-13; Luka 9:28-36
Na nꞌhwe̱n cininhin mꞌba huri, Yeesu be̱ ra̱ga̱ni Biituru, na̱ Yaakubu, na̱ Yoohana, be̱ ꞌye̱e̱ wyan paaku yaan undu na za̱ka̱ri, aba ne̱e̱ kaun baa ka̱. Na aba ne̱e̱ piree, mꞌpirwa nꞌnde̱e̱be̱ mꞌba he̱re̱ge̱ na̱ aꞌuba̱ ndaaba,
aꞌwana nde̱e̱be̱ aba ba̱ni tande̱ manyan manyan, na ta̱hyan butu za naa nii ara ta̱ha̱mbara sabu kaba ne̱e̱ na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana.
Aba nda̱i kacita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Muusa na̱ Iliya, abaa nda mazama na̱ Yeesu.
Sa̱i Biituru bwa hin Yeesu, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, uhuri gama na ga̱tu ne̱e̱ pina, xta̱ta̱ nꞌdura̱ nꞌtaatu, bika̱ bindaabi, bika̱ binaa Muusa, bika̱ binaa Iliya.>>
Biituru hin kunnu na̱ wana ajikici ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, bwa yancin ri na hyan bucici.
Bunaa huwa̱ ta̱cita̱, kurara bwa guna̱ni wyan, aba hange̱ ta̱ꞌnꞌga na̱ arara ma hyaan, <<Buna̱nna bwa taa shi Baa buniimi, bunaa ga̱n hura̱gi ta̱ruba̱. Shiraga ma bwa.>>
Na aba gura̱a̱ gwatana, aba nda̱ci Muusa na̱ Iliya, kaba na̱ Yeesu aba bwa̱ci.
Na abaa cíin kuꞌundu bwa, Yeesu be̱ kooci wyan xata bisa̱ koo butu ri aba nda̱i, kuhwe̱n na Buyoo Butu bwa hiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱.
Aba shii muu nꞌsume̱ sundaaba, abaa mahantaana koo imba̱nu shi ta̱hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱.
Sa̱i aba ha̱nta̱ni buu, aba hin, <<Imba̱ shani nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin mꞌba hin, ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ Iliya kúshe̱, naazhin Ala̱masiihu jaa?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Mahanda manu, Iliya ta ja̱a̱ jaa yigo wana biꞌa̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni iri hyo̱. Too, mbata shi ta̱cita̱ ta̱yata nata̱ ta̱gi ta̱hin Buyoo Butu nii swa ta̱guma koo ta̱ya̱, abaa gaa buu mahwa, shii kunnunu?
Ai, Iliya hoo jaa, awyatu aba ndaaki buu ri na aba ribi, haruwa na aba tataga inii nda.>>
Yeesu kuda̱gahini baa bunaa bihwaanwun naa we̱
Maatiyu 17:14-21; Luka 9:37-43
Na Yeesu na̱ aba taatu aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱ paaka ana jwarigi, aba nda̱i bigudu naa yaburi riini wyan. Nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin mꞌbaa nda kuda̱ga na̱ aba.
Na aba nda̱i Yeesu, bigudu hyo̱ be̱ jikita̱ni ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, aba hiiki, aba mazooni na sumo̱ zhagu waabe̱ xazumani buu.
Yeesu be̱ ha̱nta̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Kuda̱ga na ba̱ ga̱hiin nda na̱ aba?>>
Kuuyaan butu paakii bigudu bwa hin, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, ga̱n na ga̱mii sháapi baa buniimi bunaa bihwaanwun naa we̱ be̱ yanshin be̱ mazama ta̱cita̱.
Ha̱ni na iri be̱ híike be̱, ita pa be̱ pwan na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n ma zhizhiba. Ita shana be̱ bunaa bana afucukwa na̱ nu, bunaa hinkinran aya̱n, ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabwa ta̱nje̱ ga̱gau. Ga̱n bishi anaa jwarigi xaba̱ha̱ni buu, ama aba a̱rici.>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni wyan be̱ hin, <<Ga̱hin awyatu na niina, iza nꞌgata ta̱pana, hyo̱ nii ke̱nye̱n naa ga̱n hunrani na̱ ga̱hin! Ya̱ ha̱ni ga̱n naa na̱ ga̱hin ga̱n jaa rukuta̱? Nꞌiyaagi ma bwa baa.>>
Sa̱i aba iyaagi buu bwa baa.
Naa hwaanwun be̱ nda̱i Yeesu, be̱ pa̱ bwa pwan na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n, ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabwa ta̱baa zhizhiba, bwaa mambida̱, nu ndaabwa bwaa bana afucukwa.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ha̱nta̱ni ashin, <<Ya̱ ha̱ni ta iri na̱nna be̱ takota̱ni bwa?>>
Ashin aba hin, <<Ta bwa ge̱.
Mahwarapi Bihwaanwun ta bwa be̱ na̱ ra koo na̱ ma̱ni wana hyan bikwane̱ be̱. Kuu-nii ara yaanyini ta̱ta̱nndaaka, ha̱nga ambishiri nda̱tu, u-ta̱nndaaki.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Wana ba̱ gaa hin, <Kuu-nii ara>? Hwe̱n nii ara ta̱nda hyo̱ iri kuunaa pa̱nii gata na̱ bwa.>>
Kupita ashin na baa aba ta̱a̱ni nu aba hin, <<Mꞌpa̱nii gata kuge̱, nꞌguni wana hyan ma duwa̱na̱a̱ gata ta̱pana na̱ bwa!>>
Na Yeesu be̱ nda̱i wyatu nii duwa̱ni kuta̱wuce, be̱ hiika̱ni be̱e̱ hwaanwun naa we̱, be̱ hin, <<Gaa bihwaanwun naa ta yansan baa mazama ta̱cita̱ na̱ nꞌta̱tuba̱, iihin báni paaku baa buyata, ta-gura̱a̱ ta̱na̱ paaku baa buyata mayaan.>>
Bihwaanwun naa we̱ be̱ ta̱ ta̱ꞌungwa, be̱ zha̱a̱nta̱ni baa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, naazhin be̱ ba̱ni. Baa bubwa taa hakuu na ꞌwi, awyatu hwarapi aba hoo hyan, <<Ai, baa buꞌwi.>>
Ama Yeesu be̱ kota̱ni ara na baa, be̱ ta̱ baa bishita̱, bwa hiiki, bwa e̱she̱.
Na Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni ina, ana jwarigi aba ha̱nta̱ni buu ta̱swee, aba hin, <<Na̱ wana ba̱ ga̱tu ta a̱rici bihwaanwun yata naa we̱ ta̱ba̱ha̱na̱?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Ai, bihwaanwun hakii na̱nna a̱cii bana sa̱i kuna̱ ro̱pe̱.>>
Yeesu gura̱a̱ nda mazama nama ta̱ꞌwa̱ ta̱nde̱e̱be̱
Maatiyu 17:22-23; Luka 9:43-45
Sa̱i Yeesu na̱ ana jwarigi, aba ga̱a̱ kaba pa̱ri, abaa hura̱ ta̱hani, aba jwara̱gani kuta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Gaalili. Ama Yeesu be̱ taribici buyaan buyansun paaka aba ne̱e̱,
wana binii ga̱gaagana ana jwarigi. Be̱ hin wyan, <<Anii pana Buyoo Butu kuꞌnꞌara na nꞌawyatu ana ribici be̱. Aba nii kuna be̱, hwe̱n na hin taatu bihiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱.>>
Ama aba e̱nshe̱nshe̱n iri na be̱ cici, aba gura̱a̱ ha̱nga rukwanyan xaha̱nta̱ni buu.
Iyaa ta huri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱?
Maatiyu 18:1-5; Luka 9:46-48
Aba wuci Kapanahu. Na aba ne̱e̱ na̱ ina, Yeesu be̱ ha̱nta̱ni ana jwarigi, <<Mazama nama mbata ga̱hin tanii nda na̱ yo̱n?>>
Aba naanyin wau wau na̱ wana na̱ yo̱n, atanii nda kuda̱ga ta̱hyan iyaa ta hura̱gi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ kaba ne̱e̱.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hunrani, be̱ nꞌgani upwa na ree, be̱ hin wyan, <<Hyo̱ bunaa ribi bushi butu o̱to̱, ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ bushii naa ta̱hakana hyo̱, bushi bugyama naa wyatu hyo̱.>>
Be̱ rágani buyaan baa bunaa njeke, be̱ shaani bwa, bwa e̱she̱ na̱ awyantancin ndaaba. Be̱ wuguda̱ni bwa baa na̱ aꞌuba̱ nde̱e̱be̱, be̱ hin wyan,
<<Hyo̱ bunaa ra̱a̱ be̱e̱ binaa njeke haki na̱nna nꞌara nꞌree na̱ wana ga̱mi, ga̱n ta bwa nꞌra̱a̱. Bunaa nꞌra̱a̱ ga̱mi, shii kuga̱n ta bwa nꞌra̱a̱, hyo̱ na̱ Baaba nimi na nꞌkáji ta bwa ra̱a̱.>>
Bunaa za mayaan na̱ ga̱tu, bunda̱a̱tu ta
Maatiyu 18:6-9; Luka 9:49-50; 17:1-2
Aba na̱ kunnu, sa̱i Yoohana bwa hin buu, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, ta̱ndái buyaan bunii ba̱ha̱na̱a̱ nꞌhwaanwun na nꞌwe̱ na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ ruzha̱a̱ rundaabi ta ga̱tu yánshin be̱, na̱ wana buza na̱ ga̱tu.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin be̱, <<Ta-yansan ma be̱. Buza naa nii nda ri na ta̱jikita̱na̱ na̱ ta̱kai nata̱ ruzha̱a̱ runiimi, bugura̱a̱ ara ta̱nda mazama nama uwa̱ maniimi ha̱ni ka̱.
Hyo̱ bunaa za mayaan na̱ ga̱tu, bunda̱a̱tu ta.
Kwayaa na buu pa̱ ma ma̱ni nama ta̱swa, koo bikoopi ka̱, wana ishi ana Ala̱masiihu, mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, Hwe̱n jaa gaa ta̱pana funa̱ kubutu yata.
<<Inii sha ri na ambishiri bunaa shaani buka̱ kuꞌmꞌmwaan na̱nna na mꞌpa̱ni nꞌgata wa̱ka̱mi nꞌnje̱ pinsan. Huri gama aka̱da̱gi be̱ hyoo na nama na o̱to̱ na̱ ruru, amunsani be̱ kurwaga na iri.
Kuꞌara ndaa na̱maa shaana u-nje̱ pinsan, ꞌyapa wuun! Huri gama u-ta̱ni paaku bina̱ na mahwa na̱ ara ka̱, na hyan u-ga̱a̱ nꞌara nꞌndaabi hyo̱ u-ta̱ni paaku ra na̱ nꞌara nꞌree. Ubwa ra, ajaa ara wuun ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱hina̱.+ :43 Ta̱yaan ta̱taga ta̱ka̱ ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa aaya 44 kunna: <<Nꞌkaba pa̱ri, <Acincin na ta naa re̱ wyan a̱cii ꞌwa̱, ubwa ra jaa ꞌwa̱ga̱ mahwa.> >>Kubuna ndaa mayaan na̱maa shaana u-nje̱ pinsan, sa̱i u-ꞌya̱pi wuun. Huri gama u-ta̱ni paaku bina̱ na mahwa na̱ buna ka̱, na hyan aabwe̱ paaku ra na̱ mꞌbuna nꞌree.+ :45 Ta̱yaan ta̱taga ta̱ ka̱ ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa aaya 46 kunna: <<Nꞌkaba pa̱ri, <Acincin na ta naa re̱ wyan a̱cii ꞌwa̱, ubwa ra jaa ꞌwa̱ga̱ mahwa.> >>Kuyishe ndaa na̱maa shaana u-nje̱ pinsan, sa̱i u-ya̱a̱cigi wuun. Huri gama u-ta̱ni paaku ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n na̱ yishe ka̱, na hyan aabwe̱ paaku ra na̱ ayishe ree.
Nꞌkaba pa̱ri,
<< <Acincin na ta naa re̱ wyan a̱cii ꞌwa̱,
ubwa ra jaa ꞌwa̱ga̱ mahwa.>
Anii ha̱mbaraga koo buya̱ na̱ ra sabu, haruwa na aba ta a̱sa̱ga̱na̱ ri na aba hiin shinraanwyan Hwe̱n na̱ wun.
<<Wun shi ri na zumaa, ama kuza mꞌmasuunran mandaabwa, na̱ ba̱ ga̱hin nii a̱sa̱ga̱na̱ wuun? Sha ma haka na mꞌbaa masuunran nama wun, inaa na̱ hunranhunran na gama na̱ aya̱na̱nhin.>>

Ta̱tazhigana buꞌa̱
Maatiyu 19:1-12; Luka 16:18
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ga̱a̱ bibe̱ ko, be̱ huri bibiin naa ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya na̱ hira̱ree na Rwaga na Joodan. Awyatu hwarapi aba gura̱a̱ ura̱ka̱ku waabe̱, be̱ gura̱a̱ naa ga̱gaagana wyan haruwa na be̱ ya̱wa̱ni.
Ayaan Faraasiya aba jaa waabe̱ xama̱a̱nwya̱ni buu. Aba ha̱nta̱ni buu, aba hin, <<Ta̱bishi, Nꞌgira̱nshin nda̱a̱tu ta̱mpa̱ni butu ta̱zhiga̱ni aꞌa̱yo?>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Maya̱ mazama mata Muusa bwa taa pana ma nu?>>
Sa̱i aba ra̱ni buu, aba hin, <<Muusa tapana nu ta̱hyan xubutu pa̱ni aꞌa̱yo takaada na ta̱kuna ta̱wya̱ri, bugura̱a̱ cipana bwa.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Na̱ wana ta̱tibici mazama maniinhin mata mashaani Muusa bwa taa taagaga ma kunnu.
Ama tana Hwe̱n bwa nje̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana, utanda butu wya̱ri na̱a̱ a̱.
Na̱ wana kunnu, butu nii gaa ashin na̱ aya̱na̱, bumaꞌa̱npa̱nta̱ni na̱ aꞌa̱yo,
aba reeko ashi ri ka̱. Iyeebe, ajaa sha wyatu reeko, sa̱i da̱i ashi ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ka̱.
Na̱ wana kunnu, ri na Hwe̱n bwa wa̱ta̱ku, xbuyaan buta hoosa̱.>>
Na aba gura̱a̱ kushiika ina, sa̱i aba upwa na ree aba ha̱nta̱ni Yeesu mꞌba maya̱nu mazama.
Sa̱i be̱ hin, <<Hyo̱ butu naa ta̱zhiga̱ni a̱yo, bwa zha̱a̱ buyaan buꞌa̱, bunje̱ ta pinsan na banshaun kaꞌa̱yo.
Kushi buꞌa̱ nuu ga̱a̱ wya̱rugo, bwa gii kuuyaan butu, bunje̱ ta pinsan na banshaun kawya̱rugo.>>
Yeesu sha̱a̱gi mꞌmwaan rubara̱ka
Maatiyu 19:13-15; Luka 18:15-17
Uyaan hwe̱n awyatu abaa iyagi mꞌmwaan wana xbica̱guda̱a̱ga̱gi muu nꞌara, ama ana jwarigi abaa hyaan awyatu hana.
Na Yeesu be̱ nda̱i ri na baa nda, be̱ gware̱ me̱. Be̱ hin wyan, <<Hakata ma mꞌmwaan nꞌjaa wa̱ka̱mi, ta-yansan ma muu, na̱ wana ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱shi nata̱ ana ne̱e̱ haku mꞌmwaan na̱nna.
Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, hyo̱ bunaa ra̱a̱ci ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n haku mꞌmwaan na̱nna na nꞌnjeke, bujaa da̱ba ta̱ta̱na̱ kuta̱ba ta̱gwama.>>
Sa̱i be̱e̱ shapaga mꞌba mꞌmwaan, ma hwaamaa muu, ma cagudaagaga muu nꞌara.
Butu naa mꞌbaa ri ma̱
Maatiyu 19:16-30; Luka 18:18-30
Na Yeesu be̱ hiin naa gaa kaba pa̱ri, kuuyaan butu bwa wuce na sumo̱, bwa ta̱ runrun na uba̱ nde̱e̱be̱, bwa ha̱nta̱ni buu, bwa hin, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi binaa mahanda, iba̱ ga̱n nda na hyan ma da̱ba ta̱nda bina̱ na mahwa?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni be̱, be̱ hin, <<Iba̱ shani gaa nꞌnꞌgani binaa mahanda? Buza naa shi naa mahanda, sa̱i ku-Hwe̱n bwaa ka̱.
Bi-yan da̱i ri na Nꞌgira̱nshin nda̱a̱tu mꞌba hin, <Ta-kuna butu. Ta-nda banshaun. Ta-nda zumba̱. Ta-hyan ri na shi ta̱be̱ ishi mahanda. Ta-pira̱ buyaan. Cina̱na̱ abaaba ndaa na̱ ada̱a̱da̱ ndaa.> >>
Bwa butu bwa hin, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, hyo̱ ga̱n ta hoo jwara̱ga iri ya̱nu ta nꞌta̱njeke ta̱niimi.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ gwatani bwa ta̱gwatana nata̱ ta̱ruba̱, be̱ hin bwa, <<Iri ka̱ taa bwani ta̱nda. Jaga, sáanhinai hyo̱ iri na gaa mꞌbaa, u-pa̱ga̱ni aꞌwa̱ta̱gi, bi-nii masha̱a̱ga̱ iri ma̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱. U-jaa naazhin u-nꞌjwara̱ga.>>
Na butu bwa hange̱ kunnu, bwa ha̱nsha̱nha̱ni apusa̱ka ndaabwa, bwa huri giyo na̱ ame̱ ta̱gura, na̱ wana buꞌmꞌbaa ri ma̱.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ke̱ce̱e̱ke̱, be̱ gwatagani ana jwarigi, be̱ hin wyan, <<Ujaa da̱a̱ra̱ mahwa, ana mꞌbaa ri ma̱, ata̱ni kuta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n.>>
Ana jwarigi aba nje̱ kuma̱ na aba hange̱ mazama maya̱nu. Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ gura̱a̱ hyan wyan, <<Ga̱hin mꞌmwaan niimi, ma jaa da̱a̱ra̱ mahwa, ta̱ta̱na̱ kuta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n.
Manii hura̱ ta̱yoo uraakumi uta̱ni na̱ riyishe na zhimbira, na hyan butu naa mꞌbaa iri ma̱ buta̱ni kuta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n.>>
Na ana jwarigi aba hange̱ kunnu aba duwa̱ni ta̱nda ma̱, abaa mahantaana ma hyaan, <<Kushi kunnu, iyaa nu nii ara ta̱nda bina̱?>>
Yeesu be̱ gwatani wyan, be̱ hin, <<Iri na nga̱za̱ni butu wuma, a̱cii ngazana Hwe̱n ta̱nda, wana Uhwe̱n nii ara ta̱nda hyo̱ komba̱ri.>>
Sa̱i Biituru bwa gunii nu, bwa hin, <<Ga̱tu na ga̱tu hoo gáa hyo̱ iri nda̱tu, ga̱tuu jwarigi.>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Nꞌyan kunnu, nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, hyo̱ ana gáa nꞌina ndaabwa, koo aya̱na̱ba, koo aya̱ndoo, koo ashoo, koo mꞌmwaan, koo nꞌcima, na̱ wana nimi, koo na̱ wana mazama nama zumaa,
ri na abaa da̱ba nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu, inii hura̱ biyina̱ ka̱, kuꞌina na bwa gáa, na̱ aya̱na̱ba, na̱ aya̱ndoo, na̱ mꞌmwaan, na̱ nꞌcima, ama huku na̱ ngwan ta̱swa. Jaa kuuga̱a̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana bugura̱a̱ da̱ba bina̱ na mahwa.
Awyatu hwarapi ana ta sha wyatu o̱to̱ na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana, aja̱a̱ sha ana njeke kuꞌaꞌuba̱ na Hwe̱n. Ana njeke na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana aba ja̱a̱ sha awyatu o̱to̱ kuꞌaꞌuba̱ na Hwe̱n.>>
Yeesu gura̱a̱ cita̱ kiibe̱e̱ ꞌwa̱
Maatiyu 20:17-19; Luka 18:31-34
Aba nꞌta̱hani zhagu Hurushaliima, Yeesu iyeebe ndaaba. Ana jwarigi buu abaa jikita̱ga̱. Bigudu naa tajwárige̱ wyan ta̱baa aba hange̱ rukwanyan. Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ gura̱a̱ pe̱e̱n ana be̱ tazwara nii biin, be̱ ke̱ne̱ ta̱bisa̱ga̱ wyan ri na nii nda nii be̱.
Be̱ hin, <<Ga̱tu na ga̱tu nii hura̱ katanu Hurushaliima. Anii pana Buyoo Butu kapirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin. Anii ndaaka buu ta̱suuga̱ nata̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱, apa̱ni buu kawyatu na shici Ayaahudiya.
Aba nii naa ndaga buu umuntun na uwa̱, atupa̱ga̱ni buu macimi, azware̱ buu uduun, akwane̱ buu. Na̱ hwe̱n na hin taatu bikúshe̱e̱ wuma.>>
Yaakubu na̱ Yoohana aro̱pe̱ Yeesu yaanyini
Maatiyu 20:20-28
Yaakubu na̱ Yoohana mꞌmwaan na n-Zabadi, mꞌba jaa paa Yeesu, mꞌba hin buu, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, ta̱hin maa rupa u-ta̱ndaaki iri na ga̱tu ribi.>>
Sa̱i be̱ hin wyan, <<Iba̱ ga̱hin ribi maa ndaaka ma?>>
Aba hin buu, <<Ta̱ne̱e̱ na̱ ro̱pe̱ ta̱hyan, hwe̱n na gaa ta̱ni paaku ta̱gwama ta̱ndaabi, buka̱ hunrana na̱ ara kataga ndaa, buka̱ hunrana na̱ ara kagura̱ ndaa.>>
Ama sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Iyancin ri na ga̱hiin rupa. Inii ara ta̱swa nii koopi naa ta̱guma binaa ga̱n swa? Koo inii ara aanje̱ ma baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ baba̱tiisa̱ma na ta̱guma na abaa nꞌnda?>>
Aba ra̱ni, aba hin, <<Ga̱tu nii ara.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Inii swa nii koopi naa ga̱n swa, aba na̱maa nda ma baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ baba̱tiisa̱ma na aba nii nꞌnda.
Ama ta̱hunrana nꞌkataga koo kagura̱, shii ga̱n ta nii pana wuun. Pa̱ri kaya̱nu, kashi naka Hwe̱n bwa hoo sha̱a̱ga̱ ayaan ana bwa ka̱shi.>>
Na aꞌupwa na bwa̱ci ana be̱ tazwara ba hange̱ ri na Yaakubu na̱ Yoohana aba nje̱, aba gware̱ sume̱ na̱ aba.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ nꞌgani wyan be̱ hin, <<Iyan ana shici Ayaahudiya, ana aba sha̱pi ashi ana ta̱gwama, ata bisa̱a̱ awyatu ndaaba ta̱kai, wyatu o̱to̱ ndaaba taa ata zhintaana awyatu ndaaba.
Ama shii kunnu mꞌba nii sha wunhin. Na hyan ma shi kunnu, hyo̱ bunaa ribi bushi butu o̱to̱ niinhin, xbushi bugyama naa ya̱na̱ba hyo̱.
Bunaa ribi bushii o̱to̱, xbushi bugyama naa koo buya̱.
Koo ga̱n Buyoo Butu nꞌjaa, shii na̱ wana hyan anaa nꞌndaaka tuma, ama wana masha bugyama, ma gura̱a̱ pana hyuhyu nimi wana xawyatu hwarapi bini.>>
Buruba̱ huwa̱gi
Maatiyu 20:29-34; Luka 18:35-43
Sa̱i aba wuci Yeriiko. Aba ma bana taa Yeriiko, bibe̱ na̱ ana jwarigi buu, na̱ ayaan wyatu hwarapi. Kuuyaan buruba̱ bwa ne̱e̱, ruzha̱a̱ rundaabwa Baratimawusu, buyoo Timawusu. Bwa hunrani nii biin naa yo̱n ma rupa ri.
Na bwa hange̱ Yeesu na Naazare nu nii hura̱, bwa ke̱ne̱ nu ta̱taa, ma hyaan, <<Yeesu buna biikorogo naa Dawuda, ha̱nga mbishiri nimi!>>
Ayaan hwarapi abaa hyaan be̱ hana, ma hyaan be̱ nda wau. Bwa duwa̱ni kunnu ta̱taana na̱ kai, ma hyaan, <<Buna biikorogo naa Dawuda, ha̱nga mbishiri nimi!>>
Na Yeesu be̱ hange̱ be̱, be̱ e̱nshe̱n, be̱ hin, <<Nꞌgaagi ma be̱.>>
Sa̱i aba nꞌgani buruba̱, aba hin be̱, <<Nda ta̱ga̱da̱ri! Hiika̱, bina̱maa nꞌga.>>
Buruba̱ bwa hin kaki, bwa mo̱nshe̱n da̱bi na o̱to̱ ndaabwa, bwa huri paaki Yeesu.
Yeesu be̱ ha̱nta̱ni be̱, <<Iba̱ gaa ribi iindaaki?>>
Buruba̱ bwa hin, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, nꞌribi ta̱huwa̱ga̱ pa̱ri.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin bwa, <<Hura̱. Ta̱panaa gata ndaabi ku-Hwe̱n ta̱ta ta̱a̱kuda̱gahini.>> Kupita bwa huwa̱gi pa̱ri, bwa jwarigi Yeesu, aba huri da̱nda̱.

Yeesu ta̱ni Hurushaliima
Maatiyu 21:1-11; Luka 19:28-40; Yoohana 12:12-19
Na aba goki Hurushaliima, Yeesu na̱ ana jwarigi buu aba wuci nꞌcice̱pe̱ na nꞌaba ta hyan Batafaji na̱ Be̱tani paa Biꞌundu naa Iꞌwe̱e̱ na Zaitu. Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ka̱ji ana jwarigi buu reeko,
be̱ hin wyan, <<Hura̱ ma bicice̱pe̱ naa ne̱e̱ iyeebe ninhin. Kuta̱naa ta̱na̱ buu, inii ndaya bizhe̱nke̱n ufuni, binaa aba ta ka̱ta̱ncin mahwa. Irígijige buu, iꞌwaan buu pina.
Kuuyaan buu ha̱nta̱ni ma, <Na̱ wana ba̱ ga̱hiin nda kunta?> hyan ma be̱, <Butu O̱to̱ taa ribi buu, bunii kúshihine̱ buu kunrun.> >>
Aba huri, aba nda̱i bizhe̱nke̱n ufuni na̱ ayaan dubo do̱ko̱ na̱ yo̱n. Aba ma rigijiga̱ be̱e̱ zhe̱nke̱n,
sa̱i wyatu na taꞌisaga kaun aba hin wyan, <<Mbata ye̱e̱ ga̱hiin nda? Na̱ wana ba̱ ga̱hin rigijiga̱ bizhe̱nke̱n yata?>>
Sa̱i aba ra̱ni wyan kuharuwa na Yeesu be̱ tabishi wyan, aba wyatu aba hakaci wyan xahuri nii be̱e̱ zhe̱nke̱n.
Aba iyaagi Yeesu bizhe̱nke̱n, aba ba̱ra̱gi ada̱bi ndaaba na o̱to̱ na̱ abaa nde̱e̱be̱. Yeesu be̱ ka̱ta̱ni buu, be̱ hunrani.
Sa̱i wyatu hwarapi aba ba̱ra̱gi ada̱bi ndaaba na o̱to̱ na̱ yo̱n, aka̱ aba ba̱ra̱gi aba̱ba na nꞌshuwa na̱ yo̱n ana aba kúsagi na̱ aga do̱ko̱ na̱ yo̱n.
Awyatu na iyeebe na̱ ana ta̱baa, abaa taa sunu, ma hyaan,
<<Hoosaana!
Rubara̱ka naru Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n ruba ne̱e̱ hiku kuunaa jaa nꞌta̱kai ta̱ndaabwa!
Rubara̱ka ruba ne̱e̱ kuta̱gwama nata̱ wuci nata̱ adaada nda̱tu Dawuda.
Hoosaana nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.>>
Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni Hurushaliima, be̱ huri paaku Ina na Hwe̱n, be̱ gwataagani hyo̱ komba̱ri ki. Ha̱ni ya̱nu wana hwe̱n hwii, be̱ ba̱ni ce̱pe̱ be̱ huri Be̱tani na̱ ana jwarigi buu upwa na ree.
Yeesu pa̱ni ꞌwe̱e̱ na waanwan nu
Maatiyu 21:18-19
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, aba ga̱a̱ Be̱tani. Ha̱ni ya̱nu, Yeesu be̱ taha̱nga rumunro̱n.
Be̱ bwe̱ yishe, be̱ nda̱i waanwan aba̱ba zhe̱n, be̱ ja̱a̱ xbide̱be̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱ri kaun. Na be̱ wuci kubwa ꞌwe̱e̱, be̱ nda̱i kaba̱ba, ta̱ꞌwa̱ri ta̱ba za, na̱ wana shici ke̱nye̱n naa bwa ta ꞌwara.
Sa̱i be̱ pa̱ni bwa waanwan nu, be̱ hin, <<xBuyaan buta gura̱a̱ re̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱ri ta̱ndaabi mahwa!>> Ana jwarigi hyo̱ aba hange̱ ri na be̱ cici.
Yeesu a̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni Ina na Hwe̱n
Maatiyu 21:12-17; Luka 19:45-48; Yoohana 2:13-22
Na aba ta̱ni Hurushaliima, Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n, be̱ ga̱ci awyatu na nii sa̱a̱nha̱na̱a̱ na̱ ana nii saan ꞌwaa na̱ ame̱ ndaabwa. Be̱ gura̱a̱ taacigaga ateeburu ana wyatu na nii hira̱gaga ayuwa na̱ nꞌzhe̱nke̱n na nꞌana nii sa̱a̱nha̱na̱a̱ nꞌhuunruun na nꞌina.
Be̱ gura̱a̱ yansan koo buya̱ xbusha̱pi yaanyini buhuri na̱ be̱ kubambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n.
Be̱ ga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni wyatu be̱ hin, <<Ata̱gi na̱ takaada na Hwe̱n ta̱hyan,
<< <Anii hyan Ina nimi shi
Ina na ro̱pe̱ na wyatu hyo̱.>
Ta ga̱hin ba̱ha̱ni wuun <paaka azumba̱ aba ta masoo.> >>
Apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin aba hange̱ mazama ma ya̱nu hyo̱, abaa wyanzan haruwa na abaa kuna buu. Aba hange̱ rukwanyan, wana hyo̱ bigudu jikita̱ni na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱nde̱e̱be̱.
Ha̱ni ya̱nu na hwe̱n bwa hwii, Yeesu na̱ ana jwarigi buu aba ba̱ni ce̱pe̱.
Waanwan na Yeesu be̱ pa̱ni nu hoogi
Maatiyu 21:20-22
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, abaa hura̱ paaku bwa waanwan, sa̱i aba nda̱i uhoogi tana nga̱nga̱nda̱.
Biituru bwa mata̱ma̱nriin, bwa hin Yeesu, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, gwatana! Waanwan na gaa tapa̱ni nu hoogi!>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, <<Pana ma nꞌgata ku-Hwe̱n!
Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, kubutu za maree maree bwa pa̱nii gata, bunii ara ta̱hyan undu na̱nna, <Hiika̱, u-mamunsani na̱ rwaga na o̱to̱,> Hwe̱n nii ndaaka be̱ wuun.
Na̱ wana kunnu, nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, komba̱ri ga̱hin wya̱nzhin huku na̱ ro̱pe̱, kiipa̱nii gata na̱ bwa, yansun ma ta̱hyan ihoo da̱ba wuun.
Hyo̱ ha̱ni na ga̱hiin nda ro̱pe̱, ta-ha̱mba̱ga̱ ma pinsan na buyaan bubwaa ndaaki ma nii gata niinhin, wana hyan xAbaaba ninhin na ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ taa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ ma pinsan ninhin.>>+ :25 Ta̱yaan ta̱taga ta̱ka̱ ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa aaya 26 kunna: Ama kiitanaa ha̱mba̱a̱ga̱na̱ awyatu pinsan na abaa ndaaki ma, kunnu taa Abaaba ninhin na ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ abaa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ ma pinsan ninhin.Aha̱nta̱ni paaku ta̱kai // nata̱ Yeesu ta̱ba báni
Maatiyu 21:23-27; Luka 20:1-8
Aba gura̱a̱ ta̱na̱ Hurushaliima. Na Yeesu be̱e̱ raan bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n, ayaan apirisiti na o̱to̱, na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin, huku na̱ wyatu o̱to̱ ndaaba, aba jaa paa Yeesu.
Aba hin buu, <<Nꞌta̱ya̱ ta̱kai ta̱ta gaa ndaga hyo̱ iri na̱nna? Iyaa ta pa̱ni ta̱ba ta̱kai?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Ga̱n na̱maa hantana ma taa mayaan mazama maka̱. Kiiꞌmꞌbishi muu, ga̱n taa maa nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ ma koo nꞌta̱kai nata̱ iyaa ga̱n ndaga iri na̱nna.
Ta̱kai nata̱ Yoohana bwa ta naa ndaga baba̱tiisa̱ma ta̱shi nata̱ Hwe̱n koo ta̱shi nata̱ butu wuma?>>
Kaba kaba aba pa̱shi kuda̱ga, aba hin, <<Kuta̱hin, <Ta̱báni ku-Hwe̱n,> binii ta̱hyan, <Iba̱ shani ga̱hin pa̱ncin nꞌgata na̱a̱ bwa?>
Ama kuta̱hin, <Ta̱báni kubutu wuma> ...>> (Ashiragi rukwanyan naru ri na wyatu baa ndaaka wyan, na̱ wana wyatu hyo̱ shii ta̱hyan Yoohana bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ta.)
Na̱ wana kunnu, aba ra̱ni mazama nama Yeesu, aba hin, <<Ga̱tu yancin.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Ga̱n taa maa, ga̱n jamaa bisa̱ ma koo na̱ nꞌta̱ya̱ ta̱kai ta̱ta ga̱n ndaga ri na̱nna.>>

Ta̱kun nata̱ ahwaanyan na we̱
Maatiyu 21:33-46; Luka 20:9-19
Yeesu be̱ re̱ iyeebe na̱ mꞌmazama nꞌta̱kun. Be̱ hin, <<Buyaan butu tanda cima na ꞌwe̱e̱ na iinabi, bwa riini wuun na̱ nꞌta̱ma, bwa nje̱ paaku ta̱naa pinra̱a̱n ma̱ni nama ta̱ꞌwa̱ri, bwa ta̱ bizhe̱nke̱n naa iyo̱. Bwa pa̱ni wuun unda kayaan hwaanyan, bwa ja̱a̱ ta̱yaan ce̱nye̱n.
Na ha̱ni na gwashi na ta̱ꞌwa̱ri bwa nje̱, sa̱i bwa ka̱ji bugyama ndaabwa ka̱, ta̱hyan xburáagi bwa ta̱taa ta̱ndaabwa nata̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱ri.
Ama ana taꞌunda cima aba kota̱ni bwaa gyama, aba pa̱ bwa dibi, bwa huri kunta maha̱nda̱.
Bwa butu naa cima bwa gura̱a̱ kada yaan bugyama, ana taꞌunda cima aba gura̱a̱ cwaaga bwaa gyama, aba ba̱sa̱ni bwa ri na̱ hyuhyu.
Na bwa ka̱ji yaan, aba kwane̱ bwa. Ayaan hwarapi na bwa ta gura̱a̱ kada aba da̱ba̱gi aka̱, aba kunai aka̱.
Bubwa butu naa cima bwa ta mꞌbaa butu ka̱ naa bwani bwa, buyoo bunaa bwa hura̱gi ta̱ruba̱. Ta̱hakana bwa ka̱jii yoo, bwa shii nii gata ta̱hyan, <Kanda̱i be̱e̱ biniimi anii cina̱na̱ buu.>
<<Ama aba wyatu na taꞌunda cima aba mahin, <Manje̱ to̱n, nde̱e̱ bunaa ja̱a̱ hya̱su ree ubwa cima, xta̱kwane̱ be̱ ubwa cima shi nda̱tu.>
Sa̱i aba kota̱ni be̱, aba kwane̱ be̱, aba bwe̱ ruꞌwa̱ rundaabwa na̱ ꞌyafu na ubwa cima.>>
Yeesu be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Too, iba̱ ga̱hin yan butu naa cima nii jaa bunje̱? Ai, bunii jaa bukunai ana bwa tapa̱ni unda na cima yata, bupa̱ni ayaan ubwa cima.
Icita̱gici mazama mana̱nna na̱ takaada na Hwe̱n? Ta̱hyan,
<< <Utari na awyatu na ta̱ma aba hwashe̱ ta̱hyan uza bina̱,
ubwa ta shi na hura̱gi hyo̱ bina̱ kuta̱ma.
Uya̱nu shi ta̱nda nata̱ Hwe̱n,
ubwa shi iri na yaburi nꞌsuyishe sunda̱a̱tu.> >>
Sa̱i awyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya abaa wyanzan haruwa na hyan xakota̱ni Yeesu na̱ wana aꞌe̱nshe̱n ta̱hyan na̱ aba ta be̱e̱ nda ta̱ba ta̱kun. Ama aba hange̱ rukwanyan naru bigudu naa awyatu. Wana kunnu aba ga̱a̱ buu, aba huri.
Ta̱hantana nata̱ // ta̱pana Kaisa ga̱ndu
Maatiyu 22:15-22; Luka 20:20-26
Naa ke̱nye̱n be̱ hiin naa ta ge̱, sa̱i aba ka̱ji ayaan Afaraasiya na̱ awyatu na bugwama Hirudu, wana hyan kaka̱ra̱a̱gi Yeesu ta̱ruma ade̱be̱ azha̱a̱ buu na̱ mꞌmazama mande̱e̱be̱.
Na aba wuce, aba hin buu, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, ta̱yan ta̱hyan bu-shi naa mahanda. Wakaa, awyatu ashi iri ka̱, gaa a̱cii bisa̱a̱ ta̱hura̱ kuuyaan, gaa ta naa ga̱gaagana uyo̱n na Hwe̱n to̱n na̱ mꞌmahanda. Too, bi-nda̱i ta̱hyan unje̱ to̱n ta̱pa̱ni ga̱ndu ku-Kaisa bugwama naa Rooma koo na?
Ta̱pa̱ni koo ta̱ta pana?>>
Ama Yeesu be̱ hoo insan ta̱hyan ashi agura̱ na wyatu. Be̱ hin wyan, <<Iba̱ shani ga̱hin hiin mꞌmaanwyana? ꞌWaan ma aba yuwa na azurufa xnꞌnda̱i.>>
Na aba pa̱ni buu aba yuwa, be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan, <<Mꞌpirwa na̱ nꞌruzha̱a̱ naru iyaa ta runa̱nna?>>
Aba ra̱ni, aba hin, <<Na Kaisa ta.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Too, pana ma iri na shi na Kaisa ku-Kaisa, ipa̱ni iri na shi na Hwe̱n ku-Hwe̱n.>>
Na be̱ bishi wyan kunnu aba nje̱ kuma̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Ta̱hantana nata̱ ta̱hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱
Maatiyu 22:23-33; Luka 20:27-40
Sa̱i ayaan Asaduukiya, ana hin kubutu ꞌwi buꞌa̱cii hiika̱, aba jaa paa Yeesu. Aba ha̱nta̱ni buu mꞌba mazama ta̱hyan,
<<Biwya̱ra̱mi, Muusa tata̱taagaga na̱ Nꞌgira̱nshin ta̱hyan, kubutu ꞌwi bwa ga̱a̱ a̱yo na za mꞌmwaan, xbuya̱na̱ sha̱pi aꞌa̱yo, buma̱nta̱a̱ni bwa mꞌmwaan.
Too, atanda ayaan awyatu na̱ aya̱na̱ba aba ta̱nda̱ra̱. Bunaa yigo tazhaa buꞌa̱, bwa ꞌwi bwa za be̱e̱.
Buyaan buya̱na̱ bwa gura̱a̱ zhaa bwaa a̱, bwa ꞌwi taa bwa za be̱e̱. Bunaa hin taatu bwa taa kunnu.
Hyo̱ kunnu aba ta̱nda̱ra̱ aba zha̱a̱gi bwaa a̱, aba ꞌwa̱gi, bwa zaa naa mꞌbaa be̱e̱ na̱a̱ bwa. Bwaa a̱ taa ta̱hakana bwa jaa bwa ꞌwi.
Na ta̱hyan hyo̱ ata̱nda̱ra̱ azha̱a̱gi bwa, hwe̱n na ta̱hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱ aꞌa̱yo iyaa bwaa sha?>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Ai, iri na ga̱hin shii na̱ nꞌgata niinhin iza to̱n, na̱ wana iꞌe̱nshe̱nshe̱n mazama nama takaada na Hwe̱n, ga̱hin gura̱a̱ci yansun ta̱kai nata̱ Hwe̱n.
Uha̱ni na ana ꞌwa̱gi abaa hiika̱ka̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱, awyatu wya̱ri ja̱a̱cii zhaaga a̱, aꞌa̱ aba ja̱a̱cii giya̱ga̱ ta̱wya̱ri, aja̱a̱ naa haka atuma na Hwe̱n nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
Too, na̱ mꞌmazama nama ta̱hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱, itacita̱gici na̱ takaada na Muusa, kiiꞌuꞌwe̱e̱ binaa sa̱pi naa tanaa huna̱ ra na̱ ahira̱ ceeku? Hwe̱n bwa tahyan Muusa, <Ga̱n ta nꞌshi Hwe̱n na Ibiraahin na̱ Hwe̱n na Isiyaaku na̱ Hwe̱n na Yaakubu.>
Ubwa ta shici Uhwe̱n na awyatu na ꞌwa̱gi, ama ubwa shi Uhwe̱n na awyatu ana ne̱e̱ wuma. Itama̱a̱ ta̱wajigaa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.>>
Nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌhura̱gi hyo̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱
Maatiyu 22:34-40; Luka 10:25-28
Biyaan biwya̱ra̱mi naa Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa be̱ ne̱e̱, be̱ shiragi ukuda̱ga na abaa nda. Sa̱i be̱ hange̱ Yeesu ra̱ni to̱n, sa̱i be̱ ha̱nta̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Biya̱a̱ gira̱nshin na Hwe̱n bwa ta pana Muusa taa shi naa hura̱gi hyo̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Binaa hura̱gi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ hyo̱ be̱ taa shi, <Shiraga ma awyatu na Isiraaꞌila, Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n nda̱tu, uka̱ ubwa ne̱e̱.
Ruba̱ Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n ndaa nii gata ndaabi hyo̱, na̱ hyo̱ wuma ndaa, na̱ hyo̱ ahari ndaa, na̱ hyo̱ ikai ndaa.>
Binaa jwárige̱ tashi, <Ruba̱ butu naa nꞌharu nꞌndaabi haruwa na gaa ribi hyuhyu ndaa.> Nꞌyaan nꞌgira̱nshin nꞌza na nꞌhuri na̱nna ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.>>
Sa̱i bibe̱e̱ wya̱ra̱mi na Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa be̱ hin Yeesu, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, to̱n na̱ gaa cici, Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n uka̱ ne̱e̱, uyaan za kubwa.
Ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ ma ruba̱ wuun na̱ hyo̱ bigata niimi na̱ hyo̱ ahari nimi na̱ hyo̱ ikai nimi, ma gura̱a̱ ruba̱ butu naa nꞌharu niimi haruwa na ga̱n nꞌribi hyuhyu nimi. Ubwa ta hura̱gi hyo̱ nꞌta̱pana ibikico̱ na ta̱huunha̱na̱ na̱ iyaan ri na ta̱pana Hwe̱n ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.>>
Na Yeesu be̱ nda̱i haruwa na be̱ ndaaki buu mazama na̱ nꞌta̱yansun, sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin buu, <<Bi-ne̱e̱ do̱ko̱ na̱ nꞌta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n mbaa.>> Na mꞌba hwii bwa zaa naa gura̱a̱ mꞌbaa bishita̱ naa ta̱hantana buu yaan ri.
Ta̱hantana nata̱ iyaa ta shi Ala̱masiihu
Maatiyu 22:41-46; 23:1-36; Luka 20:41-47
Uha̱ni na Yeesu be̱ tanaa ga̱gaagana awyatu na̱ bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n, sa̱i be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Iba̱ shani nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin mꞌbaa hyaan Ala̱masiihu shi buyoo Dawuda?
Dawuda na̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa tanda mazama na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱a̱ Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n, ta̱hyan,
<< <Butu O̱to̱ tahyan Butu O̱to̱ niimi,
<<Hunrana nꞌkataga kaniimi,
sa̱i kunshaani awyatu naa ribici
gaa fo̱nje̱ wyan na̱ kokobi na buna ndaa.>> >
Ta na ta̱hyan Dawuda taꞌnꞌgana Ala̱masiihu <Butu O̱to̱,> too, na bwa nii gura̱a̱ sha buyoo ha̱ni ka̱?>> Na awyatu aba hange̱ mazama nama be̱ cici, koo buya̱ bwa hange̱ gama na ta̱shiraga.
Yeesu ma ga̱gaagana wyan, sa̱i be̱ hin, <<Iya ma shukuu na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin, na̱ wana ata ruba̱ ta̱taana ada̱bi na o̱to̱ anaa riinshina̱ na̱ aba, aba ta ruba̱ azumanu na maca̱ma̱nta̱n paaka kasuwa.
Aba ta gura̱a̱ ruba̱ paaka hura̱gi gama na hunranhunran na̱ aka̱ta̱ku koo paaku abuki.
Aba ta shi ana ta naa pira̱ga̱ aꞌa̱ na suwya̱rugooba suba ꞌwa̱gi, aba za mꞌpirwa na̱ ro̱pe̱ ngiswan kawyatu aba ne̱e̱. Ana nii nda kunnu, aba ta shi ana ja̱a̱ hura̱ga̱ ta̱swa ngwan.>>
Ba̱iko naa a̱ naa awya̱rugo ba ꞌwi
Luka 21:1-4
Na Yeesu be̱ hunrani do̱ko̱ na̱ paa abaa zwagagana ba̱iko na Ina na Hwe̱n, be̱ gwatagi kawyatu abaa zwagagana ayuwa kuruꞌwana naru ta̱sha̱a̱ga̱ ba̱iko. Awyatu hwarapi ana mꞌbaa ri aba zwa̱ga̱ga̱ni ayuwa o̱to̱.
Sa̱i kuuyaan buꞌa̱ bunaa awya̱rugo ba ꞌwi, bwa shi ꞌwa̱ta̱gi, bwa wuce, bwa zwa̱ga̱ni aniinii ree na wucici kobo.
Yeesu be̱ nꞌgani ana jwarigi waabe̱, be̱ hin wyan, <<Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, iri na buꞌwa̱ta̱gi na̱nna bwa zwa̱ga̱ni, ihuri na awyatu ba pa̱ga̱ni hyo̱.
Hyo̱ ndaaba apa̱ga̱ni na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌmꞌbaa nata̱ aba mꞌbaagi ta, ama bubwa, na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwa̱ta̱gi ta̱ndaabwa ta bwa pa̱ni hyo̱ ina bwa mashikani.>>

Ta̱huza̱a̱ga̱ nata̱ Ina na Hwe̱n
Maatiyu 24:1-2; Luka 21:5-6
Na Yeesu be̱e̱ báni Ina na Hwe̱n, sa̱i buka̱ kana jwarigi buu bwa ha̱nta̱ni buu, bwa hin, << Biwya̱ra̱mi, gwatana katari na̱nna ana rushama na̱ iri na ta̱ma ta̱na̱nna nata̱ zumaa kuta̱ba ne̱e̱.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Bi-nda̱i hyo̱ ta̱ma ta̱na̱nna nata̱ yaburagi? Anii huza̱a̱ga̱ tuun hyo̱. Uza yaan tari na nii bwata ucagudana na̱a̱ ya̱na̱.>>
Ungwan na yigo
Maatiyu 24:3-14; Luka 21:7-19
Yeesu ma hunrana na̱ Biꞌundu naa Iꞌwe̱e̱ na Zaitu, na gwatagi Ina na Hwe̱n, sa̱i Biituru, na̱ Yaakubu, na̱ Yoohana, na̱ Andaraawa, aba jaa waabe̱ ta̱swee. Aba ha̱nta̱ni,
<<Ta̱bishi, na̱ ya̱ ha̱ni nu iri ya̱nu ibe̱ ja̱a̱ nda? Imbata ga̱tu ja̱a̱ ndaya na ja̱a̱ ta̱bisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan iri ya̱nu goki ta̱nda?>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ke̱ne̱ wyan ta̱bisa̱ga̱, <<Sha̱a̱ ma suha̱nka̱ri suniinhin ki, xbuyaan butaa pira̱ ma.
Awyatu hwarapi ja̱a̱ jaa ahin ga̱n taꞌnꞌkáji wyan, ahin aba ta shi Ala̱masiihu, aba nii shana apiri awyatu hwarapi.
Ta-ha̱nga ma rukwanyan ga̱hin ha̱ngaga anii ndaga agyasa do̱ko̱ na̱ ga̱hin, koo tutu na̱ ga̱hin. Ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ iri ya̱nu ndagi hyo̱, ama ubwa ta shici ta̱hyan uha̱ni nu wuce.
Ce̱nye̱n na̱ ce̱nye̱n ta̱ja̱a̱ naa nda gagu, ta̱gwama na̱ nꞌta̱gwama ta̱ba ja̱a̱ naa nda gyasa. Ce̱nye̱n ta̱ba ja̱a̱ zha̱a̱nta̱na̱ pa̱ri goo goo, rumunro̱n ruba ja̱a̱ nda. Ama hyo̱ ya̱nu ubwa shici kwan ubwa ngwan, ushi haku ta̱raan wunsa̱n na gaa hiin hwan cima.
<<Ga̱hin na̱ hyuhyu ninhin sha̱a̱ ma suha̱nka̱ri suniinhin ki, wana ana̱maa kota̱ga̱na̱ ma, aaꞌye̱e̱ ma kuta̱suuga̱, aada̱ba̱gi ma na̱ aka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya. Aba na̱maa iya ma kagwamina na̱ nꞌgwama na̱ wana iꞌnꞌjwarigi. Na hyan icici mazama maniimi na̱ aꞌuba̱ ndaaba.
Ta ta̱huwa̱ nata̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana ta̱ba wuco, ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ abisa̱gi koo biya̱ korogo mazama nama zumaa.
Hyo̱ ha̱ni na abaa kota̱ni ma, abaa ꞌye̱e̱ ma kuta̱suuga̱, xutaa ta ma gbi na̱ iri na ga̱hin nii cita̱. Cita̱ ma hyo̱ iri naa jábani ma na̱ bwa ha̱ni, wana shici ga̱hin taa nii nda mazama, Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n ta.
<<Buya̱na̱a̱ naa butu bwa ja̱a̱ panaa ya̱na̱ akwane̱ bwa, ashin ba ja̱a̱ pana buyoo akwane̱ bwa, mꞌmwaan ba ja̱a̱ kiciika nꞌga̱a̱ sushoo na̱ aya̱ndoo nꞌshani akunai wyan.
Koo buya̱ na̱maa gaa ma na̱ wana iꞌnꞌjwarigi, ama hyo̱ bunaa ta̱a̱ gata macimi bwa wuci huwo na bwa ri ya̱nu hyo̱, Hwe̱n ja̱a̱ biha̱na̱ be̱.
<<Ija̱a̱ ndaya iri na yinzhin na we̱ na ja̱a̱ ꞌwaan ta̱huza̱a̱ga̱ iꞌe̱she̱ paaka shici na hyan iꞌisa na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n. (Butu naa nii cita̱ga̱ xbuꞌe̱nshe̱n ki!) Too, sa̱i ana ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya uja̱a̱ sha ga̱ga̱ga̱ agida̱ga̱gi, aka̱ta̱ni nꞌundu.
Bunaa ne̱e̱ na̱ asa̱ku, xbuciin xbuta ta̱na̱ ina bushápi yaan ꞌwaa.
Bunaa tane̱e̱ na̱ cima, xbuta hyan bunii giye bushɑ́pi da̱bi ndaabwa.
Iiyirigani ma aꞌa̱ na suhuba̱ na̱ aꞌa̱ na hyaabu na̱ bwa ha̱ni ya̱nu!
Nda ma ro̱pe̱ ta̱hyan ubwa ha̱ni xuta wuce ha̱ni na robi.
Ungwan na ubwa ha̱ni ja̱a̱ hura̱gi mamboo ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, una tanje̱ce̱ ta na Hwe̱n bwa nje̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana. Aba jaa gura̱a̱ duwa̱na̱ ta̱nda wuun mahwa.
Bwa shi Hwe̱n bwa ha̱sa̱a̱ci mꞌba nꞌhwe̱n, ata jaa da̱ba butu wuma naa tanii bina̱ na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana. Ama wana ambishiri na ana Hwe̱n bwa takasa, sa̱i bwa ha̱sa̱a̱ ngiswan na mꞌba nꞌhwe̱n.
<<Na̱ bwa ha̱ni, koo buya̱ buuhin ma, <Gwatana, nde̱e̱ Ala̱masiihu na paa,> koo <Nde̱e̱ beree piree,> ta-pana ma gata na̱a̱ bwa.
