Aꞌala̱masiihu na̱ acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ana ta̱be̱ aja̱a̱ wuce anaa ndaga iri na ta̱jikita̱na̱ na̱ iri na ta̱pa rukwanyan wana hyan anaa pira̱ ana Hwe̱n bwa takasa, aba nii ara.
Na̱ wana kunnu, sha̱a̱ ma suha̱nka̱ri suniinhin ki, igwataga ri ya̱nu na ja̱a̱ naa ndaga! Ga̱n ta ga̱mii bisa̱gi ma ta ibe̱ wuco.
Kuswa naa Yoo Butu
Maatiyu 24:29-31; Luka 21:25-28
<<Na̱ ha̱ni na ungwan na̱ mamboo maya̱nu mꞌba hwii ta̱hura̱ hyo̱,
<< <Uhwe̱n nii ta̱na̱ ta̱yincincin,
upyanda bwa jaa ta,
nꞌgwasu mꞌba nii naa kínai na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱,
iri na yaburagi ina ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ibe̱ nii naa zha̱a̱nta̱n.>
<<Naazhin inda̱i ga̱n Buyoo Butu wuci cuun na̱ ame̱ na arara, na̱ nꞌta̱kai o̱to̱ na̱ nꞌta̱shapaciga ta̱niimi.
Naazhin bwaa káji atuma ndaabwa, awuna̱a̱nyin bwa ana bwa takasa na̱ hwe̱n ta̱báni zhagu hwe̱n ta̱ꞌira̱ na̱ zuba zhagu ruꞌwa. Unii sha paa sa̱ra̱ri yana bwa swe̱n na̱ paaku ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱ba swe̱n.
Ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ uꞌwe̱e̱ na waanwan
Maatiyu 24:32-35; Luka 21:29-33
<<Too, insan ma yaan ri kuꞌwe̱e̱ na waanwan. Kiinda̱i aba̱ba ndaabwa ana ange̱ nii kina ana fo aba ke̱ne̱ ta̱tansan, iyan ta̱hyan ushuyo goki.
Kunnu taa ha̱ni na ga̱hin nda̱i iri ya̱nu nii ndaga, yansun ma ta̱hyan ubwa ha̱ni na kuswa goki, une̱e̱ re̱ na̱ adubo.
Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, awyatu na ha̱ni yana ajaa huwa̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱, sa̱i kiri ya̱nu ndagi hyo̱.
Ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n ta̱ja̱a̱ huwa̱ ta̱foga̱, ama mazama maniimi maza nama ja̱a̱ foga̱ mahwa.
Buza naa yan uhwe̱n koo ha̱ni na kuswa na Ala̱masiihu
Maatiyu 24:36-44
<<Buza naa yan ubwa hwe̱n koo ha̱ni na iri ya̱nu be̱e̱ nda, koo atuma na Hwe̱n ana ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, koo Buyoo, kaba Shin ta yan.
Naa ma ga̱ri, ishii aha̱nka̱ri ki, na̱ wana iyancin hwe̱n koo ha̱ni na iri ya̱nu be̱e̱ nda.
<<Unii sha haku butu naa hiin jaga ta̱hani, bwa hoosa̱ga̱ni agyama ndaabwa tuma na koo buya̱ bwaa naa nda, bubishi naa ta ha̱mba adubo xbunaa ga̱ri bugwataga ki.
Na̱ wana kunnu, naa ma ga̱ri wana iyancin ha̱ni na butu naa ina bwa ja̱a̱ giye. Buja̱a̱ ara ta̱giye koo na̱ shurugo koo na̱ gita hooso koo na̱ uka̱nrin ma taga ungwa koo na̱ bunwan maza.
xButa jaa he̱e̱n buza̱a̱ bujaa wuta̱ni na̱ nꞌrabi.
Iri na ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, nꞌnii bisa̱ga̱ ta koo buya̱ ta̱hyan, naa ma ga̱ri!>>

Awyatu o̱to̱ maga̱ga̱a̱gi xakwane̱ Yeesu
Maatiyu 26:1-5; Luka 22:1-2; Yoohana 11:45-53
Nꞌhwe̱n ree nꞌtabwa na hyan anje̱ Ubuki na Ta̱matamanrinyan Ta̱hanrinyan Nꞌina, na̱ Ubuki na Buroodi na za Yisiti. Sa̱i apirisiti na o̱to̱, na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi na nami Nꞌgira̱nshin, abaa wyanzan yo̱n na hyan akota̱ni Yeesu, akwane̱ buu ta̱swee.
Ama abaa hyaan, <<Shii na̱ nꞌhwe̱n na nꞌabuki na̱ wana xawyatu ta hiika̱hina̱ gagu.>>
Buꞌa̱ shani Yeesu mariga̱ na̱ Be̱tani
Maatiyu 26:6-13; Yoohana 12:1-8
Yeesu ma naa na̱ ina naa yaan butu na̱ Be̱tani, bunaa aba ta nꞌgana Siima, bunaa taꞌmꞌbaa suguma nasu tutuu. Be̱ ma re̱ shami, sa̱i buyaan buꞌa̱ bwa wuce na̱ mꞌmariga̱ nama nꞌshima nama mꞌbaa yuwa o̱to̱, nama ba nje̱ na̱ naridi kubwa, da̱ nii ndaashi naa aba nje̱ na̱ atari na rushama. Sa̱i bwa hwaaci bindaashi, bwa zooni mꞌba mariga̱ na̱ hyuhyu na Yeesu.
Aka̱ ana tanaa kaun, aba gware̱ sume̱, abaa mahyaan, <<Iba̱ shani aba kuha̱ni mariga̱ nama yuwa o̱to̱ kunta?
Ashi kasa̱a̱nha̱ni mꞌba mariga̱ nama ayuwa aba tanii wuta̱ yo̱ ka̱ na tuma na rwaru na butu, apa̱ga̱ni aꞌwa̱ta̱gi, uhurici?>> Aba ndaaki bwaa a̱ gagu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Ama Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Hakata ma bwa, iba̱ shani ga̱hin kaki bwa? Ai, iri na zumaa ta bwa nꞌndaaki.
Aꞌwa̱ta̱gi tanaa koya̱ hwe̱n na̱ ga̱hin, inii ara ta̱ta wyan ara koya̱ ha̱ni ga̱hin ribi, ama ga̱n shii koya̱ hwe̱n ga̱n naa na̱ ga̱hin.
Bunje̱ iri na bwaa ara ta̱nda, na bwa nꞌshani mariga̱ na̱ wana ta̱wuma̱na̱ ta̱niimi nata̱ wuci.
Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, hyo̱ paa abaa bisa̱ga̱ awyatu mazama nama zumaa na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana anii naa cita̱ga̱ iri na bwa nje̱, wana hyan xanaa tamanrinyaan bwa.>>
Yaahuda ra̱ni ta̱hyan bunii pana Yeesu
Maatiyu 26:14-16; Luka 22:3-6
Too, sa̱i Yaahuda Isikariyo̱ti buka̱ kaꞌupwa na ree ana be̱ tazwara, bwa ja̱a̱ paaka apirisiti na o̱to̱ na hyan bumaga̱ga̱a̱gi na̱ aba xbupa̱ni Yeesu.
Na aba hange̱ kunnu, aba hange̱ gama ta̱ꞌo̱to̱. Ubwa shani aba hin anii pana bwa ayuwa o̱to̱. Yaahuda bwaa wyanzan haruwa na hyan bupa̱ni Yeesu.
Yeesu re̱ shami na ta̱makwaakaa na̱ ana jwarigi buu
Maatiyu 26:17-25; Luka 22:7-14,21-23; Yoohana 13:21-30
Na̱ hwe̱n na yigo na Buki na Buroodi na za Yisiti, uhwe̱n na aba ta shinraan agwashe̱ na Ubuki na Ta̱matamanrinyan Ta̱hanrinyan Nꞌina, sa̱i ana jwarigi aba ha̱nta̱ni buu, <<Pee gaa ribi ta̱ja̱a̱ ta̱ꞌá̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni pa̱ri naka ta̱re̱ shami na Ta̱matamanrinyan Ta̱hanrinyan Nꞌina?>>
Sa̱i be̱ ka̱ji aba ree, ta̱hyan, <<Ta̱na̱ ma ce̱pe̱, inii ndaya buyaan butu ta̱ndani bisoso na̱ ma̱ni, ijwara̱ga bwa hyo̱ paa bwa ta̱ni.
Hyo̱ ina na bwa ta̱ni, hyan ma butu naa ina bwa, <Biwya̱ra̱mi hin, ta̱bisa̱a̱ udura̱ na bwaa re̱ shami na Ubuki na Ta̱matamanrinyan na̱ ana bwa tazwara.>
Buna̱maa bisa̱a̱ ma udura̱ na o̱to̱ na aba ma̱ da̱da̱da̱ naa ya̱na̱, una mꞌbaa hyo̱ iri na ga̱hin ribi. Kaba ga̱hin nii á̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni, isha̱a̱gi bwa shami.>>
Sa̱i aba ta̱ni ce̱pe̱, aba wuta̱ni hyo̱ komba̱ri haruwa na Yeesu be̱ tabishi wyan, aba a̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni paaku ta̱re̱ shami na Ubuki na Ta̱matamanrinyan kaun.
Na shurugo bwa nje̱, sa̱i Yeesu na̱ aꞌupwa na ree na jwarigi buu, aba ja̱a̱ ubwa ina.
Aba ma re̱ shami, sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, buka̱ bunaa ga̱n re̱ shami na̱a̱ bwa pina buna̱ma mꞌpana kana nꞌribici.>>
Sa̱i aba gware̱ sume̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, abaa hantaana buu wyatu ka̱a̱ ka̱a̱, <<Koo ga̱n ta?>>
Be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Buka̱ kuga̱hin upwa na ree taa na̱ma mꞌpana, bunaa ga̱n re̱ shamii gwaga ka̱ na̱a̱ bwa.
Ga̱n Buyoo Butu nii ꞌwa̱ haruwa na aba tataga mazama maniimi hasaa. Ama ta̱guma ta̱ne̱e̱ kubutu naa nii mꞌpana, manii hura̱a̱ga̱ bwa katama̱ncincin bwa!>>
Shami na ta̱makwaakaa na Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu
Maatiyu 26:26-30; Luka 22:14-20; 1 Akorinti 11:23-25
Aba ma re̱ shami, sa̱i Yeesu be̱ sha̱pi buroodi, be̱ gooji Hwe̱n, be̱ ya̱biza̱gi, be̱ pa̱ga̱ni ana jwarigi buu, ma hyaan, <<Raa ma, ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱niimi ta̱ta.>>
Na be̱ hwii, be̱ sha̱pi bikoopi naa ma̱ni nama iinabi, be̱ gooji Hwe̱n, be̱ pa̱ni wyan, aba swa̱gi nii be̱ hyo̱ ndaaba.
Sa̱i be̱ hin wyan, <<Na̱nna ta shi mahiin maniimi nama ta̱masha̱a̱ga̱ nama ga̱n nii wyashika na̱ wana wyatu hwarapi.
Mahanda mata ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, nꞌjaa gura̱a̱ swa ma̱ni nama ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ iinabi kiike̱nye̱n naa ga̱n nii swa nama fo na̱ nꞌta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n.>>
Na aba zhe̱nye̱n zha̱a̱ na ta̱yaba Hwe̱n, aba huri Biꞌundu naa Iꞌwe̱e̱ na Zaitu.
Biituru ja̱a̱ hyan buyancin Yeesu
Maatiyu 26:31-35; Luka 22:31-34; Yoohana 13:36-38
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Hyo̱ ninhin ga̱hin ja̱a̱ gida̱ga̱ga̱, iꞌnꞌga̱a̱, haruwa na aba ta̱gi na̱ takaada na Hwe̱n ta̱hyan,
<< <Ga̱n nii kuna buꞌiyo̱,
ika̱ra̱bi ga̱ta̱a̱gi.>
Bike̱nye̱n naa ga̱n hiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱, nꞌja̱maa gira ma ta̱wuta̱ Gaalili.>>
Na̱ ha̱ni bwa, Biituru bwa ra̱ni bwa hin, << Koo hyo̱ ndaaba gida̱ga̱gi, ga̱n jamaa gaa.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin Biituru, <<Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱, ba̱re na̱ gita, ta uka̱nrin bwa ta̱ ungwa maree, bu-nii cita̱ ta̱hyan bu-nꞌyancin mataatu.>>
Biituru bwaa hyaan ji, <<Koo ana̱ma nꞌkuna da̱nda̱ na̱ gaa, nꞌjaa hyan iiyancin.>> Kunnu taa hyo̱ ndaaba.
Yeesu nje̱ ro̱pe̱ na̱ cima na Gata̱samaani
Maatiyu 26:36-46; Luka 22:39-46
Aba huri paaki cima na aba ta hyan Gata̱samaani, sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Hunraana ma pina. Ga̱n nii jaga ma njé̱e̱ ro̱pe̱.>>
Be̱ sha̱pi Biituru na̱ Yaakubu na̱ Yoohana aba huri. Nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu be̱ makaki ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ ngwan na wuci.
Be̱ hin wyan, <<Ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱niimi ta̱shiragi ta̱guma haku ta̱hyan nꞌnii ꞌwa̱. Hunrana ma pina, inaa ga̱ri.>>
Na be̱ huri iyeebe ge̱, be̱ gii pwan na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n, be̱ nje̱ ro̱pe̱, be̱ hin, kumanii nda, xaya̱a̱cigi buu na̱ na̱nna ha̱ni na ngwan.
Be̱ nꞌgagani, be̱ hin, <<Ada, Abaaba nimi, komba̱ri ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌara nꞌndaabi. Nꞌya̱a̱cigi nii na̱nna koopi naa ngwan. Hyo̱ na̱ kunnu, nda iri na gaa ribi, shii iri na ga̱n ribi.>>
Na be̱ nje̱ ro̱pe̱, be̱ kúshiike̱ paaka aba taatu, be̱ wuta̱ni wyan na̱ nꞌrabi. Be̱ hin Biituru, <<Siima, bu-ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌrabi? Ka̱i, bi-jaa ara ta̱naa ga̱ri koo nata̱ ha̱ni ge̱?
Naa ma ga̱ri, inaa nda ro̱pe̱ na̱ wana ga̱hin jaa mamunsana kuta̱maanwyana. Mahanda bigata taa ribi, ama ta ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ba ga̱a̱.>>
Be̱ gura̱a̱ kushiika xbinje̱ ro̱pe̱, be̱e̱ cita̱ga̱ haku yigo.
Na be̱ kúshiike̱ mayaan, be̱ wuta̱ni wyan na̱ nꞌrabi, na̱ wana ayishe ndaaba cigi na̱ nꞌrabi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱. Aba yancin iri na hyan abishi buu.
Be̱ gura̱a̱ kúshiike̱ mataatu, be̱ hin wyan, <<Nꞌrabi nꞌta ga̱hin taagi ga̱hiin ha̱nka̱nka̱na̱? Nꞌrabi nꞌgii! Bike̱nye̱n nje̱ na aba nii pana ga̱n Buyoo Butu kuꞌnꞌara na nꞌwyatu na pinsan.
Hiika̱ ma xta̱nhuri! Nde̱e̱, bunaa nii mꞌpana taa wuce.>>
Akota̱ni Yeesu
Maatiyu 26:47-56; Luka 22:47-53; Yoohana 18:3-12
Yeesu ma nda mazama na̱ aba, sa̱i Yaahuda buka̱ kaba upwa na ree, bwa jaa na̱ awyatu hwarapi, aba há̱mba̱a̱gi nꞌsa̱nka̱ri na̱ nꞌsungo. Apirisiti na o̱to̱, na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin, na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na awyatu, aba káji wyan.
Yaahuda na nii pana wyan Yeesu, bwa hoo macíta̱gi na̱ aba ta̱hyan, <<Bunaa ga̱n nii hwaamana, bwa taa shi Yeesu. Kota̱na̱ ma be̱, ihuri, iha̱mba̱ga̱ be̱ ki.>>
Kunta̱wuta̱ nata̱ Yaahuda, bwa ta̱ta̱hura̱ paa Yeesu, bwa hin buu, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi.>> Sa̱i bwa hwaamani Yeesu.
Sa̱i awyatu aba kota̱ni Yeesu, aba ha̱mba̱gi buu kami.
Sa̱i buyaan buka̱, bunaa taꞌisa do̱ko̱ na̱ Yeesu, bwa cwáanrinye̱n sa̱nka̱ri, bwa ꞌya̱pi bugyama naa butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti ce̱be̱.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Nꞌshi butu naa nii hiika̱hina̱a̱ gagu nuu, na ga̱hin báni na̱ nꞌsa̱nka̱ri na̱ nꞌsungo na hyan iꞌnꞌkota̱ni?
Koya̱ hwe̱n ga̱n ta naa na̱ ga̱hin ma naa ga̱gaagana wyatu na̱ bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n, ga̱hin nꞌkota̱ncin. Ma nje̱ to̱n na̱ wana ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ iri na ta̱gi na̱ takaada na Hwe̱n icigi.>>
Kupita, ana jwarigi aba gida̱ga̱gi, aba ga̱a̱ buu be̱e̱ ka̱.
Buyaan baa bubwa jwarigi Yeesu ta̱baa, bwa taanicin da̱bi, kuzuzu na liilin bwaa ka̱. Aba hiin kota̱na̱ be̱,
bwa ba̱na̱a̱ni wyan, aba ra̱a̱ be̱ zuzu ndaabwa na̱ kai, bwa gidigi wa̱ra̱.
Yeesu kawyatu na taꞌyapa mazama
Maatiyu 26:57-68; Luka 22:54-55,63-71; Yoohana 18:13-14,19-24
Aba ꞌye̱e̱ Yeesu kuꞌina na butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti. Apirisiti na o̱to̱, na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya, na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin, aba mawuna̱ni kaun hyo̱.
Biituru bwa jwarigi Yeesu ta̱baa ta̱hakana. Bwa jwarigi buu ji hara̱ bambanu na ina na butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti. Bwa hunrani huku na̱ awyatu na ta ha̱mba ina ma ha̱nga ra.
Apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ hyo̱ awyatu na ta ꞌyapa mazama, abaa wyanzan ri na nii bisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan Yeesu nje̱ pinsan akwane̱ buu, ama aba de̱be̱ce̱.
Awyatu hwarapi aba cita̱gi ta̱be̱ nata̱ iri na Yeesu be̱ nje̱ce̱, sunu sundaaba suba ja̱a̱ci suka̱.
Hyo̱ mꞌmaya̱nu, ayaan aba gura̱a̱ cita̱ ta̱be̱ hiku ta̱hyan,
<<Ta̱hange̱ bihin, <Ga̱n nii huza̱a̱ga̱ Ina na Hwe̱n yana na wyatu aba tama, ma ma yaan na̱ nꞌhwe̱n taatu una shici ta̱ma nata̱ butu wuma.> >>
Hyo̱ na̱ kunnu, sunu sundaaba suba ja̱a̱ci suka̱.
Na butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti bwa hange̱ kunnu, bwa hiiki na̱ wyantancin ndaaba, bwa ha̱nta̱ni Yeesu, bwa hin, <<Bi-za ri na gaa gura̱ha̱na̱? Iri na aba cici na̱ wana ndaa paa?>>
Ama Yeesu be̱ ne̱e̱ wau, be̱ ra̱ncin be̱.
Butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti bwa gura̱a̱ hantana buu, <<Gaa ta shi Ala̱masiihu, Buyoo Hwe̱n na ga̱tu yaba?>>
Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Ga̱n ta. Ija̱a̱ ndaya ga̱n Buyoo Butu hunrani nii biin naa ara kataga na Hwe̱n na Hura̱gi Ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, ma cíin na̱ arara nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.>>
Sa̱i butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti bwa ha̱nji da̱bi ndaabwa, bwa hin, <<Ta̱ya̱ ta̱ha̱nga hiku ga̱tun wyanzan?
Ihange̱ hwashe̱ na be̱ nje̱! Imbata ga̱hin hin?>>
Sa̱i awyatu hyo̱ aba ꞌya̱pi mazama xakwane̱ buu.
Aka̱ aba ke̱ne̱ ta̱busa̱ga̱ buu macimi, aba ka̱da̱gi buu ayishe, aba imi buu ri, ma hyaan buu, <<Cita̱, buna buu ba̱sa̱ni!>> Ana ta ha̱mba aba sha̱pi buu abaa ꞌyama buu ri.
Biituru hin buyancin Yeesu
Maatiyu 26:69-75; Luka 22:56-62; Yoohana 18:15-18,25-27
Biituru bwa ne̱e̱ kunrin na bambanu na ina, kiiyaan be̱e̱ biꞌa̱ binaa nii ndaaka butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti tuma be̱ jaa kaun.
Na be̱ nda̱i Biituru ma ha̱nga ra, be̱ gwatagi bwa ga̱ri ga̱ri, be̱ hin be̱, <<Gaa maa, huku gaa ne̱e̱ na̱ Yeesu na Naazare yata!>>
Biituru bwa hin buyancin Yeesu, bwa gura̱a̱ hyan, <<Ga̱n maa, nꞌyancin iri na gaa cita̱ga̱ mahwa.>> Na Biituru bwa cici kunnu, bwa huri ka̱ta̱ku na bwa ina. Bike̱nye̱n be̱ ta̱ci du, uka̱nrin bwa ta̱ ungwa.+ :68 Bike̱nye̱n be̱ ta̱ci du, uka̱nrin bwa ta̱ ungwa: Ta̱yaan ta̱taga ta̱ka̱ ta̱za mazama mana̱nna.Na be̱ be̱e̱ biꞌa̱ be̱ gura̱a̱ ndaya bwa kaun, sa̱i be̱ bishi awyatu na isagi kaun, be̱ hin, <<Buna̱nna, bunaawan huku na̱ aba.>>
Biituru bwa gura̱a̱ hyan buyancin Yeesu.
Naa ke̱nye̱n be̱ huri ge̱, ana taꞌisaga do̱ko̱ na̱ Biituru aba hin bwa, <<Mahanda, gaa maa huku gaa ne̱e̱ na̱ aba. Shii butu naa Gaalili ta gaa shi nuu?>>
Ama Biituru bwaa mapagana nu ma taaga sa̱nsan na̱ aꞌuba̱ ndaaba, bwa hin, <<Ga̱n yancin butu naa ga̱hin nda mazama mandaabwa.>>
Bike̱nye̱n be̱ ta̱ci uka̱nrin bwa ta ungwa na hin reenu. Na̱ ha̱ni ya̱nu, Biituru bwa mata̱ma̱nriin mazama nama Yeesu be̱ tabisa̱ bwa ta̱hyan, <<Ta uka̱nrin bwa ta̱ ungwa maree, bu-nii cita̱ ta̱hyan bu-nꞌyancin mataatu.>> Na bwa mata̱ma̱nriin mazama maya̱nu, bwa pa̱shi nꞌungwa.

Aꞌye̱e̱ Yeesu kugwamina Bilaatu
Maatiyu 27:1-2,11-14; Luka 23:1-5; Yoohana 18:28-38
Ta na̱ bunwan maza apirisiti na o̱to̱, huku na̱ awyatu o̱to̱, na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na̱ hyo̱ awyatu na ta ꞌyapa mazama aba maga̱ga̱a̱gi. Sa̱i aba ka̱da̱gi Yeesu, aba ꞌye̱e̱ buu ku-Bilaatu na Arooma aba tasha̱a̱ bwa shi gwamina.
Bilaatu bwa ha̱nta̱ni Yeesu, <<Gaa taa shi bugwama naa Ayaahudiya?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Kunnunu kugaa hin.>>
Sa̱i apirisiti na o̱to̱ aba ke̱ne̱ ta̱cita̱ga̱ iri hwarapi na we̱ na aba hin binje̱.
Sa̱i Bilaatu bwa gura̱a̱ hantana buu bwa hin, <<Bi-jaa rana wyan na̱ hyo̱ iri na̱nna na aba na̱maa hyaan bi-nje̱?>>
Ama Yeesu be̱ hincin koori, ubwa shani Bilaatu bwa jikita̱ni.
Too, aya̱wa̱ni koya̱ ha̱ni na Buki na Ta̱matamanrinyan Ta̱hanrinyan nꞌina, Bilaatu ta tazhigaaga wyan butu ka̱ naa bwake̱ na̱ zhaaro bunaa awyatu aba ro̱pe̱ xata̱zhiga̱ni.
Butu naa tanaa na̱ ha̱ni ya̱nu na̱ zhaaro, ata nꞌgana be̱ Baraba, huku na̱ ana tahiika̱hina̱ gagu aba kwane̱ butu.
Sa̱i awyatu aba ja̱a̱ paaku Bilaatu, aba ro̱pe̱ bwa xandaaki wyan iri na bwa ya̱wa̱ni ta̱naa ndaakaka wyan na̱ koya̱ yo̱.
Bilaatu bwa ra̱ni wyan bwa hin, <<Iita̱zhiga̱a̱gi ma bugwama naa Ayaahudiya?>>
Na ta̱hyan buꞌe̱nshe̱n na̱ wana ta̱ribici Yeesu ta̱ta apirisiti na o̱to̱ aba íye̱ buu waabwa.
Ama na̱ bwa ha̱ni apirisiti na o̱to̱ aba hurupa̱ga̱ni awyatu ce̱be̱ xahin xata̱zhiga̱a̱gi wyan Baraba shii Yeesu.
Sa̱i Bilaatu bwa ha̱nta̱ni wyan, <<Iba̱ ga̱hin ribi xnꞌnje̱ na̱a̱ na̱nna naa ga̱hin nꞌga bugwama naa Ayaahudiya?>>
Aba ta̱a̱ni sunu suka̱ ma hyaan, <<xAka̱bi buu na̱ guguji!>>
Bilaatu bwa hin wyan, <<Wana ba̱? Uya̱ pinsan be̱ nje̱?>>
Aba duwa̱ni sunu ta̱taana xaka̱bi buu na̱ guguji.
Na ta̱hyan Bilaatu ribi na hyan bucaanhini awyatu me̱ sa̱i bwa ta̱zhiga̱a̱gi wyan Baraba. Na aba hwii Yeesu nꞌdunduun ta̱zura, bwa pa̱ni buu kasooja xaka̱bi buu.
Asooja nii ndaga Yeesu umuntun
Maatiyu 27:27-31; Yoohana 19:2-3
Asooja aba huri na̱ Yeesu zhagu baariki, bambanu na ka̱ta̱ku na gwamina una aba ta hyan <<Piritooriyumu.>> Aba wuna̱ni hyo̱ asooja naa be̱e̱ ko.
Aba ta̱a̱ni buu uda̱bi na shenje na ne̱e̱ haku naa gwama, aba nje̱ bigita̱ naa sa̱pi aba huuta̱ni Yeesu na̱ hyuhyu.
Aba ke̱ne̱ buu ta̱naa zumaana azumanu na hwashe̱, ma hyaan, <<xNꞌhwe̱n nꞌndaabi nꞌduwa̱ni hwarapi, bugwama naa Ayaahudiya.>>
Abaa basagana buu angwo na̱ hyuhyu, ma busa̱ga̱ buu macimi. Aba sa̱nsain na̱ arunrun ndaaba na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n kuta̱hyan anii paga buu hunrun.
Na aba hwii ta̱ndaaka Yeesu hyo̱ umuntun, sa̱i aba ya̱a̱cigi buu bwa da̱bi na ta̱gwama, aba ta̱a̱ni buu nde̱e̱be̱ ꞌwana. Naazhin aba ba̱ha̱ni buu ha na hyan aka̱bi buu na̱ guguji.
Aka̱bi Yeesu na̱ guguji
Maatiyu 27:32-44; Luka 23:26-43; Yoohana 19:17-27
Sa̱i kuuyaan butu bunaa aba ta nꞌgana Siima, butu naa Kuraane, bushooba naa Aleka̱zanda na̱ Rufusu, bunaa tabáni aga bwa ma tá̱ni ce̱pe̱. Asooja aba shani bwa ga̱ga̱ga̱ xbusha̱pi uguguji na Yeesu.
Aba ꞌye̱e̱ Yeesu kupa̱ri naka aba ta nꞌgana na̱ n-Ta̱yaahudiya Gola̱gota, ane̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan, <<Ka̱a̱ta̱ra̱ na Hyuhyu>>.
Kaba aba tapana buu ma̱ni nama iꞌwe̱e̱ na iinabi huku na̱ mꞌmariga̱ nama muru+ :23 mariga̱ nama muru: Ushi mayaan mariga̱ nama shi haku njibi na suguma.ama be̱ ga̱a̱ ta̱swa.
Too, sa̱i asooja aba ka̱bi buu na̱ guguji. Aba mahoosa̱ga̱ni aꞌwana nde̱e̱be̱ kaba kaba, aba nje̱ umuntun na ta̱kasa xanda̱i iri na koo buya̱ bwaa ara ta̱da̱ba.
Utasha bike̱nye̱n naa ta̱ruma ta̱tundushi nata̱ bunwan maza aba takaba Yeesu.
Na̱ bwa guguji na aba takaba buu aba ta̱ ta̱yaan ta̱ꞌyantan nata̱ tacita̱ iri na aba tahyan binje̱, <<Bugwama naa Ayaahudiya.>>
Aba gura̱a̱ kaba azumba̱ ree, buka̱ na̱ nꞌkataga, buka̱ na̱ nꞌkagura̱.+ :27: Ta̱yaan ta̱taga ta̱ta mꞌbaa aaya 28 kunna: Na̱nna tashi ta̱ciga̱ nata̱ acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ba tacita̱ ta̱bata ciga̱, ta̱hyan, <<Aja̱a̱ yibaku buu huku na̱ ana pinsan.>>Awyatu na tanaa hura̱ga̱ kaun abaa zuga buu aza̱zama na hwashe̱ ma cwaagaga buu, ma hyaan, <<Ka̱i! Nde̱e̱ sugaa ne̱e̱. Gaa naa tahyan bu-nii huza̱ Ina na Hwe̱n, u-gura̱a̱ ma wuun na̱ nꞌhwe̱n nꞌtaatu,
too, mabiha̱ni, u-cíin kuguguji yata.>>
Kunnu taa apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin abaa gisa Yeesu mazama nama we̱, abaa mahyaan, <<Bibiha̱ni ayaan ama ta be̱ a̱rici ta̱biha̱na̱ hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱!
Uꞌala̱masiihu na̱nna, wa̱i bugwama naa Isiraaꞌila, xbuciin na̱ guguji yata na hyan kuta̱nda̱i ta̱pa̱ni nꞌgata nii be̱!>> Azumba̱ na aba takaba huku na̱ Yeesu, abaa zuga buu taa mazama nama uwa̱.
Ta̱ꞌwa̱ nata̱ Yeesu
Maatiyu 27:45-56; Luka 23:44-49; Yoohana 19:28-30
Na̱ hwe̱n da̱, ta̱yincincin ta̱ba guna̱ni hyo̱ ta̱ba ce̱nye̱n ubwa wuciha̱ni zhagu ta̱ruma ta̱taatu nata̱ hwe̱n.
Na̱ nꞌta̱ruma ta̱taatu nata̱ hwe̱n Yeesu be̱ taani nu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, be̱ hin, <<E̱lai, E̱lai, lama sabaka̱taani?>> ta̱hyan, <<Uhwe̱n nimi, Uhwe̱n nimi, iba̱ shani gaa mꞌmo̱nshe̱n?>>
Ayaan na isagi kaun aba hange̱, aba hin, <<Ha̱nga, be̱ nu ma nꞌga bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Iliya.>>
Sa̱i buyaan buka̱ ndaaba bwa gidigi, bwa jwábani sooso na̱ ma̱ni nama iinabi nama sa̱mbi. Bwa tutuba̱ni wuun na̱ angwo na ꞌwe̱e̱, bwa cikaa Yeesu wana hyan biswa̱. Bwa hin, <<Isa ma, xta̱ngwataaga ta̱nnda̱i koo Iliya nii cíin, buciinha̱ni buu kaun.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ta̱a̱ni nu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, be̱ ciinha̱ni nꞌhunjo̱, be̱ ꞌwi.
Uzuzu na ta naa na̱ ame̱ na Ina na Hwe̱n bwa maha̱nda̱ga̱su maree ta da̱da̱da̱ bwa ciin kunrin.
Usooja na o̱to̱ na taꞌisa kaun bwa gwatagi kiibe̱ ꞌwi, bwa hin, <<Mahanda, butu na̱nna Buyoo Hwe̱n ta.>>
Ayaan a̱ aba tanaa, ana taꞌisaga katakii, aba gwataagi. Na̱ ame̱ ndaaba Maariyamu na Magadalina, na̱ Saloomi, na̱ Maariyamu ada̱a̱da̱ na Yaakubu na Njeke na̱ na Yusufu.
Ata jwárige̱ Yeesu ta na̱ Gaalili ma ndaakaka buu iri na be̱ ribi. Ayaan a̱ taa ahwarapi ana Hurushaliima ana tahure huku nii be̱ atanaa taa kaun.
Ta̱wuma̱na̱ nata̱ Yeesu
Maatiyu 27:57-61; Luka 23:50-56; Yoohana 19:38-42
-43 Na shurugo bwa nje̱ buyaan butu Yusufu bwa jaa. Bwa shi butu naa báni ce̱pe̱ na Arimatiya, bwa shi bunaa bina̱ kawyatu o̱to̱ na ta ꞌyapa mazama, bwa taha̱mbaga xbunda̱i ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n. Wana ta̱hyan ane̱e̱ na̱ shiri wana hwe̱n na bunwan na shi na ha̱nka̱na̱, Yusufu bwa maginii, bwa ja̱a̱ ku-Bilaatu, bwa ha̱nta̱ni xbupa̱ni be̱ ruꞌwa̱ naru ta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ Yeesu.
Bilaatu bwa jikita̱ni na bwa hange̱ ta̱hyan Yeesu hoo ꞌwa̱. Sa̱i bwa nꞌgani usooja na o̱to̱, bwa ha̱nta̱ni ta̱hyan koo Yeesu hoo ꞌwa̱.
Na bwa hange̱ mashi kunnu na̱ nu na bwa sooja, bwa pa̱ni Yusufu ruꞌwa̱ naru ta̱ꞌwaba.
Yusufu bwa shé̱e̱n zuzu na liilin na ta̱wuma̱na̱, bwa cíinha̱ni ta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ ruꞌwa̱ naru Yeesu bwa rigi na̱ bwa zuzu na liilin, bwa zwa̱ga̱ni na̱ uya̱ na aba takinda̱ na̱ apaga. Naazhin bwa riinha̱ni yaan tari bwa guna̱ni nu na uya̱.
Maariyamu na Magadalina, na̱ Maariyamu ada̱a̱da̱ na Yusufu, aba nda̱i uya̱ paaka aba wuma̱ni ruꞌwa̱ naru Yeesu.

Ta̱hiika̱ nata̱ Yeesu kuꞌuya̱
Maatiyu 28:1-8; Luka 24:1-12; Yoohana 20:1-10
Na hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya bwa huri, Maariyamu na Magadalina, na̱ Saloomi, na̱ Maariyamu ada̱a̱da̱ na Yaakubu, aba shé̱e̱n mariga̱ nama nꞌshima, na hyan xashani ta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ Yeesu.
Na̱ hwe̱n na yigo na nꞌhwe̱n nꞌta̱nda̱ra̱, hwe̱n ma punshin, aba huri kuꞌuya̱.
Ta aba wuco uya̱, abaa maga̱gaaga ta̱hyan, <<Iyaa ta nii ta̱nriinha̱na̱na̱ utari kuꞌuya̱?>>
Na aba wuci kuꞌuya̱, aba bwe̱ yishe, aba nda̱i utari na yaburi na aba taguna̱ni uya̱ ahoo riinha̱na̱ wuun.
Na aba ta̱ni uya̱, aba nda̱i sa̱mba̱ri na hunrani nii biin naa kataga, bwa taani da̱bi na tande̱ paawu, aba hange̱ rukwanyan.
Bwa hin wyan, <<Ta-ha̱nga ma rukwanyan. Inii wyanzan Yeesu na Naazare na aba takaba na̱ guguji. Biza pina. Bihiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱. Nde̱e̱ ma paaka aba tataahini buu kana.
Hura̱ ma, ibishi ana jwarigi buu, hyo̱ na̱ Biituru, ta̱hyan bina̱maa gira ma wuco Gaalili. Piree kata ga̱hin nii ndaya buu, haruwa na be̱ taabisa̱ ma.>>
Aꞌa̱ aba ga̱a̱ uya̱, aba huri nꞌsumo̱, ma jikita̱ga̱ nꞌrukwanyan, aba nje̱ kuma̱. Aba bishici koo butu na̱ wana ahange̱ rukwanyan.
[Ta̱yaan ta̱taga ta̱ka̱ nata̱ yigo ta za aaya na 9-20]
Yeesu mabisa̱a̱ ki-Maariyamu na Magadalina
Maatiyu 28:9-10; Yoohana 20:11-18
Na Yeesu be̱ hiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱, na̱ bunwan maza kuhwe̱n na yigo na nꞌhwe̱n nꞌta̱nda̱ra̱, Maariyamu na Magadalina ta tagira buu ta̱ndaya, buꞌa̱ naa be̱ taba̱ha̱na̱ wyatu na hira̱ na we̱ ta̱nda̱ra̱.
Bwaa a̱ bwa huri, bwa bishi awyatu na be̱ tanaawan na ba, ana ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ ta̱gura na̱ nꞌungwa.
Na aba hange̱ ta̱hyan Yeesu ne̱e̱ buwuma, bwaa a̱ tandái buu, aba pa̱ncin nꞌgata na̱ ri naa bwa hin.
Na maya̱nu mꞌba huri, Yeesu be̱ gura̱a̱ bisa̱a̱ hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱ na̱ nꞌyaan mꞌpirwa goo kayaan reeko ana jwarigi buu, ana tanaa nꞌta̱hani banu ce̱pe̱.
Aba reeko ya̱nu, na aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱, aba bishi ana tabwata, aba taa maa aba pa̱ncin nꞌgata kiri na aba bishi wyan.
Na ha̱ni bwa huri, Yeesu be̱ báncinye̱n paaka upwa na̱a̱ ka̱, ha̱ni na abaa re̱ shami. Be̱ ndaaki wyan bashi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ wana ta̱tibici mazama mandaaba na̱ nꞌta̱pa̱ncin nꞌgata kana bishi wyan ta̱hyan bihiiki.
Be̱ gura̱a̱ hyan wyan, <<Hura̱ ma kope hyo̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana, ibisa̱gi hyo̱ wyatu mazama nama zumaa.
Koo buya̱ pa̱nii gata aba nje̱ be̱ baba̱tiisa̱ma Hwe̱n nii biha̱na̱ be̱, ama koo buya̱ pa̱nciin gata, Hwe̱n nii ndaaka be̱ suuga̱ nasu ngwan.
Nde̱e̱ iri na ana pa̱ni nꞌgata na̱ ga̱n baa ara ta̱nda na: Na̱ nꞌta̱kai ta̱niimi+ :17 Na̱ nꞌta̱kai ta̱niimi Ushi iri ka̱ na̱ Na̱ nꞌruzha̱a̱ runiimi. aba nii ba̱ha̱na̱ wyatu na hira̱ na we̱. Aba nii cita̱ga̱ mazama nꞌta̱ce̱pe̱ goo goo.
Aba nii ha̱mba̱a̱ga̱ suhwaa na̱ nꞌara nꞌndaaba koo agura̱a̱ swa manwyanrin, mꞌba jaa nda wyan koori. Aba nii cagudaagaga ana ha̱ngagici sa̱ nꞌara, akuda̱gagi.>>
Asha̱pi Yeesu zhagu ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱
Luka 24:50-53; Tuma 1:9-11
Na Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwa hwii ta̱bisa̱ga̱ wyan mazama, Hwe̱n bwa sha̱pi buu da̱da̱da̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, be̱ hunrani na̱ ara kataga na Hwe̱n.
Ana jwarigi, aba ba̱ni, abaa jabaga kope, ma bisa̱ga̱ wyatu mazama nama zumaa. Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu be̱ ne̱e̱ huku na̱ aba, be̱ shani iri na ta̱jikita̱na̱ na abaa ndaga ibe̱ bisa̱a̱ wyatu mazama mandaaba mashi mahanda.
LUK - Pangu
Luka
Luk
Luka
Mazama nama zumaa nama Yeesu kuta̱taga nata̱ Luka
Mazama nama zumaa nama Yeesu kuta̱taga nata̱
Luka
Iri na ta̱yansun na yigo
Butu naa ta̱gi mazama nama zumaa nama takaada na Luka, ulikita bwa tasha, butashici Buyaahudiya. Atasha̱a̱ ta̱hyan butaꞌura̱ku na̱ aka̱ ana Yeesu be̱ tazwara. Atasha̱a̱ ta̱hyan atataga takaada na̱nna na̱ yo̱ 59-63 koo 70-80 na̱ nꞌta̱mantan nata̱ Yeesu. Luka tataagaga muu kuuyaan butu Tiyoofilu. Bwa butu tasha butu naa ca̱ma̱ncin ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ Rooma. Tiyoofilu butahoo ha̱nga mazama maka̱ nama zumaa nama Yeesu. Sa̱i Luka bwa ribi ta̱hyan xbuyansun hiku, ta̱hyan kunnu mꞌba shi, iri na bwa hange̱.
Luka bwa ta̱a̱ga̱gi bwa hyo̱ ki mꞌba mazama. Na sha̱pi ta̱ma̱ncin nata̱ Yeesu, ujabagu nde̱e̱be̱, utuma nde̱e̱be̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwa̱ ta̱nde̱e̱be̱, na̱ hiiko nde̱e̱be̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱, hyo̱ ki kiꞌibe̱ iri be̱ ndagi.
Na̱ bwa ha̱ni Arooma tare̱ kai na ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Isiraaꞌila ma ndaaka wyan ta̱gwama na̱ nꞌtugusu. Kaisa butasha bugwama naa o̱to̱ naa hyo̱ ce̱nye̱n nata̱ asooja na Rooma aba tare̱ na̱ gyasa.
Luka tataga takaada na̱nna wana hyan bubisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan Yeesu ta shi bunaa Hwe̱n bwa tacita̱ hiku, unii káji, bibiha̱ni wyatu nde̱e̱be̱.
Iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱
Iri na ta̱yansun na yigo :1-4Ta̱ma̱ncin nata̱ Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ nata̱ Yeesu :5--2:52Tuma na Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma :1-20Baba̱tiisa̱ma na Yeesu na̱ nꞌta̱maanwyana ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ na̱ ahira̱ :21--4:13Tuma na Yeesu na̱ Gaalili :14--9:50Yeesu ga̱a̱ Gaalili zhagu Hurushaliima :51--19:27Utuma na Yeesu na ta̱makwaakaa na̱ ngwan nde̱e̱be̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwa̱ ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ :28--23:56Ta̱hiika̱ nata̱ Yeesu kuta̱ꞌwa̱, na̱ nꞌta̱mabisa̱a̱ hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱, na̱ katanu nde̱e̱be̱ zhagu ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ :1-53
Ri na shani Luka // bwa ta̱gi takaada na̱nna
Iizumani, butu o̱to̱ Tiyoofilu.
Awyatu hwarapi nje̱ xata̱gi kiꞌiri be̱ na ndaga na̱ ha̱ni nda̱tu.
Ata̱gi iri na ga̱tu hange̱ paaka na nda̱i iri ya̱nu nꞌsuyishe sundaaba ta na̱ ayigo, na̱ ana bisa̱gi awyatu mazama nama Hwe̱n+ :2 Hwe̱n: Ruyaan ruzha̱a̱ naru aba ta nꞌgana Hwe̱n taru shi Gumataana.Na̱ wana kunnu, butu o̱to̱ Tiyoofilu, na̱ wana ta̱hyan nꞌgwataagani, ga̱n ha̱nta̱a̱ni iri ya̱nu ki hyo̱, ta nꞌta̱pasa ta̱nde̱e̱be̱, ga̱n nda̱i uzumaa maa taagaga wuun ki haruwa na ibe̱ ndagi hyo̱.
Nꞌnje̱ na̱nna na̱ wana hyan u-yansun wuun, ushi mahanda haruwa na abaa ga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni wuun.
Butuma naa Hwe̱n // cici ta̱ma̱ncin nata̱ // Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma
Nii ke̱nye̱n naa Hirudu bwa tasha bugwama naa ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya, uyaan upirisiti+ :5 upirisiti: Gwatana paa Haruwa na Ayaan Kala̱ma aba Shi, kala̱ma na <<Pirisiti>>.tanaa na aba ta nꞌgana Zakaariya, na biigudu naa apirisiti na mꞌbáni ina na Abiija. Ruzha̱a̱ naru a̱yo ruba shi Aliizabatu, be̱ taa maa be̱ báni bikorogo naa Haruuna.
Hyo̱ reeko ndaaba ashi awyatu na bina̱ ku-Hwe̱n, aba jwarigi hyo̱ Nꞌgira̱nshin na̱ iri na Hwe̱n bwa hin xanje̱.
Ama aba za mꞌmwaan na̱ wana Aliizabatu de̱be̱ce̱ ta̱mantan, hyo̱ reeko ndaaba aba hoo nꞌgaga.
Yaan hwe̱n, Zakaariya be̱ ne̱e̱ na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n na Ayaahudiya+ :8 Ina na Hwe̱n na Ayaahudiya: Gwatana paa Haruwa na Ayaan Kala̱ma aba Shi.na̱ Hurushaliima. Be̱e̱ nda tuma nde̱e̱be̱ na upirisiti haruwa na aba hoosa̱ga̱gi xnꞌgudu nꞌnaa nda.
Aba ka̱shi Zakaariya kiigudu nde̱e̱be̱ na̱ umuntun na ta̱kasa, haruwa na aba sha̱a̱gi apirisiti xanaa nda. Aba ka̱shi buu ta̱hyan xbita̱ni ame̱ na Ina na Hwe̱n, bipé̱e̱ nꞌhyoo na nꞌturaare na̱ ame̱.
Awyatu hwarapi aba ne̱e̱ na̱ sa̱ra̱ri ma nda ro̱pe̱ nii ke̱nye̱n naa be̱ tanaa pé̱e̱ turaare.Altar of incense|hk00260c.tif|col|LUK 1:8-17|Horace Knowles|Bizhe̱nke̱n naa nꞌhyoo na nꞌturaare ta̱pa|1:11Kuutuma naa Hwe̱n+ :11 Kuutuma naa Hwe̱n: Gwatana paa Haruwa na Ayaan Kala̱ma aba Shi, kala̱ma na <<Butuma naa Hwe̱n>>.bwa wuce waabe̱, bwa e̱she̱ nii biin naa kataga naa bizhe̱nke̱n naa nꞌhyoo na nꞌturaare ta̱pa+ :11 bizhe̱nke̱n naa nꞌhyoo na nꞌturaare ta̱pa: Gwatana paa Haruwa na Ayaan Kala̱ma aba Shi.Na Zakaariya be̱ nda̱i butuma naa Hwe̱n, bigata nde̱e̱be̱ be̱ ta̱ buga̱, rukwanyan ruba kota̱ni buu.
Ama butuma naa Hwe̱n bwa hin buu, <<Ta-ha̱nga rukwanyan, Zakaariya. Hwe̱n tara̱ni ro̱pe̱ ndaa. Aliizabatu aꞌeeboo ana̱maa mantana be̱e̱ binaa wya̱ri, bi-nii pa buu ruzha̱a̱ Yoohana.
Binii sha naa na̱maa shaana u-hange̱ gama na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱da̱ri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, awyatu hwarapi aba nii ha̱nga gama nii be̱,
na̱ wana be̱e̱ binii sha butu naa bina̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ku-Hwe̱n. XBita swa mahwa ma̱ni nama ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ ꞌwe̱e̱ na iinabi, koo iyaanyini na be̱ nii swa inaa nda buu. Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n nii naa huku nii be̱ ta aba ma̱nta̱n buu.
Binii kúshihine̱ awyatu hwarapi na Isiraaꞌila ku-Butu O̱to̱ ndaaba Hwe̱n.
Binii sha naa nii naa iyeebe na Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n, na̱ nꞌta̱kai nii gata naa bure haku Iliya, butu naa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama+ :17 butu naa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama: Gwatana paa Haruwa na Ayaan Kala̱ma aba Shi, kala̱ma na <<Ana ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama>>.Binii ꞌwaan hunranhunran na gama kashoo na̱ mꞌmwaan nꞌndaaba. Binii gura̱a̱ kúshihine̱ awyatu na tibici mazama ashi ana tibi, aba jwarigi yo̱n na bina̱. Kunnu bwa nii a̱sa̱a̱ga̱na̱ nꞌgata na nꞌwyatu, ajaa nda̱i Butu O̱to̱ ndaaba Hwe̱n.>>
Zakaariya be̱ hin butuma naa Hwe̱n, <<Na ga̱n yansun iri ya̱nu na gaa cici inii sha mahanda? Ga̱n na nꞌshi butu naa ange̱, buꞌa̱ niimi taa bwa hura̱ni ta̱ma̱ncin.>>
Butuma naa Hwe̱n bwa hin, <<Ga̱n ta Jibiraaꞌilu, bunaa ta isa na̱ aꞌuba̱ na Hwe̱n. Hwe̱n taꞌnꞌkáji maa bisa̱ maya̱nu mazama nama zumaa.
Ta na gaa ra̱ncin ta̱hyan mazama maniimi mashi mahanda, bi-jaa gura̱a̱ ara mazama ta̱cita̱, bi-nii naa wau ji kiike̱nye̱n naa ta̱ma̱ncin jaa ta̱ba nje̱.>>
Awyatu aba hunraani, aba hambe̱ ta̱bani nata̱ Zakaariya, abaa maga̱gaaga nꞌsume̱ sundaaba ta̱hyan mbata shani be̱ cé̱e̱ bike̱nye̱n kunna na̱ ame̱ na Ina na Hwe̱n.
Na be̱ báni, be̱ a̱rici ta̱cita̱ mazama na̱ nu. Be̱e̱ ndaakaka wyan mazama kuna̱ ara, aba e̱nshe̱n ta̱hyan Hwe̱n bisa̱a̱ buu yaanyini na̱ ame̱ na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n, ta shani be̱ a̱rici ta̱cita̱ mazama.
Na nꞌhwe̱n nꞌnde̱e̱be̱ na nꞌtuma na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n mꞌba hwii, be̱ kwashe̱e̱ke̱ ina.
Na nꞌhwe̱n mꞌba huri ge̱, aꞌa̱yo Aliizabatu, aba cigi huba̱, be̱ ne̱e̱ na̱ ina mꞌpyanda nꞌta be̱ ba̱ncin sa̱ra̱ri.
Aliizabatu be̱ hin, <<Hwe̱n ta ndaaki na̱nna, ta bwa hange̱ ambishiri nimi ta̱hakana, bwa nꞌya̱a̱cigi na̱ nꞌkogi na̱ aꞌuba̱ na aya̱too.>>
Butuma naa Hwe̱n wuce // ki-Maariyamu
Na Aliizabatu be̱ nje̱ mꞌpyanda nꞌcininhin na huba̱, Hwe̱n bwa káji butuma ndaabwa Jibiraaꞌilu kuyaan ce̱pe̱ na ne̱e̱ na̱ Gaalili, una aba ta nꞌgana Naazare.
Ubwa káji be̱ tuma paakii yaan be̱e̱ biꞌa̱ naa aba ta nꞌgana Maariyamu, binaa aba tahoo pana buyaan butu Yusufu na biikorogo naa bugwama Dawuda, xbunaa zhaa.
Naa butuma naa Hwe̱n bwa wuce waabe̱, bwa zumani buu, bwa hin buu, <<Gaa, Hwe̱n ndaaki rubara̱ka, ubwa ne̱e̱ huku na̱ gaa.>>
Na Maariyamu be̱ hange̱ zumanu, aba shaani buu suro̱be̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, be̱ hin nii gata nde̱e̱be̱, aya̱ zumanu nu nuunu.
Butuma naa Hwe̱n bwa hin buu, <<Ta-ha̱nga rukwanyan, Maariyamu. Bi-shi bunaa Hwe̱n bwa ka̱shi, bwaa ndaaki rubara̱ka.
Gaa nii ciga̱ huba̱, u-ma̱ncin be̱e̱ biwya̱ri, u-pa̱ buu ruzha̱a̱ Yeesu.
Binii sha butu o̱to̱. Aba nii hyan buu Buyoo Hwe̱n na Hura̱gi Ta̱ꞌo̱to̱. Uhwe̱n ta nii pana buu bizhe̱nke̱n naa ta̱gwama nata̱ daada nde̱e̱be̱ Dawuda.
Binii ha̱mba̱ga̱ mahwa ta̱gwama nata̱ Isiraaꞌila, ta̱gwama ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ ta̱ba jaa huwa̱ mahwa!>>
Maariyamu be̱ ha̱nta̱ni butuma naa Hwe̱n, <<Na iri ya̱nu be̱ nii nda, na ga̱n tayancin butu wya̱ri?>>
Butuma naa Hwe̱n bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n taa nii cíin binaa huku na̱ gaa, ta̱kai nata̱ Uhwe̱n na Hura̱gi Ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ta̱ba na̱maa guna̱a̱na̱. Na̱ wana kunnu, be̱e̱ binaa bure naa gaa mantan, anii hyan buu Buyoo Hwe̱n.
Nde̱e̱ ayami Aliizabatu, bunaa aba tahyan bujaa mantan, niina yana biꞌmꞌbaa huba̱ mꞌpyanda nꞌcininhin, hyo̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌnꞌga ta̱nde̱e̱be̱.
Iri za na nii ngazana Hwe̱n ta̱nda.>>
Maariyamu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Ga̱n bugyama naa Hwe̱n ta. Iri ya̱nu xishi haruwa na gaa hin.>> Na be̱ hwii ta̱cita̱ga̱, butuma bwa huri.
Maariyamu ja̱a̱ ki-Aliizabatu
Nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu, Maariyamu be̱ ta̱cii ke̱nye̱n, be̱ nje̱ shiri, be̱ huri yaan ce̱pe̱ na ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌundu na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya.
Na be̱ wuci, be̱ ta̱ni ina na Zakaariya, be̱ zumani Aliizabatu.
Na Aliizabatu be̱ hange̱ zumanu, bibibe̱e̱ binaa ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ nde̱e̱be̱ be̱ mado̱ge̱. Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ wuce, be̱ ne̱e̱ huku nii be̱.
Aliizabatu be̱ ta̱a̱ni nu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, be̱ hin, <<Gaa bunaa Hwe̱n bwa hura̱gi ta̱ndaaka rubara̱ka ta gaa shi kaꞌa̱, be̱e̱ binaa ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ ndaa be̱ shi naa rubara̱ka!
Na na̱nna iri na gama be̱ wuce na ada̱a̱da̱ na Butu O̱to̱ niimi aba jaa wa̱ka̱mi?
Bike̱nye̱n naa ga̱n tahange̱ azumanu ndaa, be̱e̱ binaa ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ nimi be̱ mado̱ge̱ na̱ wana ta̱ga̱da̱ri.
Bunaa rubara̱ka ta gaa shi na gaa pa̱nii gata ta̱hyan tuma na̱nna na Hwe̱n bwa káji wakaa nii sha mahanda.>>
Zha̱a̱ na Maariyamu // na ta̱yaba Hwe̱n
Maariyamu be̱ hin,
<<Bigata niimi ya̱ba̱ni Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n.
Ga̱n ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ga̱da̱ri wana Hwe̱n nimi na mꞌbiha̱ni,
na̱ wana umata̱ma̱nriin na̱ ga̱n,
koo na ga̱n shi bugyama ndaabwa
naa shici yaanyini na bina̱.
Niina ye̱e̱, hyo̱ awyatu aba nii naa ma nꞌhyaan
Hwe̱n nꞌndaaki rubara̱ka,
na̱ wana Hwe̱n na hura̱gi ta̱kai na̱ nꞌta̱gwama
bwa nꞌndaaki iri na yaburi.
Bwa taa shi bunaa ne̱e̱ sabu bwa za pinsan.
Ambishiri ndaabwa za haru mahwa
kawyatu na pa̱ wuun hunrun.
Na̱ ara ndaabwa na kai ta bwa nje̱
iri hwarapi na yaburagi.
Bwa ga̱ci awyatu na ma̱a̱
suhyu sundaaba ta̱mashapaciga
na̱ hyo̱ iri na aba ne̱e̱ na̱ ruwashi
na̱ be̱ nii gata ndaaba.
Bwa ciinha̱ni nꞌgwama na̱ nꞌta̱gwama ta̱ndaaba,
bwa sha̱pa̱cigi ana shici koo yaanyini.
Bwa ciga̱hini ana rumunro̱n na̱ iri na zumaa,
bwa pa̱ ana mꞌbaa iri na nꞌara nꞌndaaba sumo̱,
aba huri maha̱nda̱.
Bwa ta̱guni agyama ndaabwa Isiraaꞌila,
bwa ta matamanrinyan ta̱ndaaka
awyatu ndaabwa ambishiri,
na̱ wana haruwa na bwa na sha̱a̱
na̱ adaadoo nda̱tu,
Ibiraahin na̱ mꞌmwaan nꞌndaabwa,
yo̱o̱ na̱ nꞌyo̱.>>
Maariyamu be̱ nje̱ mꞌpyanda nꞌtaatu huku na̱ Aliizabatu, naazhin be̱ kwashe̱e̱ke̱ ina.
Ta̱ma̱ncin nata̱ // Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma
Na ha̱ni bwa nje̱ na Aliizabatu be̱e̱ mantan be̱e̱ binde̱e̱be̱, be̱ ma̱ncin be̱e̱ binaa wya̱ri.
Awyatu na nꞌharu na̱ adiindiin nde̱e̱be̱ aba hange̱ iri na Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n bwa ndaaki buu ambishiri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, aba nje̱ ta̱ga̱da̱ri huku nii be̱.
Na be̱e̱ bibe̱ nje̱ nꞌhwe̱n nꞌta̱ndatu, aba jaa xaꞌya̱pi buu ta̱wya̱ri, apa̱ buu ruzha̱a̱ naru baaba nde̱e̱be̱ Zakaariya.
Da̱a̱da̱ nde̱e̱be̱ aba hin, <<Aaꞌa, anii pa buu ruzha̱a̱ Yoohana.>>
Aba hin buu, <<Buza yaan butu naa mꞌbaa ruzha̱a̱ ruya̱nu na̱ diin ninhin.>>
Nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu, aba ndaaki ashin mazama na̱ ara, ruya̱ ruzha̱a̱ be̱e̱ pa be̱e̱.
Zakaariya be̱ nje̱ haruwa na hyan xapa̱ni buu iri na ta̱ꞌyantan ta̱taga+ :63 iri na ta̱ꞌyantan ta̱taga: Ta shi allo.be̱ ta̱, <<Ruzha̱a̱ runde̱e̱be̱ ruta rushi Yoohana!>> Hyo̱ awyatu na tanaa piree aba jikita̱ni.
Na̱ nꞌta̱naa huwa̱ ta̱ta ruzha̱a̱, Zakaariya be̱ a̱ri mazama ta̱cita̱, be̱ ke̱ne̱ Hwe̱n ta̱yaba.
Awyatu na nꞌharu aba hange̱ rukwanyan ma jikita̱ga̱ na̱ iri na nje̱, mazama mꞌba maga̱ci kope na̱ ce̱nye̱n nata̱ ne̱e̱ na̱ undu na ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya.
Koo buya̱ naa hange̱ mazama maya̱nu bwaa makicihinaa muu nii gata ta̱hyan, <<Imbata be̱e̱ bina̱nna be̱ ja̱a̱ sha?>> Na̱nna shi ta̱hyan ta̱kai nata̱ Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ne̱e̱ huku nii be̱e̱ bibe̱e̱.
Zakaariya ya̱bi Hwe̱n
Aba na̱ kunnu, Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ pa̱ni Zakaariya, ashin na Yoohana, ta̱kai. Be̱e̱ cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama nama bwa ribi xbicici,
<<XTa̱nya̱ba̱ni Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n na Isiraaꞌila,
na̱ wana uwuce,
uta̱mbiha̱ni ga̱tu awyatu ndaabwa.
-70 Na̱ haruwa na bwa na hyan bunii nda hasaa
kawyatu na ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ana ne̱e̱ sabu,
ta̱hyan, unii ta̱nda̱a̱ba butu naa nii ta̱mbiha̱na̱
bunaa báni paakii korogo
na buugyama ndaabwa Dawuda.
Unii ta̱mbiha̱na̱ kuꞌnꞌara
na nꞌwyatu ana ta̱nribici ta̱ndaya
na̱ ana ta̱nga̱a̱.
Kuubwa na nda na adaadoo,
kunta bwa nii ta̱ndaaka ambishiri.
Bwa mata̱ma̱nriin xbuciga̱hini ta̱masha̱a̱ga̱
nata̱ bwa tanda na̱ aba,
usa̱nsan na bwa tandaaka daada nda̱tu Ibiraahin,
ta̱hyan unii ta̱mbiha̱na̱ kawyatu ana ta̱nribici,
na̱ wana ga̱tun nii naa ndaga
iri na Hwe̱n bwa hin,
ga̱tun jaa mꞌbaa rukwanyan.
Na̱ kunnu, ta̱naa sabu
nꞌta̱jwara̱ga Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n
hyo̱ nꞌhwe̱n nꞌnda̱a̱tu.
Gaa, be̱e̱ biniimi,
ana̱maa nꞌgana butu naa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n
na Hura̱gi Ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ mazama.
Wana bi-nii naa iyeebe na Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n,
u-a̱sa̱ga̱a̱gi wuun yo̱n,
bi-nii bisa̱a̱ awyatu ndaabwa yo̱n na ta̱bina̱
paaku Hwe̱n bwa jaa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ wyan
pinsan ndaaba.
Na̱ wana o̱to̱ na ambishiri na Hwe̱n nda̱tu,
Ala̱masiihu+ :78 Ala̱masiihu: Gwatana paa Haruwa na Ayaan Kala̱ma aba Shi.nii jaa na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱
haku ta̱gwaan nata̱ hwe̱n na nii báni hwe̱n ta̱bani,
ma ta̱ra̱ka̱ni kana hunrani nꞌta̱yincincin
na̱ ana hunrani na̱ hunrun na ta̱ꞌwa̱,
uta̱ꞌye̱e̱ kuhunranhunran na ta̱bure.>>
Sa̱i Yoohana bwa mawaani, bwa nje̱ kai na mazama na̱ tuma ndaabwa ta̱nda. Bwa hunrani na̱ ahira̱ ceeku, kiike̱nye̱n naa bwa báni bwaa bisa̱ga̱ awyatu na Isiraaꞌila mazama nama Hwe̱n.

Ta̱ma̱ncin nata̱ Yeesu
Maatiyu 1:18-25
Na̱ nꞌhwe̱n ya̱nu, Kaisa+ :1 Kaisa: Gwatana paa Haruwa na Ayaan Kala̱ma aba Shi.Ago̱sita, bugwama naa o̱to̱ naa Rooma, bwa pa̱ni nu ta̱hyan xaro̱be̱ hyo̱ awyatu na ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ ta̱gwama nata̱ o̱to̱ nata̱ Rooma.
Ya̱nu ta shi ta̱ruba nata̱ yigo nii ke̱nye̱n naa Kiriniya, bwa tasha gwamina na ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Suuriya.
Hyo̱ awyatu koo buya̱ bwa huri ce̱pe̱ ndaabwa na̱ wana xaro̱be̱ wyan.
Yusufu taa be̱ ga̱a̱ ce̱pe̱ na Naazare na ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Gaalili. Be̱ ja̱a̱ Baitalaami na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya, uce̱pe̱ na aba ma̱ncin bugwama Dawuda nu. Yusufu be̱ ja̱a̱ piree na̱ wana bishi butu naa báni bigudu naa Dawuda.
Yusufu be̱ huri huku na̱ Maariyamu, na aba na hoo pana buu xbinaa zhaa, na̱ wana xaro̱be̱ wyan huku. Nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu, be̱ taꞌmꞌbaa huba̱.
Na aba ne̱e̱ piree na̱ Baitalaami, kiike̱nye̱n naa ta̱ma̱ncin ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ ta̱ba nje̱.
Be̱ ma̱ncin be̱e̱ binaa wya̱ri nde̱e̱be̱ naa yigo. Be̱ rigi buu na̱ zuzu na hyaabu, be̱ taahini buu na̱ ruꞌwana naru aba ta naa paga bikico̱ shami na̱ ame̱ naruba, na̱ wana ade̱be̱ce̱ dura̱ paaku ta̱ta̱na.
Aꞌiyo̱ na̱ atuma na Hwe̱n
Nii biin binaa ce̱nye̱n ta̱ya̱nu, ayaan iyo̱ na ka̱ra̱bi aba ne̱e̱, ata naa rota̱ga̱ na̱ sa̱ra̱ri, aha̱mba ka̱ra̱bi ndaaba na̱ gita.
Mayaan mazama mꞌba za, aba nda̱i butuma naa Hwe̱n na̱ aba, aba nda̱i ta̱gwaan nata̱ Hwe̱n, ta̱ba ta̱ra̱ka̱ni paaka ba ne̱e̱, aba hange̱ rukwanyan ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Butuma naa Hwe̱n bwa hin wyan, <<Ta-ha̱nga ma rukwanyan! Shiraga ma, iiꞌíyaagi ma mazama nama zumaa, nama nii shaana awyatu hyo̱ ahange̱ gama ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Ba̱re yana, hina na̱ ce̱pe̱ na Dawuda, aama̱nta̱ni ma butu naa na̱maa biha̱na̱ ma, Ala̱masiihu Uhwe̱n.
Na̱nna ta nii sha iri na na̱maa bisa̱a̱ ma mazama maniimi mashi mahanda: Inii wuta̱na̱ arigi bibe̱e̱ na̱ zuzu na hyaabu, aba taahini buu na̱ ruꞌwana naru aba ta naa paga bikico̱ shami na̱ ame̱ naruba.>>
Mayaan mazama mꞌba za, atuma na Hwe̱n hwarapi na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ aba ne̱e̱ huku na̱a̱ tuma naa Hwe̱n naa yigo. Abaa yaba Hwe̱n, abaa hyaan,
<<Ta̱yabana Hwe̱n na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱!
Na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n hunranhunran gumunu
naa huku na̱ awyatu
na Hwe̱n bwa ndaaki rubara̱ka.>>
Na atuma na Hwe̱n aba mahooshi na̱ aba, aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱. Aꞌiyo̱ na ka̱ra̱bi aba mahin, <<XTa̱nja̱a̱ Baitalaami ta̱ndái iri na nje̱, ina Hwe̱n bwa ta̱mbishi.>>
Aba huri na̱ ha̱ni, aba wuta̱ni Maariyamu na̱ Yusufu, aba nda̱i be̱e̱ bitaa na̱ ruꞌwana naru aba ta naa paga bikico̱ shami na̱ ame̱ naruba.
Na aꞌiyo̱ na ka̱ra̱bi aba nda̱i be̱e̱, aba cita̱gi iri na butuma naa Hwe̱n bwa tabisa̱gi wyan na̱ wanaa be̱e̱ bibe̱e̱.
Bo̱do̱ awyatu na hange̱ maya̱nu mazama, aba ha̱mba̱a̱gi sunu na̱ wana iri na aꞌiyo̱ na ka̱ra̱bi aba cici.
Maariyamu be̱ shii iri ya̱nu hyo̱, be̱e̱ makicihinaa wuun na̱ ame̱ nde̱e̱be̱.
Aꞌiyo̱ na ka̱ra̱bi aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱ paaki ka̱ra̱bi ndaaba, abaa zhinyan zha̱a̱ na yabi na Hwe̱n na̱ wana iri na aba hange̱, aba nda̱i. Hyo̱ iri nje̱, kaba tabishi wyan.
Apa̱ Yeesu ruzha̱a̱
Na hwe̱n bwa riini, aba ꞌya̱pi bibe̱e̱ ta̱wya̱ri, aba pa̱ buu ruzha̱a̱ Yeesu+ :21 Yeesu: Ruyaan ruzha̱a̱ naru aba ta nꞌgana Yeesu taru shi Iisa.naru butuma naa Hwe̱n bwa na pa buu ta Maariyamu be̱ cigo huba̱ nde̱e̱be̱.
Aꞌye̱e̱ Yeesu Ina na Hwe̱n
-24 Naa ke̱nye̱n be̱ nje̱, Maariyamu be̱ hiin bwaciga ta̱shiri nata̱ ta̱ma̱ncin. Maariyamu na̱ Yusufu aba ja̱a̱ Ina na Hwe̱n na Ayaahudiya na̱ Hurushaliima. Aba hin anii shinraanwyan Hwe̱n iri, kuharuwa na Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n bwa tapana Muusa mꞌba hin xanje̱, <<Ahuunruun reeko koo nꞌhuunruun na nꞌina+ :22-24 nꞌhuunruun na nꞌina: Ta shi nꞌtatabara.nꞌreeko aba nii shinran.>> Maariyamu na̱ Yusufu aba sha̱pi Yeesu zhagu Hurushaliima na̱ wana xapa̱ni buu ku-Hwe̱n. Kunnunu aba ta̱gi na̱ Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n ta̱hyan, <<Hyo̱ baa buwya̱ri naa yigo naa aba ma̱ncin, anii pe̱e̱n buu bishi iri na ta̱sabu ku-Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n.>>
Nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu, buyaan butu naa tanaa na̱ Hurushaliima, bunaa aba ta hyan Samiinu. Bwa shi butu naa bina̱. Bwa jwarigi Hwe̱n ki. Bwa hambe̱ bike̱nye̱n naa Hwe̱n bwa nii káji buyaan bunaa nii biha̱na̱ Isiraaꞌila. Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ ne̱e̱ huku na̱a̱ bwa.
Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ tabisa̱ be̱, bujaa ꞌwa̱ ta bwa nda̱i Ala̱masiihu na Hwe̱n.
Naa Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ sha̱pi be̱, bwa ta̱ni bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n. Nii ke̱nye̱n naa ashoo aba na iya Yeesu Ina na Hwe̱n na̱ wana haruwa na Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa+ :27 Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa: Gwatana paa Haruwa na Ayaan Kala̱ma aba Shi.mꞌba tahyan xanje̱.
Samiinu bwa ra̱a̱ bibibe̱e̱ na̱ nꞌara nꞌndaabwa, bwa ya̱bi Hwe̱n, bwa hin,
<<Uhwe̱n na hura̱gi ta̱kai ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa hyo̱,
niina nꞌcipani ga̱mi
bugyama ndaabi gumunu,
haruwa na gaa tahyan bi-nii nda.
Na̱ wana ayishe nimi nda̱i
bunaa nii biha̱na̱ awyatu ndaa,
bunaa gaa tasha̱a̱ ta̱hyan bunii biha̱na̱ awyatu hyo̱,
koo buya̱ bwaa ndaya be̱.
Bwa taa shi ta̱gwaan nata̱ na̱maa bisa̱a̱ gaa,
kawyatu ana shici Ayaahudiya,
buꞌwaan ta̱shapaciga kawyatu ndaa Isiraaꞌila.>>
Ashin na̱ aya̱na̱ nde̱e̱be̱ aba ha̱mba̱a̱gi sunu na̱ iri na Samiinu bwa cici na̱ wana nde̱e̱be̱.
Samiinu bwa sha̱a̱gi wyan rubara̱ka. Bwa hin Maariyamu aya̱na̱ na be̱e̱, <<Uhwe̱n ka̱shi be̱e̱ bina̱nna na̱ wana binii sha ta̱kinaa na̱ nꞌta̱hiika̱ nata̱ awyatu hwarapi na̱ Isiraaꞌila. Binii sha iri na awyatu hwarapi aba jaa ruba̱.
Ta shani sushe̱re̱ nasu nꞌgata nꞌndaaba subaa bara̱nwyan. Iri ya̱nu be̱ na̱maa hanshinhina ame̱, hakii sa̱nka̱ri tibii gata ndaabi.>>
Nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu, biyaan bikamance̱n, Hannatu, be̱ wuce waaba, be̱ shi buꞌa̱ naa nii cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama. Buyoo Fanuyila, bunaa bikorogo naa Asha. Binje̱ hunranhunran na ta̱wya̱ri nꞌyo̱ nꞌta̱nda̱ra̱ hwii,
awya̱rugo aba ꞌwi. Niina nꞌyo̱ nꞌnde̱e̱be̱ kuje ta̱ndatu na̱ nꞌna̱nshin. Biꞌa̱cii gaa Ina na Hwe̱n ma ndaaka Hwe̱n tuma gita na̱ hwe̱n huku na̱ ro̱pe̱ na̱ ruꞌure̱ ta̱nda.
Na be̱ wuce waaba, be̱e̱ ndaaka Hwe̱n zumanu. Be̱ cici mazama namaa bibe̱e̱ kawyatu na ta ha̱mbaga ke̱nye̱n naa Hwe̱n bwa nii káji buyaan bunaa nii biha̱na̱ awyatu na Hurushaliima.
Na Yusufu na̱ Maariyamu aba hwii ta̱nda hyo̱ iri na Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n mꞌba hin xanje̱ buꞌa̱ bwa ma̱ncin baa buwya̱ri naa yigo, sa̱i aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱ ce̱pe̱ ndaaba, Naazare na Gaalili.
Be̱e̱ bibe̱ mawaani, be̱ nje̱ kai, be̱ cigi nꞌta̱yansun. Rubara̱ka naru Hwe̱n ruba ne̱e̱ huku nii be̱.
Yeesu, be̱e̱ binaa njeke, // na̱ ame̱ na Ina na Hwe̱n
Koya̱ yo̱ ashoo na Yeesu aba ta jaga Hurushaliima na̱ wana Ubuki na Ta̱matamanrinyan Ta̱hanrinyan Nꞌina.+ :41 Ubuki na Ta̱matamanrinyan Ta̱hanrinyan Nꞌina: Gwatana paa Haruwa na Ayaan Kala̱ma aba Shi.Na Yeesu be̱ cigi nꞌyo̱ nꞌupwa na̱ nꞌreeko na̱ nꞌta̱mantan, sa̱i aba ja̱a̱ Ta̱mawuna̱na̱ ta̱ya̱nu haruwa na Ayaahudiya aba ta naa ndaga.
Na Ubuki na Ta̱matamanrinyan Ta̱hanrinyan Nꞌina ta̱ba hwii, aba humuni yo̱n na̱ wana hyan xakwashe̱e̱ke̱ ina. Ki-Yeesu bibibe̱e̱, be̱ e̱she̱ ta̱baa na̱ Hurushaliima, ashoo aba yancin.
Aba shii ta̱hyan bine̱e̱ na̱ awyantancin na awyatu, na̱ wana kunnu aba nje̱ ta̱hani rwaru ka̱. Naazuma aba ke̱ne̱ wyanzun nde̱e̱be̱ paaku diin ndaaba na̱ nꞌta̱shika ta̱ndaaba,
aba nda̱ci buu. Na̱ wana kunnu, aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱ Hurushaliima na̱ wana hyan awyánzhin buu piree.
Na̱ uhwe̱n na hin taatu, aba wuta̱ni buu bihunrani na̱ bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n huku na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi. Be̱ shiragi wyan ma hantaana wyan mazama.
Hyo̱ ana shiraagi buu, aba ha̱mba̱a̱gi sunu na̱ wana ta̱yansun ta̱nde̱e̱be̱, na̱ haruwa na be̱e̱ ranaa wyan mazama.
Ashoo nde̱e̱be̱ aba jikita̱ni na aba nda̱i buu piree. Aya̱na̱ nde̱e̱be̱ aba hin buu, <<Be̱e̱ biniimi, na̱ wana ba̱ gaa ta̱ndaaki kunna? Ga̱n na̱ abaaba ndaa ta̱na̱maa wyanzan, ga̱tuu nda̱ci.>>
Be̱ ra̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Na̱ wana ba̱ ga̱hin nii nꞌwyanzan? Iyancin ta̱hyan uhuri gama ma naa na̱ ina na Baaba nimi?>>
Aba e̱nshe̱nshe̱n koo iba̱ mazama maya̱nu mande̱e̱be̱ mꞌba shi.
Be̱ hiiki, be̱ jwarigi wyan, aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱ Naazare huku, be̱ tibi wyan mazama. Aya̱na̱ mayaan aba ha̱mba̱gi iri ya̱nu hyo̱ nii gata ndaaba.
Yeesu be̱e̱ maduwa̱na̱ ta̱mawaana na̱ nꞌta̱yansun Hwe̱n, awyatu aba duwa̱ni buu ta̱ruba̱ na̱ nꞌta̱pa zha̱munkun.

Mazama nama // Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma
Maatiyu 3:1-12; Marukusu 1:1-8; Yoohana 1:19-28
-2 Na̱ yo̱ na hin upwa na̱ ta na ta̱gwama nata̱ Kaisa Tabaariya, na bwa tasha bugwama naa o̱to̱ na Rooma, mazama nama Hwe̱n mꞌba wuce ku-Yoohana, buyoo Zakaariya, na̱ ahira̱ ceeku. Na̱ ha̱ni ya̱nu, Buntu Bilaatu+ :1-2 Bilaatu: Gwatana paa Haruwa na Ayaan Kala̱ma aba Shi.bwa tasha gwamina na ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya. Hirudu Antipasi bwa tasha bugwama naa Gaalili, buya̱na̱ naa o̱to̱ Filibu bwa tasha bugwama naa Ituuriya na̱ Tarakoonita. Lisaaniya bwa tasha bugwama naa Abilinii. Hanasu na̱ Kayaapa aba tasha awyatu o̱to̱ na apirisiti na n-Ayaahudiya.
Na̱ ha̱ni ya̱nu, Yoohana bwa jwara̱gagani kope na̱ ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Rwaga na Joodan ma bisa̱ga̱ awyatu ta̱hyan xapa̱ni pinsan baa, ajaa, andagi wyan baba̱tiisa̱ma+ :3 baba̱tiisa̱ma: Gwatana paa Haruwa na Ayaan Kala̱ma aba Shi.na hyan abisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan apa̱ni pinsan baa, Hwe̱n bwa jaa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ wyan pinsan ndaaba nii gata ndaabwa.
Kaba ta̱gi na̱ takaada na bunaa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Ishaaya ta̱hyan,
<<Ta̱ꞌnꞌga ma nꞌga na̱ ahira̱ ma hyaan,
<A̱sa̱ga̱a̱ga̱ ma Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n yo̱n,
ika̱mbiga̱gi ayo̱n na bwaa jwára̱gani.
Ciga̱hina̱a̱ ma hyo̱ akoko koko,
iga̱ci koya̱ undu nii undu nge̱n.
Ayo̱n ana ngunta̱in ika̱mbiga̱gi wyan.
Ayo̱n ana zumaancin iꞌa̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni wyan.
Hyo̱ awyatu wuma abaa ndaya
ku-Hwe̱n bwaa biha̱na̱ wyan.> >>
Wana kunnu, Yoohana bwa hin awyatu hwarapi na jaa waabwa, wana xbundagi wyan baba̱tiisa̱ma, <<Ga̱hin suhwaa nasu we̱, iyaa bishi ma ta̱hyan gida̱ga̱na̱ ma ta̱suuga̱ nasu wuci?
Nda ma iri na hyan ibisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan ipa̱ni pinsan baa. Ta-hyan ma na̱ nꞌsume̱ suniinhin, <Ibiraahin ta shi adaada na adaadoo nda̱tu.> Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, Hwe̱n nii ara ta̱ndaaka Ibiraahin mꞌmwaan katari na̱nna.
Ahoo sha̱a̱ aca̱gu na̱ kunrun kunrun na ꞌwe̱e̱, hyo̱ uꞌwe̱e̱ na nje̱ce̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ bina̱, aꞌya̱pa̱gi wuun, abwagi na̱ ra.>>
Awyatu aba ha̱nta̱ni Yoohana, <<Iba̱ ga̱tu nda?>>
Bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Hyo̱ bunaa mꞌbaa ada̱bi ree, buka̱a̱shii naa za. Bunaa mꞌbaa shami, buhooshi na̱a̱ naa za shami.>>
Awyatu na ta naa raaga ga̱ndu aba wuce taa xandagi wyan baba̱tiisa̱ma, aba hin, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, iba̱ ga̱tu nda?>>
Bwa hin wyan, <<Kiinii raaga ga̱ndu, ta-raa ma uhuri kabaa hin ma naa raaga ma.>>
Ayaan asooja taa aba wuce, aba ha̱nta̱ni, <<Ga̱tu taa paa? Iba̱ ga̱tu nda?>>
Bwa hin, <<Ta-shana ma koo buyaan buupa̱ni ma ayuwa na̱ nꞌtugusu. Ta-nda ma ta̱be̱ wana buupa̱ncin ma. Isa ma kuna̱ funa̱ ninhin.>>
Na̱ wana awyatu ha̱mbagi zhagu na Ala̱masiihu, abaa hyaan na̱ nꞌsume̱ sume̱ sundaaba, koo Yoohana ta shi bunaa Hwe̱n bwa káji.
Yoohana bwa hin wyan hyo̱ ndaaba, <<Ga̱n na̱maa ndaga ma baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ ma̱ni, ama buyaan buwuci bunaa ga̱n wucici ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ koo ge̱. Nꞌjwaci na hyan ma rigijiga̱ uhwa̱ na akandaga ndaabwa. Bwa taa shi naa na̱maa ndaga ma baba̱tiisa̱ma nii Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n na̱ baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ ra.
Bwa shi haku butu naa ha̱mba̱gi ukada ndaabwa na pyashi, na bwaa pyasa shami ndaabwa. Buwuna̱a̱ni hyo̱ shami, buzooga̱ni na̱ nꞌndukwa nꞌndaabwa. Ama buhuunha̱ni nꞌshasu kura na za ta̱kuna.>>
Na̱ mꞌmayaan mazama mahwarapi nama Yoohana bwa ndaakaki awyatu mꞌbashi numa. Bwa gura̱a̱ bisa̱ga̱ wyan mazama nama zumaa.
Anje̱ Yeesu baba̱tiisa̱ma
Maatiyu 3:13-17; Marukusu 1:9-11
-22 Na Yoohana bwa ndagi awyatu hyo̱ baba̱tiisa̱ma, Yeesu na̱ hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱ bwa nje̱ buu baba̱tiisa̱ma. Yeesu ma nda ro̱pe̱, ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱ba gunii, Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ cíin na̱ hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱ na̱ mꞌpirwa na nꞌhuunruun. Aba hange̱ ta̱ꞌnꞌga na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ma hyaan, <<Gaa taa shi Baa buniimi, bunaa ga̱n huri ta̱ruba̱, ga̱n mashiragi na̱ gaa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.>>
Yoohana bwa gura̱a̱ ndaaka bugwama Hirudu Antipasi bashi, wana ta̱hyan buzha̱a̱ Hiruudiya aꞌa̱yoo ya̱na̱ Filibu, na̱ yaan iri hwarapi na we̱ na bwa ndagi. Hirudu bwa gura̱a̱ ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ mazama, bwa kota̱ni Yoohana, bwa zwa̱ga̱ni na̱ zhaaro.
Bikorogo naa Yeesu
Maatiyu 1:1-17
Na Yeesu be̱ nje̱ nꞌyo̱ sukuje taatu, be̱ pa̱shi tuma nde̱e̱be̱.
Awyatu na shapa ta̱hyan be̱ taa shi buyoo Yusufu,
Yusufu bwa shi buyoo Heeli,
Heeli buyoo Matata̱,
Matata̱ buyoo Laawi,
Laawi buyoo Maaliki,
Maaliki buyoo Yanna,
Yanna buyoo Yusufu,
Yusufu buyoo Mataatiya,
Mataatiya buyoo Amosu,
Amosu buyoo Nahum,
Nahum buyoo Azaaliya,
Azaaliya buyoo Najaaya,
Najaaya buyoo Maꞌata,
Maꞌata buyoo Mataatiya,
Mataatiya buyoo Shimeya,
Shimeya buyoo Yusuka̱,
Yusuka̱ buyoo Yuuda,
Yuuda buyoo Yuwanan,
Yuwanan buyoo Re̱sa,
Re̱sa buyoo Zerubaabili,
Zerubaabili buyoo Sheyalitiyali,
Sheyalitiyali buyoo Niiri,
Niiri buyoo Maaliki,
Maaliki buyoo Adi,
Adi buyoo Kosama,
Kosama buyoo Ilimadaama,
Ilimadaama buyoo Ira̱,
Ira̱ buyoo Jooshuwa,
Jooshuwa buyoo Iliyiza̱ra̱,
Iliyiza̱ra̱ buyoo Yorima̱,
Yorima̱ buyoo Matata̱,
Matata̱ buyoo Laawi,
Laawi buyoo Samiinu,
Samiinu buyoo Yaahuda,
Yaahuda buyoo Yusufu,
Yusufu buyoo Yuna̱ma̱,
Yuna̱ma̱ buyoo Iliyakimi,
Iliyakimi buyoo Meeleya,
Meeleya buyoo Me̱na,
Me̱na buyoo Mataata,
Mataata buyoo Natani,
Natani buyoo Dawuda,
Dawuda buyoo Yeese,
Yeese buyoo Obedi,
Obedi buyoo Bowaazu,
Bowaazu buyoo Salumu,
Salumu buyoo Nasho,
Nasho buyoo Amiinada,
Amiinada buyoo Aramu,
Aramu buyoo He̱zuro,
He̱zuro buyoo Peruzu,
Peruzu buyoo Yaahuda,
Yaahuda buyoo Yaakubu,
Yaakubu buyoo Isiyaaku,
Isiyaaku buyoo Ibiraahin,
Ibiraahin buyoo Teera,
Teera buyoo Nahuru,
Nahuru buyoo Serugu,
Serugu buyoo Reeyu,
Reeyu buyoo Pe̱le̱gu,
Pe̱le̱gu buyoo Ibiru,
Ibiru buyoo Sheela,
Sheela buyoo Kenan,
Kenan buyoo Arufakushadu,
Arufakushadu buyoo Shemu,
Shemu buyoo Nuhu,
Nuhu buyoo Laamiki,
Laamiki buyoo Metuseela,
Metuseela buyoo E̱no̱ku,
E̱no̱ku buyoo Yaaridi,
Yaaridi buyoo Mahaleele,
Mahaleele buyoo Kenan,
Kenan buyoo E̱no̱shu,
E̱no̱shu buyoo Sha̱tu,
Sha̱tu buyoo Adamu,
Adamu bunaa Hwe̱n.

Bupira̱ bwa ma̱a̱nwya̱ni Yeesu
Maatiyu 4:1-11; Marukusu 1:12-13
Na Yeesu be̱ kúshiike̱ ku-Rwaga na Joodan, Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ ne̱e̱ huku nii be̱, be̱ ꞌye̱e̱ buu na̱ ame̱ naa zaga naa aga.
Kabata Bupira̱+ :2 Bupira̱: Gwatana paa Haruwa na Ayaan Kala̱ma aba Shi.bwa ma̱a̱nwya̱ni buu nꞌhwe̱n handa na̱ wana xbinje̱ iri na ruhaki. Naa ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu be̱ hwii, be̱ hange̱ rumunro̱n ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ wana bire̱ce̱ koori.
Sa̱i Bupira̱ bwa hin buu, <<Kuu-shi Buyoo Hwe̱n, shana tari na̱nna ushi buroodi.>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni bwa, be̱ hin, <<Ata̱gi na̱ takaada na Hwe̱n, <Shii kini shami ta butu bwa ta nda bina̱.> >>
Kabata Bupira̱ bwa sha̱pi buu kayaan pa̱ri naka za̱ka̱ri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, bwa bisa̱a̱gi buu hyo̱ ta̱gwama nata̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n, hyo̱ nii ke̱nye̱n ge̱.
Bupira̱ bwa hin buu, <<Ga̱n na̱maa pana ta̱kai na̱ hyo̱ iri na̱nna na gama ishi ndaa hyo̱, na̱ wana aꞌmꞌpa̱ni wuun. Ga̱n nii ara ta̱pana wuun hyo̱ kuunaa ga̱n ribi.
Hyo̱ una̱nna unii sha ndaa, gaa mꞌpa̱ hunrun.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin bwa, <<Ata̱gi ta̱hyan,
<< <Pa Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n ndaa hunrun,
kuubwa gaa nii naa ndaaka tuma!> >>
Bupira̱ bwa sha̱pi buu zhagu Hurushaliima, bwa ꞌye̱e̱ buu ta da̱da̱da̱ na Ina na Hwe̱n na Ayaahudiya, bwa hin buu, <<Kuu-shi Buyoo Hwe̱n, guba̱ pita paa gaa ne̱e̱, u-ke̱ne̱ na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n.
Na̱ wana ata̱gi ta̱hyan,
<< <Uhwe̱n nii shana atuma ndaabwa aasa̱a̱ki,
gaa jaa magumahina.
Ana̱maa raa na̱ nꞌara nꞌndaaba,
na̱ wana gaa jaa basana
mꞌbuna nꞌndaabi na̱ paga.> >>
Ama Yeesu be̱ ga̱a̱, be̱ hin bwa, <<Ata̱gi ta̱hyan, <Ta-maanwyana Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n ndaa.> >>
Na Bupira̱ bwa hwii Yeesu ta̱maanwyana koya̱a̱ biin, sa̱i bwa ga̱a̱ buu kwan.
Yeesu be̱ pa̱shi // tuma nde̱e̱be̱ na̱ Gaalili
Maatiyu 4:12-17; Marukusu 1:14-15
Yeesu be̱ kwashe̱e̱ke̱ Gaalili, ta̱kai nata̱a̱ Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n ta̱ba ne̱e̱ huku nii be̱. Mazama mꞌba riini wyan kope na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Gaalili.
Yeesu be̱e̱ ga̱gaagana wyan na̱ aka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya+ :15 aka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya: Gwatana paa Haruwa na Ayaan Kala̱ma aba Shi, kala̱ma na <<Ka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya>>.kwayaa bwaa yaba buu.
Aga̱a̱ Yeesu na̱ Naazare
Maatiyu 13:53-58; Marukusu 6:2-6
Yeesu be̱ ja̱a̱ Naazare, paakii be̱ mawaani. Be̱ ta̱ni ka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya na̱ hwe̱n ndaaba na ha̱nka̱na̱, haruwa na be̱ ta naa ndaga. Na be̱ hiiki, be̱ hiin cita̱ga̱ ta̱ꞌyantan.
Aba pa̱ni buu takaada na Ishaaya, butu naa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama. Be̱ pipigi takaada, be̱ wya̱nzhin, be̱ de̱be̱ pa̱ri paaka ba ta̱gi ta̱hyan,Books in the time of Jesus|hk00153c.tif|col|LUK 4:16-21|Horace Knowles|Atakaada na̱ ha̱ni na Yeesu|4:17<<Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n ne̱e̱ huku na̱ ga̱mi,
na̱ wana buꞌnꞌka̱shi ma íyaagi
aꞌwa̱ta̱gi mazama nama zumaa.
Bwa nꞌka̱ji tuma ma bisa̱ wyan
ta̱hyan ana ka̱da̱a̱gi,
anii rigijiga̱ wyan amata̱a̱,
aruba̱ aba nii huwa̱ga̱ pa̱ri,
ana aba zhintaani,
aba nii zhincinyan wyan, amata̱a̱.
Bwaꞌnꞌka̱ji ma bisa̱ga̱ awyatu ta̱hyan
bike̱nye̱n goki na Hwe̱n
bwaa ndaaka awyatu iri na zumaa.>>
Na be̱ hwii ta̱cita̱ga̱ ta̱ꞌyantan, be̱ pipi takaada, be̱ kushihinani butu naa ta ha̱mba ka̱ta̱ku, be̱ hunrani. Bo̱do̱ awyatu na tane̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ na ka̱ta̱ku aba zooni buu suyishe.
Be̱ ke̱ne̱ ta̱ga̱gaagana wyan, <<Mana̱nna mazama nama Hwe̱n nama ta̱gi macigi ba̱re na̱ ce̱be̱ ninhin.>>
Hyo̱ ndaaba ana tanaa piree abaa nda mazama mande̱e̱be̱ nama gama aba hange̱ rukwanyan na̱ mazama nama zumaa nama nii bánai na̱ nu nde̱e̱be̱, abaa hantaana, abaa hyaan, <<Ka̱i! Buna̱nna shii baa bunaa Yusufu ta nuu bwa shi?>>
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Ga̱n yan ina̱maa mꞌbisa̱ ta̱kun ta̱ya̱nu, <Butu naa njibi, makuda̱gahini.> Ga̱hin nii nꞌhyan, <Nda iri ya̱nu na ga̱tu hange̱ bi-njé̱e̱ na̱ Kapanahu pina na̱ ce̱pe̱ ndaa taa.> >>
Be̱ gura̱a̱ hyan wyan, <<Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, butu naa nii cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama shii hyo̱ aba ta ruba̱ be̱ na̱ ce̱pe̱ ndaabwa.
Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, nii ke̱nye̱n naa Iliya butu naa nii cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, aꞌa̱ tanaa ahwarapi ana suwya̱rugooba suba taꞌwa̱ga̱ pina na̱ Isiraaꞌila. Nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu ashira̱ aba ke̱nce̱n nꞌyo̱ nꞌtaatu na̱ mꞌpyanda nꞌcininhin, rumunro̱n ruba nje̱ kope na̱ nꞌta̱ba ce̱nye̱n.
Hwe̱n bwa ka̱jici Iliya zhagu kaꞌa̱ na suwya̱rugooba suba taꞌwa̱ga̱, kupaa kuuyaan buꞌa̱ naa awya̱rugo aba na ꞌwa̱ na̱ Zarefa na ne̱e̱ na̱ Sidon ta bwa takada buu.
Nii ke̱nye̱n naa butu naa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama E̱lisha mayaan, aza mꞌmbwa+ :27 aza mꞌmbwa: Awyatu na suguma nasu tutuu na ta̱ꞌwaba.ahwarapi ane̱e̱ na̱ Isiraaꞌila, ama aba kuda̱gahincin koo buka̱ ndaaba suguma, ku-Naaman butu naa ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Suuriya ta aba takuda̱gahina bwaa ka̱.>>
Na awyatu na tanaa na̱ ame̱ na ka̱ta̱ku aba hange̱ mazama maya̱nu, sa̱i nꞌgata nꞌndaaba hyo̱ mꞌba ha̱nsha̱nha̱ni.
Aba hiiki, aba pa̱ Yeesu sumo̱ nꞌta̱baa nata̱ ce̱pe̱, aba ꞌye̱e̱ buu da̱da̱da̱ na undu na aba tama ce̱pe̱ ndaaba na̱ bwa. Aba ribi xata̱a̱cigi buu, bikínai tapiree da̱da̱da̱ na undu,
ama sa̱i be̱ huri na̱ awyantancin ndaaba, be̱ huri ta̱hani ta̱nde̱e̱be̱.
Yeesu pa̱a̱ hwaanwun naa we̱ sumo̱
Marukusu 1:21-28
Yeesu be̱ huri cuun Kapanahu, yaan ce̱pe̱ na̱ Gaalili. Na̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya+ :31 hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya: Gwatana paa Haruwa na Ayaan Kala̱ma aba Shi.be̱ ta̱ni ka̱ta̱ku, be̱ ke̱ne̱ ta̱ga̱gaagana wyan.
Abaa jikita̱ga̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ na̱ wana mazama mande̱e̱be̱ maꞌmꞌbaa ta̱kai.
Na̱ ame̱ na ka̱ta̱ku, butu bwa ne̱e̱ bunaa butu naa hira̱ bwa jwarigi. Bwa ta̱a̱ni nu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱,
<<Ka̱i! Yeesu naa Naazare, nꞌnda̱i ruwa ndaa na̱ ga̱tu? Bi-jaa ta u-ta̱ga̱ci? Ga̱n yan iyaa ta gaa shi, gaa taa shi Buyata naa ne̱e̱ Sabu bunaa Hwe̱n!>>
Yeesu be̱ yinzha̱nkani butu naa hira̱, <<Nda wau! Bana na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ butu yata!>> Sa̱i butu naa hira̱ bwa sha̱pa̱cigi butu, bwa pa̱ be̱ pwan na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n na̱ aꞌuba̱ ndaaba. Bwa ba̱ni, bwa ga̱a̱ butu, bwa hiiki, bwa magumahincin.
Sa̱i awyatu hyo̱ aba ha̱mba̱a̱gi sunu, abaa mahyaan, <<Ya̱ iri na mazama mana kunna? Na̱ nꞌta̱kai na̱ nꞌta̱gwama ta buna̱nna butu bwa hiika̱ni nꞌhwaanwun na nꞌwe̱ ta mꞌba ba̱ni!>>
Na̱nna iri na Yeesu be̱ nje̱ ibe̱ shaani, abaa cita̱ga̱ mazama mande̱e̱be̱ kope na̱ ce̱nye̱n ta̱ba.
Yeesu be̱ kuda̱gahini // awyatu hwarapi
Maatiyu 8:14-17; Marukusu 1:29-34
Yeesu be̱ ba̱ni ka̱ta̱ku, be̱ huri ina na Siima+ :38 Siima: Yeesu be̱ pa̱ Siima ruyaan ruzha̱a̱, Biituru. Aya̱na̱wan na a̱ aba hange̱ce̱ sa̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwaba mamboo ta̱ꞌo̱to̱. Aba bishi Yeesu mazama xbikuda̱gahini wyan.
Be̱ ja̱a̱, be̱ e̱she̱ do̱ko̱ na̱ wyansun ndaaba, be̱ hiika̱ni ta̱ꞌwaba mamboo xta̱ta̱zhiga̱ni be̱. Kupita ubwa ta̱zhiga̱ni be̱, bwa hiiki mayaan, bwa ndaaki wyan tuma.
Na hwe̱n bwa iri, koo buya̱ butu naa mꞌbaa bunaa hange̱ce̱ sa̱, na̱ koya̱ iri na suguma, aba iyagi wyan ki-Yeesu. Be̱ a̱nta̱a̱ni wyan hyo̱ ndaaba na̱ ara, be̱ kuda̱gahinai wyan hyo̱.
Awyatu na hira̱ aba ba̱ni nꞌta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ awyatu hwarapi, abaa taga ta̱ꞌungwa, abaa hyaan, <<Gaa Buyoo Hwe̱n ta!>> Ama Yeesu be̱ hiika̱ni wyan, be̱ yanshin wyan mazama, na̱ wana ta̱hyan ayan be̱ taa shi Ala̱masiihu, bunaa Hwe̱n bwa káji.
Yeesu be̱e̱ ga̱gaagana awyatu
Marukusu 1:35-39
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, Yeesu be̱ ga̱a̱ ce̱pe̱ bwa, be̱ ja̱a̱ paaka za koo butu. Awyatu abaa wyanzan buu, aba nda̱i kiibe̱. Aba nje̱ haruwa na aba nii ara, ayanshin buu zhagu kayaan mayaan.
Ama be̱ hin wyan, <<Huri gama maꞌiya mazama nama zumaa nama ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n kayaan ce̱pe̱, na̱ wana ya̱nu ta shaani Hwe̱n bwa nꞌkáji ga̱mi.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ huri, be̱e̱ bisa̱ga̱ wyan mazama nama zumaa na̱ aka̱ta̱ku na ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌyapa nata̱ Yaahudiya.

Yeesu nꞌgani ana jwarigi buu // ana yigo
Maatiyu 4:18-22; Marukusu 1:16-20
Uyaan hwe̱n na Yeesu be̱ e̱she̱ na̱ inza̱n na Rwaga na O̱to̱ na Janiisarata+ :1 Rwaga na O̱to̱ na Janiisarata: Ta shi ruyaan ruzha̱a̱ naru Rwaga na O̱to̱ na Gaalili.awyatu abaa wuce kuta̱wuce do̱ko̱ nii be̱ na hyan ashiraaga mazama nama Hwe̱n.
Be̱ nda̱i ahantun na ma̱ni ree, ana ne̱e̱ na̱ inza̱n na rwaga na o̱to̱. Ana awyatu na kota̱ga̱ni na nꞌjooshiipa aba isaagi, abaa ha̱mbaraga ataaro.
Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni na̱ ame̱ na hantun ka̱ una shi na Biituru, be̱ bishi bwa ta̱hyan xbututumaa wuun ge̱ na̱ ame̱ na ma̱ni. Sa̱i be̱ hunrani na̱ ame̱ ma ga̱gaagana awyatu.Fishing net|hk00206c.tif|col|LUK 5:1-11|Horace Knowles|Ataaro|5:2Na be̱ hwii mazama, be̱ hin Biituru, <<Iya hantun kiiko naa iri, ita̱zhiga̱ni ataaro ninhin, imáni nꞌjooshiipa.>>
Biituru bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Butu o̱to̱, ga̱ri ta ga̱tu roci pina ma nda tuma ga̱tu kota̱ncin koori. Ama na gaa hin, nꞌnii tazhigana ataaro.>>
Na aba ta̱zhiga̱ni ataaro, aba kota̱ni nꞌjooshiipa ma̱ na nꞌta̱hyan ataaro ndaaba aba ribi ta̱naa kasaga.
Na aba nda̱i kunta, aba nꞌgani na̱ ara aya̱na̱ba na aba tanii kota̱ga̱na̱ nꞌjooshiipa xajaa na̱ hantun ndaaba, aguni wyan. Aba jaa na̱ hantun ndaaba, aba ciga̱hinii wyan da̱a̱da̱a̱, aba hantun aba ribi ta̱naa ira̱ga̱ na̱ wana maca̱ma̱nta̱n.
Na Siima Biituru bwa nda̱i iri na nje̱, bwa she̱nshe̱n na̱ aꞌuba̱ na Yeesu, bwa hin, <<Butu O̱to̱, hiika̱ do̱ko̱ na̱ ga̱mi, ga̱n shi butu naa pinsan.>>
Na̱ wana ta̱hyan Biituru na̱ ana aba tanaa kota̱ga̱na̱ nꞌjooshiipa atanda kuma̱ na̱ wana nꞌjooshiipa na nꞌaba kota̱ni ma̱.
Kunnu taa maa, Yaakubu na̱ Yoohana mꞌmwaan na n-Zabadi, aya̱na̱ba na kota̱ga̱ni na nꞌjooshiipa, aba nje̱ kuma̱.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin Biituru, <<Ta-ha̱nga rukwanyan, niina awyatu ta gaa naa nꞌdúubagi shii nꞌjooshiipa.>>
Na aba mánai hantun ndaaba na̱ inza̱n na rwaga na o̱to̱, aba ga̱a̱ komba̱ri na̱ komba̱ri, aba jwarigi Yeesu.
Yeesu kuda̱gahini // butu naa za mꞌmbwa
Maatiyu 8:1-4; Marukusu 1:40-45
Yaan hwe̱n na Yeesu be̱ ne̱e̱ na̱ yaan ce̱pe̱, buyaan butu bunaa suguma nasu tutuu hyo̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwaba bwa wuce. Na bwa nda̱i Yeesu, bwa hin sa̱nsantun na̱ aꞌuba̱ nde̱e̱be̱, bwa rupani buu ta̱hyan, <<Butu O̱to̱, kuu-ribi, bi-nii ara u-nꞌkuda̱gahini nꞌsuguma suniimi ma naa sabu.>>
Yeesu be̱ cikaa ara nde̱e̱be̱, be̱ a̱nta̱ni bwa ma hyaan, <<Nꞌribi. Kuda̱ga, u-naa sabu!>> Kupita suguma ta̱ba hwii, bwa kwade̱ge̱.
Yeesu be̱ bishi bwa ta̱hyan, <<Ta-bisa̱ kwan buyaan, sa̱i kuu-ja̱a̱ paaku pirisiti ubwaa nda̱i. Naazhin u-bisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan bi-kwade̱ge̱ na̱ nꞌsuguma sundaabi. U-gura̱a̱ mabwaciga ta̱shiri nata̱ ta̱shinran bikico̱, ku-Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa mꞌba hin, awyatu yansun ta̱hyan bi-ne̱e̱ sabu.>>
Hyo̱ nꞌta̱hyan Yeesu tahyan xata bisa̱ koo buyaan, mꞌba mazama mꞌbaa duwa̱na̱ kuta̱mawyasa. Awyatu abaa wuce kuta̱wuce na hyan ahange̱ mazama mande̱e̱be̱, akuda̱gahinai wyan na̱ nꞌta̱hange̱ce̱ sa̱ ta̱ndaaba.
Ama Yeesu be̱ ta he̱e̱n bihuri paaka za koo butu, wana hyan binje̱ ro̱pe̱.
Yeesu kuda̱gahini // butu naa ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ba so
Maatiyu 9:1-8; Marukusu 2:1-12
Uyaan hwe̱n na Yeesu be̱e̱ nda ta̱ga̱gaagana, ayaan Afaraasiya+ :17 Afaraasiya: Gwatana paa Haruwa na Ayaan Kala̱ma aba Shi.na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin+ :17 nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin: Gwatana paa Haruwa na Ayaan Kala̱ma aba Shi.na n-Muusa aba hunraani kaun. Ana tajábagi kope na̱ Gaalili na̱ Yaahudiya na̱ uce̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ Hurushaliima. Ta̱kai nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ba ne̱e̱ da̱nda̱ na̱ Yeesu nata̱ ta̱kuda̱gahina awyatu na ha̱ngagici sa̱.
Ayaan awyatu aba wuce ana shápi buyaan butu bunaa ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ba so, bwa taa taa na̱ aco̱ko̱. Abaa nda xata̱ha̱ni be̱ na̱ ame̱ na ina, arota̱a̱ be̱ na̱ aꞌuba̱ na Yeesu.
Wana hwarapi na awyatu ana ne̱e̱, aba de̱be̱ce̱ pa̱ri paaku ta̱ta̱ha̱na̱ bwa. Aba ka̱ta̱ni da̱da̱da̱ na ta̱biyana nata̱ aba ba̱ri kuta̱bara nata̱ bwa ina, aba be̱e̱ ibwa. Aba ciinha̱ni bwa huku na̱ aco̱ko̱ na bwa taa na̱ aba, aba rota̱a̱ bwa na̱ wyantancin naa gudu naa awyatu na̱ aꞌuba̱ na Yeesu.A man is lowered in front of Jesus|DN00444b.tif|col|LUK 5:17-25|Dunham Images|Aba ciinha̱ni butu na̱ aꞌuba̱ na Yeesu|5:19Na Yeesu be̱ nda̱i kaba pa̱ni nꞌgata nꞌndaaba nii be̱, be̱ hin bwaa naa taa, <<Bushikaa niimi, iiha̱mba̱ga̱ncin pinsan ndaa.>>
Nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na̱ Afaraasiya abaa ma huwo na̱ nꞌsume̱ sume̱ sundaaba, <<Iyaa ta na̱nna na̱ mazama nama hwashe̱ kunnu ku-Hwe̱n? Iyaa ta nii ara ta̱yaaciga butu pinsan naa shici Uhwe̱n?>>
Yeesu be̱ hoo ndaya iri na abaa mahyaan na̱ nꞌgata nꞌndaaba, be̱ hin wyan, <<Wana ba̱ ga̱hin makicihinaa mazama maya̱nu na̱ nꞌgata nꞌniinhin?
Ya̱ ta huri ta̱yoo ahin, <Iiha̱mba̱ga̱ncin pinsan ndaa,> koo ahin, <Hiika̱, u-huri ta̱hani>?
Too, nꞌribi ta̱hyan iyansun, Buyoo Butu mꞌbaa ta̱kai na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana nata̱ ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ncin butu pinsan.>> Sa̱i be̱ hin bubwa butu naa ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ba so, <<Iihin, hiika̱, u-sha̱pi aco̱ko̱ ndaa, u-huri giyo.>>
Kupita na̱ aꞌuba̱ na awyatu, butu bwa hiiki, bwa sha̱pi aco̱ko̱ na bwa tataa na̱ aba, bwa huri giyo ma yaba Hwe̱n.
Hyo̱ ndaaba aba nje̱ ma̱ wa̱ta̱ku na̱ nꞌrukwanyan ma yaba Hwe̱n, ma hyaan, <<Ba̱re ta̱nnda̱i iri na rukwanyan!>>
Yeesu nꞌgani Laawi
Maatiyu 9:9-13; Marukusu 2:13-17
Na maya̱nu mꞌba hwii, Yeesu be̱ ba̱ni hwa. Be̱ nda̱i butu naa ta naa raaga ga̱ndu bunaa aba ta nꞌgana Laawi+ :27 Laawi: Laawi ta aba ta nꞌgana Maatiyu.bwa hunrani kutuma ndaabwa. Yeesu be̱ ciita̱a̱gi bwa yishe, be̱ hin bwa, <<Nꞌjwárige̱.>>
Laawi bwa hiiki, bwa ga̱a̱ komba̱ri, bwa jwarigi Yeesu.
Sa̱i Laawi bwa ndaaki Yeesu ubuki na o̱to̱ na̱ ina ndaabwa. Awyatu na ta naa raaga ga̱ndu ahwarapi na̱ ayaan awyatu, aba cigi da̱ ma re̱ shami na̱ aba.
Ama Afaraasiya na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nꞌndaaba nami Nꞌgira̱nshin aba pa̱shi nꞌduunrin, aba kaki ana jwarigi Yeesu, ma hyaan wyan, <<Iba̱ shani ga̱hin re̱ shami na̱ awyatu na ta naa raaga ga̱ndu na̱ ana ga̱a̱ci pinsan?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni wyan be̱ hin, <<Awyatu na ne̱e̱ kami, uza na nii shana wyan amakaka na̱ butu naa njibi, kana ha̱ngagici sa̱.
Nꞌja̱a̱ci ma nꞌgana awyatu na bina̱, xapa̱ni pinsan baa, kana ga̱a̱ci pinsan.>>
Aha̱nta̱ni Yeesu // mazama nama ruꞌure̱ ta̱nda
Maatiyu 9:14; Marukusu 2:18-22
Sa̱i aba hin Yeesu, <<Awyatu na jwarigi Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma ata nda ruꞌure̱ na̱ ro̱pe̱ koya̱ ha̱ni, kunnu taa ana jwarigi Afaraasiya. Ama andaa, aba koya̱ ha̱ni anaa re̱, anaa swa.>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Ine̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan, inii ara ta̱yansan ta̱shika nata̱ ne̱e̱ da̱nda̱ na̱ butu naa zha̱a̱ buꞌa̱ ta̱re̱ shami na̱ hwe̱n na buki, aba na̱ bwa buki? Majaa nda.
Ama uhwe̱n wuci na aba ja̱a̱ shapa butu naa nje̱ ta̱wya̱ri, uha̱ni ya̱nu ta abaa naa ndaga ruꞌure̱ naazhin.>>
Yeesu be̱ bishi wyan mazama mana̱nna na̱ nꞌta̱kun, <<Buza naa nii handa da̱bi na fo, busha̱pi, buda̱ba̱ni da̱bi na gwashe̱. Kuunje̱ kunnu, bukunha̱ni na fo, una gwashe̱ bwa jaa gura̱a̱ magiya̱ na̱ na fo.
Buza naa nii zooga̱na̱ ma̱ni nama nꞌko̱ro̱ nama fo na̱ nꞌsoso na nꞌta̱sha̱a̱ ma̱ni nama gwashe̱. Kuunje̱ kunnu, ma̱ni nama nꞌko̱ro̱ nama fo manii punsa̱n nꞌsoso mawya̱shiki, nꞌsoso na nꞌta̱sha̱a̱ ma̱ni nꞌkuni.
Majaa nda. Na huri ta shi, xazooga̱ni ma̱ni nama nꞌko̱ro̱ nama fo kuna̱ nꞌsoso na nꞌfo.
Buza naa nii swa ma̱ni nama nꞌko̱ro̱ nama gwashe̱, buhin buribi nama fo. Bunii hyan, <Nama gwashe̱ mahuri gama.> >>

Ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ Yeesu // nata̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱
Maatiyu 12:1-8; Marukusu 2:23-28
Yaan hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya, Yeesu be̱ ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱hani na̱ ana jwarigi buu, abaa raan cima na shami. Ana jwarigi buu abaa hwara̱pigaga mꞌmansan na nꞌshami, abaa hwapaga na̱ ara, abaa re̱.
Ayaan Afaraasiya aba ha̱nta̱ni, <<Iba̱ shani ga̱hin nda iri na Nꞌgira̱nshin mꞌba hin xata nda na̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ nda̱tu?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Ka̱i! Icita̱gici iri na Dawuda bwa tanda ha̱ni na bwa na̱ awyatu ndaabwa na aba hange̱ rumunro̱n?
Bwa ta̱ni ina na Hwe̱n, bwa sha̱pi buroodi na aba sha̱a̱gi ku-Hwe̱n, aba re̱, bwa na̱ awyatu ndaabwa. Uburoodi na shi kapirisiti baa ka̱ abaa ara ta̱re̱.>>
Yeesu be̱ wanyin mazama mande̱e̱be̱, be̱ hin, <<Buyoo Butu taa shi Butu O̱to̱ naa hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱.>>
Yeesu kuda̱gahini butu // na̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱
Maatiyu 12:9-14; Marukusu 3:1-6
Na̱ yaan hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya, Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni ka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya, be̱e̱ ga̱gaagana wyan. Butu bwa ne̱e̱, bunaa ara ndaabwa na kataga bwa swa̱.
Nꞌyaan nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na̱ Afaraasiya aba tahunraana, aba gwataagi, anda̱i koo Yeesu nii kuda̱gahina be̱ na̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na̱ wana ade̱be̱ iri na hyan abishi awyatu binje̱ iri na zumaancin.
Yeesu be̱ hoo yansun hyo̱ iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌgata nꞌndaaba. Be̱ hin butu bwa naa ara bwa swa̱, <<Híike, u-jaa, u-isa na̱ aꞌuba̱ na awyatu paan.>> Bubwa butu bwa hiiki, bwa ja̱a̱, bwa e̱she̱ kaun.
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Iiha̱nta̱ni ma, mbata Nꞌgira̱nshin nda̱a̱tu mꞌba ta̱mpa̱ni ta̱nnje̱ na̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱? Ta̱nnje̱ iri na bina̱ koo na we̱, ta̱biha̱na̱ koo ta̱kuna?>>
Be̱ gwatani wyan hyo̱, naazhin be̱ hin bwa butu, <<Cikaa ara ndaa.>> Bubwa butu bwa cikaa ara, uꞌara ndaabwa ubwa kwade̱ge̱.
Afaraasiya na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin aba gware̱ sume̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, aba pa̱shi ta̱maga̱gaaga haruwa na abaa nda na̱ Yeesu.
Yeesu zwa̱ri atuma upwa na ree
Maatiyu 10:1-4; Marukusu 3:13-19
Na̱ nꞌhwe̱n ya̱nu, Yeesu be̱ ka̱ta̱ni undu xbinjé̱e̱ ro̱pe̱. Be̱ roci ma nda ro̱pe̱ ku-Hwe̱n.
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, be̱ nꞌgani awyatu na jwarigi buu, be̱ zwa̱ri aꞌupwa na reeko ana hyan anaa sa̱ nii be̱, ana be̱ tapa ruzha̱a̱ atuma na be̱ tazwara. Azha̱a̱zha̱a̱ ndaaba na:
Siima, bunaa Yeesu be̱ tapa ruzha̱a̱ Biituru,
na̱ Andaraawa buya̱na̱ naa Biituru,
na̱ Yaakubu,
na̱ Yoohana,
na̱ Filibu,
na̱ Baatalomi,
na̱ Maatiyu,
na̱ Toma,
na̱ Yaakubu buyoo Hala̱fa,
na̱ Siima, bunaa aba ta hyan butahura̱ ta̱ꞌisa hiku na̱ ce̱nye̱n ta̱ndaabwa,
na̱ Yaahuda buyoo Yaakubu,
na̱ Yaahuda Isikariyo̱ti, bunaa ja̱a̱ pana akwane̱ Yeesu.
Yeesu kuda̱gahinai awyatu
Maatiyu 4:23-25
Yeesu be̱ cíin undu huku na̱ atuma na be̱ tazwara upwa na reeko, be̱ e̱she̱ kuyaan koko na ha̱a̱n ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, huku na̱ awyatu hwarapi ana shi ana jwarigi buu. Na̱ nꞌkaba pa̱ri, awyatu hwarapi ana jaa kope na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya na̱ Hurushaliima, na̱ ce̱nye̱n nata̱ ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Taaya na̱ Sidon ana ne̱e̱ do̱ko̱ na̱ inza̱n na rwaga na o̱to̱.
Ana jaa na̱ wana xahange̱ mazama nama Yeesu, akuda̱gagi na̱ nꞌsuguma sundaaba. Be̱ kuda̱gahinai awyatu na nꞌhwaanwun na nꞌwe̱ mꞌba yanshin ta̱mataa.
Koo buya̱ bwa nje̱ buꞌa̱nta̱ni buu, na̱ wana ta̱kai ta̱báni waabe̱, aba kuda̱gagi bo̱do̱.
Yeesu ga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni // ana jwarigi buu
Maatiyu 5:1-12
Yeesu be̱ gwatani ana jwarigi buu. Be̱ hin,
<<Awyatu na ꞌwa̱ta̱gi,
ishi ana Hwe̱n bwa ndaaki rubara̱ka,
ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱shi ta̱niinhin.
Awyatu na rumunro̱n niina,
ishi ana Hwe̱n bwa ndaaki rubara̱ka,
inii ciga̱.
Awyatu na nii nꞌgaaga niina,
ishi ana Hwe̱n bwa ndaaki rubara̱ka,
inii ꞌwa̱ nꞌratu.
Ga̱hin, ishi ana Hwe̱n bwa ndaaki rubara̱ka
kawyatu ga̱a̱ ma,
abaa pe̱e̱n ma nii biin, abaa cwaaga ma,
abaa hyaan ma ga̱hin awyatu na we̱.
Abaa hyaan ma hyo̱ maya̱nu
na̱ wana ijwarigi Buyoo Butu!
<<Kumanje̱ kunnu, ha̱nga ma gama, inje̱ ta̱hibwa na̱ nꞌta̱guba̱ga̱, na̱ wana ufuna̱ ninhin ja̱a̱ naa o̱to̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱. Kunta ta adaadoo ndaaba aba tandaaka awyatu na ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ana taaríge̱ ma.
<<Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma,
ga̱hin awyatu na mꞌbaa iri ma̱ niina,
ihoo ha̱nga masuunran maniinhin.
Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma,
ga̱hin awyatu na cigi niina,
ija̱a̱ hunrana na̱ nꞌrumunro̱n.
Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma,
ga̱hin awyatu na nꞌratu niina,
ija̱a̱ naa na̱ nꞌsuro̱be̱ na̱ nꞌungwa.
Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma,
ga̱hin na awyatu abaa yaba ma,
na̱ wana kunta ta adaadoo ndaaba aba na ndaaka
acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ana ta̱be̱.
Ruba̱ ma anaa ribici ma
Maatiyu 5:38-48; 7:12
<<Ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, ga̱hin naa shiraagi, ruba̱ ma anaa ribici ma, inaa ndaakaka anaa ga̱a̱ ma iri na zumaa.
Inaa ndaakaka ana na̱maa pagana ma nu na we̱ rubara̱ka, inaa ndaakaka ana na̱maa pa ma ngwan ro̱pe̱.
Kuuyaan buupa̱shi na̱ ce̱be̱ na̱nna, u-kicihinani be̱ uyaan. Kuuyaan buura̱a̱ da̱bi ndaa na o̱to̱, ta-yansan be̱ binaa me̱.
Hyo̱ buna buuro̱pe̱ iri, u-pa̱ni be̱. Buna buura̱a̱ga̱gi iri, ta-hantana be̱ buukushihinani.
Inaa ndaakaka ma awyatu haruwa na ga̱hin ribi xana maa ndaakaka ma taa.
<<Kiiribi kawyatu naa ribi ma, uya̱ funa̱ ga̱hin nii da̱ba? Koo awyatu na pinsan ata ruba̱ awyatu na ribi wyan.
Kiinii ndaga iri na bina̱ kawyatu na ta naa maa ndaaka ma iri na bina̱, na ga̱hin nii da̱ba funa̱? Koo awyatu na pinsan ata nda kunnu.
Kushi kawyatu na na̱maa kuna ma wyaan ga̱hin nii pagana ta̱ꞌwapa, na ga̱hin nii da̱ba funa̱? Koo awyatu na pinsan, ata naa pagana ta̱ꞌwapa kawyatu na pinsan, na̱ wana hyan ajaa kushihinani wyan nge̱n.
<<Ga̱hin, ruba̱ ma anaa ribici ma, indaaki wyan iri na zumaa, pana ma ta̱ꞌwapa nata̱ ga̱hin jaa sha̱a̱ bigata ana̱maa kuna ma wyaan. Ta̱naa ndaga kunnu, ta ga̱hin nii da̱ba funa̱ o̱to̱, ishi mꞌmwaan na n-Uhwe̱n na Hura̱gi Ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, wana ushi una bina̱ kawyatu na a̱cii gooda̱ na̱ awyatu na ambyau.
XIshi awyatu na mbishiri, hakuu Shiinhin bwa shii naa mbishiri.
Ta-hyan ma kwayaa nje̱ pinsan
Maatiyu 7:1-5
<<Ta-ndaaka ma kwayaa suuga̱, ga̱hin taa maa Hwe̱n bwa jamaa ajamaa ndaaka ma suuga̱. Ta-hyan ma ayaan ashi awyatu na we̱, ga̱hin taa maa aba jamaa hyan ma ishi awyatu na we̱. Ta-ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ ma awyatu pinsan na abaa ndaaki ma, ga̱hin taa maa aba jamaa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ ma pinsan na ga̱hin ndaaki wyan.
Pana ma, ga̱hin taa maa aapa̱ni ma. Kiinje̱ kunnu inii raa ruꞌwana bwaa, aciga̱hini sururu uma ta̱ ta̱naa kinaa, u-cinta̱ni da̱bi aaka̱ncinha̱nini ma na bwe̱. Ruꞌwana naru ga̱hin ma̱a̱nyin wyan na̱ ruba, ruba ta Hwe̱n bwa na̱maa maanwyan ma na̱ ruba taa.>>
Yeesu be̱ bishi wyan mayaan mazama nꞌta̱kun, <<Buruba̱ ta naa mana buruba̱ angwo? Kanje̱ kunnu, hyo̱ aba nii mazwagana na̱ ibwa.
Bunaa abaa ga̱gaagana buhurici biwya̱ra̱mii ndaabwa, koo buya̱ bunaa hwii ta̱yansun ta̱ndaabwa, bunii naa hakii wya̱ra̱mi ndaabwa.
<<Ka̱i! Na̱ wana ba̱ gaa nda̱i bishashabi binaa ne̱e̱ na̱ ayishe na ayami, ama gaa nda̱ci uguguji na ne̱e̱ na̱ andaa yishe?
Na gaa nii ara ta̱hyan ayami, <Buya̱tu, xiiya̱a̱cigi bishashabi binaa ne̱e̱ na̱ ayishe ndaa.> Gaa na bi-maꞌa̱rici uguguji na ne̱e̱ na̱ ayishe ndaa ta̱yaaciga? Gaa butu naa za mahanda, yaaciga kwan uguguji na ne̱e̱ na̱ andaa yishe, naazhin u-a̱ri bishashabi naa ne̱e̱ na̱ ayishe na ayami ta̱yaaciga.
Ata insan ꞌwe̱e̱ // paaku ta̱ꞌwa̱ri ta̱ndaabwa
Maatiyu 7:16-20; 12:33-35
<<Kunta ta, uꞌwe̱e̱ na zumaa uꞌa̱cii ꞌwara ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ zumaancin, uꞌwe̱e̱ na zumaancin uꞌa̱cii ꞌwara ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ zumaa.
Ata insan koya̱ ꞌwe̱e̱ paaku ta̱ꞌwa̱ri ta̱ndaabwa. Za haruwa na aba nii gwasa ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ waanwan kusunrun koo uriga̱ kusa̱pi.
Butu naa bina̱ buta naa nda iri na bina̱, na̱ wana iri na bina̱ ta ne̱e̱ nii gata ndaabwa. Butu naa we̱ buta naa nda iri na zumaancin, na̱ wana iri na ne̱e̱ nii gata ndaabwa zumaancin. Iri na ne̱e̱ nii gata ibe̱ ta ta naa báni na̱ nu ndaabwa.
Awyatu reeko ana ta̱ma
Maatiyu 7:24-27
<<Na̱ wana ba̱ ga̱hin nii nꞌga, <Butu O̱to̱,> ga̱hin na, ga̱hin ga̱a̱ ta̱nda iri na ga̱mii hin ma nda ma?
Kwayaa na jaa wa̱ka̱mi, bwa nꞌshiragi, bwa nje̱ iri na ga̱n hin be̱ xbunje̱, nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ ma iri na butu naa bwa shi.
Bwa taa shi haku butu naa hiin ma ina ndaabwa, bwa kinji nꞌce̱nye̱n gba̱nga̱m, bwa she̱re̱ ta̱ma da̱da̱da̱ na tari. Na rwaga bwa cigi na̱ ma̱ni, ma̱ni mꞌba wuce xmata̱a̱cigi ina, ama ibe̱ zha̱a̱nta̱ncin na̱ wana buna shira wuun kami.
Kwayaa na hange̱ mazama maniimi, bwa nje̱ce̱ iri na ga̱n hin be̱ xbunje̱, nge̱n bwa ne̱e̱ na̱ butu naa ma̱ ina ndaabwa, bwa ma̱ncin wuun kami kunrin. Na rwaga bwa cigi na̱ ma̱ni, ma̱ni mꞌba ta̱tumaa ina, ina bwa huzhi ye̱ge̱ye̱ge̱.>>

Sooja na o̱to̱ // na pa̱nii gata ki-Yeesu
Maatiyu 8:5-13
Na Yeesu be̱ hwii iri ya̱nu hyo̱ ta̱cita̱ga̱ nꞌsuce̱be̱ nasu awyatu, be̱ ta̱ni Kapanahu.
Sooja na o̱to̱ kasooja na ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Rooma bwa tanaa, bwa mꞌbaa bugyama naa bwa hura̱gi ta̱ruba̱, bwa hange̱ce̱ sa̱ ma nda nꞌta̱ꞌwa̱.
Na ubwa sooja na o̱to̱ bwa hange̱ mazama nama Yeesu, bwa ka̱ji ayaan awyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya xarúpe̱ buu bijaa bikuda̱gahini bugyama ndaabwa.
Awyatu o̱to̱ aba ja̱a̱ paa Yeesu, aba ro̱pe̱ buu xbijaa bikuda̱gahini bugyama naa sooja. Aba hin, <<Butu na̱nna bugii na hyan u-ndaaki be̱ iri na bwa ribi,
na̱ wana buribi awyatu nda̱tu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, bwa ta̱ma̱ni ka̱ta̱ku wa̱tu.>>
Yeesu be̱ huri huku na̱ aba.
Na aba goki ina, ubwa sooja bwa ka̱ji ta̱shika ta̱ndaabwa, bwa hin xabishi Yeesu, <<Butu o̱to̱, ta-naa makwasa ꞌye̱n na̱ ga̱mi, ga̱n jwaci na hyan u-tá̱ni ina nimi.
Ga̱n gura̱a̱ ndaya shii sa̱i kunjaa wakaa. Cita̱ kumazama, bugyama niimi nii kuda̱ga.
Na̱ wana ga̱mi hyuhyu nimi nꞌne̱e̱ taa kunrin naa yaan, ayaan sooja aba ne̱e̱ taa kunrin nimi. Ga̱n ta hyan buka̱, <Jaga,> buja̱a̱, ma hyan buyaan, <Jaa,> bujaa. Ma hyan gyama niimi, <Nda kunna,> bunje̱ wuun.>>
Na Yeesu be̱ hange̱ kunnu, be̱ jikita̱ni mꞌmazama nama sooja, be̱ ke̱ce̱e̱ke̱ kiigudu naa awyatu be̱ hin wyan, <<Ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, ga̱n tade̱be̱ce̱ butu naa pa̱ni bigata hakuu na̱nna hyo̱ na̱ Isiraaꞌila.>>
Ta̱shika nata̱ sooja bwa takada tuma aba kúshiike̱ ina, aba nda̱i bugyama ndaabwa kwade̱ge̱.
Yeesu hiika̱hini be̱e̱ // binaa buꞌa̱ naa wya̱rugo aba ꞌwi
Bike̱nye̱n be̱ ta̱ci, Yeesu be̱ ja̱a̱ yaan ce̱pe̱ na aba ta hyan Nayin, ana jwarigi buu nii gudu na awyatu hwarapi aba huri huku nii be̱.
Na aba goki inco̱n naa be̱e̱ cice̱pe̱, aba nda̱i bigudu naa awyatu, aba shápi ruꞌwa̱ naru be̱e̱ biwya̱ri. Be̱ shi kiibe̱ kuuꞌa̱ naa awya̱rugo aba ꞌwi bwa za ta̱wya̱ri. Awyatu ndaabwa hwarapi ana jwárige̱ bwaa a̱.
Na Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu be̱ nda̱i bwaa a̱, be̱ cigi na ambishiri ndaabwa, be̱ hin bwaa a̱, <<Ta-naa nꞌgaga.>>
Be̱ ja̱a̱ do̱ko̱, be̱ a̱nta̱ni aco̱ko̱ na ruꞌwa̱, awyatu na shápi aco̱ko̱ aba e̱she̱. Be̱ hin, <<Baa, iihin hiika̱ isa!>>
Nii ke̱nye̱n be̱, baa bunaa taꞌwi bwa hiiki bwa nda mazama, Yeesu be̱ ꞌye̱e̱ be̱ kaya̱na̱ ndaabwa.
Koo buya̱ bwa hin baka, wana iri na nje̱, abaa yaba Hwe̱n. Abaa hyaan, <<Bunaa nii cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama naa o̱to̱ taa wuce wa̱tu.>> Aka̱ abaa hyaan, <<Hwe̱n tajaa ubiha̱ni awyatu ndaabwa.>>
Mazama nama iri na Yeesu be̱ nje̱ mꞌba ga̱ci kope na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya, na̱ mꞌbiin na nꞌta̱ba ce̱nye̱n.
Yeesu nje̱ mazama // nama Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma
Maatiyu 11:2-19
Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma bwa hange̱ hyo̱ iri na nje̱ paaka na jwarigi bwa. Bwa nꞌgani areeko ana jwarigi bwa,
bwa ka̱ji wyan tuma paa Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu xahántani buu, <<Gaa taa shi Ala̱masiihu bunaa ga̱tu ha̱mbagi bunii jaa, koo ta̱ha̱mbaga buyaan?>>
Na awyatu ya̱nu reeko aba wuce paa Yeesu, aba hin, <<Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma ta̱káji wakaa xta̱ha̱nta̱ni, <Gaa taa shi Ala̱masiihu bunaa ga̱tu ha̱mbagi bunii jaa, koo ta̱ha̱mbaga buyaan?> >>
Na̱ ha̱ni ya̱nu, Yeesu be̱ kuda̱gahinai awyatu hwarapi na ha̱ngagici sa̱, na̱ nꞌsuguma sundaaba, be̱ pa̱gi nꞌhwaanwun na nꞌwe̱ sumo̱, be̱ shani aruba̱ hwarapi aba huwa̱gi.
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni awyatu na Yoohana bwa káji, <<Kushiika ma ku-Yoohana, ibishi be̱ iri na ga̱hin nda̱i, na̱ iri na ga̱hin hange̱. Aruba̱ huwa̱gi, agurubi abaa jabaaga, awyatu ana za mꞌmbwa aba kuda̱gagi sabu, awo̱nro̱n aba tuba̱gi mazama ki, awyatu na ꞌwa̱gi aba hiika̱ki, aba bisa̱gi aꞌwa̱ta̱gi mazama nama zumaa.
Hwe̱n ndaaki butu naa za maree maree na̱ ga̱mi rubara̱ka.>>
Na awyatu na Yoohana bwa takáji aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱, Yeesu be̱e̱ nda mazama nii gudu na awyatu nama Yoohana, <<Iyaa ta ga̱hin tabana ta̱ndái na̱ hira̱ ceeku? Bunaa ne̱e̱ haka awyamu na nge̱nshe̱n na pyara bwaa puuka̱ koya̱a̱ biin?
Too, iyaa ta ga̱hin taja̱a̱ ta̱ndái? Bunaa ta̱a̱ni aꞌwana na yuwa? Nde̱e̱! Ana ta̱a̱ni aꞌwana na yuwa aba ne̱e̱ na̱ hunranhunran na masuunran, ane̱e̱ paaku ta̱gwama, shii na̱ aga.
Iyaa ta ga̱hin taja̱a̱ ta̱ndái? Butu naa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama? Too, ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, buna̱nna buhuri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ butu naa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama.
Yoohana ta shi bunaa utakaada na Hwe̱n aba tacita̱ ta̱hyan,
<< <Nde̱e̱! Ga̱n nii káji butuma niimi iyeebe ndaa,
bunaa na̱maa a̱sa̱ga̱a̱ga̱ yo̱n ta gaa wuco.>
Ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, buza butu wuma naa wuci Yoohana. Ama bunaa shi njeke njeke na̱ bina̱ ta̱za paaku ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n, buhuri bwa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.>>
Na hyo̱ awyatu aba hange̱ kunnu, huku na̱ awyatu na ta naa raaga ga̱ndu, aba ra̱ni ta̱hyan uyo̱n na Hwe̱n bwa ta shi na ta̱to̱n, na̱ wana Yoohana ndagi wyan baba̱tiisa̱ma.
Hyo̱ na̱ kunnu, Afaraasiya na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin aba ga̱a̱ ta̱nda iri na Hwe̱n bwa ribi na̱ aba, na̱ wana aga̱a̱ u-Yoohana ndagi wyan baba̱tiisa̱ma.
Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Haki ba̱ ga̱n nii kuta̱a̱ awyatu naa ke̱nye̱n yana ashi?
Ashi hakii gudu na mꞌmwaan na nꞌne̱e̱ paaku pa̱ri naka umuntun, abaa ma nꞌga azha̱a̱zha̱a̱ ndaaba, abaa hyaan,
<< <Ga̱tuu hurupa̱a̱ga̱ga̱ ma suru,
ga̱hin ga̱a̱ ta̱hibwa!
Ga̱tuu zhinyaana ma zha̱a̱ na ta̱ꞌwa̱,
ga̱hin ga̱a̱ ta̱naa nꞌgaaga!>
<<Kunnu taa mayaan Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma bwa wuce, bwa jaa re̱ga shami ninhin, bwa jaa swaga yaanyini na nii naa nda bwa. Hyo̱ mꞌmaya̱nu ga̱hin hyaan, <Wyatu na hira̱ jwarigi bwa.
Buyoo Butu bwa wuce, bwaa re̱ga shami ninhin, bwaa swaga iri ninhin na gama. Hyo̱ mꞌmaya̱nu ga̱hin hyaan, <Nde̱e̱! Bumama̱a̱ ta̱re̱e̱ bwa shi sowa̱, bwa shi ta̱shika nata̱ awyatu na ta naa raaga ga̱ndu na̱ awyatu na ga̱a̱ci pinsan.>
Hyo̱ na̱ kunnu, awyatu na yan ta̱yansun nata̱ Hwe̱n aba bisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan ushi mahanda.>>
Buꞌa̱ naa pinsan // shani Yeesu mariga̱
Buyaan Bufaraasiya naa aba ta nꞌgana Siima, bwa nꞌgani Yeesu shami ta̱re̱ na̱ ina ndaabwa. Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni ina na bwaa Faraasiya be̱ hunrani na hyan bire̱ shami.
Buyaan buꞌa̱ naa hunrani na̱ bwa ce̱pe̱, butanaa, bunaa hunranhunran ndaabwa bwa shi kuna pinsan. Bwa hange̱ Yeesu ne̱e̱ na̱ ina naa Faraasiya. Bwa shápi bindaashi naa aba ta san na̱ ayuwa o̱to̱, na̱ mꞌmariga̱ nama nꞌshima da̱.
Bwa ta̱ni, bwa hunrani nii biin naa mꞌbuna nde̱e̱be̱ ma nꞌgaga. Bwa jwa̱bi mꞌbuna na n-Yeesu cwe̱e̱n na̱ mꞌmaraba mandaabwa, ma shishimaa muu na̱ nꞌta̱hinje ta̱ndaabwa, ma hwaama muu. Bwaa shanaa muu mꞌba mariga̱.A woman wipes Jesus feet|WA03839b.tif|col|LUK 7:36-50|Wade Images|Buꞌa̱ nii shishimaa mꞌbuna na n-Yeesu|7:38Naa Faraasiya naa taꞌnꞌgana Yeesu bwa nda̱i iri na buꞌa̱ bwaa nda, bwa hin nii gata ndaabwa, <<Butu na̱nna bushici butu naa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama.
