XBwa shi mahanda Hwe̱n ta káji be̱, kuuyan buꞌa̱ na nii antaana be̱. Buꞌa̱ naa pinsan ta.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin bwaa Faraasiya, <<Siima, ga̱n mꞌbaa iri na ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱.>>
Siima bwa hin, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, mꞌbishi.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Buyaan butu bwa ꞌwa̱a̱pi ayaan awyatu reeko ayuwa, buka̱ ayuwa azurufa nꞌyina̱ nꞌta, buyaan kuje ta.
Hyo̱ ndaaba aba reeko buza na a̱ri ta̱ndupa, bwa ga̱a̱gi wyan wyaan. Ta̱ndaya ta̱ndaabi, buya̱a̱ taa nii hura̱ be̱ ta̱ruba̱?>>
Siima bwa ra̱ni, <<Na̱ nꞌta̱ndaya ta̱niimi, bunaa aba taga̱a̱gi na huri o̱to̱.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Bi-nje̱ suuga̱ ki.>>
Yeesu be̱ ke̱ce̱e̱ke̱ kuubwaa a̱, be̱ hin Siima, <<Gwatana a̱a̱ na̱nna. Na ga̱n tá̱ni ina ndaa, gaa mꞌpa̱ncin ma̱ni nama ta̱ha̱mbara aputu na mꞌbuna, ama buꞌa̱ na̱nna bwa jwa̱bi mꞌbuna nꞌniimi na̱ mꞌmaraba, bwa shishe̱me̱ na̱ nꞌta̱hinje ta̱ndaabwa.
Na ga̱n tá̱ni ina ndaa, gaa nꞌhincin koo ha̱nnu na̱ wuco, ama buꞌa̱ na̱nna tana ga̱n tawuce buga̱a̱ci ta̱naa antaana mꞌbuna niimi na̱ nu ndaabwa.
Gaa nꞌshancin mariga̱ na̱ hyuhyu nimi, ama bwaa bwaa nꞌshani mariga̱ nama nꞌshima na̱ mꞌbuna niimi.
Ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱, aha̱mba̱gici apinsan ndaabwa hwarapi mahwa, ta shani bwa bisa̱a̱ ta̱ruba̱ ta̱ndaabwa na̱ ga̱n. Ama bunaa aba ha̱mba̱ga̱ncin pinsan ge̱, bubisa̱a̱ ta ta̱ruba̱ ta̱ndaabwa ge̱.>>
Nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu, Yeesu be̱ hin bwaa a̱, <<Aaha̱mba̱ga̱ncin pinsan ndaa.>>
Awyatu ka̱ ana abaa re̱ shami na̱ aba, aba pa̱shi ta̱naa macita̱ga̱ na̱ nꞌsume̱ sundaaba, <<Iyaa ta na̱nna bwa shi, na bwa nii hyan aaha̱mba̱ga̱ncin pinsan?>>
Yeesu be̱ hin a̱, <<Ta̱panaa gata ndaabi kuga̱n ta̱a̱biha̱ni, hura̱ gumunu.>>

Aꞌa̱ na ne̱e̱ huku na̱ Yeesu
Naa ke̱nye̱n be̱ huri ge̱, Yeesu be̱ jwara̱gagani ace̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ na̱ nꞌcice̱pe̱ na nꞌnjeke ma bisa̱ga̱ mazama nama zumaa nama ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n. Atuma upwa na ree na be̱ tazwara ma naawan nii be̱,
na̱ ayaan aꞌa̱ ana be̱ kuda̱gahinii nꞌhwaanwun na nꞌwe̱ na̱ nꞌsuguma sundaaba. Azha̱a̱zha̱a̱ ndaaba na:
Maariyamu, binaa aba ta nꞌgana Magadalina,
binaa aba taba̱ha̱na̱ awyatu na hira̱ ta̱nda̱ra̱,
Yowana aꞌa̱yo Kuuza,
butu o̱to̱ naa tuma na ina naa gwama Hirudu,
Suuzaana,
na̱ ayaan aꞌa̱ hwarapi.
Aba a̱ abaa sanwyaan wyan iri na aba ribi na̱ iri ndaaba.
Mazama nama ta̱kun nama buhwaanyan
Maatiyu 13:1-9; Marukusu 4:1-9
Na awyatu hwarapi aba mawuna̱ni, awyatu abaa duwa̱ni kuta̱wuce kuꞌnꞌcice̱pe̱ na̱ nꞌcice̱pe̱, Yeesu be̱ bishi wyan mazama mana̱nna na̱ nꞌta̱kun,
<<Buyaan buhwaanyan tabana na̱ kaasu xbuwya̱shi na̱ cima. Na bwaa wyasa ibe̱ kaasu, ika̱ ibe̱ kinai na̱ yo̱n, awyatu aba fo̱nje̱ wuun, nꞌno̱no̱ mꞌba ta̱in wuun.
Ika̱ ibe̱ kinai kapaga, na ibe̱ báni, pa̱ri kaba hoogi, ibe̱ ꞌwi wana be̱e̱ ko za ta̱ra̱mi.
Ika̱ ibe̱ kinai kuꞌasa̱pi, na ibe̱e̱ mawaani, asa̱pi aba hwii wuun ta̱tuba̱ga̱, ibe̱ nje̱ce̱ bina̱.
Ika̱ ibe̱ kinai kupa̱ri naka mꞌbaa mawundu, na ibe̱ báni, ibe̱ nje̱ bina̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, be̱ ꞌwa̱ruba̱ni biyina̱ ka̱ kaba tawyasa.>>
Na be̱ cici maya̱nu, be̱ ta̱a̱ni nu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, be̱ hin, <<Hyo̱ bunaa mꞌbaa ce̱be̱ na ta̱tuba̱ xbutibi.>>
Yeesu be̱ bishi aꞌupwa na ree // iri na shani ta̱ba ta̱kun
Maatiyu 13:10-17; Marukusu 4:10-12
Ana jwarigi buu upwa na ree aba ha̱nta̱ni buu iri na ta̱ba ta̱kun ta̱ba hin.
Be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Ga̱hin, aapa̱ni ma na hyan iyansun ashe̱re̱ na ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n. Ama aka̱ ga̱n bisa̱gi wyan kuꞌnꞌta̱kun, wana,
<< <Anii gwataaga aba jaa ndaya,
ashiraaga aba jaa yansun iri na cici.>
Yeesu be̱ bishi wyan // iri na ta̱ba ta̱kun // nata̱a̱ hwaanyan ta̱ba shi
Maatiyu 13:18-23; Marukusu 4:13-20
<<Too, iri na ta̱ba ta̱kun ta̱ba shi na. Ikaasu ta shi haku mazama nama Hwe̱n.
Ikaasu na kinai na̱ yo̱n ibe̱ ta shi haka awyatu na hange̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n. Ama Bupira̱ bwa wuce, bwa ya̱a̱cigi muu na̱ nꞌgata nꞌndaaba wana ta̱hyan xata pana nꞌgata nꞌndaaba mabiha̱ni wyan.
Ikaasu na kinai na̱ apaga ibe̱ ta shi haka awyatu na hange̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n, aba ra̱a̱ muu nꞌara nꞌree. Ama mꞌba irici na̱ nꞌgata nꞌndaaba wana ashi haki shami na e̱she̱ be̱ za anga̱nga̱nda̱ na iri na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n. Kungwan wuce ape̱e̱n muu nii inro̱n, aba jaa isa na̱ nꞌta̱pana nꞌgata nꞌndaaba.
Ikaasu na kinai kuꞌasa̱pi ibe̱ ta shi haka awyatu ana hange̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n. Ama kane̱e̱ ji yaan ha̱ni wana ta̱makaka na̱ iri na sa̱ra̱ri yana na̱ hunranhunran na mansuunran, ushaani wyan aba jaa mawaana na hyan anje̱ kaasu na bina̱.
Ikaasu ina kinai nii koo naa mawundu, ibe̱ ta shi haka awyatu na hange̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n, aba ha̱mba̱gi muu bigata ka̱ na̱ akuri, sa̱i na mꞌba mazama mꞌba nje̱ kaasu na bina̱.
Ta̱kun nata̱ maza̱ki nama ra
Maatiyu 4:21-25
<<Buza naa nii pantaan pitila buꞌuuta̱ni wuun ugwambwa, koo busoo wuun na̱ kunrin na wyansun. Na̱ nꞌta̱nda kunnu, sa̱i da̱i buca̱guda̱ni wuun nii ꞌwa̱ruꞌwa̱ru wana ta̱hyan ana nii tá̱ni agwataga ta̱gwaan.
Hyo̱ iri na ne̱e̱ ta̱swee, anii bara̱nwyan wuun na̱ sa̱ra̱ri. Iri na guna̱a̱ni, anii guna̱a̱ wuun inaa hoo.
Na̱ wana kunnu, iya ma shukuu iyansun mazama nama ga̱hin shiraagi. Wana ta̱hyan ana nꞌshiraagi ki, Hwe̱n nii duwa̱na̱ wyan ta̱yansun. Ana yancin koo ge̱, aba ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan aba yan, ge̱ na aba yan Hwe̱n nii yaaciga wyan wuun.>>
Aya̱na̱ Yeesu na̱ aya̱na̱ba
Maatiyu 12:4-50; Marukusu 3:31-35
Too, sa̱i aya̱na̱ Yeesu na̱ aya̱na̱ba aba jaa xanda̱i buu, ama wana hwarapi na awyatu na ne̱e̱ aba a̱rici ta̱wuta̱ paa be̱ ne̱e̱.
Sa̱i buyaan butu bwa bishi Yeesu ta̱hyan, <<Ada̱a̱da̱ ndaa na̱ ayamboo aꞌisagi na̱ sa̱ra̱ri, aribi ta̱a̱ndaya.>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Ana hange̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n, aba jwarigi muu, aba nje̱ iri na mꞌba hin xanje̱, aba ta shi ada̱a̱da̱ nimi na̱ aya̱too.>>
Yeesu shani upyara na̱ ma̱ni // aba nje̱ fo̱n
Maatiyu 8:23-27; Marukusu 4:35-41
Uyaan hwe̱n Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni na̱ awyatu na jwarigi buu, be̱ hin wyan, <<XTa̱ka̱a̱ci ma hira̱ree na rwaga na o̱to̱.>> Sa̱i aba pa̱shi ta̱hani.
Aba na̱ nꞌta̱hani, sa̱i nꞌrabi mꞌba sha̱pi Yeesu. Kupyara bwa punshin munta̱ kpukpukpu na̱ kai ma puuka̱ na̱ ame̱ na bwa rwaga na o̱to̱. Uhantun ndaaba bwa ribi ta̱ciga̱ na̱ ma̱ni, koo buya̱ bwa sha̱pi ta̱hyan bunii ꞌwa̱.Jesus rebukes the wind and the waves|WA03848b.tif|col|LUK 8:23-25|Wade Images|Yeesu yinzha̱nkani upyara na̱ ma̱ni|8:24Sa̱i ana jwarigi buu aba ja̱a̱ paa Yeesu, aba hiika̱hini buu, ma hyaan, <<Butu O̱to̱, Butu O̱to̱! Ta̱na̱manhuwa̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱.>>
Be̱ zhe̱mbe̱, be̱ yinzha̱nkani pyara na̱ ama̱ma̱ni na nii rokuuco, aba nje̱ fo̱n.
Be̱ hin ana jwarigi buu, <<Ipa̱ncin nꞌgata niinhin na̱ ga̱mi?>>
Ama aba ha̱ngagi rukwanyan, aba nje̱ kuma̱, abaa mahyaan, <<Ya̱ butu na kunna? Bunaa upyara na̱ ata na ma̱ni mꞌba nje̱ iri na bwa hin xmanje̱!>>
Yeesu kuda̱gahini // butu naa mꞌbaa awyatu na hira̱
Yeesu na̱ awyatu na jwarigi buu aba ta̱ta̱hura̱ nꞌta̱hani, aba ka̱a̱ci Rwaga na O̱to̱ na Gaalili, aba wuci ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Agarasa̱na nata̱ ne̱e̱ kaun.
Yeesu ma ca̱a̱n kuꞌinza̱n, be̱ ura̱ku kuna̱ butu naa awyatu na hira̱ aba jwarigi bunaa bwa ce̱pe̱. Bunaa pa̱ nꞌyo̱, bwa ta̱a̱nici da̱bi, bwa a̱cii ara ta̱hunrana na̱ ina kupaa kaꞌabotubotu na paga na aba ta naa wuma̱a̱na̱ awyatu.
Na bwa nda̱i Yeesu, bwa ta̱a̱ni nu, bwa kinai pwan na̱ aꞌuba̱ nde̱e̱be̱, ma hyaan, <<Yeesu, Buyoo Hwe̱n na Hura̱gi Ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, iba̱a̱ ta̱ gbi na̱ ga̱mi? Iiro̱pe̱, ta-mꞌpa ngwan.>>
Bucici kunnu, wana ta̱hyan, Yeesu hoo hyan bihwaanwun naa we̱ xbiba̱ni na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabwa. Koo na aba ta he̱e̱n aka̱da̱a̱gi bwa na̱ akaca ara na̱ mꞌbuna aha̱mba̱ga̱ bwa, buhwii wyan ta̱ka̱kasa bihwaanwun ꞌye̱e̱ be̱ aga paaka za koo butu.
Yeesu be̱ ha̱nta̱ni bwa, <<Iyaa ta shi ruzha̱a̱ rundaabi?>>
Bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Bigudu,>> wana ta̱hyan awyatu na hira̱ hwarapi tane̱e̱ na̱a̱ bwa.
Aba rupani buu ma makusuma̱a̱ ji nii be̱ ta̱hyan xbita ta̱tumaa wyan kuꞌibwa na maꞌira̱ mandaabwa mꞌba swe̱nce̱n.
Bigudu naa sudo̱n nasu ina suhwarapi suba tanaa piree nii biin binaa undu ma re̱ ta̱re̱e̱. Awyatu na hira̱ aba ro̱pe̱ Yeesu ta̱hyan xbiga̱a̱ wyan ata̱ni suun. Be̱ ga̱a̱ wyan.
Sa̱i aba awyatu na hira̱ aba ga̱a̱ bubwa butu, aba ta̱ni sudo̱n nasu ina. Suba sudo̱n suba hiiki na̱ nꞌsumo̱, suba huri cuun kusha̱ru naa undu, suba mazooni na̱ ame̱ na dabu na o̱to̱, suba gura̱kakani ma̱ni, suba hwii ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱.
Na aba awyatu na tane̱e̱ na̱ iyo̱ na suba sudo̱n aba nda̱i kunta, aba gida̱ga̱gi zhagu ce̱pe̱ na̱ nꞌinro̱n na nꞌce̱pe̱ xabisa̱gi awyatu.
Awyatu aba bánai xanda̱i iri na nje̱. Na aba wuce paa Yeesu, aba nda̱i bubwa butu naa awyatu na hira̱ aba ba̱ni waabwa, buhunrani do̱ko̱ na̱ Yeesu. Bwa ta̱a̱ni da̱bi, aha̱nka̱ri ndaabwa fo̱n. Rukwanyan ruba kota̱ni wyan hyo̱ ndaaba.
Ana tanaa na̱ ha̱ni na ibe̱ iri be̱ tanda, abaa bisa̱ga̱ awyatu haruwa na bwa nje̱, bwa binini.
Too, hyo̱ awyatu na ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Agarasa̱na, aba ro̱pe̱ Yeesu ta̱hyan xbiga̱a̱gi wyan ce̱pe̱ ndaaba, wana ta̱hyan rukwanyan rukota̱ni wyan ta̱ꞌo̱to̱. Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni, be̱ kwashe̱e̱ke̱.
Na Yeesu be̱ hiin hura̱, bwa butu naa be̱ taba̱ha̱ni awyatu na hira̱ bwa ro̱pe̱ buu ta̱hyan xahurogo da̱nda̱ na̱a̱ bwa. Ama Yeesu be̱ kwashe̱he̱ne̱ bwa, be̱ hin bwa,
<<Giya̱ ina, u-bishi awyatu ndaa iri na Hwe̱n bwaa ndaaki.>> Sa̱i bubwa butu bwa jwara̱gagani hyo̱ ubwa ce̱pe̱ ma cita̱ga̱ iri na Yeesu be̱ ndaaki bwa.
Buyoo Yaarisu // na̱a̱ a̱ naa a̱nta̱ni da̱bi na Yeesu
Na Yeesu be̱ kwashe̱e̱ke̱ hira̱ree na rwaga na o̱to̱, awyatu hwarapi aba ra̱a̱ buu nꞌara nꞌree, wana ta̱hyan atahoo ha̱mbaga buu.
Kuyaan butu naa aba ta nꞌgana Yaarisu, bunaa shi butu o̱to̱ naa ka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya, bwa wuce na̱ aꞌuba̱ na Yeesu, bwa mata̱ pa̱m do̱ko̱ na̱ mꞌbuna nꞌnde̱e̱be̱. Bwa ro̱pe̱ buu xbijaa ina ndaabwa,
wana ta̱hyan be̱e̱ bindaabwa binaa a̱ binaa bwa mashikani bika̱, binaa nꞌyo̱ nꞌupwa na̱ nꞌree, binii nda na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwa̱.
Na Yeesu be̱ kota̱ni yo̱n na zhagu ina na Yaarisu, awyatu aba jwarigi buu abaa masuka koo biya̱a̱ biin.
Na̱ ame̱ na aba awyatu, buꞌa̱ bwa ne̱e̱ bunaa mꞌbaa suguma nasu bwaa zoo mahiin nꞌyo̱ nꞌupwa na̱ nꞌree. Bwa hwii hyo̱ iri ndaabwa ta̱wyashikaka kawyatu na njibi,+ :43 Ta̱taga nata̱ yigo ta̱ka̱ ta̱za mazama mana̱nna, Bwa hwii hyo̱ iri ndaabwa ta̱wyashikaka kawyatu na njibi.ama buza naa a̱ri ta̱kuda̱gahina bwa.
Sa̱i bwa pe̱ke̱ wyantancin na awyatu, bwa a̱nta̱ni da̱bi na Yeesu nii biin. Kupita mahiin nama bwa tanaa bana mꞌba ꞌya̱pi.
Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Iyaa ta nꞌa̱nta̱ni?>>
Koo buya̱ bwa hin shii bwa ta. Biituru bwa hin, <<Butu O̱to̱, awyatu riini kope ta abaa masuka.>>
Ama Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Buyaan buꞌnꞌa̱nta̱ni, nꞌhange̱ ta̱kai ta̱ba̱ni na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwaba ta̱niimi, ta shani ga̱n yan.>>
Na bwaa a̱ bwa nda̱i ta̱hyan aꞌipitani bwa, bwa ba̱ni ma jikita̱, bwa mata̱ pa̱m na̱ aꞌuba̱ na Yeesu. Pita na̱ uba̱ na awyatu hyo̱, bwa bisa̱gi buu iri na shani bwa a̱nta̱ni buu na̱ kuubwa kwade̱ge̱ kupita.
Yeesu be̱ hin bwa, <<Be̱e̱ biniimi, ta̱panaa gata ndaabi kuga̱n ta̱a̱biha̱ni. Hura̱ gumunu.>>
Yeesu ma cita̱ga̱ kunnu, kuutuma bwa wuce, bunaa ina na Yaarisu ma bisa̱ga̱ Yaarisu ta̱hyan, <<Ta-maa ma biwya̱ra̱mi yata ngwan ꞌye̱n, da̱du ndaa hoo ꞌwa̱.>>
Ama na Yeesu be̱ hange̱ kunnu, be̱ hin Yaarisu, <<Ta-ha̱nga rukwanyan, kuu-shii bigata na̱ ga̱mi, binii gura̱a̱ kúshe̱ buwuma.>>
Na be̱ wuci bwa ina, be̱ ta̱ncin na̱ awyatu ma̱, sa̱i ku-Biituru na̱ Yoohana na̱ Yaakubu, na̱ ashin na be̱e̱ na̱ aya̱na̱.
Hyo̱ awyatu na ne̱e̱ na̱ bwa ina abaa taaga maraba, aka̱ ma nꞌgaaga na̱ wana be̱e̱ bibe̱e̱. Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Ta-naa nꞌgaaga ma, biꞌwici, bitaa ta nꞌrabi.>>
Hyo̱ ndaaba abaa ꞌwa̱ buu nꞌratu, wana ta̱hyan ayan be̱e̱ bihoo ꞌwa̱.
Yeesu be̱ kota̱ni be̱e̱ bibe̱e̱ ara, be̱ ta̱a̱ni nu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, be̱ hin, <<Be̱e̱ biniimi, hiika̱!>>
Be̱e̱ bibe̱e̱ be̱ kúshihine̱ nꞌhunjo̱, be̱ he̱e̱n kaki. Yeesu be̱ bishi wyan ta̱hyan xapa̱ buu shami.
Ana ma̱ncin buu aba nje̱ kuma̱, Yeesu be̱ kooci wyan ta̱hyan xata bisa̱ koo buyaan iri na nje̱.

Yeesu ka̱ji ana be̱ tazwara // upwa na ree
Maatiyu 10:5-15; Marukusu 6:7-13
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ nꞌgani ana be̱ tazwara upwa na̱ ree, hyo̱ ndaaba na̱ ha̱ni ka̱, be̱ pa̱ni wyan ta̱kai na̱ nꞌta̱gwama na ta̱hyan xaba̱ha̱ni hyo̱ awyatu na hira̱ na we̱ na̱ nꞌta̱kuda̱gahinaa suguma.
Too, sa̱i be̱ ka̱ji wyan ta̱hyan xaja̱a̱ abísa̱gi awyatu mazama nama ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n, akuda̱gahinai awyatu.
Be̱ hin wyan, <<Ta-shapa ma koori na̱ nꞌta̱ba ta̱hani, ta-shapa ma angwo, koo ka̱fu, koo shami, koo yuwa, koo maa uyaan da̱bi na hin reenu.
Hyo̱ paa ina na ga̱hin wuci abaa ra̱a̱ ma, inaa rota̱ga̱ na̱ bwa ina hara̱ kiike̱nye̱n naa ga̱hin gaa ubwa ce̱pe̱.
Hyo̱ uce̱pe̱ na ga̱hin wuci abaa ra̱a̱ci ma, iba̱ni wuun, ibukuta̱gi aputu na mꞌbuna nꞌniinhin, ta shi ibisa̱a̱ wyan ta̱hyan aꞌmꞌbaa suuga̱ ku-Hwe̱n.>>
Sa̱i aba huri, aba jwara̱gagani nꞌcice̱pe̱ nꞌcice̱pe̱ hyo̱ ma nda mazama nama zumaa ma kuda̱gahinaa awyatu kope.
Hirudu ra̱shi iri na ta̱nda
Maatiyu 14:1-12; Marukusu 6:14-29
Na Hirudu Antipasi bunaa tanaa na̱ nꞌta̱gwama nata̱ Gaalili, bwa hange̱ mazama nama iri na nii ndaga, bwa ra̱shi iri na ta̱nda. Wana ta̱hyan awyatu ka̱ nii hyaan Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma tahíike kuta̱ꞌwa̱.
Aka̱ abaa hyaan Iliya ta gura̱a̱ kúshiike̱, aka̱ abaa hyaan buyaan bunaa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama naa hasaa bwa taa kúshe̱e̱ wuma.
Hirudu bwa hin, <<Nꞌtahoo ꞌyapa Yoohana hyuhyu. Too, buya̱ butu nu ga̱n ha̱ngaga iri ya̱nu ndaabwa?>> Sa̱i bwaa nda haruwa na hyan bunda̱i Yeesu.
Yeesu pa̱ awyatu dubu ta shami
Maatiyu 14:13-21; Marukusu 6:30-44; Yoohana 6:1-14
Na ana be̱ tazwara upwa na ree aba kúshiike̱, aba bisa̱gi Yeesu hyo̱ iri na aba ndagi. Sa̱i be̱ sha̱pi wyan baa ka̱ nii be̱ zhagu yaan bibiin naa ce̱pe̱ na aba ta nꞌgana Batasaida.
Na awyatu aba hange̱ bine̱e̱ piree, aba jwarigi buu. Be̱ ra̱a̱ wyan nꞌara nꞌree, be̱ bisa̱gi wyan mazama nama ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n, be̱ kuda̱gahinai ana ha̱ngagici sa̱.
Na hwe̱n bwa pa̱ ta̱ꞌira̱, aba upwa na̱ ree aba jaa waabe̱ aba hin buu, <<Cipana awyatu xahura̱gi kuꞌnꞌcice̱pe̱ na̱ nꞌina na nꞌnaanyin kaun, awyanza̱in shami na̱ paaku rocu na̱ wana paa ga̱tun ne̱e̱ za iri na ne̱e̱ pina.>>
Ama Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Ga̱hin, pa ma wyan shami na ta̱re̱ mana.>>
Aba hin buu, <<Hyo̱ iri na ga̱tu mꞌbaa hurici mꞌburoodi nꞌta na̱ nꞌjooshiipa nꞌree. Sa̱i da̱i kuta̱nii jaga ta̱sáanyin awyatu na̱nna shami o̱to̱ na hyo̱ ndaaba.>>
Awyatu wya̱ri aba tanaa do̱ko̱ adubu ta.
Yeesu be̱ hin ana jwarigi buu, <<Hyan ma awyatu, xamata̱gi nꞌgudu sukuje ta ta ta, ahunraana.>>
Aba nje̱ iri na be̱ hin wyan xanje̱, awyatu aba hunraani hyo̱.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ sha̱pi mꞌba mꞌburoodi nꞌta na̱ nꞌjooshiipa nꞌree, be̱ ka̱cihini yishe da̱da̱da̱, be̱ gooji Hwe̱n, be̱ kusagi wyan, be̱ pa̱ni ana jwarigi buu xahoosa̱ga̱ni awyatu.
Hyo̱ ndaaba aba re̱, aba ciga̱gi. Na aba hwii, aba wuna̱a̱ni na bwe̱ nꞌtumunsun nꞌupwa na̱ nꞌree.
Biituru cici Yeesu shi naa Hwe̱n
Maatiyu 16:13-19; Marukusu 8:27-29
Uyaan hwe̱n Yeesu be̱ ma nda ro̱pe̱ be̱e̱ ka̱, ana jwarigi buu aba ne̱e̱ do̱ko̱. Be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Iyaa awyatu aba nii hyaan nꞌshi?>>
Aba ra̱ni, aba hin, <<Aka̱ nii hyaan gaa taa shi Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma, aka̱ aba nii hyaan gaa taa shi Iliya bunaa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, aka̱ abaa nii gura̱a̱ hyaan buyaan bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama naa hasaa taa kúshe̱ buwuma.>>
Be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan, <<Ga̱hin paa? Iyaa ta ga̱hin hyaan nꞌshi?>>
Biituru bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Gaa taa shi Ala̱masiihu na Hwe̱n.>>
Yeesu cici ta̱ꞌwa̱ ta̱nde̱e̱be̱
Maatiyu 16:20-28; Marukusu 8:31--9:1
Yeesu be̱ kooci wyan ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ xata bisa̱ koo buka̱ mꞌba mazama.
Be̱ gura̱a̱ hyan wyan, <<Mahanda, ga̱ga̱ga̱ Buyoo Butu bwa nii swa ta̱guma koo ta̱ya̱. Awyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya na̱ apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin abaa gaa buu. Ga̱ga̱ga̱ abaa kuna buu buꞌwi, uhwe̱n na hin taatu buhiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱.>>
Too, sa̱i be̱ hin wyan hyo̱ ndaaba, <<Hyo̱ bunaa nꞌribi ta̱ꞌnꞌjwara̱ga xbuga̱a̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa, busha̱pi uguguji+ :23 uguguji: Gwatana paa Haruwa na Ayaan Kala̱ma aba Shi.ndaabwa na ta̱ꞌwa̱ koya̱ hwe̱n, buꞌnꞌjwara̱ga.
Hyo̱ bunaa ribi ta̱wungumana hyuhyu ndaabwa, buja̱a̱ci da̱ba wuun. Ama hyo̱ bunaa ga̱a̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa wana ga̱mi, buja̱a̱ da̱ba wuun.
Uya̱ funa̱ butu bwa de̱be̱, kuude̱be̱ iri na sa̱ra̱ri yana hyo̱, bwa ja̱a̱ci da̱ba ta̱nda bina̱ na mahwa?
Hyo̱ bunaa hange̱ nꞌkogi na nꞌta̱nyansun na̱ mꞌmazama maniimi, Buyoo Butu taa bwa ja̱a̱ ha̱nga nꞌkogi na nꞌta̱nyansun bwa, ha̱ni na bwa ja̱a̱ wuce na̱ nꞌta̱gwama ta̱ndaabwa na̱ nꞌta̱gwama nata̱ Ashin Hwe̱n na̱ nata̱ atuma ndaabwa ana ne̱e̱ sabu.
Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, suga̱hin ne̱e̱ pina ane̱e̱ ana jaa ꞌwa̱, sa̱i kanda̱i ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n.>>
Yeesu he̱re̱ge̱ mꞌpirwa
Maatiyu 17:1-8; Marukusu 9:2-8
Na nꞌhwe̱n nꞌta̱ndatu mꞌba huri na be̱ nje̱ mazama mꞌba, Yeesu be̱ sha̱pi Biituru na̱ Yoohana na̱ Yaakubu, aba ka̱ta̱ni da̱da̱da̱ na undu nii be̱ xanjé̱e̱ ro̱pe̱.
Be̱ ma nda ro̱pe̱, apusa̱ka nde̱e̱be̱ aba he̱re̱ge̱ mꞌpirwa, aꞌwana nde̱e̱be̱ aba kwashe̱ tande̱ paawu ma shapaga ayishe.
Mayaan mazama mꞌba za, kawyatu ree abaa nda mazama nii be̱, Muusa na̱ Iliya, ana ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama.
Aba taa maa koo buya̱ paawu munta̱ manyan manyan na ta̱báni na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ma nda mazama na̱ Yeesu nama kiibe̱e̱ ꞌwa̱ na̱ Hurushaliima ku-Hwe̱n bwa tasha̱a̱ unii nda.
Biituru na̱ ana tanaa na̱a̱ bwa aba tanaa na̱ nꞌrabi. Na aba hiika̱ki, aba nda̱i ki-Yeesu, be̱ e̱she̱ na̱ maza̱ki manyan manyan na̱ awyatu ree ana ne̱e̱ ma isaga nii be̱.
Na aba awyatu aba huri, aba ga̱a̱ Yeesu, Biituru bwa hin buu, <<Butu o̱to̱, uhuri gama na ga̱tu ne̱e̱ pina. XTa̱ta̱ nꞌdura̱ nꞌtaatu, bika̱ bindaabi, bika̱ binaa Muusa, bika̱ binaa Iliya.>> Bucici kunnu ama bwa yancin iri na bwaa cita̱ga̱.
Bwa ma cita̱ga̱ kunnu urara bwa guna̱ni wyan, rukwanyan ruba kota̱ni ana jwarigi buu.
Aba hange̱ ta̱ꞌnꞌga na̱ arara ma hyaan, <<Buna̱nna taa shi Baa buniimi bunaa ga̱n ka̱shi. Shiraga ma bwa.>>
Na mꞌba mazama mꞌba hwii, Yeesu be̱ bwe̱ be̱e̱ ka̱. Ana jwarigi buu aba nje̱ wau, aba bishici koo buyaan ha̱ni ya̱nu kwan, iri na aba nda̱i.
Yeesu kuda̱gahini baa // bunaa butu naa hira̱ bwa jwarigi
Maatiyu 17:14-18; Marukusu 9:14-27
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, Yeesu na̱ ana jwarigi buu ataatu aba cíin undu. Sa̱i kiigudu naa awyatu ma̱ be̱ wuce ki-Yeesu be̱ ne̱e̱.
Kuuyaan butu bwa wuce, bwa ta̱a̱ni nu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ kiigudu naa awyatu, bwa hin, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, iirupani, ha̱nga ambishiri na baa buna̱nna niimi, kuubwa ta ga̱n mashikani.
Butu naa hira̱ ta he̱e̱n bwa kota̱ni buu, buta shaana buu bimata̱a̱gi ta̱ꞌungwa kunta ꞌye̱n. Bwa butu naa hira̱ buta he̱e̱n kuuza̱ta̱ni buu, bushaani ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ ta̱naa jikita̱ga̱, unu nde̱e̱be̱ naa bana fucukwa. Bujaa gaa buu sa̱i kuugumahinai buu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Ga̱n taro̱pe̱ anaa jwarigi xaba̱ha̱ni bwa, ta bwa nga̱za̱ni wyan.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Ga̱hin awyatu na ha̱ni yana iza nꞌgata ta̱pana, iꞌmꞌbaa suhari nasu we̱. Ya̱ ha̱ni ga̱n naa na̱ ga̱hin ga̱n jaa rukuta̱? ꞌWaan aya̱bi paan.>>
Bwa baa ma hure, sa̱i butu naa hira̱ bwa sha̱pa̱cigi bwa, bwa ta̱a̱ baa na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n pwan ma zhizhiba. Ama Yeesu be̱ yinzha̱nkani bihwaanwun naa we̱, be̱ kuda̱gahini bwa baa. Naazhin be̱ sha̱pi bwa baa, be̱ pa̱ni ashin.
Hyo̱ ndaaba ana tanaa piree aba jikita̱ni wana ta̱kai nata̱ Hwe̱n.
Yeesu gura̱a̱ cita̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱ ta̱nde̱e̱be̱
Maatiyu 17:22-23; Marukusu 9:30-32
Na awyatu abaa jikita̱ga̱ na̱ iri na Yeesu be̱ ndagi, Yeesu be̱ hin ana jwarigi buu,
<<Shiraaga ma ki, ta-haasana ma iri na ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ ma. Anii pana Buyoo Butu kuꞌnꞌara na nꞌawyatu ana ribici be̱.>>
Ama ana jwarigi buu aba yancin mazama nama be̱ ne̱e̱ na̱ mꞌmaba, asooni wyan wana xata yansun. Aba hange̱ rukwanyan naru ta̱hantana buu iri na mꞌba mazama mꞌba hin.
Iyaa ta huri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱?
Maatiyu 18:1-5; Marukusu 9:33-37
Sa̱i aba ke̱ne̱ ta̱maga̱a̱ga̱nu ta̱hyan, iyaa ta huri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ kaba ne̱e̱.
Ama Yeesu be̱ e̱nshe̱n iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌsume̱ sundaaba. He̱e̱n be̱ shápi be̱e̱ binaa njeke, be̱ e̱she̱ do̱ko̱ nii be̱.
Be̱ hin wyan, <<Hyo̱ bunaa ra̱a̱ be̱e̱ bina̱nna nꞌara nꞌree na̱ wana ga̱mi, buꞌnꞌra̱a̱ ta ga̱mi. Hyo̱ bunaa nꞌra̱a̱ ga̱mi, bura̱a̱ ta Baaba nimi ana nꞌkáji. Na̱ wana ta̱hyan bunaa shi njeke njeke suga̱hin ne̱e̱, bwa taa shi butu naa huri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.>>
Bunaa za mayaan na̱ ga̱hin // buniinhin ta
Marukusu 9:38-40
Sa̱i Yoohana bwa hin Yeesu, <<Butu O̱to̱, ta̱ndái buyaan bunii ba̱ha̱na̱a̱ awyatu na hira̱ na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ ruzha̱a̱ rundaabi, ta ga̱tu yánshin bwa, wana ta̱hyan buza na̱ ga̱tu.>>
Ama Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Ta-yansan ma bwa! Hyo̱ bunaa za mayaan na̱ ga̱hin, buniinhin ta.>>
Asamaariya anaa yaan // bicice̱pe̱ aga̱a̱ Yeesu
Na ha̱ni nde̱e̱be̱ bwa goki na ta̱shapa Yeesu zhagu da̱da̱da̱, be̱ pa̱ yima̱a̱ na zhagu Hurushaliima.
Be̱ he̱e̱n be̱ ka̱ji atuma xanaa hura̱. Aba aba ja̱a̱, aba ta̱ni yaan bicice̱pe̱ naa Asamaariya wana hyan aꞌa̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni biko na̱ wuco nde̱e̱be̱.
Ama awyatu na be̱e̱ cice̱pe̱ aba ra̱a̱ci buu na̱ wana ta̱hyan ayan bihiin hura̱ ta Hurushaliima.
Na ana jwarigi buu, Yaakubu na̱ Yoohana, aba hange̱ kunnu, aba hin, <<Butu O̱to̱, bi-ribi xta̱hin ura uciin na̱ nꞌta̱ra uhuunha̱ni wyan hyo̱?>>
Ama Yeesu be̱ ke̱ce̱e̱ke̱, be̱ hin wyan hana.
Sa̱i aba kwashe̱ yaan bicice̱pe̱.
Ta̱guma nata̱ ne̱e̱ // nata̱ ta̱jwara̱ga Yeesu
Maatiyu 8:19-22
Aba nꞌta̱hani na̱ yo̱n, buyaan bubwa hin Yeesu, <<Nꞌna̱maa jwara̱ga hyo̱ paa gaa ja̱a̱.>>
Ama Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Suwa nasu aga suꞌmꞌbaa aꞌibwa na ta̱naa, nꞌno̱no̱ mꞌba mꞌbaa ta̱hurugo nata̱ rocu, ama Buyoo Butu bwaa za ina na hyuhyu ndaabwa.>>
Sa̱i be̱ hiin yaan, <<Jaa, u-shi bunaa nꞌjwarigi.>>
Ama bwa butu bwa hin, <<Butu O̱to̱, xnꞌgii kwan ina ma wuma̱ni baaba nimi.>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Hakata ana ꞌwa̱gi xawuma̱a̱ni ana ꞌwa̱gi, ama gaa, jaga, u-bisa̱gi awyatu mazama nama ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n.>>
Buyaan bubwa hin, <<Ee, Butu O̱to̱, nꞌna̱maa jwara̱ga, ama xnꞌja̱a̱ ma cipani awyatu na ina nimi kwan.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin bwa, <<Hyo̱ bunaa nii nda ta̱ga̱wa̱ nii ga̱wa̱ naa inaa, bwaa gwatagana ta̱baa, bujaa magiya̱ na̱ tuma ta̱naa nda kuta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n.>>

Yeesu ka̱ji awyatu // kuje ta̱nda̱ra̱ na ree
Na maya̱nu mꞌba hwii, Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwa ka̱shi ayaan kuje ta̱nda̱ra̱ na ree na jwarigi buu. Bwaa kadaga wyan awyatu ree ree xanaa hura̱na̱ bwa kukoya̱ ce̱pe̱ na̱ koya̱ pa̱ri paa bwa ribi ta̱jabaga.
Bwa bishi wyan ta̱hyan, <<Uguba̱ jwa o̱to̱, awyatu na tuma aba hwaani. Nda ma ro̱pe̱ ku-Butu O̱to̱ naa guba̱ xbukáji atumashini kubwa guba̱.
Hura̱ga̱ ma, ga̱n ta ga̱mii ka̱da̱gi ma tuma haki ka̱ra̱bi na̱ ame̱ na akura̱na̱.
Ta-shapa ma ruꞌwana naru ta̱zwagana yuwa koo ka̱fu. Ta-shapa ma yaan kandaga. Ta-maa ma azumanu ngiswan na̱ yo̱n.
<<Koya̱ ina ga̱hin ta̱ni, izumaani wyan, ihin, <Hunranhunran na gama na̱ nꞌta̱bure kawyatu na ina yana.>
Kuunaa ta̱bure ne̱e̱ kaun, rubara̱ka runiinhin naru ga̱hin rupani Hwe̱n runaa na̱a̱ bwa. Kuuza, ruukushitani ma.
Inaa na̱ bwa ina, ire̱, iswa̱ hyo̱ koya̱ iri na iri na abaa pa̱ni ma wana uzumaa butu naa tuma bura̱a̱ funa̱ ndaabwa. Iga̱a̱ ta̱naa hira̱gaga nꞌina.
<<Koya̱ ce̱pe̱ ga̱hin wuci abaa ra̱a̱ ma nꞌara nꞌree, ire̱ koya̱ iri na iri na abaa pa̱ni ma.
Ikuda̱gahinai ana ha̱ngagici sa̱ pita. Ihin wyan, <Ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ne̱e̱ do̱ko̱ na̱ ga̱hin.>
Ama koya̱ ce̱pe̱ ga̱hin ta̱ni abaa ra̱a̱ci ma, ijwara̱gagani kope na̱ bwa ce̱pe̱, inaa hyaan,
<Hyo̱ na putu na a̱npin mꞌbuna nꞌnda̱a̱tu ta̱a̱bukuta̱ga̱ni ma, tabisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan Hwe̱n ya̱a̱cigi ara na̱ ga̱hin. Ama yansun ma ta̱hyan ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ne̱e̱ do̱ko̱.>
Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, uhwe̱n na ta̱suuga̱ anii hura̱ ta̱pa ce̱pe̱ ya̱nu ngwan kaba tandaaka awyatu na So̱do̱m.
Ace̱pe̱ na ga̱a̱ ta̱pana pinsan baa
Maatiyu 11:20-24
<<Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma, ga̱hin awyatu na Koraasi! Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma, ga̱hin awyatu na Batasaida! Ri na rukwanyan na ga̱n ndagi wunhin, ibe̱ shi, be̱ ta ga̱n ndagi wuun na̱ Taaya na̱ Sidon, kahoo pana pinsan baa hasaa. Kata̱a̱ga̱ni ta̱wuzuwuzu, kahunraani ana mazooga̱na̱ nꞌto̱n na̱ hyuhyu, na hyan abisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan apa̱ni pinsan baa.
Ama uhwe̱n na ta̱suuga̱, anii hura̱ ta̱ndaaka awyatu na Taaya na̱ Sidon kuri na̱ ga̱hin na ga̱a̱ ta̱gaa pinsan.
Ga̱hin maa, awyatu na Kapanahu, inda̱i ta̱hyan ija̱a̱ hura̱ koo buya̱ ta̱raa ku-Hwe̱n na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱? Too, uja̱a̱ci hura̱. Uja̱maa bwé̱e̱ ma kunrin, kupa̱ri naka awyatu na ꞌwa̱gi.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin ana jwarigi buu, <<Buna buu shiragi ma, buꞌnꞌshiragi ta ga̱mi. Buna buu ga̱a̱ ma, buꞌnꞌga̱a̱ ta ga̱mi. Bunaa nꞌga̱a̱ ga̱mi, buga̱a̱ ta bwaa naa nꞌkáji.>>
Kuswa na aba kuje ta̱nda̱ra̱ na ree
Na kuje ta̱nda̱ra̱ na ree aba kúshe̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱da̱ri, aba hin, <<Butu O̱to̱, hyo̱ na awyatu na hira̱ ana we̱ maa ata ta̱pa̱ni suhyu sundaaba na ga̱tu nje̱ mazama na̱ nꞌruzha̱a̱ rundaabi.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Nꞌnda̱i Bupira̱ kíne̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, haku ta̱manyan manyan nata̱ ta̱.
Shiraga ma! Nꞌhoo maa pana ma ta̱kai na ta̱hyan ifo̱nje̱ suhwaa, na̱ nꞌsuna, na̱ nꞌta̱swa hyuhyu, na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ butu bunaa buu ribici ma. Za iri na we̱ na na̱maa ta ma.
Hyo̱ na̱ kunnu, ta-ha̱nga ma gama wana ta̱hyan awyatu na hira̱ na we̱ ataa pa̱ni ma suhyu sundaaba. Nda ma ta̱ga̱da̱ri wana ta̱hyan ata̱ ruzha̱a̱ runiinhin na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.>>
Yeesu ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ na tande̱
Maatiyu 11:25-27; 13:16-17
Na̱ ha̱ni ya̱nu, na Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ shaani Yeesu be̱ ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ na tande̱, Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Ada, Butu O̱to̱ naa hya̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, iigooji wana ta̱hyan bi-soo iri na̱nna kawyatu na be̱te̱re̱ge̱ na̱ mꞌmahunre̱n, gaa bisa̱a̱ wuun kana be̱te̱re̱ge̱ce̱ haku mꞌmwaan. Ada, kunta ta gaa huri ta̱ruba̱ unje̱.
<<Ada nimi mꞌpa̱ni hyo̱ iri. Bwa za naa yan, koo iyaa ta Buyoo bubwa shi, kaba Shin. Bwa za naa yan, koo iyaa ta Ada aba shi, kuubwaa Yoo na̱a̱ naa Buyoo bubwa ribi xbuyansun.>>
Yeesu be̱ ke̱ce̱e̱ke̱ kana jwarigi buu, be̱ bishi wyan na̱ nꞌta̱swee, <<Ishi awyatu na Hwe̱n bwa ndaaki rubara̱ka wana inda̱i iri na̱nna nꞌsuyishe suniinhin.
Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, awyatu na ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama na̱ nꞌgwama nꞌhwarapi ataruba̱ ta̱ndaya iri na ga̱hin nda̱i, aba nda̱ci wuun. Ataruba̱ ta̱ha̱nga iri na ga̱hin hange̱, aba hange̱ce̱.>>
Busamaariya naa bina̱
Biyaan biwya̱ra̱mi naa Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n bwa tapana Muusa be̱ hin kaki xbima̱a̱nwya̱ni Yeesu. Be̱ hin, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, iba̱ ga̱n nda ma da̱ba ta̱nda bina̱ na mahwa?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Mbata ta̱gi na̱ Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa? Kuu-nii cita̱ga̱ muu, na mꞌba hin?>>
Bwa butu bwa hin, <<Ahin, ruba̱ Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n ndaa nii gata ndaabi hyo̱, na̱ wuma ndaa hyo̱, na̱ kai ndaa hyo̱, na̱ ahari ndaa hyo̱. U-ribi butu naa nꞌharu ndaabi haruwa na gaa ribi hyuhyu ndaa.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin be̱, <<Bi-cici to̱n. Nda kunnu, bi-nii nda bina̱.>>
Ama bibe̱e̱ wya̱ra̱mi be̱ hiin bisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan be̱e̱ huri ta̱yansun. Be̱ hin Yeesu, <<Iyaa ta shi butu naa nꞌharu niimi?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Anje̱ yaan butu naa híike na̱ Hurushaliima. Bwaa hure cuun zhagu Yeriiko. Bwa ura̱ku na̱ azumba̱. Aba ta̱a̱cigi be̱ aꞌwana ndaabwa, aba ra̱a̱ be̱ hyo̱ ꞌwaa. Aba pa̱ be̱ dibi, aba cini be̱ ta̱kuna ge̱. Aba huri, aba ga̱a̱ be̱ pita.
<<Tapata, kuyaan upirisiti bwa kota̱ni bwa yo̱n. Na bwa nda̱i butu naa taa, bwa ka̱shi nii biin, bwa huri iri ndaabwa.
Kunnu mayaan Bulaawi+ :32 Bulaawi: Butu naa tuma na Ina na Hwe̱n na Ayaahudiya.na bwa wuce, bwa nda̱i bwa butu naa taa, bwa ka̱shi nii biin, bwa huri iri ndaabwa.
<<Tapata, buyaan Busamaariya bwa nꞌta̱hani, bwa jwara̱gani bwa yo̱n, bwa nda̱i butu taa. Ambishiri aba kota̱ni be̱ naa bwa butu.
Bwa ja̱a̱, bwa ha̱mba̱ra̱gi be̱ suguma na̱ mariga̱ na̱ ma̱ni nama ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nama njibi, naazhin bwa ka̱da̱a̱gi be̱. Bwa ca̱guda̱ni be̱ na̱ zhe̱nke̱n ndaabwa, bwa ꞌye̱e̱ be̱ ina paa aba ta naa ha̱nka̱nka̱na̱ na̱ yo̱n, bwaa nuwyan be̱.
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, bwa shápi ayuwa azurufa reeko, bwa pa̱ni butu naa ina. Bwa hin be̱, <Nꞌgwatagana butu na̱nna, iri na gaa kwane̱ ta̱baa ta̱niimi, kunkúshe̱, nꞌna̱maa ndupa wuun hyo̱.> >>
Na Yeesu be̱ hwii, be̱ ha̱nta̱ni be̱e̱ wya̱ra̱mi naa Nꞌgira̱nshin, be̱ hin buu, <<Ta̱ndaya ta̱ndaabi, awyatu ya̱nu taatu, iyaa ta shi butu naa nꞌharu kubutu naa azumba̱ aba taꞌya̱pi yo̱n?>>
Be̱e̱ wya̱ra̱mi naa Nꞌgira̱nshin be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Bunaa tanje̱ ambishiri ndaabwa.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin be̱, <<Gaa taa maa jaga nda kunnu.>>
Yeesu ja̱a̱ ku-Mara̱ta // na̱ Maariyamu
Na Yeesu be̱ ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hani na̱ awyatu nde̱e̱be̱ na jwarigi buu, aba wuci biyaan bicice̱pe̱ paakuu yaan buꞌa̱ naa aba ta nꞌgana Mara̱ta. Bwa ra̱a̱ buu na̱ ina ndaabwa.
Bibe̱ Mara̱ta be̱ mꞌbaa buyaan buya̱na̱ naa aba ta nꞌgana Maariyamu. Binaa tahunrana do̱ko̱ na̱ Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu, be̱ shiragi mazama mandaabwa.
Mara̱ta bibe̱, utuma na shami ta̱nda bwa sha̱pi aha̱nka̱ri nde̱e̱be̱. Be̱ ja̱a̱ paa Yeesu, be̱ hin buu, <<Butu O̱to̱, bi-nda̱ci ta̱hyan buya̱tu niimi buꞌnꞌga̱a̱ ga̱n ka̱ ga̱n nda tuma? Bisa̱ be̱ xbujaa buꞌnꞌguni.>>
Ama Butu O̱to̱ bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin buu, <<Ka̱i, Mara̱ta, Mara̱ta, aha̱nka̱ri ndaa ahiiki, gaa ma ma̱a̱ ta̱makaka na̱ iri hwarapi.
Bishi kuu-shii aha̱nka̱ri ndaa na̱ iri ka̱. Maariyamu, bika̱shi iri na huri bina̱, buza naa nii raa buu.>>

Ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ Yeesu // nata̱ ro̱pe̱ ta̱nda
Maatiyu 6:9-13; 7:7-11
Uyaan hwe̱n, Yeesu be̱e̱ nda ro̱pe̱ nꞌkayaan pa̱ri. Na be̱ hwii ro̱pe̱ ta̱nda, buyaan buka̱ kana jwarigi buu, bwa hin buu, <<Butu O̱to̱, ta̱ga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni haruwa na ro̱pe̱ ta̱nda, haku Yoohana bwa tabisa̱a̱ga̱ ana jwarigi bwa taa.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Kiihiin nda ro̱pe̱, ihin,
<< <Ada, xapa̱ ruzha̱a̱ rundaabi naru ne̱e̱ sabu hunrun.
Shaana ta̱gwama ta̱ndaabi ta̱wuce pina.
U-ta̱pa̱ koya̱ hwe̱n shami na rwaru.
Ta-ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ pinsan nda̱tu nii gata ndaabi,
haruwa na ga̱tu ha̱mba̱ga̱ncin
ana ta̱ndaaki pinsan.
Ta-ta̱ꞌiya paaku ta̱maanwyana.> >>
Be̱ gura̱a̱ hyan wyan, <<Ahin buyaan buꞌmꞌbaa bushika, bwa ja̱a̱ waabwa na̱ gita ꞌya̱piga̱su, bwa hin be̱, <Bushikaa niimi, nꞌwa̱a̱pi aburoodi taatu,
na̱ wana bushikaa niimi ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hani, ta bwa káshi wa̱ka̱mi, ta ga̱n za shami na ta̱pa be̱.>
<<Bushikaa ndaabwa naa bwa ja̱a̱ wyanzun na shami waabwa, bura̱ni na̱ dura̱, buhin, <Ta-naa ma nꞌsha̱a̱ ga̱mi. Pa̱ri kaguna̱ni, gita nje̱, ga̱n na̱ mꞌmwaan ta̱hoo taaga. Nꞌjaa ara mahiika̱ maa sháapi shami niina.>
Ama ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, koo buribici ta̱hiika̱, busháapi be̱ shami na̱ wana bushi bushikaa ndaabwa, ama na̱ wana bunii sha̱a̱ be̱ ji, bunii hiika̱, busháapi be̱ iri na bwa ribi na̱ wana bunii sha̱a̱ be̱.
<<Na̱ wana kunnu, ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, naa rupa ma ji, ana̱maa pana ma iri na ga̱hin rupani. Naa wyanzan ma ji, inii da̱ba. Naa gba̱a̱nta̱a̱na̱ ma ji, ana̱maa guna̱a̱nwya̱n dubo.
Na̱ wana koo buya̱ naa rupani, anii pana be̱. Koo buya̱ naa wya̱nzhin, bunii da̱ba. Koo buya̱ naa gba̱a̱nta̱ni anii guna̱a̱nwya̱n be̱ adubo.
<<Iyaa ta suga̱hin ne̱e̱ awyatu na mꞌmwaan, kuuyoo burupani be̱ bijooshiipa, bupa̱ni buu hwaa na wuma?
Koo kuurupani be̱ ange̱n, bupa̱ni be̱ ana? Majaa nda!
Kuga̱hin awyatu na shi na we̱, iyan iri na gama na ga̱hin nii pana mꞌmwaan nꞌniinhin, kuu-Shiinhin naa ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ bunaa nii pana Bihwaanwun ndaabwa kana rupani bwa?>>
Yeesu na̱ Shatan
Maatiyu 12:22-30; Marukusu 3:20-27
Yaan hwe̱n, Yeesu be̱e̱ pa butu naa hira̱ naa we̱ bunaa ta yansan mazama ta̱cita̱ sumo̱ kuuyaan butu. Na butu naa hira̱ bwa ba̱ni, butu bwaa cita̱ga̱ mazama, bigudu naa awyatu be̱ jikita̱ni.
Awyatu ka̱ abaa hyaan, <<Binii paga awyatu na hira̱ sumo̱ na̱ wana Baꞌala̱zabu+ :15 Baꞌala̱zabu: Baꞌala̱zabu ta shi ruyaan ruzha̱a̱ naru Shatan.bugwama naa awyatu na hira̱ taa pa̱ni buu ta̱kai.>>
Awyatu ka̱ aba ribi xama̱a̱nwya̱ni buu. Aba kaki buu ji xbinje̱ iri na ta̱jikita̱na̱, wana hyan ayansun ta̱hyan Hwe̱n ne̱e̱ nii be̱.
Yeesu be̱ e̱nshe̱n nꞌgata nꞌndaaba, be̱ hin, <<Koya̱ ta̱gwama nata̱ mahoosa̱ga̱gi ta̱nii gataaga. Ina na mahooshi maree, inii huza̱.
Inii hyaan ga̱n mꞌbaa ta̱kai nata̱ Baꞌala̱zabu bugwama naa awyatu na hira̱. Ama ku-Shatan nii nda gagu na̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa na hyan buꞌmꞌpa̱ni ta̱kai nata̱ hyan ma pa awyatu ndaabwa na hira̱ sumo̱, ta̱gwama ta̱ndaabwa ta̱ba jaa isa.
Ama kuga̱n nii paga awyatu na hira̱ sumo̱ na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ bugwama naa awyatu na hira̱, too, awyatu ninhin naa jwarigi ma haan? Aba taamaa anii paga awyatu na hira̱ sumo̱, nꞌta̱kai nata̱ iyaa abaa nda? Aba maa ana̱maa ndaaka ma suuga̱ na̱ iri na ga̱hin cici.
Kushi na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ta ga̱n paga awyatu na hira̱ sumo̱, too, ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱wuce wunhin.
<<Kubutu naa kai+ :21 Kubutu naa kai: Butu naa kai ta shi haku Shatan.bunje̱ shiri ki na̱ ꞌwaa na gagu, buha̱mba ina ndaabwa, ꞌwaa na ina ndaabwa nii naa kami.
Ama jaa kuuyaan bunaa huri be̱ kai, bwa ke̱ne̱ gagu na̱a̱ bwa, bura̱a̱ be̱ hyo̱ ꞌwaa na gagu na bwa tamashikani, buhoosa̱ga̱gi ꞌwaa na bwa ra̱a̱ kawyatu ndaabwa.
<<Koo buya̱ butu naa jaa nda huku na̱ ga̱mi, bunaa nꞌga̱a̱ buta bwa shi. Bunaa nꞌnguncin ta̱wuna̱a̱na̱, bunii gata ta.
<<Kiihwaanwun naa we̱ ba̱ni kubutu, bita naa riinshina̱ paaka za wyanfo̱n na̱ wana xbide̱be̱ kuta̱ha̱nka̱na̱. Kiide̱be̱ce̱, bihin, <Nꞌnii kushiika kubutu naa ga̱n tabáni waabwa.>
Kiikúshiike̱, be̱ wuta̱ni ina ha̱riki, ibe̱ ne̱e̱ sabu,
bikwashe̱e̱ke̱, bijaa na̱ nꞌyaan nꞌhwaanwun nꞌta̱nda̱ra̱ na nꞌhuri na nꞌyigo ta̱we̱, nꞌta̱ni kubutu yata mayaan. Haruwa na butu bwaa naa uhuri na yigo ta̱we̱.>>
Yeesu ma huwa̱ ta̱cita̱ga̱ ri ya̱nu, buyaan buꞌa̱ bwa báni na̱ awyantancin naa gudu, bwa ta̱a̱ni nu, <<Hwe̱n ndaaki buꞌa̱ naa buu ma̱ncin rubara̱ka na̱ maya̱a̱suba̱ nama gaa swa̱!>>
Yeesu be̱ kushihinani bwaa a̱ nu, be̱ hin, <<Rubara̱ka ruhuri ta̱naa kana hange̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n aba jwarigi muu.>>
Awyatu ribi ta̱ndaya // ri na hyan ajikita̱ni
Maatiyu 12:38-42
Na bigudu be̱e̱ duwa̱ni kuta̱wuce, Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Na̱nna ta shii ke̱nye̱n naa awyatu na niina na we̱. Aꞌnꞌha̱nta̱ni xandaaki wyan iri na ta̱bisa̱a̱, iyaan iri na ta̱bisa̱a̱ be̱ za na ga̱n nii bisa̱a̱ wyan, kina Yunuusa.
Haruwa na Yunuusa bwa tasha iri na ta̱bisa̱a̱ kawyatu na Nineba ta̱hyan Hwe̱n ta káji be̱, kunta ta ga̱n Buyoo Butu ga̱n nii sha nii ke̱nye̱n naa awyatu na niina ta̱hyan Hwe̱n ta nꞌkáji.
Hwe̱n na ta̱suuga̱, Bisorooniya naa Sheeba nii hiika̱ biꞌisa, bibishi awyatu naa ke̱nye̱n yana ta̱hyan anje̱ce̱ sa̱, na̱ wana bitabáni ce̱nye̱n nata̱ me̱mi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, be̱ shiragi mazama nama maca̱ma̱nta̱n nama ta̱yansun nata̱ Bugwama Suleemaanu. Niina butu naa huri Suleemaanu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ bwa na na̱ aba.
Hwe̱n na ta̱suuga̱, awyatu na Nineba anii báni kunnu taa, aꞌisaga huku na̱ awyatu naa ke̱nye̱n yana, abishi wyan anje̱ce̱ sa̱, na̱ wana aba pa̱ni pinsan baa wana ta̱bisa̱ga̱ nata̱ Yunuusa be̱ tabisa̱ wyan. Niina, butu naa huri Yunuusa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ bwa na na̱ aba.
Pitila na ta̱ꞌwaba
Maatiyu 5:15; 6:22-23
<<Buza naa nii pantaan pitila busoo wuun koo buꞌubi wuun bitumunsun. Uhuri gama ashii wuun nii ꞌwa̱ruꞌwa̱ru na̱ wana kwayaa na nii tá̱ni bunda̱i pa̱ri gwaan.
Ayishe ndaa ta shi pitila na ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabi. Kayishe ndaa ne̱e̱ gumunu, hyo̱ ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabi ta̱ba ne̱e̱ gwaan. Ama kayishe ndaa za gumunu, hyo̱ ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabi ta̱shi ta̱yincincin.
Magwatani, u-nda̱i, koo ta̱gwaan nata̱ gaa mꞌbaa ta̱shi ta̱yincincin na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabi.
Kuta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabi hyo̱ ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa ta̱gwaan, ta̱ba za pa̱ri naka mꞌbaa ta̱yincincin, ta̱gwaan ta̱ta gaa shi haruwa na ta̱gwaan nata̱ pitila ta̱ba ta tara̱kana pa̱ri.>>
Yeesu ba̱nra̱nyin ashe̱re̱ // na Afaraasiya na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi // nami Nꞌgira̱nshin
Maatiyu 23:1-36; Marukusu 12:38-40
Na Yeesu be̱ hwii mazama maya̱nu ta̱cita̱ga̱ sabu, buyaan Bufaraasiya bwa nꞌgani buu shami ta̱re̱ na̱ ina ndaabwa. Be̱ bicigi pa̱ri, be̱ hunrani paaki shami ta̱re̱.
Bufaraasiya bwa nda̱i Yeesu shikicici ara na be̱ hiin re̱ shami kuꞌnꞌgira̱nshin ndaaba mꞌba hin, bwa jikita̱ni.
Nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu, ku-Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwa hin be̱, <<Ga̱hin Afaraasiya ita ha̱mbara abaa na nꞌjogo na̱ nꞌgwaga ki, ama iga̱a̱ ame̱ ninhin na̱ nꞌta̱shiri na̱ mꞌmaꞌwe̱n.
Nꞌguzha̱ni, shici Hwe̱n ta nje̱ hyo̱ ame̱ na̱ abaa na mꞌba?
Pana ma aꞌwa̱ta̱gi shami na ne̱e̱ nii gwaga niinhin, na hyan ga̱hin jaa mꞌbaa ta̱shiri na̱ ame̱ ninhin mahwa.
<<Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma ga̱hin Afaraasiya, ita he̱e̱n ipa̱ni Hwe̱n ta̱taa ta̱ka̱ kuta̱taa ta̱ꞌupwa nata̱ mꞌmbwaga na nꞌga̱hin mꞌbaa, ama ga̱hin mata̱ma̱nriincin na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌyapa mazama ki na̱ nꞌta̱ruba̱ nata̱ Hwe̱n. Naa nda ma wuun hyo̱, shii iga̱a̱ ika̱.>>
<<Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma ga̱hin Afaraasiya, ihuri ta̱ruba̱ pa̱ri naka hura̱gi gama ta̱hunrana paaka aka̱ta̱ku, ga̱hin ribi azumanu na maca̱ma̱nta̱n kukasuwa.
<<Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma, ishi awyatu na sume̱ nasu we̱ haku suꞌuya̱ nasu kinda̱gi aba dibi suun she̱nre̱n, suba mama̱a̱ nge̱n na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n, awyatu abaa fundaga suun na aba yancin.>>
Biyaan biwya̱ra̱mi naa Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n bwa tapana Muusa be̱ hin, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, kuu-nii hyaan kunnu, bi-nii ta̱cwaagaga nu.>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma ga̱hin nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin, na̱ wana ita para ꞌwaa na ca̱ma̱ncin, ita̱ndani ayaan na aba jaa ara, ama ga̱hin jaa cikaa koo bimbwa, ita̱ndani wuun butu.
<<Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma, ida̱ba̱a̱ga̱ni awyatu na ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama na yigo suꞌuya̱ sabu, ana adaadoo ninhin aba takunaa.
Ga̱hin na̱ nꞌsuhyu suniinhin, ira̱ni ta̱hyan iri na adaadoo ninhin aba tanda ine̱e̱ to̱n, na aba takunaa awyatu na ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, na ga̱hin da̱ba̱a̱ga̱ni wyan suꞌuya̱.
Ta shani Hwe̱n ta̱yansun ta̱ndaabwa ta̱ba hin, <Ga̱n nii iyaaga wyan awyatu na nii naa ma nꞌcita̱a̱ga̱ mazama na̱ atuma na ga̱n zwa̱ri, anii kunaa aka̱, abaa pa aka̱ ngwan, andaaki aka̱ iri na zumaancin.>
Na̱ wana kunnu, ga̱hin awyatu na niina, ana̱maa pa ma ta̱guma na̱ wana kunai kunai na ga̱hin nje̱ na awyatu na ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ta na aba nje̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana.
Ta mahiin nama tawyashika nama Habiila, hara̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱ nata̱ Zakaariya, bunaa aba takuna na wyantancin na bizhe̱nke̱n naa bikico̱ ta̱huunha̱na̱ na̱ udura̱ na bure na Ina na Hwe̱n. Kunnunu ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, anii pa awyatu na niina ta̱guma na̱ wana hyo̱ ndaaba.
<<Ija̱a̱ swa ta̱guma ga̱hin nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin, iha̱mba̱gi iri na ta̱guna̱a̱ ina na ta̱yansun, ama ga̱hin ta̱ncin, ga̱hin ga̱a̱ci ayaan ana ribi tunu xata̱ni.>>
Na Yeesu be̱ ga̱a̱ pa̱ri kaba, Afaraasiya na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin aba gware̱ sume̱ nii be̱, ma kiba buu, ma hantaana buu mazama mahwarapi,
ma wyanzan xbicici iri na za to̱n, azha̱a̱ buu na̱ nꞌta̱ruma.

Yeesu kooci awyatu // na̱ nꞌta̱shici agura̱ na awyatu
Maatiyu 10:26-27
Ha̱ni na awyatu dubu hwarapi aba mawuna̱ni ma mafundata. Na yigo, Yeesu be̱ hin ana jwarigi buu, <<Mahooshi ma na yisiti na Afaraasiya, bine̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan ashi agura̱ na awyatu.
Za iri na guna̱ni na jaa guna̱a̱, ibe̱ za iri na ne̱e̱ ta̱swee na aba jaa yansun.
Wana kunnu, hyo̱ iri na ga̱hin cici ta̱swee, anii ha̱nga wuun na̱ sa̱ra̱ri. Koo iri na ga̱hin cici ta̱swee na̱ ame̱ na dura̱, anii katana sa̱ku na dura̱ acici wuun.
Bunaa abaa wasa
:28-31
<<Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma ta̱shika ta̱niimi, ta-wasa ma bunaa nii kuna ta̱ꞌwaba ama bwa jaa gura̱a̱ ara ta̱nda yaanyini, bwa hwii tuun ta̱kuna.
Bunaa hyan ihange̱ rukwanyan rundaabwa, bwa taa shi Hwe̱n, bunaa ta̱hyan kuuhwii ta̱kuna ta̱ꞌwaba, buꞌmꞌbaa ta̱kai nata̱ hyan buuzwa̱ga̱ni kura na za ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱. Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, bwa taa shi naa ta̱wasa.
<<Shii nꞌsweeswee nꞌta na nꞌnjeke nꞌta aba ta sa̱a̱nha̱na̱ aniinii ree? Hyo̱ na̱ kunnu Uhwe̱n ha̱a̱sa̱ncin koo bika̱ na mꞌba.
Kai! Hyo̱ maa ta̱hinje nata̱ hyuhyu ninhin ubwa rubaagi. Wana kunnu, ta-ha̱nga ma rukwanyan. Ihuri nꞌsweeswee bina̱ ku-Hwe̱n mahwa.
Ta̱cita̱ ta̱ruba̱ Yeesu // kaꞌuba̱ na awyatu
Maatiyu 10:32-33; 12:32; 10:19-20
<<Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, hyo̱ bunaa cici ta̱hyan buꞌnꞌribi na̱ aꞌuba̱ na awyatu, ga̱n Buyoo Butu ja̱a̱ cita̱ ta̱hyan ga̱n ribi be̱ taa na̱ aꞌuba̱ na atuma na Hwe̱n.
Bunaa hin bwaa nꞌyancin na̱ aꞌuba̱ na awyatu, nꞌja̱a̱ci yansun be̱ taa na̱ uba̱ na atuma na Hwe̱n.
Hyo̱ bunaa cici yaan iri na we̱ kuga̱n Buyoo Butu Hwe̱n jaa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ bwa pinsan ndaabwa. Ama bunaa cici yaan iri na hwashe̱ kii-Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n, Hwe̱n nii ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ bwa pinsan nii gata ndaabwa.
<<Kaaꞌíye̱ ma na hyan aama̱a̱nwya̱a̱ni ma kuka̱ta̱ku na̱ aꞌuba̱ na awyatu na ta̱gwama na̱ awyatu na ta̱suuga̱, xutaa ta ma bigata buga̱ na̱ iri na hyan icici koo imaba̱ha̱ni,
na̱ wana ta̱hyan na̱ bwa ha̱ni, Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n na̱maa ga̱gaagana ma iri na hyan icici.>>
Mazama nama iguzha̱ni // na mꞌbaa iri ma̱
Buyaan butu na̱ ame̱ naa bigudu naa awyatu bwa hin Yeesu, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, bisa̱ buya̱tu xbuhooshi na̱ ga̱n iri na baaba nda̱tu aba ta̱ga̱a̱gi.>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Bushikaa niimi, iyaa mꞌpa̱ni ta̱sha butu naa ta̱suuga̱, koo bunaa hooso, gaa na̱ ayami nata̱ iri na baaba ninhin abaa ga̱a̱gi ma?>>
Be̱ re̱ iyeebe ma bisa̱ga̱ wyan hyo̱ ndaaba, <<Mahooshi ma na̱ nꞌta̱koya̱ ta̱ruba̱ nata̱ iri ma̱. Wana ta̱hyan shii iri ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa ma̱, ta shi bushi butu, koo hamba gaa mꞌbaa.>>
Sa̱i be̱ bishi wyan mana̱nna mazama nꞌta̱kun, <<Atanda yaan butu naa taꞌmꞌbaa iri ma̱, bunaa icima ndaabwa be̱ tanda shami ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Bwa pa̱shi ta̱maga̱gaaga ta̱hyan, <Nꞌza paaku ta̱sha̱a̱ga̱ shami. Mbata ga̱n nda?>
<<Bwa mahin, <Nꞌyan iri na ga̱n nda. Nꞌnii huza̱a̱ga̱ hyo̱ nꞌndukwa niimi ma maa na nꞌhura̱gi o̱to̱ na nꞌfo paa ga̱n sha̱a̱ hyo̱ ꞌwaa nimi na cima na̱ yaan ꞌwaa nimi.
Ma hyan hyuhyu nimi, <<Kai! Mꞌmꞌbaa shami na̱ yaan ꞌwaa o̱to̱ na ga̱n naa re̱ nꞌyo̱ nꞌhwarapi. Ha̱nka̱na̱, u-naa re̱, u-naa swa, u-hange̱ masuunran.>> >
<<Ama Uhwe̱n bwa hin be̱, <Gaa guzha̱ni, ba̱re yana na̱ gita aribi hyuhyu ndaa ta̱shapa. Too, iꞌwaa na gaa wuna̱ni inii sha na iyaa?> >>
Yeesu be̱ wanyin mꞌba mazama ta̱hyan, <<Kunta mꞌba ja̱a̱ sha kubutu naa mawuna̱a̱nyin ꞌwaa na sa̱ra̱ri yana, bwa za ꞌwaa na bwa mawuna̱a̱nyin ku-Hwe̱n.>>
Ta-makaka ma na̱ yaanyini
Maatiyu 6:25-34
Yeesu be̱ hin ana jwarigi buu, <<Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, na̱ wana kunnu ta-makaka ma na̱ hyuhyu ninhin na̱ wana shami na ga̱hin nii naa re̱, koo aꞌwana na ga̱hin nii naa taagana na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwaba ta̱niinhin.
Na̱ wana ta̱hyan, butu huri shami, ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ba huri ꞌwana.
Gwatana ma ano̱no̱. Iyan! Aꞌa̱cii nda ta̱bira, aba a̱cii nda guba̱, aba za nꞌndukwa koo adura̱ na ta̱sha̱a̱ga̱ shami. Hyo̱, Hwe̱n ta ta naa biga wyan. Iyan! Ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ga̱hin huri ano̱no̱ bina̱.
Iyaa ta suga̱hin ne̱e̱ pina na ga̱hin makaki, bunii ara ta̱duwa̱na̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa koo ge̱ nꞌhwe̱n na nꞌta̱ꞌwa̱?
Kiijaa ara ta̱nda iri ya̱nu ge̱, too, iba̱ shani ga̱hin makaki na̱ ya̱nu iri?
<<Gwatana ma kuta̱sumu ta̱ba ta mawaana na̱ ahira̱. Ta̱ba a̱cii nda tuma, ta̱ba a̱cii mandaaka ꞌwana na ta̱taana. Ama nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma koo bugwama Suleemaanu hyo̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ta̱ndaabwa, buta nda ruzhanna rundaabwa ruba jaa wuta̱ gama na ta̱sumu.
Too, ku-Hwe̱n nii ara ta̱ndaaka awyamu na aga kunnu, awyamu na ta hyaan kane̱e̱ ba̱re na̱ bunwan ahuni ra, kuga̱hin? Ka̱i ma, ipa̱ni nꞌgata kuge̱ ku-Hwe̱n.
Ta-makaka ma na̱ wyanzun kuna̱ iri na ga̱hiin re̱, koo ga̱hiin swa, ta-makaka ma maa mahwa.
Wana ta̱hyan, ana yancin Hwe̱n maa ata naa na̱ wyanzun na iri ya̱nu hyo̱, kuga̱hin naazhin na Bushiinhin Hwe̱n hoo yansun iribi ri ya̱nu hyo̱.
Kiipa̱ni ma suhyu suniinhin na̱ nꞌgata nꞌniinhin kiri na ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n, una̱maa pana ma hyo̱ ibe̱ iri ya̱nu.
Ta̱wuna̱na̱ iri na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱
Maatiyu 6:19-21
<<Ta-ha̱nga ma rukwanyan, ga̱hin bigudu niimi naa njeke, na̱ wana ta̱hyan Bushiinhin Hwe̱n buhoo maa zwara ma, ija̱a̱ ta̱na̱, ihunraana kuta̱gwama ta̱ndaabwa.
Sa̱a̱nha̱na̱a̱ ma iri na ga̱hin mꞌbaa, ipa̱ga̱ni aꞌwa̱ta̱gi aba yuwa, imasha̱a̱gi iri na za kuta̱huwo, iri na za kuta̱ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ mahwa da̱da̱da̱ paa buzumba̱ bwa jaa shapa wuun na̱ paa are̱e̱ aba jaa re̱.
Na̱ wana ta̱hyan, paa iri ndaa na bina̱ be̱ ne̱e̱, kabata bigata ndaabi be̱e̱ naa.
Agyama na ne̱e̱ na̱ iyo̱
<<Naa ma na̱ shiri, ipa̱nta̱a̱nyin ira ninhin inaa huna̱ ji.
Naa ma haka gyama ana hambe̱ butu naa ina xbugiye kubuki na ta̱wya̱ri na̱ gita. Kuugiye, bwa gba̱a̱nta̱ni dubo, agunii kunrun.
Unii shana andaaki aba agyama iri na ta̱ga̱da̱ri, jaa butu naa ina bwa wuce, bwa nda̱i wyan ga̱ri. Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, bunii taaciga da̱bi ndaabwa na o̱to̱ wana xbuhoosa̱ni wyan shami, buhin wyan, <Hunraana ma, ire̱gi shami>, buꞌíyaagi koo buya̱ shami ndaabwa.
Andaaki agyama iri na ta̱ga̱da̱ri, jaa kubutu naa ina ndaaba bwa kúshe̱ na̱ gita ꞌya̱piga̱su koo na̱ kasu, buwuta̱ni wyan ga̱ri na̱ iyo̱.
<<Yansun ma ta̱hyan, kubutu naa ina yan ha̱ni na buzumba̱ bwaa ta̱na̱ ina ndaabwa, bujaa hakata bwa xbuta̱ni ina ndaabwa.
Too, naa ma na̱ shiri, Buyoo Butu ja̱a̱ jaa na̱ ha̱ni na ga̱hin shiici bunii jaa.>>
Bugyama naa bina̱ // koo bunaa za bina̱
Maatiyu 24:45-51
Biituru bwa hin, <<Butu O̱to̱, maya̱nu mazama mashi kumanda̱a̱tu koo mashi nama koo buya̱?>>
Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwa ra̱ni bwa, bwa hin, <<Iyaa nu shi bugyama ya̱nu naa bina̱ naa jwarigi ki nꞌta̱yansun kunnu? Bwa taa shi bunaa butu naa ina ndaabwa bwa shii bwa xbugwataga ina ndaabwa, bunaa paga ya̱na̱ba ndaabwa gyama shami na̱ ha̱ni na ta̱to̱n.
Bugyama naa rubara̱ka ta, jaa butu naa ina bwa wuce, bwa wuta̱ni bwa ma nda tuma ndaabwa.
Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, bunii pana bwaa gyama xbuha̱mbana be̱ ꞌwaa ndaabwa hyo̱.
Ama kuubwaa gyama nda̱i ta̱hyan, <Butu naa ina nimi giici na̱ ha̱ni,> bwa ke̱ne̱ ta̱da̱ba̱ga̱ aya̱na̱ba gyama na a̱ na̱ ana wya̱ri, bwa ke̱ne̱ ta̱re̱ ma nda swagi-swagi hara̱ ta̱naa nda be̱,
jaa butu naa ina ndaabwa bwa kúshe̱ na̱ ha̱ni na bwaa gyama bwa yancin. Butu naa ina nii pa be̱ dibi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, bupa̱ be̱ sumo̱, buyibaku be̱ na̱ ana tibici mazama.
<<Hyo̱ bugyama naa yan iri na butu naa ina ndaabwa bwa ribi xbunje̱ wuun, bwa nje̱ce̱ shiri na ta̱nda, koo bwa gura̱a̱ci nda iri na aba ribi xbunje̱, anii pa be̱ dibi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Ama hyo̱ bugyama naa yancin iri na butu naa ina ndaabwa bwa ribi xbunje̱, bwa gura̱a̱ nda iri na nii shana adibi be̱, anii da̱ba̱ be̱ washi. Hyo̱ bunaa aba pa̱ni iri o̱to̱, iri o̱to̱ aba nii ruba̱ waabwa. Bunaa aba hura̱gi ta̱pana iri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, iri na hura̱gi o̱to̱ abaa ruba̱ waabwa.
Yeesu ꞌwaan ta̱mahoosa̱ga̱ga̱
Maatiyu 10:34-36
<<Ura ta ga̱n ꞌwaan ma pa na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana. Ta̱ruba̱ ta̱niimi kahoo shana wuun.
Mꞌmꞌbaa baba̱tiisa̱ma na shi ga̱ga̱ga̱ ma nda, ga̱n makaki ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ kunhoo nda wuun.
Ine̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan uhunranhunran na bure ta ga̱n íye̱ na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana? Aaꞌa, shii hunranhunran na bure, ama ta̱mahoosa̱ga̱ga̱.
Niina, nii ke̱nye̱n naa wuci awyatu ta ana ne̱e̱ na̱ ina ka̱, anii mahoosa̱ maree, aba jaa maꞌunso̱n. Ataatu aba jaa maꞌunso̱n na̱ aree, aree aba jaa maꞌunso̱n na̱ ataatu.
Ashin na̱ baa buwya̱ri aba jaa maꞌunso̱n. Aya̱na̱ na̱ baa bunaa a̱ aba jaa maꞌunso̱n. Aꞌuugo na̱ a̱yo yoo aba jaa maꞌunso̱n.>>
Ta̱ꞌinsan ha̱ni
Maatiyu 16:2-3
Yeesu be̱ hin awyatu, <<Ita he̱e̱n kiinda̱i ururo shée, ihin, <Ashira̱ nii kina,> ake̱ne̱ kumahanda.
Kiinda̱i mꞌpyara nii hura̱ zuba, ihin, <Anii nda mamboo,> manje̱ kumahanda.
Awyatu na za mahanda, iꞌa̱ri ta̱ꞌinsan kuꞌnꞌce̱nye̱n na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱ba ne̱e̱, ama ga̱hin a̱rici ta̱ꞌinsan kuꞌmꞌpirwa na̱ uha̱ni yana ubwa ne̱e̱.
Maga̱ga̱a̱gi ma na̱ butu // na buuꞌye̱e̱ kuta̱suuga̱
Maatiyu 5:25-26
<<Imbata shani ga̱hin na̱ nꞌsuhyu suniinhin ga̱hin jaa ara ta̱nda suuga̱ to̱n?
Kuuyaan buuꞌye̱e̱ kuta̱suuga̱, u-nje̱ haruwa na hyan imaga̱ga̱a̱gi ta ga̱hin na̱ yo̱n. Kuu-ga̱a̱, buuꞌye̱e̱ kubutu naa ta̱suuga̱. Butu naa ta̱suuga̱ buuꞌye̱e̱ kubutu naa ta ha̱mba zhaaro. Butu naa ta ha̱mba zhaaro buuzwa̱ga̱ni na̱ zhaaro.
Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, bi-jaa bana nii be̱e̱ ko, sa̱i kuu-pa̱ga̱ni hyo̱ ta̱re̱ga ta̱ndaabi, za iri na nii bwa.>>

Ta̱pana pinsan baa koo ta̱ꞌwa̱
Nii ke̱nye̱n yeree, ayaan awyatu na tanaa kaun aba bishi Yeesu mazama nama Bilaatu bwa takunaa ayaan awyatu na Gaalili na̱ ha̱ni na abaa shinraanwyan Hwe̱n bikico̱.
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Ishii ta̱hyan, na̱ wana akunai awyatu na Gaalili yata, ta shi ahuri koo buya̱a̱ Gaalili pinsan ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa?
Aaꞌa, mahwa ahurici. Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, kiipa̱ncin pinsan baa, ga̱hin huwa̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱ kunta.
Koo inda̱i ta̱hyan, awyatu upwa na ta̱ndatu ana ta̱ma nata̱ za̱ka̱ ta̱ba tazha̱ntana na̱ Saluwa, ahuri koo buya̱ pinsan ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa na̱ Hurushaliima?
Too, shii nuunu. Kiipa̱ncin pinsan baa, ga̱hin huwa̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱ kunta.>>
Mazama nama waanwan // na za ta̱ꞌwa̱ri
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ bishi wyan mayaan mazama, be̱ hin, <<Ana ndaa yaan butu, bwa mꞌbaa ꞌwe̱e̱ na waanwan na̱ cima ndaabwa na ꞌwe̱e̱ na iinabi. Bwa ja̱a̱ xbugwa̱shi ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ bwa waanwan bwa de̱be̱ce̱ koo ta̱ka̱.
Bwa hin butu naa ne̱e̱ na̱ bwa cima, <Bi-nda̱i, nꞌyo̱ nꞌtaatu nꞌta ga̱n jábagi na hyan ma gwasa ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ ꞌwe̱e̱ na̱nna, ga̱n jaa da̱ba. Taa wuun! Mbata shani bwa cita̱ni biko ꞌye̱n?>
<<Ama butu naa ne̱e̱ na̱ bwa cima bwa hin, <Butu o̱to̱ niimi, gaa wuun baan. XNꞌwuna̱a̱nyin wuun ce̱nye̱n ma zooga̱ga̱ wuun ta̱ki.
Kunje̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱ri yo̱ na wuci, u-ga̱a̱ wuun, kunje̱ce̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱ri, u-jaa ta̱a̱ wuun.> >>
Yeesu kuda̱gahini buꞌa̱ // naa suguma suba nguncin
Na̱ yaan hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya, Yeesu be̱e̱ ga̱gaagana wyan na̱ yaan ka̱ta̱ku ndaaba.
Buyaan buꞌa̱ bunaa butu naa hira̱ naa we̱ bwa shaani suguma suba swa̱ be̱, nꞌyo̱ nꞌupwa na̱ nꞌta̱ndatu. Bwa nguncin, bwa a̱rici ta̱makambiga.
Na Yeesu be̱ nda̱i bwa, be̱ nꞌgani bwa na̱ aꞌuba̱ nde̱e̱be̱, be̱ hin, <<Buꞌa̱, Uhwe̱n ya̱a̱cigi suguma sundaabi.>>
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ca̱guda̱a̱gi bwa nꞌara. Kupita bwa ka̱mbigi sada, bwaa yaba Hwe̱n.
Ama butu o̱to̱ naa bwa ka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya bwa gware̱ me̱, wana Yeesu kuda̱gahini butu na̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱. Bwa hin awyatu, <<Nꞌhwe̱n nꞌcininhin nꞌta nꞌne̱e̱ na nꞌtuma ta̱nda ku-Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa mꞌba hin. Jaa ma na̱ nꞌhwe̱n nꞌya̱nu aakuda̱gahini ma, shii hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱.>>
Ama Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Awyatu na za mahanda! Iihin ma, iyaa ta suga̱hin ne̱e̱ a̱cii rigijiga̱ binaa koo zhe̱nke̱n ndaabwa, bupé̱e̱ wuun ma̱ni hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱?
Uhurici gama ta̱hyan arigijigi buꞌa̱ na̱nna suguma sundaabwa na̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱? Bwaa naa shii korogo naa Ibiraahin bunaa Bupira̱ bwa takadaga ba̱re nꞌyo̱ nꞌupwa na̱ nꞌta̱ndatu.>>
Na be̱ cici kunnu, hyo̱ awyatu na taribici buu aba hange̱ nꞌkogi. Hyo̱ awyatu na bwa̱ci aba hange̱ gama na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱da̱ri na̱ wana iri na zumaa na be̱ nje̱.
Mazama nama bikaasu // naa masa̱ta
Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ne̱e̱ haki ba̱? Na̱ ba̱ abaa kuta̱a̱ tuun?
Ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ne̱e̱ hakii kaasu, na biikaasu naa hura̱gi mawuzhira̱ naa masa̱ta+ :19 masa̱ta: Bikaasu naa masa̱ta bishi iri na aba ta zoona̱ na̱ shiipa. Be̱ wuzhiri be̱ ta nda o̱to̱ haku ꞌwe̱e̱.Binaa aba be̱re̱ na̱ cima, be̱ báni, be̱ mawaani, be̱ ba̱ni ꞌwe̱e̱, nꞌno̱no̱ mꞌba ndagi ta̱hurugo na̱ ruun na bwa ꞌwe̱e̱.>>
Mazama nama yisiti
Maatiyu 13:33
Yeesu be̱ gura̱a̱ hantana be̱ hin, <<Iba̱ ga̱n kuta̱a̱ ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n na̱ be̱?
Ta̱ne̱e̱ haku nꞌhyun na nꞌyisiti na mꞌbuꞌa̱ bwa hincin na̱ nꞌhyun o̱to̱, bwa hange̱ hyo̱ na̱ mꞌba nꞌhyun mꞌba she̱ke̱re̱ke̱.>>
Dubo na ta̱suswee
Maatiyu 7:13-14,21-23
Yeesu be̱ gura̱a̱ kota̱na̱ yo̱n zhagu Hurushaliima ma ga̱gaagana awyatu na̱ ace̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ na̱ na nꞌnjeke.
Buyaan bubwa ha̱nta̱ni buu, bwa hin, <<Butu o̱to̱, kawyatu ha̱hamba tanii da̱ba ta̱bina̱ ku-Hwe̱n?>>
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan,
<<Maka̱nta̱ni ma ita̱ni na̱ adubo na ta̱suswee, na̱ wana ta̱hyan ahwarapi nii ruba̱ xade̱be̱ ta̱ta̱na̱, aba jaa ara.
Kubutu naa ina hoo hiika̱ bwa guna̱ni dubo, inii isaga na̱ hwa ma gbaantaan dubo, inaa ma kusuma̱a̱ ma hyaan, <Butu o̱to̱ ta̱gunii dubo.>
<<Bubwa bura̱ni, buhin, <Nꞌyancin kuga̱hin báni.>
<<Inii pasa nꞌungwa ma hyaan, <Ga̱tu naa ta re̱ shami da̱nda̱ na̱ gaa, gaa nje̱ ta̱ga̱gaagana na̱ ce̱pe̱ nda̱tu.>
<<Bubwa bugura̱a̱ hyan, <Awyatu na we̱, nꞌyancin kuga̱hin báni. Hiika̱ ma na̱ aꞌuba̱ nimi!>
<<Kabata ga̱hin naa nꞌgaaga nii mbwa ta̱re̱, ga̱hin nda̱i Ibiraahin na̱ Isiyaaku na̱ Yaakubu na̱ hyo̱ ana ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama kupa̱ri naka ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n. Ga̱hin, aaga̱a̱ ma pata.
Awyatu abaa naa jábagi kope na̱ hwe̱n ta̱bani, na̱ hwe̱n ta̱ꞌira̱, na̱ ruꞌwa, na̱ zuba, ahunraana ta̱re̱ shami paaku buki na ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n.
Kabata ana yigo abaa sha ana ta̱hakana, ana ta̱hakana ashi ana yigo.>>
Yeesu ꞌyantani Hurushaliima
Maatiyu 23:37-39
Na̱ ha̱ni ya̱nu, ayaan Afaraasiya aba wuce, aba hin Yeesu, <<Hiika̱ pina, u-huri kayaan na̱ wana Hirudu buuribi ta̱a̱kuna.>>
Be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Jaga bisa̱ ma butu naa maka̱ri nama uwa̱a̱ ya̱nu ta̱hyan, <Ba̱re na̱ bunwan nꞌnii ba̱ha̱na̱a̱ awyatu na hira̱, ga̱n gura̱a̱ kuda̱gahinaa awyatu, uhwe̱n na hin taatu ta ga̱n huwa̱ tuma nimi.>
Hyo̱ na̱ mꞌmaya̱nu, nꞌnii re̱ iyeebe na̱ tuma nimi ga̱ga̱ga̱ zhagu Hurushaliima ba̱re, na̱ bunwan, na̱ bunwan ree. Na̱ wana unje̱ce̱ ta̱hyan ahin bunaa nii cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama buꞌwi, ubwa jaa sha na̱ Hurushaliima!
<<Ka̱i, awyatu na Hurushaliima! Ka̱i, awyatu na Hurushaliima! Ga̱hin naa nii kunaa ana nii cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ma gyasa tari kana Hwe̱n bwa káji wunhin! Mahwarapi ga̱n ribi ta̱a̱wuna̱a̱na̱ ma haku kuya bwa ta hyaan uwuna̱a̱ni ayoo na̱ apyami ndaabwa, ama ga̱hin ga̱a̱.
Nde̱e̱, aga̱a̱ ma pata, uce̱pe̱ ninhin ha̱nda̱! Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, ijaa gura̱a̱ ma nꞌndaya, sa̱i kuhwe̱n na ga̱hin hin, <Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n ndaaki rubara̱ka, bunaa wuce na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ Hwe̱n.> >>

Yeesu kuda̱gahini butu // na̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱
Na̱ yaan hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya, Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni ina naa yaan butu o̱to̱ naa Afaraasiya, na hyan bire̱ shami. Awyatu aba zooni buu suyishe.
Kuyaan butu bwa ne̱e̱ na̱ aꞌuba̱ na Yeesu, bunaa nꞌara na̱ mꞌbuna mꞌba mutaanyin.
Yeesu be̱ ha̱nta̱ni Afaraasiya na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin, be̱ hin, <<Nꞌgira̱nshin nda̱a̱tu ta̱pa̱ni ta̱kuda̱gahini butu na̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱?>>
Sa̱i aba naanyin wau wau. Yeesu be̱ a̱nta̱ni bwa butu, be̱ kuda̱gahini bwa, be̱ hin bwa xbuhuri ta̱hani ta̱ndaabwa.
Yeesu be̱ ha̱nta̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Suga̱hin ne̱e̱ pina, iyaa ta be̱e̱+ :5 be̱e̱: Ta̱yaan ta̱ꞌyantan ta̱hin, zhe̱nke̱n.koo binaa bindaabwa be̱e̱ kinaa na̱ ibwa na̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱, bwa jaa nda na̱ ha̱ni xbuya̱a̱cigi buu?>>
Ama aba a̱rici buu ta̱rana koo maka̱.
Shapa hyuhyu ndaa // bishici koori
Na Yeesu be̱ nda̱i ta̱hyan aka̱ ana aba bisa̱gi shami ta̱re̱ anii wyanzaan kiikoo naa hunranhunran naa hura̱gi gama, be̱ bishi wyan hyo̱ ndaaba mana̱nna mazama,
<<Kaabíshe buki na ta̱wya̱ri, ta-makwasa ta̱hunrana nii koo naa hura̱gi gama. Wana ta̱hyan bi-yancin koo butu naa ta̱wya̱ri buꞌmꞌbaa buyaan buna buuhuri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa.
Butu naa buki na ta̱wya̱ri bujaa hin, <Hiika̱, u-pa̱ butu na̱nna pa̱ri.> Ukwashe̱ na̱ pa̱ri naka ma̱a̱ncin gama. Ure̱ nꞌkogi na yamboo.
Ama kaabíshe buki, gaa wuci, u-hunrana na̱ pa̱ri naka shici naka hura̱gi gama, na̱ wana hyan jaa kubutu naa ta̱wya̱ri buundai, buuhin, <Bushikaa niimi, kátani paan.> Bi-nii hura̱ ta̱da̱ba ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ kawyatu na aba taabisa̱gi ma na̱ aba.
Too, hyo̱ bunaa mapa̱ zha̱munkun, anii husana be̱, hyo̱ bunaa mahusani, anii pa be̱ zha̱munkun.>>
Ta-nda iri na hyan // aando̱pe̱ pina
Yeesu be̱ hin bunaa tabíshe buu shami ta̱re̱, <<Kuu-hiin bísa̱gi awyatu shami ta̱re̱, ta-bíshe kuushika ndaabi koo diin ndaa koo awyatu na nꞌharu nꞌndaabi ana mꞌbaa iri. Wana ta̱hyan kuu-nje̱ kunnu aja̱maa bíshe taa, ajamaa ndo̱pe̱ sugaa ndaaki wyan.
Ama kuu-nii bísa̱gi awyatu shami ta̱re̱, u-bísa̱gi aꞌwa̱ta̱gi na̱ awyatu na nꞌara mꞌba swa̱, na̱ agurubi, na̱ aruba̱.
Na̱ kunta ta gaa da̱ba rubara̱ka. Na̱ wana ta̱hyan ayata ajamaa ara ta̱a̱ndupa. Uhwe̱n ta na̱maa ndupa, ha̱ni na awyatu na suhari nasu bina̱ abaa hiika̱ka̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱.>>
Mazama nama buki na o̱to̱
Maatiyu 22:2-10
Na buka̱ bunaa tanii re̱ shami da̱nda̱ na̱ Yeesu bwa hange̱ kunnu bwa hin, <<Bunaa rubara̱ka ta bunaa ja̱a̱ re̱ shami na̱ buki na wuci na ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin bwa, <<Ana nda buyaan butu, bunaa tanda buki na o̱to̱, bwa bísa̱gi awyatu hwarapi buki.
Na ha̱ni na buki bwa nje̱, bwa ka̱ji gyamaa ndaabwa tuma xbuꞌnꞌgani awyatu na aba tabísa̱gi buki, <Hure ma, ahwii komba̱ri ta̱ndaga.>
<<Ama hyo̱ ndaaba abaa huwa̱na̱ bwa kuꞌmꞌbanibani na nꞌaba ribici ta̱jábagi. Bunaa yigo bwa hin, <Nꞌsa̱n cima, ta ga̱n ribi ma nda̱i wuun ga̱ga̱ga̱. Kusu nꞌre̱e̱gi kuri.>
<<Buyaan bubwa hin, <Nꞌsa̱n inaa na ta̱ga̱wa̱ iꞌupwa, ta ga̱n ribi ma máanwyani wuun. Kusu nꞌre̱e̱gi kuri.>
<<Buyaan bubwa hin, <Nꞌhwii kuta̱wya̱ri ta̱nda, ta shani ga̱n jaa díbe̱ ta̱jaa.>
<<Sa̱i bwaa gyama bwa kúshe̱, bwa bishi butu naa ina ndaabwa iri na aba bísa̱gi bwa. Bwa butu naa ubwa buki bwa gware̱ me̱ na̱ aba ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, bwa hin bubwaa gyama, <Na̱ ha̱ni, jwara̱gagana ce̱pe̱ na̱ nꞌsunsuun sunsuun na̱ ayo̱n yo̱n yo̱n, u-wa̱na̱a̱ni aꞌwa̱ta̱gi na̱ awyatu na nꞌara mꞌba swa̱, na̱ aruba̱, na̱ agurubi.>
<<Sa̱i bubwaa gyama bwa kúshe̱ kunrun kunrun, bwa hin butu naa ina, <Butu o̱to̱, nꞌnjé̱e̱ iri na gaa tahin. Ama pa̱ri kata bwe̱.>
<<Butu naa ina bwa hin bugyama ndaabwa, <Bana ce̱pe̱. U-jwara̱gagani ayo̱n ana o̱to̱ na̱ ana njeke, u-njé̱e̱ na awyatu xajábagi wana hyan uꞌina nimi cigi.
Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, hyo̱ aya̱nu na aba tabísa̱gi ana yigo, buzaa naa nii hunkuntana masuunran nama ubwa shami na buki.> >>
Ungwan na ne̱e̱ // na̱ nꞌta̱jwara̱ga Ala̱masiihu
Maatiyu 10:37-38
Na̱ ha̱ni ya̱nu ayaan awyatu hwarapi aba jwarigi Yeesu, be̱ kíciike̱ be̱ hin wyan,
<<Hyo̱ bunaa jaa wa̱ka̱mi kuuga̱a̱ci ashin na̱ aya̱na̱, na̱ a̱yo, na̱ mꞌmwaan nꞌndaabwa, na̱ aya̱na̱ba, koo hyuhyu ndaabwa maa hyo̱, bujaa ara ta̱sha bunaa nꞌjwarigi.
Hyo̱, bunaa sha̱pici uguguji ndaabwa bwa nꞌjwarigi, bujaa ara ta̱sha bunaa nꞌjwarigi.
<<Kuuyaan buhiin nda ta̱ma, bujaa isa kwan, buga̱ga̱a̱gi ki, bunda̱i sa bwa mꞌbaa komba̱ri na nii huwa̱ ta̱ba ta̱ma nata̱ ina ndaabwa?
Kushii nuunu, bwa jaa ara ta̱huwa̱ ta̱ba ta̱ma, bwa hoo pasa. Hyo̱ ana nda̱i ta̱ba ta̱ma anaa ꞌwa̱ nꞌratu,
anaa hyaan, <Butu na̱nna pa̱shi ta̱ma ta ta̱ba nga̱zhin ta̱huwa̱.>
<<Kunnu ma yaan. Kuuyaan bugwama naa awyatu dubu upwa, bwa hiin nda gyasa na̱a̱ yaan bunaa awyatu dubu wa̱shi. Bujaa hunrana kwan, buga̱ga̱a̱gi ki, bunda̱i sa bwaa ara ta̱nda na̱ aba?
Kuujaa ara, buka̱ji atuma ndaabwa kuugwama na̱nnda̱ree, awyánzhin hunranhunran na ta̱gumunu ta bwa tutu.
Kunta taa maa ga̱hin, bunaa a̱rici ta̱gaa hyo̱ iri na bwa mꞌbaa, bujaa ara ta̱sha bunaa nꞌjwarigi.
Wun na hwii masuunran
Maatiyu 5:13; Marukusu 9:50
<<Uwun ushi iri na zumaa, ama kuza na̱ mꞌmasuunran mandaabwa, ujaa nda ta̱kushihinana wuun muu.
Uza yaan bina̱ ta̱nda na̱ cima koo mawundu nama ta̱ki, ushi kuta̱munsan.
<<Hyo̱ bunaa mꞌbaa ce̱be̱ na ta̱tuba̱, xbutibi.>>

Mazama namaa ka̱ra̱bi // naa fogi
Maatiyu 18:12-14
Yaan hwe̱n, awyatu na ta naa raaga ga̱ndu na̱ awyatu na ga̱a̱ci pinsan, aba jaa, aba shiraagi mazama nama Yeesu.
Awyatu na Afaraasiya na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin mꞌba jaa, mꞌba pa̱shi nꞌduunrin, <<Ka̱i! Butu na̱nna shi ta̱shika na awyatu na ga̱a̱ci pinsan, ta bwaa re̱ shami na̱ aba.>>
Yeesu be̱ bishi wyan mana̱nna mazama nꞌta̱kun,
<<XAhin buyaan buka̱ suga̱hin ne̱e̱ pina buꞌmꞌbaa ika̱ra̱bi biyina̱ ka̱, bika̱ be̱ fogi, na bwa nii nda? Iyan bunii gaa kuje tundushi na̱ tundushi ma re̱ ta̱re̱e̱, buja̱a̱ wyanzun naa ka̱, hara̱ bujaa ndái buu.
Jaa kuundái buu, buhange̱ gama na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱da̱ri, buta̱ndani buu nii tutu,
buꞌíye̱ buu ina, buꞌnꞌgani ta̱shika ta̱ndaabwa na̱ awyatu na nꞌharu nꞌndaabwa, buhin wyan, <Nꞌguni ma ta̱ga̱da̱ri. Nꞌhange̱ gama na ga̱n ndái bika̱ra̱bi niimi naa tafogi.>
Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, kunnunu aba nii hura̱ ta̱nda ta̱ga̱da̱ri na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ na̱a̱ butu ka̱ naa pinsan naa pa̱ni pinsan baa na̱ awyatu kuje tundushi na̱ tundushi ana bina̱, ana ribici ta̱pana pinsan baa.The lost sheep|lb00001c.tif|col|LUK 15:1-7|Louise Bass|Bika̱ra̱bi naa fogi|15:5Mazama nama yuwa // na fogi
<<XAhin, buꞌa̱ mꞌbaa ayuwa azurufa upwa, uka̱ bwa fogi, bujaa taana ra, buha̱riki ina, bugwataagani koo biya̱ biin ki, hara̱ bujaa nda̱i wuun?
Jaa kuunda̱i wuun, buꞌnꞌgani ta̱shika ta̱ndaabwa, na̱ awyatu na nꞌharu ndaabwa, buhin wyan, <Nꞌguni ma ta̱ga̱da̱ri. Nꞌhange̱ gama na ga̱n ndái ayuwa nimi na tafogi.>
Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, kunnunu Hwe̱n na̱ atuma ndaabwa aba nii nda ta̱ga̱da̱ri na̱ butu ka̱ naa pinsan naa pa̱ni pinsan baa.>>
Baa bunaa fogi
Yeesu be̱ gura̱a̱ hyan, <<Ana ndaa yaan butu bunaa na mꞌbaa mꞌmwaan nꞌreeko na nꞌwya̱ri.
Binaa njeke be̱ hin ashin, <Baaba, mꞌpa̱ni kunrun iri na shi nimi tagaa uwa̱.> Sa̱i ashin aba hoosa̱ni mꞌba mꞌmwaan nꞌreeko iri ndaabwa.
<<Na nꞌhwe̱n mꞌba huri nꞌhamba, binaa njeke be̱ sa̱a̱nha̱ni ꞌwaa nde̱e̱be̱ hyo̱, be̱ huri na̱ ayuwa ce̱nye̱n nata̱ me̱mi. Na be̱ wuci, be̱ hwii iri nde̱e̱be̱ hyo̱ ta̱wyashikaka paaku banshaun na̱ nꞌswagiswagi.
Na be̱ hwii iri nde̱e̱be̱ hyo̱ ta̱wyashikaka, hyo̱ ta̱ba ce̱nye̱n ta̱ba nje̱ rumunro̱n naru zumaancin, be̱ za koori na bwe̱.
Be̱ ja̱a̱, be̱ de̱be̱ tuma paaku butu naa ta̱ba ce̱nye̱n, butu bwa pa̱ni buu tuma na iyo̱ na sudo̱n nasu ina.
Be̱ ribi xbinaa re̱ amba̱ka̱sa̱ na sudo̱n nasu ina subaa re̱, na̱ wana bide̱be̱ce̱ naa pa̱ buu shami.
<<Na aha̱nka̱ri nde̱e̱be̱ aba kúshiike̱, be̱ hin, <Awyatu na nii ndaaka baaba tuma aꞌmꞌbaa shami o̱to̱, ga̱n pina maꞌwa̱ rumunro̱n!
Ga̱n nii hiika̱ ma kushiika kabaaba nimi ma hyan wyan, <<Baaba, ga̱n tandaaka Hwe̱n pinsan, ga̱n taandaaka gaa pinsan.
Ga̱n jwaci na hyan aꞌnꞌnꞌgani be̱e̱ bindaabi. Shaana ma sha haka gyama ndaa.>> >
Too, be̱ hiiki, be̱ jwarigi yo̱n na huri paaka ashin.
<<Na be̱ goki ina, abaaba nde̱e̱be̱ aba nda̱i buu, ambishiri aba kota̱ni wyan, aba hiiki na sumo̱, aba ta̱ buu buu, abaa hwaama buu.
<<Baa bubwa hin ashin, <Baaba, ga̱n tandaaka Hwe̱n pinsan, ga̱n taandaaka gaa pinsan. Nꞌjwaci na hyan aꞌnꞌduwa̱ni ta̱ꞌnꞌgana be̱e̱ bindaabi.>
<<Abaaba nde̱e̱be̱ aba nꞌgani agyama ndaabwa, bwa hin wyan, <Na̱ ha̱ni! Shápi ma da̱bi na o̱to̱ na hura̱gi gama, ita̱a̱ni be̱. Ibwa̱ta̱ni be̱ bimuu na̱ akandaga.
Ishápi birire̱ke̱ yata naa hura̱gi ta̱ꞌwaba, ishe̱nre̱n, ta̱nre̱, ta̱nnje̱ ta̱ga̱da̱ri na̱ nꞌta̱hibwa.
Na̱ wana baa buna̱nna niimi, na̱ ayigo buna ꞌwa̱, niina bukúshiike̱. Na yigo buna foga̱, niina ade̱be̱ be̱.> Aba ke̱ne̱ ta̱hibwa na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱da̱ri.
<<Nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu, buyoo bunaa o̱to̱ bwa na ipa̱ cima, bwa ne̱e̱ na̱ giyo ina. Na bwa goki ina, bwa hange̱ anii ꞌyama imi, abaa hibwaaga ta̱hibwa.
Bwa nꞌgani buyaan bugyama naa ina, bwa ha̱nta̱ni be̱ iri na awyatu abaa nda.
Bugyama bwa hin be̱, <Ayami naa njeke ta kúshiike̱, ta baaba ndaa aba she̱nre̱n birire̱ke̱ yata naa hura̱gi ta̱ꞌwaba na̱ wana ta̱hyan ayami kúshiike̱ ina gumunu.>
<<Buya̱na̱ naa o̱to̱ bigata ndaabwa be̱ ha̱nsha̱nha̱ni ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, bwa ga̱a̱ ina ta̱ta̱na̱. Abaaba ndaaba aba báni, aba pa̱gi be̱ kuri, aba ro̱pe̱ be̱ xbuta̱ni me̱ na ina.
Baa bubwa ra̱ni ashin, bwa hin, <Gwatana hyo̱ nꞌyo̱ nꞌna̱nna, ga̱n na̱maa ndaaka tuma hakuu gyama, nꞌtaga̱a̱ci ta̱nda iri na gaa hin xnꞌnje̱. Hyo̱ ya̱nu, bi-taꞌmꞌpa̱ncin koo biyoyo ma nꞌgana ta̱shika ta̱niimi ta̱re̱ na̱ aba.
Na be̱e̱ bina̱nna ndaabi be̱ kúshiike̱, binaa hwée iri ndaa na a̱ na uwa̱, ta gaa kunaanyin buu birire̱ke̱ yata naa hura̱gi ta̱ꞌwaba.>
<<Ashin aba hin bwa, <Be̱e̱ biniimi, koya̱ ha̱ni bine̱e̱ huku na̱ ga̱mi, hyo̱ iri na ga̱n mꞌbaa, indaa ta.
Uhuri ta̱hyan xta̱nnje̱ ta̱ga̱da̱ri na̱ nꞌgata na nꞌtande̱, na̱ wana ayami yata na̱ ayigo ana ꞌwa̱, niina bukúshiike̱. Na yigo buna foga̱, niina ade̱be̱ be̱.> >>

Mazama nama butu o̱to̱ // naa ta̱be̱
Yeesu be̱ bishi ana jwarigi buu, <<Ana nda buyaan butu bunaa na mꞌbaa iri o̱to̱, bwa pa̱ni buyaan butu ꞌwaa ndaabwa xbugwatagana be̱ bunaa sa̱a̱nha̱na̱a̱. Aba íyaagi be̱ mazama haruwa na butu ndaabwa bwaa wyashikaka ꞌwaa ndaabwa.
Butu naa ꞌwaa bwa nꞌgani be̱, bwa ha̱nta̱ni be̱, bwa hin, <Imba̱nu ga̱n hange̱ ndaa abaa cita̱ga̱? Jaa u-mꞌbisa̱gi haruwa na gaa sa̱a̱nha̱na̱a̱ ꞌwaa nimi, na̱ wana bi-jaa gura̱a̱ naa ma nꞌndaaka tuma.>
<<Butu o̱to̱ naa ꞌwaa ta̱sa̱a̱nha̱na̱a̱ bwa mahin, <Butu naa ꞌwaa bunii mꞌpa sumo̱ kutuma na ga̱n tanaa ndaaka be̱. Iba̱ ga̱n nda? Ga̱n na ga̱n za kai na cima, ga̱n shiragi nꞌkogi na nꞌta̱naa rupa awyatu iri.>
Bwa hin, <Nꞌyan iri na ga̱n nii nda, na̱ wana kaꞌmꞌpa̱ sumo̱ paaku tuma, awyatu nꞌra̱a̱ nꞌara nꞌree na̱ nꞌina nꞌndaaba.>
<<Sa̱i bwa nꞌgani hyo̱ awyatu ka̱a̱ ka̱a̱ ana butu naa ꞌwaa bwa jwara̱gagi wyaan. Bwa ha̱nta̱ni naa yigo bwa hin, <Hamba butu naa ꞌwaa nimi bwaa jwarigi?>
<<Bwa hin, <Biyina̱ ka̱ naa garuwa na mariga̱.>
<<Butu o̱to̱ naa ꞌwaa ta̱sa̱a̱nha̱na̱a̱ bwa hin be̱, <Raa takaada na wyaan na̱ ha̱ni, hunrana, u-kwane̱ biyina̱ ka̱, u-ta̱ kuje ta.>
<<Bwa ha̱nta̱ni yaan, <Gaa, hamba abaa jwarigi?> Bwa taa maa bwa hin, <Nꞌguma na nꞌala̱kama biyina̱ ka̱.>
<<Butu bwa hin be̱, <Raa takaada na wyaan, kushihina wuun ushi kuje ta̱ndatu.> Bwa jwara̱gagani wyan hyo̱, bwa ndaakaki wyan kunnu.
<<Sa̱i butu naa ꞌwaa bwa ya̱ba̱ni butu o̱to̱ naa ꞌwaa ta̱sa̱a̱nha̱na̱a̱ bunje̱ to̱n na̱ wana bunje̱ maka̱ri. Na̱ wana awyatu na sa̱ra̱ri na niina ahuri ta̱yansun ta̱jwara̱ga awyatu naa ke̱nye̱n ndaaba kawyatu na jwarigi Hwe̱n abaa nda.>>
Yeesu be̱ re̱ iyeebe nꞌta̱hyan, <<Ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, nda ma tuma na̱ iri na sa̱ra̱ri yana na ga̱hin mꞌbaa, na̱ wana hyan imade̱e̱be̱ ta̱shika. Na̱ wana jaa kiri ninhin na sa̱ra̱ri yana hwii, ide̱be̱ ta̱raa na̱ ina na mahwa na ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
<<Bunaa aba shii nii gata bunii nda iri na bina̱ na̱ iri na njeke, anii sha̱a̱ be̱ nii gata bunii nda iri na bina̱ na̱ iri na o̱to̱. Bunaa nje̱ ta̱be̱ na̱ iri na njeke, bunii nda ta̱be̱ na̱ iri na o̱to̱.
Kiinje̱ce̱ iri na bina̱ na̱ iri na sa̱ra̱ri yana, iyaa na̱maa pana ma iri na mahanda na ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱?
Kiishiici ki nii gata na̱ iri na butu, iyaa na̱maa pana ma iri na shi ninhin?
<<Butu za naa nii ara ta̱sha bugyama naa awyatu reeko, koo buga̱a̱ buka̱, buribi ka̱, koo bundaaki ka̱ iri na bina̱, koo buhwashe̱ ka̱. Majaa nda na hyan ijwara̱ga Hwe̱n, igura̱a̱ sha̱a̱ nꞌgata kayuwa ha̱ni ka̱.>>
Ta̱yaan ta̱ga̱gaagana // nata̱ Nꞌgira̱nshin
Maatiyu 11:12-13; 5:31-32; Marukusu 10:11-12
Na̱ wana Afaraasiya aribi ayuwa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, na aba hange̱ maya̱nu hyo̱, abaa taga Yeesu cuunrunkwan.
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Ga̱hin taa shi awyatu na ta hura̱ga̱ ta̱ruba̱ ta̱bisa̱a̱ na̱ aꞌuba̱ na awyatu ta̱hyan, ga̱hin taa shi ana bina̱. Ama Hwe̱n yan nꞌgata nꞌniinhin. Iri na awyatu aba pa̱ zha̱munkun, ibe̱ ta shi na Hwe̱n bwa ribici mahwa ta̱ndaya.
<<Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n bwa tapana Muusa na̱ atakaada na awyatu na ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama aba ta shi iri na awyatu aba jwarigi hara̱ kiike̱nye̱n naa Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma. Ama nii ke̱nye̱n naa aba bisa̱gi awyatu mazama nama zumaa nama ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n, kwayaa bwaa nda ta̱hyan xbude̱be̱ ta̱ta̱na̱.
Hyo̱ na̱ kunnu, uhuri ta̱yoo ce̱nye̱n na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱hwii na hyan amo̱nshe̱n ta̱ꞌyantan ta̱ka̱ nata̱ Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa.
Ta̱ga̱gaagana // na̱ wana ta̱gaa ta̱wya̱ri
<<Koo buya̱ bunaa ta̱zhiga̱ni a̱yo bwa zha̱a̱ buyaan, banshaun ta bwaa nda na̱a̱ bwa. Hyo̱ bunaa zha̱a̱ buꞌa̱ naa wya̱rugo aba ta̱zhiga̱ni, bunii nda ta banshaun na̱a̱ bwa.>>
Mazama nama butu // naa mꞌbaa iri na̱a̱ ꞌwa̱ta̱gi
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Ana nda buyaan bunaa mꞌbaa iri, bunaa ta taana ada̱bi na o̱to̱ ana ruzhanna nii da̱da̱bi naa me̱ naa yuwa, bure̱ shami na zumaa koya̱ hwe̱n.
Buyaan buꞌwa̱ta̱gi naa za koori naa suguma nata̱ nꞌfo̱nfo̱n, bunaa aba ta nꞌgana Laazaru. Bwa ta naa na̱ adubo na ina na butu naa mꞌbaa iri.
Buta ruba̱ xbunaa taan nꞌwuzu na nꞌshami na butu naa mꞌbaa iri bwaa re̱, na nꞌnii kinaa. Suwa suba ta naa wuta̱gi sunaa daan suguma sundaabwa.
<<Jaa ba̱re, butu naa za iri bwa ꞌwi, atuma na Hwe̱n aba sha̱pi be̱, aba ꞌye̱e̱ be̱ pa̱ri naka zumaa kaꞌuba̱ na Ibiraahin. Butu naa iri taa bwa ꞌwi, awyatu ndaabwa aba wuma̱ni be̱.
Bwa ne̱e̱ kupa̱ri naka zumaancin paaku ra, bwaa swa ta̱guma, bwa ka̱cihini yishe da̱da̱da̱, bwa nda̱i Ibiraahin tutu, huku na̱ Laazaru.
Bwa nꞌgani Ibiraahin, <Ada nimi, ha̱nga ambishiri nimi, káji Laazaru xbujwa̱ba̱ni bimbwa nde̱e̱be̱ na̱ ma̱ni, buꞌnꞌta̱a̱ni na̱ re̱ntun nimi na̱ wana ma ha̱nga maruma̱a̱. Nꞌshiragi ta̱guma na̱ na̱nna ra.>
<<Ibiraahin be̱ hin be̱, <Be̱e̱ biniimi, mata̱ma̱nriin bike̱nye̱n naa gaa tanaa na̱ sa̱ra̱ri, bi-taꞌmꞌbaa iri na zumaa, Laazaru bwa taza iri na zumaa, bwa ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌtuguma. Niina buhange̱ gama, gaa gaa ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌtuguma.
Shiimaa na̱ wana kunnu, wyantancin nda̱tu uꞌibwa ne̱e̱ na iri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ wana ana ribi ta̱kácigani pina, aba jaa ara, ana ribi ta̱kacigana pita, aba jaa ara.>
<<Butu naa iri bwa hin, <Ada nimi, kusu, kada Laazaru kiꞌina nda̱tu
na̱ wana mꞌmꞌbaa aya̱too na wya̱ri aba ta, xbuja̱a̱ bumánai wyan ce̱be̱ na̱ wana xata jaa pina paa ga̱n ne̱e̱ na̱ ngwan.>
<<Ibiraahin be̱ hin, <Ayamboo mꞌbaa Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa na̱ atakaada na awyatu na ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, xatibi iri na abaa bisa̱ga̱ wyan.>
<<Butu naa iri bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <Manje̱ce̱, Ada nimi, kuuyaan buja̱a̱ kaya̱too bunaa hiiki kuꞌuya̱, anii hura̱ ta̱tuba̱, apa̱ni pinsan baa.>
<<Ibiraahin be̱ hin, <Katibici iri na Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa na̱ atakaada na awyatu na ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama aba hin, koo buyaan buta hiiki kuꞌuya̱, ajaa tuba̱.> >>

Iri na ta shana pinsan // na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ncin pinsan
Maatiyu 18:6-7,21-22; Marukusu 9:42
Uyaan hwe̱n Yeesu be̱ hin ana jwarigi buu, <<Iri nii naa ga̱ga̱ga̱ na nii shaana awyatu naa ndaga pinsan, ama bunaa shaani buyaan bubwa nje̱ pinsan buja̱a̱ swa ta̱guma!
Na hyan buyaan bushaani ana̱nna ana pa̱shi ta̱jwara̱ga Hwe̱n anje̱ pinsan, unii hura̱a̱ga̱ bwa gama, aka̱da̱gi be̱ hyoo na nama na̱ ruru, ajwa̱ba̱ni be̱ na̱ ma̱ni nama iri.
Nꞌna̱maa koota̱ ma.
<<Kayaan yami ndaaki pinsan, nꞌgana be̱, u-bishi be̱ iri na bwaa ndaaki. Kuuwya̱nzhin na hyan imaꞌa̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni, ta-ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ be̱ pinsan ndaabwa nii gata.
Koo butaandaaki pinsan mata̱nda̱ra̱ na̱ hwe̱n ka̱, koya̱ ha̱ni bwa kúshe̱ bwaa hin, <Mꞌpe̱nshe̱n>, ta-ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ bwa nii gata ndaabi.>>
Ana be̱ tazwara aba hin Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu, <<Ta̱ribi ta̱duwa̱ni ta̱pana nꞌgata ku-Hwe̱n. Ta̱bishi kuga̱tuu nda ta̱de̱be̱.>>
Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<XGa̱hin mꞌbaa bigata ta̱pana o̱to̱ hakii kaasu naa masa̱ta, binaa hura̱gi mawuzhira̱ hyo̱ na̱ kaasu, ita nii hyan uꞌwe̱e̱ yeree na o̱to̱, xumwii, uꞌisa na̱ wyantancin na awa̱, ujwara̱ga mazama maniinhin, unje̱ iri na ga̱hin hin xunje̱.
Sha bugyama naa bina̱
<<XAhin suga̱hin ne̱e̱ pina, kuuyaan buꞌmꞌbaa bugyama naa nii hwana bwa cima koo ha̱mbani bwa bikico̱. Na̱ wuco ndaabwa ina buhin be̱, <Jaa re̱ shami>?
Bujaa hyan be̱ kwan, <Nda shiri, u-nꞌndaaki kwan shami nimi, u-ꞌwaan mare̱, u-jaa naa re̱ naazhin ndaa ta̱hakana.>
Bunii gooda̱ bwaa gyama wana ta̱hyan bunje̱ iri na bwa hin bwa xbunje̱?
Kunnu taa ga̱hin, ga̱hin nje̱ iri na abaa hin ma nda ma, sa̱i ihin, <Ga̱tu agyama ta ga̱tu shi. Ri na shi na hyan ta̱nje̱ ta ga̱tu nda.> >>
Yeesu kuda̱gahini // awyatu na za mꞌmbwa aꞌupwa
Yeesu be̱ na̱ zhagu Hurushaliima, be̱ jwara̱gani wyantancin na haru na Samaariya na̱ Gaalili.
Na be̱ hiin naa ta̱na̱ biyaan bicice̱pe̱, kayaan awyatu na suguma nasu tutuu upwa, aba isagi tutu,
aba ta̱a̱ni sunu ma hyaan, <<Yeesu, Butu O̱to̱, ha̱nga ambishiri nda̱tu!>>
Na Yeesu be̱ nda̱i wyan, be̱ hin wyan, <<Jaga ma kuꞌapirisiti, aanda̱i ma.>> Aba na̱ hura̱ na̱ yo̱n koo buya̱ suguma suba hwii sabu.
Buka̱ kaba tanaa, na bwa nda̱i bukwade̱ge̱, bwa kúshe̱ paa Yeesu ma taa nu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ma yaba Hwe̱n.
Bwa wuce, bwa ta̱ runrun kuꞌmꞌbuna na n-Yeesu, bwa gooji buu. Bwa shi Busamaariya.
Yeesu be̱ ha̱nta̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Kawyatu upwa ta ga̱n takuda̱gahini sabu, nꞌnda̱i ayaan atundushi?
Iba̱ shani kuugai na̱nna bwa kúshe̱ bwaa ka̱ bwaa yaba Hwe̱n?>>
Yeesu be̱ hin bwa, <<Hiika̱ ri ndaa. Ta̱panaa gata ndaabi ku-Hwe̱n ta̱a̱kuda̱gahini.>>The leper praises God|WA03879b.tif|col|LUK 17:11-19|Wade Images|Butu naa suguma nasu tutuu buya̱ba̱ni Hwe̱n|17:16Wuco na ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n
Maatiyu 24:23-28,37-41
Uyaan hwe̱n Afaraasiya aba ha̱nta̱ni Yeesu, <<Ya̱ hwe̱n ta ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱baa wuce?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, <<Ai, ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱jaa jaa u-nda̱i tuun na̱ ayishe.
Buza naa nii hyan, <Ta̱ne̱e̱ hina,> koo <Ta̱ne̱e̱ hiree>. Wana ta̱hyan ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ne̱e̱ na̱ ga̱hin.>>
Yeesu be̱ gura̱a̱ hyan ana jwarigi buu, <<Ha̱ni wuci na ga̱hin ja̱a̱ ruba̱ vwainvwain ta̱ndaya uhwe̱n ka̱ na ga̱n Buyoo Butu ga̱n ja̱a̱ kúshe̱, ga̱hin jaa ara ta̱ndaya.
Awyatu ana maa hyaan ma, <Bine̱e̱ hiree,> koo <Bine̱e̱ pina.> Ama ta-jaga ma igwatani.
Ha̱ni na ga̱n Buyoo Butu ga̱n ja̱a̱ kúshe̱, uja̱a̱ sha haku ta̱manyan manyan nata̱ ta̱gwaan nata̱ ta tara̱kana ta̱ra hyo̱.
Ama ga̱n Buyoo Butu nꞌnii swa ta̱guma ga̱ga̱ga̱ koo ta̱ya̱ iri, awyatu na ha̱ni yana aꞌnꞌga̱a̱.
<<Kubwa ta sha na̱ ha̱ni na Nuhu, kunnu taa ubwa ja̱a̱ sha na̱ ha̱ni naa ga̱n Buyoo Butu bwa ja̱a̱ kúshe̱.
Awyatu abaa re̱, abaa swa, ma zhaaga a̱, ma pagana ana a̱ ta̱wya̱ri. Bwa wuce kuha̱ni na Nuhu bwa ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni na o̱to̱, uro̱be̱ na o̱to̱ bwa wuce, ubwa hwii wyan ta̱kunaa hyo̱ ndaaba.
<<Kunnu bwa ta sha taa na̱ ha̱ni na Luutu. Awyatu abaa re̱, abaa swa, ma saan, ma sa̱a̱nha̱na̱a̱, ma biraga, ma maa ta̱ma.
Ama na̱ hwe̱n na Luutu bwa ga̱a̱ ce̱pe̱ na So̱do̱m, udaanrun na ra na tande̱ una hura̱gi mamboo na̱ wunsun ubwa cíin, bwa huunha̱ni wyan hyo̱ ndaaba.
<<Kunnu ubwa nii sha hwe̱n na ga̱n Buyoo Butu ga̱n he̱e̱n buza̱a̱ koo buya̱ buꞌnꞌnda̱i.
Uhwe̱n ya̱nu bunaa ne̱e̱ na̱ sa̱ra̱ri xbuta ta̱na̱ ina, bushápi ꞌwaa. Bunaa ta ipi xbuta gura̱a̱ giye ina.
Mata̱ma̱nriin ma iri na tata aꞌa̱yo Luutu!
Hyo̱ bunaa wungumani hyuhyu ndaabwa, bunii gaa wuun. Bunaa ga̱a̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa, buwungumani ta wuun.
Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, na̱ bwa gita awyatu ree nii taaga nꞌrabi na̱ wyansun ka̱, asha̱pi buka̱, aga̱a̱ buka̱.
Aꞌa̱ ree nii naa na̱ nama da̱nda̱, asha̱pi buka̱, aga̱a̱ buka̱.+ :35 Ta̱yaan ta̱taga nata̱ yigo ta̱ka̱ ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa aaya na 36 kunna: <<Awyatu ree nii naa na̱ cima, asha̱pi buka̱, aga̱a̱ buka̱.>>Ana jwarigi buu aba ha̱nta̱ni, aba hin, <<Pee, Butu O̱to̱?>>
Be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Paaki iri na ꞌwi ibe̱ taa, kabata ada̱ma̱a̱ aba ta mawuna̱na̱.>>

Ta-rukuta̱ na̱ nꞌta̱naa nda ro̱pe̱
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ bishi ana jwarigi buu ta̱kun ta̱na̱nna wana ta̱bisa̱a̱ wyan ta̱hyan xanaa sa̱ na̱ ro̱pe̱ koya̱ ha̱ni xata rukuta̱.
Be̱ hin, <<Ata nda buyaan butu naa ta̱suuga̱ na̱ yaan ce̱pe̱, bunaa wa̱shishi Hwe̱n, bwa cina̱ncin awyatu.
Buyaan buꞌa̱ tanaa na̱ bwa ce̱pe̱ bunaa awya̱rugo aba ꞌwi ma jabaga paa butu naa ta̱suuga̱ ma makusuma̱ xandaaki be̱ ta̱suuga̱ ki kuunaa íye̱ be̱ kuta̱suuga̱.
<<Na yigo bwa ga̱a̱ ama bwa kúshe̱, bwa mahin, <Koo na ga̱n za rukwanyan naru Hwe̱n, ga̱n cina̱ncin awyatu,
ta na ta̱hyan buꞌmꞌma̱a̱ ta̱ꞌnꞌkaka koya̱ ha̱ni, nꞌndaaki be̱ iri na bwa ribi, nꞌta jaa rukuci na̱a̱ bwa.> >>
Sa̱i Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwa hin, <<Too, ha̱nga ma iri na butu naa ta̱suuga̱ naa we̱ bwa hin.
Inda̱i ta̱hyan, Uhwe̱n ujaa ndaaka ana bwa ka̱shi ta̱suuga̱ ki, ana tanaa makusuma̱a̱ na̱a̱ bwa gita na̱ hwe̱n. Bunii nda umuntun nuu na̱ nꞌta̱pana wyan?
Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, bunii ndaaka wyan ta̱suuga̱ ki na̱ ha̱ni. Ama ha̱ni na Buyoo Butu bwa ja̱a̱ kúshe̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana, buja̱a̱ da̱ba ayaan ana pa̱ni nꞌgata na̱a̱ bwa?>>
Ta̱kun nata̱ Faraasiya // na̱ butu naa ta naa raaga ga̱ndu
Yeesu be̱ gura̱a̱ bisa̱ aka̱ ta̱kun ana masha̱pi ta̱hyan ahuri koo buya̱ butu bina̱, anaa husagana aka̱.
<<Awyatu ree tanaa, ana tajaga Ina na Hwe̱n ta̱nda ro̱pe̱. Buka̱ bwa shi Bufaraasiya, buka̱ bwa shi butu naa ta naa raaga ga̱ndu.
Sa̱i Bufaraasiya bwa hiiki, bwa e̱she̱, bwa mandaaki ro̱pe̱, ma hyaan, <Uhwe̱n, iigooji na ga̱n shici haka awyatu ka̱, ana shi azumba̱ na̱ awyatu na pira̱, na̱ awyatu na ta naa nda banshaun, koo maa haku butu yeree bunaa pira̱ naa ta naa raaga ga̱ndu.
Nꞌta nda ruꞌure̱ maree na̱ nꞌhwe̱n nꞌta̱nda̱ra̱, ga̱n ta pana ta̱taa ta̱ka̱ kuꞌupwa nata̱ komba̱ri na ga̱n de̱be̱ ku-Hwe̱n.>
<<Ama butu naa ga̱ndu ta̱raaga bwa e̱she̱ tutu. Bwa gwatancin maa koo ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ma basagana aꞌuba̱ ndaabwa na̱ ame̱ ta̱gura, ma hyaan, <Uhwe̱n, ha̱nga mbishiri nimi, ga̱n shi butu naa pinsan.> >>
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Shiraaga ma ki ihange̱, butu naa ta naa raaga ga̱ndu bwa huri giyo, bwa shi bunaa Hwe̱n bwa nda̱i bushi naa bina̱, shii Bufaraasiya. Hyo̱ bunaa ka̱cihini hyuhyu ndaabwa, anii husana bwa, bunaa mahusani, anii shapaciga bwa.>>
Yeesu sha̱a̱gi // mꞌmwaan nꞌnjeke rubara̱ka
Maatiyu 19:13-15; Marukusu 10:13-16
Na̱ ha̱ni ya̱nu awyatu abaa shápagi mꞌmwaan nꞌndaaba na nꞌnii swa ki-Yeesu na hyan bica̱guda̱a̱ga̱gi muu nꞌara. Ama ana jwarigi buu aba yinzha̱nkani awyatu xata kaka buu.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ nꞌgani mꞌmwaan nꞌnjeke xnꞌhure waabe̱, be̱ hin ana jwarigi buu, <<Hakata ma mꞌmwaan na nꞌnjeke nꞌjaa wa̱ka̱mi, ta-yansan ma muu, na̱ wana ta̱hyan ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱shi nata̱ awyatu na ne̱e̱ haku iri na mꞌmwaan nꞌna̱nna.
Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, hyo̱ bunaa pa̱nciin gata ku-Hwe̱n haku mꞌmwaan nꞌna̱nna na nꞌnjeke, bujaa da̱ba ta̱ta̱na̱ ame̱ na ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n.>>Jesus blessed the children|DN00413b.tif|col|LUK 18:15|Dunham Images|Yeesu sha̱a̱gi mꞌmwaan nꞌnjeke rubara̱ka|18:15Butu o̱to̱ naa mꞌbaa iri ma̱
Maatiyu 19:16-30; Marukusu 10:17-31
Buyaan butu o̱to̱ naa Ayaahudiya bwa ha̱nta̱ni Yeesu, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi binaa mahanda, iba̱ ga̱n nda ma da̱ba ta̱nda bina̱ na mahwa?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin bwa, <<Iba̱ shani gaa nꞌnꞌgani binaa mahanda? Buza naa shi naa mahanda, sa̱i ku-Hwe̱n bwaa ka̱.
Bi-yan da̱i iri na Nꞌgira̱nshin mꞌba hin, <Ta-nda banshaun na̱ aꞌa̱yoo yaan. Ta-kuna butu. Ta-nda zumba̱. Ta-hyan mazama nama shi ta̱be̱ mashi mahanda. Cina̱na̱ abaaba ndaa na̱ ada̱a̱da̱ ndaa.> >>
Bwa butu bwa hin, <<Ta ga̱n ge̱ ga̱n ta hoo jwara̱ga iri ya̱nu hyo̱.>>
Na be̱ hange̱ kunnu, sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin bwa, <<Iri ka̱ taa bwani ta̱nda. Sa̱a̱nha̱na̱a̱ hyo̱ iri na gaa mꞌbaa, u-pa̱ga̱ni aꞌwa̱ta̱gi, bi-nii masha̱a̱ga̱ iri ma̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱. U-jaa naazhin u-nꞌjwara̱ga.>>
Na bwa hange̱ maya̱nu mazama, mꞌba ndaakici bwa, wana buꞌmꞌbaa iri ma̱.
Na Yeesu be̱ nda̱i ta̱hyan mazama mande̱e̱be̱ mata̱ncin bwa, sa̱i be̱ hin, <<Ujaa da̱a̱ra̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na hyan butu naa mꞌbaa iri ma̱ buta̱ni kuta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n.
Unii hura̱ ta̱yoo uraakumi uta̱ni na̱ riyishe na zhimbira na hyan butu naa mꞌbaa iri ma̱, bujaa a̱ri ta̱ta̱na̱ kuta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n.>>
Na ana shiragi buu aba hange̱ kunnu, abaa mahantaana ta̱hyan, <<Too, kushi kunnu, iyaa nu nii ara ta̱nda bina̱?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Iri na nga̱za̱ni butu wuma a̱cii ngazana Hwe̱n ta̱nda.>>
Biituru bwa hin, <<Nde̱e̱, ga̱tu ta, ga̱tu hoo gaa iri nda̱tu, ga̱tuu jwarigi.>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin wyan, <<Nꞌyan kunnu. Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma ta̱hyan, hyo̱ buza naa nii gáa ina ndaabwa, koo aꞌa̱yo, koo aya̱na̱ba, koo ashin na̱ aya̱na̱, koo mꞌmwaan na̱ wana ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n,
bwa jaa da̱ba iri hwarapi niina. Jaa kuuga̱a̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana, bugura̱a̱ da̱ba ta̱nda bina̱ na mahwa.>>
Yeesu gura̱a̱ cita̱ kiibe̱e̱ ꞌwa̱
Maatiyu 20:17-19; Marukusu 10:32-34
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ pe̱e̱n aꞌupwa na ree nii inro̱n, be̱ bishi wyan ta̱hyan, <<Ga̱tu ta, ga̱tu nii hura̱ katanu Hurushaliima. Kuta̱wuci, hyo̱ iri na ana ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama aba tacita̱ ina Buyoo Butu ibe̱ nii ciga̱.
Anii pana buu kana shici Ayaahudiya, anaa ndaga buu, anaa cwaagaga buu, anaa ta̱pa̱ga̱na̱ buu macimi.
Anii zura buu uduun, akwane̱ buu, ama uhwe̱n na hin taatu bukúshe̱e̱ wuma.>>
Ama ana jwarigi buu aba e̱nshe̱nshe̱n mꞌba mazama koo maka̱, wana ta̱hyan asooni wyan iri na mꞌba mazama mꞌba shi. Ta shani aba e̱nshe̱nshe̱n mazama nama be̱e̱ cita̱ga̱.
Yeesu kuda̱gahini buruba̱
Maatiyu 20:29-34; Marukusu 10:46-52
Na Yeesu be̱ goki Yeriiko, kuuyaan buruba̱ taa bwa hunrani nii biin binaa yo̱n ma rupa ri.
Na bwa hange̱ awyatu hwarapi nii hura̱, sa̱i bwa ha̱nta̱ni imba̱nu nii nda.
Aba bishi bwa ta̱hyan Yeesu Bunaazare ta nii hura̱.
Sa̱i bwa ke̱ne̱ ta̱naa taa nu ma hyaan, <<Yeesu, buna biikorogo naa Dawuda, ha̱nga ambishiri nimi!>>
Awyatu na tanaa iyeebe aba yinzha̱nkani bwa sa bunaa wau, ama bwa duwa̱ni kuta̱taana nu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ma hyaan, <<Buna biikorogo naa Dawuda, ha̱nga ambishiri nimi!>>
Yeesu be̱ e̱she̱, be̱ pa̱ni nu xaꞌwaan bwa butu waabe̱. Na bwa wuce do̱ko̱ nii be̱, Yeesu be̱ ha̱nta̱ni bwa,
<<Iba̱ gaa ribi iindaaki?>>
Bwaa ruba̱ bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Butu O̱to̱, nꞌribi ta̱huwa̱ga̱ pa̱ri!>>
Yeesu be̱ hin bwa, <<Huwa̱ga̱! Ta̱panaa gata ndaabi ku-Hwe̱n ta̱ta ta̱a̱kuda̱gahini.>>
Kupita bwa huwa̱gi pa̱ri, bwa jwarigi Yeesu ma yaba Hwe̱n. Na awyatu aba nda̱i kunta, hyo̱ ndaaba abaa yaba taa Hwe̱n.

Yeesu na̱ Zaka
Na Yeesu be̱ ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hani, be̱ ta̱ni ce̱pe̱ na Yeriiko ma hura̱.
Buyaan butu bwa ne̱e̱ na̱ bwa ce̱pe̱, bunaa aba ta nꞌgana Zaka. Bwa shi butu o̱to̱ kawyatu na ta naa raaga ga̱ndu, bwa mꞌbaa iri na ara ndaabwa.
Bwa ribi xbunda̱i Yeesu na nii hura̱, ama bwa nge̱nshe̱nshe̱n na hyan buꞌa̱ri buu ta̱ndaya na̱ ame̱ naa gudu naa awyatu.
Na̱ wana kunnu, Zaka be̱ gidigi iyeebe, be̱ ka̱ta̱ni ꞌwe̱e̱ na waanwan na ne̱e̱ nii biin binaa yo̱n, be̱ hambe̱ xbinda̱i Yeesu na nii hura̱.
Na Yeesu be̱ wuci kuꞌwe̱e̱, be̱ ka̱cihini ayishe da̱da̱da̱, be̱ nda̱i Zaka, be̱ hin buu, <<Zaka, cíin na̱ ha̱ni pita! Ba̱re ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ ga̱n nii rota̱ na̱ ina ndaa.>>
Zaka be̱ he̱e̱n ciinwun kuꞌwe̱e̱, be̱ ra̱a̱ buu nꞌara nꞌree, be̱ huri na̱ Yeesu ina nde̱e̱be̱ ma nda ta̱ga̱da̱ri.
