Na hyo̱ awyatu aba nda̱i iri na nje̱, aba pa̱shi nꞌduunrin, ma hyaan, <<Yeesu ja̱a̱ ina na Zaka, butu naa pinsan.>>
Zaka be̱ hin kaki be̱ e̱she̱, be̱ hin Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu, <<Nꞌshiraga, ga̱n nii pana ta̱bware̱ nata̱ iri na ga̱n mꞌbaa kawyatu na za iri.>> Be̱ gura̱a̱ hyan, <<Butu O̱to̱, kuntapira̱ awyatu ga̱n ra̱a̱ haruwa na shici kunra̱a̱, nꞌnii duwa̱ga̱na̱ wyan mana̱nshin mana̱nshin kuga̱n na raa ma kushihinaana wyan.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin buu, <<Ba̱re, iyana ina bini na̱ wana butu na̱nna bubisa̱a̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa, bushi buyoo Ibiraahin ta.
Na̱ wana ga̱n Buyoo Butu nꞌjaa ma wyanzan ana fogi hakuu na̱nna xma biha̱na̱ wyan.>>
Mazama nama agyama upwa
Maatiyu 25:14-30
Naa bigudu naa awyatu aba shiraagi mazama nama Yeesu, be̱e̱ bisa̱ga̱ wyan mazama na̱ nꞌta̱kun, na̱ wana agoki Hurushaliima, awyatu aba shii na̱ nꞌgata ta̱hyan ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱wuci kunrun.
Be̱ hin, <<Ana nda buyaan butu o̱to̱, bwa hiin jaga ta̱hani pa̱ri naka me̱mi na̱ wana xapáni be̱ ta̱gwama, bukúshiike̱ ce̱nye̱n ta̱ndaabwa.
Bwa ka̱shi agyama ndaabwa upwa, bwa nꞌgani wyan, bwa pa̱ni koo buya̱ ayuwa na zinaari, bunaa nda ciripe̱ na̱ aba, hara̱ bujaa giye. Sa̱i bwa huri.
<<Awyatu na ce̱pe̱ ndaabwa aba ribici be̱, aba ka̱ji atuma ndaaba xabishi butu naa nii pana be̱ ta̱gwama ta̱hyan aribici butu yata bushi bugwama ndaaba.
<<Hyo̱ nꞌta̱hyan kunnu, aba páni be̱ ta̱gwama, bwa giye ina. Bwa nꞌgani agyama ndaabwa xbuhange̱ haruwa na aba nje̱ na̱ ayuwa na bwa tapagana wyan.
<<Bunaa yigo bwa wuce, bwa hin, <Butu o̱to̱, ayuwa ndaa duwa̱ni maꞌupwa kugaa taꞌmꞌpana.>
<<Bugwama bwa hin, <Ha̱nnu! Bugyama naa bina̱ bi-nje̱ to̱n. Tana gaa nje̱ ki na̱ iri ge̱ na abaa pa̱ni, too, nꞌshii bigata ta̱hyan bi-nii nda ki abaa pa̱ni o̱to̱, wana kunnu nꞌna̱maa pana ace̱pe̱ upwa ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱.>
<<Bunaa hin reenu bwa wuce, bwa hin, <Nꞌduwa̱ni mata.>
<<Bugwama bwa hin, <Bi-nje̱ ki, nꞌna̱maa pana ace̱pe̱ ta ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱.>
<<Buyaan bwa wuce, bwa pa̱ni haruwa na aba tapana be̱, bwa hin, <Butu O̱to̱, raa ayuwa ndaa na haruwa na gaa taꞌmꞌpana. Ga̱n takadaga wyan nꞌta̱wuzuwuzu ga̱n shii.
Na̱ wana ga̱n taha̱nga rukwanyan bu-shi butu naa da̱a̱rici. Bi-ta shapa iri na gaa tashiici, u-gubi paa gaa tabe̱re̱ce̱.>
<<Bugwama bwa hin, <Gaa bugyama naa we̱! Nꞌna̱maa ndaaka suuga̱ nge̱n na̱ iri na gaa cici. Bu-yan ga̱n shi butu naa da̱a̱rici, ga̱n ta guba̱ paa ga̱n be̱re̱ce̱?
Bu-yan kunnu, iba̱ shaani gaa tashiici ayuwa paaka hyan aduwa̱ni, jaa kunkúshiike̱ ma raa ayuwa nimi huku na̱ riba?>
<<Bugwama bwa hin ana isagi, <Raa ma ayuwa zinaari ka̱ waabwa, iduwa̱ni bunaa mꞌbaa upwa.>
<<Ama aba ra̱ni, aba hin, <Butu O̱to̱, bugyama yata hoo mꞌbaa ana gii be̱.>
<<Bugwama bwa ra̱ni, <Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma hyo̱, ana nje̱ ki na̱ iri na aba pa̱ni wyan, anii gura̱a̱ duwa̱na̱ wyan. Ama ana nje̱ce̱ ki na̱ iri na aba pa̱ni wyan, koo ge̱ na aba mꞌbaa anii raa wyan wuun.
Ama ana̱nna ana ribici xnꞌshi bugwama ndaaba, ta̱ha̱ni ma wyan pina na̱ aꞌuba̱ nimi, ikunai wyan.> >>
Yeesu ta̱ni Hurushaliima
Maatiyu 21:1-11; Marukusu 11:1-11; Yoohana 12:12-19
Na Yeesu be̱ hwii ta̱cita̱ga̱ mazama, be̱ ta̱ ta̱hura̱ katanu zhagu Hurushaliima.
Na be̱ goki nꞌyaan nꞌcice̱pe̱ na nꞌaba ta hyan Batafaji na̱ Be̱tani na ne̱e̱ nii biin naa Biꞌundu naa Iꞌwe̱e̱ na Zaitu, be̱ ka̱ji ana jwarigi buu aba ree,
be̱ hin wyan, <<Ta̱na̱ ma bicice̱pe̱ naa ne̱e̱ iyeebe ninhin. Jaa kiiwuci, inii ndaya bizhe̱nke̱n ufuni binaa aba taka̱ta̱ncin mahwa. Irígijige buu, iꞌwaan buu pina.
Kuuyaan buu ha̱nta̱ni ma, <Iba̱ shani ga̱hiin rigijiga̱ bizhe̱nke̱n?> hyan ma be̱, <Butu O̱to̱ taa ribi buu.> >>
Ana aba ka̱ji tuma aba huri, aba wuta̱ni komba̱ri to̱n haruwa na Yeesu be̱ bishi wyan.
Aba ma rigijiga̱ buu, kawyatu naa zhe̱nke̱n aba hin wyan, <<Na̱ wana ba̱ ga̱hin rigijiga̱ bizhe̱nke̱n yata?>>
Aba hin, <<Butu O̱to̱ taa ribi buu.>>
Aba íye̱ buu ki-Yeesu. Aba ba̱ra̱gi ada̱bi ndaaba na o̱to̱ na̱ abaa naa be̱e̱ zhe̱nke̱n, aba ka̱cihini Yeesu.
Na Yeesu be̱ zaci nii be̱, awyatu abaa baraga ada̱bi ndaaba na o̱to̱ na̱ yo̱n.
Na be̱ goki Hurushaliima paaku yo̱n bwa ciin kii-Undu naa Iꞌwe̱e̱ na Zaitu, hyo̱ bigudu naa awyatu na jwarigi buu abaa taagana sunu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱da̱ri ma yaba Hwe̱n wana iri na ta̱kai na aba nda̱i.
Abaa hyaan,
<<Rubara̱ka naru Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n
rune̱e̱ hiku kuugwama
naa jaa na̱ nꞌta̱kai ta̱ndaabwa!
Hunranhunran gumunu ku-Hwe̱n na̱ awyatu,
xta̱nsha̱pa̱cigi Hwe̱n.>>
Ayaan Afaraasiya ana ne̱e̱ huku nii be̱e̱ gudu aba hin, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, yansan anaa jwarigi xaga̱a̱ iri na abaa hyaan.>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, <<Ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, koo kane̱e̱ wau, atari na ne̱e̱ na̱ yo̱n anii naa taga ta̱ꞌungwa.>>
Yeesu nꞌgagi // na̱ wana Hurushaliima
Na Yeesu be̱ goki do̱ko̱ Hurushaliima, be̱ nda̱i bwa ce̱pe̱, be̱ pa̱shi nꞌungwa na̱ wana ndaabwa,
be̱ hin, <<Ga̱hin awyatu na Hurushaliima, bwa shi ga̱hin yan iri na na̱maa shaana ma niina hunranhunran gumunu, ga̱hin ta, ga̱hin jaa ara wuun ta̱ndaya niina nꞌsuyishe suniinhin.
Ha̱ni wuci na ta̱guma na awyatu naa ribici ma aba nii ma ga̱ru riinha̱nu na̱ ga̱hin, aariini ma na̱ gyasa koo biya̱a̱ biin.
Ana̱maa bukuta̱ga̱ ma, aakunai ma na̱ mꞌmwaan nꞌniinhin na̱ ame̱ na ga̱ru ninhin. Ajaa gaa koo tari ka̱ ucagudana na̱a̱ ya̱na̱, na̱ wana iga̱a̱ Hwe̱n ha̱ni na bwa jaa wunhin.>>
Yeesu na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n
Maatiyu 21:12-17; Marukusu 11:15-19; Yoohana 2:13-22
Na be̱ wuci na̱ ha̱ni ya̱nu, Yeesu be̱ ta̱ni bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n na Ayaahudiya, be̱ ga̱ci ana nii sa̱a̱nha̱na̱a̱ ꞌwaa kaun.
Be̱ hin, <<Ata̱gi na̱ takaada na Hwe̱n, <Ina nimi shi ina na abaa naa ndaga ro̱pe̱.> Ta ga̱hin ba̱ha̱ni wuun <pa̱ri naka azumba̱ aba ta masoo.> >>
Koya̱ hwe̱n Yeesu be̱ ta naa nda ta̱ga̱gaagana na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n. Ama apirisiti na o̱to̱, na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin, na̱ ayaan awyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya, abaa wyanzan haruwa na abaa kuna buu.
Ama aba de̱be̱ce̱ yo̱n na ta̱nda kunnu, na̱ wana awyatu hyo̱ ashiraagi mazama mande̱e̱be̱ ki.

Aha̱nta̱ni paaku ta̱kai // nata̱ Yeesu ta̱ba báni
Maatiyu 21:23-27; Marukusu 11:27-33
Uyaan hwe̱n na Yeesu be̱e̱ ga̱gaagana awyatu na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n na Ayaahudiya ma bisa̱ga̱ wyan mazama nama zumaa, apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na̱ ayaan awyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya aba jaa waabe̱.
Aba hin buu, <<Ta̱bishi, koo na̱ nꞌta̱ya̱ ta̱kai ta̱ta gaa mꞌbaa na gaa ndaga hyo̱ iri na̱nna? Ayaa pa̱ni ta̱ba ta̱kai?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Ga̱n na̱maa hantana ma taa. Mꞌbishi ma,
ta̱kai nata̱ Yoohana bwa ta naa ndaga baba̱tiisa̱ma, ta̱shi nata̱ Hwe̱n koo nata̱ butu wuma?>>
Aba maga̱ga̱a̱gi kaba kaba, aba hin, <<Kuta̱hin, <Ta̱báni ku-Hwe̱n,> binii hyan, <Iba̱ shani ga̱hin pa̱ncin nꞌgata na̱a̱ bwa?>
Ama kuta̱gura̱a̱ hyan, <Ta̱nda nata̱ butu ta̱ta,> hyo̱ awyatu aba nii ta̱gyasa atari. Wana ta̱hyan hyo̱ awyatu ashii ta̱hyan Yoohana bushi butu naa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama.>>
Na̱ nꞌta̱hyan kunnu, sa̱i aba hin buu, <<Ta̱yancin kuta̱ba báni.>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Ga̱n taa maa nꞌjamaa bisa̱ ma koo ta̱ya̱ ta̱kai ta̱ta ga̱n ndaga hyo̱ iri na̱nna.>>
Ta̱kun nata̱ // ahwaanyan na we̱
Maatiyu 21:33-46; Marukusu 12:1-12
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ke̱ce̱e̱ke̱ kawyatu be̱ bishi wyan ta̱na̱nna ta̱kun, <<Atanda buyaan butu naa ta hwan cima na ꞌwe̱e̱ na iinabi. Bwa pa̱ni wuun unda kayaan hwaanyan. Bwa ja̱a̱ ta̱hani nata̱ bwa cé̱e̱ bike̱nye̱n ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Na ha̱ni na gwasagi na ta̱ꞌwa̱ri bwa nje̱, bwa ka̱ji bugyama ndaabwa ka̱ ta̱hyan xbuja̱a̱ buráagi be̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ iinabi kawyatu na taꞌunda bwa cima. Ama awyatu na taꞌunda cima aba dibi bwaa gyama, aba pa̱ be̱ sumo̱, bwa huri kushiikwa nꞌara nꞌree.
Ama butu naa cima bwa gura̱a̱ káji buyaan bugyama, kiri na̱ ayigo be̱ gura̱a̱ nda. Aba pa̱ be̱ dibi, aba cwaagi be̱, aba ndaaki be̱ iri na zumaancin, aba pa̱ bwa sumo̱, bwa huri kushiikwa kunta nꞌara nꞌree.
Bwa gura̱a̱ kada naa hin taatu, kiri ka̱ be̱ gura̱a̱ nda. Bwa taa maa aba gumahinai bwa, aba bwe̱ bwa na̱ ha.Grapevine|hk00110c.tif|col|LUK 20:9-19|Horace Knowles|ꞌWe̱e̱ na iinabi|20:9<<Sa̱i bwa butu naa cima bwa mahin, <Too, iba̱ ga̱n nda? Nꞌnii kada baa buniimi bunaa ga̱n huri ta̱ruba̱, ga̱n yan kanda̱i buu, anii cina̱na̱ buu.>
<<Ama na aba awyatu na taꞌunda cima aba nda̱i buyoo buwuci, aba mahin, <Too, manje̱ to̱n! Nde̱e̱, bunaa ja̱a̱ hya̱su ree ucima bwa. XTa̱kwane̱ be̱, ubwa cima shi nda̱tu.>
Too, sa̱i aba bwe̱ be̱ na̱ ꞌyafu na ubwa cima, aba kwane̱ be̱.
<<Iba̱ ga̱hin yan butu naa cima nii nda na̱ aba?
Bunii jaga bukunai ayata na bwa tapana unda na ubwa cima, bupa̱ni ayaan.>>
Na awyatu aba hange̱ kunnu, aba hin, <<Hwe̱n pe̱e̱n maya̱nu nii inro̱n majaa sha kunnu.>>
Yeesu be̱ gwatani wyan, be̱ hin, <<Imbata mazama mayata nama aba ta̱ na̱ takaada na Hwe̱n mꞌba shi?
<< <Utari na awyatu na ta̱ma
aba hwashe̱ ta̱hyan uza bina̱,
ubwa ta shi na hura̱gi hyo̱ bina̱ kuta̱ma.> >>
<<Koo buya̱ na kinai na̱ ubwa tari bunii magumahinaa, bunaa ubwa tari bwa zhintani ubwa nii nama be̱ munta̱ ye̱ge̱ye̱ge̱.>>
Na nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na̱ apirisiti na o̱to̱ aba hange̱ kunnu, aba e̱nshe̱n ta̱hyan na̱ aba ta be̱e̱ nda na̱ aba na̱ mꞌmazama nama be̱ cici. Abaa wyanzan yo̱n na hyan akota̱ni Yeesu pita. Ama aba hange̱ rukwanyan naru awyatu xugagu ta hiika̱ aba kota̱ni buu.
Ta̱hantana nata̱ // ta̱pana Kaisa ga̱ndu
Maatiyu 22:15-22; Marukusu 12:13-17
Sa̱i aba sha̱a̱gi buu suyishe xade̱be̱ haruwa na hyan akota̱ni buu, aba ka̱ji ayaan awyatu ana ta naa nda mazama haka wyatu na bina̱. Aba ka̱ji wyan ta̱hyan kaka̱ra̱a̱gi buu bihwa̱ be̱ mazha̱a̱ na̱ mazama mande̱e̱be̱, ade̱be̱, aꞌye̱e̱ buu kugwamina, gwamina shani akota̱ni buu.
Too, sa̱i aba ha̱nta̱ni buu, aba hin, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, ta̱yan ta̱hyan mazama mandaabi na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱ndaabi ta̱ne̱e̱ to̱n, gaa sha̱pi koo buya̱ nge̱n, gaa gura̱a̱ ga̱gaagana uyo̱n na Hwe̱n na̱ mꞌmahanda.
Too, unje̱ to̱n na hyan ta̱pa̱ni Kaisa Bugwama naa Rooma ga̱ndu koo unje̱ce̱ to̱n?>>
Be̱ hoo insan maka̱ri mandaaba, be̱ hin wyan,
<<Mꞌbisa̱a̱ ma aba yuwa na azurufa. Mꞌpirwa na̱ nꞌruzha̱a̱ naru iyaa ta runa̱nna?>>
Aba ra̱ni, <<Kaisa ta.>>
Be̱ hin wyan, <<Too, pana ma iri na shi na Kaisa ku-Kaisa. Ama hyo̱ iri na shi na Hwe̱n xapa̱ni wuun ku-Hwe̱n.>>
Pita na̱ aꞌuba̱ na awyatu aba a̱rici buu ta̱zhaa na̱ mꞌmazama mande̱e̱be̱. Aba nje̱ kuma̱ kiibe̱ ra̱ni wyan, aba naanyin wau wau.
Hwe̱n na ta̱hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱ // na̱ nꞌta̱wya̱ri
Maatiyu 22:23-33; Marukusu 12:18-27
Kayaan Asaduukiya,+ :27 Asaduukiya: Gwatana paa Haruwa na Ayaan Kala̱ma aba Shi.ana hin butu a̱cii hiika̱ bwa ꞌwi, aba jaa ki-Yeesu, aba ha̱nta̱ni buu,
<<Biwya̱ra̱mi, Muusa tata̱taagaga na̱ Nꞌgira̱nshin nꞌnda̱a̱tu ta̱hyan, kubutu ꞌwi bwa ga̱a̱ buꞌa̱, bwa za mꞌmwaan, buya̱na̱ sha̱pi buzha̱a̱ buꞌa̱ yata, buma̱nta̱a̱ni buya̱na̱ yata mꞌmwaan.
Too, ata hoo nda ayaan awyatu ta̱nda̱ra̱ ana shi ta̱ma̱ncin ta̱ka̱. Bunaa o̱to̱ bwa zha̱a̱ buꞌa̱, bwa ꞌwi, bwa za mꞌmwaan.
Buya̱na̱ naa jwárige̱ bwa, bwa zha̱a̱ bubwaa a̱, bwa gura̱a̱ ꞌwa̱, bwa za mꞌmwaan.
Naa hin taatu taa maa kunnu. Aba jwara̱gani kunnu hyo̱ ata̱nda̱ra̱ ya̱nu aba zha̱a̱gi bwaa a̱, aba zaa naa ma̱ncin na̱a̱ bwaa a̱.
Bwaa a̱ bwa jaa, bwa ꞌwi taa.
Too, ta̱bishi aꞌa̱yo yaanu bwa nii sha hwe̱n na ta̱hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱? Na ta̱hyan hyo̱ ata̱nda̱ra̱ ya̱nu azha̱a̱gi bwa.>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Awyatu na sa̱ra̱ri yana ata naa zhaaga a̱, aꞌa̱ abaa giya̱ga̱ ta̱wya̱ri.
Ama ana Hwe̱n bwa nda̱i ta̱hyan agii na hyan ahiiki ku-Hwe̱n na awyatu aba hiika̱ki kuta̱ꞌwa̱, ha̱ni ya̱nu awyatu wya̱ri jaa naa zhaaga a̱, aꞌa̱ aba jaa naa giya̱ga̱ ta̱wya̱ri.
Ajaa gura̱a̱ ꞌwa̱ga̱, anaa haka atuma na Hwe̱n. Anii sha mꞌmwaan na n-Hwe̱n na̱ wana ta̱hyan ahiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱.
Ama koo kumazama nama Muusa bwa tacita̱ nama biꞌuꞌwe̱e̱ binaa sa̱pi be̱ tanaa huna̱ ra na̱ ahira̱ ceeku, ta bisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan, ana ꞌwa̱gi nii hiika̱ka̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱. Muusa tata ta̱hyan, Butu O̱to̱ bushi, <Uhwe̱n na Ibiraahin, Uhwe̱n na Isiyaaku, na̱ Uhwe̱n na Yaakubu.>
Ubwa ta shici Uhwe̱n na awyatu na ꞌwa̱gi, ama ubwa shi Uhwe̱n na awyatu ana ne̱e̱ wuma. Uya̱nu ta bisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan waabwa koo buya̱ bunaa hiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱ bushi butu wuma.>>
Nꞌyaan nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌta naa kaun mꞌba cici mazama, mꞌba hin, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, bi-cici to̱n!>>
Aba za naa gura̱a̱ ara buu ta̱hantana yaan iri.
Iyaa ta shi Ala̱masiihu?
Maatiyu 22:41-46; Marukusu 12:35-37
Yeesu be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan tahyan, <<Na aba nii hyan Ala̱masiihu shi buyoo Dawuda?
Dawuda na̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa butata na̱ takaada na Zaabura,
<< <Butu O̱to̱ tahyan Butu O̱to̱ niimi,
<<Hunrana nꞌkataga kaniimi,
sa̱i kunshaani awyatu naa ribici
gaa fo̱nje̱ wyan na̱ kokobi na buna ndaa.>> >
Ta na ta̱hyan Dawuda taꞌnꞌgana Ala̱masiihu <Butu O̱to̱> na bwa nii gura̱a̱ sha buyoo ha̱ni ka̱?>>
Awyatu ma shiraaga, be̱ bishi ana jwarigi buu ta̱hyan,
<<Iya ma shukuu na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin. Aba ta ruba̱ ta̱taana ada̱bi na o̱to̱ anaa riinshina̱ na̱ aba, aba ta ruba̱ azumanu na maca̱ma̱nta̱n kakasuwa na̱ paaka hura̱gi gama na hunranhunran na̱ aka̱ta̱ku koo paaku abuki.
Aba ta shi ana ta naa pira̱ga̱ aꞌa̱ na suwya̱rugooba suba ꞌwa̱gi, aba za mꞌpirwa na̱ ro̱pe̱ ngiswan kawyatu aba ne̱e̱. Ana nii nda kunnu, aba ta shi ana ja̱a̱ hura̱ga̱ ta̱swa ngwan.>>

Ba̱iko naa a̱ naa awya̱rugo // aba ꞌwi
Marukusu 12:41-44
Na Yeesu be̱ ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ na Ina na Hwe̱n na Ayaahudiya, be̱ gwatagi kawyatu na mꞌbaa iri abaa zwagagana yuwa na̱ ruꞌwana naru ta̱sha̱a̱ga̱ ba̱iko.
Na abaa nda kunnu, kuuꞌa̱ naa awya̱rugo aba ꞌwi bwa shi ꞌwa̱ta̱gi, bwa zwa̱ga̱ni aniinii reeko na wucici kobo.
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Mahanda, ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, ba̱iko na buꞌwa̱ta̱gi na̱nna bwa pa̱ni uhuri na awyatu aba pa̱ga̱ni hyo̱.
Na̱ wana awyatu pa̱ga̱ni ge̱e̱ge̱e̱ kiri na aba mꞌbaa, ama buꞌa̱ na̱nna bwaa pa̱ni hyo̱ na̱ ina bwa mashikani.>>
Yeesu cici iri na ja̱a̱ nda
Maatiyu 24:1-2; Marukusu 13:1-2
Ayaan awyatu ka̱ na jwarigi buu abaa cita̱ga̱ kaba ndaaki Ina na Hwe̱n ruzhanna na̱ atari na aba ma̱ wuun na̱ aba ana gama, na̱ yaan iri na awyatu aba pa̱ga̱ni Hwe̱n na duwa̱ni ta̱ma gama. Ama Yeesu be̱ hin,
<<Hyo̱ ta̱ma ta̱na̱nna nata̱ gama nata̱ ga̱hin nda̱i, ha̱ni wuci na ta̱ba ja̱a̱ huza̱a̱ga̱ hyo̱, uza yaan tari na nii bwata ucagudana na̱a̱ ya̱na̱.>>
Sa̱i aba ha̱nta̱ni buu, <<Biwya̱ra̱mi, uya̱ ha̱ni nu iri ya̱nu be̱ ja̱a̱ nda? Imba̱ iri na iri ta ga̱tu ja̱a̱ ndaya jaa bike̱nye̱n be̱ goki?>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<XBuyaan butu taa pira̱ ma. Na̱ wana awyatu hwarapi ja̱a̱ jaa ahin ga̱n ta nꞌkáji wyan, ahin aba ta shi Ala̱masiihu, ahin, <Ha̱ni wuce.> Ta-jwara̱ga ma wyan.
Bike̱nye̱n naa ga̱hin hange̱ agyasa na̱ ce̱nye̱n na̱ ce̱nye̱n, koo ugagu shi na ce̱nye̱n ta̱ka̱, ta-ha̱nga ma rukwanyan. Mahanda kunnunu, sa̱i kiri ya̱nu jaa ibe̱ nje̱ hyo̱, ama bwa shici ta̱hyan ha̱ni nu wuce.>>
Be̱ duwa̱ni ta̱hyan wyan, <<Ce̱nye̱n na̱ ce̱nye̱n ta̱nii naa nda gagu, ta̱gwama na̱ nꞌta̱gwama ta̱nii naa nda gagu.
Ce̱nye̱n ta̱ba ja̱a̱ zha̱a̱nta̱na̱, rumunro̱n ruba ja̱a̱ nda, suguma koo suya̱ iri suba ja̱a̱ naa pa̱ri kahwarapi, aba ja̱a̱ nda iri na rukwanyan ta̱pa na̱ nꞌta̱jikita̱na̱ iri na ja̱a̱ báni na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
<<Ta iri ya̱nu ibe̱ wuco, ana̱maa kota̱ga̱na̱ ma, ashani, aapa̱ ma ngwan, aaꞌye̱e̱ ma kuꞌaka̱ta̱ku na ta̱suuga̱ na̱ azhaaro, aaꞌye̱e̱ ma kuꞌnꞌgwama na̱ agwamina na̱ wana iꞌnꞌjwarigi.
Na̱nna ta na̱maa pana ma ha̱ni na hyan ibishi wyan mazama maniimi.
Ta-makaka ma na̱ wana iri na ga̱hin nii cita̱ kaꞌuba̱ ndaaba,
na̱ wana ga̱n na̱maa pana ma mazama nama ca̱ma̱ncin nama ta̱yansun na koo buka̱ paaka naa ribici ma, buzaa naa nii ara muu ta̱rana.
Koo maa awyatu naa ma̱nta̱in ma, na̱ aya̱na̱nhin, na̱ diin niinhin, na̱ nꞌta̱shika ta̱niinhin, ana̱maa pana ma kanaa ribici ma, akunai aka̱ ninhin.
Hyo̱ awyatu aba ja̱maa gaa ma na̱ wana iꞌnꞌjwarigi.
Ama za koo buka̱ niinhin naa aba nii antana.
Kiiꞌe̱she̱ ji hiku, inii da̱ba ta̱nda bina̱ na mahwa.
<<Bike̱nye̱n naa ga̱hin nda̱i asooja riini Hurushaliima, ha̱ni ya̱nu ta ga̱hin nii yansun ta̱hyan ta̱huza̱a̱ga̱ ta̱ndaabwa ta̱wuce.
Ha̱ni ya̱nu, ana ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya xagida̱ga̱gi, aka̱ta̱ni nꞌundu, amasoo. Ana ne̱e̱ na̱ Hurushaliima xaba̱ni, ana ne̱e̱ na̱ sa̱ra̱ri na ce̱pe̱ xata ta̱na̱, ahunraana.
Ya̱nu ta nii sha ha̱ni na ta̱pa wyan ta̱guma nꞌta̱suuga̱, kuꞌatakaada na awyatu na ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama aba ta̱gi bwa nii ciga̱.
Na̱ nꞌhwe̱n ya̱nu, aꞌa̱ na suhuba̱ na̱ aꞌa̱ na hyaabu aja̱a̱ hura̱ ta̱guma ta̱swa. Ame̱ ta̱gura na Hwe̱n bwa ja̱a̱ cíin kaba awyatu na Hurushaliima.
Anii kuna aka̱ na̱ gyasa, aꞌye̱e̱ aka̱ ta̱gyama kuta̱yaan ce̱nye̱n. Ana shici Ayaahudiya, aba ja̱maa kaka ma, aahusani ma na̱ Hurushaliima, sa̱i jaa bike̱nye̱n ndaaba be̱ hwii.
Kushiikwa naa Yoo Butu
Maatiyu 24:29-31; Marukusu 13:24-27
<<Aja̱a̱ ndaya mꞌpirwa nꞌhwarapi na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ paaku hwe̱n, kupyanda na̱ nꞌgwasu. Pina na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n, awyatu hyo̱ aba ja̱a̱ naa jikita̱ga̱ na̱ wana rukwanyan, na̱ wana haruwa na arwaga aba ja̱a̱ naa gusa̱ ma zha̱a̱nta̱n.
Awyatu ja̱a̱ naa taaga nꞌzha̱ra̱ na̱ wana rukwanyan, aba nii ꞌwa̱ ta̱ꞌwaba na̱ wana iri na aba nda̱i inii nda na̱ sa̱ra̱ri, na̱ iri na yaburi na ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, na nii zha̱a̱nta̱na̱.
Naazhin koo buya̱ butu ja̱a̱ nꞌndaya ndaya ga̱mi, Buyoo Butu, ma cíin kurara na̱ nꞌta̱kai na̱ nꞌta̱shapaciga ta̱niimi.
Ha̱ni na iri ya̱nu be̱ pa̱shi ta̱naa ndaga, isa ma hiku, xbigata taa ta ma buga̱. Ha̱ni goki na Hwe̱n bwa na̱maa biha̱na̱ ma.>>
Yeesu be̱ bishi wyan ta̱na̱nna ta̱kun, <<Gwatana ma uꞌwe̱e̱ na waanwan, na̱ yaan iꞌwe̱e̱.
Bike̱nye̱n naa ga̱hin nda̱i uta̱nshin aba̱ba, iyan ta̱hyan shuyo goki.
Kunnu taa, ha̱ni na ga̱hin nda̱i iri ya̱nu nii ndaga, inii yansun ma ta̱hyan ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱goki wuco.
<<Mahanda manu ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, awyatu na ne̱e̱ na̱ ha̱ni yana ajaa huwa̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱, sa̱i kiri ya̱nu hyo̱ nje̱.
Ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n ta̱ja̱a̱ huwa̱ ta̱foga̱, ama mazama maniimi maza nama ja̱a̱ foga̱ mahwa.
Ta̱koota̱ga̱ // nata̱ ta̱naa na̱ shiri
<<Naa ma na̱ shiri, nꞌre̱gire̱gi na̱ nꞌswagiswagi na̱ nꞌta̱makaka kuna̱ wyanzun na iri na sa̱ra̱ri yana, xuta hura̱ o̱to̱ na̱ nꞌgata nꞌniinhin. Na̱ wana uhwe̱n ya̱nu ta jamaa wuta̱ni ma ga̱hin jaa yansun, uukota̱ni ma haku ta̱ruma.
Uhwe̱n ya̱nu nii wuce kawyatu na ne̱e̱ na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana hyo̱.
Hunrana ma na̱ shiri, inaa nda ro̱pe̱ ji na̱ wana ta̱hyan ijaa a̱ri ta̱banana kiꞌiri ya̱nu na wuci na we̱, iꞌa̱ri ta̱ꞌisa hiku na̱ uba̱ na Buyoo Butu.>>
Koya̱ hwe̱n Yeesu be̱ ta ta̱na̱ binaa na̱ bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n, binaa ga̱gaagana wyan. Na̱ shurugo, biba̱ni, bija̱a̱ Biꞌundu naa Iꞌwe̱e̱ na Zaitu, biroci piree.
Hyo̱ awyatu aba ta mawuna̱a̱na̱ na̱ bunwan maza, ashiraaga buu na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n.

Awyatu o̱to̱ maga̱ga̱a̱gi // na hyan akwane̱ Yeesu
Maatiyu 26:1-5; Marukusu 14:1-2; Yoohana 11:45-53
Too, Ubuki na Buroodi na za Yisiti,+ :1 Ubuki na Buroodi na za Yisiti: Gwatana paa Haruwa na Ayaan Kala̱ma aba Shi.na aba ta nꞌgana Ubuki na Ta̱matamanrinyan Ta̱hanrinyan Nꞌina, ubwa goki.
Apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin abaa wyanzan haruwa na hyan akwane̱ Yeesu ta̱swee, wana ta̱hyan ashiragi rukwanyan naru awyatu.
Yaahuda ra̱ni ta̱hyan // bunii pana Yeesu
Maatiyu 26:14-16; Marukusu 14:10-11
Too, Bupira̱ bwa ta̱ni bigata naa Yaahuda bunaa aba ta nꞌgana Isikariyo̱ti, bwa shii ka̱ kaꞌupwa na ree na Yeesu be̱ tazwara.
Sa̱i bwa ja̱a̱, bwa njé̱e̱ mazama na̱ apirisiti na o̱to̱, na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na ta ha̱mba Ina na Hwe̱n na Ayaahudiya, haruwa na hyan bupa̱ni Yeesu kuꞌnꞌara ndaaba.
Aba hange̱ gama ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, aba nje̱ ta̱hyan anii pana bwa ayuwa.
Yaahuda bwa ra̱ni na̱ kunnu ma wyanzan yo̱n na hyan bupa̱ni wyan Yeesu, akota̱ni buu, awyatu aba jaa yansun.
Ta̱re̱ shami na Ta̱mawuna̱na̱ // nata̱ Ta̱matamanrinyan // Ta̱hanrinyan Nꞌina
Maatiyu 26:17-25; Marukusu 14:12-21; Yoohana 13:21-30
Na ha̱ni na Ubuki na Buroodi na za Yisiti bwa wuce, na koo buya̱ bwa nii shinran ugwashe̱ na Ubuki na Ta̱matamanrinyan Ta̱hanrinyan Nꞌina,
Yeesu be̱ ka̱ji Biituru na̱ Yoohana, be̱ hin wyan, <<Hura̱ ma, iꞌá̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni pa̱ri naka shami na ga̱tun re̱, una Ubuki na Ta̱matamanrinyan Ta̱hanrinyan Nꞌina.>>
Aba ha̱nta̱ni buu, <<Pee gaa ribi ta̱ja̱a̱ ta̱ꞌá̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni kwan?>>
Be̱ ra̱ni, be̱ hin, <<Kuta̱naa ta̱na̱ Hurushaliima, inii ndaya butu wya̱ri naa ta̱ndani soso naa ma̱ni, ijwara̱ga bwa kuꞌina na bwa ta̱ni.
Ihin be̱ butu naa ina, <Biwya̱ra̱mi hin xta̱a̱ha̱nta̱ni, ta̱bisa̱a̱ udura̱ na bwaa re̱ shami na Ubuki na Ta̱matamanrinyan Ta̱hanrinyan Nꞌina na̱ ana jwarigi bwa.>
Buna̱maa bisa̱a̱ ma udura̱ na o̱to̱ una aba ma̱ da̱da̱da̱ naa ya̱na̱ na mꞌbaa hyo̱ iri na ga̱hin ribi. Kaba ga̱hin nii á̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni hyo̱ komba̱ri.>>
Sa̱i aba huri, aba wuta̱ni komba̱ri nje̱ haruwa na Yeesu be̱ tabishi wyan, aba a̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni shami na Ubuki na Ta̱matamanrinyan kaun.
Ta̱re̱ nata̱ shami // na Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu
Maatiyu 26:26-30; Marukusu 14:22-26; 1 Akorinti 11:23-25
Na ha̱ni bwa nje̱, sa̱i Yeesu na̱ ana be̱ tazwara aba hunraani riinha̱nu da̱nda̱ na hyan are̱ shami.
Sa̱i be̱ hin wyan, <<Nꞌta ruba̱ vwainvwain ma re̱ shami na̱nna da̱nda̱ na̱ ga̱hin, una Ubuki na Ta̱matamanrinyan Ta̱hanrinyan Nꞌina, ta ga̱n pa̱shi ta̱swa ta̱guma.
Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, nꞌjaa gura̱a̱ re̱ shami na buki na̱nna, sa̱i kumba mazama nama Ta̱mawuna̱na̱ macigi kuta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n.>>
Aba ma re̱ shami, be̱ sha̱pi koopi, be̱ gooji Hwe̱n, be̱ hin, <<Raa ma, ihoosa̱ga̱gi hyo̱ ninhin, iswa̱gi.
Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, nꞌjaa gura̱a̱ swa ma̱ni nama iinabi sa̱i jaa kuta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ba wuce.>>
Na be̱ sha̱pi buroodi, be̱ gooji Hwe̱n, be̱ ya̱biza̱gi wuun, be̱ pa̱ga̱ni wyan ma hyaan, <<Ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱niimi ta̱ta, nata̱ ga̱n mꞌpa̱ni wana ninhin. Naa ndaga ma kunta wana hyan inaa ma nꞌtamanrinyaan.>>
Kunnu mayaan, na aba hwii shami ta̱re̱, be̱ sha̱pi bikoopi naa ma̱ni nama iinabi, be̱ hin, <<Bina̱nna koopi taa shi binaa ta̱masha̱a̱ga̱ nata̱ fo binaa nii ciga̱hina̱ na̱ mꞌmahiin maniimi nama ga̱n nii wyashika wana ninhin.
Ama ha̱nga ma, bunaa nii mꞌpana kana nꞌribici, bwa ta pina ma re̱ shami da̱nda̱ na̱ ga̱mi.
Ga̱n Buyoo Butu nii ꞌwa̱ ku-Hwe̱n bwa tasha̱a̱ unii nda, ama bwaa naa mꞌpa̱ni, buja̱a̱ swa ta̱guma.>>
Ana jwarigi buu aba ke̱ne̱ ta̱mahantaana koo iyaa nu ja̱a̱ nda kunnu.
Bunaa nii sha butu o̱to̱ // kana be̱ tazwara
Sa̱i aba ke̱ne̱ ta̱maga̱a̱ga̱nu na̱ nꞌta̱hyan bunaa nii sha butu o̱to̱ na̱ nꞌta̱gwama nata̱ wuci.
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Nꞌgwama na nꞌsa̱ra̱ri yana nꞌta bisa̱a̱ awyatu ndaaba ta̱kai, awyatu o̱to̱ ndaaba aba ta ruba̱ awyatu hin wyan ashi ana tanaa guna̱a̱ awyatu.
Ama na̱ ga̱hin, xuta sha kunnu. Na hyan ushi kunnu, xubutu o̱to̱ shi haku butu njeke, bunaa shi butu o̱to̱ na buuha̱mba̱gi ma, bushi hakuu gyama niinhin.
Iyaa ta huri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, bunaa hunrani ma re̱ shami koo bugyama naa hooso na shami? Shii bunaa hunrani ma re̱ shami ta nuu? Ama ga̱n ta na̱ ame̱ ninhin hakuu gyama naa hooso.
Ga̱hin taa na isa na̱ nꞌgata hiku na̱ nꞌta̱koya̱ ta̱maanwyana nata̱ ga̱n swa̱.
Iipa̱ni ma ta̱gwama haruwa na Baaba nimi aba mꞌpa̱ni,
na hyan ire̱gi, iswa̱gi paaku ta̱re̱ shami nimi nata̱ ta̱ba ta̱gwama. Ga̱hin ja̱a̱ hunraana kuꞌnꞌzhe̱nke̱n na nꞌta̱ba ta̱gwama, inaa ndaaka nꞌkorogo nꞌupwa na̱ nꞌree na n-Isiraaꞌila ta̱suuga̱.
Yeesu cici ta̱hyan Biituru // ja̱a̱ hyan buyancin buu
Maatiyu 26:31-35; Marukusu 14:27-31; Yoohana 13:36-38
<<Siima, Siima, shiraga! Shatan ribi ta̱a̱zaantaan ma haruwa na aba ta zaantan aꞌala̱kama, aya̱a̱cigi amba̱ka̱sa̱.
Ama iindaaki ro̱pe̱, Siima, na hyan gaa jaa jikita̱na̱ na̱ nꞌta̱panaa gata ndaabi. Jaa kuu-kúshe̱ wa̱ka̱mi, u-jaa duwa̱ni ayamboo ta̱taa shita̱ naa ta̱ꞌisa hiku na̱ nꞌta̱pana nꞌgata nꞌndaaba.>>
Biituru bwa hin, <<Butu O̱to̱, nꞌhoo huwa̱ shiri na ta̱hyan koo ushi zhaaro, ta̱hurogo. Kushi ta̱ꞌwa̱, ta̱ꞌwa̱a̱go.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Biituru, nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱, ba̱re na̱ gita ta uka̱nrin bwa ta̱wa̱ ungwa, bu-nii cita̱ ta̱hyan bu-nꞌyancin mataatu.>>
Shiri wana ha̱ni na ngwan
Sa̱i Yeesu be̱ ha̱nta̱ni ana be̱ tazwara, be̱ hin, <<Na ga̱n taakada ma ga̱hin za ruꞌwana naru ta̱zwagana ayuwa, ga̱hin za ka̱fu, ga̱hin za kandaga, iꞌmꞌbaa iri na ga̱hin tade̱be̱ce̱?>>
Aba ra̱ni, aba hin, <<Itaza.>>
Be̱ hin wyan, <<Ama niina, hyo̱ bunaa mꞌbaa ruꞌwana naru ta̱zwagana yuwa koo ka̱fu, xbusha̱pi, buha̱mba̱ga̱. Bunaa gura̱a̱ci mꞌbaa bisa̱nka̱ri, xbusa̱a̱nha̱ni da̱bi ndaabwa, busa̱n bika̱.
Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma ta̱hyan, ta̱ta nata̱ aba ta̱ nata̱ takaada na Hwe̱n ta̱hyan, <Aja̱a̱ yibaku buu na̱ awyatu na mꞌbaa pinsan,> ta̱nii ciga̱ na̱ hyuhyu nimi ga̱ga̱ga̱. Too, hyo̱ iri na aba tata na̱ wana ga̱mi uke̱ne̱ ta̱naa ciga̱.>>
Ana be̱ tazwara aba hin, <<Butu O̱to̱, nde̱e̱ nꞌsa̱nka̱ri nꞌree na.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Nꞌgii.>>
Yeesu nje̱ ro̱pe̱ // na̱ Biꞌundu naa Iꞌwe̱e̱ na Zaitu
Maatiyu 26:36-46; Marukusu 14:32-42
Yeesu be̱ ga̱a̱ ubwa ce̱pe̱, be̱ huri kii-Undu na Iꞌwe̱e̱ na Zaitu haruwa na be̱ ya̱wa̱ni ta̱naa ndaga. Ana be̱ tazwara aba jwarigi buu.
Na be̱ wuci be̱e̱ ko, be̱ hin wyan, <<Naa nda ma mbaa ro̱pe̱ wana ta̱hyan ta̱maanwyana ta̱ta jaa ya̱a̱cigi ta̱pana nꞌgata nꞌniinhin.>>
Be̱ huri ge̱ iyeebe ndaaba haku mame̱ma nama tari ta̱bwa, be̱ she̱nshe̱n, be̱e̱ nda ro̱pe̱,
be̱ hin, <<Ada, kuu-ribi, kusu nꞌya̱a̱cigi bikoopi na̱nna naa ngwan, ama shii ta̱hyan ta̱niimi, sa̱i ta̱ndaabi ta̱ta abaa jwara̱ga.>>
Kuutuma naa Hwe̱n na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ bwa wuce waabe̱ ma duwa̱ga̱na̱ buu bishita̱ nꞌta̱kai.
Wana ta̱hyan bimakaki ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ ngwan na wuci, be̱ duwa̱ni ta̱pa yima̱a̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ ro̱pe̱, umbwaata bwaa kinaa na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n haku nꞌka̱a̱nsa̱n na mꞌmahiin.
Na Yeesu be̱ hiiki paa ro̱pe̱ ta̱nda, be̱ kwashe̱e̱ke̱ kana be̱ tazwara, be̱ wuta̱ni wyan kuna̱ nꞌrabi wana iri na ja̱a̱ nda kiibe̱ tanaa bisa̱ga̱ wyan.
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Iba̱ shani ga̱hin ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌrabi? Hiika̱ ma, inaa nda ro̱pe̱, wana ta̱hyan ta̱maanwyana ta̱ta jaa huri ta̱panaa gata niinhin.>>
Akota̱ni Yeesu
Maatiyu 26:47-56; Marukusu 14:43-50; Yoohana 18:3-11
Be̱ mꞌmazama, kiigudu naa awyatu be̱ manra̱ncinye̱n huku na̱ Yaahuda, buka̱ kana be̱ tazwara upwa na ree, bwa íye̱ wyan. Bwa ja̱a̱ ki-Yeesu na hyan buhwaamaa buu na̱ wana hyan ana bwa jaa na̱ aba ayansun ta̱hyan be̱ ta abaa kota̱na̱.
Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Yaahuda, ka̱i, na̱ nꞌta̱mahwaamana ta̱ta gaa mꞌpana ga̱n, Buyoo Butu!>>
Na ana jwarigi buu aba nda̱i iri na hiin nda, aba ha̱nta̱ni buu ta̱hyan, <<Butu O̱to̱, ta̱nje̱ tuma na̱ nꞌsa̱nka̱ri suu?>>
Kabata buka̱ ana tanaawan nii be̱, bwa pa̱shi bugyama naa butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti nii sa̱nka̱ri, bwa ꞌya̱pi bwa ce̱be̱ na kataga.
Ama Yeesu be̱ yinzha̱nkani wyan, <<Gaa ma.>> Be̱ a̱nta̱ni ce̱be̱ na bwa butu naa aba ꞌya̱pi, be̱ kuda̱gahini bwa.
Too, Yeesu be̱ hin apirisiti na o̱to̱, na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na ta ha̱mba Ina na Hwe̱n, na̱ ayaan awyatu o̱to̱ na awyatu ana tajábani buu, <<Nꞌshi butu naa nii hiika̱hina̱a̱ gagu nuu, na ga̱hin báni na̱ nꞌsa̱nka̱ri na̱ nꞌsungo na hyan iꞌnꞌkota̱ni?
Koya̱ hwe̱n nꞌtanaa na̱ ga̱hin na̱ bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n ma naa ga̱gaagana awyatu ga̱hin nꞌkota̱ncin. Ama niina ta shi ha̱ni ninhin, na̱ ha̱ni na ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱yincincin.>>
Biituru hin buyancin Yeesu
Maatiyu 26:57-58; Marukusu 14:53-54,66-72; Yoohana 18:12-18,25-27
Aba kota̱ni buu, aba huri nii be̱, aba ꞌye̱e̱ buu ina na butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti. Biituru bwa jwárige̱ wyan ta̱baa.
Na aba wuci bwa ina, aba shani ra na̱ sa̱ra̱ri na bwa ina, awyatu aba riini bwa ra hunranhunran ma ha̱ngaaga. Biituru taa bwa wuci do̱ko̱ na̱ ra, bwaa ha̱nga huku na̱ aba.
Na ta̱gwaan nata̱ ra ta̱ba ta̱ra̱ka̱ni, be̱e̱ biꞌa̱ ka̱ naa ta naa na̱ tuma na̱ ina be̱ nda̱i Biituru ma ha̱nga ra huku na̱ aba, be̱ gwatagi bwa ki, be̱ hin, <<Buna̱nna maa bune̱e̱ huku na̱ Yeesu.>>
Ama Biituru bwa bisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan buyancin, bwa hin be̱ be̱e̱ biꞌa̱, <<Kai, be̱e̱ biꞌa̱ na̱nna! Ga̱n yancin butu na̱nna.>>
Naa ke̱nye̱n be̱ huri ge̱, buyaan bubwa e̱nshe̱n bwa, bwa hin bwa, <<Gaa maa bine̱e̱ da̱nda̱ na̱ aba.>>
Ama Biituru bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Kai, butu na̱nna! Shii ga̱n ta!>>
Na ta̱ruma ta̱ka̱ ta̱ba huri buyaan bubwa nda̱i bwa, bwaa hyaan ji, <<Kai, buna̱nna butu mahanda bwa ne̱e̱ huku na̱ Yeesu wana ta̱hyan bushi butu naa Gaalili.>>
Biituru bwa nga̱zhin na̱ kuda̱ga, <<Butu na̱nna, ga̱n na̱maa ga̱n yancin iri na gaa cita̱ga̱.>> Bwa mꞌmazama butaꞌuuta̱ncin nu, kuka̱nrin bwa ta̱ ungwa.
Na̱ bwa ha̱ni, Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwa kíciike̱, bwa gwatani Biituru. Sa̱i Biituru bwa mata̱ma̱nriin iri na Yeesu be̱ tabishi bwa ta̱hyan, <<Ba̱re na̱ gita yana ta uka̱nrin bwa ta̱ ungwa, bi-nii cita̱ ta̱hyan bi-nꞌyancin mataatu.>>
Sa̱i bwa ba̱ni ha, bwaa nꞌgaga nꞌungwa namii gata ta̱guma.
Anii ndaga Yeesu umuntun we̱
Maatiyu 26:67-68; Marukusu 14:65
Sa̱i aba awyatu na taha̱mba Yeesu, abaa ndaga buu umuntun na we̱ ma da̱ba̱ buu.
Aba ka̱da̱gi buu ayishe ma basagana buu, ma hyaan buu, <<Gaa, bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, ta̱bishi iyaa taa ba̱sa̱ni?>>
Abaa gura̱a̱ gisa buu ayaan za̱zama na hwashe̱.
Yeesu na̱ uba̱ na awyatu // na taꞌyapa mazama
Maatiyu 26:59-66; Marukusu 14:55-64; Yoohana 18:19-24
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, awyatu na taꞌyapa mazama aba mawuna̱ni. Aba shi apirisiti na o̱to̱, na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin. Asooja aba ꞌye̱e̱ Yeesu na̱ aꞌuba̱ ndaaba.
Aba hin buu, <<Kuu-shi Ala̱masiihu na Hwe̱n, ta̱bishi!>>
Be̱ hin wyan, <<Kimii bishi ma, ijaa hyan iri na ga̱mii bishi ma shi mahanda.
Kimii ha̱nta̱ni ma, ga̱hin jaa nꞌrana.
Ama hina iyeebe, ga̱n Buyoo Butu ja̱a̱ hunrana nii biin naa ara kataga+ :69 biin naa ara kataga: Bibiin binaa kataga taa shi bunaa shinyaan, koo bunaa jwárige̱ Hwe̱n.na Hwe̱n na Hwe̱n na Hura̱gi Ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.>>
Hyo̱ ndaaba aba ha̱nta̱ni buu, <<Gaa yana Buyoo Hwe̱n ta gaa shi koo?>>
Be̱ ra̱ni, <<Icici ki ta̱hyan ga̱n ta nꞌshi.>>
Aba hin, <<Maya̱ mazama mayaan ga̱tun wyanzan? Ga̱tun suhyu sunda̱a̱tu ta̱hange̱ iri na be̱ cici na̱ nu nde̱e̱be̱.>>

Aꞌye̱e̱ Yeesu // na̱ aꞌuba̱ na Buntu Bilaatu
Maatiyu 27:1-2,11-14; Marukusu 15:1-5; Yoohana 18:28-38
Hyo̱ bigudu naa awyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya be̱ hiiki, be̱ ꞌye̱e̱ Yeesu ku-Bilaatu. Bunaa aba taꞌiyaaga Yeesu bwa shi gwamina na ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya.
Kabata aba ke̱ne̱ Bilaatu ta̱bisa̱ga̱ mazama nama zumaancin nama aba hin Yeesu nii nda, aba hin, <<Ta̱kota̱ni butu na̱nna bunii cita̱ga̱ iri na zumaancin, buhin awyatu xata pana ga̱ndu ku-Kaisa, bugwama naa o̱to̱ naa Rooma. Be̱ hin mayaan, be̱ taa shi Ala̱masiihu, be̱ hin, be̱ taa shi bugwama.>>
Bilaatu bwa ha̱nta̱ni Yeesu, <<Gaa taa shi bugwama naa Ayaahudiya?>>
Yeesu be̱ hin be̱, <<Kunnunu kugaa hin.>>
Bilaatu bwa hin apirisiti na o̱to̱ nii gudu naa awyatu, <<Ga̱n nda̱ci butu na̱nna nje̱ iri na zumaancin.>>
Aba duwa̱ni ta̱cita̱, <<Na̱ iri na be̱e̱ ga̱gaagana awyatu, buhiika̱hini nꞌgata na nꞌwyatu hyo̱ na̱ ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya, buna páshi ta na̱ Gaalili ta bwa wuce pina.>>
Na Bilaatu bwa hange̱ kunnu, bwa ha̱nta̱ni wyan koo butu na̱nna bushi butu naa Gaalili.
Na bwa e̱nshe̱n Yeesu shi butu naa báni ce̱nye̱n nata̱ bugwama Hirudu Antipasi, bwa shaani aꞌye̱e̱ buu ku-Hirudu na tanaa na̱ Hurushaliima bike̱nye̱n ya̱nu.
Na Hirudu bwa nda̱i Yeesu, bwa hange̱ gama. Butaruba̱ ta̱ndaya Yeesu, buhange̱ mazama nama Yeesu ta bwa ribi xbunda̱i buu ma nda iri na rukwanyan.
Bwa ha̱nta̱a̱ni Yeesu mazama mahwarapi, Yeesu be̱ ra̱ncin koo maka̱.
Apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin aba taꞌisaga, aba duwa̱ni ta̱cita̱ Yeesu binje̱ iri na zumaancin.
Hirudu na sooja ndaabwa abaa ꞌwa̱ Yeesu nꞌratu, aba cwaagi Yeesu. Aba ta̱a̱ni buu da̱bi na ta̱gwama, aba kwashe̱he̱ne̱ buu ku-Bilaatu.
Na̱ hwe̱n bwa, Hirudu na̱ Bilaatu ana ta maꞌunso̱ncin mahwa, aba shi ta̱shika.
Bilaatu bwa wuna̱ni apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na̱ awyatu hyo̱.
Bwa hin wyan, <<Iꞌíye̱ butu na̱nna wa̱ka̱mi, ga̱hin hin bunii shana awyatu aba jaa jwara̱ga Kaisa, bugwama naa o̱to̱ naa Rooma. Ga̱n ha̱nta̱a̱ni buu na̱ uba̱ ninhin, ga̱n hange̱ce̱ iri na ga̱hin hin bunii nda na hyan akwane̱ buu.
Hirudu taa buhincin Yeesu nje̱ pinsan, ta shaani bwa kúshihine̱ buu wa̱tu. Ga̱hin taa inda̱i binje̱ce̱ iri na hyan akwane̱ buu.
Na̱ wana kunnu, ga̱n nii shana azware̱ buu nꞌdunduun ma tazhigana buu.>>+ :16 Ta̱yaan ta̱taga nata̱ yigo ta̱ka̱ ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa aaya na 17 kunna: Gwamina na Rooma ta tazhigaaga wyan butu ka̱ koya̱ yo̱ bunaa aba hambe̱ na̱ zhaaro nii ke̱nye̱n naa Ubuki na Ta̱matamanrinyan Ta̱hanrinyan Nꞌina kaba tanaa ndaga.Awyatu aba ta̱a̱ni sunu suka̱, <<Hura̱ na̱ Yeesu, u-ta̱ta̱zhiga̱a̱gi Baraba.>>
Baraba bwa na zwagana na̱ zhaaro na̱ wana buna ndaga gagu na̱ ce̱pe̱, bwa takuna butu.
Bilaatu bwa hin wyan mayaan na̱ wana buribi Yeesu ta̱tazhigana, ta shaani bwa hin wyan Yeesu nje̱ce̱ pinsan.
Ama aba re̱ iyeebe na̱ nꞌta̱taga ta̱ꞌungwa, <<XAka̱bi buu na̱ guguji! XAka̱bi buu na̱ guguji!>>
Mataatu bwa hin wyan, <<Na̱ wana ba̱ ga̱hin hin, <XAka̱bi buu na̱ guguji>? Imbata shi pinsan na butu na̱nna bwa nje̱? Ga̱n nda̱ci butu na̱nna nje̱ iri na ta̱kaba be̱ na̱ guguji. Ga̱n nii shaana azware̱ buu nꞌdunduun, ata̱zhiga̱ni buu.>>
Aba duwa̱ni ta̱ta ta̱ꞌungwa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, xu-Yeesu ꞌwi na̱ nꞌta̱kaba buu. Ta̱ꞌungwa ta̱ndaaba ta̱ba he̱re̱ge̱ Bilaatu bigata.
Bilaatu bwa ꞌya̱pi mazama xanje̱ iri na aba ribi na̱ Yeesu.
Na̱ wana kunnu bwa yáacige̱ buyaan butu naa aba tazwagana na̱ zhaaro, bunaa tahiika̱hina̱ gagu na̱ ce̱pe̱, bwa takuna butu, bunaa aba taruba̱ xata̱zhiga̱ni. Bwa pa̱ni wyan nu xanje̱ iri na aba ribi na̱ Yeesu.
Aka̱bi Yeesu na̱ guguji
Maatiyu 27:32-44; Marukusu 15:21-32; Yoohana 19:17-27; 19:17-27
Na asooja abaa hura̱ na̱ Yeesu, matutumaanwyan buu, aba nda̱i Siima na ce̱pe̱ na Kuraane na báni aga zhagu Hurushaliima, aba kota̱ni be̱, aba shaani be̱ xbuta̱ndani uguguji na aba nii kaba Yeesu, aba shaani be̱ xbusha̱pi wuun, bujwara̱ga Yeesu ta̱baa.
Awyatu hwarapi aba jwarigi buu, aꞌa̱ huku na̱ aba abaa nꞌgaaga ma pasaga suꞌuba̱ sundaaba na̱ wana iri na zumaancin na abaa ndaaka buu.
Yeesu be̱ ke̱ce̱e̱ke̱, be̱ hin wyan, <<Aꞌa̱ na Hurushaliima, ta-naa nꞌgaaga ma na̱ wana ga̱mi, naa nꞌgaga ma na̱ wana suhyu suniinhin na̱ mꞌmwaan nꞌniinhin.
Ha̱ni ja̱a̱ wuce na awyatu aba ja̱a̱ hyan, <Aꞌa̱ na ma̱ncincin na̱ nꞌta̱mba̱ra̱ ta̱ndaaba, aba swa̱ci maya̱a̱suba̱ mandaaba, abaa sha ana rubara̱ka.>
<< <Awyatu aba ja̱a̱ hyan aꞌundu, <<Ta̱zhintani!>>
Ahin nꞌundu, <<Ta̱guna̱ni!>> >
Kawyatu ndaaki ꞌwe̱e̱ na ye̱nce̱n iri na zumaancin, na bwa ja̱a̱ nda jaa bwa hoogi?>>
Aba huri na̱ ayaan awyatu reeko ana pinsan xakwane̱ wyan huku na̱ Yeesu.
Na aba wuci pa̱ri naka aba ta nꞌgana <<Ka̱a̱ta̱ra̱>>, kabata aba ka̱bi buu na̱ guguji, huku na̱ azumba̱ reeko. Buka̱ nii biin naa kataga, buka̱ nii naa kagura̱, Yeesu na̱ awyantancin ndaaba.The cross where Jesus was crucified|WA03926b.tif|col|LUK 23:33-43|Wade Images|Uguguji na aba ka̱bi Yeesu na̱ bwa|23:33Yeesu be̱ hin, <<Ada, ta-ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ wyan pinsan ndaaba nii gata ndaabi, na̱ wana ayancin iri na abaa nda.>> Asooja aba mahoosa̱ga̱ni ꞌwana nde̱e̱be̱ na̱ umuntun na ta̱kasa, anda̱i bunaa nii re̱.
Awyatu aba gwataagi iri na abaa nda. Awyatu o̱to̱ na ce̱nye̱n, abaa cwaagaga buu, aba hin, <<Bibiha̱nii awyatu, xbimabiha̱ni taa be̱ shi mahanda Ala̱masiihu, bunaa Hwe̱n bwa takasa.>>
Asooja abaa ꞌwa̱ buu nꞌratu, aba wuce do̱ko̱ nii be̱, aba pa̱ni buu ma̱ni nama iinabi nama sa̱mbi.
Aba hin buu, <<Kuu-shi mahanda bugwama naa Ayaahudiya, mabiha̱ni na̱ yata guguji.>>
Aba tata ta̱ꞌyantan na̱ guguji, da̱da̱da̱ na hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱, ta̱ba hin, <<Be̱ taa shi Bugwama naa Ayaahudiya.>>
Butu naa pinsan ka̱ naa aba takaba do̱ko̱ nii be̱, bwa cwaagani buu, bwa hin, <<Gaa maya̱a̱cigi, gaa hin bi-shi Ala̱masiihu, u-ta̱ya̱a̱cigi taa ga̱tu.>>
Buyaan butu naa pinsan ka̱ naa aba takaba nii yaan bibiin, bwa hin ya̱na̱ hana, <<Gaa bi-za rukwanyan naru Hwe̱n, gaa na nii ꞌwa̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱ ta̱ka̱ nii be̱?
Ga̱tu anii ta̱pa ngwan nge̱n na̱ wana iri na ga̱tu nje̱ na zumaancin, ama butu na̱nna nje̱ce̱ koori na zumaancin na hyan akwane̱ be̱.>>
Sa̱i bwa hin buu, <<Yeesu, nꞌta̱ma̱nriin, u-mꞌpa̱ pa̱ri jaa gaa wuci ta̱gwama ta̱ndaabi.>>
Yeesu be̱ ra̱ni be̱, <<Mahanda ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱, ba̱re bi-nii naa huku na̱ ga̱mi na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.>>
Yeesu ꞌwi
Maatiyu 27:45-56; Marukusu 15:33-41; Yoohana 19:28-30
Nii ke̱nye̱n naa hwe̱n da̱, ta̱yincincin ta̱ba guna̱ni hyo̱ pa̱ri ji, ta̱ba wuciha̱ni kiike̱nye̱n naa ta̱ruma ta̱taatu nata̱ hwe̱n.
Hwe̱n bwa ta̱ci paaka ba ne̱e̱. Sa̱i uzuzu na ta naa na̱ ame̱ na Ina na Hwe̱n+ :45 uzuzu na ta naa na̱ ame̱ na Ina na Hwe̱n: Ubwa ta shi na ta hoosa̱ Ina na Hwe̱n na Ayaahudiya mareeko, paaka za ta̱shiri na̱ paaka hura̱gi ta̱za ta̱shiri.bwa maha̱nda̱ga̱su mareeko.
Yeesu be̱ ta̱a̱ni nu, be̱ hin, <<Ada, na̱ nꞌara nꞌndaabi nꞌta ga̱n shii bihwaanwun niimi.>> Na be̱ hin kunnu, be̱ hundani nꞌhunjo̱ na nꞌta̱ꞌwa̱.The curtain of the Temple tears in two|lb00265c.tif|col|LUK 23:44-49|Louise Bass|Zuzu na Ina na Hwe̱n maha̱nda̱ga̱su mareeko|23:45Sooja na o̱to̱ kasooja na ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Rooma, bwa tanaa piree, na bwa nda̱i iri na nje̱, bwa ya̱ba̱ni Hwe̱n, bwa hin, <<Mahanda, butu na̱nna shi butu naa bina̱.>>
Awyatu na tanaa piree aba gwataagi, aba nda̱i iri na nje̱, aba ba̱sa̱ga̱ni suꞌuba̱ sundaaba, aba hura̱gi giyo ina na̱ nꞌsume̱ ta̱gura.
Bo̱do̱ awyatu na yan Yeesu, huku na̱ aꞌa̱, ana tajwárige̱ buu ta na̱ Gaalili, aba taꞌisaga katakii, aba gwataagi iri na nii nda.
Ta̱wuma̱na̱ nata̱ Yeesu
Maatiyu 27:57-61; Marukusu 15:42-47; Yoohana 19:38-42
-51 Buyaan butu tanaa, ruzha̱a̱ rundaabwa Yusufu, bunaa báni ce̱pe̱ na Arimatiya na Yaahudiya. Butanaa na̱ awyatu na ta ꞌyapa mazama na Ayaahudiya. Bwa tama̱a̱ncin ta̱ruba̱ iri na aba tanaa ndaaka Yeesu. Bwa tasha butu naa bina̱. Bwa taha̱mbaga xbunda̱i ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n.
Yusufu bwa ja̱a̱ ku-Bilaatu, bwa ha̱nta̱ni xbupa̱ni be̱ ta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ Yeesu, buwuma̱ni.
Bwa cíinha̱ni ta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ Yeesu paaka ba takaba buu, bwa rigi tuun na̱ zuzu na liilin na ta̱wuma̱na̱. Bwa zwa̱ga̱ni buu na̱ uya̱ na aba takinda̱ na̱ apaga, aba tawuma̱ncin butu na̱ bwa.
Hwe̱n na shiri nu, na hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya bwa goki ta̱wuce.
Aꞌa̱ ana tajwárige̱ Yeesu ta na̱ Gaalili, aba jwarigi Yusufu, aba nda̱i uya̱ paaka ba wuma̱ni ruꞌwa̱ naru Yeesu.
Aba huri giyo, aba de̱be̱ ꞌwaa na nꞌshima ina aba nii shana ta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ Yeesu. Ama aba ha̱nka̱ni na̱ wana hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na̱ wana ajwarigi Nꞌgira̱nshin.

Yeesu hiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱
Maatiyu 28:1-10; Marukusu 16:1-8; Yoohana 20:1-10
Hwe̱n na yigo na nꞌhwe̱n nꞌta̱nda̱ra̱, na̱ kasu na shiri, aꞌa̱ aba sha̱pi ꞌwaa na nꞌshima na ta̱shana, aba huri kuꞌuya̱.
Aba nda̱i ariinha̱ni tari na aba taguna̱na̱ uya̱.
Na aba ta̱ni uya̱, aba nda̱ci ta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu na̱ ame̱.
Aba ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan imbata nje̱, aba bwe̱ yishe nii biin, aba nda̱i awyatu reeko isagi do̱ko̱ na̱ aba na̱ aꞌwana na tande̱ manyan manyan haku be̱kuce̱ na shira̱.
Aꞌa̱ aba hange̱ rukwanyan, koo buya̱ bwa mata̱ pa̱m. Ama aba awyatu aba hin wyan, <<Na̱ wana ba̱ ga̱hiin wyanzan butu naa wuma kawyatu na ꞌwa̱gi?
Biza pina, bihiiki hyo̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱. Mata̱ma̱nriin ma na̱ iri na be̱ taabisa̱ ma bike̱nye̱n naa be̱ tanaa na̱ ga̱hin na̱ Gaalili,
<Mahanda Buyoo Butu, anii pana be̱ kawyatu na pinsan, anii kaba be̱ na̱ guguji, buꞌwi. Ama uhwe̱n na hin taatu bunii hiika̱ mayaan.> >>
Na aꞌa̱ aba hange̱, aba mata̱ma̱nriin mazama nama Yeesu be̱ tacita̱, kunnunu.
Na aba kúshiike̱ kuꞌuya̱, aba bishi hyo̱ ri ya̱nu kana jwarigi buu upwa na̱a̱ ka̱ na̱ ayaan awyatu hwarapi,
Maariyamu na Magadalina, Yowana, Maariyamu ada̱a̱da̱ na Yaakubu, na̱ ayaan ana tanaa na̱ aba, aba bishi awyatu na Yeesu be̱ tazwara.
Ama aba pa̱ncin nꞌgata na̱ iri na aꞌa̱ aba cici shi mazama nama uwa̱, mashici mahanda.
Na̱ wana kunnu, Biituru bwa hiiki na sumo̱ zhagu kuꞌuya̱, bwa shiikani ame̱ na uya̱, bwa nda̱i kuzuzu na aba tariga̱ buu na̱ bwa mataagi kubwa, ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ ta̱ba za. Bwa huri giyo, bwaa maga̱gaaga iri na nje̱.
Zhagu Imaawu
Marukusu 16:12-13
Kunnu kuhwe̱n ya̱nu, ayaan aba reeko ana jwarigi Yeesu, aba ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱hani zhagu yaan bicice̱pe̱ naa aba ta nꞌgana Imaawu, mame̱ma kiloomita upwa na̱ ka̱ na̱ Hurushaliima.
Abaa nda mazama nama iri na nje̱.
Aba macita̱ga̱ mazama ki-Yeesu be̱ wuce, be̱e̱ nda ta̱hani huku na̱ aba.
Hwe̱n bwa guniincin wyan nꞌgata xaꞌe̱nshe̱n Yeesu ta ne̱e̱ huku na̱ aba.
Be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan, <<Mazama nama ba̱ ga̱hiin nda na̱ nꞌta̱hani?>>
Aba e̱she̱ wau wau na̱ ame̱ ta̱gura.
Buka̱, bunaa aba ta nꞌgana Kiliyopa, bwa hin buu, <<Gaa taa shii gai pina na̱ Hurushaliima, bunaa yancin iri na nje̱ na̱ nꞌhwe̱n nꞌyana pina.>>
Be̱ ha̱nta̱ni wyan, <<Imba̱ iri?>>
Aba hin buu, <<Iri na nje̱ na̱ Yeesu butu naa Naazare. Bwa shi butu naa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama. Bunaa mazama mandaabwa na̱ tuma ndaabwa bwa mꞌbaa ta̱kai ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ kuꞌuba̱ na Hwe̱n na̱ aꞌuba̱ na awyatu hyo̱.
Apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ nda̱tu aba pa̱ni xakwane̱ buu, aka̱bi buu na̱ guguji,
ama ga̱tu shii ta̱hyan be̱ taa shi bunaa nii biha̱na̱ Isiraaꞌila. Iri na hura̱gi, uhwe̱n na hin taatu na ba̱re kiri ya̱nu be̱ nje̱.
Iyaanyini maa, ayaan aꞌa̱ nda̱tu ata̱pa̱ rukwanyan. Ataja̱a̱ uya̱ ba̱re na̱ bunwan maza,
aba nda̱ci ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ na̱ uya̱. Aba a̱ aba ta̱hin andái atuma na Hwe̱n, ahin wyan bihiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱.
Ayaan awyatu nda̱tu aba ja̱a̱ uya̱, aba cici andái pa̱ri haka a̱ aba tahin, aba nda̱ci Yeesu.>>
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Ka̱i, ya̱ ha̱ni ga̱hin nii pana nꞌgata na̱ iri na awyatu na ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama aba cici?
Shici ta̱hyan Ala̱masiihu nii swa̱ ta̱guma, bijaa ta̱ni pa̱ri kuta̱kai ta̱ndaabwa?>>
Be̱ pa̱shi na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ Hwe̱n bwa tapana Muusa, bo̱do̱ na̱ nata̱ awyatu na ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama aba tataga taa ta̱bisa̱ga̱ wyan hyo̱ iri na takaada na Hwe̱n bwa tacita̱ga̱ nde̱e̱be̱.
Na aba goki bicice̱pe̱ naa aba ja̱a̱, Yeesu be̱ nje̱ kiinii hura̱ iyeebe nꞌta̱hani.
Aba ro̱pe̱ buu, <<Rota̱ huku na̱ ga̱tu na̱ wana shurugo nje̱. Hwe̱n hwii, arima̱nta̱n ke̱ne̱ ta̱nda.>> Sa̱i be̱ huri huku na̱ aba, be̱ ne̱e̱ na̱ aba.
Na be̱e̱ re̱ shami huku na̱ aba, be̱ sha̱pi buroodi, be̱ gooji Hwe̱n, be̱ ya̱biza̱gi, be̱ hoosa̱ga̱ni wyan.
Nii be̱e̱ ke̱nye̱n, Hwe̱n bwa gunii wyan suyishe sundaaba, aba hiin naa insan buu, be̱ fogi.
Abaa mahantaana, <<Kai! Bigata nda̱a̱tu taguniincin bike̱nye̱n na be̱ tane̱e̱ na̱ ga̱tu na̱ yo̱n, be̱e̱ ta̱bisa̱ga̱ mazama nama ta̱gi na̱ takaada na Hwe̱n?>>
Aba hiiki, aba ma̱a̱ncin ke̱nye̱n, aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱ Hurushaliima. Aba wuta̱ni aba upwa na̱a̱ ka̱ ana jwarigi buu na̱ ayaan ana ne̱e̱ huku na̱ aba,
aba hin, <<Mahanda! Yeesu hiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱. Bitabisa̱a̱ hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱ ku-Biituru.>>
Aba ree ya̱nu, aba cita̱gi iri na tanje̱ na̱ yo̱n, haruwa na aba taꞌe̱nshe̱n Yeesu nii ke̱nye̱n naa be̱ takusagi buroodi.
Yeesu wuce kawyatu // na jwarigi buu
Maatiyu 28:16-20; Marukusu 16:14-18; Tuma 1:6-8
Aba macita̱ga̱ mazama, aba yancin, aba nda̱i ki-Yeesu e̱she̱ na̱ aba, be̱ hin wyan, <<Hunranhunran na gama naa huku na̱ ga̱hin.>>
Aba hange̱ rukwanyan, aba hoo hyan upataruwa ta.
Be̱ hin wyan, <<Iba̱ shani ga̱hin hange̱ rukwanyan? Ishici kiiꞌmꞌbaa bigata buga̱ na ga̱hin nda̱i.
Gwatana ma nꞌara nꞌniimi na̱ mꞌbuna nꞌniimi. Mahanda ga̱n ta na̱ hyuhyu nimi. Nꞌa̱nta̱ni ma ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱niimi, hyan iyansun ga̱n ta. Upataruwa za ta̱ꞌwaba na̱ aꞌunfuun kuga̱n mꞌbaa.>>
Na be̱ cici kunnu, be̱ bisa̱a̱ wyan nꞌara na̱ mꞌbuna nꞌnde̱e̱be̱.
Jida̱i aba pa̱ncin nꞌgata, aba hange̱ gama, aba shiragi rukwanyan, be̱ hin wyan, <<Iꞌmꞌbaa iri na ta̱re̱ pina?>>
Aba pa̱ni buu bijooshiipa naa nda̱shi.
Be̱ ra̱a̱, be̱ re̱ na̱ aꞌuba̱ ndaaba.
Be̱ hin wyan, <<Bike̱nye̱n naa ga̱n tanaa na̱ ga̱hin, nꞌtaabisa̱ ma bo̱do̱ iri na nii nda na̱ ga̱mi. Iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n bwa tapana Muusa, na̱ nata̱ awyatu na ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, na̱ nata̱ Zaabura, aba tacita̱ga̱ inii nda, ibe̱ na nje̱.>>
Be̱ gunii wyan nꞌgata, aba e̱nshe̱n mazama nama takaada na Hwe̱n, nama aba ta naa sa̱a̱ cita̱ga̱.
Be̱ hin wyan, <<Iri ina tataga na̱ takaada na Hwe̱n, Ala̱masiihu nii swa ta̱guma, biꞌwi. Na̱ uhwe̱n na hin taatu bihiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱.
Ha̱ni ya̱nu awyatu nii naa bisa̱ga̱ awyatu na ce̱nye̱n hyo̱ xapa̱ni pinsan baa. Aba nii bisa̱ awyatu mayaan na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ ruzha̱a̱ runde̱e̱be̱ ta̱hyan Hwe̱n jaa ha̱mba̱ga̱ pinsan na awyatu nii gata ndaabwa. Aba nii pasa muu na̱ Hurushaliima.
Ga̱hin maa inda̱i, ga̱hin yan, ibisa̱gi awyatu.
Ga̱n nii jaga maa kádaagi ma bunaa Abaaba aba tanda ala̱ka̱wa̱ri ta̱hyan ana̱maa kádaagi ma. Ama naa ma pina na̱ Hurushaliima sa̱i jaa Hwe̱n bwaa duwa̱ni ma ta̱kai na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.>>
Ta̱shapa Yeesu ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱
Marukusu 16:19-20; Tuma 1:9-11
Na be̱ ba̱ni na̱ awyatu na jwarigi buu sa̱ra̱ri, do̱ko̱ na̱ Be̱tani, be̱ ka̱cihini nꞌara da̱da̱da̱, be̱ sha̱a̱gi wyan rubara̱ka.
Nii ke̱nye̱n naa be̱ tanaa sha̱a̱ga̱ wyan rubara̱ka, be̱ ga̱a̱ wyan, Hwe̱n bwa sha̱pi buu da̱da̱da̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
Aba pa̱ buu hunrun, aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱ Hurushaliima nii gata naa tande̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Aba ne̱e̱ ji koya̱ ha̱ni na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n na Ayaahudiya ma yaba Hwe̱n.
ACT - Pangu
Tuma na atumashini na Yeesu
Tuma
Tuma
Tuma na atumashini na Yeesu
Tuma na atumashini na Yeesu
Iri na ta̱yansun na yigo
Awyatu na mꞌbaa ta̱yansun agwatagani ki, aba nda̱i ta̱hyan Luka ta ta̱gi takaada na̱nna, una aba ta nꞌgana Tuma na atumashini na YeesuUna̱nna takaada tashi na hin reenu na Luka bwa ta̱gi. Una yigo tashi na awyatu aba yan nꞌta̱hyan, Mazama nama Zumaa nama Yeesu kuta̱taga nata̱ LukaNa̱ na̱nna takaada ta Luka bwa re̱ iyeebe na̱ nꞌta̱naa cita̱ga̱ mazama nama kuꞌana tajwara̱ga Yeesu aba tanaa swa ungwan na̱ jabagu na aba nje̱ na aba jwarigi mazama nama Yeesu.
Iri na shani aba ta̱gi takaada na̱nna wana hyan abisa̱gi Tiyoofilu ki mahanda, haruwa na ukunrunkunrun na adiini yana na Kirisita aba tapasa. Ubwa takaada na̱nna mayaan ugura̱a̱ bisa̱ga̱ awyatu hiku kuꞌadiini na Kirisita aba tapasa ka-Ayaahudiya na̱ Hurushaliima zhagu kuꞌana shici Ayaahudiya, na̱ hyo̱ kope na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana. Na̱ bwa ha̱ni ata shapa ana jwarigi haka wyatu na ga̱a̱ ta̱gwama nata̱ Rooma, na̱ wana kunnu, sa̱i aba ta̱gi takaada yana na hyan acita̱ni ana jwarigi na̱ bwa ha̱ni.
Una̱nna takaada, una Tuma na atumashini na Yeesuushi haku kaaco̱ na tuma na Yeesu be̱ tanda ha̱ni na be̱ tanaa na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana, na̱ utuma na ana tajwara̱ga buu. Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n tanda tuma ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, paa be̱ ta pa ana tajwara̱ga koo ana be̱ tanaa kadaga tuma ta̱kai nata̱ ta̱nda mazama nama zumaa nama Yeesu. Ubwa takaada bisa̱gi ki tuma na Biituru, na̱ Bulusu, na̱ ayaan hwarapi ana Yeesu be̱ tanaa kadaga tuma, aba tanda. Hyo̱ paa aba nje̱ mazama nama zumaa nama Yeesu, awyatu tara̱a̱ sa̱ muu, ama na̱ ngwan ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱
Ta̱bisa̱ga̱ mazama nama zumaa na̱ Hurushaliima :1--8:3Mazama nama zumaa kuta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahuda na̱ Samaariya :4--12:25Ta̱hani nata̱ Biituru nata̱ yigo zhagu ta̱bisa̱ga̱ mazama nama zumaa :1--14:28Ta̱mawuna̱na̱ nata̱ ana jwarigi na̱ Hurushaliima :1-35Ta̱hani nata̱ Bulusu nata̱ hin reenu zhagu ta̱bisa̱ga̱ wyatu mazama nama zumaa :36--18:22Ta̱hani nata̱ Bulusu nata̱ hin taatu zhagu ta̱bisa̱ga̱ awyatu mazama nama zumaa :23--21:16Akota̱ni Bulusu na̱ Hurushaliima :17--23:22Abwake̱ Bulusu na̱ Kaisariya :23--26:32Aꞌye̱e̱ Bulusu Rooma :1--28:31
Asha̱pi Yeesu zhagu ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱
Marukusu 16:19-20; Luka 24:50-53
Butu o̱to̱ Tiyoofilu, na̱ takaada nimi na yigo, nꞌtaa taagaga hyo̱ iri na Yeesu be̱ tapasa ta̱ndaga na̱ na be̱ tapasa ta̱ga̱gaagana,
hara̱ kuhwe̱n na ba sha̱pi buu zhagu ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱. Ta aba sha̱po buu zhagu ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, be̱ ndaaki ana tajwara̱ga buu mazama ana be̱ tazwara nama báni kii-Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n.
Na aba tapa buu ngwan be̱ ꞌwi, be̱ jábagi waaba buwuma, be̱ ndagi iri hwarapi na hyan bibisa̱a̱ wyan ta̱hyan be̱ taa kúshe̱ buwuma. Na̱ nꞌhwe̱n nꞌhanda be̱e̱ bisa̱ga̱ wyan mazama nama ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n.
Uha̱ni na be̱ tanaa da̱nda̱ na ba ma re̱ shami, be̱ bishi wyan ta̱hyan, <<Ta-gaa ma kwan Hurushaliima, ha̱mbaga ma sa̱i kabaaba nimi kádaagi ma iri na aba tanda ala̱ka̱wa̱ri tahyan anii káji, ina ga̱n tahoo maa bisa̱ ma.
Yoohana tandaga wyatu baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ ma̱ni, ama hina na̱ nꞌhwe̱n hamba anii namaa ndaga ma baba̱tiisa̱ma nii Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n.>>
Ana be̱ tazwara manaawan na̱ Yeesu, sa̱i aba ha̱nta̱ni buu, <<Butu O̱to̱, niina na̱ nuu gaa nii kúshihinani Aꞌisiraaꞌila ta̱gwama ta̱nda̱a̱tu?>>
Yeesu be̱ hin wyan, <<Abaaba nimi bwa taa shi naa yan bwa hwe̱n na̱ ha̱ni, ama ga̱hin aapa̱ncin ma na hyan iyansun.
Ama ija̱a̱ da̱ba ta̱kai jaa Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ cíin na̱ hyuhyu ninhin, ga̱hin naa nda̱i ta ja̱a̱ sha ana nii naa bisa̱ga̱ awyatu mazama maniimi na̱ Hurushaliima na̱ hyo̱ o̱to̱ na ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya na̱ Samaariya na̱ hyo̱ paaka me̱mi na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana.>>
Na be̱ cici kunnu, be̱ ta̱cii ke̱nye̱n aba sha̱pi buu na̱ ayishe ndaaba da̱da̱da̱, uyaan rara bwa guna̱ni buu aba gura̱a̱cii ndaya buu.
Ha̱ni na aba tagwataaga ta̱ra, mayaan mazama mꞌba za kayaan wyatu ree ma taagana aꞌwana na tande̱ munta̱ paawu, aba isagi nii biin do̱ko̱ na̱ aba.
Sa̱i aba hin wyan, <<Ga̱hin awyatu na Gaalili iba̱ shani ga̱hin gwataagi ta̱ra? Yeesu yata na ba sha̱pi wunhin zhagu ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, bija̱a̱ gura̱a̱ kúshe̱ haruwa na ga̱hin nda̱i buu ma katana zhagu ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.>>
Aka̱shi Maataya xbuciga̱hini biko naa Yaahuda
Maatiyu 27:3-10
Sa̱i ana be̱ tazwara aba kúshiike̱ cuun kii-Undu naa Iꞌwe̱e̱ na Zaitu zhagu Hurushaliima, ta̱hani nata̱ goki kiloomita ka̱ zhagu ubwa ce̱pe̱.
Na aba ta̱ni ubwa ce̱pe̱, sa̱i aba ka̱ta̱ni dura̱ na da̱da̱da̱ paaka ba ta naa. Ana tanaa kaun na, Biituru na̱ Yoohana na̱ Yaakubu na̱ Andaraawa na̱ Filibu na̱ Toma na̱ Baatalomi na̱ Maatiyu na̱ Yaakubu Hala̱fa, na̱ Siima bunaa aba tahyan butahura̱ ta̱ꞌisa hiku na̱ ce̱nye̱n ta̱ndaabwa, na̱ Yaahuda Yaakubu.
Hyo̱ aya̱nu aba pa̱ni suhyu sundaaba ma nda ro̱pe̱ na̱ nꞌgata nꞌka̱, huku na̱ aꞌa̱ na tajwara̱ga Yeesu, Maariyamu ada̱a̱da̱ na Yeesu, na̱ aya̱na̱ba nde̱e̱be̱.
Na̱ mꞌba nꞌhwe̱n, sa̱i Biituru bwa hiiki bwa nje̱ mazama nii gudu naa wyatu ana tapana nꞌgata nꞌndaaba, atagoka̱ biyina̱ ka̱ na̱ wa̱shi,
bwa hin, <<Aya̱too ma, mashi ga̱ga̱ga̱ na hyan aciga̱hini mazama mayata nama Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ tacita̱ hasaa na̱ takaada na Hwe̱n na̱ nu na Dawuda nama Yaahuda, bunaa taꞌiya ana takota̱na̱ Yeesu.
Na yigo butanaa huku na̱ ga̱tu, bwa taꞌmꞌbaa tuma nda̱tu na Yeesu be̱ tapana bwa.>>
(Na̱ funa̱ na tuma ndaabwa na we̱ na bwa tada̱ba aba sa̱n pa̱ri, sa̱i bwa butu naa uwa̱ bwa kinai pwan na̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa, ta̱mba̱ra̱ ta̱ba punshin, iꞌwaa na me̱ ina ta̱mba̱ra̱ ta̱ndaabwa ibe̱ báni hyo̱ sa̱ra̱ri.
Hyo̱ awyatu na tanaa na̱ Hurushaliima ta yansun mꞌba mazama nama ta̱ꞌwa̱ ta̱ndaabwa, abaa nꞌga be̱e̱ ko na̱ nꞌta̱waaba <<Akala̱dama,>> tashi, pa̱ri naka mahiin.)
Sa̱i Biituru bwa gura̱a̱ hyan, <<Na ta̱hyan ata̱gi wuun na̱ takaada na Zaabura ta̱hyan, <xUpa̱ri naka bwa tahunrana kashi aka̱ngu, xata gaa buyaan buhunrana na̱ ame̱.> Aba gura̱a̱ hyan, <Biko naa bwa taha̱mba̱ga̱ naa yaburi xbuyaan busha̱pi kaun.>
<<Na̱ kunnu ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ xta̱nka̱shi butu ka̱ naa tanaa na̱ ga̱tu ha̱ni na Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwa tanaa ta̱na̱a̱ ma banaa na̱ ga̱tu wa̱tu.
Bwa butu xbushi bunaa tanaa ta na̱ ha̱ni na Yoohana bwa tanaa ndaga baba̱tiisa̱ma zhagu ha̱ni na aba tashapa Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu wa̱tu, zhagu ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱. Bwa butu xbushi naa nii ta̱guna̱ ta̱bisa̱ga̱ awyatu ta̱hyan bunda̱i ta̱hiika̱ ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ huku na̱ ga̱tu.>>
Sa̱i aba ꞌwaan awyatu ree, Yusufu bunaa ba ta nꞌgana Bara̱saba (agura̱a̱ nꞌgana be̱ Yusutusu) na̱ Maataya.
Ana jwarigi buu aba nje̱ ro̱pe̱ hyo̱ ndaaba, <<Butu O̱to̱, bi-yan bigata naa koo buya̱ butu hyo̱. Ta̱bisa̱a̱ bunaa gaa ka̱shi, kawyatu na̱nna ree,
butu naa tuma ndaa na gaa ta̱pa̱ni ta̱nda, na̱ ana gaa tazwara, una Yaahuda bwa ga̱a̱, bwa huri paaka huri ta̱ma giya̱ na̱a̱ bwa.>>
Sa̱i aba ndaaki wyan umuntun na ta̱kasa, Maataya bwa re̱, aba yibaku bwa na upwa na̱a̱ ka̱ ana Yeesu be̱ tazwara, anje̱ tuma na̱a̱ bwa.

Zhagu naa Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n
Na uha̱ni na hwe̱n na buki na Pe̱ntiko bwa nje̱, nꞌhwe̱n handa na̱ nꞌtundushi na Yeesu be̱ tahiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱, hyo̱ wyatu na pa̱ni nꞌgata aba mawuna̱ni huku biko ka̱.
Mayaan mazama mꞌba za, aba hange̱ yaanyini haku rama na pyara na kai, bwa cíin na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, bwa guna̱ni paaka ba hunraani na̱ ina.
Sa̱i ba nda̱i kiyaan iri haku nꞌre̱ntun na nꞌra ma mahoosa̱ga̱ga̱ ma zatagana koo buya̱ na̱ hyuhyu.
Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ ta̱ni koo buya̱, aba pa̱shi mazama na̱ nꞌta̱ce̱pe̱ googoogoo kii-Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ pa̱ni wyan ta̱kai nata̱ mazama.
Too, na̱ bwa ha̱ni, awyatu na jwarigi adiini na Ayaahudiya ana tajwara̱ga Hwe̱n ki na̱ ana bánai kope na̱ sa̱ra̱ri atanaa na̱ Hurushaliima.
Na aba hange̱ bwa rama, awyatu aba cigi da̱, aba jikita̱ni wana ta̱hyan koo buya̱ buhange̱ awyatu ana pa̱ni nꞌgata nii nda mazama na̱ nꞌta̱ce̱pe̱ ta̱ndaabwa.
Aba nje̱ kuma̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, ma hyaan, <<Hyo̱ awyatu na̱nna shii awyatu na Gaalili ta nuu?
Ama na hyo̱ nda̱tu ga̱tu hange̱ koo buya̱ anii nda mazama na̱ nꞌta̱ce̱pe̱ ta̱ndaabwa?
Ga̱tu na ne̱e̱, Apara̱tiya na̱ Amediya na̱ Aꞌe̱lama na̱ awyatu na Mesopotaaminyan na̱ ana ne̱e̱ kiibiin binaa Yaahudiya na̱ ana Kafadookiya na̱ ana Fantusu na̱ ana ne̱e̱ ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Aasiya,
na̱ ana Firijiya na̱ ana Pamafiliya na̱ ana Masa na̱ ana ne̱e̱ riinha̱nu na̱ Kuraane na ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Libiya, hyo̱ maa na gai ana Rooma, (ga̱tu na ana ba ma̱nta̱in na̱ n-Ta̱yaahudiya, na̱ ana pa̱ni nꞌgata nꞌndaaba aba ta̱ta̱ni),
ga̱tu na Akiriiti na̱ Alaaraba. Ga̱tu na hyo̱ ta̱hange̱ awyatu na̱nna anii nda mazama na̱ nꞌta̱ce̱pe̱ ta̱nda̱a̱tu, nama iri na yaburi na Hwe̱n bwa nje̱.>>
Hyo̱ ndaaba aba jikita̱ni, aba nje̱ kuma̱, ma mahyaan, <<Mbata na̱nna bwa shi?>>
Aka̱ abaa ndaga wyan umuntun ta̱hyan aswa̱gi ta.
Mazama nama Biituru bwa tanda hwe̱n na Pe̱ntiko
Sa̱i Biituru huku na̱ upwa na̱ ka̱ ana Yeesu be̱ tazwara, bwa hiiki na uba̱ na awyatu, bwa ta̱a̱ni nu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ bwa nje̱ mazama bwa hin, <<Ga̱hin aya̱too nimi Ayaahudiya na̱ hyo̱ ana hunrani na̱ Hurushaliima, ha̱nga ma ishiraga ki iri na ga̱n cita̱.
Awyatu na̱nna aswa̱gici suga̱hin shii na̱ nꞌgata, ta na ta̱hyan uta ma̱a̱ ta̱sha bunwan maza masakarukwa mahwée kuta̱naa kátani na hyan ta̱naa hoo ndaga wyan.
Ai, na̱nna tashi iri na bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Jowela bwa tacita̱:
<<Uhwe̱n tahyan,
<Nꞌhwe̱n na nꞌta̱makwaakaa nꞌja̱a̱ zóogi hyo̱ awyatu bihwaanwun niimi.
Mꞌmwaan nꞌniinhin na nꞌwya̱ri na̱ na nꞌa̱ nꞌja̱a̱ nda tuma na ta̱ꞌnꞌcita̱a̱ga̱ mazama.
Asa̱mba̱ri ninhin, nꞌja̱a̱ bisa̱a̱ wyan yaan ri anda̱i.
Asooho ninhin, nꞌja̱a̱ shana wyan ajaa naa ndaga ara̱rabi.
Hyo̱ maa agyama nimi, ana wya̱ri na̱ ana a̱,
na̱ mꞌba nꞌyo̱, nꞌja̱a̱ zóogi wyan bihwaanwun niimi
anje̱ tuma na ta̱ꞌnꞌcita̱a̱ga̱ mazama.
Nꞌja̱a̱ bisa̱a̱ iri na ta̱jikita̱na̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱
na̱ iri nata̱ pa rukwanyan na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n,
na̱ mahiin na̱ ra na̱ nꞌhyoo na nꞌshiri.
Uhwe̱n ja̱a̱ kushiika ta̱yincincin,
upyanda kwashe̱ swaan haku mahiin,
ta uhwe̱n na Butu O̱to̱ bwa wuco,
uhwe̱n na o̱to̱ na ta̱shapaciga.
Na̱ bwa ha̱ni ta hyo̱ bunaa nje̱ ro̱pe̱
na̱ nꞌruzha̱a̱ naru Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n bwaa da̱ba ta̱biha̱na̱.>
<<Ga̱hin ma aya̱too Isiraaꞌila, ha̱nga ma mana̱nna mazama. Yeesu butu naa Naazare, butu naa Uhwe̱n bwa tabisa̱a̱ ma ta̱hyan bushi naa ta̱hiku, paaku iri na ta̱pa rukwanyan na̱ iri na ta̱jikita̱na̱ na̱ iri na ta̱kai na bwa tashana, Yeesu be̱ ndagi. Hyo̱ iri tandaga na̱ nꞌsuyishe suniinhin ga̱hin yan.
Butu na̱nna naa aba tapana kuga̱hin haruwa na Hwe̱n bwa tahoo sha̱a̱ unii nda ta. Ga̱hin na̱ awyatu na ga̱a̱ci pinsan ana we̱ ga̱hin ta kaba be̱ na̱ guguji, ga̱hin kwane̱ be̱.
Ama Uhwe̱n tahiika̱hina̱ be̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱ bwa ya̱a̱cigi ngwan na ta̱ꞌwa̱, wana ta̱hyan bitangazana ta̱ꞌwa̱ ta̱ba a̱rici buu ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱.
Bugwama Dawuda tacita̱ mazama mande̱e̱be̱ bwa hin,
<< <Koya̱ hwe̱n ga̱n ta ndaya Butu O̱to̱ niimi,
buta naa na̱ nꞌkataga kaniimi, na hyan ga̱n jaa zha̱a̱nta̱na̱.
Na̱ wana kunnu ta bigata niimi be̱ ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ na tande̱,
ure̱ntun nimi bwaa zhinyan zha̱a̱ na ta̱ga̱da̱ri,
ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱niimi ta̱ba nii taa na̱ nꞌta̱sha̱a̱ bigata.
Na ta̱hyan bi-jaa gaa ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱niimi na uya̱,
koo gaa jaa gaa Buyata ndaabi naa ne̱e̱ Sabu xbuposhi.
Bi-nꞌga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni yo̱n na hyan uꞌnꞌye̱e̱ kuta̱nda bina̱,
ta̱naa ta̱ndaabi na̱ ga̱n ta̱ba na̱ma nꞌshaana ta̱ga̱da̱ri.> >>
<<Aya̱too ma Isiraaꞌila, nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ ma mazama mana̱nna bigata ka̱ ta̱hyan, adaada nda̱tu Dawuda taꞌwa̱ aba wuma̱ni wyan, bigunaa ndaaba be̱ tane̱e̱ hara̱ ba̱re.
Bwa tasha bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, bwa tayansun mazama nama Hwe̱n bwa tanda ala̱ka̱wa̱ri uja̱a̱ ndaaka bwa, hyo̱ nꞌta̱sa̱nsan ta̱hyan, uja̱a̱ riga̱ buka̱ kiikorogo ndaabwa ta̱gwama haruwa na bwa tariga̱ bugwama Dawuda.
Na Dawuda bwa tandaya iri na wuci iyeebe, bwa gura̱a̱ nda mazama nama ta̱hiika̱ nata̱ Ala̱masiihu kuta̱ꞌwa̱, ta̱hyan ajaa gaa be̱ na̱ aꞌuya̱, ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ ta̱ba jaa pwasa.
Hwe̱n tahiika̱hina̱ Yeesu yata kuta̱ꞌwa̱, hyo̱ nda̱tu ga̱tu shi ana nda̱i hiku, ga̱tu nii bisa̱ga̱ wyatu.
Hwe̱n sha̱pa̱cigi buu kukataga kandaabwa, be̱ gura̱a̱ raa Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n ku-Ashin kaba tahoo nda ala̱ka̱wa̱ri. Niina ta be̱ ta̱zóogi bibe̱e̱ Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n, bwa ta shi na̱nna na ga̱hin nda̱i ga̱hin hange̱.
Ai, shii Dawuda nꞌta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabwa takatana ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, ama bwa na̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa butahyan,
<< <Butu O̱to̱ tahyan Butu O̱to̱ niimi,
<<Hunrana nꞌkataga kaniimi,
sa̱i kunshaani awyatu naa ribici
gaa fo̱nje̱ wyan na̱ kokobi na buna ndaa.>> >
<<Na̱ wana kunnu, hyo̱ Aꞌisiraaꞌila xayansun ta̱hyan Yeesu yata na ga̱hin takaba na̱ guguji, Uhwe̱n pa̱ni be̱ bwa shi Butu O̱to̱ na̱ Ala̱masiihu.>>
Na awyatu aba hange̱ kunnu, mazama mꞌba a̱nta̱ni wyan na̱ nꞌgata, aba hin bwa na̱ ana be̱ tazwara, <<Aya̱too ma, mbata shi na hyan xta̱nnje̱?>>
Sa̱i Biituru bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Pana ma pinsan baa, aandaaki ma baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu na̱ wana hyan aba jamaa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ ma apinsan ninhin, ga̱hin nii gura̱a̱ da̱ba Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n ꞌye̱n.
Mana̱nna mazama nama Hwe̱n bwa tanda ala̱ka̱wa̱ri, mashi maniinhin huku na̱ mꞌmwaan niinhin, na̱ hyo̱ maa ana tane̱e̱ ta̱baa, na̱ hyo̱ ana Butu O̱to̱ nda̱a̱tu Hwe̱n bwa nꞌgani zhagu waabwa.>>
Sa̱i Biituru bwa gura̱a̱ duwa̱na̱ wyan ta̱bisa̱gi mazama nama bisa̱a̱ wyan ta̱hyan mashi nama ta̱hiku ma hwarapi na bwa a̱ra̱ga̱ni wyan, ta̱hyan, <<Ma biha̱ni ma kungwan na ne̱e̱ kuꞌawyatu ana niina, ana nii nda tuma yata na we̱.>>
Ana tarana mꞌba mazama nama Biituru aba ndaakaki wyan baba̱tiisa̱ma. Na̱ hwe̱n ya̱nu hwarapi na awyatu bwa duwa̱ni do̱ko̱ adubu taatu.
Aba duwa̱ni ta̱sha̱a̱ hyuhyu ki na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ ana Yeesu be̱ tazwara aba tanaa bisa̱ga̱ wyan, na̱ nꞌta̱naawan huku ma re̱ shami da̱nda̱ na̱ ro̱pe̱.
Hunranhunran na ana jwarigi kubwa shi
Sa̱i rukwanyan ruba kota̱ni wyan hyo̱, na Hwe̱n bwa tashana ana be̱ tazwara, abaa nda iri na rukwanyan na̱ nꞌta̱jikita̱na̱.
Hyo̱ ana tapana nꞌgata nꞌndaaba aba naawan da̱nda̱ manda tuma na̱ iri na aba mꞌbaa hyo̱ da̱nda̱.
Aba sa̱a̱nha̱nii iri na aba mꞌbaagi, aba hoosa̱ga̱gi aba pa̱ga̱ni koo buya̱ haruwa na nii nda be̱.
Koya̱ hwe̱n ata̱ni bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n na̱ nꞌgata nꞌka̱, ma re̱ shami da̱nda̱ na̱ nꞌina nꞌndaaba na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱da̱ri na̱ nꞌgata fo̱n,
ma yaba Hwe̱n, awyatu aba gura̱a̱ raa wyan hyo̱. Koya̱ hwe̱n Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n ta duwa̱na̱ wyan ana de̱be̱ ta̱biha̱na̱.

Biituru kuda̱gahini gurubi na roko
Uyaan hwe̱n Biituru na̱ Yoohana aba ne̱e̱ na̱ zhagu Ina na Hwe̱n na Ayaahudiya na hyan anje̱ ro̱pe̱ una ta̱ruma ta̱taatu na̱ hwe̱n.
Kuuyaan butu naa aba tamantan gurubi, aba shápi bwa na̱ adubo ana ba ta hyan Adubo na Rushama. Koya̱ hwe̱n ata shapa be̱ ashii be̱ na dubo yata na Ina na Hwe̱n na hyan bunaa rupa ana nii ta̱na̱a̱ yuwa.
Na bwa nda̱i Biituru na̱ Yoohana ma ta̱na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n, bwa ro̱pe̱ wyan ayuwa.
Biituru bwa gwatagi be̱ ki, kunnu taa Yoohana. Biituru bwa hin be̱, <<Ta̱gwataga!>>
Hyo̱ aha̱nka̱ri ndaabwa aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱ waaba ta̱hyan anii pana be̱ yaan ri.
Too, sa̱i Biituru bwa hin, <<Ayuwa ta ga̱n za, ama iri na ga̱n mꞌbaa ta ga̱n na̱maa pana. Na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu na Naazare, nda ta̱hani!>>
Sa̱i Biituru bwa kota̱ni be̱ ara kataga bwa sha̱pa̱cigi be̱. Kupita mꞌbuna na̱ nꞌun nami mꞌbuna nꞌndaabwa mꞌba nje̱ ka̱i.
Bwa hin kaki, bwa e̱she̱, bwa ke̱ne̱ ta̱hani, bwa hurogo tunu bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n da̱nda̱ na̱ aba. Ma nda ta̱hani ma guba̱ga̱ ma yaba Hwe̱n.
Hyo̱ awyatu aba nda̱i bwa ma nda ta̱hani, ba hange̱ bwa ma yaba Hwe̱n.
Aba e̱nshe̱n ta̱hyan bwa ta tanaa koya̱ hwe̱n na̱ Adubo na Rushama, bunaa rupa wyatu. Sa̱i aba jikita̱ni, aba nje̱ kuma̱ na̱ wana iri na nje̱ na̱a̱ bwa.
Mazama nama Biituru na̱ bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n
Ta bwa gurubi ma ha̱mba̱ga̱ Biituru na̱ Yoohana, awyatu ba gída̱ga̱gi zhagu waaba paa Ina na Hwe̱n na aba ta nꞌgana Shiraaye na Suleemaanu, aba nje̱ kuma̱ wana iri na rukwanyan na nje̱.
Na Biituru bwa nda̱i kunta, bwa hin wyan, <<Ga̱hin ma aya̱too Isiraaꞌila, iba̱ shani ina̱nna be̱e̱ shaani ma ta̱jikita̱na̱? Iba̱ shani ga̱hin ta̱gwataagi haku ta̱kai ta̱nda̱a̱tu ta̱ta, koo wana ta̱hyan ta̱huri koo buya̱ ta̱jwara̱ga Hwe̱n ta shani butu na̱nna bwa nje̱ ta̱hani?
Uhwe̱n na Ibiraahin na̱ Isiyaaku na̱ Yaakubu, Uhwe̱n na adaadoo nda̱tu ta sha̱pa̱cigi bugyama ndaabwa Yeesu. Bwa taa shi buyata naa ga̱hin tapana, ga̱hin ga̱a̱ be̱ na̱ aꞌuba̱ na gwamina Bilaatu, hyo̱ na ta̱hyan maa Bilaatu taruba̱ ta̱tazhigana be̱.
Ama ga̱hin ga̱a̱ Buyata bunaa ne̱e̱ Sabu bunaa Bina̱, ga̱hin hin xaata̱zhiga̱a̱gi ma kuunaa nii kunaa awyatu.
Ga̱hin kwane̱ naa shi hyuhyu na ta̱biha̱na̱, ama Hwe̱n bwa tahiika̱hina̱ bwa kuta̱ꞌwa̱, ga̱tu taa shi ana ta ndaya ri ya̱nu nꞌsuyishe sunda̱a̱tu.
<<Inda̱i butu na̱nna naa ga̱hin tayansun kuubwa tasha gurubi na̱ ayigo. Na̱ wana ta̱panaa gata na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ Yeesu ta̱ta bwa nje̱ kai. Na ta̱hyan ta̱panaa gata ta̱ndaabwa na̱ Yeesu ta̱ta ta̱shaani hyo̱ ta̱kuda̱ga ta̱na̱nna na uba̱ ninhin na̱ nꞌsuyishe suniinhin hyo̱.
<<Too, aya̱too ma, nꞌyan itanda na̱nna na̱ nꞌta̱yancin ta, kuharuwa na awyatu o̱to̱ ninhin ba tanda taa.
Ama na̱ kunta ta Uhwe̱n bwa ciga̱hini ta̱cita̱ nata̱ bwa tacita̱ kacita̱a̱ga̱ wuun mazama, ta̱hyan Ala̱masiihu ndaabwa nii swa ta̱guma.
Na̱ kunnu pana ma pinsan baa, ikíciike̱ ku-Hwe̱n na hyan aaya̱a̱cigi ma pinsan ninhin, Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n bwa nii hiriga nꞌgata nꞌniinhin,
bunii gura̱a̱ káji Ala̱masiihu na shi Yeesu na bwa tahoo maa kaasa ma ta na̱ ayigo.
Ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ ashii be̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, kuha̱ni na Hwe̱n bwa nii hiriga komba̱ri ishi na fo, haruwa na bwa tanda ala̱ka̱wa̱ri ta na̱ ayigo kana tanaa cita̱a̱ga̱ wuun mazama andaabwa ana ne̱e̱ sabu.
Na ta̱hyan Muusa tahyan, <Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n ninhin bunii káji bunaa nii naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama bubáni kiikorogo niinhin haruwa na bwa nꞌkáji ga̱mi, ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ ishiraaga hyo̱ iri na bwa na̱maa bisa̱ ma.
Una̱maa sha ma hyo̱ bunaa shiragici iri na bwaa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama bwaa cita̱ga̱, anii ba̱ha̱na̱ be̱ mahwa kaya̱na̱ba.>
<<Kunnu taa hyo̱ ana ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ana tapasa ku-Samaaꞌila na̱ ana ta jaa ta̱baa, tacita̱ga̱ mazama nama nꞌhwe̱n yana.
Ga̱hin taa shi mꞌmwaan na nꞌaba cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, mayaan ga̱hin shi ana hyo̱ ta̱masha̱a̱ga̱ nata̱ Hwe̱n bwa tanda na̱ adaadoo ninhin. Na ta̱hyan Uhwe̱n tahyan Ibiraahin, <Na̱ mꞌmwaan na mꞌbiikorogo ndaabi ta hyo̱ nꞌkorogo na nꞌsa̱ra̱ri yana mꞌba ja̱a̱ da̱ba rubara̱ka.>
Na Hwe̱n bwa ka̱shi bugyama ndaabwa Yeesu, butakáji be̱ kwan kuga̱hin awyatu na Isiraaꞌila, na hyan busha̱a̱gi ma rubara̱ka naru koo buya̱ bwaa kíciike̱ buga̱a̱ yo̱n ndaabwa na ambyau.>>

Biituru na̱ Yoohana na̱ aꞌuba̱ na awyatu na ta ꞌyapa mazama
Na̱ ha̱ni na Biituru na̱ Yoohana aba tanaa nda mazama na̱ awyatu, sa̱i ayaan apirisiti huku na̱ butu o̱to̱ naa ta ha̱mba Ina na Hwe̱n na̱ Asaduukiya aba jábani wyan.
Aba gware̱ me̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ wana Biituru na̱ Yoohana nii ga̱gaagana awyatu ma cita̱ga̱ ta̱hyan ana ꞌwa̱gi nii hiika̱ka̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱ haruwa na Yeesu be̱ tahiika̱.
Aba kota̱ni wyan, aba zwa̱ga̱ni wyan na̱ zhaaro sa̱i na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, wana iri tasha shurugo.
Ama awyatu hwarapi na ta ha̱nga mꞌba mazama aba pa̱ni nꞌgata nꞌndaaba. Uhwarapi na wyatu wya̱ri na pa̱ni nꞌgata bwa duwa̱ni awyatu dubu ta.
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, awyatu o̱to̱ na Ina na Hwe̱n na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na ce̱nye̱n na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa aba mawuna̱ni na̱ Hurushaliima.
Hanasu, butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti, bwa tanaa huku na̱ Kayaapa na̱ Yoohana na̱ Aleka̱zanda na̱ ayaan ana shi udiin na butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti.
Aba shápi Biituru na̱ Yoohana aba shii wyan na wyantancin, abaa hantaana wyan ta̱hyan, <<Na̱ nꞌta̱ya̱ ta̱kai ta̱ta koo na̱ nꞌruya̱ ruzha̱a̱ ruta ga̱hin nda na̱nna?>>
Too, ta̱kai nata̱ Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n ta̱ba ne̱e̱ huku na̱ Biituru, bwa hin, <<Ga̱hin awyatu o̱to̱ nda̱tu na ce̱nye̱n,
ba̱re inii ta̱hantaana ta na̱ wana iri na gama na ga̱tu ndaaki gurubi na̱nna? Ga̱hin gura̱a̱ ruba̱ ta̱yansun na bwa nje̱ bwa kwade̱ge̱?
Too, nꞌribi na hyan iyansun ga̱hin hyo̱ na̱ awyatu na Isiraaꞌila ta̱hyan, na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu butu naa Naazare ta shani butu na̱nna naa e̱she̱ na̱ uba̱ ninhin bwa kwade̱ge̱. Bwa taa shi buyata naa ga̱hin takaba, bunaa Hwe̱n bwa tahiika̱hina̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱.
Yeesu na̱nna tashi
<< <Utari una ga̱hin awyatu na ta̱ma aba hwashe̱ ta̱hyan uza bina̱,
ubwa ta shi na hura̱gi hyo̱ bina̱ kuta̱ma.>
Buyaan buza naa huri Yeesu naa nii ara ta̱shana ta̱nda bina̱, na ta̱hyan ruyaan ruzha̱a̱ ruza naru huri be̱ na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana hyo̱, na hyan kaꞌnꞌgani ruun butu de̱be̱ ta̱biha̱na̱.>>
Too, na aba wyatu o̱to̱ ba nda̱i Biituru na̱ Yoohana ta̱ kiigata macimi, aba gura̱a̱ insan ta̱hyan ashi aꞌwa̱ta̱gi ana za ta̱yansun, aba jikita̱ni. Aba e̱nshe̱n ta̱hyan ashi ana tamatuba̱ na̱ Yeesu.
Ama na aba wyatu o̱to̱ na Ina na Hwe̱n aba nda̱i bwa butu naa aba kuda̱gahini maꞌisagwa na̱ aba, aba za iri na hyan ahin.
Aba hin wyan xaba̱ni paaka aba ne̱e̱, aba maga̱ga̱a̱gi kaba kaba.
Aba hin, <<Iba̱ ga̱tu nii nda na̱ awyatu na̱nna? Hyo̱ awyatu na Hurushaliima ayan ta̱hyan, awyatu na̱nna anje̱ iri na ta̱jikita̱na̱ na yaburi, ga̱tu za haruwa na ga̱tu hyan, <Ishici kunnu.>
Ama na hyan mꞌba mazama mꞌba jaa naa maduwa̱na̱ ta̱mawyasa kope kawyatu, xta̱yinzha̱nkani wyan ta̱yanshin wyan, ta̱hyan xata gura̱a̱ ndaaka yaan mazama na̱ nꞌruzha̱a̱ ruya̱nu.>>
Sa̱i aba nꞌgani aba reeko, aba kooci wyan ta̱hyan xata gura̱a̱ duwa̱na̱ ta̱nda mazama nama Yeesu koo ta̱ga̱gaagana buyaan.
Ama Biituru na̱ Yoohana aba ra̱ni wyan ta̱hyan, <<Too, inda̱i ta̱hyan na̱ aꞌuba̱ na Hwe̱n uhuri gama ta̱huri ta̱tuba̱ mazama maniinhin na̱ nama Hwe̱n?
Ga̱tu jaa ara ta̱gaa ta̱cita̱ iri na ga̱tu nda̱i ga̱tu hange̱.>>
Na wyatu o̱to̱ aba duwa̱ni wyan ta̱koota̱ga̱ ce̱be̱, aba ta̱zhiga̱ni wyan, na̱ wana ayancin haruwa na hyan apa̱ wyan ngwan, na ta̱hyan hyo̱ awyatu nii yaba Hwe̱n na̱ wana iri na ta̱jikita̱na̱ na nje̱.
Na ta̱hyan awyatu yan ta̱hyan Uhwe̱n tashi naa nii ara ta̱kuda̱gahina butu na̱nna naa huri nꞌyo̱ handa na̱ nꞌta̱mantan.
Ana pa̱ni nꞌgata ro̱pe̱ Hwe̱n
Na aba ta̱zhiga̱ni Biituru na̱ Yoohana aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱ kaya̱na̱ba, aba bisa̱gi wyan hyo̱ iri na apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na ce̱nye̱n aba bísa̱gi wyan.
Na aba hange̱ kunnu hyo̱ ndaaba aba hiika̱hini sunu na̱ nꞌgata nꞌka̱ ku-Hwe̱n, aba hin, <<Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n na hura̱gi ta̱kai ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa hyo̱, gaa taa shi naa nje̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ na̱ rwaga na o̱to̱ na̱ hyo̱ iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ ndaaba.
Nii Hwaanwun ndaabi gaa njé̱e̱ mazama na̱ nu naa gyama ndaabi adaada nda̱tu bugwama Dawuda, gaa hin,
<< <Na̱ wana ba̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya aba gware̱ sume̱?
Nꞌkorogo upwa na̱ nꞌree na n-Isiraaꞌila mꞌba gura̱a̱ sha̱a̱ nꞌgata na̱ ri na uwa̱?
Nꞌgwama na nꞌsa̱ra̱ri yana nꞌnje̱ shiri na gagu,
awyatu o̱to̱ na ce̱nye̱n aba maꞌunpin,
aba ga̱a̱ Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n
na̱ Ala̱masiihu ndaabwa.> >>
<<Na ta̱hyan hina na̱ ce̱pe̱ na o̱to̱, Hirudu Antipasi na̱ Buntu Bilaatu amaꞌunpin suhyu sundaaba na̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya, na̱ awyatu na Isiraaꞌila, aba ribici mahwa ta̱ndaya Yeesu bugyama ndaabi naa ne̱e̱ sabu, bunaa gaa takasa.
Aba mawuna̱ni na hyan anje̱ ri na gaa tahoo sha̱a̱ gaa hakaci xinje̱ nꞌta̱ruba̱ ta̱ndaabi.
<<Too, niina Butu O̱to̱, gwatana kaba ribi ata̱ yanshin tuma ta̱naa nda. Ta̱pa ga̱tu agyama ndaa ta̱kai nata̱a̱ gata naa ta̱cita̱ mazama mandaabi ga̱tu jaa shiraga rukwanyan.
Cikaa ara ndaa na ta̱kuda̱gahina wyatu. Iri na ta̱jikita̱na̱ na̱ iri na ta̱pa rukwanyan xinje̱ na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱a̱ gyamaa ndaabi Yeesu naru ne̱e̱ sabu.>>
Na aba hwii ro̱pe̱ ta̱nda, paaka aba tamawuna̱na̱ kaba zha̱a̱nta̱ni. Sa̱i Uhwe̱n bwa ciga̱hini wyan hyo̱ ndaaba nii Hwaanwun ndaabwa, aba ke̱ne̱ ta̱cita̱ga̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n rukwanyan ruba za.
Awyatu na pa̱ni nꞌgata hoosa̱ga̱gi iri na aba mꞌbaagi
Too, hyo̱ awyatu na pa̱ni nꞌgata na̱ Yeesu aba ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌgata nꞌndaaba nꞌka̱, mazama mandaaba maka̱, ba zaa na hin iri na bwa mꞌbaa shi ndaabwa bwaa ka̱, aba hoosa̱ga̱gi hyo̱ iri na aba mꞌbaagi da̱nda̱.
Ana be̱ tazwara aba cici hiku na̱ kai ta̱hyan Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu hiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱. Ta̱pana ꞌye̱n nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ba ne̱e̱ na̱a̱ koo buya̱ o̱to̱ hyo̱ ndaaba.
Hyo̱ aba zaa naa mꞌbaaci yaanyini, na̱ wana ana mꞌbaagi nꞌcima na̱ nꞌina anii sáanhinai,
abaa iyagi aba yuwa kana Yeesu be̱ tazwara. Aba pa̱ga̱ni koo buya̱ haruwa na gii be̱.
Buyaan bunaa aba ta nꞌgana Yusufu bwa ne̱e̱, butu na biikorogo naa Laawi, bunaa ne̱e̱ na̱ ucibiri na Kuburusu, bunaa ana Yeesu be̱ tazwara aba ta naa nꞌga Bara̱naba (na shi baa bunaa ta duwa̱na̱ bigata shita̱ ta̱ta).
Kunnu taa bwa sáanhine̱ cima ndaabwa, bwa íye̱ aba yuwa kana Yeesu be̱ tazwara.

Hanaaninyan na̱ Safiiratu ꞌwi na̱ wana pira̱
Ama buyaan butu Hanaaninyan, huku na̱ aꞌa̱yo Safiiratu, butasa̱a̱nhina̱ cima na̱ ꞌwaa ndaabwa.
Na̱ nꞌta̱yansun nata̱ aꞌa̱yo bwa ta macina̱na̱ ayuwa, bwa sha̱pi kuhamba bwa ꞌye̱e̱ paaka na Yeesu be̱ tazwara, ta̱hyan aba ta hyo̱.
Sa̱i Biituru bwa hin, <<Gaa Hanaaninyan, na ta gaa hakaci Shatan bwa ta̱ni bigata ndaabi na gaa ndaaki Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n ta̱be̱? Gaa mashá̱a̱gi ayuwa ka̱ na gaa sáanhine̱ bwa cima.
Ta gaa sa̱a̱nhinu uta shici ndaa nuu? Na gaa sa̱a̱nha̱ni undaa ta bwa tashi, ataa hincin ga̱ga̱ga̱ pana. Na ta gaa gaa nje̱ na̱nna ri nii gata ndaabi? Shii kubutu ta bwaa ka̱ gaa ndaaki ta̱be̱, Uhwe̱n ta.>>
Hanaaninyan maha̱nga maya̱nu mazama, kupita bwa ꞌwi isa isa, bwa kinai. Awyatu hyo̱ na taha̱nga mꞌba mazama rukwanyan ruba kota̱ni wyan ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Asa̱mba̱ri aba hiiki aba rigi bwa na̱ zuzu, aba ba̱ha̱ni bwa, aba wuma̱ni.
Na uha̱ni bwa huri suꞌaꞌawa taatu, aꞌa̱yo ba tá̱ni aba yancin mbata nje̱.
Sa̱i Biituru bwa ha̱nta̱ni aba a̱yo bwa hin, <<Mꞌbishi, na̱nna tashi haruwa na gaa na̱ awya̱rubo ga̱hin tasáanhine̱ ubwa cima?>>
Aꞌa̱yo aba ra̱ni ba hin, <<Ee, kunta ta ba tane̱e̱.>>
Biituru bwa hin, <<Na ga̱hin yibaku suhyu suniinhin na̱ awya̱rubo ga̱hin ma̱a̱nwya̱ni Bihwaanwun naa Butu O̱to̱? Ha̱nga ta̱ha̱ni nata̱ awyatu na wuma̱ni awya̱rubo nu na dubo, gaa taa anii bana na̱ nꞌruꞌwa̱ rundaabi niina.>>
Kupita na̱ aꞌuba̱ ndaabwa bwaa a̱ bwa ꞌwi isa isa bwa kinai. Na aba sa̱mba̱ri ba ta̱ni ba wuta̱ni bwaa a̱ taa bwa hoo ꞌwa̱, aba sha̱pi bwa aba ba̱ha̱ni be̱, aba wuma̱ni be̱ nii biin binaa aba tawuma̱ni wya̱rugo.
Sa̱i rukwanyan ruba kota̱ni ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ hyo̱ awyatu na Yeesu na̱ hyo̱ ana hange̱ mꞌba mazama.
Ana Yeesu be̱ tazwara kuda̱gahinai awyatu hwarapi
Too, ana Yeesu be̱ tazwara ndagi iri hwarapi na ta̱jikita̱na̱ nꞌta pa rukwanyan na̱ aꞌuba̱ na awyatu. Hyo̱ ana pa̱ni nꞌgata ata mawuna̱na̱ na̱ Shiraaye na Suleemaanu na̱ bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n.
Awyatu na bwe̱ aba zaa naa ta̱a̱ gata macimi na hyan ashi ri ka̱ na̱ aba, hyo̱ na̱ kunnu abaa paga wyan zha̱munkun.
Hyo̱ na̱ kunnu awyatu ana pa̱ni nꞌgata na̱ Yeesu, uhwarapi na awyatu wya̱ri na a̱ bwaa duwa̱na̱ kuta̱duwa̱na̱.
Mꞌba wuci na awyatu abaa báhinai ana ha̱ngagici sa̱ na yo̱n yo̱n yo̱n ma baragana wyan wyansun na̱ ba̱ra̱shina̱, na ta̱hyan jaa Biituru bwaa hura̱ koo uhurukutu ndaabwa, ujaa hwaamaa aka̱ ndaaba akuda̱gagi
Awyatu hwarapi baa wuce kuta̱wuce kuꞌnꞌcice̱pe̱ na nꞌne̱e̱ riinha̱nu na̱ Hurushaliima, maꞌiyagi ana ha̱ngagici sa̱ na̱ ana nꞌhwaanwun na nꞌwe̱ mꞌbaa pa ngwan. Hyo̱ ndaaba aba kuda̱gahinai wyan.
Awyatu na Ayaahudiya pa̱ ana Yeesu be̱ tazwara ngwan
Sa̱i butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti nii gudu ndaabwa ana shi Asaduukiya, aba gware̱ sume̱, aba ribici iri na ana be̱ tazwara baa nda mahwa.
Aba kota̱ga̱ni ana be̱ tazwara, aba zwa̱ga̱ga̱ni wyan na̱ zhaaro.
Kuuyaan butuma naa Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n bwa jaa na̱ gita bwa guna̱a̱nyin wyan adubo, bwa báhine̱ wyan, bwa hin,
<<Jaga ma ija̱a̱ iꞌisa na̱ bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n, ibishi awyatu mazama nama ta̱biha̱na̱ nata̱ fo ta̱na̱nna.>>
Na̱ kasu na shiri kaba tabísa̱gi wyan, aba ta̱ni bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n, aba ke̱ne̱ ta̱ga̱gaagana awyatu.
Na butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti nii gudu ndaabwa aba mawuna̱ni, aba nꞌgani hyo̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na Isiraaꞌila ana ta ꞌyapa mazama aba ka̱ji zhagu zhaaro xashápi ana Yeesu be̱ tazwara.
Na ana ba ta kada aba ja̱a̱ aba nda̱ci koo butu, aba kúshiike̱, aba bishi wyan aba hin,
<<Ta̱tawuci ga̱tu wuta̱ni adubo na zhaaro guna̱ni mgbai, ana ta ha̱mba aba hambe̱ na dubo. Na ga̱tu gunii, ga̱tu nda̱ci koo buyaan na̱ ame̱.>>
Na butu o̱to̱ naa ta ha̱mba Ina na Hwe̱n na̱ apirisiti na o̱to̱ aba hange̱ mazama mꞌba, nꞌgata mꞌba ta̱ wyan buga̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, mꞌba kaki wyan na̱ nꞌgata ta̱hyan na ta mꞌba nii sha.
Sa̱i buyaan bubwa wuce kaun bwa hin wyan, <<Ai, awyatu ana ga̱hin tazwágani na̱ zhaaro aba ree isagi na̱ bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n ma ga̱gaagana awyatu.>>
Sa̱i bwa butu o̱to̱ naa ta ha̱mba Ina na Hwe̱n na̱ awyatu na tuma ndaabwa aba hin kunrun kaki aba ja̱a̱ aba kóta̱ni aba na Yeesu be̱ tazwara. Ama shii na̱ kai, na̱ wana ashiragi rukwanyan naru awyatu xata gyasa wyan atari.
Na aba íye̱ aba na be̱ tazwara, aba e̱she̱ na̱ awyantancin na wyatu o̱to̱ na ta ꞌyapa mazama. Sa̱i butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti bwa ha̱nta̱ni wyan,
bwa hin, <<Ta̱taa bishici ma hiku ta̱hyan ta-duwa̱na̱ ma yaan ta̱ga̱gaagana na̱ nꞌruzha̱a̱ ruya̱nu? Nde̱e̱ ta ga̱hin hwii ta̱ciga̱hina̱ Hurushaliima hyo̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱niinhin, hara̱ ta ga̱hin hiin ta̱shana ruhaki naru mahiin nama butu na̱nna.>>
Ama Biituru na̱ ayaan ana be̱ tazwara ba ra̱ni ba hin, <<Ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ ta̱jwara̱ga Hwe̱n na hyan ta̱jwara̱ga nama wyatu wuma.
Uhwe̱n na adaadoo nda̱tu tahiika̱hina̱ Yeesu kuta̱ꞌwa̱, bunaa ga̱hin takuna na̱ nꞌta̱swatana na̱ guguji na ꞌwe̱e̱.
Bwa taa shi naa Hwe̱n bwa sha̱pa̱cigi, bwa shii bwa nꞌkataga kandaabwa, bwa shi butu o̱to̱ na̱a̱ naa ta̱biha̱na̱. Na hyan buguna̱a̱nyin Aꞌisiraaꞌila yo̱n na ta̱pana pinsan baa, Hwe̱n bwa jaa gura̱a̱ ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ wyan apinsan ndaaba.
Ga̱tu taa shi ana nda̱i ri ya̱nu suyishe sunda̱a̱tu, kunnu taa Bihwaanwun naa Uhwe̱n bwa pa̱ni ana jwarigi aba cina̱ni wuun.>>
Na aba wyatu o̱to̱ aba hange̱ kunnu aba gware̱ sume̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, ba ribi maa kakunai ana be̱ tazwara.
Ama buyaan Bufaraasiya bunaa aba ta nꞌgana Gamaaliye, bunaa ne̱e̱ huku na̱ aba biwya̱ra̱mi naa Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa, bunaa hyo̱ awyatu aba huri ta̱cina̱na̱. Bwa hiiki kaba wyatu o̱to̱ na tamawuna̱na̱ bwa bishi wyan ta̱hyan xaba wyatu ba̱ni kwan ha.
Naazhin bwa hin aba wyatu o̱to̱, <<Ga̱hin aya̱too ma Aꞌisiraaꞌila, gwatana ma kwan ki inda̱i iri na ga̱hin hiin ndaaka awyatu na̱nna.
Nꞌyo̱ na nꞌhuri buyaan butajaa naa aba tahin sa̱ Tuudasa, bwa sha̱pi hyuhyu ndaabwa bwaa shi yaanyini. Awyatu do̱ko̱ nꞌyina̱ nꞌna̱nshin (400) tajwara̱ga bwa, ayaan aba kwane̱ bwa, awyatu ndaabwa aba ga̱ta̱a̱gi hyo̱, mandaaba mꞌba hwii.
Buyaan bubwa gura̱a̱ báni bunaa ba ta hyan Yaahuda butu naa báni kuta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Gaalili, na̱ ha̱ni na ta̱ruba, bwa ma̱ni aha̱nka̱ri na awyatu aba jwarigi bwa. Bwa taamaa ayaan aba kwane̱ bwa, awyatu ndaabwa ba ga̱ta̱a̱gi.
Too, niina maa nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma ta̱hyan, yaaciga ma ara ninhin na̱ mꞌmazama nama awyatu yata, hakata ma wyan. Kushi ri na ba shii ta̱nda, koo tuma ndaaba, ushi na butu wuma ta, unii gataaga.
Ama kushi na Hwe̱n ta, ijaa ara wyan ta̱gata. Ta-sha ma awyatu na nii nda gagu na̱ Hwe̱n.>>
Aba wyatu o̱to̱ ba ra̱ni mazama mandaabwa. Aba nꞌgani aba ana be̱ tazwara, aba hin xazuragi wyan duun. Aba kooci wyan ta̱hyan xata naa ga̱gaagana wyatu mazama nama Yeesu, naazhin aba ta̱zhiga̱ni wyan.
Aba na be̱ tazwara ba hiiki na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱da̱ri na̱ wana ta̱hyan anda̱i agii na hyan are̱ nꞌkogi, ahusani wyan na̱ wana ajwarigi Yeesu.
Koya̱ hwe̱n na̱ bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n, na̱ nꞌina ina na nꞌndaaba, aba ga̱a̱ci ta̱naa ga̱gaagana na̱ nꞌta̱bisa̱ga̱ awyatu mazama nama zumaa, ta̱hyan Yeesu tashi Ala̱masiihu.

Aka̱shi awyatu ta̱nda̱ra̱ ana hooso
Na hwarapi na awyatu na jwarigi baa duwa̱na̱ kuta̱duwa̱na̱, Ayaahudiya ana jwarigi aba tibi Ta̱helena aba pa̱shi nꞌduunrin ka-Ayaahudiya ana jwarigi aba tibi Ta̱ꞌibiraaniya. Na ta̱hyan anda̱i ata haasana aꞌa̱ ndaaba ana suwya̱rugooba suba ꞌwa̱gi paa hooso na shami na koya̱ hwe̱n.
Sa̱i aba upwa na ree na Yeesu be̱ tazwara aba nꞌgani hyo̱ wyatu ana jwarigi, xamawuna̱ni, ba hin wyan, <<Ga̱tu, xta̱nshii uha̱ni nda̱tu paaku ta̱ga̱gaagana na̱ nꞌta̱cita̱ga̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n, shii kupaa hooso na shami.
Na̱ kunnu aya̱too ma, kasa ma awyatu ta̱nda̱ra̱ ana mꞌbaa aha̱nka̱ri ana ne̱e̱ nii Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n na̱ nꞌta̱yansun, ta̱mpa̱ni wyan ubwa tuma.
Ga̱tu ta̱manta̱a̱ na̱ ro̱pe̱ ta̱naa nda na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana, na̱ nꞌta̱bisa̱ga̱ wyatu mazama nama Hwe̱n.>>
Hyo̱ awyatu aba hange̱ gama na mazama nama aba cici. Azha̱a̱zha̱a̱ na ana aba takasa na:
Isitafanu, butu naa mꞌbaa ta̱kai nata̱a̱ Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n, bwa mꞌbaa bigata ta̱pana o̱to̱
na̱ Filibu,
na̱ Burokoorasa,
na̱ Nikano,
na̱ Tiimo,
na̱ Bara̱mina,
na̱ Nikola, butu naa Antiyaakiya bunaa tata̱na̱ Ta̱yaahudiya, bwa jwarigi Yeesu.
Aba shápi aba wyatu aba bisa̱a̱ wyan kana be̱ tazwara, aba sha̱a̱gi wyan nꞌara na nꞌrubara̱ka ma ndaaka wyan ro̱pe̱.
Mazama nama zumaa nama Hwe̱n mꞌbaa mawya̱shi kope. Uhwarapi na ana jwarigi bwa duwa̱na̱ kuta̱duwa̱na̱ na̱ Hurushaliima. Apirisiti ahwarapi aba ra̱a̱ ta̱ba ta̱panaa gata na̱ nꞌta̱jwara̱ga.
Akota̱ni Isitafanu
Too, Isitafanu butu naa mꞌbaa ta̱kai nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, bwaa ndaga iri na ta̱jikita̱na̱ na yaburagi na̱ aꞌuba̱ na wyatu.
Sa̱i ayaan ana ka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya ana ba tahyan Ka̱ta̱ku na Ana Ba̱ni Ta̱gyama, abaa maga̱a̱ga̱nu na̱ Isitafanu. Aba tasha Ayaahudiya ana Kuraane na̱ Alekazandiriya, na̱ ayaan ana ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Kilikiya, na̱ ana Aasiya.
Ama aba za naa a̱ri be̱ ta̱re̱e̱hina na̱ nꞌta̱maga̱a̱ga̱nu na̱a̱ bwa, na̱ wana bunii nda mazama na̱ nꞌta̱yansun nata̱a̱ Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n.
Sa̱i aba nda̱i ayaan ta̱swee aba hurupa̱ga̱ni wyan ce̱be̱ ta̱hyan xanje̱ ta̱be̱ ahin, <<Ta̱hange̱ bunii cwaaga Muusa, bwaa gura̱a̱ ndaakaka Hwe̱n mazama nama hwashe̱.>>
Na̱ kunnu aba hiika̱hini nꞌgata na nꞌawyatu, na̱ wyatu o̱to̱ na ce̱nye̱n, na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin. Aba hiika̱ni bwa, aba kota̱ni bwa, aba ꞌye̱e̱ bwa kawyatu o̱to̱ nata̱ ꞌyapa mazama.
Sa̱i ana aba tahin xanje̱ ta̱be̱, aba hin, <<Butu na̱nna koya̱ ha̱ni buta naa nda mazama nama uwa̱ nama Ina na Hwe̱n na ta̱sabu na̱ Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n bwa tapana Muusa.
Ta̱hange̱ bwa bunii hyaan, Yeesu yata na Naazare nii huza̱a̱ga̱ pa̱ri kayana, bigura̱a̱ ta̱hira̱ga nꞌgira̱nshin nda̱a̱tu na n-Muusa bwa tata̱gaaga.>>
Hyo̱ ana tanaa piree paaka wyatu ba tamawuna̱na̱ aba zooni bwa suyishe na̱ wana anda̱i apusa̱ka ndaabwa ane̱e̱ hanyan hanyan haka naa butuma naa Hwe̱n.

Mazama nama Isitafanu bwa tanda
Sa̱i butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti bwa ha̱nta̱ni Isitafanu ta̱hyan, <<Kunnu mazama maya̱nu mꞌba shi?>>
Iri na Isitafanu bwa tarana na, <<Ga̱hin aya̱too ma na̱ abaaboo nimi, nꞌshiraga ma. Uhwe̱n na huri ta̱shapaciga tabisa̱a̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa kuꞌadaada nda̱tu Ibiraahin ha̱ni na bwa tanaa na̱ ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Mesopotaaminyan, ta bwa hunro̱no̱ na̱ ce̱pe̱ na Harana.
Hwe̱n bwa hin buu, <Gaa ce̱nye̱n ta̱ndaabi na̱ awyatu ndaa, uhuri kuce̱nye̱n nata̱ ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱a̱.>
Sa̱i adaada nda̱tu aba ga̱a̱ ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Akaladiya, aba ja̱a̱ aba hunrani na̱ Harana. Na ashin aba ꞌwi, Hwe̱n bwa ꞌye̱e̱ aba daada nda̱tu ce̱nye̱n ta̱na̱nna nata̱ ga̱hin hunrani nꞌta̱ba niina.
Hwe̱n ta pa̱ncin bwa xbuhya̱su ce̱nye̱n ta̱yana, koo ta̱funda buna maka̱. Ibiraahin bwa ta taza mꞌmwaan na̱ bwa ha̱ni. Sa̱i ubwa ndaaki be̱ ala̱ka̱wa̱ri ta̱hyan unii shana ta̱ba ce̱nye̱n ta̱shi ta̱ndaabwa na̱ mꞌmwaan nꞌndaabwa na̱ nꞌwuci ta̱baa.
Hwe̱n bwa gura̱a̱ bisa̱ buu ta̱hyan, <Awyatu ndaa ana wuci ta̱baa aja̱a̱ hunrana nꞌta̱yaan ce̱nye̱n na ta̱shici ta̱ndaaba, aba ja̱a̱ sha agyama, ma pa wyan ngwan nꞌyo̱ nꞌyina̱ nꞌna̱nshin (400).
Nꞌja̱a̱ ndaaka awyatu na ta̱ba ce̱nye̱n ta̱suuga̱ ana ba̱ha̱ni wyan agyama. Mꞌba mꞌmwaan niimi nii báni, agáa ta̱ba ce̱nye̱n ajaa ana ma nꞌndaaka tuma na ta̱pa hunrun na̱ pa̱ri kayana.>
<<Hwe̱n bwa pa̱ni Ibiraahin haruwa na ta̱ꞌyapa ta̱wya̱ri nata̱ butu wya̱ri, ta̱masha̱a̱ga̱ nata̱ aba tamasha̱a̱ga̱ na̱ Hwe̱n na̱ bwa ha̱ni. Bwa ta tashana na Ibiraahin bwa ma̱ncin Isiyaaku na nꞌhwe̱n ta̱ndatu mꞌba cigi aba ꞌya̱pi Isiyaaku ta̱wya̱ri. Isiyaaku ta tamantan Yaakubu, Yaakubu bwa ma̱nta̱in adaadoo nda̱tu upwa na ree.
