<<Kaba adaadoo nda̱tu aba ribici buya̱na̱a̱ba Yusufu, aba sa̱a̱nha̱ni be̱ na hyan bushii gyama na̱ ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Masa. Ama Hwe̱n bwa tanaa na̱a̱ be̱,
bwa biha̱ni be̱ hyo̱ kungwan. Ubwa sha̱pa̱cigi be̱, bwa shi naa mꞌbaa ta̱yansun kaꞌuba̱ na Firiꞌauna bugwama naa Masa. Firiꞌauna bwa pa̱ni Yusufu gwamina na ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Masa, bwa pa̱ni be̱ mayaan butu o̱to̱ naa awyatu ndaabwa hyo̱, ana ka̱ta̱ku na ta̱gwama.
<<Aba na̱ kunnu, kurumunro̱n ruba ta̱ni ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Masa na̱ Kaꞌaana, huku na̱ ungwan na adaadoo nda̱tu aba taza shami.
Na Yaakubu bwa hange̱ Masa mꞌbaa shami, sa̱i bwa ka̱ji ayoo adaadoo nda̱tu xashé̱e̱n shami, uya̱nu ta tasha zhagu ndaaba na yigo.
Ta̱hani ta̱ndaaba nata̱ hin reenu, Yusufu be̱ bisa̱a̱ hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱ kuꞌaya̱na̱ba, Firiꞌauna bwa e̱nshe̱n wyan.
Too, sa̱i Yusufu be̱ ka̱ji ashin Yaakubu, xajaa hyo̱ diin ndaaba, aba tanaa awyatu kuje ta̱nda̱ra̱ na ta.
Too, sa̱i Yaakubu bwa huri Masa, kabata bwa taꞌwa̱ hyo̱ na̱ adaadoo nda̱tu.
Aba sha̱pi wyan zhagu She̱ke̱me̱, aba wuma̱ni wyan na̱ aꞌuya̱ na Ibiraahin bwa tasan na̱ ayuwa na azurufa paaku mꞌmwaan na n-Hamo̱ro̱ na̱ bwa She̱ke̱me̱ na̱ ame̱ na ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Kaꞌaana.
<<Na uha̱ni bwa goki, na Hwe̱n bwa tandaaka Ibiraahin ala̱ka̱wa̱ri, awyatu nda̱tu abaa duwa̱na̱ hwarapi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ Masa.
Sa̱i aba nje̱ buyaan bugwama na̱ Masa, naa yancin koo iyaa ta shi Yusufu.
Bwaa gwama tapira̱ awyatu nda̱tu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ma pa ngwan, paa bwa tashana wyan xamunsain mꞌmwaan na nꞌaba hwii kuta̱mantaan, na̱ wana hyan nꞌwa̱gi.
<<Na̱ bwa ha̱ni ta aba tamantan Muusa be̱e̱ binaa rugama gama. Aba nje̱ hyaabu nde̱e̱be̱ mꞌpyanda nꞌtaatu na̱ ina na ashin.
Na ba mo̱nshe̱n buu, buyoo Firiꞌauna naa a̱ bwa sha̱pi Muusa bwa waanhini be̱ hakuu yoo.
Aba ga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni Muusa be̱ yan hyo̱ ta̱bita̱riga nata̱ wyatu na Masa, be̱ mꞌbaa ta̱kai nata̱ mazama na̱ paaku tuma nde̱e̱be̱.
<<Uyaan hwe̱n na be̱ nje̱ nꞌyo̱ handa sa̱i be̱ shii bija̱a̱ paaka wyatu nde̱e̱be̱, Aꞌisiraaꞌila.
Na be̱ wuci, be̱ nda̱i butu naa Masa bunii pira̱ butu nde̱e̱be̱ Buꞌisiraaꞌila. Be̱ ja̱a̱ xbiguni bwa, bikunaanyin bwa wyaan, uꞌara bwa hura̱ni buu, be̱ kwane̱ bwa butu naa Masa.
Muusa tasha̱a̱ ta̱hyan koo aya̱na̱ba nde̱e̱be̱ nii insan ta̱hyan Hwe̱n ta káji buu xbiya̱a̱cigi wyan kungwan, ama aba e̱nshe̱nshe̱n.
<<Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, be̱ gura̱a̱ jabana wyan, sa̱i be̱ nda̱i Aꞌisiraaꞌila aree nii nda gagu. Be̱ ribi na hyan xamaꞌa̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni, sa̱i be̱ hin wyan, <Iba̱ shani ga̱hin magbaantaan ri kunta, iyancin ta̱hyan ishi awyatu na ya̱na̱ba?>
<<Ama bwaa naa nii pira̱ buya̱na̱, bwa tutumaa Muusa pata bwa hin buu, <Iyaa shii na hyan ushi butu o̱to̱ nda̱a̱tu na̱a̱ naa ta̱suuga̱?
Bi-ribi na hyan u-nꞌkwane̱ kugaa takwane̱ butu naa Masa hundara?>
Na Muusa be̱ hange̱ kunnu, sa̱i be̱ gidigi, be̱ huri ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Midiyana paa be̱ shi bugai, kaba be̱ tazhaa buꞌa̱, be̱ ma̱ncin mꞌmwaan nꞌree na nꞌwya̱ri.
<<Na nꞌyo̱ nꞌhanda mꞌba huri, buyaan Butuma naa Hwe̱n bwa bántani buu na̱ ahira̱ ceeku, do̱ko̱ na̱ Undu na Sinai haku daanrun na ra na biꞌuꞌwe̱e̱ binaa sa̱pi naa nii huna̱.
Na Muusa be̱ nda̱i sa̱i be̱ jikita̱ni ta̱hyan imbata na̱nna ri. Na be̱ wuce do̱ko̱, be̱ hange̱ Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n nii nꞌga buu ma hyaan,
<Ga̱n ta nꞌshi Uhwe̱n na adaadoo ndaa, Uhwe̱n na Ibiraahin na̱ Isiyaaku na̱ Yaakubu.> Na Muusa be̱ hange̱ kunnu ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ ta̱baa jikita̱, be̱ hange̱ rukwanyan be̱ a̱rici ta̱gwatana.
<<Sa̱i Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n bwa hin buu, <Yaaciga akandaga ndaa, paa gaa ne̱e̱ kashi naka ga̱n masha̱a̱gi.
Nꞌnda̱i mahanda ungwan na baa pa awyatu nimi na̱ Masa. Nꞌhange̱ nꞌungwa ndaaba, ta shani ga̱n cíin ma biha̱na̱ wyan. Too, jaga iika̱ji tuma Masa.>
<<Too, be̱ Muusa na aba tagaa na̱ ayigo, aba hin buu, <Iyaa ta shii u-shi butu o̱to̱ naa ta̱suuga̱?> Bubwa ta Uhwe̱n bwa takáji kuutuma ndaabwa. Bwa bántani Muusa kiiꞌuꞌwe̱e̱ binaa sa̱pi binaa tanaa huna̱ ra na̱ ahira̱ ceeku ta̱hyan xbubishi buu binii sha butu o̱to̱ na̱a̱ naa ta̱biha̱na̱.
Be̱ taa shi naa tabiha̱na̱ wyan kuce̱nye̱n nata̱ Masa. Be̱e̱ ndaga iri nata̱ pa rukwanyan na̱ nata̱ jikita̱na̱, bwa ka̱a̱cihini wyan ku-Rwaga na O̱to̱ na Ya̱ma̱+ :36 Rwaga na O̱to̱ na Ya̱ma̱: Ruzha̱a̱ runa̱nna tarushi naru mahanda naru bwa rwaga, ama ta̱taga ta̱ka̱ ta̱ba ta naa nꞌga wuun Rwaga na O̱to̱ na Shenje.aba nje̱ nꞌyo̱ handa na̱ ahira̱ ceeku.
<<Bibe̱ Muusa na̱ hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱ ta tabisa̱ awyatu na Isiraaꞌila ta̱hyan, <Uhwe̱n nii káji buyaan bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama kiikorogo niinhin subwa taꞌnꞌkáji ga̱mi.>
Muusa tanaa paa kuta̱mawuna̱a̱na̱ nata̱ awyatu na Hwe̱n na hira̱ ceeku. Butuma naa Hwe̱n bwa nje̱ mazama na̱ Muusa na̱ adaadoo nda̱tu na̱ Undu na Sinai, paa bwa taraa mazama nama ta̱nda bina̱ bwa ta̱nꞌiyaagi.
<<Ama adaadoo nda̱tu aba tagaa ta̱jwara̱ga mazama nama Muusa, aba ga̱a̱ be̱, aba ribi xakwashe̱ Masa.
Aba hin buya̱na̱ naa o̱to̱ Haruuna, <Ta̱ndaaki ayaan hwe̱n ana ga̱tu nii jwara̱ga na̱ wana ta̱hyan Muusa yata na tata̱báhine̱ ku-Masa ta̱yancin na ta̱ bwa.>
Na̱ bwa ha̱ni aba nje̱ iri hakii rire̱ke̱, abaa ndaakaka buu buki, ma shinraanwyan buu bikico̱, abaa nda ta̱ga̱da̱ri na̱ iri na aba nje̱ na̱ nꞌara nꞌndaaba.
Na̱ kunnu sa̱i Uhwe̱n bwa pa̱ni wyan baa, bwa hakaci wyan abaa paga hwe̱n na̱ pyanda na̱ nꞌgwasu hunrun. Una̱nna ta nje̱ to̱n na̱ ri na ta̱ na̱ takaada na acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ta̱hyan,
<< <Ga̱hin Aꞌisiraaꞌila, ga̱n ta nuu ga̱hin taꞌnꞌshinraanwyan bikico̱ ga̱hin mꞌpa̱ni
na̱ nꞌyo̱ handa na̱ ahira̱ ceeku?
Ai, aha̱nka̱ri ninhin ane̱e̱ kupaa kiisakaru naa hwe̱n yata na ga̱hin nje̱ Moleki ma riinshina̱ na̱ bwa,
nii gwasu yata naa ga̱hin pa̱ ruzha̱a̱ Rifan,
ta̱hyan iri yata na ga̱hin ndagi na hyan inaa paga wuun hunrun.
Na̱ kunnu ga̱n na̱maa iya ma pata tutu iyeebe na Baabila.>
<<Na yigo adaadoo nda̱tu ta mꞌbaa Bidura̱ naa Ta̱sabu naa Hwe̱n, binaa aba tashapa kope aba hiin hura̱, tashi ta̱hyan Uhwe̱n ne̱e̱ na̱ aba huku na hira̱. Bidura̱ naa Hwe̱n bwa ta hyan Muusa xbinje̱, aba nje̱ buu to̱n haruwa na Hwe̱n bwa tabisa̱ be̱.
Bidura̱ naa adaadoo nda̱tu ba tahya̱su, aba shápi buu aba íye̱ pina kuce̱nye̱n ta̱yana na̱ ha̱ni na Jooshuwa. Hwe̱n bwa pa̱ nꞌyaan korogo sumo̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ba ce̱nye̱n na̱ ayishe ndaaba. Bidura̱ tanaa pina kuwuco na bugwama Dawuda.
<<Dawuda tada̱ba ta̱raa ku-Hwe̱n, bwa ro̱pe̱ xbuma̱ paaku ta̱naa paga wuun hunrun, Uhwe̱n na adaada nda̱tu Yaakubu.
Ama Suleemaanu ta tandaaka Hwe̱n ta̱ma.
Hyo̱ na̱ kunnu mahanda ubwa shi Bunaa hura̱gi Ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ buꞌa̱cii naa na̱ ina na butu wuma bwa ma̱. Haruwa na bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama bwa tahyan,
<< <Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n hin, <<Ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱ta ta̱shi bizhe̱nke̱n naa ta̱gwama ta̱niimi,
nꞌce̱nye̱n mꞌba shi paaku ta̱ zataa mꞌbuna nꞌniimi.
Uya̱ ina nu ga̱hiin mꞌmana?
Koo pe̱kata kashi paa ha̱nka̱na̱ nimi?
Shii ga̱n ta nꞌnje̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ hyo̱?>>>
<<Ga̱hin awyatu ana tibici mazama, ana hyuhyu ta̱guma, ana mꞌbaa ce̱be̱ na unfuun! Ishi haku sushoohin nasu tanaa sa̱ koya̱ ha̱ni suga̱a̱ ta̱jwara̱ga Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n. Kunta ta taa ga̱hin ga̱hin ndaga.
Kacita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, bunii bunaa aba ta pa̱ci ngwan? Atakuna ana tanda mazama nama zhagu na Butu naa Bina̱, buyata naa ga̱hin tapana, ga̱hin kwane̱ be̱.
Ga̱hin naa tama raaga Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n katuma na Hwe̱n, ga̱hin ga̱a̱ muu ta̱jwara̱ga gudusu!>>
Akwane̱ Isitafanu na̱ nꞌta̱gyashi
Na awyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya aba hange̱ kunnu abaa fukaa gata ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ma re̱ mꞌmbwa na̱a̱ bwa.
Ama Isitafanu, Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ ne̱e̱ na̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa, bwa gwatagi ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, bwa nda̱i ta̱gwaan nata̱ kuta̱shapaciga nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ba ne̱e̱ na̱ Yeesu be̱ e̱she̱ nꞌkataga naka Hwe̱n.
Bwa hin wyan, <<Nde̱e̱ nꞌnda̱i ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱gunii, na̱a̱ Yoo Butu ma isa nꞌkataga naka Hwe̱n.>>
Ama aba zooni ta̱ꞌungwa, aba zooga̱ni ce̱be̱ ndaaba ma̱ni, aba ja̱pita̱ni bwa huku.
Aba ba̱ha̱ni bwa ta̱baa nata̱ ce̱pe̱ na̱ kai, ma gyasa bwa atari. Aba ana shi ana tandaya mꞌba mazama aba ya̱a̱ciga̱gi nꞌda̱da̱bi nꞌndaaba aba sha̱a̱gi muu paa buyaan baa bunaa ba ta hyan Shawulu.
Aba ma gyasa Isitafanu atari bwa nje̱ ro̱pe̱ bwa hin, <<Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu raa bihwaanwun niimi.>>
Sa̱i bwa she̱nshe̱n na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n, bwa ta̱a̱ni nu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ bwa hin, <<Butu O̱to̱ ta-ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ wyan pinsan na̱nna.>> Na bwa cici kunnu, bwa ꞌwi.

Shawulu bwa hange̱ kugama na̱ nꞌta̱kuna nata̱ Isitafanu.
Shawulu yanshin awyatu na pa̱ni nꞌgata ta̱mataa
Na̱ hwe̱n ya̱nu, aba kaki wyatu na Yeesu aba yanshin wyan ta̱ma taa ana ne̱e̱ na̱ Hurushaliima. Hyo̱ aba gida̱ga̱gi zhagu kuꞌnꞌcice̱pe̱ na nꞌnaanyin na̱ Samaariya na̱ nꞌnaanyin na̱ Yaahudiya, kana Yeesu be̱ tazwara ta tabwa ta.
Sa̱i kawyatu na jwarigi Hwe̱n ki aba wuma̱ni Isitafanu, aba nꞌgaagi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ wana ndaabwa.
Shawulu bwaa gata awyatu na Yeesu, bwaa ta̱na̱a̱ nꞌina ina ma kota̱ga̱na̱ wyatu wya̱ri na a̱, ma zwagagana wyan na̱ zhaaro.
Filibu cita̱gi mazama nama zumaa na̱ Samaariya
Awyatu na pa̱ni nꞌgata ana na magata aba ba̱ni Hurushaliima, aba ja̱a̱ kope, ma bisa̱ga̱ wyatu mazama nama zumaa nama Yeesu.
Filibu+ :5 Filibu bunaa shi buka̱ kuꞌata̱nda̱ra̱ ana aba na kasa ana hooso na shami. Gwatana 6:5.bwa huri yaan ce̱pe̱ na Samaariya, ma bisa̱ga̱ wyan mazama nama Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Na wyatu hwarapi aba hange̱ mazama aba nda̱i yaan iri na rukwanyan na bwaa ndaga, nii gata ka̱, aba jaa do̱ko̱, aba shiraagi be̱.
Nꞌhwaanwun na nꞌwe̱ mꞌba ba̱nii kawyatu hwarapi nꞌta̱ꞌungwa, awyatu na mꞌbuna mꞌba swa̱ na̱ agurubi hwarapi aba kuda̱gagi.
Na̱ wana kunnu, aba hange̱ gama ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ bwa ce̱pe̱.
Buyaan butu Siima buna naa na̱ bwa ce̱pe̱, bunaa tanaa sa̱ ndaga iri na ta̱gigiriga̱ ma maa awyatu na Samaariya rukwanyan bwa masha̱pi bwa taa shi naa hura̱gi na̱ ri naa bwaa nda.
Wyatu o̱to̱ na̱ mꞌmwaan hyo̱ abaa hyaan, <<Butu na̱nna ta̱kai nata̱ Hwe̱n yata na aba tahyan na o̱to̱.>>
Aba shii nꞌgata ndaaba kuna̱a̱ bwa na̱ wana buta̱a̱ ke̱nye̱n kaun ma ndaga ri na ta̱jikita̱na̱ na̱ ri naa bwaa gigiriga̱hina̱a̱.
Na wyatu aba pa̱ni nꞌgata kumazama nama zumaa nama Filibu bwaa nda nama ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n, na̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, aꞌa̱ na̱ awyatu wya̱ri aba ndagi wyan baba̱tiisa̱ma.
Bwa Siima taa maa bwa pa̱nii gata aba nje̱ bwa baba̱tiisa̱ma. Bwa jwarigi Filibu hyo̱ paa bwa ja̱a̱, na bwa nda̱i Filibu nii ndaga ri na ta̱jikita̱na̱ na̱ na ta̱pa rukwanyan, bwa nje̱ kuma̱.
Na ana Yeesu be̱ tazwara na̱ Hurushaliima aba hange̱ awyatu na Asamaariya ara̱a̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n, aba ka̱ji Biituru na̱ Yoohana waaba.
Na aba wuci, aba ndaaki ana pa̱ni nꞌgata ro̱pe̱ na ta̱da̱ba Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n,
na̱ wana Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n ta ciincin kwan na̱a̱ koo buka̱ ndaaba, ata huwa̱ wyan kuta̱ndaga baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu.
Nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu, Biituru na̱ Yoohana aba ca̱guda̱a̱ga̱gi ana pa̱ni nꞌgata nꞌara na nꞌrubara̱ka, aba de̱be̱ Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n.
Na Siima bwa nda̱i na̱ nꞌta̱cagudaaga ara ta̱ta aba ta da̱ba Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n, sa̱i bwa hiin pana wyan ayuwa na̱ wana xbude̱be̱ ta̱ba ta̱kai,
bwa hin, <<Ga̱n taa maa mꞌpa̱ni ma taa ta̱kai, na̱ wana bunaa ga̱n ca̱guda̱a̱gi ara bude̱be̱ Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n.>>
Ama Biituru bwa hin be̱, <<Gaa na yuwa ndaa, kuna̱ ma! Bi-ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan na yuwa ta gaa da̱ba ri ta̱ꞌye̱n na Hwe̱n?
Tuma na̱nna, bi-za ruwa na̱ be̱ koo ge̱, wana bigata ndaabi za ki kaꞌuba̱ na Hwe̱n.
Sa̱i u-pa̱ni pinsan baa na̱ wana iri yata na we̱, u-ro̱pe̱ Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n koo ubwa jaa ha̱mba̱ga̱ pinsan ndaa nii gata ndaabwa na̱ iri na gaa hoo sha̱a̱ nii gata ndaabi na zumaancin.
Na̱ wana nꞌnda̱i bine̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ribici, pinsan bwa gura̱a̱ maa kadaga.>>
Siima bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Nꞌrupani ma Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n, na̱ wana koo iri ka̱ na ga̱hin cici xita nda na̱ ga̱mi.>>
Na Biituru na̱ Yoohana aba cici hiku, aba bisa̱gi wyatu mazama nama Yeesu, naazhin aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱ Hurushaliima. Abaa cita̱ga̱ mazama nama zumaa na̱ nꞌcice̱pe̱ na n-Samaariya.
Filibu ura̱ku na̱ butu naa Habasha
Uyaan hwe̱n buyaan butuma naa Hwe̱n bwa hin Filibu, <<Hiika̱, uja̱a̱ ruꞌwa, uhumuni yo̱n na báni Hurushaliima ubwa ja̱a̱ Gaaza, uyo̱n na báni bizaga naa aga.>>
Filibu bwa hiiki, bwa huri. Kuuyaan butu naa Habasha, bwa shi butu o̱to̱ naa ca̱ma̱ncin kuta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Kandisi Bisorooniya naa Habasha, bwa shi bunaa ta naa sha̱a̱ga̱ga̱ buu ayuwa, bunaa tajaga Hurushaliima xbunjé̱e̱ ro̱pe̱.
Bwa ne̱e̱ na̱ kushiikwa ina, bwa hunrani nii keeke na biindakwa. Bwaa cita̱ga̱ ba̱da̱ ba̱da̱ takaada na butu naa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Ishaaya.
Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ hin Filibu, <<Wuta̱ do̱ko̱ kiikeeke na biindakwa yata u-naa na ba.>>
Filibu bwa gidigi zhagu waabwa, bwa hange̱ be̱ macita̱ga̱ takaada na bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Ishaaya. Bwa ha̱nta̱ni be̱ bwa hin, <<Butu o̱to̱, bi-e̱nshe̱n iri na gaa cita̱ga̱?>>
Bwa ra̱ni, <<Pee ye̱e̱? Sa̱i kuuyaan buꞌmꞌbisa̱gi.>> Bwa hin Filibu xbuka̱ta̱ni bikeeke na biindakwa, ahunraana da̱nda̱.
Bibiin naa ta̱taga nata̱ takaada na Hwe̱n nata̱ bwaa cita̱ga̱ mana,
<<Ama̱ni be̱ hakii ka̱ra̱bi zhagu kuta̱shinran.
Hakii ka̱ra̱bi be̱ ne̱e̱ wau paakuu naa nii huuna buu ta̱hinje ta̱nde̱e̱be̱,
kunta be̱ guniincin nu nde̱e̱be̱.
Aba husani be̱,
aba ndaakici be̱ ta̱suuga̱ to̱n.
Iyaa nii ara ta̱cita̱ga̱ mazama nama mꞌmwaan nde̱e̱be̱?
Na ta̱hyan akwane̱ buu na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana.>>
Sa̱i butu bwa hin Filibu, <<Mazama nama yaan bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama na̱nna bwaa nda? Mazama mandaabwa koo namaa yaan?>>
Filibu bwa gunii nu bwa pa̱shi kuta̱taga ta̱yata nata̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n zhagu kuta̱yaan ta̱taga, be̱e̱ bisa̱ga̱ be̱ mazama nama zumaa nama Yeesu.
Aba nꞌta̱hani, aba wuci paakii yaan bida̱dabu, bubwa butu bwa hin, <<Gwatana. Nde̱e̱ ma̱ni! Imba̱ nii yansan gaa jaa nꞌnda baba̱tiisa̱ma?>>+ :36 Ta̱yaan ta̱taga ta̱ka̱ ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa aaya na 37 kunna: Filibu bwa hin, <<Kuu-pa̱nii gata ndaabi ka̱, iindaaki.>> Bwa butu o̱to̱ bwa hin, <<Mꞌpa̱nii gata na̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu Buyoo Hwe̱n ta.>> Bwa pa̱ni nu xaꞌisaa bikeeke na biindakwa. Hyo̱ ndaaba aba reeko aba ciin aba ta̱ni ma̱ni, sa̱i Filibu bwa nje̱ butu bwa baba̱tiisa̱ma.
Na aba báni kuma̱ni, Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ sha̱pi Filibu. Bwa butu bwa gura̱a̱ci ndaya be̱, ama bwa huri na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱da̱ri.
Sa̱i Filibu bwa manda̱i kuna̱ ce̱pe̱ na aba tahyan Azotusu. Sa̱i bwa ja̱ba̱gi hyo̱ nꞌcice̱pe̱ ma bisa̱ga̱ mazama nama zumaa, hara̱ bwa wuci uce̱pe̱ na aba tahyan Kaisariya.

Shawulu ke̱ce̱e̱ke̱ bwa jwarigi Yeesu
Tuma 22:6-16; 26:12-18
Shawulu bwa duwa̱ni kuta̱kaka ana jwarigi Yeesu. Bwaa hyaan munrun bunii naa kunaa wyan. Bwa ja̱a̱ paa butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti,
bwa hin, xapa̱ni be̱ atakaada na pa̱ni be̱ ta̱kai zhagu aka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya ana ne̱e̱ na̱ ce̱pe̱ na Dimasiku, na ta̱hyan kuuwuta̱ni wyatu na jwarigi Yo̱n na Yeesu, butu wya̱ri koo buꞌa̱, bukota̱ga̱ni wyan, bukádaagi wyan buꞌye̱e̱ Hurushaliima.
Na bwa ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hani, bwa goki Dimasiku, kumayaan maza̱ki nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ mꞌba tára̱kani paakuu bwa ne̱e̱.
Sa̱i bwa kinai pwan na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n, bwa hange̱ kumazama nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ mꞌba hin bwa, <<Shawulu! Shawulu! Na̱ wana ba̱ gaa nꞌkaki?>>
Bwa hin, <<Butu o̱to̱, iyaa nu ya̱nu gaa shi?>>
Mazama mꞌba ráni ta̱hyan, <<Ga̱n ta Yeesu bunaa gaa kaki.
Hiika̱ u-ta̱ni ce̱pe̱, piree kata aba na̱maa bisa̱ iri na ga̱n nꞌribi ga̱ga̱ga̱ u-nje̱.>>
Wyatu ndaabwa na bwa ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hani na̱ aba, aba ne̱e̱ wau aba a̱rici mazama ta̱cita̱, aba hange̱ mazama, ama aba nda̱ci koo butu.
Shawulu bwa hiiki, bwa gunii ayishe, ama bwa ba̱nii ruba̱. Awyatu na bwa ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hani na̱ ba aba kota̱ni be̱ ara zhagu Dimasiku.
Bwa pa̱ nꞌhwe̱n nꞌtaatu bwa huwa̱gici, bwa re̱ce̱, bwa swa̱ci.
Na̱ Dimasiku, buyaan butu naa jwarigi ne̱e̱ bunaa aba ta nꞌgana Hanaaninyan. Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwa bisa̱a̱ be̱ yaan ri haka ra̱rabi, bwa nje̱ mazama na̱a̱ bwa, <<Hanaaninyan!>>
Bwa ra̱ni, <<Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu, ga̱n na!>>
Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwa hin be̱, <<Hiika̱, jwara̱gana yo̱n na aba ta nꞌgana Yo̱n na Ka̱mbigi, u-ja̱a̱ ina na Yaahuda, u-ha̱nta̱ni koo buyaan butu ne̱e̱ bunaa báni Tarususu, bunaa aba ta nꞌgana Shawulu. Bune̱e̱ na̱ ro̱pe̱ kaun.
Ga̱n bisa̱a̱ bwa ri haka ra̱rabi, bwa nda̱i buyaan butu naa ruzha̱a̱ Hanaaninyan bwa tá̱ni bwa ca̱guda̱a̱gi bwa ara na rubara̱ka na hyan buhuwa̱gi mayaan.>>
Hanaaninyan be̱ hin, <<Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu, nꞌhange̱ ri na butu ya̱nu paaka wyatu hwarapi iri na we̱ na bwaa ndaaka awyatu ndaa anaa jwarigi na̱ Hurushaliima.
Apirisiti na o̱to̱ aba pa̱ni be̱ ta̱kai xbukota̱ni hyo̱ butu naa ta naa paga hunrun na̱ nꞌruzha̱a̱ rundaabi.>>
Yeesu bwa hin be̱, <<Gaa da̱i hura̱, bushi butu naa ga̱n ka̱shi xbundaaki tuma nata̱ iya mazama maniimi kawyatu na shici Ayaahudiya, na̱ nꞌgwama nꞌndaaba, na̱ awyatu na Isiraaꞌila taa.
Ga̱n na̱ hyuhyu nimi nꞌnii bisa̱a̱ be̱ ngwan na bwaa swa ga̱ga̱ga̱ na̱ wana buꞌnꞌjwarigi.>>
Sa̱i Hanaaninyan be̱ ja̱a̱, be̱ ta̱ni ina na Shawulu bwa ne̱e̱ na̱ bwa. Be̱ cikaa ara be̱ ca̱guda̱a̱gi bwa, be̱ hin, <<Buya̱tu Shawulu, Yeesu ta nꞌkáji, buyata naa gaa taꞌura̱ku na̱ yo̱n na gaa tajwárige̱. Buribi u-gura̱a̱ huwa̱ga̱, buusha̱a̱gi Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n hiku.>>
Kupita, iyaanyini be̱ ke̱ne̱ hakii gugu kayishe na Shawulu, bwa gura̱a̱ huwa̱ga̱ mayaan. Sa̱i bwa hiiki, aba nje̱ be̱ baba̱tiisa̱ma.
Bwa re̱ naazhin shami, bwa gura̱a̱ nda kai.
Shawulu cita̱gi mazama nama zumaa na̱ Dimasiku
Shawulu bwa duwa̱ni nꞌhwe̱n ta̱ pa kawyatu na jwarigi Yeesu na̱ Dimasiku.
Bike̱nye̱n be̱ ta̱ci du, Shawulu bwaa bisa̱ga̱ wyatu mazama nama Yeesu na̱ aka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya ta̱hyan, be̱ taa shi Buyoo Hwe̱n.
Hyo̱ wyatu na hange̱ be̱ macita̱ga̱ kunnu, aba jikita̱ni ma hyaan, <<Ka̱i, shici buna̱nna ta tanaa kunaa awyatu ana ta naa paga hunrun na̱ nꞌruzha̱a̱ ruyata na̱ Hurushaliima nuu? Bujaa pina na̱ wana hyan xbukota̱ga̱ni wyan, aka̱da̱a̱gi wyan, buꞌye̱e̱ wyan kapirisiti na o̱to̱.>>
Ama Shawulu bwa duwa̱ni ka̱i, bwa duwa̱ni aha̱nka̱ri na awyatu na Ayaahudiya ta̱hiika̱hina̱ ana hunrani na̱ Dimasiku, bwaa bisa̱ga̱ wyan hiku Yeesu ta shi Ala̱masiihu.
Shawulu ba̱na̱ni bizu ka-Ayaahudiya
Na nꞌhwe̱n hamba mꞌba huri, Ayaahudiya aba hwii shiri haruwa na ta̱kuna Shawulu.
Na̱ gita na̱ hwe̱n abaa ha̱mbaaga adubo na ce̱pe̱ na̱ wana ta̱kuna be̱. Ama bwa hange̱ iri na aba ribi ta̱nda.
Ama na̱ gita awyatu ndaabwa na jwarigi aba zwa̱ga̱ni be̱ nii tumunsun, aba pa̱ tumunsun hwa̱, aba ciinha̱ni be̱ na yaan dubo na ga̱ru.
Shawulu kwashe̱e̱ke̱ Hurushaliima
Na Shawulu bwa wuci Hurushaliima, bwa ribi ta̱naawan na̱ awyatu na jwarigi Yeesu, ama aba hange̱ rukwanyan rundaabwa. Aba ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan, bunii kunaawyan ta mꞌbuna.
Sa̱i Bara̱naba bwa ꞌye̱e̱ be̱ paaka ana Yeesu be̱ tazwara. Bwa bisa̱gi wyan haruwa na Shawulu bwa taꞌura̱ku na̱ Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu na̱ yo̱n, bwa ma jaga Hurushaliima, na̱ haruwa na Butu O̱to̱ bwa tanje̱ mazama na̱a̱ bwa, na̱ haruwa na Shawulu bwa bisa̱gi awyatu mazama nama zumaa nama Yeesu na̱ Dimasiku rukwanyan ruba za.
Shawulu bwa ke̱ne̱ ta̱nda iri huku na̱ aba na̱ Hurushaliima, rukwanyan ruba za naru ta̱bisa̱ga̱ wyatu mazama nama Yeesu.
Bwaa gura̱a̱ ndaga mazama na̱ kuda̱ga na̱ Ayaahudiya ana tibi Ta̱helena, hyo̱ na̱ kunnu, abaa wyanzan xakwane̱ be̱.
Na wyatu ndaabwa ana jwarigi aba hange̱ kunnu, aba sha̱pi be̱ zhagu Kaisariya, aba ka̱ji be̱ zhagu Tarususu ce̱pe̱ ndaabwa.
Na̱ ha̱ni ya̱nu, awyatu Yeesu na ne̱e̱ na̱ ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya, na̱ Gaalili, na̱ Samaariya aba de̱be̱ hunranhunran na ta̱gumunu. Aba hunrani kami, abaa duwa̱na̱ hwarapi na̱ nꞌgata ta̱pana na̱ Yeesu, huku nii shita̱ ta̱ta nata̱a̱ Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n.
Biituru kuda̱gahini Iniyasu
Na Biituru bwa hwii ta̱jabaga pa̱ri hyo̱, bwa gura̱a̱ jaga kawyatu na Hwe̱n ana ne̱e̱ na̱ ce̱pe̱ na Liida.
Piree be̱ ura̱ku na̱a̱ yaan butu naa aba ta nꞌgana Iniyasu, buna mꞌbuna mꞌba swa̱, bwa taa suguma nꞌyo̱ nꞌta̱ndatu bwa a̱rici ta̱bana.
Biituru bwa hin buu, <<Iniyasu, Ala̱masiihu Yeesu taa kuda̱gahini. Hiika̱, u-sha̱pi ba̱ra̱shina̱ ndaa.>> Kupita Iniyasu be̱ hiiki.
Awyatu hwarapi na Liida na̱ wyatu na Shaaronu, aba nda̱i butu naa kwade̱ge̱, aba kíciike̱ aba pa̱ni nꞌgata nꞌndaaba ku-Yeesu.
Biituru kuda̱gahini Tabiita na taꞌwi
Na̱ ce̱pe̱ na Joopa, buyaan buꞌa̱ naa pa̱nii gata ku-Yeesu naa aba ta hyan Tabiita, agura̱a̱ hyan be̱ Dokasu, bwa tanaa nda iri na bina̱ koya̱ ha̱ni, bwa tanaa ndaakaka aꞌwa̱ta̱gi iri na aba ribi.
Na̱ ha̱ni ya̱nu, bwa hange̱ce̱ sa̱, bwa ꞌwi. Na ba zware̱ be̱ ma̱ni, aba taahini be̱ kudura̱ na ne̱e̱ da̱da̱da̱ naa ya̱na̱.
Na ta̱hyan Liida mame̱mincin na̱ Joopa, ana jwarigi aba hange̱ Biituru ne̱e̱ na̱ Liida, aba ka̱ji wyatu ree zhagu waabwa, xarúpe̱ bwa xbujaa waaba na̱ ha̱ni.
Sa̱i Biituru bwa huri huku na̱ ba. Na bwa wuci, aba ꞌye̱e̱ be̱ bwa dura̱. Hyo̱ aꞌa̱ na suwya̱rugooba suba ꞌwa̱gi, aba isagi do̱ko̱ na̱a̱ bwa ma nꞌgaaga, abaa bisa̱a̱ga̱ aꞌwana na̱ yaan ꞌwaa na be̱ Dokasu na ndaakaka wyan ha̱ni na be̱ tane̱e̱ na̱ aba.
Biituru bwa hin wyan hyo̱ ndaaba xaba̱ni kubwa dura̱. Bwa she̱nshe̱n na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n bwa nje̱ ro̱pe̱. Bwa ke̱ce̱he̱ne̱ ruba ruꞌwa̱, bwa hin, <<Tabiita! Hiika̱!>> Be̱ gunii ayishe nde̱e̱be̱. Na be̱ nda̱i Biituru, be̱ hiiki, be̱ hunrani.
Biituru bwa cikaa ara, bwa guni buu, be̱ hiiki. Sa̱i bwa nꞌgani ana pa̱ni nꞌgata na̱ aꞌa̱ ana suwya̱rugooba suba ꞌwa̱gi, bwa bishi wyan ta̱hyan bikúshe̱e̱ wuma.
Mazama mꞌba maga̱ci kope na̱ Joopa. Do̱ko̱ wyatu hyo̱ aba pa̱ni nꞌgata ku-Yeesu.
Biituru bwa pa̱ nꞌhwe̱n nꞌhwarapi na̱ Joopa, paaku ina naa yaan busupi naa atutuu Siima.

Koneliyusu nꞌgani Biituru
Na̱ ce̱pe̱ na Kaisariya, buyaan butu ne̱e̱ bunaa aba ta nꞌgana Koneliyusu. Bwa shi sooja na o̱to̱ kasooja na ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Rooma. Bwa ne̱e̱ nii yaan bigudu naa aba ta hyan Bigudu naa Itaaliya.
Bwa shi butu naa jwarigi Hwe̱n ki, bo̱do̱ na̱ awyatu na ina ndaabwa, bwa ta naa paga Hwe̱n hunrun. Bwa ta naa ndaakaka aꞌwa̱ta̱gi na Yaahudiya ri hwarapi na zumaa. Bwa ta naa na̱ ro̱pe̱ ku-Hwe̱n koya̱ ha̱ni.
Yaan hwe̱n, bike̱nye̱n naa hwe̱n bwa hiriki ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, bwa nda̱i butuma naa Hwe̱n hiku haka ra̱rabi, bwa wuce waabwa, bwa hin, <<Koneliyusu!>>
Be̱ gwatagi bwa ga̱ri ga̱ri, na̱ nꞌrukwanyan be̱ hin, <<Butu O̱to̱, iba̱ gaa ribi?>>
Butuma bwa hin bwa, <<Ro̱pe̱ ndaa na̱ iri na zumaa na gaa ndaakaka aꞌwa̱ta̱gi, ibe̱ ta wuci ta uba̱ na Hwe̱n, ta ibe̱ shi ri na ta̱naa matamanrinyaan waabwa.
Niina káji ayaan wyatu wya̱ri Joopa paakuu yaan butu naa aba ta hyan Siima bunaa aba ta gura̱a̱ nꞌgana Biituru.
Bune̱e̱ na̱ ina na Siima busupi naa atutuu, ina ndaabwa ne̱e̱ do̱ko̱ na̱ rwaga na o̱to̱.>>
Naa bwaa tuma bwa huri, Koneliyusu bwa nꞌgani agyama ndaabwa reeko, na̱ yaan sooja na jwarigi taa Hwe̱n ki, ana ta naa ndaaka be̱ tuma.
Na bwa hwii ta̱cita̱ga̱ hyo̱ iri na nje̱, bwa ka̱ji wyan zhagu Joopa.
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, bike̱nye̱n naa hwe̱n da̱, atuma na Koneliyusu aba ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hani, aba goki bwa ce̱pe̱. Biituru bwa ka̱ta̱ni ta̱biyana nata̱ aba ba̱ri kuta̱bara da̱da̱da̱ xbunje̱ ro̱pe̱.
Bwa hange̱ rumunro̱n ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, bwa ribi yaanyini ta̱re̱. Na abaa ndaaka be̱ shami, bwa nda̱i iri haka ara̱rabi.
Bwa nda̱i ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ta̱ gunii, iyaanyini be̱ wuci cuun haku shika na zuzu na ta̱maguna̱na̱, na̱ mꞌbiin nde̱e̱be̱ nꞌna̱nshin.
Na̱ ame̱ nde̱e̱be̱, koya̱ iri na bikico̱ be̱ ne̱e̱ na mꞌbuna nꞌna̱nshin, na̱ na mꞌbaa mꞌpirwa na nꞌsuhwaa na̱ awyaanwyana, na̱ ano̱no̱.
Bwa hange̱ mayaan mazama mꞌba hin, <<Biituru, hiika̱, shinran, u-re̱ wuun.>>
Sa̱i Biituru bwa hin, <<Shii nuunu! Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n, nꞌta re̱ce̱ iri na zumaancin koo ina za sabu, kuꞌnꞌgira̱nshin nda̱a̱tu mꞌba yanshin.>>
Sa̱i bwa gura̱a̱ ha̱nga uyaan nu, na mahin reenu, ubwa hin, <<Iri na Hwe̱n bwa nje̱ sabu, ta hyan wuun ishi na zumaancin.>>
Iri ya̱nu tanda mataatu, bike̱nye̱n be̱ ta̱ci, aba sha̱pi wuun da̱da̱da̱.
Biituru bwa yancin, bwaa maga̱gaaga koo iya̱ iri na iri ta be̱ shi. Kawyatu na Koneliyusu bwa káji aba isagi na inco̱n, ahoo hantana ina na Siima busupi.
Aba ma hantana mataagana nu koo Siima buna aba ta hyan Biituru te̱ne̱ pina.
Ta Biituru ma makicihinaa nii gata na̱ iri na bwa nda̱i haka ra̱rabi, Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ hin be̱, <<Nde̱e̱ wyatu taatu ta maa wyanzan.
Hiika̱, u-ciin, u-jwara̱ga wyan. Ta-sha̱a̱ nꞌgata nꞌreeko, wana ga̱n ta nꞌkáji wyan.>>
Sa̱i Biituru bwa ciin zhagu kaba wyatu, bwa hin wyan, <<Ga̱n ta ga̱hin nꞌwyanzan. Imbata shi iri naa íye̱ ma?>>
Aba hin, <<Uyaan sooja na o̱to̱ na ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Rooma, bunaa aba ta nꞌgana Koneliyusu, bwa ta ta̱káji. Bwaa shi butu naa bina̱, bunaa wa̱shi Hwe̱n. Bwa tanaa pagaga wuun hunrun, bunaa hyo̱ awyatu na Ayaahudiya ba ta naa cita̱ga̱ mazama nama iri na bina̱ na bwaa nda. Butuma naa Hwe̱n naa bure bwa shaani bwa ta̱káji, u-ja̱a̱ ina ndaabwa, buhange̱ ri na gaa hyan.>>
Sa̱i Biituru bwa ta̱ha̱ni wyan, bwa pa̱ wyan paaku ta̱rota̱.
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, bwa hiiki, aba huri huku na̱ ayaan ana jwarigi ana Joopa aba ꞌye̱e̱ bwa.
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n mayaan, aba ta̱ni Kaisariya. Koneliyusu tahoo sha̱a̱ nii gata anii jaa, bwa nꞌgani diin ndaabwa na̱ nꞌta̱shika ta̱ndaabwa.
Biituru ma huwa̱ kuta̱ta̱na̱ ina, Koneliyusu bwa ra̱ga̱ni bwa, bwa she̱nshe̱n na uba̱ ndaabwa ma pa bwa hunrun.
Biituru bwa hiika̱hini be̱ ma hyaan, <<Hiika̱, ga̱n taa maa butu wuma ta ga̱n shi haku gaa.>>
Biituru ma nda mazama na̱a̱ bwa, abaa ta̱ni ina, aba wuta̱ni awyatu hwarapi ura̱ku na̱ ina.
Bwa hin wyan, <<Ga̱hin yan nꞌgira̱nshin nꞌnda̱a̱tu nꞌyanshin Buyaahudiya bunje̱ iri huku na̱a̱ naa shici Yaahudiya, koo buja̱a̱ paakii yaan bikorogo goo. Ama Hwe̱n mꞌbisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan, ta-hyan kwayaa bushi naa za sabu koo bunaa ta̱shiri.
Na̱ wana kunnu, na aba nꞌgani nꞌjaa, ga̱n hincin nꞌjaa jaga. Too, niina nꞌribi ma yansun iri na shaani ga̱hin nꞌgani.>>
Sa̱i Koneliyusu bwa hin, <<Hwe̱n nꞌtaatu na nꞌhuri, haki ke̱nye̱n yana, bike̱nye̱n naa ta̱ruma ta̱taatu nata̱ hwe̱n bwa hiriki, ga̱n ma nda ro̱pe̱ na̱ ina nimi, kuuyaan butu ta bwa e̱she̱ na uba̱ nimi. Bwa ta̱a̱ni aꞌwana na tande̱ paawu.
Butu bwa hin, <Koneliyusu, Hwe̱n ra̱ni ro̱pe̱ ndaa, iri na zumaa na gaa ta naa ndaaka aꞌwa̱ta̱gi, ishi ri na Hwe̱n bwa tanaa matamanrinyan.
Na̱ wana kunnu, kada atuma zhagu Joopa aꞌnꞌgani Siima, bunaa aba ta gura̱a̱ nꞌgana Biituru. Buciin kiꞌina na busupi Siima, bunaa ina ndaabwa bwa ne̱e̱ do̱ko̱ na̱ rwaga na o̱to̱.>
Bwa ta shaani ga̱n káji buu xbuuꞌnꞌgani gaa, ta gaa nje̱ to̱n. Too, ga̱tu na ga̱tu mawuna̱ni na̱ uba̱ na Hwe̱n, ta̱shiraagi hyo̱ iri na Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n bwaa bishi u-ta̱bishi.>>
Biituru nje̱ mazama na̱ ina na Koneliyusu
Sa̱i Biituru bwa pa̱shi mazama ta̱cita̱ga̱ na̱ ina na Koneliyusu bwa hin, <<Mahanda, ga̱n yan ta̱hyan Hwe̱n a̱cii shika ta̱naa bisa̱a̱ga̱ ta̱hura̱ nata̱ wyatu,
buta raa koo buya̱ kope bwa báni bunaa tanaa paga wuun hunrun, na̱a̱ naa tanaa nda iri to̱n.
Iyan tuma na Hwe̱n bwa na káji kuga̱tu awyatu na Isiraaꞌila, nama hunranhunran nata̱ gumunu ku-Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, binaa shi Butu O̱to̱ naa kwayaa.
Iyan iri na tanda na mazama mꞌba tamagata hyo̱ mꞌbiin na n-Yaahudiya, mꞌba páshi ta na̱ Gaalili, tanii ke̱nye̱n naa Yoohana bwa tacita̱ga̱ mazama nama baba̱tiisa̱ma.
Iyan ta̱hyan Yeesu butu naa Naazare, haruwa na Hwe̱n bwa tasha̱a̱ga̱ buu Bihwaanwun ndaabwa na̱ nꞌta̱kai. Be̱ jwara̱gagani hyo̱, ma ndaga ri na zumaa, be̱e̱ kuda̱gahinaa ana Bupira̱ bwa yanshin ta̱mataa, na̱ wana Hwe̱n ne̱e̱ huku nii be̱.
Ga̱tu taa shi ana nda̱i iri nꞌya̱nu suyishe sunda̱a̱tu hyo̱ ina Yeesu be̱ nje̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya na̱ ame̱ na Hurushaliima. Ta aba takuna buu, kuta̱kaba buu na̱ guguji na ꞌwe̱e̱.
Ama ta Hwe̱n bwa hiika̱hini buu na̱ hwe̱n na hin taatu, bwa shaani wyatu ba nda̱ya̱gi buu.
Be̱ bisa̱a̱ci hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱ kawyatu hyo̱, kuga̱tu ana Hwe̱n bwa tahoo zwara xta̱shi ana nii bisa̱ga̱ wyatu hiku. Ga̱tu taa shi ana re̱, ga̱tu swa̱ nii be̱ bike̱nye̱n naa be̱ tahiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱.
Be̱ ta̱hin xta̱naa bisa̱ga̱ wyatu ta̱hyan be̱ taa shi bunaa Hwe̱n bwa shii bunaa ndaakaka ana hoo ꞌwa̱ga̱ na̱ ana tane̱e̱ wuma ta̱suuga̱.
Hyo̱ awyatu na tanaa cita̱a̱ga̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, ayan hiku ta̱hyan koo buya̱ naa pa̱ni nꞌgata na̱ Yeesu, Hwe̱n jaa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ bwa pinsan ndaabwa na̱ nꞌta̱kai ta̱nde̱e̱be̱.>>
Uhwe̱n pa̱ni ana shici Ayaahudiya Bihwaanwun ndaabwa
Biituru macita̱ga̱ mazama, Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ cíin hyo̱ kawyatu na shiraagi bwa.
Awyatu na Ayaahudiya ana shi ta̱shika nata̱ Biituru ana pa̱ni nꞌgata, abaa jikita̱ga̱ na aba nda̱i Hwe̱n sha̱a̱gi ana shici Ayaahudiya taa Bihwaanwun ndaabwa.
Na̱ wana ahange̱ wyan macita̱ga̱ mazama nꞌta̱ce̱pe̱ googoogoo ma yaba Hwe̱n.
Ha̱ni ya̱nu, Biituru bwa hin ana ne̱e̱ nuu bwa.
<<Buyaan bune̱e̱ bunaa nii yansan andaaki wyatu na̱nna baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ ma̱ni? Hwe̱n sha̱a̱gi wyan Bihwaanwun ndaabwa taa haruwa na ga̱tu tada̱ba.>>
Sa̱i Biituru bwa hin xanje̱ wyan baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Sa̱i aba ro̱pe̱ Biituru xbuduwa̱a̱gi wyan nꞌhwe̱n ge̱.

Biituru bisa̱gi wyatu na jwarigi na Hurushaliima mazama
Awyatu na Yeesu be̱ tazwara na̱ ayaan wyatu ana pa̱ni nꞌgata ana ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya, aba hange̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya ara̱a̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n.
Na Biituru bwa ja̱a̱ Hurushaliima, ayaan Ayaahudiya ana pa̱ni nꞌgata aba hin buu hana.
Aba hin, <<Na̱ wana ba̱ gaa ta ja̱a̱ paaka wyatu ana ta ꞌya̱pici ta̱wya̱ri gaa gura̱a̱ re̱ shami huku na̱ aba?>>
Sa̱i Biituru bwa bisa̱gi wyan kikiki hyo̱ iri na tanje̱, bwa hin,
<<Nꞌtane̱e̱ na̱ ce̱pe̱ na Joopa, ma nda ro̱pe̱, ga̱n nda̱i yaanyini haka ra̱rabi ga̱n nda̱i shika na zuzu na̱ mꞌbiin ndaabwa nꞌna̱nshin ma cíin to̱n wa̱ka̱mi.
Na ga̱n gwatani ki ga̱n nda̱i koya̱ iri na bikico̱ ina mꞌpirwa googoogoo na aga, na̱ koya̱ iri na bikico̱ na mꞌbuna nꞌna̱nshin, na̱ nꞌsuhwaa na̱ awyaanwyana, na̱ ano̱no̱ huku.
Ga̱n hange̱ mayaan mazama mꞌba hin, <Biituru, hiika̱, shinran, u-re̱ wuun.>
Ama ga̱n hin, <Majaa nda, Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n! Iyaanyini na zumaancin, koo ina za sabu, ita ta̱ncin nu nimi, kuꞌnꞌgira̱nshin nꞌnda̱a̱tu mꞌba yanshin.>
<<Sa̱i mazama mꞌba ra̱ni nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, mꞌba hin mareeko, <Iri na Hwe̱n bwa nje̱ sabu, tahyan wuun ishi na zumaancin.>
Iri ya̱nu tanda mataatu, naazhin iri na ne̱e̱ haku zuzu na yaburi na̱ iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ nde̱e̱be̱ be̱ kwashe̱e̱ke̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
<<Nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu to̱n, kaꞌawyatu taatu ya̱nu na aba takáji wa̱ka̱mi ta na̱ Kaisariya aba isagi na dubo na ina na ga̱n ne̱e̱ na̱ bwa.
Bihwaanwun be̱ hin xnꞌjwara̱ga wyan, xnꞌta sha̱a̱ nꞌgata ree. Aya̱too na̱nna cininhin ana taꞌnꞌíye̱ hara̱ ta̱jan ta̱ni ina na butu na̱nna naa takáji.
Sa̱i bwa ta̱bishi haruwa na bwa tanda̱i butuma naa Hwe̱n e̱she̱ na̱ ina ndaabwa, ma hyaan be̱, <Kada wyatu zhagu Joopa, aꞌnꞌgani Siima, bunaa aba gura̱a̱ nꞌgana Biituru.
Bwa ta na̱maa iyaagagi mazama nama gaa nii da̱ba ta̱mabiha̱na̱, gaa na̱ awyatu na ina ndaa hyo̱.>
<<Kuta̱naa pasa ta̱bisa̱ga̱ wyan mazama, kii-Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ cíin, be̱ ta̱ni wyan, haruwa na be̱ na ciin na̱ ga̱tu ta na̱ ayigo.
Sa̱i ga̱n mata̱ma̱nriin yaan ta̱cita̱ nata̱ Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu, haruwa na bwa na hyan, <Yoohana tandaga wyatu baba̱tiisa̱ma kuna̱ ma̱ni. Ama ga̱hin, nii Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n ta aba na̱maa ndaga ma baba̱tiisa̱ma.>
Na ta̱hyan Hwe̱n pa̱ni wyan ta̱yansun haku haruwa na bwa na ta̱pana taa ga̱tu, bike̱nye̱n naa ga̱tu tapana nꞌgata ku-Butu O̱to̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, iyaa ga̱n shi na hyan ma yansan Hwe̱n?>>
Na Ayaahudiya na jwarigi aba hange̱ kunnu, aba yancin ri na hyan acici, abaa yaba Hwe̱n ma hyaan, <<Ka̱i, hyo̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya taa, Hwe̱n ndaaki wyan haruwa na hyan apa̱ni pinsan baa, ade̱be̱ bina̱ na mahwa.>>
Awyatu na Yeesu na̱ ce̱pe̱ na Antiyaakiya
Bigudu naa wyatu na pa̱ni nꞌgata aba maga̱ci na̱ wana ngwan nii ke̱nye̱n naa aba tahoo kuna Isitafanu. Aka̱ aba huri ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Finikiya na̱ Kuburusu na̱ ce̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ Antiyaakiya na Suuriya. Abaa bisa̱ga̱ kana shi Ayaahudiya mazama nama Hwe̱n.
Ama aka̱ ana pa̱ni nꞌgata na̱ Kuburusu na̱ Kuraane, ana tahura̱ Antiyaakiya abaa bisa̱ga̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya mazama nama zumaa nama Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu.
Ta̱kai nata̱ ara na Hwe̱n ta̱ba ne̱e̱ huku na̱ aba, ta̱ba shaani wyatu hwarapi aba pa̱ni nꞌgata ndaaba, aba kíciike̱ aba jwarigi Yeesu.
Mazama nama iri na nje̱ na̱ Antiyaakiya, awyatu na Yeesu aba hange̱ muu na̱ ace̱be̱ ndaaba hyo̱ na̱ Hurushaliima. Aba ana Yeesu aba ka̱ji Bara̱naba zhagu Antiyaakiya.
Na bwa wuci, bwa nda̱i ri na gama na Hwe̱n bwa ndaaki wyan, bwa hange̱ gama, bwa duwa̱ni hyo̱ ana jwarigi bishita̱ naa ta̱hyan xaha̱mba̱ga̱ nꞌgata ndaaba ta̱pana hiku ku-Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu.
Bwa Bara̱naba taa bwa shi butu naa bina̱, bwa mꞌbaa ta̱kai nata̱a̱ gata ta̱pana na̱ Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n. Sa̱i wyatu hwarapi ba kúshitani Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu.
Bara̱naba piree na̱ Antiyaakiya, bwa huri Tarususu wyanzun na Shawulu.
Na bwa nda̱i Shawulu, bwa ꞌye̱e̱ bwa Antiyaakiya. Aba nje̱ yo̱ na munrun abaa mawuna̱a̱na̱, ma ga̱gaagana ana pa̱ni nꞌgata hwarapi. Na̱ Antiyaakiya ta aba na gira ta̱ꞌnꞌgana wyatu na Yeesu Akirisita.
Nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu ta ayaan cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama ana Hurushaliima ba na jaa Antiyaakiya.
Buka̱ kaba na naa, bunaa aba ta nꞌgana Agabusu, bwa hin kaki, bwa nje̱ mazama, na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n, bwa hin anii nda rumunro̱n naru o̱to̱ na̱ ce̱nye̱n nata̱ ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ na̱ta̱ Rooma ta̱hwarapi. (Ya̱nu ta nda ha̱ni na ta̱gwama nata̱ Kalaudiyusu bugwama naa o̱to̱ naa Rooma.)
Awyatu na jwarigi na Antiyaakiya koo buya̱ bwa mahin bunii kada na̱ ri na bwa nii ara ta̱pana kawyatu na jwarigi ana ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya.
Kunnunu aba na nda, aba pa̱ni Bara̱naba na̱ Shawulu xaꞌiyaagi wyatu o̱to̱ na wyatu na jwarigi na̱ Hurushaliima.

Wyatu na Yeesu za hunranhunran na gama
Na̱ ha̱ni ya̱nu, bugwama Hirudu Agiripa bwa ke̱ne̱ ta̱naa sha̱a̱ aka̱ ana pa̱ni nꞌgata ma kota̱ga̱na̱ wyan.
Hirudu bwa shaani aba kwane̱ Yaakubu nii sa̱nka̱ri, buya̱na̱ naa Yoohana.
Na Hirudu bwa nda̱i Ayaahudiya hange̱ gama na ri na bwa nje̱, bwa shaani aba kota̱ni Biituru taa, nii ke̱nye̱n naa Ubuki na Buroodi na za Yisiti nu.
Na asooja ba kota̱ni Biituru, aba zwa̱ga̱ni bwa na̱ zhaaro. Aba ta̱a̱gi asooja nꞌgudu nꞌna̱nshin nꞌna̱nshin xaha̱mba bwa. Hirudu bwa tahoo sha̱a̱ nii gata ndaabwa, bunii iya bwa paaka wyatu xandaaki bwa ta̱suuga̱ bike̱nye̱n naa Ubuki na Ta̱matamanrinyan Ta̱hanrinyan Nꞌina ta̱ba ba̱ni.
Na Biituru bwa ta naa na̱ zhaaro, wyatu na Yeesu aba maka̱nta̱ni ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ ro̱pe̱ ku-Hwe̱n.
Ta̱biha̱na̱ Biituru kuzhaaro
Na̱ gita na aba ja̱a̱ ba̱ha̱na̱ Biituru andaaki bwa ta̱suuga̱ jaa bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, Biituru ma kadaga na̱ akaca reeko, bwa taa awyantancin na asooja reeko ana hambe̱ bwa, na̱ ayaan ana hambe̱ adubo.
Mayaan mazama mꞌba za, butuma naa Hwe̱n bwa wuce, mayaan maza̱ki mꞌba ta̱ra̱ka̱ni paaka ba ne̱e̱ na̱ dura̱. Butuma naa Hwe̱n bwa pa̱sa̱gi Biituru nii biin bwa hiika̱hini bwa, bwa hin bwa, <<Hiika̱ na̱ ha̱ni.>> Akaca na takadaagi na̱ ara aba riijiga̱gi.
Butuma bwa gura̱a̱ hyan bwa, <<Kadaga kapa ndaa na̱ akandaga ndaa.>> Biituru bwa nje̱ kunnu. Butuma bwa gura̱a̱ hyan bwa, <<Taana da̱bi ndaa na o̱to̱, u-nꞌjwara̱ga banu.>>
Sa̱i bwa jwárige̱ butuma banu, bwa yancin iri na butuma bwaa nda ishi mahanda, bwa shii ta̱hyan iri haka ra̱rabi ta bwa nda̱i.
Na aba huri awyatu na hambe̱ ana yigo na̱ ana hin reenu, aba wuci paaka inco̱n na ta̱ruma na ba̱ni ce̱pe̱, ubwa inco̱n bwa magunii. Aba ba̱ni. Na aba wuci paaku yo̱n bwa swe̱n, kupita butuma bwa mahooshi na̱a̱ bwa.
Na aha̱nka̱ri na Biituru ba kúshiike̱, bwa mahin, <<Niina ye̱e̱ nꞌyan ushi mahanda Uhwe̱n ta káji butuma ndaabwa ta bwa mꞌbiha̱ni paaku nꞌara na n-Hirudu, na̱ hyo̱ maꞌwe̱n nama Ayaahudiya ba na nꞌsha̱a̱ga̱.>>
Na Biituru bwa nda̱i kiri be̱ shi, bwa ja̱a̱ ina na Maariyamu ada̱a̱da̱ na Yoohana na aba ta hyan Marukusu, paaka wyatu hwarapi ba mawuna̱ni abaa nda ro̱pe̱.
Bwa gba̱a̱nta̱ni adubo na ina, kiiyaan be̱e̱ biꞌa̱ naa tanaa nda tuma na̱ bwa ina naa aba ta hyan Rooda, be̱ shiikani xbinda̱i iyaa nu.
Na be̱ hange̱ nu na Biituru ta, be̱ guniincin dubo, be̱ kwashe̱e̱ke̱ ina na̱ ame̱ na sumo̱ wana ta̱ga̱da̱ri be̱ bishi wyatu na jwarigi ta̱hyan, <<Biituru ree e̱she̱ na dubo.>>
Aba hin buu, <<Bi-ndagi mꞌpe̱re̱.>> Be̱e̱ cita̱ga̱ ji. Aba shii ta̱hyan, <<Bihwaanwun ndaabwa nu.>>
Biituru bwaa gba̱a̱nta̱a̱na̱ ji. Na aba gunii aba nda̱i Biituru ta koo buya̱ bwa hin baka.
Bwa ndaaki wyan mazama na̱ ara anaa wau. Naazhin bwa bisa̱gi wyan haruwa na Hwe̱n bwa báhine̱ bwa zhaaro. Bwa hin wyan, <<Bisa̱ ma Yaakubu na̱ ayaan aya̱too iri na nje̱.>> Naazhin bwa huri kayaan pa̱ri.
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, asooja aba nje̱ kuma̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ wana ri na tanje̱ na̱ Biituru.
Na Hirudu bwa wya̱nzhin bwa, bwa nda̱ci bwa. Naazhin bwa nꞌgani ana tahambe̱ bwa ha̱nta̱a̱ni wyan, bwa shaani xakunai wyan.
Na maya̱nu mꞌba hwii, Hirudu bwa hiiki nii biin naa Yaahudiya, bwa huri Kaisariya xbupé̱e̱ nꞌhwe̱n kaun.
Hirudu Agiripa ꞌwi
Nii ke̱nye̱n be̱, Hirudu bwa gware̱ me̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na wyatu na Taaya na̱ ana Sidon. Nii gata ka̱, aba wuta̱ni Bilasa̱ta̱su butu o̱to̱ naa ka̱ta̱ku na ta̱gwama xbuguni wyan. Bwa ra̱ni ta̱hyan bunii guna̱ wyan. Naazhin aba ja̱a̱ paa Hirudu ta̱ma a̱sa̱a̱ga̱na̱ hunranhunran, na̱ wana kabata aba ta naa da̱baga shami paaku ce̱nye̱n nata̱ bwaa gwama.
Na̱ bwa hwe̱n na aba maꞌa̱sa̱ga̱ni, Hirudu bwa ta̱a̱ni da̱bi ndaabwa na ta̱gwama, bwa hunrani nii zhe̱nke̱n naa ta̱gwama, naazhin bwa bisa̱gi wyan mazama mahwarapi.
Naa gudu be̱ hange̱ ri na bwa cici, aba ta̱a̱ni nu, abaa hyaan, <<Ha̱nga ma maya̱nu! Unu na yaan hwe̱n nu, shici na butu wuma!>>
Kupita, buyaan butuma naa Hwe̱n bwa ta̱ be̱ suguma, na̱ wana buya̱ba̱ncin Hwe̱n. Acincin ba ta̱ni be̱, abaa re̱ be̱ hara̱ bwa ꞌwi.
Mazama nama zumaa nama Hwe̱n mꞌbaa mawyasa, awyatu na jwarigi abaa duwa̱na̱ kuta̱duwa̱na̱.
Na aba hwii tuma na aba na hyan wyan xanje̱, Bara̱naba na̱ Shawulu ba ga̱a̱ Hurushaliima aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱ Antiyaakiya, aba mata̱a̱go huku na̱ Yoohana bunaa aba ta hyan Marukusu.

Aka̱ji Bara̱naba na̱ Shawulu xanje̱ tuma na Hwe̱n
Na awyatu na Yeesu ana Antiyaakiya, ayaan acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi, azha̱a̱zha̱a̱ ndaaba na: Bara̱naba, Samiinu (bunaa aba ta hyan Bushiri) na̱ Lushiyusu na Kuraane, Manaaye (bunaa mawaani na̱ ina naa gwama Hirudu Antipasi), na̱ Shawulu.
Ha̱ni na abaa pagaga Hwe̱n hunrun nꞌruꞌure̱, Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ hin, <<Mꞌpe̱e̱nyin ma Bara̱naba na̱ Shawulu nii biin, na̱ wana tuma na ga̱n nꞌgani wyan xandaaki.>>
Na aba nje̱ ruꞌure̱ na̱ ro̱pe̱, aba ca̱guda̱a̱ga̱gi Bara̱naba na̱ Shawulu nꞌara na nꞌrubara̱ka, aba cipani wyan.
Bara̱naba na̱ Shawulu ja̱a̱ Kuburusu
Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n ka̱ji Bara̱naba aba na̱ Shawulu. Na yigo aba ja̱a̱ ce̱pe̱ na Salukiya, piree aba tata̱na̱ hantun na ma̱ni zhagu ucibiri na Kuburusu.
Na aba wuci ce̱pe̱ na Salamisi na ne̱e̱ na̱ Kuburusu, aba cita̱gi mazama nama Hwe̱n na̱ aka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya. Yoohana Marukusu na tanaawan na̱ aba bwaa guna̱a̱ wyan.
Na aba riini hyo̱ ucibiri, aba wuci ce̱pe̱ na Pafosa̱, aba ura̱ku na̱a̱ yaan Buyaahudiya bunaa aba ta hyan Buyoo Jooshuwa, bunaa ta naa gigiriga̱hina̱a̱ ri, bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama naa ta̱be̱,
bunaa ta naawan na̱ gwamina Sarijiyusu Bulusu. Gwamina bwa shi butu naa mꞌbaa ta̱yansun ta̱ꞌo̱to̱. Bwa nꞌgani Bara̱naba na̱ Shawulu wana xbuhange̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n.
Ama bunaa tanaa gigiriga̱hina̱a̱ ri Alimasa (ruzha̱a̱ rundaabwa runu n-Ta̱helena) bwa na ma̱a̱ncin ta̱ruba̱ ri na baa nda, bwaa nda haruwa na hyan xbuyanshin gwamina ta̱shiraga wyan wana hyan xuta panaa gata.
Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ pa̱ni Shawulu bunaa aba tahyan Bulusu ta̱kai, bwa ciita̱a̱gi Alimasa ayishe,
bwa hin, <<Gaa buyoo bupira̱! Gaa bu-nii nda kuda̱ga hyo̱ na̱ iri na gama! Bu-ma̱a̱ pira̱, gaa mꞌbaa maꞌwe̱n. Bi-jaa gaa iyo̱n na ka̱mbiga̱gi na Hwe̱n ta̱naa hanshinhina?
Niina Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n ta buusha̱a̱gi ara na ta̱swa ngwan, bunii shaana u-shi buruba̱. Bi-nii taa ke̱nye̱n bi-jaa huwa̱ga̱ pa̱ri.>> Kupita buka̱ na̱ ta̱yincincin ta̱ba guna̱ni ayishe ndaabwa, bwaa wyagadaga pa̱ri mawyanzan naa nii ka̱da̱ka̱ be̱.
Na gwamina bwa nda̱i ri na nje̱, bwa pa̱nii gata, bwa jikita̱ni nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ mazama nama Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu.
Bulusu nje̱ mazama na̱ Antiyaakiya na Pisidiya
Bulusu na̱ wyatu ndaabwa na ta̱hani aba ga̱a̱ Pafosa̱, aba ka̱ciga̱ni na̱ hantun na ma̱ni zhagu Para̱ga na ne̱e̱ na̱ ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Pamafiliya. Na̱ nꞌkaba Yoohana na aba ta hyan Marukusu bwa gáa wyan bwa kúshiike̱ Hurushaliima.
Aba ba re̱ iyeebe aba ta̱ ta̱hura̱ zhagu Antiyaakiya na ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Pisidiya. Hwe̱n na Ha̱nka̱na̱ aba ta̱ni ka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya aba hunraani.
Na aba hwii ta̱cita̱ga̱ takaada na Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa na̱ ana acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, awyatu o̱to̱ na ka̱ta̱ku aba nꞌgani wyan, aba hin, <<Aya̱too ma, kii mꞌbaa mayaan mazama nama ga̱hin nii duwa̱na̱ nꞌshita̱ ta̱ta awyatu, kusu nda ma.>>
Sa̱i Bulusu bwa hin kaki isa isa, bwa sha̱pa̱cigi ara na hyan xanje̱ wau, bwa hin, <<Ga̱hin aya̱too ma Isiraaꞌila, na̱ ayaan ana nii paga Hwe̱n hunrun, shiraaga ma!
Uhwe̱n na wyatu na Isiraaꞌila, utakasa adaadoo nda̱tu, bwa shaani bigudu yana be̱ nje̱ hwarapi ha̱ni na aba ne̱e̱ na̱ ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Masa, bwa gura̱a̱ báhine̱ wyan kuce̱nye̱n ta̱ba na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ huri koo ta̱ya̱.
Bwa nje̱ kuri na aba hara̱ nꞌyo̱ bihanda na̱ ahira̱ ceeku.
Bwa ra̱a̱ nꞌkorogo nꞌta̱nda̱ra̱ ce̱nye̱n, na̱ ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Kaꞌaana, bwa pa̱ni wyatu na Isiraaꞌila xahya̱su.
Iri ya̱nu na nda nꞌyo̱ yina̱ nꞌna̱nshin na̱ kuje ta.
<<Na mꞌba hwii, Hwe̱n bwa pa̱ni wyan awyatu na ta̱suuga̱, bwa wuci kiike̱nye̱n naa Samaaꞌila Bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama.
Ha̱ni ya̱nu wyatu aba wya̱nzhin xapa̱ni wyan bugwama. Sa̱i Hwe̱n bwa pa̱ni wyan Shawulu buyoo Kishi, butu naa bikorogo naa Be̱njami, bwa nje̱ ta̱gwama nꞌyo̱ handa.
Na Hwe̱n bwa ya̱a̱cigi Shawulu, bwa shii Dawuda bwa shi bugwama ndaaba, bunaa Hwe̱n bwa tacita̱ mazama mandaabwa nama ta̱hiku, ta̱hyan, <Ga̱n de̱be̱ Dawuda buyoo Yeese, bunaa nꞌce̱e̱n me̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, bunaa nii nꞌndaaka hyo̱ iri na ga̱n ribi.>
<<Paakii korogo naa butu na̱nna ta Hwe̱n bwa takadaagi Isiraaꞌila Yeesu, bunaa nii biha̱na̱ wyan haruwa na bwa tanda ala̱ka̱wa̱ri.
Ta Yeesu be̱ wuco, Yoohana na Baba̱tiisa̱ma bwa tahoo bisa̱ga̱ Aꞌisiraaꞌila hyo̱ ta̱hyan xapa̱ni pinsan baa, andagi wyan baba̱tiisa̱ma.
Ha̱ni na Yoohana bwa goki ta̱huwa̱ tuma ndaabwa, bwa hin, <Iyaa ga̱hin yan nꞌshi? Shii ga̱n ta nꞌshii bwa. Ama buyaan buwuci ta̱baa ta̱niimi bunaa ga̱n jwaci koo ta̱bwaciga akandaga ndaabwa.>
<<Ga̱hin aya̱too ma, bikorogo naa Ibiraahin, na̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya ana nii paga Hwe̱n hunrun, ga̱tu ta aba ta̱nꞌiyaagi mazama mana̱nna nama ta̱biha̱na̱.
Ana hunrani na̱ Hurushaliima na̱ wyatu o̱to̱ ndaaba, aba e̱nshe̱nshe̱n Yeesu ta shi naa nii biha̱na̱ wyan, aba gura̱a̱ci insan mazama nama acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama nama aba tanaa cita̱a̱ga̱ koya̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ ndaaba. Ama aba ciga̱hini mazama nama acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama paaka aba taꞌya̱pi mazama nama ta̱kuna Yeesu.
Tana ta̱hyan binje̱ce̱ pinsan na hyan xakwane̱ buu, ama mꞌba kakici wyan, aba ro̱pe̱ Bilaatu bupa̱ni wyan buu akwane̱.
Na aba ciga̱hini hyo̱ iri na aba na taga na̱ wana nde̱e̱be̱, aba cíinha̱ni buu kuguguji na ꞌwe̱e̱, aba zwa̱ga̱ni buu kuꞌuya̱.
Ama Hwe̱n bwa hiika̱hini buu kuta̱ꞌwa̱.
Mahwarapi be̱ tanaa jábagi kawyatu na tajwárige̱ buu na̱ Gaalili zhagu Hurushaliima, niina aba ta shi ana nii bisa̱ga̱ awyatu nda̱tu ri ya̱nu hiku.
<<Ga̱tu ta̱a̱ bisa̱gi ma mazama maya̱nu nama zumaa, nama Hwe̱n bwa tanda ala̱ka̱wa̱ri na̱ adaadoo,
butaciga̱hina̱ muu, kuga̱tu na shi mꞌmwaan nꞌndaaba, ha̱ni na bwa tahiika̱hina̱ Yeesu kuta̱ꞌwa̱. Haruwa na mꞌba ta̱gi ku-Zaabura na hin reenu, ta̱hyan,
<< <Gaa be̱e̱ biniimi ta,
ba̱re mꞌmabisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan nꞌshi ashibo.>
Hwe̱n tahiika̱hina̱ Yeesu kuta̱ꞌwa̱, na̱ wana ta̱hyan bijaa gura̱a̱ ꞌwa̱ mayaan, koo ta̱pwasa. Kunnunu, Hwe̱n taciga̱hina̱ ta̱cita̱ ta̱ndaabwa ta̱hyan,
<< <Ga̱n na̱maa pana rubara̱ka naru ta̱sabu, naru ga̱n tanda ala̱ka̱wa̱ri nꞌnii ndaaka Dawuda.>
Uyaan Zaabura uhin,
<< <Bujaa gaa Buyata ndaabi naa ne̱e̱ Sabu xbuposhi.>
<<Na Dawuda be̱ hwii tuma na Hwe̱n bwa tapana buu na̱ ha̱ni nde̱e̱be̱, be̱ ꞌwi, aba wuma̱ni buu huku na daadoo nde̱e̱be̱, ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ ta̱ba poshi.
Ama bunaa Hwe̱n bwa tahiika̱hina̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱, butaposhishi na̱ uya̱.
<<Na̱ wana kunnu aya̱too ma, yansun ma ta̱hyan paa butu na̱nna Yeesu kata ga̱tuu bishi ma ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ncin pinsan ninhin.
Waabe̱ kata hyo̱ bunaa ra̱a̱ buu, Hwe̱n bwa nii ndaya ta̱hyan bushi naa bina̱, paaku Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa mꞌba jaa ara ta̱nda na̱ pinsan hyo̱.
Na̱ wana kunnu, kwayaa xbunaa za̱nda̱, wana iri na ta̱gi ina acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama aba tacita̱ ita jaa nje̱ na̱ ga̱hin, ta̱hyan Hwe̱n hin,
<< <Shiraaga ma, ga̱hin ana tanaa maꞌnꞌhusagana ma ꞌwa̱ nꞌratu!
Jikita̱na̱ ma iꞌwa̱gi!
Na ta̱hyan ga̱n nii nda yaan tuma nii ke̱nye̱n niinhin,
una ga̱hin jaa panaa gata na̱ bwa,
koo buyaan buubishi ma.> >>
Na Bulusu na̱ Bara̱naba ba ba̱ni kuka̱ta̱ku, sa̱i aba ro̱pe̱ wyan xakúshiike̱ yaan hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na wuci agura̱a̱ nda iri na mꞌba mazama.
Naa gudu be̱ ga̱ta̱a̱gi, awyatu hwarapi aba jwarigi Bulusu na̱ Bara̱naba, Ayaahudiya na̱ ana tata̱na̱ adiini ndaaba. Aba reeko ba ro̱pe̱ wyan ta̱hyan xaꞌisa hiku ata̱ ta̱hura̱ nꞌta̱pana nꞌgata ku-Hwe̱n.
Na bwa hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ bwa riini, awyatu haku hyo̱ ce̱pe̱ aba mawuna̱ni ba shiraagi mazama nama Yeesu.
Na awyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya aba nda̱i hwarapi na wyatu, aba ribici mahwa. Aba pa̱shi ta̱hyaan mazama nama Bulusu mashici mahanda ma nda mazama nama hwashe̱.
Ama aba reeko, aba pa̱shi ta̱naa bisa̱ga̱ wyan mazama rukwanyan ruba za, aba hin, <<Ga̱hin taa shi ana yigo ana hyan aabisa̱gi ma mazama nama zumaa nama Yeesu. Too, ta na ga̱hin ga̱a̱ muu, ga̱hin nda̱i ta̱hyan ishici ana nii nda bina̱ na mahwa. Ta na mꞌbashi kunnu, niina ta̱nii jaga paaka na shiici Ayaahudiya.
Na̱ wana kunta ta Uhwe̱n bwa ta̱nhin, paa ubwa hin,
<< <Iishii, ushi ta̱gwaan kana shici Ayaahudiya
na̱ wana u-íye̱ ta̱biha̱na̱ hara̱ kuta̱huwo hyo̱ nata̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana.> >>
Na ana shici Ayaahudiya aba hange̱ kunnu, aba hange̱ gama ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, aba ya̱ba̱ni ta̱cita̱ nata̱ Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu. Hyo̱ ana bana sha̱a̱ga̱ ta̱da̱ba bina̱ na mahwa aba pa̱ni nꞌgata.
Mazama nama Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu mꞌbaa duwa̱na̱ kuta̱naa mawyasa na̱ nꞌta̱ba ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ ta̱ba ce̱nye̱n hyo̱.
Ama Ayaahudiya aba zwage̱ ayaan a̱ ana aba ta pa hunrun, ana jwarigi Hwe̱n ki, na̱ ayaan wyatu o̱to̱ na ce̱pe̱ aba hiika̱hini suha̱nka̱ri nasu wyatu. Aba pa̱ Bulusu na̱ Bara̱naba ngwan, aba pa̱ wyan sumo̱ na̱ ce̱pe̱.
Bulusu na̱ Bara̱naba aba bukuta̱gi aputu na mꞌbuna ndaaba tabisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan Hwe̱n ga̱a̱ wyan. Naazhin aba huri ce̱pe̱ na Ikooniya.
Awyatu na Antiyaakiya na jwarigi Yeesu aba hange̱ gama ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ ne̱e̱ huku na̱ aba ma duwa̱na̱ wyan ta̱kai.

Bulusu na̱ Bara̱naba ne̱e̱ na̱ Ikooniya
Na̱ Ikooniya, Bulusu na̱ Bara̱naba aba gura̱a̱ nda kuharuwa na ba tanaa ndaga, aba ta̱ni ka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya. Ayaahudiya na̱ ayaan wyatu na shici Ayaahudiya ahwarapi aba ra̱a̱ mazama mandaaba.
Ama ayaan Ayaahudiya na ra̱a̱ci mazama mandaaba, abaa zuga ma hanshinhina ana shici Ayaahudiya ta̱hyan xata tuba̱ mazama mꞌba.
Koo na mꞌbashi kunnu, Bulusu na̱ Bara̱naba aba ta̱a̱ ke̱nye̱n kaun, ma bisa̱ga̱ wyan mazama nama zumaa nama Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bigata ka̱. Butu O̱to̱ bwa nje̱ tuma na̱ ka̱i ndaabwa, paaku bwa shaani ana be̱ tazwara abaa ndaga iri na ta̱jikita̱na̱.
Ama wyatu na bwa ce̱pe̱ aba mahooshi maree, aka̱ ba jwarigi Ayaahudiya, ayaan wyatu aka̱ ba jwarigi ana Yeesu be̱ tazwara.
Aka̱ Ayaahudiya huku na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ ndaaba na̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya, aba maga̱ga̱a̱gi haruwa na aba nii ndaaka ana be̱ tazwara ri na zumaancin, ata̱gi wyan atari.
Na aba hange̱ iri na Ayaahudiya aba ribi ta̱nda, aba gida̱ga̱gi zhagu kuꞌace̱pe̱ na Lisitira na̱ Darabe kuꞌnꞌyaan nꞌcice̱pe̱ nꞌndaaba na nꞌne̱e̱ na̱ mꞌbiin nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Likooniya.
Kaba aba tare̱ iyeebe nꞌta̱cita̱ga̱ mazama nama zumaa.
Bulusu cita̱gi mazama nama zumaa Lisitira
Ha̱ni na aba ne̱e̱ na̱ Lisitira, buyaan butu bunaa aba ma̱ncin gurubi bwa ja̱ba̱gici bwa hunrani.
Bwa shiragi ku-Bulusu bwaa bisa̱ga̱ wyan mazama nama zumaa. Sa̱i Bulusu bwa gwatagi be̱ ki bwa e̱nshe̱n ta̱hyan butu na̱nna bupa̱nii gata kumazama na hyan xakuda̱gahini be̱.
Sa̱i Bulusu bwa ta̱a̱ni nu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ bwa hin, <<Hiika̱, u-maꞌisaaga na̱ mꞌbuna nꞌndaabi.>> Butu bwa hin kaki, bwa pa̱shi ta̱hani.
Naa gudu be̱ nda̱i ri na Bulusu bwa nje̱, abaa ta ta̱ꞌungwa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ce̱pe̱ ta̱ndaaba aba hin, <<Mahanda, ayaan hwe̱n cíin ba̱re wa̱tu na̱ mꞌpirwa na nꞌwyatu.>>
Aba pa̱gi wyan azha̱a̱zha̱a̱ na ahwe̱n ndaaba na̱ n-Ta̱helena. Bara̱naba bwa shi Zeyusu, Bulusu bwa shi Heremesu wana bwa taa shi bugwama naa mazama.
Sa̱i gumagira̱ na o̱to̱ na Zeyusu bunaa dura̱ ndaabwa na gumagira̱ bwa ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱baa nata̱ ce̱pe̱, bwa shápi inaa na̱ nꞌta̱sumu nata̱ ruzhanna xapa̱ wyan hunrun. Bwa ꞌwaan na̱ inco̱n na ce̱pe̱, bwa na̱ awyatu aba hiin shinraanwyan wyan ibe̱ inaa.
Ama na Bara̱naba na̱ Bulusu aba hange̱ iri na hiin nda, aba ha̱nda̱a̱gi ada̱bi ndaaba wana ame̱ ta̱gura, aba gida̱ga̱gi zhagu paa wyatu ma hyaan,
<<Na̱ wana ba̱ ga̱hin nda kunna? Awyatu wuma ta ga̱tu shi haku ga̱hin, ta̱a̱ꞌiyaagi ma mazama nama zumaa, na̱ wana iga̱a̱ iri yata na uwa̱, ikúshiike̱ ku-Hwe̱n na ne̱e̱ buwuma, una nje̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, nꞌce̱nye̱n, na̱ rwaga na o̱to̱ hyo̱ na̱ iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ aba.
Na yigo utagaa awyatu na sa̱ra̱ri yana xajwara̱ga iyo̱n goo goo.
Hyo̱ mꞌmazama maya̱nu, uta ga̱a̱ci hyuhyu ndaabwa na za yaan ri na gama na bwa bisa̱a̱ na bwa nje̱. Ubwa ta taa pa ma ashira̱, na̱ ushuyo na gama. Uuciga̱hini ma na̱ shami, inje̱ ta̱ga̱da̱ri.>>
Hyo̱ na̱ mazama maya̱nu dike̱ aba taꞌara ta̱yansan awyatu ashinraanyin wyan inaa apa̱ wyan hunrun.
Aba manda kunnu sa̱i ayaan Ayaahudiya aba jaa ta na̱ Antiyaakiya na̱ Ikooniya aba huri kai na awyatu na ce̱pe̱. Aba ta̱gi Bulusu tari, aba buburi bwa ta̱baa nata̱ ce̱pe̱ ta̱hyan buhoo ꞌwa̱.
Sa̱i ana jwarigi Yeesu aba riini bwa, bwa hiiki, bwa kwashe̱e̱ke̱ ame̱ na ce̱pe̱. Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, bwa huri Darabe huku na̱ Bara̱naba.
Kushiikwa Antiyaakiya na Suuriya
Na Bulusu na̱ Bara̱naba ba cita̱gi mazama nama zumaa na̱ Darabe, aba de̱be̱ ana jwarigi hwarapi kaun, aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱ Lisitira na̱ Ikooniya na̱ Antiyaakiya na Pisidiya.
Abaa duwa̱ni ana jwarigi nꞌshita̱ ta̱taga, ma bisa̱ga̱ wyan xaꞌisa hiku na̱ nꞌgata ndaaba ta̱pana ku-Hwe̱n, ma hyaan wyan, <<Ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ ta̱nswa̱ ngwan ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ga̱tu ribi ta̱ta̱na̱ kuta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n.>>
Aba de̱e̱be̱ wyan wyatu o̱to̱ kiikoya̱ gudu naa awyatu na Yeesu aba ne̱e̱. Aba ro̱pe̱ Hwe̱n huku nꞌta̱re̱ce̱ shami na̱ wana ndaaba, aba pa̱ni wyan ku-Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu naa aba pa̱ni nꞌgata na̱a̱ bwa.
Sa̱i aba ba̱ni kuce̱nye̱n nata̱ Pisidiya zhagu Pamafiliya.
Na aba cita̱gi mazama nama Hwe̱n na̱ Para̱ga, aba huri ce̱pe̱ na Ataaliya.
Piree kata aba na ta̱na̱ hantun na ma̱ni kushiikwa Antiyaakiya na Suuriya, paa ta na̱ ayigo aba tapana wyan nu na bure kutuma ndaaba na aba hwii.
Na aba wuci, aba wuna̱ni wyatu na Yeesu, aba cita̱gi hyo̱ iri na Hwe̱n bwa ndaaki wyan, na̱ haruwa na Hwe̱n bwa guna̱a̱nyin ana shici Ayaahudiya uyo̱n na ta̱panaa gata.
Aba ta̱a̱ ke̱nye̱n na wyatu na jwarigi kaun.

Awyatu o̱to̱ na jwarigi mawuna̱ni na̱ Hurushaliima
Sa̱i ayaan wyatu ana báni ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahudiya, aba jaa Antiyaakiya, abaa ga̱gaagana ana pa̱ni nꞌgata ta̱hyan, <<Sa̱i kaaꞌya̱pa̱gi ma ta̱wya̱ri ku-Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa mꞌba hin, kushii nuunu ijaa bina̱na̱.>>
Shii wumo̱ na ta̱ge̱ Bulusu na̱ Bara̱naba aba tanda na̱ mꞌba mazama. Awyatu o̱to̱ ndaaba aba shaani Bulusu na̱ Bara̱naba na̱ ayaan awyatu ana pa̱ni nꞌgata xaja̱a̱ Hurushaliima andái awyatu o̱to̱ na̱ ana be̱ tazwara ana ne̱e̱ kaun, amagá̱gaagi na̱ wana mꞌba mazama.
Sa̱i awyatu na Yeesu aba ka̱ji wyan, aba jwara̱gani kuce̱nye̱n nata̱ Finikiya na̱ Samaariya ma bisa̱ga̱ awyatu mazama nama kawyatu na shici Ayaahudiya aba pa̱ni nꞌgata nꞌndaaba. Uya̱nu bwa shani hyo̱ ana pa̱ni nꞌgata nje̱ ta̱ga̱da̱ri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Na aba wuci Hurushaliima, hyo̱ awyatu na Yeesu na̱ ana be̱ tazwara na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ ndaaba na jwarigi, aba zumani wyan na̱ wuco. Sa̱i Bulusu na̱ Bara̱naba aba bisa̱gi wyan ku-Hwe̱n bwa nje̱ tuma na̱ aba.
Ama ayaan ndaaba ana shi Afaraasiya aba hiiki aba hin, <<Ana jwarigi aba shici Ayaahudiya ta̱hyan ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ sa̱i kaꞌya̱pa̱gi wyan ta̱wya̱ri agura̱a̱ jwara̱ga nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa.>>
Ana be̱ tazwara na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ aba hunrani xahange̱ kaba nii nda mꞌmaba mazama.
Na aba ta̱a̱ ke̱nye̱n ma maga̱a̱ga̱nu, sa̱i Biituru bwa hiiki bwa hin wyan, <<Aya̱too ma iyan ta̱hyan ta na̱ ayigo Uhwe̱n taꞌnꞌkasa ga̱n na̱ ame̱ nda̱tu ta̱hyan wa̱ka̱mi kata awyatu ana shici Ayaahudiya baa ha̱nga mazama nama zumaa, apa̱ni nꞌgata.
Uhwe̱n na yan bigata naa koo buya̱, bwa bisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan ura̱a̱ wyan paa bwa tapana wyan Hwaanwun ndaabwa, kubwa ta̱mpa̱ni ga̱tu.
Ubwa bisa̱a̱ci ta̱hura̱ ta̱ruba̱ kunga̱tu na̱ aba, na bwa ta a̱sa̱a̱ga̱na̱ nꞌgata nꞌndaaba paa ta̱pana nꞌgata ku-Yeesu.
Na̱ wana kunnu, iba̱ shani ga̱hin hiin maanwyana Hwe̱n, na ga̱hin hiin ta̱ndana hyo̱ ana jwarigi iꞌwaa ina ga̱tu koo adaadoo nda̱tu zaa naa taꞌara ta̱shapa?
Ama ga̱tu pa̱ni nꞌgata nꞌnda̱a̱tu ta̱hyan na̱ nꞌta̱pana ꞌye̱n nata̱ Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu ta̱ta ga̱tu de̱be̱ ta̱nda bina̱ haruwa na aba de̱be̱ taa ta̱nda bina̱.>>
Hyo̱ awyatu na tamawuna̱na̱ aba nje̱ wau na aba shiragi Bara̱naba na̱ Bulusu nii bisa̱ga̱ wyan ku-Hwe̱n bwa nje̱ iri na ta̱hyan baka na̱ nꞌta̱jikita̱na̱ na̱ aba kana shici Ayaahudiya.
Na aba hwii mazama, sa̱i Yaakubu bwa hiiki bwa hin, <<Aya̱too ma, nꞌshiraga ma.
Ku-Siima Biituru bwa tanaa bisa̱ga̱ haruwa na ku-Hwe̱n bwa tabisa̱a̱ ta̱ruba̱ ta na̱ ayigo kana shici Ayaahudiya, bwa ka̱shi ayaan kiigudu ndaaba aba shi andaabwa.
Una̱nna ta nje̱ to̱n na̱ mꞌmazama nama acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, kaba ta̱ muu ta̱hyan,
<< <Shii kumaya̱nu, nꞌnii gura̱a̱ kúshe̱
ma gura̱a̱ ma iꞌina naa gwama Dawuda na huzhi.
Koo na ibe̱ ga̱ta̱a̱gi, nꞌnii gura̱a̱ ma wuun,
ma hiika̱hina̱ wuun.
Na̱ kunta ta ana bwe̱ aba nii nama nꞌwyanzan ga̱n Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n,
nꞌne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan, ana shici Ayaahudiya ana ga̱n ka̱shi xashi nimi.
Kunnu Uhwe̱n bwa tacita̱,
bwaa naa tandaga hyo̱ iri ya̱nu atahoo yansun wuun ta mꞌmagwashe̱.> >>
Yaakubu bwa re̱ iyeebe mꞌmazama ta̱hyan, <<Na̱ wana kunnu, nꞌnda̱i ta̱hyan xta̱ta mꞌmaa ma ta̱kaka ana shici Ayaahudiya ana hwii kuta̱kíciike̱ ta̱jwara̱ga Hwe̱n.
Uhuri ta̱hyan ta̱ndaaki wyan utakaada, ta̱bishi wyan xata nda iri na nii shana wyan ta̱shiri ina gumaka, xata nda banshaun, xata re̱ sunda na aba pigira̱ni ruru, na̱ sunda ta̱re̱ huku mꞌmahiin.
Na̱ wana ta na̱ ayigo, na̱ koya̱ ce̱pe̱ awyatu tanaa, ana ta naa sa̱ anaa ga̱gaagana awyatu Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa aba ta naa sa̱ cita̱ga̱ muu na̱ aka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya koya̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya.>>
Utakaada una báni kawyatu o̱to̱ ana pa̱ni nꞌgata
Too, sa̱i ana be̱ tazwara na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ hyo̱ awyatu na Yeesu aba nda̱i ta̱hyan, uzumaa na hyan aka̱shi aka̱ ndaaba aka̱ji wyan Antiyaakiya huku na̱ Bulusu na̱ Bara̱naba. Sa̱i aba ka̱shi Yaahuda bunaa aba tahyan Bara̱saba, na̱ Saila, ana shi awyatu o̱to̱ kana jwarigi.
Aba pa̱ni wyan utakaada una tahyan:
<<Utakaada una báni kaya̱na̱nhin ana Yeesu be̱ tazwara na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na ana jwarigi, ana hunrani na̱ Hurushaliima. Zhagu kaya̱too nda̱tu ana shici Ayaahudiya na̱ Antiyaakiya na̱ ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Suuriya na̱ nata̱ Kilikiya. Azumanu!
Ta̱hange̱ ta̱hyan ayaan wyatu nda̱tu aahiika̱hini ma aha̱nka̱ri ninhin na̱ mꞌmazama mandaaba nama abaa bisa̱ga̱ ma, ga̱tu ta ga̱tu ta ka̱jici wyan.
Na̱ wana kunnu ta hyo̱ nda̱tu ga̱tu nda̱i tahyan uhuri gama ta̱a̱kádaagi ma ayaan wyatu, na̱ aribi nda̱tu Bara̱naba na̱ Bulusu,
ana shi na pa̱ni suhyu sundaaba na̱ wana Butu O̱to̱ nda̱a̱tu Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Ta shani ga̱tu káji Yaahuda na̱ Saila na hyan aabisa̱gi ma na̱ nu ndaaba iri na shi na ga̱tu tági.
Na ta̱hyan Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n nda̱i uzumaa ga̱tu ga̱tu nda̱i taa kunnu, ta̱hyan xataa sha̱a̱ga̱ ma iꞌwaa nama maca̱ma̱nta̱n na huri na̱nna na shi ga̱ga̱ga̱:
Bwa tashi, ma pe̱e̱n ma kushami na aba ndaaki gumaka. Ta-re̱ ma sunda huku mꞌmahiin koo iri na aba pigira̱ni ruru. Ta-naa nda ma banshaun. Kiiꞌa̱ri ta̱mapyaan kiri ya̱nu hyo̱, inje̱ iri na ta̱to̱n.
Iha̱nka̱ni gumunu.>>
Hyo̱ ana ba takada tuma, aba huri Antiyaakiya. Na aba wuci, aba wuta̱ni ana pa̱ni nꞌgata aba pa̱ni wyan bwa takaada.
Na aba cita̱gi ubwa takaada, aba nje̱ ta̱ga̱da̱ri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ wana mazama nama aba hange̱ nama duwa̱ni wyan shita̱ ta̱ta.
Sa̱i Yaahuda na̱ Saila, ana shi acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, aba ndaaki ana pa̱ni nꞌgata mꞌbashi numa na̱ mꞌmayaan mazama mahwarapi nama duwa̱ni wyan ta̱ta shita̱ na̱ nꞌgata ndaaba.
Na aba pé̱e̱ kaun nꞌhwe̱n, ana pa̱ni nꞌgata ba cipani wyan gumunu, aba hure kuswa Hurushaliima kana ta kada wyan tuma.+ :33 Ta̱yaan ta̱taga nata̱ yigo ta̱ka̱ ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa aaya na 34 kunna: Ama Saila bwa nda̱i ta̱hyan uzumaa na hyan bunaa kaun kwan.Bulusu na̱ Bara̱naba aba pa̱ nꞌhwe̱n kaun na̱ Antiyaakiya. Aba na̱ ayaan wyatu hwarapi ana nii ga̱gaagana, abaa gura̱a̱ nda mazama nama Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu kaun.
Bulusu na̱ Bara̱naba amahooshi
Na nꞌhwe̱n mꞌba huri hwarapi, sa̱i Bulusu bwa hin Bara̱naba, <<xTa̱ja̱ba̱gi kuꞌnꞌcice̱pe̱ na nꞌga̱tu tahoo jabaga ga̱tu bisa̱gi awyatu mazama nama Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu, ta̱nnda̱i kana pa̱ni nꞌgata aba re̱ iyeebe mꞌmaba.>>
Bara̱naba butaruba̱ ta̱shapa Yoohana bunaa aba ta hyan Marukusu ahuri da̱nda̱.
Ama Bulusu bwa nga̱zhin na̱ kuda̱ga ta̱hyan xata hura̱ da̱nda̱. Wana ta̱hyan Yoohana Marukusu tagaa wyan ta na̱ ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Pamafiliya bwa jaa gura̱a̱ nda tuma na baa nda, da̱nda̱ na ba.
Abaa maga̱a̱ga̱nu, hara̱ ta̱ba ꞌye̱e̱ wyan aba mahooshi. Bara̱naba bwa sha̱pi Marukusu aba ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni, aba huri ucibiri na Kuburusu.
Bulusu bwa ka̱shi Saila. Ana jwarigi ba pa̱ni wyan nu na bure, sa̱i aba huri.
Sa̱i aba jwara̱gani kuꞌnꞌcice̱pe̱ na n-Suuriya na̱ Kilikiya, ma duwa̱ga̱na̱ shita̱ ta̱taga kuꞌawyatu na Yeesu.

Timooti jwarigi Bulusu na̱ Saila
Bulusu ja̱a̱ Darabe na̱ Lisitira. Buyaan butanaa bunaa pa̱nii gata, bunaa ruzha̱a̱ rundaabwa ruba shi Timooti. Be̱e̱ binaa buyaan buꞌa̱a̱ Ta̱yaahudiya naa pa̱nii gata, ashin ba shi Buhelena.
Awyatu na pa̱ni nꞌgata ana Lisitira na̱ Ikooniya aba tanaa yaba bwa.
Bulusu bwa taruba̱ Timooti ꞌye̱e̱ be̱. Na̱ wana hyo̱ Ayaahudiya ana hunrani kaun ayan ta̱hyan ashin shi Buhelena, sa̱i bwa nje̱ mazama na̱ Timooti bwa sha̱pi bwa aba kaꞌya̱pi bwa ta̱wya̱ri.
Na aba huri ma jwara̱gagana nꞌcice̱pe̱ nꞌcice̱pe̱ ma bisa̱ga̱ awyatu kaun mazama nama takaada na báni kana be̱ tazwara na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na jwarigi na̱ Hurushaliima kabaa jwara̱ga muu.
Na̱ kunnu awyatu na Yeesu abaa duwa̱na̱ nꞌshita̱ na̱ nꞌta̱pana nꞌgata na̱ hwarapi koya̱ hwe̱n.
Bulusu nda̱i ri haka ra̱rabi na butu naa Makidooniya
Sa̱i aba jwara̱gagani kuce̱nye̱n nata̱ Firijiya na̱ Galaatiya, na̱ wana Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n yanshin wyan ta̱nda mazama nama zumaa na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Aasiya.
Na aba wuce kuharu na Misiya, aba ribi ta̱ta̱na̱ Bitiniya ama Bihwaanwun naa Yeesu be̱ yanshin wyan ta̱ta̱na̱.
Aba jwara̱gani Misiya, aba huri cuun kuce̱pe̱ na Toruwasu.
Na gita bwa nje̱ Bulusu bwa nda̱i yaanyini haka ra̱rabi. Bwa nda̱i butu naa Makidooniya, bwa e̱she̱ ma rupa be̱ ta̱hyan, <<Kusu jaa Makidooniya u-ta̱guni.>>
Bulusu ma ndaya ibe̱ ri haka ra̱rabi, sa̱i ga̱tu nje̱ shiri na̱ ha̱ni ga̱tu ja̱a̱ ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Makidooniya, na̱ wana ta̱yan ta̱hyan Uhwe̱n ta ta̱ꞌnꞌgani na hyan ta̱ja̱a̱ ta̱ndaaki wyan mazama nama zumaa.
Liidiya pa̱nii gata na̱ Yeesu
Ga̱tu ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni na̱ Toruwasu ga̱tu ka̱mbigi ta̱hani kucibiri na ce̱pe̱ na Samutarikiya. Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n ga̱tu re̱ iyeebe kuce̱pe̱ na Niyapolisu.
Na̱ nꞌkaba ga̱tu huri Filibi ubwa tashi uce̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ na Makidooniya. Uce̱pe̱ na Filibi bwa shi na ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ na ta̱gwama nata̱ o̱to̱ nata̱ Rooma. Ga̱tu pa̱ kaun nꞌhwe̱n.
Na̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya ga̱tu ba̱ni dubo na ce̱pe̱ ga̱tu huri inza̱n na wyanfo̱n, paa ga̱tu shii ta̱hyan awyatu nii ura̱ku kaun paa ro̱pe̱ ta̱nda. Ga̱tu hunrani pita ga̱tu nje̱ mazama na̱ aꞌa̱ na tamawuna̱na̱ kaun.
Na̱ ame̱ na aꞌa̱ na tanaa kaun, buyaan butanaa, naa ba ta nꞌgana Liidiya bunaa tajwara̱ga Hwe̱n na Ayaahudiya. Buta sha naa báni ce̱pe̱ na Tayatira, bwa tanaa sa̱a̱nha̱na̱a̱ ayaadi na mꞌbaa yuwa o̱to̱ ana ma̱ni nama shenje. Bwa ta̱shiragi, Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n bwa gunii bigata ndaabwa, bwa pa̱nii gata na̱ iri na Bulusu bwaa cita̱ga̱.
Bubwa a̱, na̱ ana ina ndaabwa ba ndagi wyan baba̱tiisa̱ma, sa̱i bwa ta̱ro̱pe̱, bwa hin, <<Kiiꞌnꞌsha̱pi ta̱hyan nꞌshi naa pa̱nii gata ku-Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu, xta̱ja̱a̱ ma ina nimi.>> Bwa ta̱kaki ji, ga̱tu ja̱a̱.
Abwake̱ Bulusu na̱ Saila na̱ zhaaro
Uyaan hwe̱n na ga̱tu jaga paa ro̱pe̱ ta̱nda, ga̱tu ura̱ku nii yaan be̱e̱ biꞌa̱, binaa shi bugyama. Be̱ mꞌbaa butu naa hira̱, be̱ shi naa tanaa ndaga shiga, be̱ tanaa da̱a̱baga ana hya̱a̱ buu ayuwa o̱to̱.
Be̱ be̱e̱ biꞌa̱ be̱ ta̱jwárige̱ ta̱baa, ma taa nu mahyaan, <<Ana̱nna wyatu agyama na Hwe̱n na Hura̱gi Ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ta, ahin maa bisa̱ga̱ ma ta suga̱hin nda ibini.>>
Be̱e̱ cita̱ga̱ kunnu nꞌhwe̱n hwarapi. Sa̱i Bulusu bwa gware̱ me̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, bwa ke̱ce̱e̱ke̱ bwa hin bubwa butu naa hira̱, <<Na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, iihin bana na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ be̱e̱ bina̱nna!>> Kupita butu naa hira̱ bwa ba̱ni bwa ga̱a̱ buu.
Na ana hya̱a̱ be̱e̱ bibe̱e̱ aba nda̱i ta̱hyan uyo̱n na ba ta naa da̱ba yuwa na̱ bwa guna̱ni, aba kota̱ni Bulusu na̱ Saila, aba ꞌye̱e̱ wyan kawyatu o̱to̱ na kasuwa.
Na aba ꞌye̱e̱ wyan kuꞌuba̱ na awyatu o̱to̱ na ta̱suuga̱, aba hin, <<Awyatu na̱nna Ayaahudiya, anii ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ ce̱pe̱ nda̱tu hyo̱.
Aba nii gura̱a̱ ga̱gaagana iri na shici na hyan ta̱jwara̱ga, koo ta̱naa nda, wana ta̱hyan ta̱shi Arooma.>>
Awyatu ba mazooni huku na̱ aba, sa̱i awyatu o̱to̱ na ta̱suuga̱ aba shaani xata̱a̱ciga̱gi wyan aꞌwana ndaaba nꞌtugusu ma handaaga wyan, aba da̱ba̱gi wyan na̱ angwo.
Na aba hwii wyan ta̱da̱ba̱ga̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, aba shani aba ꞌye̱e̱ wyan zhaaro, aba hin butu naa ta ha̱mba xbuha̱mba wyan ki, xata jaa gida̱ga̱gi.
Bunaa ta ha̱mba na bwa hange̱ kunnu, bwa pa̱gici wyan ha̱ba̱ sa̱i bwa ꞌye̱e̱ wyan udura̱ na ta na̱ ame̱, bwa ca̱guda̱ga̱ni mꞌbuna ndaaba na̱ ꞌwe̱e̱ na ta ha̱mba̱ga̱ mꞌbuna bwa bwake̱.
Tapiree na̱ gita hooso, Bulusu na̱ Saila abaa nda ro̱pe̱ ma zhinyaan zha̱a̱ na yabi na Hwe̱n, ayaan taa na aba tabukaka na̱ zhaaro aba shiraagi.
Mayaan mꞌba za sa̱i ce̱nye̱n ta̱ba mazha̱a̱nta̱ni ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na tashana kunrin na aba she̱re̱ ta̱ba ta̱ma bwa zha̱a̱nta̱ni. Sudubo hyo̱ suba guna̱a̱nyin ha̱ni ka̱, akaca ana koo buya̱ bunaa aba tabuka aba rigijigi.
Butu naa ta ha̱mba zhaaro bwa zhe̱mbe̱, bwa nda̱i sudubo suguna̱a̱nyin, bwa cwaanriin bisa̱nka̱ri xbumashe̱nre̱n, wana bune̱e̱ ta̱hyan awyatu na bwa tabukaki gida̱ga̱gi.
Ama Bulusu bwa ta̱a̱ni nu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ bwa hin be̱, <<Ta-magumahina, ga̱tu naa ne̱e̱ hyo̱ nda̱tu!>>
Sa̱i butu naa ta ha̱mba zhaaro bwa hin xaꞌwaan apitila. Sa̱i bwa hin kaki bwa ta̱ni ame̱ ba̱ri, bwa taa na̱ aꞌuba̱ na Bulusu na̱ Saila ma jikita̱ wana rukwanyan.
Bwa báhine̱ wyan hwa, bwa ha̱nta̱ni wyan ta̱hyan, <<Awyatu o̱to̱, imbata shi na ga̱n nda mabanana?>>
Aba hin bwa, <<Panaa gata ndaabi ku-Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu, bi-nii da̱ba ta̱nda bina̱, gaa na̱ ina ndaa hyo̱.>>
Sa̱i aba bishi bwa mazama nama Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwa na̱ hyo̱ awyatu na ina ndaabwa.
Na̱ ubwa ha̱ni na̱ gita bwa, sa̱i bwa sha̱pi wyan bwa ha̱mba̱ra̱gi suguma sundaaba, bwa butu na̱ hyo̱ awyatu na ina ndaabwa aba ndagi wyan baba̱tiisa̱ma.
Sa̱i bwa ta̱ha̱ni wyan ina ndaabwa, bwa pa̱ wyan shami, bwa ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ga̱da̱ri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ hyo̱ na̱ ina ndaabwa na̱ wana apa̱ni nꞌgata ku-Hwe̱n.
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, awyatu o̱to̱ na ta̱suuga̱ aba káji awyatu na kapa ta̱hyan, <<xAja̱a̱ atázhigani awyatu yata.>>
Sa̱i butu naa ta ha̱mba zhaaro bwa iyaagi Bulusu utuma na ba bishi bwa ta̱hyan, <<Awyatu o̱to̱ na ta̱suuga̱ hin xaata̱zhiga̱ni ma. Na̱ wana kunnu báni ma ihuri gumunu.>>
Ama Bulusu bwa hin, <<Ai, atata̱da̱ba̱gi na̱ aꞌuba̱ na awyatu, na ba tata̱ndaakici ta̱suuga̱, koo na ga̱tu shi Arooma. Aba gura̱a̱ ta̱zwagana na̱ zhaaro, niina ta aba nii ta̱ba̱ha̱na̱ ta̱swee? Majaa nda! xAjaa nꞌsuhyu sundaaba ata̱ba̱ha̱ni.>>
Sa̱i aba awyatu na kapa aba huri ba bishi awyatu o̱to̱ na ta̱suuga̱ ubwa tuma. Na aba hange̱ ta̱hyan Bulusu na̱ Saila ashi awyatu na Rooma, rukwanyan ruba kota̱ni wyan.
Sa̱i aba jaa aba ro̱pe̱ wyan ta̱hyan xare̱ kuri, aba báhine̱ wyan, abaa rupa wyan ta̱hyan xaga̱a̱ ubwa ce̱pe̱.
Na Bulusu na̱ Saila ba ba̱ni na̱ bwa zhaaro, aba huri paa ina na Liidiya, paa aba taꞌura̱ku na̱ ana pa̱ni nꞌgata, aba duwa̱ni wyan nꞌshita̱ na nꞌta̱panaa gata. Aba ga̱a̱ naazhin bwa ce̱pe̱.

Bulusu nje̱ ta̱maga̱a̱ga̱nu na̱ Tasaloonika
Na Bulusu na̱ Saila ba jwara̱gani kuce̱pe̱ na Amfiboolisi na̱ ce̱pe̱ na Apolooniya, aba wuci Tasaloonika, paa uka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya bwa ne̱e̱.
Sa̱i Bulusu bwa ta̱ni waaba haruwa na bwa ya̱wa̱ni, hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ taatu shiitaku shiitaku ma maga̱a̱ga̱nu na̱ awyatu na̱ mꞌba mazama nama takaada na Hwe̱n.
Bwaa bisa̱ga̱ wyan hiku ta̱hyan ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ Ala̱masiihu swa̱ ngwan, bigura̱a̱ hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱. Bulusu bwa hin wyan, <<Yeesu yata na ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, be̱ taa shi Ala̱masiihu.>>
Sa̱i ayaan Ayaahudiya na̱ Ahelena ana jwarigi Hwe̱n ki ahwarapi, huku na̱ ayaan a̱ na mꞌbaa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ aba ra̱ni mꞌba mazama, aba pa̱ni nꞌgata, aba jwarigi Bulusu na̱ Saila, aba shi ri ka̱.
Ama ayaan Ayaahudiya aba ribici mꞌba mazama wana ahuri ta̱jwara̱ga Bulusu na̱ Saila, aba wuna̱a̱ni awyatu na uwa̱ na kasuwa, aba hiika̱hini aha̱nka̱ri na wyatu kope na̱ ce̱pe̱. Aba huzhi nꞌsumo̱ zhagu ina na Yaso̱no̱ abaa wyanzan Bulusu na̱ Saila na hyan abáhine̱ wyan, aꞌíye̱ wyan kawyatu na ce̱pe̱.
Na aba nda̱ci wyan, aba kota̱ni Yaso̱no̱ na̱ ayaan na pa̱ni nꞌgata, aba ꞌye̱e̱ wyan na̱ kai kawyatu na ta ꞌyapa mazama, ma taga ta̱ꞌungwa ma hyaan, <<Awyatu yata na ta hiika̱hini aha̱nka̱ri na awyatu kope na̱ ce̱nye̱n, aba na wuce pina.
Yaso̱no̱ na maa pa̱ wyan pa̱ri na̱ ina ndaabwa. Hyo̱ aba na ga̱a̱ ta̱jwara̱ga nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Kaisa ma hyaan buyaan bugwama ne̱e̱ naa aba ta nꞌgana Yeesu.>>
Na awyatu na ce̱pe̱ na̱ awyatu na ta ꞌyapa mazama na ce̱pe̱ aba hange̱ kunnu, aha̱nka̱ri ndaaba ba hiiki.
Aba ta̱zhiga̱ncin Yaso̱no̱ na̱ ayaan na pa̱ni nꞌgata, sa̱i na aba ra̱a̱ ta̱re̱ga aba ta̱zhiga̱ni wyan.
Bulusu na̱ Saila bisa̱gi wyatu mazama na̱ Biriya
Na gita bwa nje̱, ana pa̱ni nꞌgata aba cipani Bulusu na̱ Saila, aba ree aba huri ce̱pe̱ na Biriya. Na aba wuci kaun, aba ta̱ni ka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya.
Too, awyatu na Biriya aba ba huri ana Tasaloonika ta̱sha awyatu na suha̱nka̱ri, na aba taraa mazama nama Hwe̱n kunrun, ma gwataagana ki utakaada na Hwe̱n koya̱ hwe̱n xanda̱i koo iri na Bulusu bwaa cita̱ga̱ shi mahanda.
Na̱ kunnu Ayaahudiya hwarapi aba pa̱ni nꞌgata, kunnu taa ayaan a̱ na Ahelena ana aba ta pa hunrun, na̱ ayaan awyatu wya̱ri ahwarapi na Ahelena.
Ama na Ayaahudiya ana Tasaloonika aba hange̱ ta̱hyan Bulusu nii bisa̱ga̱ awyatu mazama nama Hwe̱n na̱ Biriya, sa̱i aba ja̱a̱ aba hurupa̱ga̱ni awyatu ce̱be̱ kaun ma hiika̱hina̱a̱ wyan aha̱nka̱ri.
Kupita kunrun aya̱too na pa̱ni nꞌgata aba shaani Bulusu bwa huri inza̱n na rwaga na o̱to̱, ama Saila na̱ Timooti ba e̱she̱ kwan na̱ Biriya.
Awyatu na taꞌiya bwa, aba wuciha̱ni bwa uce̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ Atina, bwa káji wyan tuma xaja̱a̱ abishi Saila na̱ Timooti ta̱hyan xanjé̱e̱ na̱ ha̱ni ajwárige̱ bwa kunrun.
Bulusu nje̱ mazama na̱ awyatu na Atina
Too, na Bulusu bwa ha̱mbagi Saila na̱ Timooti na̱ Atina, sa̱i bwa gwatani ubwa ce̱pe̱ ucigi da̱ na̱ ri na ba mandaakaki na baa paga hunrun bwa gware̱ me̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Buta jaga aka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya, bunaa maga̱a̱ga̱nu na̱ Ayaahudiya na̱ ayaan Ahelena ana jwarigi Hwe̱n ki. Na̱ akasuwa mayaan bunaa nda na̱ ana shi ana ne̱e̱ kaun koya̱ hwe̱n.
Bwa gura̱a̱ ura̱ku na̱ ayaan ana yan aba jwarigi ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ Epikuuriyusu na̱ Zeeno+ :18 Zeeno: Buta sha butu o̱to̱ naa biigudu naa Asitookiya.ma maga̱a̱ga̱nu na̱ aba. Na bwa bishi wyan mazama nama Yeesu na̱ nama ta̱hiika̱, aka̱ ba hin, <<Imbata butu na̱nna naa aza̱zama bwa ribi ta̱hyan kwan?>> Aka̱ aba hin, <<Ta̱nnda̱i kuunii nda mazama nama ahwe̱n na ayaan na ga̱tu yancin.>>
Sa̱i aba sha̱pi bwa, aba ꞌye̱e̱ bwa kii-Undu naa Arasa paa awyatu na ta ꞌyapa mazama na ce̱pe̱ ba tamawuna̱na̱, aba hin bwa, <<Ta̱bisa̱gi ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ fo nata̱ gaa cita̱ga̱ ta̱hange̱ ki.
Na̱ wana ta̱tahange̱ce̱ iri na mazama maya̱nu nama ga̱tu hin baka ta ga̱tu ribi ta̱yansun imbata mꞌba shi.>>
Hyo̱ Aꞌatina na̱ agai na hunrani kaun ata hura̱ ta̱pana ha̱ni ndaaba anaa nda na̱ nꞌta̱cita̱ga̱ na̱ nꞌta̱shiraga ri na fo na abaa cita̱ga̱.
Sa̱i Bulusu bwa hiiki, bwa e̱she̱ na̱ aꞌuba̱ na awyatu na ta ꞌyapa mazama, bwaa ndaaka wyan mazama bwa hin, <<Ga̱hin awyatu na Atina, nꞌnda̱i ta̱hyan ishi awyatu na huri ta̱ruba̱ ta̱jwara̱ga ahwe̱n ninhin na̱ koya̱ yo̱n.
Nꞌnda̱i na ga̱n raanwyan ma gwatagana ki, ta ga̱n nda̱ya̱gi paaki iri ninhin na ga̱hin paga hunrun, iꞌmꞌbaa biyaan bizhe̱nke̱n binaa bikico̱ ta̱huunha̱na̱ binaa ba ta̱ WANA UHWE̱N NA GA̱TU YANCIN. Too, uyata na ga̱hin tanaa paga hunrun na ga̱hin yancin, ubwa ta ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ ma.
Ubwa ta shi Uhwe̱n na nje̱ sa̱ra̱ri na̱ hyo̱ iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ bwa. Ta na ta̱hyan bwa taa shi Butu O̱to̱ naa nꞌce̱nye̱n na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, buꞌa̱cii hunrana na̱ ina na ta̱naa paga hunrun na butu wuma bwa ma̱.
Butu bwa jaa ara wuun ta̱ndaaka yaan ri, bwa za iri na bwa ta wyanzan kubutu. Bwa taa shi naa ta shaana koo buya̱ bunje̱ bina̱ na̱ nꞌhunjo̱ na mꞌbwaa hunda, na̱ hyo̱ iyaan ri.
Bwa taa shi na nje̱ hyo̱ nꞌkorogo kubutu ka̱, wana hyan ahunrana kope na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana. Bwa ndagi haru na uha̱ni nata̱ naa, bwa ndagi haru haru na kiiko naa koo biya̱a̱ gudu be̱e̱ hunrana.
Uhwe̱n nje̱ kunnu wana hyan awyánzhin wuun, anii wyagadaga wuun na hyan awuta̱ni wuun, koo na ta̱hyan uza tutu kuhyo̱ nda̱tu.
<Na ta̱hyan na̱ bwa ta ga̱tu ne̱e̱ wuma, ga̱tu ma dugaga, ga̱tu ne̱e̱.> Kuꞌizha̱a̱ ninhin ka̱ be̱e̱ hyaan, <Ga̱tu ta̱nda nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ta ga̱tu shi.>
<<Na ta̱hyan butu shi ta̱nda nata̱ Hwe̱n, ai, umanje̱ce̱ ta̱nshii ta̱hyan Uhwe̱n shi haku mꞌpirwa na nꞌzinaari, koo na nꞌazurufa, koo na nꞌtari, una butu bwa nje̱ na̱ nꞌta̱yansun ta̱ndaabwa.
Na yigo Uhwe̱n tajaa ndaakaka wyatu ta̱suuga̱ haruwa na pinsan ndaaba, na̱ wana atayancin. Ama niina Uhwe̱n ribi koo buya̱ kope xbupa̱ni pinsan baa.
Too, bwa tahoo kasa uhwe̱n na ta̱ndaaka awyatu na sa̱ra̱ri yana ta̱suuga̱ nata̱ ta̱to̱n, kuunaa bwa takasa. Uhwe̱n ta bisa̱a̱ ta̱nda kunnu wyatu hyo̱ hiku, paa bwa tahiika̱hina̱ bwa butu kuta̱ꞌwa̱.>>
Na aba hange̱ Bulusu cici mazama nama ta̱hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱, aka̱ ba ꞌwi bwa nꞌratu, aka̱ aba hin bwa, <<Ta̱ribi ta̱jaa gura̱a̱ ha̱nga ki mazama maya̱nu.>>
Na̱ maya̱nu ta Bulusu bwa tahuwa̱ mazama ma ndaabwa na̱ aba.
Ama aka̱ ba jwarigi bwa, ba pa̱ni nꞌgata nꞌndaaba. Na̱ ame̱ ndaaba aba tashi Diyonisiyusu, bwa shi buka̱ kawyatu na ta ꞌyapa mazama, na̱a̱ yaan buꞌa̱ ruzha̱a̱ rundaabwa Damarisu, na̱ ayaan wyatu.

Hunranhunran na Bulusu na̱ uce̱pe̱ na Korinti
Too, sa̱i Bulusu bwa ga̱a̱ uce̱pe̱ na Atina, bwa huri uce̱pe̱ na Korinti.
Kaba bwa tawuta̱na̱ buyaan Buyaahudiya naa ba ta nꞌgana Akiila, butu naa ba ma̱ncin na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Fantusu. Bwa ta ta̱cii ke̱nye̱n ta̱wuce, bwa na̱ aꞌa̱yo Birisikila, ana báni ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Itaaliya, wana Kaisa Kalaudiyusu hin hyo̱ butu naa shi Buyaahudiya xbuga̱a̱ ce̱pe̱ na Rooma. Bulusu bwa ja̱a̱ xbunda̱i wyan,
na ta̱hyan uciripe̱ ndaabwa shi iri ka̱ na̱ na bwa butu naa ta̱naa ndaga nꞌsakaru na mꞌba ta biyana na̱ tutuu. Bwa e̱she̱ kaun, abaa nda tuma da̱nda̱.
Bwa ta naa nda ta̱maga̱a̱ga̱nu koya̱ hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya na̱ ame̱ na ka̱ta̱ku ndaaba ma nda haruwa na hyan buke̱ce̱he̱ne̱ Ayaahudiya na̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya.
Na Saila na̱ Timooti ba jaa ku-Makidooniya, Bulusu bwa duwa̱ni ta̱pana hyo̱ uha̱ni ndaabwa paa kuta̱ga̱gaagana, ma bisa̱ga̱ Ayaahudiya hiku ta̱hyan Yeesu tashi Ala̱masiihu.
Ama aba ga̱a̱ni be̱, abaa cwaaga be̱ kuta̱cwaaga. Na̱ wana kunnu sa̱i bwa bukuta̱gi aꞌwana ndaabwa bwa hin wyan, <<Ruhaki rune̱e̱ na̱ hyuhyu ninhin, ga̱n za mayaan na̱ ga̱hin. Niina ye̱e̱ ga̱n nii hura̱ paaka na shici Ayaahudiya.>>
Na̱ nꞌkaba bwa huri paakuu yaan butu Titiyusu Yusutusu, butu naa tajwara̱ga Hwe̱n ki, bwa ta shici Buyaahudiya. Uꞌina ndaabwa ne̱e̱ maantaan na̱ ka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya.
Sa̱i Kiripusu, butu o̱to̱ naa ka̱ta̱ku, bwa pa̱nii gata ndaabwa ku-Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu, hyo̱ na̱ awyatu na ina ndaabwa. Ayaan Akorinti hwarapi abaa pagana nꞌgata nꞌndaaba taa na aba hange̱ mazama nama Bulusu, aba ndagi wyan baba̱tiisa̱ma.
Uyaan hwe̱n na̱ gita Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwa bisa̱a̱ Bulusu yaan ri haka ra̱rabi, bwa nje̱ mazama na̱a̱ bwa ta̱hyan, <<Ta-ha̱nga rukwanyan, naa nda ta̱ga̱gaagana, ta-naa wau.
Nꞌne̱e̱ huku na̱ gaa, bwa zaa naa nii nda gagu koo yaanyini na̱ gaa, na̱ wana awyatu hwarapi na ce̱pe̱ yana ashi animi.>>
Bulusu bwa hunrani kaun uyo̱ ka̱ na̱ mꞌpyanda nꞌcininhin, ma ga̱gaagana wyatu mazama nama Hwe̱n.
Na̱ ha̱ni na Galiyo bwa shi gwamina na ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Akaya, ayaan Ayaahudiya aba manje̱ gudu, aba ja̱ba̱ni Bulusu, aba ꞌye̱e̱ bwa paaku ta̱suuga̱.
Aba hin, <<Butu na̱nna shaani awyatu anaa paga Hwe̱n hunrun na̱ yo̱n na nꞌgira̱nshin mꞌba yanshin.>>
Bulusu ma nda shiri na hyan bucici mazama, sa̱i Galiyo bwa hin Ayaahudiya, <<Ga̱hin Ayaahudiya, xbwa shi yaan pinsan na njeke ta bwa nje̱, koo uyaan pinsan na o̱to̱, kimii shiragi ma.
Ama na bwa shi ta̱maga̱a̱ga̱nu ta̱ta nata̱ mazama huwa̱, na̱ azha̱a̱zha̱a̱, na̱ nꞌgira̱nshin niinhin, sa̱i da̱i ija̱a̱ inaa nda. Ga̱n jaa nda ta̱suuga̱ nata̱ iri ya̱nu.>>
Sa̱i bwa pa̱ wyan sumo̱ kudura̱ na ta̱suuga̱.
Sa̱i hyo̱ ndaaba aba kota̱ni Sosutanusu butu o̱to̱ naa ka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya, aba pa̱ be̱ dibi pita na̱ bambanu na dura̱ na ta̱suuga̱. Ama Galiyo ubwa za na ta̱ bwa gbi.
Bulusu kwashe̱e̱ke̱ Antiyaakiya na Suuriya
Na maya̱nu mꞌba huri, sa̱i Bulusu bwa duwa̱ni mꞌpyanda na̱ Korinti. Naazhin bwa cipani ana pa̱ni nꞌgata. Bwa ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni da̱nda̱ na̱ Birisikila na̱ Akiila, aba kota̱ni yo̱n na ja̱a̱ Suuriya. Ama ta ba huro, sa̱i Bulusu bwa hwaane̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa na̱ Kankiriya wana butanda ala̱ka̱wa̱ri.+ :18 Ta̱huuna hyuhyu ku-Ayaahudiya ta bisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan butu ciga̱hini mazama nama bwa tanje̱. Na aba wuci Afisa, kaba Bulusu bwa ta gaa Birisikila na̱ Akiila, Bulusu bwa ta̱ni ka̱ta̱ku bwaa ma ga̱a̱ga̱nu na̱ Ayaahudiya.
Aba ro̱pe̱ be̱ ta̱hyan xbuduwa̱ni ta̱pa nꞌhwe̱n waaba, ama bwa ga̱a̱.
Ama na bwa gaa kaun bwa bishi wyan ta̱hyan, <<Ku-Hwe̱n shani, nꞌnii kúshiike̱ pina.>> Naazhin bwa ga̱a̱ Afisa, bwa ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni.
Na bwa ciin na̱ Kaisariya, bwa huri Hurushaliima, bwa zumani awyatu na Yeesu, naazhin bwa huri Antiyaakiya.
Na bwa ta̱ kaun bike̱nye̱n, bwa jwara̱gagani riinha̱nu ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Galaatiya na̱ Firijiya, ma jwara̱gagana ce̱pe̱ ce̱pe̱ ma duwa̱ga̱na̱ hyo̱ ana pa̱ni nꞌgata ta̱taga shita̱.
Afolosu bisa̱gi awyatu mazama na̱ Afisa
Na̱ ha̱ni ya̱nu sa̱i kuuyaan Buyaahudiya bunaa aba ta nꞌgana Afolosu bwa jaa Afisa. Bubwa bwa shi butu naa ce̱pe̱ na Alekazandiriya, bunaa a̱ri mazama bwa yan utakaada na Hwe̱n ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Aga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni bwa ki mazama nama yo̱n na Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n, bwa ta isa hiku na̱ mꞌmazama mandaabwa, bwa tanaa ga̱gaagana ki mazama nama Yeesu na̱ mꞌmahanda suꞌmꞌba hin. Ama huwa̱ kubaba̱tiisa̱ma na Yoohana bwa yan.
Bwa ke̱ne̱ ta̱bisa̱ga̱ wyatu mazama na̱ ka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya, hyo̱ na̱ kai na ta̱yansun ta̱ndaabwa. Na Birisikila na̱ Akiila aba hange̱ mazama mandaabwa, aba nꞌgani bwa, aba duwa̱ni bwa ta̱ga̱gaagana yo̱n na Hwe̱n hiku nꞌta̱hiku.
Na Afolosu bwa ribi ta̱kacigana Akaya, ana pa̱ni nꞌgata aba ta̱ bwa shita̱, aba ta̱a̱ga̱gi bwa takaada ta̱hyan xara̱a̱ bwa nꞌara nꞌree. Na Afolosu bwa wuci kaun, bwa shi butu naa bina̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ kana pa̱ni nꞌgata nꞌndaaba kuta̱pana ꞌye̱n nata̱ Hwe̱n.
Na̱ wana ta̱hyan bure̱e̱hini Ayaahudiya na̱ aꞌuba̱ na wyatu, na̱ mꞌmazama nama bwa bisa̱gi wyan hiku nama takaada na Hwe̱n ta̱hyan Yeesu tashi Ala̱masiihu.

Bulusu na̱ Afisa
Na̱ ha̱ni na Afolosu bwa ne̱e̱ na̱ Korinti, Bulusu bwa jwara̱gagani hyo̱ ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ ta̱ba ce̱nye̱n, bwa wuci kuce̱pe̱ na Afisa, kaba bwa tawuta̱na̱ ayaan ana jwarigi Yeesu.
Bwa ha̱nta̱ni wyan, <<Ita da̱ba ta̱raa Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n ha̱ni na ga̱hin tapana nꞌgata?>>
Aba hin bwa, <<Ga̱tu maa ga̱tu tahange̱ce̱ ta̱hyan yaan ri ne̱e̱ na shi Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n.>>
Sa̱i Bulusu bwa ha̱nta̱ni wyan, <<Too, uya̱ baba̱tiisa̱ma nu ga̱hin taraa?>>
Aba hin, <<Una Yoohana.>>
Bulusu bwa hin, <<Ai, baba̱tiisa̱ma na Yoohana tabisa̱a̱ awyatu apa̱ni pinsan baa, bwa bisa̱gi awyatu xapa̱ni nꞌgata nꞌndaaba kuunaa wuci ta̱baa ta̱ndaabwa, na shi Yeesu.>>
Na aba hange̱ kunnu, sa̱i aba ndagi wyan baba̱tiisa̱ma na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ Yeesu.
Na Bulusu bwa sha̱a̱ta̱a̱gi wyan nꞌara na nꞌrubara̱ka, sa̱i Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ cíin na̱ hyuhyu ndaaba, ma ndaga mazama na̱ nꞌta̱ce̱pe̱ googoogoo, abaa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama.
Hyo̱ aba tanaa awyatu wya̱ri aꞌupwa na ree.
Sa̱i Bulusu bwa ta̱ni ka̱ta̱ku na Ayaahudiya ma nda mazama bigata ka̱. Bwa nje̱ mꞌpyanda nꞌtaatu ma maga̱a̱ga̱nu na̱ aba, bwa a̱ra̱ga̱ni aka̱ kumazama nama ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n.
Ama na aka̱ aba hwashe̱ mꞌba mazama aba ga̱a̱ ta̱pana nꞌgata nꞌndaaba, ma ndaaka Yo̱n na Yeesu kuhwashe̱ kaꞌuba̱ na wyatu hyo̱. Sa̱i Bulusu bwa sha̱pi ana pa̱ni nꞌgata, bwa mape̱e̱n. Koya̱ hwe̱n bwaa ga̱gaagana ana ne̱e̱ kaun na̱ dura̱ na ta̱ga̱gaagana na Tiranusu.
Nꞌyo̱ nꞌree bwa tanaa nda mꞌba mazama kunnu, hara̱ ana hunrani na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Aasiya ba hange̱ mazama nama Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu, Ayaahudiya na̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya hyo̱.
Mꞌmwaan na n-Sikeba
Na̱ Bulusu ta, Uhwe̱n bwa tanda iri na yaburagi na ta̱jikita̱na̱, na aba tayancin mahwa,
na ta̱hyan koo bidiiko naa ta̱ꞌinca̱a̱n hukuruko koo uda̱bi na tuma na a̱nta̱ni ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabwa, aba sha̱pi, aba ca̱guda̱a̱ga̱gi ana ha̱ngagici sa̱, akuda̱gagi. Nꞌhwaanwun na nꞌwe̱ mayaan mꞌba̱ni, nꞌga̱a̱ wyan.
Sa̱i ayaan Ayaahudiya ana tanaa jwara̱gagana ce̱pe̱ ce̱pe̱ anaa ba̱ha̱na̱a̱ nꞌhwaanwun na nꞌwe̱, aba nje̱ haruwa na hyan anje̱ tuma na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu kana mꞌbaa nꞌhwaanwun na nꞌwe̱. Abaa hyaan, <<Na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ Yeesu bunaa Bulusu bwaa nda mazama ma nde̱e̱be̱, iiro̱pe̱ bana.>>
Too, nꞌyaan mꞌmwaan wya̱ri nꞌta̱nda̱ra̱ tanaa kaun, na nꞌyaan pirisiti na o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya na aba ta nꞌgana Sikeba, hyo̱ ndaaba abaa nda kunnu.
Yaan hwe̱n biyaan bihwaanwun naa we̱ be̱ ra̱ni wyan, be̱ hin, <<Nꞌyan Yeesu, ga̱n hange̱ mazama nama Bulusu, too ga̱hin paa, abwaa ga̱hin shi?>>
Sa̱i bubwa butu na bihwaanwun naa we̱, bwa gubi, bwa ja̱pita̱ni wyan aba a̱ra̱ga̱ncin bwa, aba swa̱gi dibi na zumaancin ta̱ndaya, aba ba̱nii hwa wa̱ra̱ koo buya̱ mahiin zwaan.
Na ana hunrani na̱ Afisa, Ayaahudiya na̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya, hyo̱ rukwanyan ruba kota̱ni wyan na aba hange̱ iri na nje̱, aba duwa̱ni ta̱pa ruzha̱a̱ naru Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu zha̱munkun.
Awyatu ahwarapi ana tapana nꞌgata nꞌndaaba, baa cita̱ga̱ iri na we̱ na aba tandaga na̱ uba̱ na wyatu.
Awyatu hwarapi ana tanaa gigiriga̱hina̱a̱ ri, aba shápagi atakaada ndaaba aba huunha̱ni wyan na̱ aꞌuba̱ na wyatu. Na ba ga̱ga̱a̱gi ayuwa na aba nii ara ta̱san aba takaada, aba kota̱ni arwaru na tuma dubu kuje ta.
Na̱ kunnu mazama nama Hwe̱n mꞌba mawya̱shi, mꞌbaa duwa̱na̱ ta̱kai.
Ugagu na̱ Afisa
Na maya̱nu mꞌba hwii, sa̱i Bulusu bwa mahin nii gata ndaabwa, kuuhwii ta̱jabaga ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Makidooniya na̱ nata̱ Akaya, bunii jaga Hurushaliima. Bwa hin mayaan, <<Kunwuci kaun, ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ ga̱n jaga uce̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ Rooma.>>
Sa̱i bwa ka̱ji ana ta naa guna̱a̱ bwa tuma aree, Timooti na̱ Erasutusu zhagu Makidooniya, bwaa bwa e̱she̱ kwan na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Aasiya.
Na̱ bwa ha̱ni ta aba ta̱hiika̱hina̱ nꞌgata na nꞌawyatu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ wana bwa Yo̱n na Yeesu.
Ta̱ba ta̱hiika̱hina̱ nꞌgata ta̱ta pasa kuuyaan buruma naa ba ta nꞌgana Dimitiriyusu, naa tanaa nda tuma na azurufa na ta̱naa pyapaga iꞌwaa na mꞌbaa mꞌpirwa na nꞌina na Aratemisu ndaaba na aba tanaa paga hunrun. Bubwa na̱ awyatu ndaabwa atanaa da̱ba ayuwa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ bwa ciripe̱.
Bwa nꞌgani awyatu na ta naa nda iri na ubwa ciripe̱ na̱ hyo̱ ana mꞌbaa iri na bwa ciripe̱, bwa hin wyan, <<Ga̱hin awyatu wuma, iyan ta̱hyan na̱ na̱nna ciripe̱ ta ga̱tu tanaa da̱ba yuwa na̱ bwa.
Ga̱hin hange̱, ga̱hin gwatagi ta̱hyan shii kupina na̱ Afisa, do̱ko̱ hyo̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Aasiya bwa butu ya̱nu Bulusu bwa pira̱gi wyatu hwarapi. Bwa ke̱ce̱he̱ne̱ wyan nꞌgata, ma hyaan ahwe̱n na butu bwa nje̱ na̱ ara ndaabwa shici hwe̱n na mahanda.
Too, ukina ne̱e̱. Anii ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ ruzha̱a̱ naru ciripe̱ nda̱tu, aba nii ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ ina yana na bihwe̱n naa a̱ naa hura̱gi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ Aratemisu, asha̱pi wuun ushici koo yaanyini, ayanshin wuun ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ta̱ndaabwa. Be̱e̱ naa ta̱hyan hyo̱ ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Aasiya, ka̱i hyo̱ maa sa̱ra̱ri yana baa paga buu hunrun.>>
Na ba hange̱ kunnu, aba gware̱ sume̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, abaa taagana sunu ha̱ni ka̱ mahyaan, <<Ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ta̱ne̱e̱ ku-Aratemisu na Aꞌafisa!>>
Hyo̱ ubwa ce̱pe̱ bwa yimani. Awyatu aba mazooni tunu kupa̱ri naka ta̱mawuna̱a̱na̱, abaa mánai Gaayusu na̱ Arisitarakusu awyatu na Makidooniya, ana shi ana Bulusu na ta̱ha̱ni.
