Bulusu bwa ribi xbuta̱ni paa aba mawuna̱ni, ama ana pa̱ni nꞌgata kaun aba yanshin bwa.
Ayaan awyatu o̱to̱ na ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Aasiya ana shi ta̱shika na̱ Bulusu, aba kádaagi bwa, ma paga bwa akuri xbuta ta̱na̱ paa wyatu aba mawuna̱ni.
Paaka aba tamawuna̱na̱, wyatu aba ne̱e̱ yimo̱ yimo̱, ahwarapi maa aba yancin maa na íye̱ wyan kaun. Ana̱nna ma cita̱ga̱ mana̱nna goo, ana̱nna macita̱ga̱ mana̱nna goo.
Ayaan Ayaahudiya aba tutumaa buyaan butu naa aba ta nꞌgana Aleka̱zanda, bwa ka̱cihini ara ndaabwa da̱da̱da̱ na hyan bubisa̱gi awyatu mazama kuꞌmꞌba shi.
Ama na aba nda̱i ta̱hyan bushi Buyaahudiya ba ta̱a̱ni sunu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ma hyaan, <<Ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ta̱ne̱e̱ ku-Aratemisu na Aꞌafisa!>> Abaa nda kunnu zhagu aꞌawa ree.
Ta̱hakana naazhin butu naa ta naa taagaga wyan ta̱ꞌyantan na̱ bwa ce̱pe̱ bwa shani aba ne̱e̱ wau, bwa hin wyan, <<Ga̱hin awyatu na Afisa! Koo buya̱ yan ta̱hyan, uce̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ Afisa ta shi na ha̱mba̱gi ina na ta̱pa hunrun na Aratemisu una hura̱gi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, na̱ utari na mꞌpirwa nde̱e̱be̱ na takíne̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
Na ta̱hyan zaa naa nii hyan shii nuunu na̱ ya̱nu ri, ai, sa̱i inje̱ fo̱n, iꞌye̱e̱ komba̱ri shukuu.
Iꞌíye̱ awyatu na̱nna pina ana nje̱ce̱ zumba̱ na̱ ina nda̱tu koo mayaan mazama nama hwashe̱ kuhwe̱n nda̱tu Aratemisu.
Ama ku-Dimitiriyusu na̱ awyatu na ciripe̱ ndaabwa mꞌbaa mayaan mazama na̱ aba, udura̱ na ta̱suuga̱ ne̱e̱ hoo, wyatu na ta̱suuga̱ aba ne̱e̱, xaꞌye̱e̱ kaun mꞌba mazama.
Ama kiyaan ri ne̱e̱ goo na ga̱hin ribi ta̱yansun, sa̱i xija̱a̱ kuꞌawyatu na ta ꞌyapa mazama, imagá̱gaagi.
Niina nꞌne̱e̱ nꞌrukwanyan, kata̱nꞌnꞌgani kuꞌawyatu o̱to̱ na Rooma, ta̱yancin iri na ga̱tu bisa̱ wyan na nje̱ ba̱re, wana iri za na shi mahanda na shani ta̱hiika̱hina̱ nꞌgata.>>
Na bwa cici kunnu, bwa cipani awyatu, aba hura̱gi.

Bulusu kwashe̱e̱ke̱ Makidooniya na̱ Helena
Na ubwa yimo̱ bwa hwii, sa̱i Bulusu bwa nꞌgani ana jwarigi, bwa duwa̱ni wyan shita̱ ta̱ta, bwa cipani wyan. Na̱ nꞌkaba bwa huri ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Makidooniya.
Bwaa jwara̱gagana nꞌko nꞌko ma hura̱ ma nda mazama mahwarapi nama ta̱duwa̱na̱ ana pa̱ni nꞌgata ta̱taa shita̱, na̱ nꞌkaba bwa wuci ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Helena.
Bwa nje̱ kaun mꞌpyanda nꞌtaatu. Bwa ma nda shiri na hyan buta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni buhuri ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Suuriya, sa̱i ayaan Ayaahudiya ba ndaaki bwa shiri na zumaancin. Na̱ kunnu sa̱i bwa huri ta̱ruba̱ xbukwashe̱ Makidooniya.
Awyatu na taꞌiya bwa na, Sufata buyoo Farusu naa báni Biriya, na̱ Arisitarakusu na̱ Sakundusu ana báni Tasaloonika, na̱ Gaayusu na báni Darabe, na̱ Timooti, hyo̱ maa na̱ Tikikusu na̱ Tarofimusu ana báni ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Aasiya.
Atata̱gira ta̱hani, aba ta̱hambe̱ na̱ Toruwasu.
Na Ubuki na Buroodi na za Yisiti bwa hwii, ga̱tu báni ga̱tu gaa Filibi na̱ hantun na ma̱ni. Na̱ nꞌhwe̱n nꞌta ga̱tu wuta̱ni wyan na̱ Toruwasu. Na̱ bwa Toruwasu ta ga̱tu tanda nꞌhwe̱n nꞌta̱nda̱ra̱.
Bulusu makooka̱a̱ ta̱jaga Toruwasu
Na̱ hwe̱n na yigo na maako, ga̱tu mawuna̱ni na hyan ta̱ya̱biza̱gi buroodi ta̱hoosa̱ga̱gi. Sa̱i Bulusu bwa ndaaki wyan mazama. Na̱ wana buyan buja̱a̱ hura̱ na̱ bunwan, bwa hoosa̱ni gita mꞌmazama.
Aba pa̱nta̱a̱nyin ira na̱ bwa dura̱ na aba ma̱ da̱da̱da̱ naa ya̱na̱ paa ga̱tu tamawuna̱na̱ na̱ bwa.
Buyaan baa bunaa ba ta nꞌgana Yutikusu, bwa ma hunrana na̱ adubo na taaga, sa̱i nꞌrabi mꞌba kaki be̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ ha̱ni na Bulusu bwa tanaa nda mazama mandaabwa ji. Nꞌrabi mꞌba sha̱pi Yutikusu ma hwa, bwa kíne̱ ta da̱da̱da̱ na ta̱ma nata̱ hin taatu, aba sha̱pi bwa ruꞌwa̱.
Bulusu bwa cíin kunrin bwa gii pwan na̱a̱ bwa, bwa wuguda̱ni bwa baa, bwa hin wyan, <<xUtaa kaka ma, ai, bune̱e̱ buwuma.>>
Sa̱i Bulusu bwa kwashe̱ katanu, bwa ya̱biza̱gi buroodi, ga̱tu re̱gi. Bwa re̱ iyeebe na̱ mꞌmazama kubunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, naazhin bwa huri.
Aba huri na̱a̱ bwa baa buwuma, aba duwa̱ni shita̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Ta̱hani nata̱ báni Toruwasu zhagu Militusu
Bulusu bwa ta̱hura̱ni zhagu ce̱pe̱ na Asusu na̱ mꞌbuna, paa ga̱tu tasha̱a̱ ta̱ꞌura̱ku na̱a̱ bwa, ga̱tu ga̱tu huri iyeebe na̱ hantun na ma̱ni.
Na bwa ta̱wuta̱ni na̱ Asusu, ga̱tu sha̱pi bwa na̱ hantun na ma̱ni zhagu Mitilini.
Ga̱tu re̱ iyeebe nꞌta̱hani na̱ bwa hantun na ma̱ni. Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n ga̱tu wuci do̱ko̱ na̱ ucibiri na Kiyoso. Na bunwan bwa gura̱a̱ haan ga̱tu gura̱a̱ wuta̱ Samoso, na bunwan bwa gura̱a̱ haan ga̱tu wuci Militusu.
Ta na̱ ayigo Bulusu tahiincin bunii ca̱a̱n na̱ Afisa, na̱ wana xbuta ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ ha̱ni na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Aasiya. Bwa makwasa, sa bwa nii ara ta̱wuta̱ Hurushaliima ta uhwe̱n na buki na Pe̱ntiko bwa wuce.
Bulusu cipani awyatu o̱to̱ na jwarigi ana Afisa
Na̱ Militusu ta Bulusu bwa takada xaꞌnꞌgani awyatu o̱to̱ na awyatu na Yeesu ana Afisa.
Na aba wuce bwa bishi wyan ta̱hyan, <<Ga̱hin nꞌsuhyu suniinhin iyan uhunranhunran na ga̱n nje̱ na̱ ga̱hin, ta na ga̱n fo̱nje̱ ce̱nye̱n ta̱yana nata̱ ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Aasiya.
Nꞌndaaki Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu tuma, ga̱n mamo̱nshe̱n hyo̱ na̱ mꞌmaraba. Ga̱n re̱ kuri na̱ nꞌta̱maanwyana nata̱ nꞌjábagani, nata̱ Ayaahudiya aba nꞌndaaki shiri na we̱.
Hyo̱ na̱ kunnu, ga̱n ga̱a̱ci ta̱na maa bisa̱ga̱ ma iri na na̱maa bina̱ ma, na̱ sa̱ra̱ri na̱ nꞌina nꞌina.
Nꞌnje̱ mazama maka̱ kana shi Ayaahudiya na̱ ana shici, nama ta̱pana pinsan baa na̱ nꞌta̱kíciike̱ ku-Hwe̱n, na̱ nꞌta̱pana nꞌgata ku-Butu O̱to̱ nda̱a̱tu Yeesu.
<<Ga̱n nda̱i Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n mꞌbisa̱a̱ ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ nꞌnii hura̱ Hurushaliima. Ga̱n yancin iri na nii nꞌta piree,
koo na ga̱n nda̱i na̱ koya̱ ce̱pe̱ Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n nii mꞌbisa̱ga̱ ta̱hyan ta̱buka na̱ zhaaro na̱ ngwan goo goo taꞌnꞌhambe̱.
Ama ga̱n sha̱pici hyuhyu nimi nꞌshi yaanyini, ga̱n nii ara ta̱huwa̱ tuma na Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwa mꞌpa̱ni, una ta̱bisa̱ awyatu hiku mazama nama zumaa nama ta̱pana ꞌye̱n nata̱ Hwe̱n.
<<Nꞌyan ta̱hyan ga̱hin yana na ga̱n riinshini wunhin maa bisa̱ga̱ ma mazama nama ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n, iza naa nii gura̱a̱ nꞌndaya.
Na̱ wana kunnu, ba̱re nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma ki ta̱hyan nꞌza ruhaki naru koo buyaan na̱ hyuhyu nimi,
na̱ wana ta̱hyan nꞌza ri na ga̱mii sooni ma ina shi hyo̱ na Hwe̱n bwa ribi iyansun.
Imagwatani hiku na̱ hyo̱ ana Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ shani ga̱hin shi ana ta̱gwatana wyan. Inaa nda kiiwo na bigudu naa awyatu na Yeesu, ana Hwe̱n bwa ta mada̱a̱ba na̱ mꞌmahiin namaa Yoo.
<<Nꞌyan ta̱hyan kunhuri ayaan na we̱ haka kura̱na̱ anii jaa, ajaa gaa bibe̱e̱ gudu.
Koo na̱ ame̱ ninhin maa aka̱ nii híike ake̱ne̱ aza̱zama na shici mahanda na hyan ama̱ni ana jwarigi Yeesu waaba.
Na̱ kunnu sa̱i inaa na̱ shiri, imata̱ma̱nriin nꞌyo̱ nꞌtaatu na na̱ ga̱hin, hwe̱n na̱ gita nꞌtaga̱a̱ci ta̱naa maa basa ma hyo̱ na̱ mꞌmaraba.
<<Niina iishii ma kuꞌnꞌara na n-Hwe̱n. Mazama nama ta̱pana ꞌye̱n ta̱ndaabwa xmaa pe̱e̱n ma nii inro̱n, mꞌba ta mashi nama na̱maa ara ta̱duwa̱na̱ ma ta̱kai, igura̱a̱ hya̱su ri na zumaa huku na̱ hyo̱ awyatu na Yeesu.
Ga̱n shiici ame̱ na̱ ayuwa koo iꞌwaa koo aꞌwana na ruzhanna naa yaan.
Ga̱hin nꞌsuhyu suniinhin inda̱i ta̱hyan nꞌnje̱ ta tuma na̱ ara nimi, na hyan ma da̱ba iri na ga̱n na̱ awyatu nimi na ta̱hani ga̱tu ribi.
Na̱ hyo̱ utuma na ga̱n ndaga na̱ nꞌara niimi, na bisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan bwa ta nii shana ta̱ꞌa̱ri ta̱gwatana ana za iri na nꞌara nꞌndaaba. Imata̱ma̱nriin sa̱ na̱ mꞌmazama nama Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu ta̱hyan, <Ta̱pana ta̱huri ta̱raa rubara̱ka.> >>
Na Bulusu bwa hwii ta̱cita̱ga̱, bwa she̱nshe̱n na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n, bwa nje̱ ro̱pe̱ huku hyo̱ na̱ aba.
Sa̱i hyo̱ ndaaba aba ke̱ne̱ nꞌungwa, aba makusuma̱a̱ na̱a̱ bwa ma hwaama bwa paa kuta̱cipana bwa.
Ame̱ ta̱gura ndaaba taduwa̱na̱ o̱to̱ wana buhin wyan ajaa gura̱a̱ ndaya bwa. Na̱ nꞌkaba aba ꞌye̱e̱ bwa ta paa hantun na ma̱ni.

Ta̱hani nata̱ Bulusu zhagu Hurushaliima
Na ga̱tu huri ga̱tu ga̱a̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na Afisa na̱ yama, ga̱tu ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni, ga̱tu ka̱mbigi ta̱hani zhagu ucibiri na Koosa̱. Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n ga̱tu wuci ucibiri na Rodusu, sa̱i ga̱tu wuci ce̱pe̱ na Patara.
Na ga̱tu wyanzan hantun ga̱tu nda̱i una nii kacigana zhagu ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Finikiya, ga̱tu ta̱ni wuun.
Na ga̱tu bwe̱ yishe ga̱tu nda̱i ucibiri na Kuburusu, ga̱tu ga̱a̱ kaun ara kagura̱, ga̱tu ta̱ta̱hura̱ nꞌta̱hani kuce̱nye̱n nata̱ Suuriya. Ga̱tu ciin na̱ ce̱pe̱ na Taaya na̱ wana ta̱hyan kaba ta ubwa hantun bwa ta ciinha̱na̱ ꞌwaa.
Na ga̱tu wuci, ga̱tu wuta̱ni ana jwarigi Yeesu kaun, ga̱tu nje̱ nꞌhwe̱n ta̱nda̱ra̱ huku na̱ aba. Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ bishi wyan ta̱hyan xabishi Bulusu xbuta jaga Hurushaliima.
Na uha̱ni nda̱tu na ta̱hura̱ bwa nje̱, ga̱tu re̱ iyeebe nꞌta̱hani, hyo̱ ana jwarigi na̱ aꞌa̱ na̱ mꞌmwaan nꞌndaaba aba ta̱shée ta ta̱baa nata̱ ce̱pe̱. Ga̱tu sa̱nsain pita hyo̱ na̱ inza̱n na rwaga na o̱to̱, ga̱tu nje̱ ro̱pe̱,
ga̱tu macipani. Too, sa̱i ga̱tu ta̱ni hantun, aba ba kwashe̱e̱ke̱ giyo ina.
Na ga̱tu ga̱a̱ Taaya, ga̱tu wuci Tolemayisi, ga̱tu ma zumaani na̱ aya̱too na pa̱ni nꞌgata, ga̱tu roci hwe̱n ka̱ waaba.
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, ga̱tu huri Kaisariya, ga̱tu ta̱ni ina na Filibu butu naa ta naa bisa̱ga̱ awyatu mazama nama zumaa. Bwa shi ka̱ kuꞌata̱nda̱ra̱ na aba takasa wana hooso na shami na̱ Hurushaliima. Ga̱tu ne̱e̱ waabwa.
Bwa mꞌbaa mꞌmwaan nꞌa̱ nꞌna̱nshin na nꞌtagiici ta̱wya̱ri na nꞌta naa nda tuma na acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama.
Too, na ga̱tu pa̱ kaun nꞌhwe̱n, buyaan bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama naa ba ta nꞌgana Agabusu bunaa báni kuꞌnꞌundu na nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Yaahuda.
Na bwa jaa kaun, bwa sha̱pi kapa na Bulusu, bwa maka̱da̱gi nꞌara na̱ mꞌbuna nꞌndaabwa na̱ bwa kapa, bwa hin, <<Iri na Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱ hin na, <Kunna Ayaahudiya na Hurushaliima baa kadaga bunaa hya̱a̱ kapa na̱nna, agura̱a̱ pana be̱ kana shici Ayaahudiya.> >>
Na ga̱tu hange̱ kunnu, sa̱i ga̱tu na̱ ana pa̱ni nꞌgata na tanaa piree ga̱tu ro̱pe̱ Bulusu xbuta jaga Hurushaliima.
Bulusu bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Iba̱ shani ga̱hin nꞌgaaga ga̱hin nꞌkusa̱a̱n bigata? Ai, nꞌhoo ta ta̱kuke, shii maa kuta̱kadaga, koo ta̱kuna aba na̱ma nꞌkuna na̱ Hurushaliima na̱ wana Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu.>>
Na ga̱tu nda̱i ta̱hyan ta̱ꞌa̱ra̱ga̱ncin be̱, ga̱tu hakaci, ga̱tu hin, <<xTa̱sha̱a̱ nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱cigi.>>
Na nꞌhwe̱n mꞌba huri, ga̱tu nje̱ shiri ga̱tu huri Hurushaliima.
Ayaan ana jwarigi na̱ Kaisariya aba ta̱ꞌye̱e̱, aba ta̱shée kuꞌina na Manason bunaa ga̱tu ta̱na na̱ ina ndaabwa. Bwaa shi butu naa ucibiri na Kuburusu, buka̱ kana tajwara̱ga ta na̱ ayigo.
Bulusu jwarigi ri na Ayaahudiya ba hin wana mazama nama zumaa
Na ga̱tu wuce Hurushaliima aya̱too na pa̱ni nꞌgata aba ta̱ra̱a̱ nꞌara nꞌree.
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, Bulusu bwa ta̱sha̱pi zhagu paa Yaakubu, awyatu o̱to̱ na awyatu na Yeesu ana Hurushaliima aba tanaa hyo̱ kaun.
Na bwa hwii zumanu, sa̱i bwa bisa̱gi wyan ki iri na Hwe̱n bwa nje̱ na̱ tuma ndaabwa na mazama nama Hwe̱n kana shici Ayaahudiya.
Na aba hange̱ kunnu, sa̱i aba ya̱bi Hwe̱n. Aba hin Bulusu, <<Too buya̱tu, bu-nda̱i Ayaahudiya adubu hwarapi ta pa̱ni nꞌgata ku-Yeesu, hyo̱ aba shi ana za mꞌpirwa na̱ Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa ta̱jwara̱ga.
Ahoo bisa̱ ana pa̱ni nꞌgata pina na̱ Hurushaliima ta̱hyan bi-nii ga̱gaagana Ayaahudiya ana hunrani huku na̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya xaga̱a̱ ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ Muusa. Aba gura̱a̱ ha̱nga ta̱hyan bi-nii hyaan xata naa ꞌyapaga mꞌmwaan ta̱wya̱ri, koo ajwara̱ga nꞌyaan nꞌgira̱nshin nda̱a̱tu.
Too, na ga̱tu nii nda? Ta̱yan anii ha̱nga zhagu ndaa.
<<Na̱ wana kunnu ha̱nga iri na ga̱tu ribi u-nje̱ na. Ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa awyatu na̱nshin ana nje̱ ala̱ka̱wa̱ri.
Hura̱ na̱ aba u-ja̱a̱ u-jwara̱ga bo̱do̱ nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌta̱bwaciga ta̱shiri, u-pa̱ni wyan ayuwa na ta̱huunaa wyan wana ta̱bisa̱a̱ iciga̱hini ala̱ka̱wa̱ri. Na̱ kunnu ta koo buya̱ bwaa yansun ta̱hyan iri na aba hange̱ ndaa ishici mahanda, anda̱i ta̱hyan gaa bi-shi naa jwarigi nꞌgira̱nshin nda̱a̱tu.
<<Ama na̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya, ta̱hoo kada takaada, ga̱tu bishi wyan ta̱hyan, xamape̱e̱n kushami na aba ndaaki gumaka. xAta re̱ sunda huku mꞌmahiin koo iri na aba pigira̱ni ruru. xAta nda banshaun.>>
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, Bulusu bwa sha̱pi aba wyatu ba bwácigagi ta̱shiri da̱nda̱. Naazhin bwa ta̱ni bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n na Ayaahudiya na hyan bubishi awyatu na ne̱e̱ kaun hwe̱n na ta̱ciga̱hina̱ ta̱bwaciga ta̱shiri, andaaki koo buya̱ ba̱iko.
Akota̱ni Bulusu na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n
Na mꞌba nꞌhwe̱n ta̱nda̱ra̱ mꞌba goki ta̱ciga̱, ayaan Ayaahudiya ana ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Aasiya aba nda̱i Bulusu na̱ bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n. Aba hurupa̱ga̱ni hyo̱ awyatu ce̱be̱, aba kota̱ni bwa,
ma ta ta̱ꞌungwa ma hyaan, <<Ga̱hin aya̱too ma Aꞌisiraaꞌila, ta̱guni ma! Nde̱e̱ butu yata ta naa tanaa jwara̱gagana kope maga̱gaagana wyatu na hyan ahusani Nꞌgira̱nshin nda̱a̱tu na̱ hina Ina na Hwe̱n yana nda̱tu. Na̱ nꞌta̱shápi munrun Ahelena na hyan buha̱nsha̱nha̱ni pa̱ri kayana naka ta̱sabu.>>
Ahin kunnu na̱ wana atahoo ndaya Bulusu na̱ Tarofimusu, butu naa Afisa, na̱ ce̱pe̱. Ubwa shani aba shii ta̱hyan koo Bulusu ta̱ni huku na̱a̱ bwa Ina na Hwe̱n.
Sa̱i hyo̱ uce̱pe̱ bwa yimani, awyatu aba hiikooko aba gidigoogo aba ja̱a̱ aba kota̱ni Bulusu, aba buburi bwa ha na Ina na Hwe̱n, aba guna̱a̱ni sudubo maza.
Aba ma nda na hyan akwane̱ bwa, sa̱i mazama mꞌba wuci paa butu o̱to̱ naa hyo̱ nꞌgudu na nꞌasooja na Rooma ta̱hyan Hurushaliima ree na̱ gagu na zumaancin.
Bwa nje̱ na̱ ha̱ni, bwa de̱be̱ asooja na̱ asooja na o̱to̱ bwa ka̱ji wyan na̱ nꞌsumo̱ paa baa nda ubwa wumo̱. Na awyatu na tanii ꞌyama Bulusu ri ba nda̱i butu o̱to̱ na̱ asooja ndaabwa awuci, aba ga̱a̱ Bulusu ta̱naa ꞌyama ri.
Sa̱i butu o̱to̱ naa asooja bwa ja̱a̱ bwa kota̱ni Bulusu, bwa shani aba ka̱da̱gi bwa na̱ akaca ree. Naazhin bwa ha̱nta̱ni wyatu iyaa ta Bulusu bwa shi na̱ mbata bwa nje̱?
Be̱e̱ gudu be̱e̱ ta ta̱ꞌungwa, ana̱nna macita̱ga̱ na̱nna, ana̱nna macita̱ga̱ na̱nnda̱ree. Bwa shaani aba huri na̱ Bulusu baariki na sooja wana iwumo̱ ma̱a̱, bwa a̱rici ta̱ꞌinsan yaanyini.
Na Bulusu na̱ asooja ba ne̱e̱ na̱ adubo xanaa katana, iwumo̱ na wyatu bwa ma̱a̱ sa̱i na asooja ba sha̱pi bwa.
Be̱e̱ gudu naa wyatu naa tajwárige̱ abaa ta ta̱ꞌungwa ma hyaan, <<Kuna ma be̱! Kuna ma be̱!>>
Bulusu ndaaki bigudu naa awyatu mazama
Na aba goki bwa ta̱ta̱ha̱na̱ baariki na asooja, sa̱i bwa hin butu o̱to̱ ndaaba, <<Koo bi-nii mꞌpa nu manda mazama na̱ gaa?>>
Sa̱i butu o̱to̱ bwa hin bwa, <<Ka̱i, bu-a̱ri Ta̱helena?
Shii gaa ta shi butu yata naa Masa na tashana gagu nꞌyo̱ na nꞌhuri, gaa ra̱ga̱ni awyatu adubu na̱nshin na tanaa kunaa awyatu na̱ aga?>>
Sa̱i Bulusu bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Aaꞌa, ga̱n shi Buyaahudiya bunaa Tarususu butu naa ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Kilikiya. Ga̱n butu naa uce̱pe̱ yata na o̱to̱ na maca̱ma̱nta̱n ta. Kusu nꞌhakata ma bisa̱ awyatu na̱nna mazama.>>
Bwa butu o̱to̱ bwa ga̱a̱ bwa xbunje̱ mazama, Bulusu bwa pa̱shi adubo ta̱katana, bwa e̱she̱, bwa ka̱cihini ara da̱da̱da̱ xawyatu naa wau. Na aba nje̱ fo̱n, bwa ndaaki wyan mazama na̱ nꞌta̱ce̱pe̱ nata̱ Ta̱ꞌaramaya.

Sa̱i bwa hin, <<Ga̱hin aya̱too na̱ abaaboo ma, nꞌshiraga ma maa bisa̱ga̱ ma iri na tanda na̱ wana iyansun nꞌnje̱ce̱ pinsan.>>
Na aba hange̱ bwa macita̱ga̱ mazama nꞌta̱ce̱pe̱ ta̱ndaaba, aba duwa̱ni ta̱nda wau. Ha̱ni ya̱nu bwa hin,
<<Ga̱n Buyaahudiya ta ga̱n shi, aꞌmꞌma̱ncin na̱ Tarususu na ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Kilikiya, ama ga̱n mawaani pina na̱ Hurushaliima. Na̱ ara na Gamaaliye ta ga̱n nje̱ makaranta, paa ga̱n yan nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌadaadoo hyo̱. Ga̱n tanaa sa̱ ndaaka taa Hwe̱n tuma hiku, haku ga̱hin ga̱hin nda ba̱re.
Ga̱n yanshin ana jwarigi Yo̱n na̱nna na Yeesu ta̱mataa. Ga̱n kunaa aka̱, ma kadaaga hyo̱ wyatu wya̱ri na̱ aꞌa̱, ga̱n zwagagana wyan na̱ zhaaro.
Butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti na̱ hyo̱ awyatu ana ta ꞌyapa mazama anii ara ta̱a̱bisa̱ ma. Waaba kata ga̱n tanaa sa̱ ma raa atakaada zhagu kaya̱too Ayaahudiya na̱ Dimasiku ma jaga kaun wana hyan ma kota̱ga̱na̱ aba wyatu ma íye̱ wyan Hurushaliima apa̱ wyan ngwan.
Bulusu bisa̱gi wyatu kuubwa kíciike̱
Tuma 9:1-19; 26:12-18
<<Na ga̱n ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hani, ga̱n na goka̱ Dimasiku, na̱ hwe̱n da̱, maza̱ki maba tára̱kani na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ manyan riinha̱nu paa ga̱n ne̱e̱.
Sa̱i ga̱n kinai na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n, ga̱n hange̱ kumazama mahyaan, <Shawulu! Shawulu! Na̱ wana ba̱ gaa nꞌkaki?>
<<Sa̱i ga̱n ra̱ni, <Butu o̱to̱, iyaa nu ya̱nu gaa shi?>
<<Mꞌba hin, <Ga̱n ta Yeesu na Naazare bunaa gaa kaki.>
Awyatu na tanaa na̱ ga̱mi atandaya maba maza̱ki, aba hange̱ce̱ mazama nama abaa mꞌbisa̱ga̱.
<<Too, sa̱i ga̱n ha̱nta̱ni, <Butu O̱to̱, mꞌbata ga̱n nda?>
<<Sa̱i bwa nꞌhin, <Hiika̱, u-ta̱ni Dimasiku, kaba ta aba na̱maa bisa̱ hyo̱ iri na gaa nda.>
Ga̱n ba̱nii ruba̱ na̱ wana maza̱ki mama̱a̱ kai. Awyatu na tanaa na̱ ga̱mi, aba nꞌkota̱ni ara zhagu Dimasiku.
Kuuyaan butu naa aba ta nꞌgana Hanaaninyan naa tanaa kaun bwa jaa wa̱ka̱mi. Bushi butu naa jwarigi Hwe̱n ki haruwa na nꞌgira̱nshin nꞌnda̱a̱tu mꞌba hin, bunaa hyo̱ Ayaahudiya aba ta cina̱na̱.
Bwa e̱she̱ do̱ko̱ na̱ ga̱mi, bwa hin, <Buya̱tu Shawulu, gura̱a̱ huwa̱ga̱ mayaan.> Kupita pita ayishe nimi aba gunii, ga̱n a̱ri be̱ ta̱ndaya.
<<Sa̱i bwa nꞌhin, <Hwe̱n na adaadoo nda̱tu taaka̱shi wana u-yansun ta̱sha̱a̱ ta̱ndaabwa. U-nda̱i Butu naa Bina̱, u-hange̱ mazama na̱ nu ndaabwa,
na̱ wana u-bishi koo buya̱ iri na gaa nda̱i bwa manda, gaa gura̱a̱ ha̱nga.
Too, imba̱ gaa hambe̱? Hiika̱ xaanje̱ baba̱tiisa̱ma, xaaha̱mba̱ri pinsan ndaa paaku ta̱ꞌnꞌgana ruzha̱a̱ rundaabwa.>
Ta̱ꞌnꞌgana nata̱ Bulusu zhagu kana shici Ayaahudiya
<<Na ga̱n kwashe̱e̱ke̱ Hurushaliima, ga̱n nda ro̱pe̱ na̱ bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n, sa̱i ga̱n nda̱i iri haka ra̱rabi.
Ga̱n nda̱i bwa ta ma nꞌhyaan, <Nda na̱ ha̱ni u-ga̱a̱ Hurushaliima, na̱ wana awyatu na pina jaa raa mazama mandaabi nama gaa bisa̱ga̱ wyan maniimi.>
<<Ga̱n ga̱n hin, <Butu O̱to̱, aba taa maa ayan, ta̱hyan, koya̱ ka̱ta̱ku nda̱tu, nꞌka̱da̱a̱gi ana ta pana nꞌgata nꞌndaaba wakaa, ga̱n zwa̱ga̱ga̱ni wyan na̱ zhaaro, ga̱n gura̱a̱ paga wyan dibi.
Na̱ ha̱ni na aba na kuba̱ga̱ mahiin nama Isitafanu na tanaa bisa̱ga̱ awyatu iri na gaa ndagi, ga̱n taꞌisa kaun. Ga̱n tandaya ine̱e̱ to̱n iri na aba tandaaka be̱, ga̱n na ha̱mba ada̱bi na awyatu na takuna be̱.>
<<Sa̱i bwa nꞌhin ga̱mi, <Hiika̱, u-huri, ga̱n namaa kada tuma tutu paaka wyatu na shici Ayaahudiya.> >>
Bigudu be̱ na shiraga Bulusu sa̱i kiike̱nye̱n naa bwa cici mazama maya̱nu. Naazhin aba ta̱a̱ni ta̱ꞌungwa ma hyaan, <<Kuna ma be̱! xAhooshi iri na butu na̱nna na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana, xbuta nda bina̱!>>
Abaa ta ta̱ꞌungwa, ma bwaga ada̱bi ndaaba na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n, ma taraga aputu ma gyasa.
Na̱ wana iri na baa nda, butu o̱to̱ naa asooja bwa hin xaꞌye̱e̱ Bulusu baariki, azware̱ bwa nꞌdunduun, aha̱nta̱a̱ni bwa iri na shaani abaa taga ta̱ꞌungwa kunta.
Na aba hwii bwa ta̱kadaga na hyan azware̱ bwa nꞌdunduun, sa̱i Bulusu bwa hin sooja na o̱to̱ na taꞌisa do̱ko̱, <<Manje̱ to̱n kuꞌnꞌgira̱nshin mꞌba hin xazware̱ butu naa shi Rooma nꞌdunduun, na aba ta ndaakici be̱ suuga̱?>>
Na sooja na o̱to̱ bwa hange̱ kunnu, sa̱i bwa ja̱a̱ paa butu o̱to̱ ndaabwa, bwa hin be̱, <<Imba̱nu gaa ribi ta̱nda? Butu yata bushii Rooma.>>
Sa̱i butu o̱to̱ bwa jaa paa Bulusu bwa hin, <<Mꞌbishi mahanda, gaa bu-shii Rooma?>>
Sa̱i Bulusu bwa hin, <<Nꞌshi.>>
Bubwa butu o̱to̱ bwa hin, <<Ga̱n mbaa na yuwa o̱to̱ ga̱n tada̱ba ta̱sha Burooma.>>
Sa̱i Bulusu bwa hin, <<Ga̱n, na̱ bwa maa aba mꞌma̱ncin.>>
Na̱ wana kunnu, ana tahoo sha̱a̱ anii hantaana bwa aba jikici, aba ma̱ni ta̱baa. Bubwa butu o̱to̱ taa na bwa hange̱ Bulusu bushi Rooma, bwa hange̱ rukwanyan, wana butahoo ufuna̱ bwa.
Bulusu paaka wyatu na ta ꞌyapa mazama
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, sa̱i butu o̱to̱ bwa rigijigi Bulusu. Bwa ribi ta̱yansun buhange̱ ki iri na Ayaahudiya aba ribi ta̱nda na̱ Bulusu. Na̱ wana kunnu bwa shaani apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ hyo̱ awyatu na taꞌyapa mazama xamawuna̱ni. Bwa shápi Bulusu bwa isaa be̱ na̱ awyantancin ndaaba xbuhange̱ iri na shaani.

Sa̱i Bulusu bwa gwatagi wyatu na ta ꞌyapa mazama ga̱ri ga̱ri, bwa hin, <<Ga̱hin aya̱too ma, ujabagu na ga̱n nje̱ haru zhagu ba̱re, nꞌza yaanyini na rukwanyan kuga̱n ne̱e̱ na̱ aꞌuba̱ na Hwe̱n.>>
Kuta̱naa ha̱nga maya̱nu, sa̱i Hanaaninyan butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti bwa pa̱ni wyatu na taꞌisaga do̱ko̱ na̱ Bulusu nu xaba̱sa̱ni be̱ na̱ nu.
Bulusu bwa hin be̱, <<Gaa butu naa uwa̱ ta gaa shi. Hina nii ke̱nye̱n ge̱, Hwe̱n na̱maa basana taa! Bi-hunrani gaa ꞌya̱pi mazama na̱ wana nꞌgira̱nshin, gaa ta gaa shaani aba mꞌba̱sa̱ni, ta̱basana nata̱ za to̱n na̱ nꞌgira̱nshin.>>
Ana taꞌisaga kaun do̱ko̱ na̱ Bulusu aba hin, <<Kunta ta gaa nii husana butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti na Hwe̱n?>>
Sa̱i Bulusu bwa hin, <<Aya̱too ma, ga̱n tayancin bushi butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti. Na̱ wana ata̱gi ta̱hyan, <Ta-cwaaga butu o̱to̱ naa awyatu ndaa.> >>
Bulusu bwa hoo insan ta̱hyan awyatu na ta ꞌyapa mazama, aka̱ ashi Asaduukiya, aka̱ aba shi Afaraasiya, sa̱i bwa ta̱a̱ni nu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ ame̱ ndaaba, bwa hin, <<Aya̱too ma, ga̱n Bufaraasiya ta, diin na Afaraasiya. Wana ga̱n shii bigata niimi kuta̱hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱, ta shaani abaa nꞌndaaka ta̱suuga̱.>>
Na bwa cici kunnu, kuda̱ga bwa hiiki paaka Afaraasiya na̱ Asaduukiya, ta̱mawuna̱na̱ ta̱ba mahooshi maree.
Asaduukiya aba hin ta̱hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱ ta̱za, atuma na Hwe̱n aba za, nꞌhwaanwun mꞌba za. Afaraasiya aba hin hyo̱ ataatu ya̱nu ane̱e̱ hyo̱.
Sa̱i kuda̱ga bwa hiiki ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, nꞌyaan nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin ana shi Afaraasiya aba e̱she̱ ga̱ga̱bu, abaa nda kuda̱ga aba hin, <<Ga̱tu nda̱ci butu na̱nna nje̱ pinsan. Ta̱shii ta̱hyan koo biyaan bihwaanwun, koo butuma naa Hwe̱n ta bwa nje̱ mazama na̱a̱ bwa.>>
Na kuda̱ga bwa nje̱ kai ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, sa̱i butu o̱to̱ naa asooja bwa hange̱ rukwanyan xata jaa gumahinai Bulusu. Bwa pa̱ni nu xbigudu naa asooja cíin arágani Bulusu na̱ kai, aꞌye̱e̱ bwa baariki na asooja.
Na̱ gita bwa, sa̱i Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwa wuce bwa e̱she̱ do̱ko̱ na̱ Bulusu, bwa hin be̱, <<Ta kiishita̱. Haruwa na gaa bisa̱ga̱ awyatu mazama maniimi hiku na̱ Hurushaliima, ga̱ga̱ga̱ gaa nii bisa̱ga̱ awyatu mazama maniimi nama zumaa na̱ Rooma.>>
Ta̱maga̱gaaga ta̱kuna Bulusu
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, ayaan Ayaahudiya aba mawuna̱ni ta̱swee aba ta̱a̱ sa̱nsan ta̱hyan ajaa swa, aba jaa re̱ koori sa̱i kaba kwane̱ Bulusu.
Ana na nda shiri ya̱nu na we̱, ana hura̱ awyatu bihanda.
Sa̱i aba ja̱a̱ paa apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ aba hin, <<Ta̱njé̱e̱ sa̱nsan na yaburi, ta̱jaa swa, ga̱tu jaa re̱, sa̱i ta̱kwane̱ Bulusu.
Gaa na̱ awyatu na ta ꞌyapa mazama bisa̱ ma butu o̱to̱ naa asooja xbugura̱a̱ kúshihine̱ Bulusu kaꞌuba̱ ninhin, inje̱ kiihiin duwa̱na̱ ta̱hantaana bwa ki. Ha̱ni na abaa hure na̱ yo̱n ta̱kwane̱ bwa.>>
Na gyaaru na Bulusu ba hange̱ iri na aba ribi ta̱nda, bwa ja̱a̱ bwa ta̱ni baariki bwa bishi Bulusu.
Bulusu bwa nꞌgani sooja ka̱ na o̱to̱ na Rooma bwa hin be̱, <<Iya baa buwya̱ri na̱nna paa butu o̱to̱, buꞌmꞌbaa mazama nama bwaa bisa̱ be̱.>>
Sa̱i ubwa sooja bwa ra̱ga̱ni bwa baa buwya̱ri, bwa ꞌye̱e̱ be̱ paa butu o̱to̱. Bwa sooja bwa hin buu, <<Butu yata naa zwagani na̱ zhaaro Bulusu, butaꞌnꞌnꞌgani, bwa nꞌro̱pe̱, nꞌíye̱ baa buwya̱ri na̱nna wakaa, buꞌmꞌbaa mazama nama bwa na̱maa bisa̱.>>
Bubwa butu o̱to̱ bwa kota̱ni bwa baa ara, aba mape̱e̱n nii biin, bwa hin bwa, <<Imba̱nu gaa hin ma mꞌbisa̱?>>
Bwa hin, <<Ayaan Ayaahudiya amaga̱ga̱a̱gi ta̱hyan ana̱maa rupa u-kúshihine̱ Bulusu na̱ bunwan kawyatu na ta ꞌyapa mazama anje̱ kahiin duwa̱ni bwa ta̱hantaana ki.
Ama ta-nda kunnu, awyatu huri bihanda ana masoo na̱ wana jaa kuunii hure, ajaa kwane̱ bwa. Ahoo taa sa̱nsan ajaa re̱ aba jaa swa sa̱i akwane̱ bwa. Ahoo nda shiri, aahambe̱ kugaa u-pa̱ni wyan nu.>>
Sa̱i butu o̱to̱ bwa kooci bwa, bwa hin, <<Ta-bisa̱ koo butu ta̱hyan bi-mꞌbishi mazama maya̱nu.>> Bwa cipani bwa baa.
Aꞌye̱e̱ Bulusu paa Gwamina Feelisi
Na̱ ha̱ni ya̱nu, sa̱i butu o̱to̱ bwa nꞌgani sooja ndaabwa reeko na o̱to̱, bwa hin wyan, <<Nda ma shiri na̱ wana inii jaga Kaisariya nii ke̱nye̱n naa ta̱ruma ta̱tundushi na gita, na̱ asooja nꞌyina̱ nꞌreeko. Igura̱a̱ shapa na̱ ayaan sooja kuje ta̱nda̱ra̱ ana ta nda gyasa na̱ indakwa, na̱ ayaan asooja nꞌyina̱ nꞌreeko ana ta nda gyasa na̱ maanshin.
Igura̱a̱ da̱ba indakwa na Bulusu bwaa katana na̱ wana hyan buwuci gumunu paa Gwamina Feelisi.>>
Bwa butu o̱to̱ bwa ta̱gi takaada na hin kunna:
<<Kuga̱n Kalaudiyusu Lisiyasu, zhagu kubutu o̱to̱ Gwamina Feelisi. Iizumani ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Butu yata, Ayaahudiya takota̱ni be̱, do̱ko̱ akwane̱ be̱. Na ga̱n hange̱ bushii Rooma, ga̱n ka̱ji bigudu naa asooja nimi xaráa be̱.
Ga̱n ꞌye̱e̱ be̱ kawyatu ndaaba na ta ꞌyapa mazama na hyan ma ha̱nga iri na aba hin bunje̱.
Nꞌnda̱i ta̱hyan anii ndaaka be̱ mazama nama nꞌgira̱nshin nꞌndaaba, ama upinsan na aba hin bunje̱, ujwaci na ta̱kadaga be̱ koo ta̱kuna be̱.
Na aba mꞌbishi uyaan shiri na aba ndaaki be̱ na zumaancin na ta̱kuna be̱, ga̱n makoshi ta̱ꞌiya be̱ wakaa. Ga̱n bishi awyatu na íye̱ suuga̱ sundaabwa xaabishi pinsan na bwa nje̱ na̱ uba̱ ndaa.
Mꞌba hwii.>>
Asooja aba sha̱pi Bulusu haruwa na aba tahin wyan, aba ꞌye̱e̱ be̱ ce̱pe̱ na Antipaatirisi na̱ gita.
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, aba kwashe̱e̱ke̱ baariki ndaaba, huwa̱ kasooja na ndakwa aba huri na̱ Bulusu.
Na asooja na ndakwa aba wuci Kaisariya, aba pa̱ni gwamina utakaada, aba ga̱a̱ Bulusu kaun na̱ nꞌara nꞌndaabwa.
Na gwamina bwa cita̱gi ta̱ba ta̱ꞌyantan, bwa ha̱nta̱ni Bulusu koo bushi butu naa ta̱ya̱ ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱. Na bwa hange̱ bubáni Kilikiya,
bwa hin, <<Nꞌja̱a̱ ha̱nga mazama mandaabi ha̱ni na wyatu naa íye̱ suuga̱ sundaabi jaa aba wuce.>> Sa̱i gwamina bwa hin xaha̱mba Bulusu kaun na̱ ka̱ta̱ku na ta̱gwama unaa gwama Hirudu bwa ta ma.

Ayaahudiya ꞌye̱e̱ suuga̱ nata̱ Bulusu paa Feelisi
Na nꞌhwe̱n ta mꞌba huri, sa̱i Hanaaninyan butu o̱to̱ naa apirisiti na bwa jaa huku na̱ ayaan wyatu o̱to̱ na̱ ayaan looya na aba ta hyan Tara̱tulusu, na̱ wana aꞌye̱e̱ suuga̱ nata̱ Bulusu kugwamina.
-3 Aba ta̱ha̱ni Bulusu, sa̱i Tara̱tulusu bwa ta̱ha̱ni mazama paa gwamina bwa hin:
<<Butu o̱to̱ Feelisi, Hwe̱n duwa̱ni ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, awyatu nda̱tu kope paa aba ne̱e̱ aagooji ta̱ꞌo̱to̱. Paa ta̱yansun ta̱ndaabi ta̱ta aba tada̱ba hunranhunran gumunu hasaa, gaa ta ndaya ri na ne̱e̱ tutu ta shani hunranhunran na wyatu nda̱tu bwa zumaa.
Ama na̱ wana ga̱n jamaa hanshinhina ha̱ni ndaa, nꞌne̱e̱ na̱ ro̱pe̱, na̱ wana ha̱nka̱ri ndaa, shiraga iri ge̱ na ga̱tu namaa bisa̱.
Butu na̱nna bushi naa tanaa hiika̱hina̱ ha̱nka̱ri na wyatu, ta bwa íye̱ gagu paa Ayaahudiya hyo̱ kope na̱ sa̱ra̱ri. Bwa gura̱a̱ sha butu o̱to̱ na biigudu naa uwa̱ binaa aba ta nꞌgana Anaazare.
Bwa ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan bunii hanshinhina Ina na Hwe̱n, ta shaani ga̱tu kóta̱ni be̱.+ :6 Ta̱taga ta̱ka̱ ta̱duwa̱ni ta̱hyan kunna: Ta̱ribi kuta̱ndaaki bwa suuga̱ na̱ nꞌgira̱nshin nda̱a̱tu. Ama Lisiyasu, butu o̱to̱ naa sooja, bwa jaa, bwa ta̱ra̱a̱ga̱gi bwa na̱ kai. Bwa shani ana íye̱ butu na̱nna suuga̱ xajaa na uba̱ ndaa.Gaa na̱ hyuhyu ndaa kuu-ha̱nta̱a̱ni be̱, bi-nii maha̱ngaaga hyo̱ ri na ga̱tu íye̱ suuga̱ sundaabwa.>>
Awyatu o̱to̱ na Yaahudiya taa maa aba hin taa kunnu, ara̱ni hyo̱ ri na Tara̱tulusu bwa cici shi mahanda.
Bulusu maya̱a̱cigi kaꞌuba̱ na Feelisi
Na gwamina bwa pa̱ni ara na hyan Bulusu nje̱ mazama, sa̱i bwa hin, <<Nꞌnii mayaaciga hyuhyu nimi na̱ ame̱ na tande̱, ta na ta̱hyan ga̱n yan bi-nje̱ nꞌyo̱ nꞌhwarapi ma ndaaka wyatu na̱nna ta̱suuga̱.
Ai, kuu-ha̱nta̱a̱ni bi-nii insan ta̱hyan nꞌhwe̱n nꞌtahurici nꞌupwa na̱ nꞌreeko kuga̱n wuci Hurushaliima ma paga Hwe̱n hunrun kaun.
Ana̱nna ana nꞌíye̱ suuga̱, ata nꞌwuta̱ncin ma nda kuda̱ga na̱a̱ yaan, koo nꞌhiika̱hini ha̱nka̱ri na wyatu na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n, koo na̱ aka̱ta̱ku nda̱tu, koo nii yaan bibiin binaa ce̱pe̱ yana.
Iri na abaa cita̱ga̱ nimi niina ajaa ara ta̱bisa̱a̱ ibe̱ na mahanda.
<<Iri ka̱ na ga̱n ra̱ni ishi mahanda, tashi ga̱n jwarigi Hwe̱n na daadoo nda̱tu, ta̱jwara̱ga nata̱ Yo̱n na̱nna na Yeesu, ta aba hin ta̱shi nata̱ bigudu naa uwa̱. Ga̱n ra̱a̱ hyo̱ iri na ta̱gi nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ Muusa na̱ atakaada na acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama.
Nꞌshii bigata niimi paa Hwe̱n, haruwa na ana̱nna aba tanaa nda, ta̱hyan anii hiika̱hina̱ ana ꞌwa̱gi, ana bina̱ na̱ ana shici na bina̱ hyo̱.
Ta shani koya̱ ha̱ni ga̱n shii nii gata niimi, ga̱n jaa mꞌbaa mayaan, koo yaanyini na nꞌkaki kaꞌuba̱ na Hwe̱n koo awyatu.
<<Nꞌyo̱ nꞌhwarapi ga̱n kayaan, ta ga̱n kúshiike̱ Hurushaliima na̱ wana hyan ma iyaagi wyatu nda̱tu aꞌwa̱ta̱gi ꞌwaa, ma pana Hwe̱n ba̱iko.
Sa̱i aba nꞌwuta̱ni na̱ Ina na Hwe̱n, ga̱n ma huwo ta̱bwaciga hyuhyu nimi ta̱shiri, ga̱n na za nii yaan bigudu, ga̱n hiika̱hincin ha̱nka̱ri na wyatu.
Ama ayaan Ayaahudiya ana ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Aasiya ana tanaa piree, aba ta shi kajaa hina na uba̱ ndaa kaꞌíye̱ ta̱suuga̱ ta̱niimi aba nda̱i aꞌmꞌbaa mazama na̱ ga̱mi.
xAwyatu na̱nna acita̱gi pinsan na aba nꞌkota̱ni na̱ bwa ha̱ni na aba nꞌwuta̱ni na uba̱ na wyatu na ta ꞌyapa mazama.
Sa̱i da̱i kushi wana mayaan mazama maka̱ mata nama ga̱n tacita̱, nama ga̱n tataana nu, ha̱ni na ga̱n na isa na uba̱ ndaaba, ga̱n hin, <Na̱ wana na ta̱hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱ ta̱ta abaa ndaaka suuga̱ ba̱re na uba̱ ninhin.> >>
Akota̱ni Bulusu na̱ Kaisariya
Feelisi yan iri hwarapi ina Yo̱n na Yeesu, bwa isaa wyan, bwa hin, <<xUbutu o̱to̱ na sooja Lisiyasu wuce, naazhin ga̱n ꞌyapa ta̱suuga̱.>>
Sa̱i bwa pa̱ni sooja na o̱to̱ na Rooma xbuha̱mba Bulusu, ama xbuta yansan be̱ ta̱mataa, xawyatu ndaabwa naa jábagi, anaa iyaagagi be̱ ri na bwa ribi.
Na nꞌhwe̱n mꞌba huri ge̱, Feelisi bwa kúshiike̱ na̱ aꞌa̱yo Durusila, buyaan Buyaahudiya. Bwa ka̱ji xaꞌíye̱ Bulusu, bwa shiragi bwa kuubwa bisa̱ga̱ wyan kiigata ndaabwa ta̱pana ku-Ala̱masiihu Yeesu be̱ ne̱e̱.
Bulusu bwaa cita̱ga̱ mazama nama iri na ne̱e̱ to̱n, na̱ ta̱mahumuna̱ hyuhyu, na̱ hwe̱n na ta̱suuga̱ nata̱ wuci. Na bwa hange̱ kunnu, rukwanyan ruba kota̱ni Feelisi, sa̱i bwa hin Bulusu, <<Kushiika ye̱e̱ niina. Jaa kunde̱be̱ ha̱ba̱, nꞌja̱maa nꞌgáni.>>
Feelisi bwa shii ta̱hyan Bulusu nii pana be̱ yuwa, ta shani bwaa nꞌgagana be̱ do̱ko̱ do̱ko̱ ma ndaga mazama na̱a̱ bwa.
Ama na nꞌyo̱ reeko mꞌba huri, Fokiyusu Fesutusu bwa ra̱a̱ bizhe̱nke̱n naa ta̱gwamina ku-Feelisi. Feelisi bwa ga̱a̱ Bulusu na̱ zhaaro na̱ wana buribi xbucaanhini Ayaahudiya me̱.

Aꞌye̱e̱ suuga̱ nata̱ Bulusu ku-Fesutusu
Na nꞌhwe̱n nꞌtaatu mꞌba nje̱ na Fesutusu bwa hiin pasa tuma na gwamina, bwa ga̱a̱ Kaisariya zhagu Hurushaliima.
Apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya aba ja̱a̱ aba ꞌye̱e̱ suuga̱ nata̱ Bulusu waabwa.
Aba ro̱pe̱ be̱, xbundaaki wyan ta̱bure akúshihine̱ Bulusu Hurushaliima na̱ wana ashii ayaan xaha̱mba, jaa bwaa hura̱ akota̱ni be̱, akwane̱ be̱ na̱ yo̱n.
Fesutusu bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin, <<Ahambe̱ Bulusu na̱ Kaisariya, nꞌjaa taa ke̱nye̱n, nꞌnii majabaaga.
xAwyatu o̱to̱ ninhin jaa ta̱ja̱ba̱go, kuubwa butu nje̱ iri na pinsan iꞌíye̱ suuga̱ sundaabwa kaun.>>
Hurici nꞌhwe̱n ta̱ndatu koo upwa waaba, bwa kwashe̱e̱ke̱ Kaisariya. Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n bwa hunrani nii zhe̱nke̱n naa ta̱suuga̱, bwa ka̱ji xarágani Bulusu na uba̱ ndaabwa.
Na Bulusu bwa wuce, Ayaahudiya na ta jaa na̱ Hurushaliima aba riini be̱, abaa iyagi mazama mahwarapi nama cima̱ncin nama aba jaa ara ta̱bisa̱a̱ mashi mahanda.
Sa̱i Bulusu bwa maba̱ha̱ni hyuhyu ndaabwa, bwa hin, <<Ga̱n ndaakici nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Ayaahudiya, koo Ina na Hwe̱n, koo Kaisa pinsan.>>
Na Fesutusu bwa ribi ta̱caanhina Ayaahudiya me̱, bwa ha̱nta̱ni Bulusu, <<Koo bi-ribi u-ja̱a̱ Hurushaliima aandaaki suuga̱ na uba̱ nimi piree na̱ mana̱nna mazama?>>
Bulusu bwa hin, <<Nꞌne̱e̱ na̱ ina na ta̱suuga̱ na Kaisa, pina kata kashi paaka hyan aꞌnꞌndaaki suuga̱. Nꞌndaakici Ayaahudiya pinsan, gaa maa bi-yan kunnu mꞌbashi.
Kunshi butu naa pinsan, ga̱n nje̱ ri na hyan aꞌnꞌkwane̱, ga̱n jaa gaa aꞌnꞌkwane̱. Ama kuta̱suuga̱ nasu aba íye̱ suniimi ta̱shii mahanda, buza naa nii pana wyan ga̱mi. Ga̱n ro̱pe̱ xasha̱pi suuga̱ suniimi aꞌye̱e̱ paa Kaisa.>>
Na Fesutusu bwa hwii ta̱hantaana wyatu ndaabwa ana ta ꞌyapa mazama, bwa hin, <<Kunnu, bi-wya̱nzhin xasha̱pi suuga̱ sundaabi paa Kaisa, paa Kaisa kata gaa hura̱.>>
Fesutusu na̱ Agiripa nje̱ mazama nama Bulusu
Na nꞌhwe̱n mꞌba huri ge̱, Bugwama Agiripa na̱a̱ ya̱na̱a̱ naa a̱ Banisi+ :13 Bugwama Agiripa na̱ Banisi ashi mꞌmwaan na buugwama Hirudu Agiripa, gwatana ma Tuma 12:20-25aba jaa Kaisariya na̱ wana ta̱zumana Fesutusu.
Na ta̱hyan anii pa nꞌhwe̱n nꞌhwarapi kaun, sa̱i Fesutusu bwa pe̱e̱ mazama nama Bulusu kuugwama. Fesutusu bwa hin, <<Buyaan butu ne̱e̱ buna Feelisi bwa taꞌnꞌgaaga na̱ zhaaro.
Ha̱ni na ga̱n na naa na̱ Hurushaliima, apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ wyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya bana íye̱ suuga̱ sundaabwa, aba ribi nꞌya̱pi suuga̱ sundaabwa ta̱hyan bunje̱ pinsan.
Ama ga̱n bishi wyan ta̱hyan ga̱tu awyatu na Rooma ta̱ya̱wa̱nincin ta̱naa ndaakaka wyatu suuga̱ ta ga̱tu hungwa wyan na̱ aꞌuba̱ na ana íye̱ wyan suuga̱ aba ma gwataaga, agura̱a̱ pa wyan ha̱ba̱ xacita̱gi mazama koo amaba̱ha̱ni na̱ nꞌta̱suuga̱ nasu aba íye̱ wyan.
<<Na aba wuce huku na̱ ga̱mi, ga̱n ta̱cii ke̱nye̱n. Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, ga̱n ka̱ta̱ni zhe̱nke̱n naa ta̱suuga̱, ga̱n hin xashápi bwa butu.
Na wyatu na íye̱ be̱ ta̱suuga̱ aba hiiki aba cita̱gi mazama, aba ꞌye̱e̱ce̱ mayaan mazama nama iri na zumaancin na ga̱n shii ta̱hyan ahin bunje̱,
sa̱i kumazama nama aba ribici Bulusu naa cita̱ga̱ nama adiini ndaaba, na̱ butu yata na ꞌwi naa shi Yeesu naa Bulusu bwaa hyaan bune̱e̱ buwuma.
Na ga̱n ga̱n za iri na hyan ma hyan na̱ haruwa na aba hin, sa̱i ga̱n ha̱nta̱ni Bulusu koo buribi buja̱a̱ Hurushaliima andaaki be̱ ta̱suuga̱ na̱ ri na aba hin.
Na Bulusu bwa ro̱pe̱ xaꞌye̱e̱ ta̱suuga̱ ta̱ndaabwa ku-Kaisa bugwama naa o̱to̱ buꞌya̱pi ta̱suuga̱, sa̱i ga̱n hin xaha̱mba be̱ kuha̱ni na ga̱n kada aꞌye̱e̱ be̱ paa Kaisa.>>
Sa̱i bugwama Agiripa bwa hin Fesutusu, <<Ga̱n maa nꞌribi ma shiraga be̱.>>
Sa̱i Fesutusu bwa hin, <<Bi-ja̱a̱ ha̱nga muu na̱ bunwan.>>
Bulusu na̱ aꞌuba̱ naa gwama Agiripa
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, sa̱i Agiripa na̱ Banisi aba ta̱a̱ni ada̱bi na ta̱gwama, aba ta̱ni ka̱ta̱ku na ta̱suuga̱ na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ na gyasa na̱ wyatu o̱to̱ na ce̱pe̱. Sa̱i Fesutusu bwa pa̱ni nu xata̱ha̱ni Bulusu.
Sa̱i Fesutusu bwa hin, <<Bugwama Agiripa, na̱ awyatu na ne̱e̱ hina hyo̱ na̱ ga̱tu, butu bwa na bunaa hyo̱ wyatu na Ayaahudiya aba na íye̱ ta̱suuga̱ ta̱ndaabwa wa̱ka̱mi na̱ Hurushaliima, na̱ hina mayaan, hara̱ abaa ta ta̱ꞌungwa maꞌnꞌhyaan xata gaa be̱ buwuma.
Ama ga̱n nda̱ci bunje̱ ri na wuciha̱ni na hyan akwane̱ be̱. Tana ta̱hyan bwa na̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa buro̱pe̱ xaꞌye̱e̱ ta̱suuga̱ ta̱ndaabwa paaku bugwama naa o̱to̱ Kaisa, ga̱n hin nꞌnii kada aꞌye̱e̱ be̱ waabwa.
<<Ama nꞌza mayaan mazama nama bina̱ nama ga̱n nii taagaga butu o̱to̱ bugwama na̱ wana ndaabwa. Na̱ wana kunnu nꞌíye̱ bwa kaꞌuba̱ ninhin hyo̱, na uba̱ ndaa hiku bugwama Agiripa, na̱ wana kuta̱nhwii be̱ ta̱hantaana ma da̱ba ri na ga̱n taga.
Nꞌta̱ndaya ta̱niimi, unje̱ce̱ to̱n aka̱ji butu naa zhaaro bunaa za yaan ri na bisa̱a̱ iri na we̱ na bwa nje̱ zhagu Rooma.>>

Bulusu maba̱ha̱ni kaꞌuba̱ na Agiripa
Na̱ bwa ha̱ni, sa̱i Agiripa bwa hin Bulusu, <<Aapa̱ nu, maba̱ha̱ni.>> Nii ke̱nye̱n be̱, Bulusu bwa ka̱cihini ara, bwa pa̱shi mazama nama hyan bumaba̱ha̱ni,
<<Nꞌta̱ to̱n, bugwama Agiripa, ta na ta̱hyan na uba̱ ndaa ta ga̱n maba̱ha̱na̱ hyuhyu nimi ba̱re na̱ aza̱zama na awyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya aba íye̱ suuga̱ suniimi,
wana ta̱hyan biza mꞌpirwa ta̱yansun hyo̱ iri na nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Ayaahudiya na̱ iri na aba ne̱e̱ na̱ kuda̱ga na̱ be̱. Na̱ wana kunnu, iiro̱pe̱, re̱ kuri, nꞌshiraga ki.
<<Hyo̱ wyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya, ayan hyo̱ hunranhunran na ga̱n nje̱ ha̱ni na ga̱n tashi be̱e̱, tana yigo na ga̱n tanaa na̱ ce̱pe̱ nimi na̱ Hurushaliima kuba̱re yana.
Ana nꞌyansun hasaa, hara̱ maa karibi anii ara ta̱hyan ga̱n shi Bufaraasiya ta ana hura̱gi ta̱jwara̱ga nꞌgira̱nshin yata ki na nꞌadiini nda̱tu.
Niina nꞌe̱nshe̱n na uba̱ ndaa aꞌnꞌndaaki ta̱suuga̱ na̱ wana nꞌshii bigata na̱ ala̱ka̱wa̱ri na Hwe̱n bwa tanda ta na̱ adaadoo nda̱tu.
Ala̱ka̱wa̱ri yata tashi na nꞌkorogo nꞌnda̱a̱tu nꞌupwa na̱ nꞌreeko mꞌba tasha̱a̱ nꞌgata ta̱nii ciga̱. Tashani abaa mapa dibi ma paga Hwe̱n hunrun koya̱ hwe̱n na̱ gita. Bugwama, na̱ wana ga̱n shii bigata nꞌta̱ciga̱hina̱ ta̱yata hiku ta̱ta Ayaahudiya aba nda̱i ta̱shi pinsan.
Mbata shani nꞌta̱ndaya ta̱niinhin, ga̱hin nda̱i majaa nda Hwe̱n hiika̱hini wyatu na hoo ꞌwa̱?
<<Ga̱n na̱ hyuhyu nimi maa na̱ ayigo, nꞌtandaya ma nje̱ to̱n, ma nda komba̱ri na nii yansan mazama nama Yeesu Bunaazare ta̱re̱ iyeebe.
Iri na ga̱n na nda nu na̱ Hurushaliima, hara̱ ga̱n de̱be̱ ta̱kai paaka apirisiti na o̱to̱ wana ma kadaaga ayata na pa̱ni nꞌgata na̱ zhaaro. Hyo̱ na̱ ha̱ni na aba tanaa kunaa wyan, ga̱n tanaa sa̱ ma ta wyan ta̱kai.
Hyo̱ aka̱ta̱ku ndaaba ga̱n na jwara̱gagana ga̱n pa wyan ngwan wana hyan anaa ndaga mazama nama hwashe̱ nꞌruzha̱a̱ naru Yeesu. Na̱ wana nꞌtaribici wyan mahwa, ga̱n mata̱ ta̱naa jwara̱gagana nꞌcice̱pe̱ na nꞌta̱yaan ce̱nye̱n ma yansan wyan ta̱mataa.>>
Haruwa na Bulusu bwa taraa Yeesu
Tuma 9:1-19; 22:6-16
<<Yaan hwe̱n, ga̱n ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hani zhagu Dimasiku, nꞌta̱kai nata̱ apirisiti na o̱to̱ na̱ takaada na ta̱kai na aba mꞌpa̱ni.
Bugwama, bike̱nye̱n naa hwe̱n da̱, ga̱n na̱ yo̱n nꞌta̱hani, ga̱n nda̱i maza̱ki nama huri nama hwe̱n, mꞌba tára̱kani nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, mꞌba ta̱ra̱ka̱ni riinha̱nu na̱ ga̱mi na̱ wyatu na ga̱n ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hani na̱ aba.
Hyo̱ ga̱tu kinai na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n, sa̱i ga̱n hange̱ mazama na̱ Ta̱ꞌaramaya, <Shawulu Shawulu, na̱ wana ba̱ gaa mꞌpa kaki? Bi-nii mapa ngwan ꞌye̱n na gaa nꞌribici.>
<<Sa̱i ga̱n hin, <Butu o̱to̱, iyaa nu ya̱nu gaa shi?>
<<Sa̱i Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwa nꞌhin, <Ga̱n ta Yeesu bunaa gaa kaki.
Too hiika̱ isa isa. Mꞌmabisa̱a̱ hyuhyu nimi wakaa na̱ wana iika̱shi u-shi bugyama na̱ bunaa nii bisa̱ wyatu iri na gaa nda̱i gaa hange̱ hiku inimi na̱ yaanyini na ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ iyeebe.
Ga̱n na̱maa biha̱na̱ kawyatu ndaa, na̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya, ana ga̱n na̱maa kada tuma waaba.
Bi-nii guna̱a̱ suyishe sundaaba akíciike̱ kuta̱yincincin zhagu kuta̱gwaan, paa kuta̱gwama nata̱ Bupira̱ zhagu paaku Hwe̱n. Na̱ kunnu Hwe̱n bwa jaa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ wyan pinsan ndaaba, na̱ ta̱hya̱su pa̱ri huku na̱ wyatu na Hwe̱n bwa pe̱e̱n aba shi ndaabwa, wana apa̱ni nꞌgata wa̱ka̱mi.>
<<Bugwama, wana kunnu, nꞌga̱a̱ci ta̱jwara̱ga ri yata haka ra̱rabi na báni ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
Nꞌtapasa ta̱bisa̱ga̱ wyatu na̱ Dimasiku, naazhin ga̱n nje̱ na̱ Hurushaliima na̱ hyo̱ mꞌbiin na Yaahudiya, naazhin ga̱n ndaaki wyatu na shici Ayaahudiya xapa̱ni pinsan baa, akúshiike̱ paaku Hwe̱n, anje̱ ri na nii bisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan apa̱ni pinsan baa.
Ta shani ayaan Ayaahudiya aba nꞌkota̱ni na̱ bambanu na Ina na Hwe̱n, ta aba ribi hyan aꞌnꞌkwane̱.
Ama Hwe̱n bwaa mꞌpyaanwyan nii inro̱n bwa wuce kuba̱re bike̱nye̱n yana, ta shani ga̱n e̱she̱ ga̱n nda mazama nama Yeesu kawyatu o̱to̱ na̱ ana njeke. Bwa shici iyaanyini goo ga̱n cita̱ga̱, sa̱i da̱i iri na Muusa na̱ acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama aba tahyan inii nda,
ibe̱ ta shi, mahanda Ala̱masiihu nii swa ta̱guma, bishii naa yigo naa nii hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱. Na̱ kunnu ta be̱ nii íye̱ awyatu kuta̱gwaan nata̱ mazama nama zumaa, hyo̱ kawyatu nde̱e̱be̱ na̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya.>>
Bulusu bwa ma mayaaciga hyuhyu ndaabwa, sa̱i Fesutusu bwa ta̱a̱ni nu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ bwa hin, <<Bulusu bi-ndagi mꞌpe̱re̱, ta̱yansun nata̱ gaa mꞌbaa o̱to̱ ta̱a̱ke̱ce̱he̱ne̱ hyuhyu.>>
Sa̱i Bulusu bwa hin, <<Butu o̱to̱ Fesutusu, Hwe̱n duwa̱ni ta̱kai, shii mꞌpe̱re̱ nꞌta. Iri na ga̱n cita̱ga̱ mahanda mata ibe̱ shi ina bina̱.
Ai, bugwama yan hyo̱ iri ya̱nu, ta ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ mazama rukwanyan ruba za. Ga̱n yan ta̱hyan buyan wuun hyo̱, na̱ wana anje̱ce̱ ri ya̱nu ta̱swee.
Bugwama, bi-ra̱a̱ mazama nama acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama? Ga̱n yan mashi kunnu.>>
Bugwama Agiripa bwa ra̱ni, bwa hin Bulusu, <<Bi-ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan nii ke̱nye̱n ge̱ ma sha Ukirisita?>>
Bulusu bwa hin, <<Koo nii ke̱nye̱n ge̱ koo binaa nge̱nshe̱n, nꞌne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan Hwe̱n nii shana shii gaa ka̱, hyo̱ ana nꞌshiraagi ba̱re, ashi haku ga̱mi, ama shici na̱ akaca na̱nna.>>
Sa̱i bugwama na̱ gwamina na̱ Banisi na̱ hyo̱ ayaan ana tahunraana aba hiiki.
Na aba ba̱ni paa ta̱suuga̱ aba mahin, <<Butu na̱nna nje̱ce̱ ri na wuci ta̱guna̱na̱ koo ta̱kuna be̱.>>
Na̱ wana kunnu, Agiripa bwa hin Fesutusu, <<xBwa shici butu na̱nna bwa ꞌye̱e̱ce̱ suuga̱ sundaabwa paa Kaisa, kata̱zhiga̱ni be̱.>>

Bulusu ta̱ni hantun na ma̱ni zhagu Rooma
Na aba ta̱hwii ta̱ꞌa̱sa̱a̱ga̱na̱ ta̱nu hantun na ma̱ni zhagu Itaaliya, Bulusu na̱ ayaan wyatu na zhaaro, aba pa̱ni yaan sooja na o̱to̱ paakii gudu naa sooja na Kaisa ta̱ha̱mba wyan, bunaa aba ta hyan Yuliyusu.
Ga̱tu ta̱ni yaan hantun na báni Adiramitiyumu, una tajwara̱gagana ayaan ce̱pe̱ na ne̱e̱ na̱ mꞌbiin na n-Aasiya, ga̱tu pa̱shi ta̱hani. Arisitarakusu, buyaan butu naa Tasaloonika na ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Makidooniya, bwa ne̱e̱ huku na̱ ga̱tu.
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, ga̱tu wuci Sidon. Kabata Yuliyusu bwa ndaaki Bulusu ri na bure, paakuu bwa na hakata be̱ bwa ja̱a̱ kuta̱shika ta̱ndaabwa, xapági be̱ ri na bwa ribi.
Na ga̱tu hiiki kaun na̱ hantun na ma̱ni, upyara bwa hiin ta̱yansan. Sa̱i ga̱tu ra̱a̱n ta̱baa nata̱ ucibiri na Kuburusu paa pyara bwa ma̱a̱ncin kai.
Na ga̱tu ka̱ciga̱ni rwaga na o̱to̱ na maꞌira̱ na ne̱e̱ do̱ko̱ na̱ ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Kilikiya na̱ Pamafiliya, ga̱tu wuci Mira na ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Likiya.
Kabata bwa sooja na o̱to̱ bwa de̱be̱ yaan hantun na báni Alekazandiriya na nii jaga ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Itaaliya, bwa ta̱ta̱ha̱ni na̱ ame̱.
Ga̱tu pa̱ nꞌhwe̱n nꞌhwarapi ma nda ta̱hani shukuu, ga̱tu wuci dike̱ do̱ko̱ na̱ ce̱pe̱ na Kinidusu. Na pyara bwa tata̱yansan ta̱hura̱ iyeebe, sa̱i ga̱tuu raan bibiin naa ma̱a̱ncin pyara, ta̱baa nata̱ cibiri naa Kiriiti do̱ko̱ na̱ ce̱pe̱ na Sala̱moni.
Ga̱tu jwara̱gani inza̱n bizu hara̱ ga̱tu wuci kayaan pa̱ri naka aba ta hyan Pa̱ri naka Hura̱gi Gama Kuta̱masoo, do̱ko̱ na ce̱pe̱ na Lasiya.
Ta̱hoo ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ ke̱nye̱n ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, uyo̱ bwa ke̱ne̱ ta̱huwa̱, ushuyo wuci+ :9 ushuyo wuci Ta̱ta nata̱ yigo ta̱ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan, Ubuki na hwe̱n na Ta̱shapa Ruhaki naru Pinsan bwa huri Ata nda buki na̱nna na̱ nꞌta̱huwa̱ nata̱ pyanda na hin ta̱ndushi koo ta̱pasa nata̱ pyanda na hin upwa. Ubwa ha̱ni ata nda pyara na za nꞌhiro̱ na̱ kai na̱ rwaga na o̱to̱.na ta̱hani ta̱ba jaa zumaa. Sa̱i Bulusu bwa kooci wyan,
bwa hin, <<Awyatu ma, ga̱n nda̱i ta̱hani ta̱yana ta̱jaa mꞌbaa bina̱, ta̱nii mꞌbaa kina, shii kubina̱ na ꞌwaa na̱ hantun kubwa, hyo̱ na̱ nꞌga̱tu.>>
Ama ubwa usooja na o̱to̱ bwa huri ta̱shiraga mazama nama butu naa nii mana hantun na̱a̱ naa hya̱a̱ wuun, bwa ga̱a̱ nama Bulusu bwaa cita̱ga̱.
Na ta̱hyan paaku ta̱sha̱a̱ hantun do̱ko̱ na̱ Lasiya kazumaancin na hyan hantun jira, sa̱i aba hwarapi aba huri ta̱ruba̱ xta̱re̱ iyeebe nꞌta̱hani, xta̱maka̱nta̱ni ta̱wuci ce̱pe̱ na Finiki mꞌba nii nda, wana ahwii shuyo kaun. Finiki ushi tasha na hantun na ma̱ni na ne̱e̱ na̱ Kiriiti na gwatagi zuba na hiin gwataga hwe̱n ta̱ꞌira̱ na̱ nꞌruꞌwa naru hiin gwataga hwe̱n ta̱ꞌira̱.
Upyara punshin na̱ rwaga na o̱to̱
Na upyara na báni ruꞌwa bwa pa̱shi ta̱naa kumba̱ga̱ni ge̱e̱ge̱e̱, wyatu aba shii ta̱hyan ri na aba ribi ta wuci, aba máni ta̱ruma nata̱ ta ha̱mba̱ga̱ hantun, aba jwarigi do̱ko̱ nii biin binaa ucibiri na Kiriiti.
Bike̱nye̱n be̱ ta̱ci du, kuyaan pyara na kai bwa puuka̱ni na báni zuba na gwatagi hwe̱n ta̱bani, na báni kubwa cibiri.
Na pyara bwa zha̱a̱nta̱ni hantun, hantun bwa a̱rici ta̱gwataga paaku pyara bwa báni, ana nii mana bwa hantun aba hakaci upyara bwaa ta̱mana.
Na ga̱tu huri ta̱baa nata̱ biyaan bicibiri binaa aba ta hyan Kauda, paaku pyara bwa ma̱ncin kai, dike̱ ga̱tu tamáni hantun na njeke zhagu kuhantun na o̱to̱ ga̱tu zwa̱ga̱ni.
Na ga̱tu hwii ta̱zwagana awyatu na nii mana aba nje̱ maka̱ri aba ka̱da̱a̱gi ihwa̱ riinha̱nu kuhantun na o̱to̱ wana uta hwaataga. Aba gura̱a̱ ciinha̱na̱a̱ ta̱ruma nata̱ cima̱nciin na ta hasaa ta̱hani nata̱ hantun wana xupyara naa tutumaanwyan wuun, wana aba a̱rici ta̱naa mana hantun. Ana nda kunnu na̱ wana rukwanyan xuhantun tajaa bwe̱ wyan kange̱nshe̱n na Sira̱tusu ana ta cwara iri.
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, aba pa̱shi ꞌwaa ta̱ꞌushiga̱ga̱ na̱ ame̱ na hantun ma bwaga wuun na̱ ma̱ni, wana ma̱ni manii gusa̱, mꞌbaa ta̱bibika̱ka̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Na̱ hwe̱n na hin taatu, aba gura̱a̱ bwaga yaan ꞌwaa na ta̱naa mana hantun na̱ ame̱ na ma̱ni.
Na ga̱tu pa̱ nꞌhwe̱n nꞌhwarapi, ga̱tu nda̱ci hwe̱n koo nꞌgwasu, upyara na ruro ma ta̱puuka̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, ga̱tu ya̱a̱cigi nꞌgata ta̱jaa nda bina̱.
Na ta̱hyan ata̱a̱ ke̱nye̱n are̱ce̱ shami, sa̱i Bulusu bwa hiiki isa isa na wyantancin ndaaba, bwa hin, <<Wyatu ma, bwa shi ga̱hin tatibi mazama maniimi ta̱hyan ta-gaa ma ucibiri na Kiriiti, kungwan na̱nna na̱ iri na fogi nje̱ce̱.
Niina nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, ta ma kiigata macimi, buza naa iri be̱ nii ta ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabwa kuhantun ta nii ira̱ na̱ ma̱ni.
Na̱ wana gita na hundara, buyaan butuma naa Hwe̱n una ga̱n shii ndaabwa, una ga̱n jwarigi, butaꞌe̱she̱ do̱ko̱ na̱ ga̱mi,
bwa nꞌhin, <Bulusu, ta-ha̱nga rukwanyan. Mahanda bi-nii isa na uba̱ na Kaisa u-cici mazama. Na̱ wana ndaa ta Hwe̱n nꞌta̱kai ta̱ndaabwa ta̱ta bwa nii biha̱na̱ wyatu na gaa ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hani na̱ aba.>
Na̱ wana kunnu, wyatu ma, duwa̱na̱ ma kiigata ta̱ta macimi, ga̱n pa̱nii gata ku-Hwe̱n kubwa mꞌbisa̱gi, kunnu mꞌba nii sha.
Ama yansun ma ta̱hyan ga̱ga̱ga̱ pyara bwa nii ta̱mbwa kayaan nge̱nshe̱n ana yaan cibiri, hantun hwaatagi.>>
Pyara bwe̱ hantun na̱ ucibiri
Na̱ gita na hin upwa na̱ na̱nshin, pyara bwaa mana hantun na̱ asumo̱ ku-Rwaga na O̱to̱ na Meditereeniya. Bike̱nye̱n naa gita ꞌya̱piga̱su, wyatu na nii mana hantun aba hoo sha̱a̱ ta̱hyan ta̱goki nꞌce̱nye̱n.
Aba ma̱a̱ maꞌira̱ nama ma̱ni, mꞌba wuci ta̱funda nata̱ buna biyina̱ ka̱ na̱ wa̱shi. Na ga̱tu gura̱a̱ hura̱, aba gura̱a̱ maa maꞌira̱, aba de̱be̱ ta̱funda nata̱ buna kuje tundushi.
Rukwanyan ruba kota̱ni wyan, xuhantun ta jaa maꞌuri na̱ atari, aba gura̱a̱ ciinha̱na̱a̱ ta̱ruma ta̱na̱nshin nꞌta̱baa nata̱ hantun na ta hasaa ta̱hani. Sa̱i aba shii suyishe ma nda ro̱pe̱ wana xubunwan ha̱a̱n na̱ ha̱ni.
Ama wyatu na nii mana hantun aba nje̱ ta̱hyan xagidigi. Mꞌba nje̱ce̱, aba ca̱a̱nha̱ni hantun na njeke ma nda riinshina̱ kanii ciinha̱na̱ arunruma na ne̱e̱ na̱ aꞌuba̱ na hantun.
Sa̱i Bulusu bwa hin sooja na o̱to̱ na̱ ayaan sooja, <<Kawyatu na̱nna e̱she̱she̱ kuhantun na̱nna, za haruwa na baa bina̱.>>
Na aba hange̱ kunnu, sa̱i asooja abaa ꞌyapaga ihwa̱ na hantun na njeke ubwa zwii ma̱ni.
Na bunwan bwa goki ta̱haan, Bulusu bwaa rupa wyan, xare̱gi shami, bwa hin, <<Ba̱re nꞌhwe̱n upwa na̱ nꞌna̱nshin na ga̱hin nje̱ na ga̱hin makaki bwa zaa naa re̱ koori.
Kusu re̱ ma shami na̱ wana suhyu suniinhin subini, iri za na nii ta koo biswa̱ri niinhin.>>
Na Bulusu bwa cici kunnu, bwa sha̱pi buroodi na̱ uba̱ ndaaba, bwa gooji Hwe̱n, bwa ya̱biza̱gi, bwa re̱ge̱ ta̱re̱.
Hyo̱ ndaaba koo buya̱ bwa ta̱zhiga̱ni gata, aba re̱gi shami.
Hyo̱ nda̱tu na̱ ame̱ na hantun ga̱tu nꞌyina̱ nꞌreeko na̱ kuje ta̱nda̱ra̱ na̱ cininhin (276).
Na aba re̱ shami aba ciga̱gi, aba bwagi ala̱kama na bwe̱ hyo̱ na̱ ma̱ni wana xaha̱sa̱a̱ hantun maca̱ma̱nta̱n.
Na bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n, awyatu na nii mana hantun aba yancin paaka aba ne̱e̱, ama aba e̱nshe̱n yaan bisusooru binaa ange̱nshe̱n. Aba shii ta̱hyan anii iya hantun paaku aba nge̱nshe̱n aꞌisaa wuun kaun.
Aba ka̱sa̱gi ihwa̱ hyo̱ ina ta̱ruma nata̱ ca̱ma̱cin nata̱ ta hasaa ta̱hani nata̱ hantun, aba ga̱a̱ tuun na̱ ma̱ni. Nii ke̱nye̱n ya̱nu to̱n, aba tunfunriin ihwa̱ na ta kadaga mꞌpa̱paaru na nꞌtanaa kicihinaa hantun. Sa̱i aba hiika̱hini uzuzu na o̱to̱ na ta naa na̱ hyuhyu na hantun haruwa na mꞌpyara mꞌbaa naa tutumaanwyan wuun iyeebe. Aba sha̱a̱ta̱ni hyuhyu zhagu bisusooru naa inza̱n na rwaga.
Ama na ga̱tu wuci yaan biko paaka arwaga ba ura̱ka̱ku, hantun bwa ta̱ni na̱ ange̱nshe̱n, uhyuhyu bwa maka̱bi na̱ ange̱nshe̱n bwa a̱rici ta̱maduga. Ta̱baa nata̱ hantun ta̱ba ke̱ne̱ ta̱maburaga na̱ wana ma̱ni nama nii basagana wuun.Ship that broken|WA03994b.tif|col|ACT 27.39-41|Wade Images|Hantun na ma̱ni mꞌba hwaatagi|27:41Asooja aba hwii shiri na hyan akunai wyatu na zhaaro na̱ wana xata jaa kinai ma̱ni afogi.
Ama bwa sooja na o̱to̱ bwa yanshin wyan, na̱ wana buribi bubiha̱ni Bulusu. Na̱ wana kunnu, bwa pa̱ni nu ta̱hyan koo buya̱ naa a̱ri ma̱ni xbuke̱ne̱ ma̱ni kwan zhagu hira̱ree,
ana bwe̱ xaka̱ta̱ga̱ni akaataako, koo mꞌbubwaare̱ na nꞌhantun. Na aba nje̱ kunnu, naazhin kwayaa bwa wuci inza̱n gumunu.

Bulusu na̱ ucibiri na aba ta hyan Mala̱ta
Na ga̱tu ba̱na̱ni aba ta̱bishi ta̱hyan ruzha̱a̱ naru ubwa cibiri rushi Mala̱ta.
Aba awyatu na bwa cibiri aba ta̱ndaaki ri na bina̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱. Sa̱i aba ta̱ra̱a̱ hyo̱ nda̱tu, aba ta̱shanaanyin ra, na̱ wana ashira̱ tanaa kina ta̱hobi ta̱ba ne̱e̱.
Bulusu ma dá̱bagi ꞌwe̱e̱ bwa ma sha̱a̱ta̱ga̱na̱ na̱ ra, uhwaa bwa báni una manwyanrin nama we̱ wana mamboo nama ra, ubwa sa̱a̱ki ara na Bulusu.
Na aba wyatu naa be̱e̱ ko aba nda̱i ubwa hwaa njuunrin na̱ ara na Bulusu, aba mahyaan kaba kaba ta̱hyan, <<Butu na̱nna bushi naa kúne̱e̱ yaan, inda̱i koo na bwa ba̱na̱ni na̱ ma̱ni, ruhaki taru jwárige̱ bwa sa̱i kuuꞌwi.>>
Bulusu bwa bizhiga̱ni ara, bwa munsani hwaa na̱ ra, bwa magumahincin.
Awyatu aba ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan bunii mutaanwyan koo bukinai kunrun gba̱n buꞌwi, ama na aba ta̱a̱ ke̱nye̱n aba nda̱i za ri na ta̱ bwa, aba he̱re̱ge̱ mazama ta̱hyan bushi yaan hwe̱n ta.
Do̱ko̱ nii be̱e̱ biko, kayaan pa̱ri katanaa naka butu o̱to̱ naa ubwa cibiri, ruzha̱a̱ rundaabwa Fubuliyusu, bwa ta̱pa̱ pa̱ri ga̱tu pa̱ nꞌhwe̱n nꞌtaatu.
Ashin aba taa mamboo na̱ aꞌa̱ta̱ni. Sa̱i Bulusu bwa ta̱ni paakuu aba ne̱e̱, bwa ndaaki wyan ro̱pe̱, bwa sha̱a̱gi wyan nꞌara, ashin ba kwade̱ge̱.
Na aba nda̱i kunta, awyatu na ha̱ngagici sa̱ ana ubwa cibiri, abaa jábagi ma kuda̱gahinaa wyan.
Aba ta̱pa̱ hunrun ta̱ꞌo̱to̱. Na ga̱tu pa̱ pyanda nꞌtaatu, ga̱tu hiin hiika̱ ta̱huri ta̱hani na̱ hantun na ma̱ni, aba ta̱pa̱ga̱ni iri hyo̱ na ga̱tu ribi kuta̱ba ta̱hani.
Bulusu wuci ce̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ Rooma
Na ga̱tu hiiki sa̱i ga̱tu ta̱ni yaan hantun na ma̱ni una Alekazandiriya na hwii shuyo na̱ bwa cibiri. Aba sha̱bi hyuhyu na ubwa hantun na̱ mꞌpirwa na nꞌahwe̱n ana ta̱ree.
Ga̱tu wuci ce̱pe̱ na Sirakusu ga̱tu nje̱ kaun nꞌhwe̱n nꞌtaatu.
Na̱ nꞌkaba ga̱tu sha̱a̱ta̱ni hyuhyu kuce̱pe̱ na Rigiyumu. Na hwe̱n ka̱ bwa huri, upyara bwa híike na̱ nꞌruꞌwa, bunwan bwa ha̱a̱n ga̱tu wuci Futiyoli.
Kaba ta ga̱tu ta wuta̱na̱ aya̱too ana pa̱ni nꞌgata, aba ta̱ro̱pe̱ ta̱pa̱a̱gi wyan nꞌhwe̱n nꞌta̱nda̱ra̱, ga̱tu nje̱ nꞌhwe̱n kunnu. Na̱ kunnu da̱i ga̱tu ta wuta̱ nꞌcice̱pe̱ na ne̱e̱ riinhinu na̱ Rooma.
Na aya̱too nda̱tu ana pa̱ni nꞌgata ana ce̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ Rooma aba hange̱ wuco nda̱tu, aba jaa xata̱zumani na̱ wuco ta na̱ Kasuwa na ba ta hyan Afiyusu, na̱ pa̱ri naka ba tahyan Nꞌina na Nꞌta̱ha̱nka̱na̱ Nꞌtaatu. Na Bulusu bwa nda̱i wyan, bwa gooji Hwe̱n, bwa duwa̱ni shita̱ ta̱ta.
Na ga̱tu ta̱ni Rooma, aba pa̱ni Bulusu ina ta̱hyan xbunaa na̱ bwa aba na̱ sooja ka̱ na hambe̱ bwa.
Bulusu cita̱gi mazama nama Yeesu na̱ Rooma
Na Bulusu bwa nje̱ nꞌhwe̱n nꞌtaatu na̱ wuco Rooma, sa̱i bwa nꞌgani awyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya na ne̱e̱ kaun. Na aba mawuna̱ni, sa̱i bwa hin wyan, <<Aya̱too ma, ataꞌnꞌkota̱na̱ na̱ Hurushaliima aba nꞌye̱e̱ kawyatu o̱to̱ na Arooma na ne̱e̱ kaun, koo na ga̱n ta nje̱ce̱ koori na we̱ kuꞌawyatu nda̱tu koo kuꞌnꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌadaadoo nda̱tu.
Arooma aba nꞌha̱nta̱a̱ni, aba ribi na hyan aꞌnꞌta̱zhiga̱ni na̱ wana aꞌnꞌde̱be̱ce̱ na̱ yaan pinsan na nii shana aꞌnꞌkwane̱.
Ama na awyatu o̱to̱ na Ayaahudiya ba ga̱a̱ ta̱rana, sa̱i ubwa nꞌshaagi ga̱ga̱ga̱ ta̱hyan sa̱i kunsha̱pa̱cigi ta̱suuga̱ ta̱niimi ga̱n ꞌye̱e̱ ku-Kaisa, koo na ta̱hyan shii nꞌhiin iya nu awyatu nimi suuga̱.
Ta shani ga̱mi ribi ma ta̱ndaya, iibisa̱gi ma mazama. Yansun ma ta̱hyan aꞌnꞌka̱da̱gi na̱ akaca na̱nna na̱ wana bunaa Aꞌisiraaꞌila aba shii ta̱hyan biwuci, Ala̱masiihu.>>
Sa̱i aba ra̱ni bwa aba hin, <<Ga̱tu nda̱ci yaan takaada na báni ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Ayaahudiya na̱ mꞌmazama mandaabi, buza yaan bunda̱a̱tu naa jaa pina bwa íye̱ mazama mandaabi, koo bucici yaan ri na zumaancin na̱ gaa.
Ama ta̱ribi ta̱hange̱ kwan nꞌhunjo̱ ndaabi na̱ nu ndaa, na̱ wana ta̱hyan ta̱nda̱i kope awyatu nii cita̱ga̱ ri na zumaancin nama bigudu na̱nna naa fo.>>
Aba shii hwe̱n na ta̱ꞌura̱ku, sa̱i aba jaa awyatu hwarapi paa Bulusu bwa te̱ne̱. Bwa pa̱shi ta na̱ bunwan maza kushurugo bwaa bisa̱ga̱ wyan mazama nama ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ma hurupa̱ga̱na̱ wyan ce̱be̱ ta̱hyan Yeesu be̱ taa shi naa Hwe̱n bwa káji. Bwaa nda tuma na̱ atakaada na nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa na̱ ana acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama.
Aka̱ aba pa̱ni sume̱ sundaaba na̱ ri na bwa cici, aka̱ aba pa̱ncin nꞌgata.
Na̱ wana kunnu aba mapa̱ncin sume̱ suka̱ kaba kaba. Ta aba ga̱a̱ kaun sa̱i Bulusu bwa bishi wyan mazama ma ka̱ bwa hin, <<Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n tacita̱ mahanda na be̱ tanda mazama na̱ adaadoo ninhin kunu na bucita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama Ishaaya, ta̱hyan,
<< <Jaga paaka awyatu na̱nna, u-hin,
<<Ta̱ha̱nga inii ha̱nga, ama ga̱hin jaa yansun iri na aba hin mahwa,
ta̱ndaya inii ndaya, ama ga̱hin jaa huwa̱ga̱ iri na aba nje̱ mahwa.>>
Na̱ wana nꞌgata na nꞌawyatu na̱nna shirigi,
aba bukakani suce̱be̱ sundaaba,
aba guna̱a̱ni suyishe sundaaba,
na̱ wana hyan xata ndaya nꞌsuyishe sundaaba,
xata ha̱nga nꞌsuce̱be̱ sundaaba,
xata insan na̱ nꞌgata nꞌndaaba iri na ne̱e̱,
na hyan ayimirike wa̱ka̱mi ma kuda̱gahina wyan.>
<<Too, yansun ma ta̱hyan, Uhwe̱n káji mazama nama ta̱biha̱na̱ mandaabwa mꞌba wuce tapaa awyatu na shici Ayaahudiya. Aba baa shiraga ara̱a̱ muu.>> + :28 Ta̱yaan ta̱taga ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa aaya na 29 kunna: Na bwa cici kunnu, sa̱i Ayaahudiya aba ba̱ni ma maga̱a̱ga̱nu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ kaba kaba.Bulusu bwa hunrani hyo̱ nꞌyo̱ nꞌree na̱ bwa ina ma pagana yuwa na bwa ina, ma raaga hyo̱ ana jaa waabwa.
Na ta̱hyan ayanshincin bwa mazama nama ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱naa nda. Bwaa nda ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ Butu O̱to̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu na za rukwanyan.
EPH - Pangu

Afisa
Iri na ta̱yansun na yigo
Bulusu ta tataga takaada na̱nna ha̱ni na bwa ne̱e̱ na̱ zhaaro na̱ Rooma. Butataga wuun kuꞌaba gwatani na̱ yo̱ na hin 60 na̱ nꞌta̱mantan nata̱ Yeesu. Butataga na̱nna takaada bwa ka̱ji wuun ku-Aꞌafisa nꞌta̱hyan, kacita̱gi, agura̱a̱ kada wuun kuꞌayaan nꞌgudu na nꞌawyatu na Yeesu.
Ubwa takaada tasha na bisa̱gi awyatu ku-Hwe̱n bwa ribi ta̱wuna̱a̱na̱ awyatu hyo̱ ku-Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, shii kawyatu hyo̱ na̱ iri na bwa nje̱ na ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n. Ubwa takaada tasha na duwa̱nii shita̱ ta̱ta kana pa̱ni nꞌgata ku-Yeesu, na hyan ayansun ashi iri ka̱ shii kuna̱ nu.
Utakaada tapasa ta̱nda mazama nama ta̱maꞌunpa̱n suhyu ishi ri ka̱. Hwe̱n takasa ana shi ndaabwa, paa bwa bisa̱a̱ ta̱pana ꞌye̱n ta̱ndaabwa, na bwa taha̱mba̱ga̱ncin wyan pinsan ndaaba wana Buyoo, Ala̱masiihu Yeesu. Uhwe̱n bwa gura̱a̱ ciga̱hina̱ ala̱ka̱wa̱ri paa bwa tapana wyan Bihwaanwun ndaabwa.
Na̱ ame̱ na takaada na̱nna, Bulusu cita̱gi kujabagu na zumaa una awyatu na Ala̱masiihu bwa ne̱e̱. Bwa gura̱a̱ ndaga mazama mahwarapi paa aba nꞌgani awyatu na Ala̱masiihu ta̱ꞌwaba, Ala̱masiihu be̱ shi hyuhyu na ta̱ba ta̱ꞌwaba. Bwa gura̱a̱ kuta̱a̱ wyan na̱ nꞌta̱ma nata̱ e̱she̱ hiku. Ala̱masiihu be̱ shi haku tari na shani ta̱ba ta̱ma ta̱ba e̱she̱ hiku. Be̱ shi hakuu naa zha̱a̱ buꞌa̱ naa fo, awyatu nde̱e̱be̱ aba shi haku aꞌa̱yo. Hyo̱ ya̱nu Uhwe̱n tanda wuun wana hyan ruzha̱a̱ rundaabwa rude̱be̱ ta̱shapaciga.
Iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱
Azumanu :1-2 Ala̱masiihu na̱ awyatu nde̱e̱be̱ :3--3:21 Hunranhunran na fo na̱ Ala̱masiihu :1--6:20Ta̱wanyan :21-24
Azumanu
Takaada na̱nna shi na báni kuga̱n Bulusu, butumashini naa Ala̱masiihu Yeesu kuta̱sha̱a̱ nata̱ Hwe̱n.
Zhagu kawyatu na Hwe̱n ana ne̱e̱ na̱ ce̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ Afisa, ana pa̱ni nꞌgata nꞌndaaba hiku ku-Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Ta̱pana ꞌye̱n na̱ hunranhunran na̱ nꞌta̱gumunu ku-Hwe̱n Ada nda̱tu na̱ Butu O̱to̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu xta̱naa huku na̱ ga̱hin.
Rubara̱ka naru Hwe̱n kuꞌnꞌhwaanwun nda̱a̱tu
xTa̱nya̱bi ma Hwe̱n una shi Ada na Butu O̱to̱ nda̱a̱tu Ala̱masiihu Yeesu. Bwa ta̱nndaaki rubara̱ka naru hyo̱ iri na zumaa ina báni nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱. Unje̱ kunnu na̱ wana ta̱maꞌunpa̱n ta̱nda̱a̱tu huku na̱ Ala̱masiihu.
Ta aba njiwo usa̱ra̱ri yana, utata̱nkasa ku-Ala̱masiihu, na hyan ta̱nshi ana ta̱sabu na za yaan randa kaꞌuba̱ ndaabwa. Wana ta̱ruba̱ ta̱ndaabwa,
Uhwe̱n tahoo ta̱nshapa ta̱nshi mꞌmwaan ndaabwa paaku tuma na Ala̱masiihu Yeesu. Hwe̱n bwa ribi unje̱ kunnu wana umacaanhini me̱.
xTa̱nya̱bi Hwe̱n na̱ wana iri na ta̱bure na bwa ta̱mpa̱ni ꞌye̱n, na báni kuu-Yoo bunaa bwa hura̱gi ta̱ruba̱.
Hwe̱n ta tata̱biha̱na̱ paaku mahiin nama Ala̱masiihu be̱ tawyashika, ta bwa ta̱mha̱mba̱ga̱ncin pinsan nda̱tu nii gata ndaabwa. Unje̱ kunnu na hyan ubisa̱a̱ ta̱pana ꞌye̱n ta̱ndaabwa ta̱yaburi.
-9 Uta̱mpa̱ni tuun nata̱ za haru huku na̱ nꞌta̱bita̱riga na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌinsan hyo̱. Ubwa shani ga̱tun yan ashe̱re̱ na ame̱ ndaabwa na iri na bwa shii ta̱nda ku-Ala̱masiihu. Unje̱ ya̱nu na hyan umacaanhini me̱.
Kubwa shii nii gata ta̱hyan kuha̱ni nje̱, unii wuna̱a̱na̱ iri hyo̱ ina ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ na̱ ina ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n kuta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Ala̱masiihu.
Na̱ wana ta̱maꞌunpa̱n ta̱nda̱a̱tu huku na̱ Ala̱masiihu, ta Hwe̱n bwa tata̱kasa ga̱tu shi ana ja̱a̱ hya̱su iri na bwa tanda ala̱ka̱wa̱ri. Hasaa bwa tahoo sha̱a̱ ya̱nu. Bwa nje̱ komba̱ri nꞌta̱sha̱a̱ ta̱ndaabwa.
Ta̱sha̱a̱ nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ta ta̱shi, ga̱tu Ayaahudiya, ga̱tu naa re̱ge̱ ta̱sha̱a̱ nꞌgata nꞌnda̱a̱tu ku-Ala̱masiihu xta̱ꞌwaan ta̱yaba na̱ nꞌta̱shapaciga ku-Hwe̱n.
Ga̱hin ana shici Ayaahudiya, ihoo ha̱nga taa mazama nama mahanda, mazama nama zumaa nama Hwe̱n bwaa biha̱ni ma. Too, ha̱ni na ga̱hin tapana nꞌgata niinhin ku-Ala̱masiihu, Hwe̱n taaꞌinsan ma ga̱hin shi ande̱e̱be̱, paaku bwa taapana ma Bihwaanwun ndaabwa, kubwa tahoo nda ala̱ka̱wa̱ri hasaa.
Be̱e̱ Hwaanwun ta tata̱bisa̱ ta̱hyan Uhwe̱n nii ta̱pana iri na bwa ta ta̱nndaaka ala̱ka̱wa̱ri nde̱e̱be̱ hiku na ga̱tu ja̱a̱ nꞌhya̱su. Ta shani ga̱tun yan ta̱hyan hina iyeebe Hwe̱n nii biha̱na̱ ana shi ndaabwa. Unje̱ kunnu hyo̱ wana hyan ta̱nya̱bi ta̱shapaciga ta̱ndaabwa.
Ro̱pe̱ na Bulusu wana ana pa̱ni nꞌgata ana Afisa
Na̱ wana kunnu, ta na ga̱n hange̱ mazama maniinhin haruwa na ga̱hin pa̱ni nꞌgata ku-Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu, na̱ haruwa na ga̱hin ribi awyatu na Hwe̱n hyo̱,
nꞌta ga̱a̱ci ta̱naa gooda̱ga̱ Hwe̱n na̱ wana ninhin. Hyo̱ uha̱ni na ga̱n nda ro̱pe̱, nꞌtaa ndaaka ma
ta̱hyan Uhwe̱n na Butu O̱to̱ nda̱a̱tu Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, Ada na hura̱gi ta̱shapaciga hyo̱, xuupa̱ni ma ta̱bita̱riga kii-Hwaanwun ndaabwa na̱ nꞌta̱duwa̱na̱ ta̱bisa̱ga̱ ma haruwa na hyan iduwa̱ni ta̱yansun wuun.
Ga̱n gura̱a̱ nda ro̱pe̱ ta̱hyan Uhwe̱n shani nꞌgata niinhin nꞌgunii iꞌe̱nshe̱n koo imbata shi ta̱sha̱a̱ bigata yata naa bwaa nꞌgani ma na̱ wana ta̱ba, igura̱a̱ yansun o̱to̱ na maca̱ma̱nta̱n nama iri na yaburi na awyatu ndaabwa ba ja̱a̱ hya̱su.
Ga̱n gura̱a̱ naa nda ro̱pe̱ ji ta̱hyan iyansun ikai na ta̱kai ta̱ndaabwa na hura̱ni ta̱yansun, na nii nda tuma na̱ nꞌga̱tu ana pa̱ni nꞌgata kuubwa. Ta̱kai ta̱yata nata̱ nii nda tuma na̱ nꞌga̱tu, ta̱ka̱ ta̱ba shi na̱ nꞌta̱kai
nata̱ tahiika̱hina̱ Ala̱masiihu kuta̱ꞌwa̱, ta̱ba gura̱a̱ pa buu paaku ta̱hunrana kukataga kandaabwa nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
Kaba ta Ala̱masiihu be̱ ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱gwama ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ kuhyo̱ ana ta̱gwama na̱ ana ha̱mba̱gi ta̱gwama na̱ ana ta̱kai na̱ ana ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ koo ta̱ya̱. Biꞌmꞌbaa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ nata̱ ne̱e̱ iyeebe na koo ta̱ya̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, shii kuna̱ ha̱ni yana, hyo̱ na̱ uha̱ni na ja̱a̱ wuce.
Uhwe̱n tashana komba̱ri ibe̱ pa̱ni hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱ ku-Ala̱masiihu, ubwa gura̱a̱ shaana buu be̱ shi hyuhyu na hyo̱ iri wana awyatu nde̱e̱be̱ hyo̱.
Awyatu nde̱e̱be̱ aba shi ta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ Ala̱masiihu. Kuꞌana pa̱ni nꞌgata ta be̱ shi naa ciga̱hini komba̱ri ki, haruwa na be̱e̱ be̱ shi ta̱ciga̱hina̱ nata̱ komba̱ri kope.

Ta̱gaa ta̱ꞌwa̱ zhagu ta̱nda bina̱
Na̱ ayigo itasha haka awyatu na ꞌwa̱gi na̱ wana ijwarigici Hwe̱n ma ndaga pinsan.
Na̱ ha̱ni ya̱nu ita jwara̱ga ayo̱n na sa̱ra̱ri yana, na̱a̱ gwama naa shi upyara yata Bupira̱, bunaa shi bihwaanwun yata naa uwa̱ naa tanaa hurupa̱ga̱na̱ ce̱be̱ na ana ga̱a̱ ta̱jwara̱ga Hwe̱n.
Hyo̱ nda̱tu kunnu ga̱tu tansha na̱ ayigo, ta̱tanaa nda iri kina shi ina ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ba ribi, na̱ ina bigata nda̱a̱tu na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ba hin ta̱nnje̱. Na̱ kunnu kuꞌahari nda̱tu na butu wuma, ushi na hyan ame̱ ta̱gura na Hwe̱n tacíin wa̱tu haruwa na aba nii cíin kukoo buya̱.
Ama Uhwe̱n bwa shi naa za mꞌpirwa na̱ ambishiri. Ta̱ruba̱ ta̱ndaabwa kunga̱tu ta̱ba yaburi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱,
bwa tata̱mpana bina̱ na mahwa huku na̱ Ala̱masiihu, koo na ga̱tu tansha ana ꞌwa̱gi na̱ wana pinsan nda̱tu. Kuta̱pana ꞌye̱n nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ta ubwa taabiha̱na̱ ma.
Utata̱hiika̱hina̱ huku na̱ Ala̱masiihu kuta̱ꞌwa̱, bwa ta̱mpa̱ paaka hunranhunran da̱nda̱ nii be̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, wana ta̱maꞌunpa̱n ta̱nda̱a̱tu nii be̱.
Uhwe̱n tanda kunnu wana hyan uha̱ni na wuci xubisa̱a̱ ta̱pana ꞌye̱n ta̱ndaabwa nata̱ za mꞌpirwa na̱ o̱to̱. Ta̱ba ta̱pana ꞌye̱n utata̱mbisa̱a̱ tuun paaku Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Ai, kuta̱pana ꞌye̱n nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ta bwa taabiha̱na̱ ma, na ga̱hin ta panaa gata ku-Ala̱masiihu. Ya̱nu ubwa shici wana yaan ri na ga̱hin nje̱ ta, ta̱pana nata̱ iri na gama nata̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ta.
Ubwa shici funa̱ na tuma ninhin na bina̱ ta, ta̱hyan xbuyaan buta nda ruwashi na̱ be̱.
Ga̱tun nꞌsuhyu sunda̱a̱tu ta̱nshi tuma na Hwe̱n ta. Ubwa gura̱a̱ ta̱mmantan ku-Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, na hyan ta̱nnje̱ tuma na bina̱ una bwa tahoo ta̱nsha̱a̱ga̱ hasaa ta̱naa nda.
Ala̱masiihu shii awyatu bigwaga ka̱
Wana kunnu, ga̱hin ana shici Ayaahudiya kuta̱ma̱ncin, mata̱ma̱nriin ma kuga̱hin tanaa na̱ ayigo. Ana nii maꞌnꞌga, <<ana ꞌya̱pa̱gi ta̱wya̱ri>> atanaa sa̱ maa nꞌga ma <<ana ꞌya̱pa̱gici ta̱wya̱ri>>. Ta̱ba ta̱ꞌyapa ta̱wya̱ri ta̱shi huwa̱ iri na awyatu aba ta ndaaka ta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ awyatu.
Mata̱ma̱nriin ma ta̱hyan na̱ bwa ha̱ni itazaagwa da̱nda̱ na̱ Ala̱masiihu. Ga̱hin tashici awyatu na ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ naa gudu naa Isiraaꞌila. Ga̱hin taza ta̱taa na̱ ala̱ka̱wa̱ri na Hwe̱n bwa tamasha̱a̱ga̱ na̱ aba. Itanaa na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana na zaa gata ta̱sha̱a̱, ga̱hin taza huku na̱ Hwe̱n.
Ga̱hin naa tanaa sa̱ inaa tutu, niina na̱ ta̱maꞌunpa̱n nata̱ ga̱hin ma unpin na̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, wana mahiin nama be̱ tawyashika ta ga̱hin de̱be̱ ta̱wuta̱ do̱ko̱ na̱ bwa.
Ala̱masiihu na̱ hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱ ta shi hunranhunran na ta̱gumunu kunga̱tu. Paa be̱ tawa̱ta̱ku ana shi Ayaahudiya na̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya aba shi bigwaga ka̱, be̱ gura̱a̱ huza̱ ubuga̱ na tata̱nhoosa̱ na̱ aba.
Bitaꞌaragana ta̱kuna ta̱suuga̱ ta̱yata, nata̱ mꞌba Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa na nꞌtashana ta̱nda ri ga̱ga̱ga̱, paa be̱ tapana ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱nde̱e̱be̱. Bitaꞌwaan hunranhunran na ta̱gumunu kuꞌana shi Ayaahudiya aba maꞌunso̱n na̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya. Be̱ shani awyatu ree aba shi bigwaga ka̱ na hyan ashi bigwaga ka̱ nii be̱.
Bitanda kunnu wana hyan biꞌa̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni aba reeko ya̱nu na̱ Hwe̱n, paaku ta̱ꞌwa̱ ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ na̱ guguji. Be̱ kwane̱ ta̱maribici nata̱ tanaa kunga̱tu.
Bitaꞌwaan mazama nama zumaa nama hunranhunran na ta̱gumunu kuga̱hin ana shici Ayaahudiya ana tanaa tutu na̱ Hwe̱n, na̱ hunranhunran na ta̱gumunu yata ku-Ayaahudiya ana tanaa do̱ko̱ na̱ bwa.
Kii-Hwaanwun ndaabwa ka̱ yata ta, hyo̱ nda̱tu ga̱tun ara ta̱jaga paaku Hwe̱n Ada wana Ala̱masiihu.
Too, kuga̱hin ana shici Ayaahudiya, igura̱a̱cii sha agai, ga̱hin jaa hyan iza paa kuta̱naa. Ishi awyatu na ina ka̱ da̱nda̱ na̱ awyatu na Hwe̱n. Mahanda ga̱hin shi awyatu na Hwe̱n.
Ataciba̱ ina na̱nna kuta̱ma nata̱ atumashini na̱ nata̱ acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama. Ala̱masiihu Yeesu na̱ hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱ ta shi utari na hura̱gi bina̱ hyo̱ kuta̱ba ta̱ma.
Be̱ taa shani ina na̱nna ibe̱ mayibaku da̱nda̱, ibe̱e̱ maduwa̱na̱ ta̱mawaana, ibe̱ shi ina na ta̱sabu paaku ta̱naa paga Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n hunrun.
Na̱ wana ta̱maꞌunpa̱n ta̱niinhin nii be̱ ta abaa ma̱ ma yibaku na̱ ayaan na hyan ishi ina paa Hwe̱n bwa hunrani kii-Hwaanwun ndaabwa.

Utuma na Bulusu bwa tandaaka ana shici Ayaahudiya
Na̱ wana kunnu, iindaaki ma ro̱pe̱ ku-Hwe̱n, ga̱n Bulusu bunaa bwake̱ na̱ wana Ala̱masiihu Yeesu mꞌpa̱ni tuma maa ndaaka ma ana shici Ayaahudiya.
Nꞌshii nii gata hiku ihange̱ utuma na ta̱pana ꞌye̱n na Hwe̱n bwa mꞌpa̱ni maa bisa̱ga̱ ma.
Kuga̱n tahoo taga washi na̱ ayigo ta̱hyan, Hwe̱n mꞌbisa̱a̱ ashe̱re̱ na iri na bwa ribi ta̱nda, ta ubwa shani ga̱n yan wyan.
Kiicita̱gi ta̱ꞌyantan ta̱na̱nna nata̱ ga̱n ta̱gi, inii ara ta̱ꞌinsan iri na ga̱n yan kuꞌashe̱re̱ ana ne̱e̱ ku-Ala̱masiihu.
Hasaa Hwe̱n tabisa̱a̱ci ashe̱re̱ na̱nna na ame̱ ndaabwa kawyatu, ama niina ta Uhwe̱n bwa ba̱nriin wyan, kuꞌatumashini na̱ acita̱a̱ga̱ wuun mazama ana ne̱e̱ sabu paakii Hwaanwun ndaabwa.
Iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ ndaabwa ta shi, paaku mazama nama zumaa, ana shici Ayaahudiya anii hya̱su rubara̱ka naru Hwe̱n nge̱n na̱ Ayaahudiya. Ashi awyatu na ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ka̱ hyo̱, aba gura̱a̱ mꞌbaa ta̱taa ta̱ndaaba na̱ ala̱ka̱wa̱ri na Hwe̱n bwa tandaaka wyan ku-Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Nꞌshi bugyama naa mazama mana̱nna nama zumaa kuta̱pana ꞌye̱n nata̱ Hwe̱n bwa mꞌpa̱ni ga̱mi kuta̱kai ta̱ndaabwa.
Koo na ga̱n shi bunaa hura̱gi ta̱ge̱ kawyatu na Hwe̱n, hyo̱ na̱ kunnu ta Uhwe̱n bwa mꞌpa̱ni ta̱yansun nata̱ hura̱gi bina̱ nata̱ ta̱naa bisa̱ga̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya mazama nama hyo̱ iri na zumaa na Ala̱masiihu, na za haru na ta̱ga̱gaagana.
Bwa nꞌka̱shi wana hyan ma gura̱a̱ bisa̱ga̱ koo buya̱ ushiri na ashe̱re̱ naa gata ndaabwa. Hwe̱n na nje̱ komba̱ri ta tasha̱a̱ wuun hasaa ta na̱ nꞌta̱pasa nata̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana.
Niina ta̱sha̱a̱ ta̱ndaabwa ta̱ta ta̱shi, xanje̱ tuma na̱ awyatu na Yeesu abisa̱gi ta̱bita̱riga nata̱ Hwe̱n kuta̱ba ne̱e̱ goo goo, kana ta̱gwama na̱ nꞌta̱kai ana ne̱e̱ da̱da̱da̱.
Uya̱nu nje̱ nꞌta̱sha̱a̱ bigata naa Hwe̱n bwa tahoo sha̱a̱ hasaa, utanda wuun paaku Butu O̱to̱ nda̱a̱tu Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Na̱ wana Ala̱masiihu na̱ nꞌta̱panaa gata nda̱a̱tu nii be̱ ta ga̱tun ara ta̱jaga paa Hwe̱n bigata ka̱ na̱ nꞌta̱naa fo̱n.
Wana kunnu iiro̱pe̱ ma kusu ta̱hyan ta-yaaciga maa gata na̱ wana ngwan na ga̱n swa wana ninhin, una nii sha ta̱shapaciga ta̱niinhin.
Uro̱pe̱ kuꞌawyatu na Afisa
Na̱ wana kunnu sa̱i ga̱n she̱nshe̱n, ga̱n nje̱ ro̱pe̱ ku-Hwe̱n Ada nda̱tu
bunaa shi naa shii hyo̱ nꞌgudu na nꞌawyatu na ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n na̱ ana ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
Nꞌne̱e̱ na̱ ro̱pe̱ ta̱hyan xuupa̱ ma ta̱yansun paaku ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ nata̱ ta̱shapaciga ta̱ndaabwa, xuuta̱ maa shita̱ nꞌta̱kai ta̱ndaabwa, wana hyan iꞌa̱ri ta̱ꞌisa ki na̱ nꞌgata niinhin kii-Hwaanwun ndaabwa.
Nꞌne̱e̱ na̱ ro̱pe̱ ya̱nu na hyan Ala̱masiihu hunrana na̱ nꞌgata nꞌniinhin haruwa na ga̱hin pa̱ni nꞌgata nii be̱. Ga̱n gura̱a̱ nda ro̱pe̱ ta̱hyan xta̱ruba̱ ta̱niinhin ta̱shi haka nga̱nga̱nda̱ na cibi hiku na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n haku ta̱ma nata̱ aba cibi hiku,
wana hyan ga̱hin na̱ hyo̱ awyatu na Hwe̱n iꞌmꞌbaa ta̱kai nata̱ ta̱ꞌinsan kumahaan na̱ ngiswan na̱ mꞌmame̱ma na̱ maꞌira̱ na ta̱ruba̱ nata̱ Ala̱masiihu be̱ ta̱nribi kuta̱ba ne̱e̱.
Igura̱a̱ yansun ta̱ruba̱ ta̱na̱nna nata̱ hura̱ni ta̱yansun hyo̱, wana hyan iꞌmꞌbaa ahari ana ne̱e̱ to̱n ana Hwe̱n.
Ta̱shapaciga xta̱naa na̱ Hwe̱n nda̱tu! Bwa ta mꞌbaa ta̱kai nata̱ ta̱nda tuma kunga̱tu na huri hyo̱ ina ga̱tu ro̱pe̱, koo ina ga̱tu makicihinaa na̱ ame̱ nda̱tu.
Ta̱shapaciga xta̱naa waabwa kiri na bwa nje̱ kawyatu na Yeesu na̱ iri na bwa nje̱ ku-Ala̱masiihu hyo̱ koya̱ ha̱ni niina na̱ mꞌmahwa mꞌmahwa! xMashi kunnu.

Ta̱maꞌunpa̱n nꞌta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu
Na̱ wana kunnu, ga̱n butu naa bwake̱ na̱ zhaaro wana Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu, nꞌna̱maa rupa ma, nda ma hunranhunran una magii nꞌta̱ꞌnꞌgana ta̱yata nata̱ Uhwe̱n bwaa nꞌgani ma.
Sha ma ana za hyuhyu ta̱shapaciga, ishi ana maꞌye̱e̱ shukuu na̱ akuri, ishi ana tanaa mahakataga buyaan bubwa wa̱jiga̱a̱ na̱ wana ta̱ruba̱ nata̱ ga̱hin maribi.
Maka̱nta̱ni ma na hyan iꞌa̱ri ta̱nda hunranhunran yata naa unpin ma, haruwa na Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱e̱ pa̱ni ma, paaku hunranhunran na ta̱gumunu naa shii ma da̱nda̱.
Ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ka̱ ga̱tu shi, Bihwaanwun ka̱ ga̱tu mꞌbaa. Kunnu taa ta̱sha̱a̱ bigata ka̱ yata ta̱ba ne̱e̱ nata̱ Hwe̱n bwaa nꞌgani ma wana ta̱ba.
Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu ka̱ ga̱tu mꞌbaa, ta̱jwara̱ga ta̱ka̱ ga̱tu jwarigi, baba̱tiisa̱ma ka̱ ne̱e̱.
Uhwe̱n ka̱ ne̱e̱, na shi Ashin na koo buya̱. Bwa taa shi naa ne̱e̱ da̱da̱da̱ na wyatu hyo̱, bwaa nda tuma ndaabwa kawyatu hyo̱, bwa ne̱e̱ na̱ awyatu hyo̱.
Hyo̱ nda̱tu koo buya̱ butaraa ta̱pana ꞌye̱n goo goo haruwa na Ala̱masiihu be̱ hoosa̱ga̱gi tuun.
Ta shani takaada na Hwe̱n bwa hin,
<<Ha̱ni na be̱ takatana da̱da̱da̱
be̱ sha̱pi ana ba kota̱ga̱ni, aba huri huku nii be̱,
be̱ gura̱a̱ pana ta̱pana ꞌye̱n goo goo kawyatu.>>
Iba̱ aba ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan, <<Be̱ takatana>>? Ubisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan na̱ ayigo bitacíin ta kunrin na sa̱ra̱ri yana.
Be̱e̱ naa tacíin na̱ ayigo, be̱ taa shi naa takatana da̱da̱da̱ na hyan biciga̱hini nꞌce̱nye̱n ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ hyo̱.
Be̱ taa shi naa tapagana ta̱yansun kawyatu nde̱e̱be̱, aka̱ atumashini, aka̱ acita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, aka̱ ana nii ndaga mazama nama zumaa, aka̱ aꞌiyo̱ na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi na nꞌana pa̱ni nꞌgata.
Tuma ndaaba tashi na hyan awyatu na Hwe̱n aꞌa̱ri ta̱ndaaka bwa tuma na hyan aꞌa̱ri ta̱ma ta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ Ala̱masiihu.
Na̱ kunnu ta ga̱tu nii maꞌunpa̱n nꞌta̱jwara̱ga Hwe̱n na̱ nꞌta̱yansun Buyoo bundaabwa, ta̱shi awyatu ana mahumuni suhyu sundaaba hiku na̱ nꞌta̱jwara̱ga wuun. Na̱ kunnu ta ga̱tu nii nꞌsha ana wuciha̱ni ta̱ciga̱hina̱ na̱ta̱ Ala̱masiihu.
Ta̱jaa nꞌsha haku mꞌmwaan ana abaa kicihinaa suha̱nka̱ri sundaaba, mꞌpyara na nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana mꞌbaa shapaga aha̱nka̱ri ndaaba. Awyatu na maka̱ri na̱ mꞌmahunre̱n baa kicihinaa wyan ma pira̱ga̱ wyan.
Na̱ kunnu kuta̱cici mahanda na̱ nꞌta̱ruba̱, sa̱i ta̱mawaani na̱ komba̱ri nda̱tu, ta̱nwuciha̱ni haku Ala̱masiihu na shi hyuhyu na ta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ awyatu nde̱e̱be̱.
Be̱ taa shi naa ha̱mba̱gi hyo̱ nꞌun na nꞌta̱ꞌwaba, ta̱ba makota̱ni ta̱ba maha̱mba̱gi paa kutuma nata̱a̱ koo biya̱a̱ nii. Paaku tuma na koya̱a̱ un naa ta̱to̱n, ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱baa mawaana, ta̱baa mama na̱ ahari na ta̱maruba̱.
Jabagu na fo nꞌta̱maꞌunpa̱n na̱ Ala̱masiihu
Too, na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌo̱to̱ nata̱ Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, ga̱n na̱maa koota̱ga̱ ma ta̱hyan, ta-nda ma hunranhunran haku na awyatu ana yancin Hwe̱n, ana tanaa makicihinaa nii gata na̱ iri na za hyuhyu.
Ame̱ ndaaba cigi da̱ na̱ nꞌta̱yincincin. Ahooshi wyan na̱ bina̱ ta̱nda na Hwe̱n bwaa pagana, wana ta̱yincincin nata̱ aba mꞌbaa na̱ nꞌta̱ta̱bici mazama.
Aba zaga nꞌkogi, apa̱ni suhyu sundaaba paaku ta̱naa nda banshaun na̱ ta̱ruba̱ nata̱ ta̱naa ndaga iri na mꞌbaa daba. Aba ribici ta̱gaa wuun.
Una̱nna ushici ujabagu una abaa ga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni ma na Ala̱masiihu.
Tana ta̱hyan ihange̱ mazama nama Yeesu, aba gura̱a̱ maa ga̱gaagana ma mazama nama mahanda nama báni waabe̱,
munsan ma suhari nata̱ zumaancin nata̱ ga̱hin taꞌmꞌbaaga hasaa, ta̱ruba̱ nata̱ iri ma̱ na̱ apira̱ na ta kuha̱na̱ suhari suya̱nu.
Uhuri gama Uhwe̱n he̱re̱ge̱ nꞌgata nꞌniinhin na̱ nꞌsuhari suniinhin.
Shapa ma suhari suyata nasu fo nasu Hwe̱n bwa taanda ma na̱ mꞌpirwa nꞌndaabwa, Ubwa shi naa bina̱ bwa ne̱e̱ sabu.
Na̱ wana kunnu, koo buya̱ xbuga̱a̱ sa̱ ta̱naa cita̱ga̱ ta̱be̱, bubishi sa̱ buya̱na̱ iri na shi mahanda na̱ wana hyo̱ nda̱tu ta̱nshi nꞌun na nꞌta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ka̱.
<<Kiine̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ ta̱gura, xutaa shana ma pinsan ta̱nda.>> xAme̱ ta̱gura ninhin taa iya ma kiike̱nye̱n naa hwe̱n ta̱ꞌira̱,
na ta̱hyan ame̱ ta̱gura ta pa Bupira̱ ha̱ba̱.
Kuu-shi buzumba̱, sa̱i u-ga̱a̱ ta̱naa ndaga zumba̱. Na̱ kunnu sa̱i u-naa nda tuma na bina̱ na̱ nꞌara ndaabi na na̱maa pa iri na shi ndaa na mahanda, na hyan kuu-de̱be̱ u-gwatani ana za iri na nꞌara ndaaba.
Ta-gaa ma mahwa mazama nama uwa̱ manaa bánai na̱ nu ninhin, sa̱i kumazama nama bina̱ nama hyan maduwa̱ni ana shiragi muu bishita̱ ta̱ta kuꞌiri na aba ribi na bina̱.
Ta-ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ ma Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n bigata na̱ jabagu ninhin. Wana bibe̱ taa taaꞌinsan ma ga̱hin shi ande̱e̱be̱, bishaani Hwe̱n biha̱ni ma na̱ uhwe̱n na ta̱biha̱na̱.
Mahooshi ma na̱ koya̱ iri na nꞌgata na nꞌshiri, na̱ ame̱ ta̱gura, na̱ nꞌgata mamboo, na̱ gagu, na̱ nꞌta̱cwaa, na̱ koya̱ iri ina shi na we̱.
Na̱ kunnu sa̱i ximandaakaki iri na bina̱, iꞌmꞌbaa ambishiri, iga̱a̱ ta̱naa maha̱mba̱a̱ga̱na̱ pinsan, haruwa na Hwe̱n bwa taaha̱mba̱ga̱ncin ma pinsan nii gata ndaabwa na̱ wana Ala̱masiihu.

Hunranhunran na̱ nꞌta̱gwaan
Tana ta̱hyan ishi mꞌmwaan na n-Hwe̱n bwa hura̱gi ta̱ruba̱, shapa ma ahari ndaabwa na̱ hunranhunran ninhin.
xUjabagu ninhin naa hura̱ huku nꞌta̱ruba̱, haruwa na Ala̱masiihu be̱ ta̱nribi. Be̱ pa̱ni hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱ wana nꞌga̱tu, haku bikico̱ na aba pa̱ni xashe̱nre̱n ina mꞌbaa nꞌshima na nꞌzumaa ku-Hwe̱n.
Ta-haashiga ma iyaan ri na banshaun koo na̱ yaan ri na shi na daba koo nꞌta̱maa ta̱ruba̱ iri ma̱. Uya̱nu magiici mahwa kawyatu na Hwe̱n.
Uzumaancin na hyan inaa nda mazama nama uwa̱ koo ta̱naa cita̱ga̱ iri na nꞌkogi koo umuntun na uwa̱, na̱ nꞌta̱naa nda iri ya̱nu uhuri gama inaa sa̱ gooda̱ga̱ Hwe̱n.
Yansun ma ta̱hyan bunaa nii nda banshaun koo ri na shi na daba koo nꞌta̱maa ta̱ruba̱ iri ma̱, buyata buza iri na bwaa hya̱su kuta̱gwama nata̱ Ala̱masiihu nata̱ shi nata̱ Hwe̱n. Buyata bune̱e̱ nge̱n na̱a̱ naa nii paga iri na shici Hwe̱n hunrun.
Ta-hakata ma ayaan piri ma na̱ mꞌmazama mandaaba nama uwa̱, na̱ wana Hwe̱n ja̱a̱ pa ana ga̱a̱ ta̱jwara̱ga wuun ngwan.
Ta-mayibaku ma na̱ aba.
Na̱ ayigo, itaciga̱ da̱ na̱ nꞌta̱yincincin, ama niina ishi ana ta̱gwaan ku-Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu. Na̱ wana kunnu, nda ma hunranhunran na awyatu na ta̱gwaan.
Ta̱gwaan ta̱ta ta̱shi nata̱ ta mantan ahari na zumaa na̱ iri na ne̱e̱ to̱n na̱ ina shi mahanda.
Iya ma shukuu iwya̱nzhin ina nii caanhina Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n me̱.
Ta-mayibaku ma inaa nda iri na we̱ na ta̱yincincin na wyatu baa nda, na̱ kunnu sa̱i iba̱nriin ubwa tuma kuta̱gwaan.
Ushi iri na nꞌkogi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ta̱cita̱ iri na ana jwarigici Hwe̱n abaa nda ta̱swee.
Ha̱ni na aba ba̱nriin iri ya̱nu na̱ nꞌta̱gwaan, koo buya̱ nii ndaya wuun ki,
wana ta̱hyan ina ta̱gwaan ta shi na tabisa̱a̱ komba̱ri ki. Ta shani aba hin,
<<Zhimba, gaa naa ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌrabi,
u-hiiki kuta̱ꞌwa̱,
Ala̱masiihu na̱maa tára̱kaaki ta̱gwaan.>>
Hunranhunran na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱a̱ Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n
Nda ma aha̱nka̱ri na̱ hunranhunran ninhin. Ta-hunrana ma haku nꞌguzha̱ni ama haku ana be̱te̱re̱ge̱.
Nda ma tuma hiku na̱ koya̱ ha̱ba̱ na ga̱hin de̱be̱, wana ta̱hyan nꞌhwe̱n na nꞌta̱we̱ nꞌna.
Wana kunnu ta-naa nda ma iri ma̱ na za hyuhyu, ama insan ma kwan ta̱sha̱a̱ nata̱ Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu kuta̱ba shi.
Ta-maa ma ta̱swa nata̱ ma̱ni nama iinabi, na na̱maa kuha̱na̱ ma jabagu ninhin. Na̱ nꞌta̱naa nda kunnu hakata ma Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n naawan na̱ ga̱hin hiku.
Naa nda ma koya̱ iri na zha̱a̱ na ta̱yaba Hwe̱n na̱ aya̱na̱nhin. Naa nda ma zha̱a̱ na̱ imi nii gata niinhin hyo̱ ku-Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu.
Gooda̱ sa̱ ma Ada Hwe̱n na̱ hyo̱ komba̱ri, na̱ wana Butu O̱to̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Hunranhunran na aꞌa̱ nꞌsuwya̱rugooba
Pana ma suhyu suniinhin imajwara̱ga wana ipa̱ Ala̱masiihu zha̱munkun ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Ga̱hin aꞌa̱ na ta̱wya̱ri, pana ma suhyu suniinhin kusuwya̱rugoohin haruwa na ga̱hin ta pana hyuhyu ninhin ku-Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu.
Na ta̱hyan butu wya̱ri taa shi hyuhyu na aꞌa̱yo haruwa na Ala̱masiihu be̱ shi hyuhyu na awyatu nde̱e̱be̱. Be̱ taa shi naa biha̱ni awyatu ana shi ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱nde̱e̱be̱.
Haruwa na awyatu nde̱e̱be̱ aba pa̱ni suhyu sundaaba ku-Ala̱masiihu, kunta taa aꞌa̱ na ta̱wya̱ri xapa̱ni suhyu sundaaba kusuwya̱rugooba na̱ hyo̱ komba̱ri.
Ga̱hin suwya̱rugoo, ruba̱ ma aꞌa̱ ninhin haruwa na Ala̱masiihu be̱ ribi awyatu nde̱e̱be̱. Be̱ pa̱ni hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱, be̱ ꞌwi wana ndaaba,
wana hyan anaa sabu ku-Hwe̱n paaku ta̱ha̱mbara wyan na̱ ma̱ni kumazama nama Hwe̱n.
Bitanda kunnu wana hyan, ha̱ni na be̱e̱ mashaapa awyatu nde̱e̱be̱ waabe̱ hakuu a̱a̱ naa fo azumaa ta̱gwataga, aba jaa mꞌbaa ta̱yaan ta̱shiri ama anaa sabu na za randa.
Kunnu taa, xubutu wya̱ri buribi aꞌa̱yo haruwa na bwa ribi ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabwa, wana ta̱hyan butu naa ribi aꞌa̱yo, hyuhyu ndaabwa ta bwa ribi.
Wana buza naa ta gaa ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabwa, sa̱i bupa̱ tuun shami, bugwataga tuun ki haku Ala̱masiihu be̱ ta gwataga awyatu nde̱e̱be̱.
Nꞌga̱tun ta ta̱nshi ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱nde̱e̱be̱.
Kutakaada na Hwe̱n bwa hin, <<Na̱ wana kunnu, butu nii gaa ashin na̱ aya̱na̱, bumaꞌa̱npa̱nta̱ni na̱ aꞌa̱yo, aba reeko ashiiri ka̱.>>
Una̱nna ta shi ashe̱re̱ nama ira̱, ga̱n ga̱n ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan haruwa na Ala̱masiihu na̱ awyatu nde̱e̱be̱ aba shi ri ka̱.
Ta ga̱n gura̱a̱ hyan xubutu wya̱ri ribi aꞌa̱yo haruwa na bwa ribi hyuhyu ndaabwa, buꞌa̱ xbucina̱ni awya̱rugo.

Mꞌmwaan na̱ ana ma̱nta̱in wyan
Ga̱hin mꞌmwaan, jwara̱ga ma mazama nama anaa ma̱ncin ma wana ga̱hin shi ana Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu, uya̱nu tashi to̱n na hyan inje̱.
Gira̱nshin naa yigo naa pa̱ni na̱ ala̱ka̱wa̱ri be̱ taa shi, <<Cina̱na̱ abaaba ndaa na̱ ada̱a̱da̱ ndaa.>>
Kiicina̱ni abaaba na̱ ada̱a̱da̱ ninhin, <<Iri nii namaa hura̱a̱ga̱ ma to̱n, ga̱hin hura̱ ta̱taa ke̱nye̱n na̱ sa̱ra̱ri.>>
Ga̱hin sushoo, ta-naa ndaaka ma mꞌmwaan niinhin gagu na ta̱ꞌye̱n, na hyan nꞌnaa fuka nꞌgata. Na̱ kunnu naa ga̱gaagana ma muu inaa basa muu una báni ku-Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu, mꞌmawaani na̱ bwa.
Agyama na̱ awyatu na ina ndaaba
Ga̱hin agyama, koo buya̱ xbujwara̱ga mazama nama butu ndaabwa naa ina naa sa̱ra̱ri yana na̱ nꞌta̱cina̱na̱ nꞌrukwanyan. Inaa ndaaka wyan tuma bigata ka̱, haku Ala̱masiihu ga̱hin ndaaka.
Ma sukutaa ma na̱ tuma na hyan icaanhini wyan me̱, xuta sha kuha̱ni na abaa gwatagi ma na hyan aaya̱ba̱ni ma. Nda ma iri na Hwe̱n bwa ribi, haka agyama na Ala̱masiihu.
Nda ma tuma ninhin na̱ ame̱ hoo, hakuu naa nii ndaaka Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu tuma, shici awyatu wuma.
Mata̱ma̱nriin ma ta̱hyan bija̱a̱ funa̱ koo buya̱, bunaa shii gyama na̱a̱ naa shici bugyama, kutuma ndaabwa na gama na bwa nje̱.
Ga̱hin taa awyatu na ina na hya̱ agyama, inje̱ taa kunnu iri ka̱. Ta-hyan ma inii naa pa wyan ngwan, imata̱ma̱nriin ta̱hyan ga̱hin na̱ aba iꞌmꞌbaa Butu O̱to̱ ka̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, bwa a̱cii naa bisa̱a̱ga̱ ta̱hura̱.
ꞌWaa na gyasa ina Hwe̱n
Mazama nama ta̱wanyan, xmaaduwa̱ni ma ta̱mataa shita̱ ku-Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n na̱ wana kai na ta̱kai ta̱ndaabwa.
Bwatana ma hyo̱ iꞌwaa na gyasa na nii yansan aagumahini ma ina Hwe̱n bwaa pa̱ni ma, wana hyan iꞌa̱ri ta̱ꞌisa hiku, iga̱a̱ maka̱ri namaa Pira̱.
Ta̱jaa nꞌnda gagu na̱ awyatu wuma haku ga̱tu, ama ta̱nii nda gagu na̱ ana ha̱mba̱gi ta̱gwama na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ we̱, na̱ nꞌgwama na nꞌo̱to̱ na nꞌsa̱ra̱ri yana na ta̱yincincin, na̱ nꞌgudu nami nꞌhwaanwun na we̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
Na̱ wana kunnu, bwatana ma hyo̱ koya̱ ꞌwaa na gyasa na Hwe̱n, wana hyan ijaa a̱ri ta̱ꞌisa hiku na̱ ha̱ni na wuci na we̱. Jaa kuhuri, anda̱i ga̱hin taa ta e̱she̱ ji hiku.
Isa ma hiku na̱ kai, xmahanda mashi ukapa ninhin na ga̱hin ta̱ na̱ ambi hiku, ta̱naa nda ri to̱n xta̱shi da̱bi ninhin na ta̱ruma na gyasa.
Ushiri na ta̱ꞌiya mazama nama zumaa nama hunranhunran na ta̱gumunu na̱ Hwe̱n xushi kandaga na mꞌbuna nꞌniinhin.
Hyo̱ maya̱nu, ta̱panaa gata xta̱shi kwashe̱ na nii ꞌwa̱ga̱hina̱ aꞌira na ra na bunaa we̱.
Huuta̱na̱ ma tagiya na ta̱ruma na shi ta̱biha̱na̱, isha̱pi bisa̱nka̱ri bina Biihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱e̱ pa̱ni ma naa shi mazama mandaabwa.
Naa nda ma ro̱pe̱ koya̱ ha̱ni haruwa na Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱e̱ hin ma, inaa ndaga ro̱pe̱ na hyo̱ iri na ga̱hin shii nii gata niinhin. Inaa nda ji, ta-rukuta̱ ma, hyo̱ ha̱ni na ga̱hin ndaaka hyo̱ awyatu na Hwe̱n ro̱pe̱.
Ga̱n taa, nꞌndaaki ma ro̱pe̱, na hyan Hwe̱n mꞌpa̱ ta̱yansun nata̱ hyo̱ ha̱ni na ga̱n nda mazama rukwanyan ruba jaa naa, ma ara ta̱bisa̱ga̱ awyatu ashe̱re̱ yata na mazama nama zumaa.
Na̱ wana mazama mana̱nna ta ga̱n shi butuma, koo na ga̱n zwagani na̱ zhaaro. Nꞌndaaki ma ro̱pe̱ na hyan ma ara ta̱bisa̱ga̱ awyatu mazama haruwa na shi ma cita̱ga̱ muu, rukwanyan ruba jaa naa. A soldier with armour|hk00194c.tif|col|EPH 6:13-17||Sooja na̱ ꞌwaa na gyasa|6:13Ta̱makwaakaa azumanu
Tikikusu, buya̱tu naa ga̱n ribi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, bunaa tanaa ndaaka Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu tuma nii gata ka̱, buna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma komba̱ri na hyan iyansun kuga̱n ne̱e̱, na̱ mbata ga̱n nda.
Nꞌkáji bwa ta wunhin na hyan iyansun kuga̱tu ne̱e̱, bugura̱a̱ maa duwa̱na̱ ma bishita̱ ta̱ta.
Hunranhunran gumunu na̱ nꞌta̱ruba̱ na̱ nꞌta̱panaa gata nata̱ Hwe̱n Ada nda̱tu na̱ Butu O̱to̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, xta̱naa hyo̱ kuꞌana pa̱ni nꞌgata.
Ta̱pana ꞌye̱n nata̱ Hwe̱n xta̱naa huku na̱ hyo̱ bunaa ribi Butu O̱to̱ nda̱a̱tu Ala̱masiihu Yeesu mꞌmahwa.
PHP - Pangu
Afilibi
Afil
Afilibi
Takaada na Bulusu bwa ta̱gi zhagu Afilibi
Takaada na Bulusu bwa ta̱gi zhagu kawyatu na
Filibi
Iri na ta̱yansun na yigo
Bulusu butumashini naa Yeesu taa tataga takaada na̱nna zhagu kuꞌawyatu na pa̱ni nꞌgata ana yigo na bwa taciba̱ na̱ ce̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ Filibi na̱ Makidooniya kuta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Arooma. Butataga takaada na̱nna ha̱ni na bwa tazwagana na̱ zhaaro na̱ ce̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ Rooma. Butataga wuun na hyan buꞌa̱sa̱ga̱ni ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ aba tanaa nda na̱ Filibi, nata̱ ta̱hyan sa̱i kubutu jwarigi Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa, naazhin bwaa da̱ba ta̱nda bina̱ na mahwa.
Butataga takaada na̱nna wana hyan bugura̱a̱ gooda̱ awyatu na Yeesu na Filibi, na aba kádaagi bwa iꞌwaa ha̱ni na bwa ne̱e̱ na̱ ngwan. Butanda tuma na̱ bwa ha̱ni na hyan bubishi wyan xaduwa̱nii shita̱, ashii bigata hiku, hyo̱ na̱ ngwan ndaabwa na̱ ndaaba. Butanda mazama na̱ bwa takaada paa bwa tahyan hana kuꞌana nii nda mazama nama zumaa aba mayibakuci na̱a̱ bwa. Buta rupa wyan ta̱hyan xahunrana fo̱n anje̱ uhunranhunran na Yeesu be̱ tanda, bwa gura̱a̱ tamanrinyaan wyan ta̱hyan ta̱maꞌunpa̱n na̱ Ala̱masiihu ta̱shi ta̱kasa nata̱ Hwe̱n shii wana ta̱jwara̱ga Nꞌgira̱nshin na Ayaahudiya. Bwa gura̱a̱ bisa̱ wyan ta̱naa na̱ Ala̱masiihu na̱ ame̱ na tande̱ ta̱ba shi.
Iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱
