Azumanu na̱ ro̱pe̱ :1-11Mazama nama ujabagu na Bulusu :12-26Ta̱naawan na̱ Ala̱masiihu :27--2:18Timooti na̱ Apaforiditusu :19-30Ta̱hyan hana ta̱maribici na̱ ngwan :1--4:9Bulusu na̱ ta̱shika ta̱ndaabwa na̱ Filibi :10-20Ta̱wanyan :21-23
Azumanu
Takaada na̱nna shi na báni kuga̱n Bulusu na̱ Timooti, agyama na Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Zhagu kuhyo̱ awyatu na Hwe̱n ana ne̱e̱ na̱ ce̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ Filibi ana shi ana Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ ninhin na̱ ana ta guna̱ na̱ tuma na Hwe̱n.
Ta̱pana ꞌye̱n na̱ hunranhunran na̱ nꞌta̱gumunu ku-Hwe̱n Ada nda̱tu na̱ Butu O̱to̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu xta̱naa huku na̱ ga̱hin.
Uro̱pe̱ na Bulusu wana Afilibi
Nꞌta gooda̱ Hwe̱n nimi koya̱ ha̱ni na ga̱n mata̱ma̱nriin na̱ ga̱hin.
Hyo̱ koya̱ ha̱ni na ga̱n maa ndaaka ma ro̱pe̱ nꞌtanaa nda na̱ ame̱ na tande̱,
na̱ wana haruwa na ga̱hin yibaku suhyu na̱ ga̱mi na̱ tuma na̱nna na ta̱naa wyasa mazama nama zumaa, ta na̱ uhwe̱n na ga̱hin pa̱shi ta̱pana nꞌgata ubwa wuce kuba̱re.
Nꞌshii nii gata hiku ta̱hyan Uhwe̱n na pa̱shi tuma na̱nna na zumaa kuga̱hin, unii re̱ iyeebe nꞌta̱naa nda wuun hara̱ kuta̱huwa̱ ta̱ndaabwa hwe̱n na Ala̱masiihu Yeesu be̱e̱ kúshe̱.
Ushi to̱n na ga̱n hange̱ gama kunnu kuhyo̱ ninhin, na̱ wana iishii ma nii gata. Itanaa huku na̱ ga̱mi na̱ nꞌta̱pana ꞌye̱n nata̱ Hwe̱n nata̱ shani ga̱tun nda tuma na̱nna na zumaa da̱nda̱ hyo̱ na̱ ha̱ni na ga̱n tanaa na̱ zhaaro, paaku ta̱ꞌisahina mazama nama zumaa ta̱hyan mashi mahanda.
Ku-Hwe̱n ta yan kuga̱mii ribi ma nii gata niimi na̱ nꞌta̱ruba̱ nata̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu be̱ mꞌpa̱ni ta̱niinhin, ta ga̱n gura̱a̱ ruba̱ ta̱a̱ndaya ma.
Uro̱pe̱ nimi tashi xta̱maruba̱ ta̱niinhin ta̱ta̱ ta̱hura̱ nꞌta̱mawaana, ire̱ iyeebe nꞌta̱duwa̱na̱ ta̱yansun nata̱ Hwe̱n na̱ nꞌta̱nda ta̱suuga̱ nata̱ mahanda,
na hyan iꞌa̱ri ta̱kasa iri na hura̱gi gama. Na̱ kunnu sa̱i inaa sabu na za yaan randa hara̱ kuhwe̱n na Ala̱masiihu Yeesu be̱e̱ kúshe̱,
ide̱be̱ funa̱ na bina̱ na shi ahari yata na ta̱to̱n ana báni waabe̱, na nii ꞌwaan ta̱yabana na̱ nꞌta̱shapaciga ku-Hwe̱n.
Bulusu hange̱ gama wana mazama nama Ala̱masiihu ma mawya̱shi
Aya̱too ma, nꞌribi na hyan iyansun ta̱hyan iri na nꞌta̱ inii shaana mazama nama zumaa mꞌbaa maduwa̱na̱ ta̱mawyasa.
Na ta̱hyan hyo̱ asooja na ta ha̱mba ka̱ta̱ku na ta̱gwama na̱ hyo̱ ana ne̱e̱ pina ayan ta̱hyan mꞌbwake̱ na̱ zhaaro wana Ala̱masiihu.
Na̱ wana ta̱buka ta̱niimi ta̱ta ta̱shani aya̱too hwarapi pina aba duwa̱ni ta̱ta bishita̱ naa ta̱naa cita̱ga̱ mazama nama Hwe̱n bigata ka̱ na za rukwanyan.
Mahanda mꞌba shi ta̱hyan aka̱ nii bisa̱ga̱ awyatu mazama nama Ala̱masiihu wana ta̱maruba̱, ta̱hyan awyatu jwara̱ga kaba. Aka̱ abaa bisa̱ga̱ awyatu nii gata naa bure.
Ana nꞌgata na mꞌbure nii bisa̱ga̱ wyatu mazama nama zumaa wana aꞌnꞌribi, aba yan ta̱hyan Hwe̱n nꞌka̱shi ma shana muu ma isa hiku ta shani aba mꞌbwake̱ na̱ zhaaro.
Ana̱nnda̱ree ana nii nda muu wana ta̱maruba̱ shici mꞌmahanda ta abaa bisa̱ga̱ wyatu mazama nama Ala̱masiihu. Anii nda muu ta wana hyan aꞌnꞌduwa̱ni ta̱na ma mꞌpa ngwan, ga̱n ma buka na̱ zhaaro.
Too, mashici koori. Nꞌne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ na tande̱ na ta̱hyan anii nda mazama nama Ala̱masiihu na̱ koya̱ yo̱n, koo ushi na ne̱e̱ to̱n koo ushici na ne̱e̱ to̱n.
Ga̱n nii ta ta̱hura̱ nꞌta̱ga̱da̱ri,
wana ga̱n yan ta̱hyan na̱ ro̱pe̱ ninhin kuga̱mi na̱ tuma naa Hwaanwun naa Ala̱masiihu Yeesu na mꞌbini, unii shana ta̱biha̱na̱ ta̱niimi.
Nꞌribi vwainvwain ga̱n gura̱a̱ sha̱a̱ nii gata niimi ta̱hyan xnꞌta kinaa na̱ tuma na Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu, ama manaa nda mꞌba mazama na za bigata buga̱ kuga̱n tanaa nda hasaa. Ga̱n shii bigata ta̱hyan ta̱naa ta̱niimi na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana ta̱nii ꞌwaan ta̱shapaciga ku-Ala̱masiihu, koo ga̱n manaa buwuma, koo ga̱n ma ꞌwa̱.
Kuga̱mi, kunne̱e̱ buwuma, nꞌne̱e̱ ta na hyan ma pa Ala̱masiihu hunrun, kushi ta̱ꞌwa̱ ga̱n ꞌwi, hyo̱ kina hura̱gi gama ta.
Ga̱n bwa nꞌtane̱e̱ buwuma, nꞌnii duwa̱na̱ ta̱nda tuma na bina̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na Ala̱masiihu. Too, nꞌyancin uya̱ ta shi na ga̱n kasa.
Nꞌnii makicihinaa na̱ iri ya̱nu ree, nꞌribi vwainvwain ma ja̱a̱ ma naa na̱ Ala̱masiihu, uya̱nu ta na̱ma nꞌhura̱a̱ga̱ gama.
Ama uhuri gama ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ma naansuun kwan wana ninhin.
Nꞌyan ta̱hyan nꞌnii naansuun kwan, ga̱n nii ta ta̱hura̱ na̱ nꞌta̱naawan na̱ ga̱hin na hyan iiguni ma iduwa̱ni ta̱yansun Hwe̱n na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱da̱ri nata̱ ga̱hin pa̱ni nꞌgata.
Jaa kungura̱a̱ jaa wunhin mayaan, iꞌmꞌbaa iri na ta̱cita̱ hiku ina ga̱hin nda ruwashi na̱ be̱ ina Ala̱masiihu Yeesu be̱ nje̱ tuma na̱ ga̱mi.
Naa nda ma jabagu na magii na̱ mꞌmazama nama Ala̱masiihu
Too, iri na hura̱gi hyo̱ ta shi naa nda ma jabagu na magii na̱ mazama nama zumaa nama Ala̱masiihu. Koo nꞌjaa wunhin, ma gura̱a̱ ma ndaya ma, koo nꞌja̱a̱ci, nꞌnii naa ha̱ngaga mazama maniinhin ma yansun ta̱hyan iꞌe̱she̱ hiku da̱nda̱, ga̱hin nda tuma da̱nda̱, mazama maniinhin maka̱, ma mapa dibi wana ta̱ꞌisahina mazama nama zumaa.
Ta-ha̱nga ma rukwanyan naru anaa kaki ma. Uya̱nu tanii bisa̱a̱ wyan ta̱hyan anii huwo ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱, ga̱hin aabiha̱ni ma. Uhwe̱n na̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa ta na̱maa biha̱na̱ ma.
Na ta̱hyan Hwe̱n pa̱ni ma ta̱ꞌye̱n ta̱ndaabwa shici ipa̱ni kuꞌnꞌgata na̱ Ala̱masiihu huwo, ama hyo̱ nꞌta̱swa ngwan wana nde̱e̱be̱.
Ine̱e̱ na̱ nꞌfwaru haruwa na ga̱hin nda̱i nꞌne̱e̱ na̱ mꞌba, ga̱hin tandaya nꞌfwaru na nꞌga̱n tanda, ga̱hin yan ta̱hyan nꞌtane̱e̱ na̱ awyantancin na mꞌba.

Shapa ma ahari na ta̱yoo ana Ala̱masiihu
Ta̱maꞌunpa̱n ta̱niinhin na̱ Ala̱masiihu ta̱a̱duwa̱ni ma bishita̱ ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa? Koo ta̱ruba̱ nata̱ be̱e̱ ribi ma ta̱a̱ruma̱nha̱ni maa gata? Koo iꞌmꞌbaa ta̱naawan nata̱a̱ Hwaanwun na Hwe̱n? Koo iꞌmꞌbaa ta̱ruba̱ na̱ ambishiri kaya̱na̱nhin?
Too, kiiꞌmꞌbaa ya̱nu kunnu nꞌna̱maa rupa ma ta̱hyan nꞌcaanhini ma ame̱ paaku ta̱sha̱a̱ mazama maka̱, ahari ka̱, ta̱ruba̱ ta̱ka̱ kaya̱na̱nhin.
Ta-nda ma yaanyini na̱ hyuhyu ta̱ruba̱ koo ta̱mashapaciga hyuhyu. Sa̱i da̱i imaciinha̱ni hyuhyu ninhin, sha̱a̱ ma ayaan na̱ nꞌgata niinhin uhuri hyuhyu ninhin.
Makaka ma na̱ iri na ayaan aba ribi, xita sha kina hyuhyu ninhin.
Ahari na ga̱hin mꞌbaa xashi iri ka̱ na̱ ana Ala̱masiihu Yeesu be̱ taꞌmꞌbaa.
Koo na ta̱hyan bitasha Hwe̱n,
ama be̱ tamasha̱pici yaanyini
na hyan binaa nge̱n na̱ Hwe̱n.
Be̱ masha̱pi na shici koori,
be̱ maciinha̱ni ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, be̱ ka̱shi ta̱sha bugyama
aba ma̱ncin buu na̱ mꞌpirwa na mꞌbutu wuma.
Na be̱ tasha butu wuma,
be̱ maciinha̱ni hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱ kunrin wana ta̱jwara̱ga Hwe̱n,
ta̱ba ta̱jwara̱ga ta̱ba sha̱pi buu kuta̱ꞌwa̱,
ta̱ꞌwa̱ nata̱ ta̱kaba buu na̱ guguji haku butu naa pinsan.
Na̱ wana kunnu, sa̱i Uhwe̱n bwa sha̱pa̱cigi buu kupa̱ri naka hura̱gi o̱to̱,
bwa pa̱ni buu ta̱gwama nata̱ huri koo ta̱ya̱ ta̱gwama o̱to̱,
na ta̱hyan koo buya̱ nii pa Yeesu hunrun, buta̱a̱gi buu runrun
ana ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ na̱ ana sa̱ra̱ri yana na̱ ana kunrin na nꞌce̱nye̱n.
Koo buya̱ butu bwaa gura̱a̱ cita̱ da̱shi ta̱hyan Ala̱masiihu Yeesu shi Butu O̱to̱,
na̱ kunnu hyo̱ awyatu sha̱pa̱cigi Uhwe̱n Ada.
Sha ma haku maza̱ki na̱ sa̱ra̱ri
Too, ga̱hin ta̱shika ta̱niimi nata̱ ga̱n nꞌribi, na̱ kunnu haruwa na ga̱hin tanaa sa̱ ijwara̱ga mazama maniimi ga̱n manaawan na̱ ga̱hin, na̱ niina na ga̱n za na̱ ga̱hin, hura̱ ma muu ta̱jwara̱ga. Maha̱ga̱ni ma ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ tuma wana hyan ide̱be̱ ta̱biha̱na̱ ta̱niinhin hiku, igura̱a̱ jwara̱ga Hwe̱n na̱ nꞌta̱cina̱na̱ wuun na̱ nꞌrukwanyan.
Na ta̱hyan Uhwe̱n ta nii nda tuma ndaabwa na̱ nꞌgata nꞌniinhin, uupa̱ni ma ta̱ruba̱ na̱ nꞌta̱kai na hyan inje̱ iri na nii caanhina wuun me̱.
Hyo̱ iri na ga̱hin hiin nda ta-naa nda ma wuun na̱ unta̱nta̱un koo ta̱naa maga̱a̱ga̱nu,
na ta̱hyan ga̱hin jaa mꞌbaa yaan randa, inaa sabu, wana ishi mꞌmwaan na n-Hwe̱n na nꞌza mayaan. Ishi maza̱ki nama ta̱ra̱ka̱ni haku nꞌgwasu na nꞌne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ mꞌba tára̱kani kusa̱ra̱ri na cigi da̱ na̱ awyatu ana za mahanda aba mꞌbaa maꞌwe̱n.
Ibisa̱gi awyatu mazama nama ta̱nda bina̱ na mahwa. Kiinje̱ kunnu, hwe̱n na Ala̱masiihu be̱e̱ kúshe̱ ga̱n ma nda ta̱ga̱da̱ri ta̱hyan nꞌkunha̱ncin ikai nimi ꞌye̱n, utuma na ga̱n nje̱ ubwa zwiici ma̱ni.
Koo ushi nꞌjaa da̱ba hyuhyu nimi nꞌnii nda ta̱ga̱da̱ri, ma wyashika mahiin maniimi haku ri na ta̱pana Hwe̱n. Maya̱nu manii mayibaku na̱ utuma na ta̱pana gata niinhin na shi haku bikico̱ na shinraanyin Hwe̱n. Nꞌribi ma nda ta̱ba ta̱ga̱da̱ri ta̱ya̱nu huku na̱ ga̱hin.
Kunnu ga̱hin taa, inje̱ ta̱ga̱da̱ri huku na̱ ga̱mi.
Timooti na̱ Apaforiditusu
Kumanje̱ to̱n, Butu o̱to̱ Yeesu bwa shani, nꞌribi ta̱káji Timooti pita wunhin na̱ nꞌhwe̱n yana wana hyan kunhange̱ waabwa suga̱hin ne̱e̱ pita, ma duwa̱na̱ bishita̱ ta̱ta.
Nꞌza buyaan buna buushii ma nii gata hakuu bwa.
Hyo̱ ana bwe̱ amakaki kuna̱ ri na suhyu sundaaba uza ri na ta̱ wyan gbi na̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Ga̱hin na̱ nꞌsuhyu suniinhin iyan ku-Timooti bwa tapana hyuhyu ndaabwa hiku na̱ nꞌta̱naa nda tuma na mazama nama zumaa, haku baa na̱ ashin.
Nꞌribi ta̱káji bwa ga̱n nda̱i kiꞌiri be̱ nje̱ na̱ ga̱mi pina.
Nꞌshii bigata hiku ku-Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu shani, nꞌjaa ce̱e̱ bike̱nye̱n, nꞌnii jaa taa pita wunhin.
Ga̱n nda̱i mazumaa na hyan maa kádaagi ma Apaforiditusu, buya̱tu naa tuma bunaa ga̱tu mapaga dibi na̱ tuma na̱a̱ bwa haka sooja. Bwa taa shi bunaa ga̱hin takáji na hyan buꞌnꞌguni sa̱ iri na ga̱n ribi.
Bumakaki ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na hyan buu nda̱i ma, bwa gura̱a̱cii sha̱a̱ bigata fo̱n na̱ wana buhange̱ ta̱hyan ihange̱ butahange̱ce̱ sa̱.
Ee, mahanda butahange̱ce̱ sa̱, buta goka̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱. Ama Uhwe̱n taha̱nga ambishiri ndaabwa, shii kambishiri ndaabwa hyo̱ na̱ animi, wana ta̱hyan ubwa shici nuunu ame̱ ta̱gura tanii mꞌmaa o̱to̱.
Na̱ kunnu ta shani ga̱n shii nii gata vwainvwain ta̱hyan nꞌnii káji bwa wunhin, na hyan kiigura̱a̱ ndaya bwa ishii nꞌgata fo̱n, ga̱n taa pina ma sha̱a̱ bigata fo̱n.
Raa ma bwa inje̱ ta̱ga̱da̱ri wana bushi buya̱na̱a̱nhin ku-Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu. Pa ma bwa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ nata̱ awyatu hakuu bwa aba gii xapa̱ wyan,
wana ta̱hyan buta hiin ꞌwa̱ na̱ tuma na Ala̱masiihu, bwa mo̱nshe̱n ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabwa wana xbuꞌnꞌguni tuma una ga̱hin jaa nꞌara ta̱ꞌnꞌguna̱.

Ta̱sha ana yan Ala̱masiihu hiku
Hyo̱ iri na nje̱ ma aya̱too nimi ma, nda ma ta̱ga̱da̱ri ku-Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu. Nꞌjaa rukuta̱ na̱ nꞌta̱namaa táagagi ma iri na ga̱n tahoo maa táagagi ma kuwana hyan uyanshin yaan ri na nii yansan ta̱pana gata niinhin.
Nda ma aha̱nka̱ri kusuwa suyata, awyatu yata na mꞌbaa suhari nasu we̱, ana ta hyan ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ xaꞌya̱pi butu ta̱wya̱ri bwa hiin da̱ba ta̱nda bina̱.
Na ta̱hyan ga̱tu naa shi ana nii paga Hwe̱n hunrun Kiihwaanwun ndaabwa, ga̱tu taa shi ana mahanda ana ꞌya̱pi ta̱wya̱ri. Ga̱tu taa shi ana nii nda ruwashi na̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu. Ubwa za na ta̱ta̱ gbi na̱ nꞌta̱jwara̱ga iri na shi na butu wuma,
koo na ta̱hyan mꞌmꞌbaa iri na shani na ibe̱ nꞌta̱ gbi na̱ iri na ga̱n nda.
Kuyaan butu nda̱i ta̱hyan ihuri be̱ ta̱ta̱ gbi na hyan bujwara̱ga iri na shi na butu wuma, ga̱n huri bwa ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa.
Ataꞌnꞌyapa ta̱wya̱ri ga̱n na̱ nꞌhwe̱n ta̱ndatu nꞌta̱mantan. Ga̱n, mahiin nama ta̱ma̱ncin nata̱ Isiraaꞌila ta̱ta, na paakii korogo naa Be̱njami, Buꞌibiraaniya naa mahanda. Nꞌta jwara̱ga Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n bwa tapana Muusa hyo̱ hiku wana nꞌtasha Bufaraasiya.
Wana nꞌta hura̱ ta̱pa yima̱a̱ kuta̱jwara̱ga Hwe̱n ki, ga̱n tanaa sa̱ makaka awyatu na Yeesu ta̱ꞌo̱to̱. Paaku ta̱naa nda iri na ta̱to̱n, nꞌta̱jwara̱ga Nꞌgira̱nshin ki na za ta̱wajigaa.
Ga̱n tanaa sa̱ ma shapa ta̱hyan iri na ga̱n tanaa nda mꞌbaa yaan bina̱, ta ga̱n nda̱i niina ishi iri na uwa̱ wana iri na Ala̱masiihu be̱ nje̱.
Shii kumaya̱nu nꞌsha̱pi komba̱ri ta̱hyan ishi na uwa̱ na̱ wana iri na hura̱gi bina̱, na hyan ma yansun hiku Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, Butu O̱to̱ niimi. Wana nde̱e̱be̱ ta ga̱n ga̱a̱ komba̱ri ta̱hyan ishi so̱nro̱n nata̱ munsan, na hyan ma sha naa Ala̱masiihu,
ma maꞌunpa̱n nii be̱. Nꞌgura̱a̱cii ma sha̱a̱ ta̱hyan Uhwe̱n nda̱i nꞌshi naa ta̱to̱n wana nꞌjwarigi Nꞌgira̱nshin, nꞌnda̱i ta̱hyan Uhwe̱n nda̱i nꞌshi naa ta̱to̱n kuta̱panaa gata na̱ Ala̱masiihu, wana uyo̱n na hyan ta̱shi ana ta̱to̱n na̱ uba̱ ndaabwa une̱e̱ kuta̱panaa gata.
Nꞌribi ma yansun Ala̱masiihu hiku, na̱ nꞌta̱kai nata̱ tahiika̱hina̱ buu kuta̱ꞌwa̱, na̱ nꞌta̱naawan da̱nda̱ nii be̱ kungwan nde̱e̱be̱, ma naa hakii be̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱ ta̱nde̱e̱be̱,
wana hyan koo na, uꞌnꞌye̱e̱ kuta̱hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱ zhagu kubina̱.
Ta̱maka̱nta̱na̱ na hyan ta̱de̱be̱ ta̱be̱sa
Shii ta̱hyan nꞌhin, nꞌhoo da̱ba hyo̱ ri ya̱nu na shi kunshi, koo nꞌhoo ara hyo̱ hiku. Ama mꞌmaka̱nta̱ni na hyan ma da̱ba ta̱sha bwa butu naa Ala̱masiihu Yeesu be̱ taruba̱ nꞌshi na be̱ taꞌnꞌkasa ga̱mi.
Aya̱too ma, nꞌtamashiici ta̱hyan nꞌhoo sha butu naa de̱be̱ ta̱be̱sa, ama mꞌpa̱ yima̱a̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ ri ka̱. Iri ka̱ na ga̱n nje̱ tashi nꞌha̱a̱sa̱ni ina ne̱e̱ ta̱baa, ga̱n sha̱a̱ta̱ni hyuhyu kina ne̱e̱ iyeebe.
Mꞌmaka̱nta̱ni na hyan ma da̱ba ta̱wuta̱ gyaga na nꞌsumo̱ ma gura̱a̱ raa funa̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ na shi una Uhwe̱n bwa ta̱nꞌnꞌgani ku-Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Hyo̱ nda̱tu ana shi ana nje̱ kai nꞌta̱panaa gata ku-Yeesu xara̱ni na̱ ina̱nna ri. Kiinda̱i ta̱hyan ira̱ncin na̱ mꞌmaba mazama, Uhwe̱n nii bisa̱a̱ ma yo̱n na hyan aꞌe̱nshe̱n ki.
Na huri hyo̱ tashi, xta̱nta̱ ma nꞌta̱hura̱ na̱ paa ga̱tu hoo nꞌwuta̱.
Aya̱too ma, naa nda ma jabagu haka nimi da̱nda̱. Sha̱a̱ ma suha̱nka̱ri suniinhin ki kuꞌana jwarigi ina ga̱tuu ga̱a̱gi ma.
Kuga̱n tanaa maa bisa̱ga̱ ma koya̱ ha̱ni niina ta ga̱n gura̱a̱ namaa bisa̱ga̱ ma hyo̱ na̱ nꞌungwa, ta̱hyan ane̱e̱ ahwarapi ana ta̱hani ta̱ndaaba ta̱ba ribici xawyatu yansun ta̱hyan imbata shani Ala̱masiihu Yeesu be̱ taꞌwa̱ na̱ guguji.
Aja̱a̱ huwa̱ ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱ ta̱hakana, wana shami na ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaaba ta̱ba ribi tashi haku hwe̱n ndaaba na abaa paga hunrun. Atanaa nda ruwashi naru iri na nꞌkogi na abaa nda, ata makaka kuna̱ ri na nii antana ta̱ꞌwaba pina na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana.
Ama ga̱tu ta̱nshi awyatu na ta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, paa Butu O̱to̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu be̱ hunrani. Ga̱tu makaki ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ kuswa nde̱e̱be̱ na hyan bita̱mbiha̱ni.
Be̱ taa shi na̱ nꞌta̱kai ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ be̱ ja̱a̱ wuna̱a̱na̱ ri hyo̱ kuta̱gwama ta̱nde̱e̱be̱, bihe̱re̱ge̱ ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱nda̱a̱tu nata̱ ja̱a̱ pwasa ta̱shi haku ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ nata̱ de̱be̱ ta̱shapaciga.

Mazama nama ta̱taa shita̱
Na̱ kunnu, aya̱too nimi, isa ma hiku ku-Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu. Ga̱hin naa shi aya̱too nimi ana ne̱e̱ nii gata niimi koya̱ ha̱ni, ana ga̱n nꞌribi kimii nda̱i ma vwainvwain, ga̱hin naa taꞌnꞌcaanhina me̱, ga̱hin shi funa̱ kutuma nimi.
Yudiya na̱ Sintiki, kusu iiro̱pe̱ ma maꞌa̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni ma nꞌta̱maꞌunso̱ncin ta̱niinhin wana ishi ana Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu.
Kunnu taa gaa buya̱tu niimi naa tuma naa ta̱hiku, kusu, guna̱ aꞌa̱ yata xamaꞌunso̱n, wana ta̱hyan amapa̱ dibi na̱ tuma na̱nna ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ ga̱mi paa ta̱naa bisa̱ga̱ awyatu mazama nama zumaa. Anje̱ tuma na̱ Kileme na̱ ayaan wyatu nimi na tuma da̱nda̱ ana Uhwe̱n bwa ta̱gi azha̱a̱zha̱a̱ ndaaba na̱ takaada na ta̱bina̱ mahwa.
Nda ma ta̱ga̱da̱ri koya̱ ha̱ni ku-Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu. Nꞌgura̱a̱ duwa̱na̱ ta̱a̱ bisa̱ ma nda ma ta̱ga̱da̱ri!
Naa nda ma ri shukuu huku na̱ aha̱nka̱ri na zumaa na koo buya̱ bwaa ndaya. Mata̱ma̱nriin ma ta̱hyan Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu goki ta̱wuce.
Ta-makaka ma na̱ yaan ri, ama na̱ koya̱ hari na ga̱hin ta̱ni, rupa ma Hwe̱n huku nꞌta̱hantana na̱ hyo̱ iri na ga̱hin ribi yibaku nꞌta̱gooda̱ wuun.
Na̱ kunnu ta Uhwe̱n bwa na̱maa pana ma ta̱naa gumunu nata̱ hura̱ni ta̱yansun nata̱ butu wuma. Ta̱gumunu ta̱ndaabwa ta̱nii ha̱mba nꞌgata niinhin na̱ iri na ga̱hin makicihinaa na̱ ame̱ ninhin wana ishi ana Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Na̱ nꞌta̱wanyan mazama, aya̱too nimi, na makicihinaa ma na̱ iri na shi na mahanda, na̱ iri na gii ta̱cina̱na̱, na̱ iri na ne̱e̱ to̱n, na̱ iri na ta̱sabu, na̱ iri na nii ꞌwaan ta̱ruba̱, na̱ iri na shi na bina̱. Hyo̱ iri na hura̱gi na̱ iri na nii ꞌwaan ta̱yabana, na makicihinaa ma na̱ ya̱nu.
Hyo̱ iri na ga̱mii ga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni ma, ga̱hin ra̱a̱ wuun, ga̱hin hange̱ nꞌcici, ga̱hin nda̱i nꞌnii nda, naa sa̱ nda ma wuun. Uhwe̱n na ta̱gumunu nii naawan na̱ ga̱hin.
Bulusu gooji awyatu na Yeesu ana Filibi
Nꞌduwa̱ni ta̱nda ta̱ga̱da̱ri ku-Butu O̱to̱ na ga̱hin gura̱a̱ nꞌgwatana. Nꞌyan ta̱hyan ita nꞌgwatana koya̱ ha̱ni, ama ide̱be̱ce̱ ha̱ba̱ na hyan ibisa̱a̱ tuun.
Shii ta̱hyan nꞌcici kunnu wana mꞌbaa yaanyini na ga̱n ribi. Ai, nꞌhoo maga̱gaagana haruwa na hyan ma naa fo̱n na̱ koya̱ iri na ri na nꞌde̱be̱.
Nꞌyan haruwa na hyan ma hunrana na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌmꞌbaa ri ma̱ koo na̱ ꞌwa̱ta̱gi. Nꞌa̱ri ta̱hunrana fo̱n na̱ koya̱ iri na ri na nꞌjábani, koo na̱ nꞌrumunro̱n koo na̱ ciga̱, koo na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌmꞌbaa ma̱ koo na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌmꞌbaa ge̱.
Nꞌnii ara ta̱nda komba̱ri kuta̱kai nata̱ Ala̱masiihu be̱ mꞌpa̱ni.
Hyo̱ na̱ kunnu, inje̱ to̱n na ga̱hin nꞌguni na̱ ngwan na ga̱n ne̱e̱ na̱ bwa.
Ga̱hin Afilibi, iyan ta̱hyan kuga̱hin taa shi ana taꞌnꞌguna̱ paa ri ta̱pagana na ga̱n pa̱shi ta̱ꞌiye̱ mazama nama zumaa kuga̱hin na̱ na ga̱n tagaa Makidooniya. Biyaan bigudu naa awyatu na Yeesu ta za naa tanda kunnu.
Koo na ga̱n tanaa na̱ Tasaloonika itaꞌnꞌkádaagi na̱ ri shii maka̱.
Shii ta̱hyan nꞌnii cita̱ga̱ mazama mana̱nna wana koo nꞌribi yaanyini wunhin, nꞌnii cita̱ga̱ ta wana nꞌribi Hwe̱n duwa̱ni funa̱ ninhin o̱to̱ wana iꞌnꞌndaaki ri na bina̱.
Nꞌra̱a̱ ꞌwaa nimi o̱to̱ una hura̱ni haruwa na ta̱ga̱gaaga. Nꞌza iyaan ri na ga̱n gura̱a̱ ruba̱, niina na ga̱n ra̱a̱ ina ga̱hin taꞌnꞌkádaagi ga̱hin páni Apaforiditusu. Ina̱nna ta shi ta̱pana nata̱ mꞌbaa nꞌshima na nꞌzumaa, na nꞌta caanhina Hwe̱n me̱, ubwa ribi muu.
Uhwe̱n na nꞌhambe̱ na̱maa pana ma hyo̱ iri na ga̱hin ribi kuꞌiri ma̱ ndaabwa wana ta̱maꞌunpa̱n ta̱niinhin na̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
xTa̱shapaciga ta̱naa huku ku-Hwe̱n Ada nda̱tu niina na̱ mꞌmahwa! xMashi kunnu.
Bulusu wanyin azumanu
Nꞌzumaanyin ma hyo̱ awyatu na Hwe̱n, ana shi ana Ala̱masiihu Yeesu. Aya̱too ana ga̱n ne̱e̱ na̱ aba pina aazúmani ma.
Na̱ hyo̱ ayaan ana Hwe̱n aazúmani ma taa huku na̱ ana ne̱e̱ na̱ tuma na̱ ka̱ta̱ku na bugwama Kaisa.
Ta̱pana ꞌye̱n nata̱ Butu O̱to̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu xta̱naa huku na̱ ga̱hin hyo̱.
COL - Pangu
Akoloosi
Akol
Akoloosi
Takaada na Bulusu bwa ta̱gi zhagu Akoloosi
Takaada na Bulusu bwa ta̱gi zhagu kawyatu na
Koloosi
Iri na ta̱yansun na yigo
Bulusu butumashini naa Yeesu taa ta̱gi takaada na̱nna zhagu kawyatu na Yeesu ana ne̱e̱ na̱ ce̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ Koloosi. Bulusu bwaa tanda̱ci wyan na̱ ayishe, ama buyaan bunaa taguna̱ bwa tuma Abafarasu bunaa ubwa ce̱pe̱, bwa taa shi naa ta ciba̱ aba awyatu na Yeesu. Bulusu tataga takaada na̱nna ha̱ni na bwa ne̱e̱ na̱ zhaaro na̱ Rooma na bwa tanda nꞌyo̱ nꞌree.
Butataga na̱nna wana hyan buꞌa̱sa̱ga̱ni ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ ta̱be̱ nata̱ aba tanaa nda na̱ ce̱pe̱ na Koloosi. Ta̱ba ta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱tahyan ta̱jwara̱ga nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌwyatu ta nii shana butu de̱be̱ bina̱ na mahwa. Na sha̱pi ta̱naa paga hunrun kuꞌayaan atuma na Hwe̱n na abaa paga hunrun, na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌyapa ta̱wya̱ri na̱ nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌta̱re̱ce̱ yaan shami.
Ubwa takaada tabisa̱a̱ ta̱hyan ta̱bina̱ hiku ta̱ne̱e̱ huwa̱ paaku Yeesu, bwa gura̱a̱ hyan Yeesu ta shi mꞌpirwa na n-Hwe̱n na nꞌta̱hiku. Yeesu ta shi bunaa tahoo naa hasaa ta aba njiwo yaan ri, nii be̱ ta aba nje̱ hyo̱ komba̱ri. Takaada bwa gura̱a̱ cita̱ ta̱hyan be̱ taa shi hyuhyu na awyatu nde̱e̱be̱, be̱ shi naa ne̱e̱ na̱ awyantancin na awyatu wuma na̱ Hwe̱n paaku ta̱naa raa ta̱suuga̱.
Iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱
Azumanu :1-8Ala̱masiihu Yeesu na̱ tuma nde̱e̱be̱ :9--2:19Ujabagu na fo da̱nda̱ na̱ Ala̱masiihu :20--4:6Ta̱wanyan :7-18
Azumanu na báni ku-Bulusu
Takaada na̱nna shi na báni kuga̱n Bulusu, butumashini naa Ala̱masiihu Yeesu kuta̱sha̱a̱ nata̱ Hwe̱n, na̱ buya̱tu Timooti.
Zhagu kawyatu na Hwe̱n ana ne̱e̱ na̱ ce̱pe̱ na o̱to̱ Koloosi ana shi aya̱too ana pa̱ni nꞌgata nꞌndaaba hiku ku-Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
xUhwe̱n Ada nda̱tu uupa̱ni ta̱pana ꞌye̱n na̱ hunranhunran na̱ nꞌta̱gumunu.
Ro̱pe̱ na̱ nꞌta̱gooda̱ na Bulusu
Koya̱ ha̱ni na ga̱tuu ndaaka ma ro̱pe̱, ta̱ta gooda̱ Hwe̱n na shi Ada na Butu O̱to̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu nda̱tu,
wana ta̱hange̱ haruwa na ga̱hin pa̱ni nꞌgata ku-Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, na̱ haruwa na ga̱hin bisa̱a̱ ta̱ruba̱ kawyatu na Hwe̱n hyo̱.
Inje̱ kunnu wana ta̱sha̱a̱ nꞌgata hiku na̱ ufuna̱ na Hwe̱n bwaa sha̱a̱gi ma nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ tana ga̱hin taha̱nga mahanda nama mazama nama zumaa.
Kumazama mayata nama zumaa mata manii mawyasa, mꞌbaa ꞌwaan ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ bina̱ kope na̱ sa̱ra̱ri na̱ jabagu na bina̱ kawyatu, haruwa na mꞌba tahira̱ga jabagu ninhin hwe̱n na ga̱hin pa̱shi muu ta̱ha̱nga, ga̱hin e̱nshe̱n mahanda nama ta̱pana ꞌye̱n nata̱ Hwe̱n kuta̱ba yaburi.
Kunta ta ga̱hin tayansun muu ku-Abafarasu, buya̱tu naa ga̱tu ribi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, bunaa pa̱nii hyuhyu ndaabwa hiku kutuma na Ala̱masiihu na shi kuta̱nii nda wunhin ta bwaa ndaaka ma wuun.
Bunaa shi naa ta̱bishi ta̱ruba̱ ta̱niinhin kawyatu na Hwe̱n nata̱a̱ Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n be̱e̱ pa̱ni ma.
Wana ya̱nu ta, ta hwe̱n na ga̱tu hange̱ ri na ga̱hin nda, ta̱ta ga̱a̱ci ta̱namaa ndaaka ma ro̱pe̱ na hyan Uhwe̱n ciga̱hini ma na̱ nꞌta̱yansun nata̱ ta̱sha̱a̱ ta̱ndaabwa, na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌinsan, na̱ nꞌta̱bita̱riga nata̱ báni kii-Hwaanwun ndaabwa.
Na̱ kunnu ta ga̱hin nii nda ujabagu una magii na̱ awyatu na jwarigi Butu O̱to̱, ubwa jabagu caanhini wuun sa̱ me̱ na̱ koya̱ yo̱n. Inaa ꞌwaanyin ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ bina̱ na̱ hyo̱ utuma na gama ninhin, inaa gura̱a̱ duwa̱na̱ ta̱mawaana nꞌta̱yansun Hwe̱n ki.
xUhwe̱n duwa̱ni ma ta̱taa shita̱ na̱ hyo̱ ta̱kai ta̱ndaabwa nata̱ za haru, wana hyan iꞌmꞌbaa ta̱ꞌisa hiku na̱ akuri da̱nda̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱da̱ri.
Inaa gooda̱ga̱ sa̱ Ada ana shani ga̱hin a̱ri ta̱da̱ba ta̱nu kuhooso na ta̱hya̱su ri na ubwa sha̱a̱gi andaabwa kuta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱gwaan.
Ubwa ta shi na ta̱ya̱a̱cigi kuta̱gwama nata̱ ta̱yincincin, bwa ta̱ꞌye̱e̱ kuta̱gwama nata̱ Buyoo bunaa bwa hura̱gi ta̱ruba̱.
Hwe̱n ta̱mbiha̱ni paaku ta̱wyashika mahiin nama Buyoo, bwa ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ncin pinsan nda̱tu nii gata ndaabwa.
Ala̱masiihu ta hura̱gi hyo̱
Ala̱masiihu ta shi mꞌpirwa na n-Hwe̱n una aba a̱rici ta̱ndaya, bwa taa shi o̱to̱ naa hyo̱ iri na ndagi.
Be̱ ta tandaga hyo̱ iri na Hwe̱n bwa taruba̱ inaa na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, ina ga̱tu ara ta̱ndaya na̱ ina ga̱tu jaa ara ta̱ndaya. Be̱ ta tandaga ta̱gwama, na̱ nꞌta̱kai, na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌo̱to̱ goo goo. Hyo̱ iri tandaga waabe̱ na̱ wana nde̱e̱be̱.
Bitahoo naa ta aba njiwo komba̱ri, be̱ gura̱a̱ shana hyo̱ iri ibe̱ ta̱ ta̱hura̱ nꞌta̱naa.
Be̱ taa shi hyuhyu na ta̱ꞌwaba, awyatu ande̱e̱be̱ aba shi ta̱ꞌwaba. Be̱ taa shi naa yigo, be̱ shi o̱to̱ naa hyo̱ kana ta̱hiika̱ kuta̱ꞌwa̱, na̱ wana kunnu ta be̱ shi naa yigo na̱ hyo̱ komba̱ri.
Hwe̱n taruba̱ xunaa na̱ ame̱ nde̱e̱be̱ na hyan biꞌmꞌbaa hyo̱ komba̱ri ndaabwa.
Kiibe̱ ta Hwe̱n bwa taꞌa̱sa̱a̱ga̱na̱ ta̱maꞌunso̱ncin nata̱ komba̱ri na bwa nje̱. Paaku ta̱wyashika mahiin mande̱e̱be̱ na̱ guguji, ta bwa ta̱nꞌwaanyin hunranhunran na ta̱gumunu kuhyo̱ iri na ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ na̱ na sa̱ra̱ri yana.
Na yigo itanaa tutu na̱ Hwe̱n, ga̱hin shi ana ribici wuun wana iri na we̱ na ga̱hin shii na̱ nꞌgata niinhin ga̱hin nda wuun.
Ama niina ta ubwaa a̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni ma ta̱maꞌunso̱ncin kuta̱ꞌwa̱ nata̱ Ala̱masiihu na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ butu wuma, na hyan uuꞌíye̱ ma waabwa, inaa sabu na za yaan randa, na za iyaan ri na hyan aandaaki ma suuga̱ kaꞌuba̱ ndaabwa.
Na ta̱hyan ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ ire̱ iyeebe na̱ nꞌta̱panaa gata na̱ iri na̱nna na shi mahanda, iꞌisa hiku nꞌta̱ba. Ta-hakata ma xaazha̱a̱nta̱ni ma kuta̱sha̱a̱ bigata yata nata̱ ga̱hin taha̱nga kumazama nama zumaa. Mazama mayata nama zumaa abisa̱gi muu kope na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana, ta ga̱n, Bulusu, Hwe̱n bwa nꞌka̱shi masha bugyama ndaabwa ma bisa̱ga̱ muu kukoo buya̱.
Utuma na Bulusu kawyatu na Yeesu
Ga̱n ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ na tande̱ na̱ wana ungwan na ga̱n swa nꞌta̱ꞌwaba ta̱niimi na̱ wana ninhin, na̱ ngwan na̱nna ta ga̱n ciga̱hini ngwan na Ala̱masiihu be̱ taswa na be̱ taꞌnꞌta nꞌnje̱ na̱ wana ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱nde̱e̱be̱, ta̱ba ta ta̱shi awyatu nde̱e̱be̱.
Nꞌshi bugyama naa awyatu nde̱e̱be̱ kutuma na Hwe̱n bwa mꞌpa̱ni wana ninhin, ma bisa̱ga̱ awyatu mazama mandaabwa hyo̱ kuꞌmꞌba shi.
Mana̱nna mazama nama ga̱n na̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma, mashi ashe̱re̱ na tanaa ta̱swee yo̱o̱ na̱ nꞌyo̱ na nꞌhura̱gi, ama niina ta aba ba̱nriin wyan kawyatu na Hwe̱n.
Hwe̱n taruba̱ ta̱bisa̱ wyan xayansun haruwa na maca̱ma̱nta̱n nama ashe̱re̱ ndaabwa mꞌba ne̱e̱, mashi maniinhin taa maa ana shici Ayaahudiya. Aba she̱re̱ tashi, Ala̱masiihu yata na ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱ ninhin, wana hyan iꞌmꞌbaa ta̱sha̱a̱ bigata hiku kuta̱taa ta̱niinhin kuta̱shapaciga ta̱nde̱e̱be̱.
Too, ta shani ga̱tu bisa̱ga̱ koo buya̱ ku-Ala̱masiihu be̱ shi. Ga̱tu gura̱a̱ ga̱gaagana na̱ nꞌta̱koota̱ga̱ koo buya̱ na̱ hyo̱ ta̱bita̱riga nata̱ Hwe̱n bwa ta̱mpa̱ni, na hyan ta̱shani koo buya̱ bumawaani hiku kuta̱panaa gata ku-Ala̱masiihu.
Na̱ wana kunnu ta ga̱n mapa dibi ma nda ji haruwa na ikai na Ala̱masiihu be̱ mꞌpagana, una ne̱e̱ na̱ ga̱mi.

Nꞌribi na hyan iyansun ta̱hyan udibi na ga̱n ma pa na hyan iiguni ma, ga̱hin na̱ awyatu na Yeesu ana Lawudikiya, na̱ hyo̱ ayaan ande̱e̱be̱ ana taꞌnꞌta̱ci yishe.
Na shani ga̱n nda kunnu ushi wana hyan aduwa̱ni ta̱taa shita̱ nii gata, ta̱maruba̱ ta̱ndaaba ta̱shani amaꞌunpin wana hyan aꞌmꞌbaa ta̱sha̱a̱ bigata hiku na ta̱yansun ashe̱re̱ na Hwe̱n ki, na shi Ala̱masiihu na̱ hyuhyu nde̱e̱be̱.
Na ta̱hyan waabe̱ kata ta̱shapaciga nata̱ ashe̱re̱ ana ta̱yansun na̱ nꞌta̱bita̱riga ta̱ba ma soo.
Nꞌna̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma ta na ta̱hyan xbuyaan butaa pira̱a̱ga̱ga̱ ma na̱ mꞌmayaan mazama nama masuunran.
Koo na ga̱n zaagwa na̱ ga̱hin, ama bihwaanwun niimi ne̱e̱ huku na̱ ga̱hin. Ga̱n ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ga̱da̱ri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ haruwa na ga̱n hange̱ imaꞌunpin hiku ga̱hin ta̱a̱ gata macimi nꞌta̱panaa gata niinhin ku-Ala̱masiihu.
Ta̱jwara̱ga Ala̱masiihu ta̱ꞌwaan jabagu na fo
Too, niina na ta̱hyan ira̱a̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu be̱ shi Butu O̱to̱ niinhin, ta ma ta̱hura̱ na̱ nꞌta̱jwara̱ga buu.
Inii ara ta̱nda kunnu ga̱hin shii ame̱ ninhin hiku nii be̱ haka nga̱nga̱nda̱ na cibi, ya̱nu tanii shana iꞌisa nꞌta̱kai na̱ nꞌta̱jwara̱ga ta̱niinhin haruwa na abaa ga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni ma, ishi ana ta gooda̱ Hwe̱n ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Ishii suha̱nka̱ri suniinhin ki xbuyaan butaa aragana ma koo buupira̱a̱ga̱gi ma na̱ nꞌta̱yaan ta̱yansun nata̱ uwa̱, nata̱ shi nata̱ báni kuꞌnꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌwyatu wuma na̱ jabagu na sa̱ra̱ri yana, ta̱ba shici nata̱ báni ku-Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Ala̱masiihu ta tanaa nꞌta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ butu wuma, be̱ ta mꞌbaa hyo̱ komba̱ri na Hwe̱n.
Ga̱hin taa iꞌmꞌbaa hyo̱ komba̱ri na ga̱hin ribi, wana ta̱maꞌunpa̱n ta̱niinhin na̱ Ala̱masiihu, bunaa shi hyuhyu nata̱ ta̱gwama na̱ nꞌta̱kai hyo̱.
Na̱ nꞌta̱ba ta̱maꞌunpa̱n ta̱ta abaa ꞌya̱pa̱gi ma ta̱wya̱ri, shii ta̱ꞌyapa nata̱ butu wuma, paa be̱e̱ ya̱a̱cigi ma na̱ nꞌsuhari suniinhin nasu we̱.
Na̱ kunnu ta, ha̱ni na abaa ndaaki ma baba̱tiisa̱ma, iri ka̱ bwa shi na̱ nꞌta̱a̱wuma̱na̱ ma na̱ Ala̱masiihu. Hwe̱n bwaa hiika̱hini ma huku nii be̱, kuta̱panaa gata niinhin kutuma na ta̱kai nata̱ Hwe̱n na tahiika̱hina̱ buu kuta̱ꞌwa̱.
Na̱ ayigo itasha haka awyatu na ꞌwa̱gi wana pinsan ninhin, na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌya̱pa̱gici ta̱wya̱ri nata̱ suhari suniinhin nasu we̱. Ama niina Uhwe̱n ta bwaa kúshihine̱ ma ana bini huku na̱ Ala̱masiihu, ubwa ta̱mha̱mba̱ga̱ncin koo yaan pinsan nda̱tu nii gata ndaabwa.
Utata̱yaaciga hwa̱ na pinsan una tata̱kadaga na̱ Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa. Ubwa ha̱nsha̱nha̱ni wuun paaku ta̱kaba na̱ guguji.
Bwa ra̱a̱ ꞌwaa na gyasa na ana ta̱gwama na̱ ana ta̱kai, bwa pa̱ wyan nꞌkogi kuhwarapi na wyatu, bwa bisa̱a̱ wyan ta̱hyan bure̱ gyasa kuta̱ꞌwa̱ nata̱ Ala̱masiihu na̱ guguji.
Na̱ wana kunnu ta-makaka ma buyaan bubwaa sha̱a̱gi ma yishe na̱ ri na ga̱hin re̱ koo ga̱hin swa, koo na̱ nꞌta̱jwarigici yaan hwe̱n na buki na adiini koo ta̱ꞌisa nata̱ pyanda koo hwe̱n na ha̱nka̱na̱ na Ayaahudiya.
Aya̱nu ta shi ahurukutu na iri na ja̱a̱ wuce, ama Ala̱masiihu tashi mahanda nama ibe̱ ri ya̱nu.
Wana kunnu ta-gaa ma buyaan buu hooshi ma na̱ funa̱ ninhin, nꞌta̱hyan bwaa shi yaan ri wana bunda̱i ri haka ra̱rabi. Buhin ma munsan ma suhyu suniinhin, inaa paga atuma na Hwe̱n hunrun. Iri na awyatu ya̱nu atanaa nda ruwashi naru za hyuhyu, aba za mꞌpirwa nꞌta̱ruba̱ hyuhyu ndaaba kubutu wuma bwa shi.
Aba jwarigici ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ Ala̱masiihu na shi hyuhyu na ta̱ꞌwaba. Be̱ taa shi naa ha̱mba̱gi hyo̱ ta̱ꞌwaba, aba sa̱nta̱a̱n nꞌun na̱ nꞌnii, aba mawaana nꞌta̱mawaana nata̱ Hwe̱n bwa ta shana.
Kuta̱ꞌwa̱ ta̱niinhin da̱nda̱ na̱ Ala̱masiihu ta̱a̱biha̱ni ma kuꞌnꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌadiini na sa̱ra̱ri yana, iba̱ shani ga̱hin ne̱e̱ na̱ hunranhunran haku ana shi na sa̱ra̱ri yana ga̱hin jwarigi nꞌgira̱nshin ndaabwa,
kuta̱hyan, <<Ta-kota̱na̱! Ta-hunkuntana masuunran! Ta-antana!>>?
Ta̱jwara̱ga iri ya̱nu shi haku ri na butu bwa ta re̱ ijaa poshi hyo̱, wana ta̱hyan anje̱ wuun mꞌmacimi nama butu.
Iri na nꞌgira̱nshin ya̱nu mꞌmꞌbaa mꞌpirwa na nꞌta̱bita̱riga nata̱ butu, wana ta̱ta shana awyatu pa̱ zha̱munkun ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ kuꞌadiini na awyatu aba mapa̱a̱gi. Bwa ta shana koo buya̱ bumo̱nshe̱n hyuhyu ndaabwa wana wyanzun na funa̱ na̱ nꞌta̱naa pa ta̱ꞌwaba ngwan. Ama hyo̱ ya̱nu ujaa yansan ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱nda pinsan.

Ta̱shapa ahari ana a̱sa̱ga̱ni na fo
Ta na ta̱hyan Hwe̱n hoo hiika̱hina̱ ma huku na̱ Ala̱masiihu, sha̱a̱ ma suyishe suniinhin kuꞌiri na ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, paaku Ala̱masiihu be̱ hunrani kukataga naka Hwe̱n.
Sha̱a̱ ma suha̱nka̱ri suniinhin kuꞌiri na ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, shici ina ne̱e̱ na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n.
Na ta̱hyan ihoo ꞌwa̱ga̱, ama aba soo kwan nꞌhunjo̱ nꞌniinhin na̱ Ala̱masiihu ku-Hwe̱n.
Ha̱ni na Ala̱masiihu na shi na ta̱pa̱ni ta̱bina̱ nata̱ fo ta̱nda̱a̱tu be̱ he̱e̱n buza̱a̱, ga̱hin taamaa ihe̱e̱n buza̱a̱ huku nii be̱ na̱ nꞌta̱shapaciga.
Wana kunnu gaa ma ta̱ruba̱ nata̱ koya̱ iri na ri ina sa̱ra̱ri yana, na shi banshaun, utuma na daba, na̱ nꞌta̱maa ta̱sha̱a̱ yishe kaꞌa̱, na̱ nꞌta̱maa ta̱sha̱a̱ ta̱nda iri na we̱ nii gata, na̱ nꞌta̱ruba̱ nata̱ iri ma̱, na shi nge̱n ta̱naa paga iri na shici Hwe̱n hunrun.
Na̱ wana iri na apinsan ya̱nu ta ame̱ ta̱gura na Hwe̱n aba ta he̱e̱n acíin kana tibici mazama.
Na yigo ga̱hin suhyu suniinhin ita naa sa̱a̱ na̱ iri na suhari suya̱nu ha̱ni na ubwa tanaa na̱ jabagu ninhin.
Ama niina gaa ma hyo̱ iri ya̱nu na shi: ame̱ ta̱gura, na̱ nꞌgata mamboo, na̱ ambyau, na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ buyaan ruzha̱a̱, na̱ mꞌmazama nama uwa̱ na̱ nꞌsunu suniinhin.
Ta-naa ma ndaakaku ma ta̱be̱ wana ihoo munsan aba ahari na yigo hyo̱ na̱ jabagu ndaaba,
ga̱hin sha̱pi ahari yata na fo anaa he̱re̱ge̱ ma na̱ mꞌpirwa na m-Bunaa nje̱ muu iyansun be̱ hiku.
Too, na ta̱hyan ide̱be̱ jabagu na fo, mayaan maza nama ta̱hyan buna̱nna shi Buyaahudiya koo bushici Buyaahudiya, buꞌya̱pi ta̱wya̱ri koo buꞌya̱pici ta̱wya̱ri, bugai koo bunaa guna̱a̱ncin yishe, koo bugyama koo bushici bugyama. Hyo̱ Ala̱masiihu ta shi komba̱ri be̱ ne̱e̱ hyo̱ na̱ nꞌga̱tu.
Na ta̱hyan Hwe̱n ka̱shi ma ishi awyatu ndaabwa ana ta̱sabu ana bwa ribi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, mꞌbaa ma ambishiri, na̱ nꞌta̱mandaakaku ri na bina̱, na̱ nꞌta̱ma̱a̱ncin hyuhyu ta̱shapaciga, na̱ nꞌta̱naa maꞌiya shukuu na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌmꞌbaa akuri.
Inaa mahakataga kuyaan buwa̱jiga̱a̱ buya̱na̱. Kuuyaan bune̱e̱ bunaa mꞌbaa mazama na̱a̱ ya̱na̱, xbuta ha̱mba̱ga̱ muu nii gata ndaabwa. Haruwa na Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwaa ha̱mba̱ga̱ncin ma pinsan ninhin nii gata ndaabwa, ga̱hin taa ta-ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ maa yaan pinsan ndaabwa.
Na hura̱gi hyo̱ tashi, maribi ma, ta̱ruba̱ ta̱ta ta̱ta̱n unpin hyo̱ da̱nda̱.
Ala̱masiihu shani ma hunranhunran na ta̱gumunu. xTa̱ba ta̱gumunu ta̱huri kai na̱ nꞌgata nꞌniinhin, na̱ wana kunnu ta abaa nꞌgani ma ishi ri ka̱ kuhunranhunran na ta̱gumunu, inaa gooda̱ga̱ Hwe̱n koya̱ ha̱ni.
Mazama nama Ala̱masiihu xmacibi nga̱nga̱nda̱ na̱ ame̱ ninhin hiku, inaa ga̱gaagana aya̱na̱nhin, inaa makoota̱ga̱ na̱ hyo̱ ta̱bita̱riga paaku tanaa zhinyaan zha̱a̱ na Zaabura na̱ koya̱ zha̱a̱ na ta̱yaba Hwe̱n. Inaa ndaga kunnu ma gooda̱ga̱ wuun hyo̱ nii gata niinhin.
Hyo̱ iri na ga̱hin nda, koo ga̱hin cita̱, inje̱ wuun wana Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu, inaa gooda̱ga̱ Ada Hwe̱n waabe̱.
Hunranhunran na zumaa na awyatu na Yeesu
Ga̱hin aꞌa̱ na ta̱wya̱ri, pana ma suhyu suniinhin kusuwya̱rugoohin wana umagii kana shi ana Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu.
Ga̱hin suwya̱rugoo, ruba̱ ma aꞌa̱ niinhin, ta-naa ndaaka ma wyan iri na zumaancin.
Ga̱hin mꞌmwaan, jwara̱ga ma mazama nama anaa ma̱ncin ma na̱ koya̱ yo̱n wana iri na Hwe̱n bwa huri nu ta̱ruba̱.
Ga̱hin sushoo, ta-naa koota̱ga̱ ma muu na̱ iri na huri kai ndaaba wana hyan ta-kusa ma muu runrun.
Ga̱hin agyama, koo buya̱ xbujwara̱ga mazama nama butu ndaabwa naa ina naa sa̱ra̱ri yana na̱ koya̱ yo̱n, xuta sha kuna yishe ta̱ndaya, haku awyatu na hiin caanhina wyatu me̱. Naa nda ma nii gata ka̱ na̱ wana icina̱ni Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu.
Hyo̱ iri na ga̱hin nda, naa nda ma wuun ame̱ hoo na ta̱hyan inii ndaaka Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu tuma shici wana awyatu wuma.
Yansun ma ta̱hyan buna̱maa pana ma ta̱taa ta̱niinhin nata̱ ga̱hin hya̱su nata̱ shi funa̱ ninhin, na ta̱hyan Butu O̱to̱ Ala̱masiihu ta ga̱hin ndaaka tuma.
Bunaa nii nda tuma na we̱ Hwe̱n nii funa̱ be̱ na̱ iri na tuma na bwa nje̱, ubwa zwa̱rici koo butu.

Ga̱hin awyatu na ina na hya̱ agyama, inaa ndaaka wyan ri na zumaa, wana iyan ta̱hyan ga̱hin taa iꞌmꞌbaa Butu O̱to̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.
Sha̱a̱ ma hyuhyu ninhin ki na̱ ro̱pe̱ ta̱naa nda, inaa zhimbaa na̱ nꞌta̱gooda̱ Hwe̱n.
Ga̱tu taa, xta̱ndaaki ma ro̱pe̱, na hyan Hwe̱n ta̱guna̱a̱nyin adubo na hyan ta̱bisa̱gi mazama mandaabwa, ta̱cici ashe̱re̱ ana shi ana Ala̱masiihu, wana ndaaba ta ga̱n kadagi.
Nda ma ro̱pe̱ na hyan ma bisa̱ga̱ muu ki haruwa na shi ma nda muu.
Naa nda ma ujabagu ninhin na̱ nꞌta̱bita̱riga kuꞌana pa̱ncin nꞌgata ku-Yeesu, inaa gura̱a̱ nda tuma na̱ koya̱ ha̱ba̱ na de̱be̱.
Koya̱ ha̱ni mazama maniinhin xmashi nama zumaa, mashi nama swaanre̱n ta̱shiraga, wana hyan iyansun haruwa na ga̱hin rana koo buya̱.
Azumanu ana ta̱makwaakaa
Nꞌkáji Tikikusu wunhin wana hyan iyansun kuga̱tu ne̱e̱. Bwa taa shi buya̱tu naa ga̱tu mata̱ni na̱a̱ bwa, bunaa pa̱ni ame̱ ndaabwa na̱ ga̱mi na̱ nꞌta̱naa nda tuma na Hwe̱n huku na̱ ga̱mi.
Buna̱maa bisa̱ ma hyo̱ iri na ga̱tu ne̱e̱ pina na̱ bwa bugura̱a̱ maa duwa̱ni maa gata ta̱taa shita̱.
Bunii máce̱e̱ huku na̱ Oniisimusu buya̱tu nda̱a̱tu naa ga̱tu mata̱ni na̱a̱ bwa, buya̱na̱a̱nhin. Ana̱maa bisa̱ga̱ ma hyo̱ komba̱ri na nii nda pina.
Arisitarakusu, bunaa ga̱tu kadagi da̱nda̱ buuzúmani ma, kunnu taa Marukusu buya̱na̱ naa Bara̱naba kuta̱ma̱ncin. Bwa ta aba tahoo maa ndaaka ma mazama mandaabwa, kuuwuce pita wunhin ira̱a̱ bwa nꞌara nꞌree.
Jooshuwa bunaa ba ta nꞌgana Yusutusu buna̱maa zúmaani ma. Awyatu yata taatu kaba ta shi Ayaahudiya ana pa̱ni nꞌgata ana nii nda tuma na ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n na̱ ga̱mi, aba tashi ana taꞌnꞌra̱ma̱nhina̱a̱ gata.
Abafarasu buya̱na̱a̱nhin, bugyama naa Ala̱masiihu Yeesu buuzúmani ma. Koya̱ hwe̱n buta na mapa dibi na̱ ro̱pe̱ wana ninhin. Bunaa rupa Hwe̱n ta̱hyan xuupa̱ ma ta̱kai na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌinsan hiku, na hyan ihumuni suhyu suniinhin, ijwara̱ga ki ta̱sha̱a̱ nata̱ Hwe̱n.
Mꞌmanda̱ya̱a̱gi na̱ ayishe nimi kuubwaa ndaaka ma tuma ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ awyatu na Yeesu ana Lawudikiya na̱ ana Hirafoolisu.
Luka na shi likita yata na ga̱tu ribi ki na̱ Demasu aazúmani ma.
Nꞌzumaanyin ma aya̱too ana Lawudikiya. Nꞌzumaanyin ma Nimfa na̱ ana Yeesu na ta mawuna̱na̱ na̱ ina nde̱e̱be̱.
Ha̱ni na abaa cita̱ga̱ni ma utakaada na̱nna, xagura̱a̱ cita̱ga̱ wuun kawyatu na Yeesu ana Lawudikiya. Ga̱hin taa ira̱a̱ una Alawudikiya, aacita̱ga̱ni ma.
Bisa̱ ma Akipusu xbumaka̱nta̱ni buciga̱hini utuma yata na Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwa pa̱ni bwa.
Ga̱n Bulusu ta ta̱gi azumanu na̱nna na̱ ara nimi. Ta-haasana ma ta̱hyan nꞌkadagi na̱ zhaaro.
xUhwe̱n pa̱ni ma ta̱pana ꞌye̱n ta̱ndaabwa ta̱naa huku na̱ ga̱hin.
TIT - Pangu
Taitusu
Tait
Taitusu
Takaada na Bulusu bwa ta̱gi zhagu paaku Taitusu
Takaada na Bulusu bwa ta̱gi zhagu paaku
Taitusu
Iri na ta̱yansun na yigo
Butumashini Bulusu taa ta̱gi takaada na̱nna zhagu kubutu ndaabwa naa tuma da̱nda̱ Taitusu, bunaa hunrani na̱ cibiri na Kiriiti. Atagáa bwa piree wana hyan xbugwataga utuma na wyatu na Yeesu ana ne̱e̱ kaun. Ubwa takaada tanda mazama nama iri taatu.
Bulusu tatamanrinyan Taitusu iri na ahari na hyan awyatu o̱to̱ na awyatu na Yeesu mꞌbaa. xUta sha iri na ahari ana uwa̱ na awyatu na Kiriiti aba mꞌbaa. Na jwárige̱ wuun ta shi, haruwa na Taitusu bwaa naa ga̱gaagana awyatu nꞌgudu nꞌgudu, ana ja̱a̱ kusa anaa ga̱gaagana mꞌmwaan na nꞌwuci. Aba gura̱a̱ pa bwa mazama ta̱hyan, xbugura̱a̱ ga̱gaagana haruwa na ujabagu una awyatu na Yeesu, na shi hunranhunran na ta̱gumunu, amaribi, aga̱a̱ ta̱naa mahoosa̱ga̱ga̱ kaba kaba, na̱ kuda̱ga na za hyuhyu.
Iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱
Azumanu :1-4Awyatu o̱to̱ na awyatu na Yeesu :5-16Tuma na nꞌgudu na nꞌwyatu na Yeesu :1-15Ta̱basa na̱ nꞌta̱koota̱ :1-11Ta̱makwaakaa :12-15
Azumanu
Takaada na̱nna shi na báni kuga̱n Bulusu, bugyama naa Hwe̱n na̱ butumashini naa Ala̱masiihu Yeesu. Hwe̱n tahoo nꞌkasa, ubwa nꞌka̱ji ma guna̱ ana pa̱ni nꞌgata, ana Hwe̱n bwa takasa, maꞌiya wyan kuta̱ga̱gaagana ki, na hyan anje̱ jabagu na Hwe̱n bwa ribi.
Uya̱nu ta nii shana wyan tasha̱a̱ nꞌgata kubina̱ na mahwa. Hwe̱n tanda ala̱ka̱wa̱ri ndaabwa hasaa, una a̱cii nda ta̱be̱.
Bwa ba̱nriin mazama mandaabwa ha̱ni na bwa ribi, paaku mazama mandaabwa ta̱cita̱ga̱ nama bwa mꞌpa̱ni. Hwe̱n bunaa ta̱mbiha̱ni bwa nꞌta̱, ma bisa̱ga̱ wyatu muu.
Zhagu paaku Taitusu, baa buniimi naa mahanda paakii gata nda̱a̱tu ta̱pana. Uhwe̱n Ada na̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu bunaa ta̱mbiha̱ni, xaapa̱ni ta̱pana ꞌye̱n na̱ hunranhunran na ta̱gumunu.
Tuma na Taitusu na̱ Kiriiti
Na̱nna ta shani ga̱mii gáa na̱ cibiri na Kiriiti na̱ wana u-a̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni iri hwarapi kaun. U-ciba̱gi awyatu o̱to̱ na awyatu na Yeesu na̱ koya̱ ce̱pe̱ haruwa na ga̱mii ga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni.
Koo buya̱ butu o̱to̱ xbushi naa za yaan randa kaꞌuba̱ na wyatu, xbushi bunaa mꞌbaa buꞌa̱ ka̱, xmꞌmwaan ndaabwa nꞌshi na mꞌpa̱ni nꞌgata ndaaba ki-Yeesu, ana aba hincin anje̱ iyaanyini na zumaancin, koo na hwashe̱.
xBubwa butu shi bunaa gwatagi ki awyatu na Yeesu, bugwataga iri na aba pa̱ni be̱ ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ ki na̱ wana Hwe̱n. xBushi naa abaa yaba, shii bunaa mꞌbaa ruwashi, koo bunaa ta gura me̱ kunrun, koo busowa̱, koo butu na gagu, koo bunaa ta ꞌwarubana ayuwa ma̱.
xBushi bunaa ta raa agai nꞌara ree, bunaa ta ruba̱ iri na bina̱, bunaa kota̱ni hyuhyu ndaabwa, bunaa ta̱to̱n, bunaa wa̱shi Hwe̱n, bunaa ta nda ri na bina̱.
xBushi bunaa ha̱mba̱gi mꞌba mazama ki nama aba ga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni be̱, hara̱ buguni ayaan ajwara̱ga ta̱ba ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ ta̱to̱n, buꞌa̱sa̱ga̱a̱gi ayaan ana ribici tuun paaka ba wa̱jiga̱a̱ ajwara̱ga ki haruwa na mꞌba shi.
Ane̱e̱ ana tibici mazama, ana nii cita̱ga̱ mazama nama uwa̱, haku ayata ana hin ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ u-ꞌya̱pi ta̱wya̱ri gaa hiin da̱ba bina̱ na mahwa.
Ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ ahin wyan hana na̱ wana anii jabaga nꞌina ina ma ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱a̱ wyatu na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ magiici wana ta̱ꞌwarubana ayuwa ma̱.
Koo Bukiriiti ndaaba ka̱, bunaa shi buwa butahoo hyan, <<Awyatu na Kiriiti ashi apunsun na awyatu, akuta̱ma̱ na gagu, arinda, ana ma̱a̱ sucicoko.>>
Haruwa na bwa cici shi mahanda. Wana kunnu, naa ndaaka wyan gagu haruwa na baa gaa ta̱shiraga ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ ta̱be̱, xashi ana ta̱hiku paaku ta̱jwara̱ga Hwe̱n.
xAga̱a̱ ta̱naa shiraaga aca̱a̱sa̱ ca̱a̱sa̱ na Ayaahudiya koo nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌawyatu ana ga̱a̱ mahanda.
Kawyatu ana nꞌgata na mꞌbure, hyo̱ iri shi na bure, ama kana nꞌgata na nꞌwe̱ ana pa̱ncin gata iri za na bure na ne̱e̱ huku na̱ aba. Nꞌgata nꞌndaaba nꞌshi na nꞌwi, aba yancin iri na zumaa koo na zumaancin.
Aba hin aba yan Hwe̱n, ama aba ga̱a̱ wuun paaku jabagu ndaaba. Ashi ana yinzhin, ana nga̱zhin, aza bina̱ koo ge̱ paaku tuma na bina̱.

Ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ ta̱to̱n
Gaa Taitusu, naa bisa̱a̱ga̱ wyatu haruwa na abaa nda jabagu na ne̱e̱ to̱n nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana.
Ga̱gaagana awyatu wya̱ri ana hoo naa masha̱a̱ xakota̱ni suhyu sundaaba, ana gii xapa̱ wyan hunrun. xAhunraana anaa za̱nda̱ ana bina̱, ana iri nii gata ta̱pana na̱ nꞌta̱ruba̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌisa hiku.
Kunnu mayaan, ga̱gaagana aꞌa̱ ana hoo naa masha̱a̱ xashi ana nii nda jabagu ndaaba na̱ nꞌta̱cina̱na̱ Hwe̱n. xAtasha ana tanaa ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ ayaan ruzha̱a̱ koo asowa̱, ashi ana nii naa ga̱gaagana ayaan iri na bina̱.
xAga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni aꞌa̱ na njeke aribi suwya̱rugooba na̱ mꞌmwaan ndaaba.
xAshi ana kota̱ni suhyu sundaaba, ana mape̱e̱n kubanshaun ta̱naa nda, anaa nda tuma na ina ndaaba ki, ana pa̱ni suhyu sundaaba kusuwya̱rugooba, wana hyan xayaan ta naa cwaaga mazama nama Hwe̱n.
Kunnu mayaan, naa koota̱ga̱ asa̱mba̱ri kota̱ni suhyu sundaaba.
Gaa taa, kiri hyo̱ u-shi bunaa abaa jwara̱ga wana tuma na bina̱ na gaa nda. Ga̱gaagana wyan na̱ nꞌta̱pa zha̱munkun hiku na̱ mꞌmahanda,
u-yansun nu ndaa na̱ mazama nama ta̱to̱n nama za ta̱cwaa, wana hyan ana ta̱nribici ahange̱ nꞌkogi, aba jaa da̱ba iri na ta̱cita̱ nda̱tu.
Ga̱gaagana agyama xatibi awyatu ndaaba na ina mazama ki na̱ koya̱ tuma, acaanhini wyan sume̱. Shici anaa maga̱a̱ga̱nu mazama na̱ aba,
xata naa ndaakaka wyan zumba̱. xAshi ana awyatu ndaaba na ina aba ta ha̱nga gama ndaaba, ata̱zhiga̱ni nꞌgata na̱ aba, na hyan ayaan nda̱i gama nama mazama nama Hwe̱n una ta̱mbiha̱ni.
Nda kunnu wana Hwe̱n ba̱nriin ta̱pana ꞌye̱n ta̱ndaabwa nata̱ íye̱ ta̱biha̱na̱ kawyatu hyo̱.
-13 Hwe̱n nii ta̱nga̱gaagana ta̱hyan xta̱nga̱a̱ ta̱jwara̱ga hari na shici andaabwa na̱ yaanyini na zumaancin na sa̱ra̱ri yana. Na̱ ha̱ni na ga̱tun ha̱mbagi nii gata ta̱sha̱a̱ hiku kuhwe̱n ya̱nu na ta̱ga̱da̱ri na Yeesu be̱e̱ kúshe̱, xta̱nje̱ hunranhunran na̱ ha̱ni yana una ta̱makota̱na̱ hyuhyu na̱ ta̱to̱n na̱ Hwe̱n ta̱jwara̱ga. Hwe̱n ya̱nu ta shi na ta̱banrinyan nata̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ nata̱ Hwe̱n nda̱tu na yaburi bunaa ta̱mbiha̱ni. Be̱ taa shi Ala̱masiihu Yeesu,
binaa tapana ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabwa ꞌye̱n na̱ wana nda̱tu, bunaa tata̱nraa kukoya̱ iri na pinsan, bwa gura̱a̱ shana ga̱tu shi andaabwa ana ta̱sabu, ana za mꞌpirwa ta̱ruba̱ ta̱nda tuma na bina̱.
Naa ga̱gaagana ana pa̱ni nꞌgata iri ya̱nu, uzumaa u-naa taga wyan nꞌshita̱, u-naa yinzhinkakana wyan na̱ hyo̱ ta̱kai. Ta-hakata buyaan buuhwashe̱.

Nda ri na zumaa
Naa tamanrinyaan ana pa̱ni nꞌgata xapa̱ni suhyu sundaaba kawyatu o̱to̱ na ta̱gwama na ce̱nye̱n, ashi ana jwarigi, ana nje̱ shiri na ta̱nda hyo̱ iri na zumaa.
xAta naa ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ buyaan ruzha̱a̱, xaga̱a̱ ta̱naa ndaga kuda̱ga na̱ awyatu, aꞌye̱e̱ koo buya̱ shukuu.
Ga̱tu maa na̱ ayigo ta̱tasha nꞌguzha̱ni, ga̱tu tantibici mazama. Aba ta̱mpiri, ga̱tun shi agyama na ta̱ruba̱ iri hwarapi na sa̱ra̱ri yana ina ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ba ribi. Ga̱tu nje̱ hunranhunran na ambyau na̱ mꞌmaꞌwe̱n, ga̱tu tamaribici.
Ama ha̱ni na Hwe̱n na ta̱mbiha̱ni bwa bisa̱a̱ ta̱pana ꞌye̱n, bwa ba̱nriin ta̱ruba̱ ta̱ndaabwa kunga̱tu.
Utata̱mbiha̱na̱ shici wana yaan tuma na ta̱to̱n na ga̱tun nje̱, ama wana ambishiri ndaabwa. Uta̱mbiha̱ni paaku ta̱ha̱mbaraga pinsan nda̱tu na̱ nꞌta̱ma̱ncin nata̱ fo paakii Hwaanwun ndaabwa,
binaa bwa ta̱nzóogi o̱to̱ paaki Ala̱masiihu Yeesu bunaa ta̱mbiha̱ni.
Wana kunnu ta Hwe̱n bwa ta̱ndaya ta̱shi ana za randa kaꞌuba̱ ndaabwa wana ta̱pana ꞌye̱n ta̱ndaabwa, ga̱tu gura̱a̱ sha awyatu na nii hya̱su bina̱ na mahwa.
Ta̱cita̱ ta̱ya̱nu ta̱shi mahanda. Ga̱n ribi u-maha̱mba̱ga̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱ya̱nu ki wana hyan ana pa̱ni nꞌgata ku-Yeesu apa̱ yima̱a̱ paaku ta̱nda ri na zumaa. Ta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱ya̱nu ta̱zumaa, ta̱ba nii ndaaka koo buya̱ bina̱.
Gaa, mape̱e̱n paaku mazama nama ta̱guzha̱n na shi azha̱a̱zha̱a̱ na daadoo na̱ nꞌta̱hiika̱hina̱ gagu na̱ kuda̱ga na za yaan bina̱ na Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa, tuma na uwa̱ ta bwa shi ꞌye̱n.
Kawyatu na̱maa iyaagagi ta̱mahoosa̱ga̱ga̱, hyan wyan hana maka̱ koo mareeko. Kanii nda ji, u-mahooshi na̱ aba.
Bi-yan da̱i ta̱hyan ashi ana ka̱shi kuyo̱n na ta̱to̱n, ana apinsan ndaaba aba bisa̱a̱ iri na ba shi.
Azumanu na ta̱makwaakaa
Ha̱ni na ga̱mii kádaagi Aritimasu koo Tikikusu sa̱i u-nje̱ haruwa na gaa ara ta̱nda u-jaa wa̱ka̱mi na̱ ce̱pe̱ na Nikapolisu wana ga̱n ribi jira kaun.
Nda haruwa na gaa ara ta̱nda u-de̱e̱be̱ Ziinasu ulooya yata na̱ Afolosu xkota̱ni yo̱n u-yansun ta̱hyan aꞌmꞌbaa hyo̱ iri na aba ribi.
Awyatu nda̱tu ushi ga̱ga̱ga̱ aꞌa̱ri ta̱naa nda tuma na bina̱, wana hyan aguni ana iri be̱ mbooni. Kanii ndaga kunnu anje̱ jabagu na bina̱.
Hyo̱ awyatu na ne̱e̱ na̱ ga̱mi aazúmani. Kusu, nꞌzumaanyin hyo̱ ana pa̱ni nꞌgata ana ta̱nribi kaun.
Ta̱pana ꞌye̱n nata̱ Hwe̱n xta̱naa na̱ ga̱hin hyo̱.
PHM - Pangu
Filimo
Fil
Filimo
Takaada na Bulusu bwa ta̱gi zhagu paaku Filimo
Takaada na Bulusu bwa ta̱gi zhagu paaku
Filimo
Iri na ta̱yansun na yigo
Filimo shi butu naa jwarigi Yeesu hiku, bwa shi butu naa ne̱e̱ na̱ awyatu na Yeesu na̱ Koloosi. Bwa mꞌbaa bugyama naa aba ta hyan Oniisimusu. Bwaa gyama butagida̱ga̱, bwa ga̱a̱ butu naa ina ndaabwa, sa̱i bwa ura̱ku na̱ Bulusu bunaa tanaa na̱ zhaaro. Na̱ wana Bulusu, Oniisimusu bwa jwarigi Yeesu. Una̱nna takaada na zhagu paaku Filimo ushi na ta̱rupa be̱, xamaꞌa̱sa̱a̱ga̱ni na̱ Oniisimusu bugyama ndaabwa. Bunaa Bulusu bwa tapana takaada na ta̱kushihina bwa, bura̱a̱ be̱, shii haku gyama, ama buya̱na̱ kiigata ta̱pana ki-Yeesu.
Iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱
Azumanu -3 Ta̱yabana Hwe̱n na̱ wana Filimo -7 Ta̱rupa wana Oniisimusu -22 Ta̱hakana -25
Azumanu
Takaada na̱nna shi na báni kuga̱n Bulusu, bunaa bwake̱ na̱ zhaaro na̱ wana nꞌnii bisa̱ga̱ wyatu mazama nama zumaa nama Ala̱masiihu Yeesu. Ubwa gura̱a̱ sha na báni kuuya̱tu nda̱a̱tu Timooti.
Zhagu paaku Filimo bushikaa nda̱a̱tu naa ga̱tu ribi, na̱ bushikaa naa tuma,
na̱ buya̱tu naa a̱ Afiya, na̱ Akipusu buya̱tu nda̱a̱tu naa ga̱tu ma pa dibi huku na̱a̱ bwa, na̱ hyo̱ awyatu na Yeesu ana ta mawuna̱na̱ na̱ ina ndaa.
Ta̱pana ꞌye̱n na̱ hunranhunran na̱ nꞌta̱gumunu ku-Hwe̱n Ada nda̱tu na̱ Butu O̱to̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu xta̱naa huku na̱ ga̱hin.
Ta̱ruba̱ na̱ nꞌta̱panaa gata nata̱ Filimo
Filimo, ga̱n ta gooda̱ Hwe̱n koya̱ ha̱ni na ga̱n na̱maa ndaaka ro̱pe̱,
wana haruwa na ga̱n hange̱ bi-pa̱nii gata paa Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu na̱ haruwa na gaa ribi hyo̱ awyatu na Hwe̱n.
Ga̱n ne̱e̱ na̱ ro̱pe̱ wana ta̱hyan bi-nii nda tuma na ta̱naawan huku nata̱ báni kuta̱panaa gata ndaabi wana ta̱hyan unii duwa̱na̱ ta̱ꞌinsan hiku nata̱ koya̱ ri na gama na ga̱tu mꞌbaa paaku Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Buya̱tu, ta̱ruba̱ ta̱ndaabi ta̱ꞌnꞌcaanhini me̱, ta̱ba nꞌduwa̱ni bishita̱ ta̱ta ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ na̱ wana gaa ta awyatu na Hwe̱n aba duwa̱ni ta̱kai.
Bulusu ro̱pe̱ wana Oniisimusu
Wana kunnu, haruwa na ga̱n shi ayami naa o̱to̱ ku-Ala̱masiihu, ga̱n nii ara ta̱nda ta̱butu wya̱ri iihin, nda iri na ne̱e̱ to̱n.
Ama wana iiribi, ta ga̱n huri ta̱ruba̱, iiro̱pe̱. Ga̱n Bulusu, ga̱n shi butu naa ange̱ naa ne̱e̱ na̱ zhaaro na̱ wana Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Iiro̱pe̱, wana baa buniimi Oniisimusu, naa ga̱n tashici ashin, niina ga̱n shi ashin paakii gata ta̱pana, ga̱n na̱ zhaaro.
Na yigo buna shici bunaa bina̱ wakaa, ama niina bushi naa bina̱ wakaa na̱ wa̱ka̱mi+ :11: Oniisimusu ta shi bunaa bina̱ n-Ta̱helena.Ga̱n nii kúshihine̱ be̱ wakaa, bunaa ne̱e̱ nii gata nimi.
Niina na ga̱n zwagani na̱ zhaaro na̱ wana mazama nama zumaa, ga̱n taruba̱ bunaa huku na̱ ga̱mi wana hyan bunaa ndaaka tuma haku gaa tanii nama nꞌndaaka gaa tane̱e̱ pina.
Ama nꞌribici ma nda yaanyini na shici nꞌtaruba̱ ta̱ndaabi, na̱ wana hyo̱ iri na gaa hiin nꞌndaaka xishi nꞌta̱ruba̱ ta̱ndaabi, nꞌribici ta̱nda yaanyini na gaa ribici.
Ta̱mahoosa̱ nata̱ Oniisimusu bwa mahooshi na̱ gaa ta̱shi nata̱a̱ ke̱nye̱n ge̱ ma ja̱a̱ ara ta̱sha jaa kuu-gura̱a̱ raa be̱ ta̱jaa shi nata̱ mahwa.
Shii ta̱hyan bushii gyama mayaan, ama buhuri kunnu, xbushi ayami na gaa ribi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ku-Ala̱masiihu. Ga̱n ribi be̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, kugaa naazhin? Bi-nii ruba̱ be̱ uhuri, haruwa na bwa shi bugyama bunaa pa̱nii gata paaku Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu.
Too, kuga̱n shi bushikaa ndaabi naa tuma, sa̱i u-ra̱a̱ be̱ nge̱n kugaa nꞌra̱a̱ ga̱mi.
Kushi ta̱hyan Oniisimusu ndaaki pinsan koo bwa ha̱mba̱gi yaan ꞌwaa ndaa, nꞌga̱a̱gi muu.
Ga̱n Bulusu ta nii taga na̱ ara nimi ta̱hyan, ga̱n na̱maa ndupa. Ta-haasana na̱ hyuhyu ndaa na gaa de̱be̱ wa̱ka̱mi.
Buya̱tu, na̱ wana kunnu nꞌndaaki ri ya̱nu wana Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu. Nꞌduwa̱nii shita̱ na̱ wana ta̱naawan ta̱nda̱a̱tu na̱ Ala̱masiihu.
Ga̱n shii bigata ki ta̱hyan, bi-nii nda iri na ga̱mii ro̱pe̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌyantan nata̱ ga̱n ta̱gi na̱ takaada na̱nna. Ga̱n yan bi-nii nda na huri na̱nna.
Na̱ ha̱ni ka̱ mayaan, nꞌa̱sa̱ga̱a̱gi dura̱ na ga̱n jaa ma ta̱na, wana ga̱n shii me̱ ta̱hyan, Hwe̱n nii rana ro̱pe̱ ninhin uꞌnꞌkúshihine̱ wunhin.
Azumanu na ta̱makwaakaa
Abafarasu, bunaa ne̱e̱ na̱ zhaaro na̱ ga̱mi na̱ wana bupa̱nii gata ku-Ala̱masiihu Yeesu buu kádaagi ma azumanu,
kunta taa ta̱shika ta̱niimi paaku tuma Marukusu, Arisitarakusu, Demasu na̱ Luka.
Ta̱pana ꞌye̱n nata̱ Butu O̱to̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, xta̱naa huku na̱ ga̱hin hyo̱.
JAS - Pangu
Yaakubu
Yaak
Yaakubu
Takaada na Yaakubu bwa ta̱gi
Takaada na
Yaakubu
bwa ta̱gi
Iri na ta̱yansun
Yaakubu bunaa ta̱gi takaada na̱nna. Ane̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan, butataga wuun na̱ nꞌyo̱ handa na̱ nꞌta zhagu kuje ta na̱ nꞌta̱mantan na̱ta̱ Yeesu. Na̱ takaada na mazama nama fo, awyatu na̱nshin ta mꞌbaa ruzha̱a̱ naru Yaakubu. Ama na aba gwataagani ki, aba nda̱i ta̱hyan Yaakubu buya̱na̱a̱ naa Yeesu taa shi naa ta̱gi utakaada na̱nna.
Na̱nna Yaakubu goo bwa ne̱e̱ na̱ Yaakubu be̱e̱ binaa Zabadi bunaa shii ka̱ kaꞌupwa na ree ana Yeesu be̱ tazwara, bunaa Hirudu bwa takuna na̱ nꞌyo̱ handa na̱ nꞌna̱nshin na̱ nꞌta̱mantan nata̱ Yeesu. Yaakubu na̱nna tasha butu o̱to̱ naa ana jwarigi Yeesu na̱ Hurushaliima, bunaa aba takuna na̱ nꞌyo̱ kuje cininhin na̱ nꞌna̱nshin na̱ nꞌta̱mantan nata̱ Yeesu.
Una̱nna takaada na Yaakubu unii ta̱ga̱gaagana haruwa na hyan ujabagu nda̱tu naa, na koya̱ ha̱ni. Yaakubu tabisa̱a̱ na̱ takaada na̱nna ta̱hyan, ta̱pana bigata ta shi ta̱nda tuma na bina̱. Bwa gura̱a̱ ta̱ga̱gaagana haruwa na tuma na ta̱pana bigata naa bina̱ be̱ ta mantan ahari na̱ tuma na bina̱. Bwa gura̱a̱ ta̱koota̱ haruwa na ta̱naa hura̱hina̱ ure̱ntun nda̱tu na̱ koo ta̱maanwyana ta̱ta ta̱de̱be̱, xta̱ta yaaciga ame̱, ta̱ga̱a̱ iri na bina̱ na ga̱tu nda. Hyo̱ ana jwarigi xaꞌisa sa̱ hiku na̱ ro̱pe̱ koya̱ ha̱ni xata rukuta̱. Aga̱a̱ ta̱sha ta̱shika na̱ ri na sa̱ra̱ri yana, wana bunaa shi ta̱shika na̱ iri na sa̱ra̱ri yana, Hwe̱n a̱cii maꞌunso̱n na̱a̱ bwa.
Iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱
Azumanu :1Ta̱panaa gata na̱ nꞌta̱yansun :2-8Ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa ri na̱ ꞌwa̱ta̱gi :9-11Ungwan na̱ nꞌta̱maanwyana :12-18Ta̱tuba̱ na̱ nꞌta̱nda tuma mꞌmazama nama Hwe̱n :19-27Ta̱koota̱ga̱ nata̱ ta̱bisa̱a̱ga̱ ta̱goo goo :1-13Ta̱panaa gata na̱ tuma ta̱nda :14-26Bunaa jwarigi na̱ nꞌta̱naa hura̱hina̱ ure̱ntun ndaabwa :1-18Ta̱sha ta̱shika na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana :1--5:6Ta̱yaan ta̱koota̱ga̱ :7-20
Ga̱n Yaakubu, bugyama naa Hwe̱n na̱a̱ naa Butu O̱to̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu. Zhagu kuꞌnꞌkorogo nꞌupwa na̱ nꞌree ana ne̱e̱ katakata kope na̱ sa̱ra̱ri. Iizumani ma.
Ta̱panaa gata // na̱ nꞌta̱bita̱riga
Aya̱too ma ana Ala̱masiihu, koya̱ ta̱maanwyana ta̱niinhin nata̱ ta̱swa ta̱guma nata̱a̱ de̱be̱ ma xta̱shi iri na ta̱ga̱da̱ri,
na̱ wana iyan ushi ta̱ꞌinsan ta̱ta ku-Hwe̱n, kuga̱hin pa̱ni nꞌgata ki-Yeesu hyan iduwa̱ni akuri.
Hakata ma akuri yata aaciga̱hinini ma tuma ndaaba na̱ wana aashaani ma ishi ana mahumuni suhyu sundaaba hiku, iꞌmꞌbaa komba̱ri.
Kuuyaan buribi ta̱sha bunaa be̱te̱re̱ge̱, xbunaa rupa Hwe̱n. Bwa taa shi bunaa ta̱tazhigaaga koo buya̱ ꞌye̱n, bwa jaa nda ruwashi, ubwa nii pana be̱.
Ama xburo̱pe̱ Hwe̱n nii gata ka̱, shii na̱ nꞌgata nꞌreeko, na̱ wana hyo̱ bunaa shiici gata ka̱ bushi haku ta na ma̱ni, pyara bwaa bibika̱ka̱ wuun koo biya̱ biin.
Butu yata xbuta sha̱a̱ ta̱hyan bunii da̱ba yaan ri ku-Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n,
wana bushi naa mꞌbaa maree maree, bwa a̱cii sha̱a̱ bigata ndaabwa bikoo ka̱.
Buya̱tu naa ne̱e̱ na̱ ꞌwa̱ta̱gi xbunje̱ ta̱ga̱da̱ri ta̱hyan Hwe̱n ta sha̱pa̱cigi be̱.
Kunta taa maa bunaa mꞌbaa iri xbunje̱ ta̱ga̱da̱ri ta̱hyan Hwe̱n ta ciinha̱ni be̱ na̱ wana bunii mahooga̱a̱ga̱ haku ta̱sumu nata̱ mꞌba̱ba.
Uhwe̱n ta he̱e̱n ubáni uta̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, ushaani mꞌba̱ba nꞌhoogi, ta̱sumu nata̱ mꞌba ta̱ke̱ne̱, gama na ta̱ba ufogi. Kunta taa bunaa mꞌbaa ri bwa nii mahooga̱a̱ga̱ kuwyanzun ndaabwa.
Ngwan // na̱ nꞌta̱maanwyana
Hwe̱n nii ndaaka butu naa nje̱ akuri na̱ nꞌta̱maanwyana ta̱ndaabwa rubara̱ka, na̱ wana bunii raa funa̱ na ta̱bina̱ mahwa una Hwe̱n bwa tanda ala̱ka̱wa̱ri ta̱hyan unii pana ana ribi wuun.
Kuta̱maanwyana nata̱ nii shana butu bwa hiin nda pinsan ta̱bicigi bwa, xbuta hyan Hwe̱n ta shani. Na̱ wana Hwe̱n a̱cii maanwyana koo buya̱ xbunje̱ ri na zumaancin. Majaa gura̱a̱ nda ama̱a̱nwya̱ni wuun na̱ mꞌmaꞌwe̱n.
Koo buya̱ butu xbuta maꞌiya kuta̱maanwyana ha̱ni na bwa ma̱a̱ ta̱ruba̱ iri na we̱ nii gata ndaabwa, ibe̱ ma̱ni be̱ kupinsan ta̱nda.
Ha̱ni na ta̱ruba̱ ri ta̱ba ma̱a̱ ta̱ba cigi huba̱, ta̱ta mantan pinsan. Pinsan taa kunje̱ o̱to̱, uta mantan ta̱ꞌwa̱.
Aya̱too nimi na ga̱n ribi, xataa pira̱ ma.
Hyo̱ iri na zumaa ibe̱ ne̱e̱ hiku ibáni ta nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ paaka Baaba Hwe̱n na nje̱ upyanda, nꞌgwasu, hwe̱n hyo̱. Ubwa uꞌa̱cii hiriga, ubwa a̱cii ha̱nza̱ma̱na̱ haku hwe̱n na tahe̱e̱n ubáni uꞌiri.
Hwe̱n nꞌta̱ruba̱ ta̱ndaabwa, ta bwa ta̱nje̱, ga̱tu shi mꞌmwaan nꞌndaabwa paaku mazama nama bwa cici nama mahanda, na̱ wana uta̱ka̱shi ta̱shi ana hura̱gi hyo̱ kiri na bwa nje̱.
Ta̱shiraga na̱ nꞌta̱nda // ri na Hwe̱n bwa cici
Aya̱too nimi na ga̱n ribi, yansun ma ta̱hyan koo buya̱ xbushi bunaa ta̱tuba̱ na̱ ha̱ni, xbuta sha naa mazama mafaara koo bunaa biigata,
na̱ wana butu na biigata a̱cii nda iri na bina̱ na Hwe̱n bwa ribi.
Na̱ wana kunnu, munsan ma hyo̱ ri yata na zumaancin na ruhaki, na̱ koya̱ maꞌwe̱n. Raa ma mazama mayata nama aba be̱re̱ na̱ nꞌgata nꞌniinhin hiku, nama na̱maa ara ma ta̱ꞌiya kuta̱biha̱na̱.
Ta-ma pira̱ ma, inaa ha̱ngaga kuta̱ha̱ngaga mazama nama Hwe̱n ꞌye̱n, ga̱hin jaa nda muu. Na̱ kunnu sha ma ana nii nda muu.
Ama bunaa hange̱ kuta̱ha̱nga mazama bwa nje̱ce̱, bushi haku butu naa magwatani mꞌpirwa ndaabwa nii ndaya,
kuta̱naa gaa pita, iri ha̱a̱sa̱ni be̱ kuubwa ne̱e̱ mꞌpirwa.
Ama butu xbushiraga bushii aha̱nka̱ri ndaabwa paaku ta̱yansun nata̱ ta̱ga̱gaagana Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n na̱ na nꞌhura̱gi ta̱da̱ba ta̱banana. Kuuhange̱ muu, bwa nje̱ muu, bwa ha̱a̱sa̱ncin muu, anii sha̱a̱ga̱ be̱ rubara̱ka kiri na bwa nje̱.
Ta̱jwara̱ga Hwe̱n // nata̱ mahanda
Kuuyaan buhin bwaa shi naa jwarigi yo̱n na Hwe̱n ki, bwa kota̱ncin nu ndaabwa kami, bwa taa nii mapira̱. Ta̱jwara̱ga ta̱ndaabwa yo̱n na Hwe̱n ta̱shi nata̱ uwa̱.
Ta̱jwara̱ga yo̱n na Hwe̱n nata̱ hura̱gi nata̱ mahanda ta̱ba ne̱e̱ sabu nata̱ Baaba Hwe̱n bwa ribi, ta shi nda ma ambishiri na aꞌa̱ na suwya̱rugooba suba ꞌwa̱gi na̱ mꞌmwaan na nꞌza sushoo na̱ ngwan ndaaba. Igura̱a̱ mape̱e̱n kiri na ta̱shiri na sa̱ra̱ri yana.

Gaa ma ta̱naa bisa̱a̱ga̱ // ta̱hura̱
Aya̱too ma, na ga̱hin nii hyan ipa̱ni nꞌgata nꞌniinhin ku-Butu O̱to̱ nda̱a̱tu Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, bunaa hura̱gi ta̱shapaciga, ta-hura̱ ma ta̱bisa̱a̱ ta̱ruba̱ kawyatu ka̱.
Ahin buyaan butá̱ni paa ga̱hin nda ta̱mawuna̱na̱ nata̱ awyatu na jwarigi Hwe̱n, bwa bwátani bimuu binaa zinaari na̱ aꞌwana ana mꞌbaa yuwa. Buyaan buꞌwa̱ta̱gi bwa wuce na̱ aꞌwana ana ta̱ya̱bizoo.
Kiihuri ta̱pana aha̱nka̱ri kuunaa bwa̱ta̱ni aꞌwana ana yuwa o̱to̱, ga̱hin hin be̱, <<Butu na̱nna, hunrana paaka hura̱gi gama,>> ihin buꞌwa̱ta̱gi, <<Isa pita,>> koo <<U-hunrana na̱ nꞌce̱nye̱n,>>
ai, inii mabisa̱a̱ga̱ ta ta̱hura̱, na ga̱hin nje̱ ta̱suuga̱ na̱ nꞌgata na nꞌwe̱.
Too, aya̱too nimi na ga̱n ribi, ha̱nga ma. Shii ana shi aꞌwa̱ta̱gi na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana ta Hwe̱n bwa takasa ashi ana mꞌbaa iri ma̱ na̱ nꞌgata ta̱pana? Ashi ana ja̱a̱ hya̱su ta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n nata̱ bwa tanda ala̱ka̱wa̱ri ta̱hyan unii pana ana ribi wuun?
Ama ga̱hin husani buꞌwa̱ta̱gi. Shii awyatu na mꞌbaa iri ma̱ ta ta namaa pira̱ ma? Aabuburi ma zhagu paaku ta̱suuga̱?
Shii aba ta ta he̱e̱n anaa gura̱a̱ nda mazama nama hwashe̱ nama ruzha̱a̱ ruyata naru ta̱hiku naru buyata naa ga̱hin shi andaabwa?
Kiihuri ta̱jwara̱ga Nꞌgira̱nshin na mꞌbuugwama Hwe̱n na nꞌta̱ na̱ takaada ndaabwa ta̱hyan, <<U-ribi butu naa nꞌharu ndaabi haruwa na gaa ribi hyuhyu ndaa,>> kiinii nda kunnu, inje̱ to̱n.
Ama kiihuri ta̱naa ma bisa̱a̱ga̱ ta̱hura̱ kawyatu ka̱, inje̱ pinsan ga̱hin shi ana ga̱a̱ Nꞌgira̱nshin ta̱jwara̱ga.
Na ta̱hyan bunaa jwarigi hyo̱ Nꞌgira̱nshin, ama bwa jwarigici bika̱, too, buga̱a̱ ta hyo̱ Nꞌgira̱nshin ta̱jwara̱ga.
Bwaa naa hin, <<Ta-nda banshaun na̱ aꞌa̱yo yaan,>> bwa taa shi na gura̱a̱ hyan, <<Ta-kuna butu.>> Kuu-nje̱ce̱ banshaun na̱ aꞌa̱yo yaan, ama gaa kwane̱ butu, bi-shi hyo̱ butu naa ga̱a̱ Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n ta̱jwara̱ga.
Nda ma mazama maniinhin na̱ tuma ninhin na̱ yo̱n na ta̱to̱n, na̱ wana ishi ana Uhwe̱n bwa ja̱a̱ ndaaka ta̱suuga̱ na̱ nꞌgira̱nshin nꞌndaabwa na nꞌta̱da̱ba ta̱banana.
Hwe̱n jaa nda ambishiri na̱ hwe̱n na ta̱suuga̱ kubutu naa za ambishiri. Ama ambishiri na Hwe̱n tanii biha̱na̱ butu kuta̱suuga̱.
Ta̱panaa gata // nata̱ za tuma ꞌye̱n ta
Aya̱too ma, ꞌye̱n ta ubwa shi na ta̱hyan xahin butu mꞌbaa bigata ta̱pana ama iri na bwaa nda ibe̱ jaa sha na zumaa. Ta̱panaa gata yata ndaabwa ta̱ja̱a̱ biha̱na̱ be̱ da̱i?
XAhin buyaan buya̱tu naa wya̱ri koo bunaa a̱ bunaa jwarigi Yeesu buza shami na ta̱naa re̱ koya̱ hwe̱n koo da̱bi na ta̱taana na hyan unje̱ be̱ vwain.
Sa̱i buyaan buniinhin buhin be̱, <<Hura̱ gumunu, uwuci kami. Hwe̱n pa̱ o̱to̱ shami na ta̱naa re̱ na̱ aꞌwana na ta̱bwatana,>> ama bwa ndaakici bwa yaanyini na bwa ribi. Too, uyata nii ndaaka be̱ yaan tuma?
Kunnu mꞌba shi, kuu-mꞌbaa kiigata ta̱pana, gaa nje̱ce̱ tuma na bina̱, ꞌye̱n ta gaa nda.
Buyaan bunii ara buhin, <<Gaa biꞌmꞌbaa bigata ta̱pana, ga̱n ga̱n ta nda tuma na bina̱.>> Too, mꞌbisa̱a̱ bigata ta̱pana ndaabi naa za tuma na bina̱ ta̱nda, ga̱n iibisa̱a̱ bigata niimi ta̱pana paaku tuma nimi na bina̱.
Bi-ra̱ni ta̱hyan ushi mahanda ta̱hyan Uhwe̱n ka̱ ta ne̱e̱? Too, uzumaa. Koo awyatu na hira̱ ara̱ni ta̱hyan Uhwe̱n ka̱ ne̱e̱, hyo̱ nꞌta̱jikita̱ga̱.
Kai guzha̱ni! XIibisa̱a̱ uyansun ta̱hyan ta̱panaa gata nata̱ za tuma na bina̱ ta̱shi iri na uwa̱.
Mata̱ma̱nriin ma adaada nda̱tu Ibiraahin bunaa tapana buyoo Isiyaaku ku-Hwe̱n haki bikico̱ kiizhe̱nke̱n naa ta̱huunha̱na̱. Na̱ wana butanda kunnu ta Uhwe̱n bwa tayansun ta̱hyan bushi butu naa bina̱.
Too, ndaya kiigata ta̱pana ndaabwa be̱e̱ hura̱ da̱nda̱ na̱ tuma ta̱nda, bigata ta̱pana be̱ cigi hiku kutuma na bwa nje̱.
Kunnu ta mazama nama ta̱ na̱ takaada na Hwe̱n mꞌba taciga̱ ta̱hyan, <<Ibiraahin pa̱nii gata ku-Hwe̱n, Uhwe̱n bwa ta yansun bushi butu naa bina̱.>> Aba gura̱a̱ nꞌgana be̱ bushikaa naa Hwe̱n.
Ndaya ma, Uhwe̱n tayansun butu bushi butu naa bina̱ paaku tuma ndaabwa, shii kuta̱panaa gata kuta̱ba.Abraham offers his son Isaac to God|lb00291c.tif|col|JAS 2:18-24|Louise Bass|Ibiraahin tapana buyoo Isiyaaku ku-Hwe̱n |2:21Kunnu taa Rahaba̱ na tasha buꞌa̱ naa banshaun, be̱ tasoo awyatu ana tanaa gwatagana pa̱ri ta̱swee na̱ ina nde̱e̱be̱, be̱ ba̱ha̱ni wyan na̱ yaan yo̱n goo. Too, Uhwe̱n tayansun buu bishi buꞌa̱ naa bina̱ paa utuma nde̱e̱be̱.
Kunta ta ubwa shi, haku ta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ butu wuma nata̱ za nꞌhunjo̱ ta̱ba shi ruꞌwa̱, kunta ta̱panaa gata nata̱ za tuma ta̱nda na bina̱ ta̱ba shi ruꞌwa̱.

Nda ma aha̱nka̱ri // na̱ nꞌre̱ntun nꞌniinhin
Aya̱too ma, xshii ta̱hyan awyatu hwarapi ta nii ruba̱ ta̱sha ana nii ga̱gaagana mazama nama Hwe̱n, na̱ wana ga̱tu na ga̱hin nda̱i ta̱nii ga̱gaagana aja̱a̱ ta̱hura̱ ta̱ndaaka ta̱suuga̱ nata̱ hura̱gi mamboo.
Na̱ wana ta̱hyan, hyo̱ nda̱tu ta̱ta he̱e̱n ta̱wa̱jiga̱a̱ mahwarapi. Too, kuuyaan bune̱e̱ bunaa a̱cii wajigaa na̱ mꞌmazama mandaabwa, buyata bushi butu hiku, bwa maꞌa̱ri ta̱maha̱mba̱ga̱ ki.
Ta̱ta he̱e̱n ta̱ta̱ bindakwa ta̱ꞌuri na̱ nu, ushaani buu binje̱ iri na ga̱tu ribi xbinje̱, ugura̱a̱ shaana buu bihuri paa ga̱tu ribi xbihuri.
Suta̱hyan, gwatana ma kuhantun na ma̱ni na o̱to̱ ubwa tanaa hura̱ na̱ upyara na kai, hyo̱ na̱ kunnu bipa̱paaru naa ta̱naa tutumaa wuun ge̱ be̱ ne̱e̱, nii be̱ ta butu naa nii tutumaa wuun bwa ta hura̱hina̱ wuun hyo̱ paa bwa ribi uhuri.
Kunnu taa, ure̱ntun na butu ta shi iri na ta̱ge̱ kuta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaabwa, hyo̱ na̱ kunnu ubwa ta shi na ta he̱e̱n unje̱ ruwashi naru iri na yaburi.
Gwatana taa birara naa pa̱ na̱ aga ge̱, nii ara ta̱huunha̱na̱ uꞌaga hyo̱.
Kunnu taa, ure̱ntun na butu ta shi haku ra, bwa ta shi iri na we̱ kuta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ butu. Uta kuna butu mahwa, ubwa ta tahanshinhina butu mahwa kujabagu ndaabwa. Ubwa re̱ntun, paaku ra na za ta̱ꞌwa̱ga̱ ta tanaa hurupa̱ga̱na̱ wuun ce̱be̱.
Butu wuma ta swa hyuhyu na koya̱ iri na bikico̱ na aga na̱ nꞌno̱no̱, na̱ nꞌsuhwaa, na̱ bikico̱ na ma̱ni,
ama bwa zaa naa nii ara ta̱swa hyuhyu na ure̱ntun na butu. Ure̱ntun shi iri na we̱ na aba jaa ara ta̱naa hura̱hina̱, ushi iri na cigi da̱ na̱ mꞌmanwyanrin nama ta̱kuna.
Na̱ bwa ta ga̱tu ta naa yaba Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n naa shi Ada nda̱tu, na̱ bwa ta ga̱tu ta gura̱a̱ naa pagana wyatu nu. Unje̱ce̱ to̱n wana ta̱hyan Hwe̱n nje̱ koo buya̱ na̱ mꞌpirwa nꞌndaabwa.
Kuna̱ bwa nu ta ga̱tu ta naa yaba buyaan, kuna̱ bwa nu ta ga̱tu ta naa pagana ayaan nu. Ka̱i, aya̱too nimi, ma magiici na̱ kunnu.
Koo inda̱i ta̱hyan, bisa̱ci ka̱ nii ara ta̱pa ma̱ni nama ta̱swa na̱ nama mꞌbaa gagu?
Aya̱too nimi, ata gwasa ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ riga̱ kuwaanwan? Koo ata gwasa ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ waanwan kiiko̱ro̱? Majaa nda. Kunnu taa bisa̱ci naa nii zoo ma̱ni nama mꞌbaa wun be̱ jaa ara ta̱pa ma̱ni nama ta̱swa.
Ta̱bita̱riga ta̱báni ku-Hwe̱n
Iyaa ta shi naa mꞌbaa ta̱bita̱riga na̱ nꞌta̱yansun kuga̱hin? Too, sa̱i bubisa̱a̱ tuun kiꞌiri na bwaa nda ina bina̱, na̱ utuma na bwaa nda na gama una ta̱bita̱riga ta̱ndaabwa ta̱ba shani bwaa nda wuun shii nꞌta̱mashapaciga.
Ama na̱ nꞌgata nꞌniinhin, iꞌmꞌbaa ta̱we̱ ta shani ga̱hin maribici mahwa na̱ nꞌta̱hyan kuga̱n ta nꞌshi. Too, gaa ma ta̱naa makwasa ta̱hyan iꞌmꞌbaa ta̱bita̱riga, na̱ wana ta̱hyan iga̱a̱ mahanda.
Ta̱ba ta̱bita̱riga ta̱shici nata̱ cíin na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, nata̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana ta̱ta huwo. Shici na ta̱a̱ Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n, kiina Buupira̱.
Hyo̱, paa gaa nda̱i kaꞌmꞌbaa ta̱we̱ nata̱ ta̱maribici na̱ nꞌta̱hyan kuga̱n, bi-nii da̱ba kaun gagu na̱ koya̱ iri na ambyau na̱ hunranhunran na za bina̱.
Ama ta̱bita̱riga nata̱ báni ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱, na̱ ayigo ta̱shi nata̱ ne̱e̱ sabu. Ta̱ba ta gura̱a̱ shaana hunranhunran na gama, nata̱ aha̱nka̱ri, nata̱ za hyuhyu ta̱guma, ta̱ba za mꞌpirwa na̱ ambishiri, ta̱ba za mꞌpirwa ta̱ndaaka yaan iri na zumaa, ta̱ba a̱cii soo mahanda koo ta̱bisa̱a̱ ta̱hura̱.
Awyatu na ta shana hunranhunran na ta̱gumunu, aba ta ta mantan awyatu ana suhari nasu bina̱, nasu aba be̱re̱ na̱ aba.

Ta̱sha ta̱shika // nata̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana
Imbata ta he̱e̱n iꞌwaan gagu na̱ kuda̱ga ninhin? Be̱ ta shi, ta̱ruba̱ nata̱ iri ma̱ ina nii nda gagu na̱ nꞌgata nꞌniinhin.
Ita he̱e̱n iwya̱nzhin ri ga̱hin jaa da̱ba, sa̱i inaa kunaa wyatu. Ita he̱e̱n iwya̱nzhin ri na̱ kai, ga̱hin jaa ara ta̱da̱ba, sa̱i ike̱ne̱ gagu na̱ kuda̱ga. Na̱ wana iro̱pe̱ce̱ Hwe̱n, ta shani ga̱hin za iri na ga̱hin ribi.
Bike̱nye̱n naa ga̱hin ro̱pe̱ Hwe̱n yaanyini, ga̱hin jaa da̱ba wuun, na̱ wana iro̱pe̱ wuun na̱ nꞌgata na nꞌzumaancin, na hyan inje̱ iri na zumaancin na̱ be̱, ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱niinhin ta̱hange̱ gama.
Ga̱hin wyatu na ne̱e̱ haka na nii nda banshaun! Iyancin ta̱hyan butu naa shi ta̱shika na̱ iri na sa̱ra̱ri yana na uwa̱, bujaa maꞌunso̱n na̱ Hwe̱n? Hyo̱ bunaa ma̱a̱ ta̱ruba̱ iri na sa̱ra̱ri yana, inii shaana bwa jaa sha bushikaa naa Hwe̱n.
Koo inda̱i ta̱hyan mazama nama takaada na Hwe̱n mashi nama uwa̱ na mꞌba hin, Hwe̱n ribici iyaanyini a̱nta̱ni bihwaanwun naa bwa ta̱nsha̱a̱gi na̱ ame̱ nda̱tu?
Ama Hwe̱n ta ta̱duwa̱na̱ ta̱pana iri ꞌye̱n kuga̱tu, ta shani takaada ndaabwa bwa hin, <<Hwe̱n a̱cii maꞌunso̱n na̱ butu naa ma̱a̱ hyuhyu ndaabwa ta̱shapaciga, ama bwa ta tazhigana ara kuunaa mahusani.>>
Na̱ wana kunnu, pana ma hyuhyu ninhin ku-Hwe̱n. Iga̱a̱ Bupira̱, buna̱maa gida̱ga̱na̱ ma.
Naa ma do̱ko̱ na̱ Hwe̱n, ubwa taa maa unii naa do̱ko̱ na̱ ga̱hin. Ga̱hin wyatu na pinsan, a̱sa̱a̱ga̱na̱ ma jabagu ninhin. Ga̱hin wyatu na maree maree, ishii nꞌgata nꞌniinhin sabu.
Nda ma ame̱ ta̱gura, nda ma nꞌungwa na̱ wana pinsan ninhin. Kicihina ma iratu ninhin ishi nꞌungwa, ame̱ tande̱ ninhin ashi ame̱ ta̱gura.
Mahusani ma ku-Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n, ubwa ta na̱maa shapaciga ma.
Ta-hyan maa yaan // bunje̱ pinsan
Aya̱too ma, ta-hyan maa yaan bunje̱ iri na zumaancin. Hyo̱ bunaa hin buya̱na̱ naa jwarigi Hwe̱n nje̱ iri na zumaancin, koo bundaaki buya̱na̱ ta̱suuga̱, bujwarigici ta Nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌta̱ruba̱ ya̱na̱. Buhin ta Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Hwe̱n nꞌshi na nꞌza to̱n na ta̱suuga̱. Kuu-shii kunnu, yansun ta̱hyan bi-jwarigici ta muu, ama bi-shi bunaa ndaaki ta muu ta̱suuga̱.
Hwe̱n ta shi bwaa ka̱ naa nii cita̱ mazama nama Nꞌgira̱nshin, bwa shi naa nii nda suuga̱. Bwa taa shi naa nii ara ta̱biha̱na̱ wyatu, bwa mꞌbaa kai na ta̱kuna. Na̱ wana kunnu, iyaa gaa shi na hyan u-ndaaki butu naa nꞌharu ndaabi suuga̱?
Ta-shapaciga ma // hyuhyu ninhin // wana bunwan
Shiraga ma, ga̱hin naa nii hyaan, <<Ba̱re koo bunwan ga̱tu ja̱a̱ jaga ce̱pe̱ na̱nnda̱ree koo na̱nna, ta̱njé̱e̱ yo̱ na munrun ma nda ciripe̱, ayuwa nda̱tu naa duwa̱na̱ o̱to̱ kaun.>>
Ga̱hin na ga̱hin yancin ri na ja̱a̱ nda na̱ bunwan. Imbata shi maa ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱niinhin? Iyan ta̱hyan ta̱shi haku buka̱ una ta he̱e̱n kune̱e̱ ujaa fogi kunrun.
Huri gama ihin, <<Jaa Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n bwa ribi, ga̱tu ne̱e̱ kami, ta̱ja̱a̱ nda na̱nna, ta̱nje̱ na̱nnda̱ree.>>
Ama ga̱hin na niina ma shapacigaga suhyu ma taa ta̱ga̱sa̱ na̱ iri na ga̱hin ribi ta̱nda. Kai! Hyo̱ ta̱shapa hyuhyu kunta ta̱zumaancin.
Wana kunnu, koya̱a̱ naa yan iri na zumaa na hyan bunje̱, bwa nje̱ce̱ wuun, pinsan ta bwa nje̱.

Yansun ma, // ga̱hin naa mꞌbaa iri ma̱
Shiraga ma, ga̱hin naa mꞌbaagi iri ma̱, naa nꞌgaaga ma ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ wana ngwan na wuci na̱ hyuhyu ninhin.
Iri na ga̱hin mꞌbaa inii pwasa, aꞌwana ninhin ana ta̱taana are̱e̱ baa huwa̱ wyan ta̱re̱.
Azinaari ninhin na̱ azurufa ninhin, ashi iri na uwa̱ na nii hanshinhina. Iri yata na ga̱hin mawuna̱a̱nyin ma̱ kiha̱nsha̱nha̱ni, ibe̱ ta shi na ja̱maa isaaga ma, ihuunha̱ni ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱niinhin paaku ra. Ga̱hin mawuna̱a̱nyin iri ma̱ na huwa̱ na sa̱ra̱ri yana bwa wuce na Hwe̱n bwa ja̱a̱ nda ta̱suuga̱.
Shiraga ma ki, ihange̱! Ufuna̱ na ga̱hin ga̱a̱ ta̱pana ana na̱maa ndaaka ma tuma na̱ nꞌcima nꞌniinhin, na̱ apira̱ na ga̱hin mꞌbaa, anje̱ nꞌungwa ku-Hwe̱n. Kunnu mayaan, nꞌungwa na nꞌawyatu na na̱maa ndaaka ma guba̱ mꞌba wuci ku-Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n naa hura̱gi ta̱kai hyo̱.
Inje̱ hunranhunran ninhin na masuunran na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana, ire̱ koya̱ shami na ga̱hin ribi ta̱re̱. Too, imandaaki ta hyuhyu ninhin fuba, haki bikico̱ na aba nii shinran.
Indaaki ana za pinsan ta̱suuga̱, ga̱hin shaani aba kunai wyan, ana za gagu na̱ ga̱hin.
Akuri na̱ ngwan
Aya̱too ma, naa ma na̱ hunranhunran na̱ akuri, kiike̱nye̱n naa Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu be̱e̱ kúshe̱. Gwatana ma kuuhwaanyan bwa ta naa na̱ akuri, ha̱ni na bwa hambe̱ icima ndaabwa nje̱ bina̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, na̱ akuri ta bwa ta ha̱mba ashira̱ ana mꞌbanu na̱ nꞌta̱giya̱ ta̱ndaaba.
Too, ga̱hin taa maa inaa na̱ hunranhunran na̱ akuri. Iꞌisa na̱ nꞌgata hiku na̱ wana ta̱hyan ukuswa na Butu O̱to̱ goki.
Aya̱too ma, gaa ma ta̱naa nda unta̱nta̱un kuga̱hin kuga̱hin, na̱ wana ta̱hyan xata jamaa ndaaki ma suuga̱. Bwaa naa nii nda ta̱ba ta̱suuga̱ bugoki wuco, bwa ta maa na̱ adubo.
Gwatana ma, aya̱too nimi, inda̱i ana ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n mazama na̱ nꞌruzha̱a̱ rundaabwa, kaba tanaa na̱ akuri, hyo̱ na̱ ngwan na aba tanaa swa.
Ga̱tu yan ta̱hyan, ana tanaa na̱ akuri ji ashi ana rubara̱ka. Ihange̱ da̱i ku-Ayuuba be̱ tanda akuri, ga̱hin yan ku-Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n bwa tandaaka buu ta̱hakana. Hwe̱n bwa shi bunaa za mꞌpirwa na aha̱nka̱ri na̱ ambishiri ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Iri na hura̱gi hyo̱ wyatu nimi, ibe̱ ta shi, ta-nda ma sa̱nsan mahwa. Ta-nda ma na̱ nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ koo na̱ sa̱ra̱ri koo na̱ iyaan ri. Kushi mahanda, xiꞌisa kuna̱ <<Kunnu>>, kushici mahanda, iꞌisa na̱ <<Shii kunnu>>, wana ta̱hyan Uhwe̱n ta jamaa ndaaki ma ta̱suuga̱.
Uro̱pe̱ naa gata ta̱pana
Koo buyaan bune̱e̱ kuga̱hin ne̱e̱ bunaa ne̱e̱ na̱ yaan ngwan? Too, xbunje̱ ro̱pe̱. Koo buyaan bune̱e̱ bunaa ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ga̱da̱ri? Too, xbure̱ iyeebe bunaa zhinyan zha̱a̱ na ta̱yaba Hwe̱n.
Koo buyaan bune̱e̱ bunaa hange̱ce̱ sa̱? XBuꞌnꞌgani awyatu o̱to̱ na awyatu na Yeesu andaaki be̱ ro̱pe̱, ashanai be̱ mariga̱ na̱ hyuhyu ma nꞌga ruzha̱a̱ naru Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu.
Uro̱pe̱ yata na aba nje̱, huku nii gata ta̱pana, unii shaana bunaa hange̱ce̱ sa̱ bukwade̱ge̱. Butu O̱to̱ taa nii kuda̱gahina be̱. Kuutanje̱ pinsan, Uhwe̱n bwa jaa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ be̱ pinsan ndaabwa.
Na̱ wana kunnu, naa ma bisa̱ga̱ ma pinsan ninhin, inaa mandaakaka ro̱pe̱, na̱ wana Uhwe̱n kuda̱gahini ma. Uro̱pe̱ na butu naa bina̱ uza mꞌpirwa na̱ nꞌta̱kota̱na̱, na̱ nꞌta̱kai.
Iliya, bunaa ta naa cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama, butu wuma ta be̱ tasha haku ga̱tu. Na be̱ tapa ayima̱a̱ na̱ nꞌta̱rupa Hwe̱n xashira̱ ta kina, aba ke̱nce̱n na̱ nꞌta̱ba ce̱nye̱n nata̱ Isiraaꞌila nꞌyo̱ nꞌtaatu na̱ mꞌpyanda nꞌcininhin.
Be̱ gura̱a̱ nda ro̱pe̱, ashira̱ aba kíne̱ nꞌta̱ra, aba shani shami be̱ nje̱.
Aya̱too ma, suga̱hin ne̱e̱ kuuyaan bufogi kuyo̱n na Hwe̱n, buyaan bubwa kúshihine̱ be̱ kuyo̱n na ta̱to̱n,
xbuyansun ta̱hyan hyo̱ bunaa kúshihine̱ butu naa pinsan kuyo̱n na ta̱to̱n, bubiha̱ni ta buyata kuta̱ꞌwa̱, ubwaa gura̱a̱ shana Uhwe̱n bwa jaa ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ bwa apinsan ndaabwa hwarapi.
TI - Pangu
Timooti
Tim
Timooti
Takaada na Bulusu bwa ta̱gi zhagu paaku Timooti na hin hiin
Takaada na Bulusu bwa ta̱gi zhagu paaku
Timooti
na hin hiin
Iri na ta̱yansun na yigo
Bulusu butumashini naa Yeesu taa ta̱gi takaada na̱nna una shi na yigo zhagu ku-Timooti. Timooti ta shi bunaa Bulusu bwa ga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni mazama nama Hwe̱n, bwa mawaani na̱ mꞌmaba. Ane̱e̱ nꞌta̱hyan Bulusu tataga takaada na̱nna na̱ Makidooniya na̱ wyantancin na nꞌyo̱ 65 na̱ 67 na̱ nꞌta̱mantan nata̱ Yeesu. Butakada bwa takaada ku-Timooti na tanaa na̱ Afisa.
Ubwa takaada ushi na nje̱ mazama nama iri taatu na shi nama ca̱ma̱nta̱n. Mazama nama yigo mashi nama hin hana na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ ta̱be̱, na̱ nꞌta̱ pa be̱ mazama ta̱hyan xbuyansun kuubwaa naa bisa̱ga̱ ana ne̱e̱ kaun mazama nama Hwe̱n. Ubwa gura̱a̱ nda mazama nama haruwa na bwaa naa hura̱hina̱ ujabagu na gama kuꞌawyatu na Yeesu, na̱ ahari na zumaa. Aba gura̱a̱ pa be̱ mazama haruwa na bwaa sha butumashini naa bina̱ naa Ala̱masiihu, na̱ hyo̱ utuma na bwaa naa ndaga hwarapi.
Iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱
Azumanu :1-2 Ta̱pa mazama nama awyatu na Yeesu na̱ awyatu o̱to̱ ndaaba :3--3:16Ta̱pa mazama ku-Timooti nama tuma ndaabwa :1--6:21
Azumanu
Takaada na̱nna shi na báni kuga̱n Bulusu butumashini naa Ala̱masiihu Yeesu. Uhwe̱n na ta̱mbiha̱ni na̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu na shani ga̱tun shii bigata aba nꞌka̱shi na̱ tuma yana.
Zhagu paaku Timooti, baa buniimi bunaa mahanda paakii gata ta̱pana.
Ta̱pana ꞌye̱n na̱ ambishiri na̱ hunranhunran na ta̱gumunu ku-Hwe̱n Ada na̱ Butu O̱to̱ nda̱a̱tu Ala̱masiihu Yeesu xta̱naa huku na̱ gaa.
Ta̱nda aha̱nka̱ri na̱ nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌta̱be̱
Haruwa na ga̱n taabisa̱ ga̱n ma hura̱ Makidooniya ta̱hyan naa na̱ Afisa. Awyatu ka̱ kaun anii ga̱gaagana iri na shici mahanda, gaa taa nii shaana aga̱a̱ wuun.
Bisa̱ wyan xaga̱a̱ ta̱naa ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ bike̱nye̱n ndaaba na̱ aca̱a̱sa̱ ca̱a̱sa̱ na̱ azha̱a̱zha̱a̱ na adaadoo na za haru. Uya̱nu ta shaana wyan ana maga̱a̱ga̱nu, aba jaa ara ta̱nda tuma na shi na ana pa̱ni nꞌgata ku-Hwe̱n.
Iri na shaani ga̱n hin xaga̱a̱ ri ya̱nu, bwa ta shi ta̱ruba̱. Ta̱ruba̱ ta̱na̱nna ta̱báni kiigata naa tande̱, ri na ga̱tu makicihinaa nii gata na ta̱sabu na̱ nꞌta̱panaa gata nata̱ mahanda.
Awyatu ka̱ ga̱a̱ iri na̱nna aba ka̱shi kuyo̱n na̱nna na mahanda, aba jwarigi mazama nama uwa̱.
Aribi ta̱sha nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nami Nꞌgira̱nshin na n-Muusa, ama aba jaa insan iri na baa ga̱gaagana koo iri na abaa nda mazama mande̱e̱be̱ ma jinyan ji iri na aba nda̱i kishi mahanda.
Ga̱tun yan ta̱hyan Nꞌgira̱nshin nꞌzumaa aba nje̱ tuma na̱ mꞌba ki haruwa na shi xanje̱.
Na ta̱hyan, anje̱ Nꞌgira̱nshin shici na̱ wana ana nii nda iri na ta̱to̱n, ama nꞌshi kana hwashe̱ Nꞌgira̱nshin, ana ta hiika̱hina̱ nꞌgata, ana yancin Hwe̱n, ana ta naa ndaga pinsan, ana wa̱shici Hwe̱n, ana ta naa nda ri na yinzhin, ana ta naa kunaa sushoo koo suya̱ndoo koo ayaan awyatu.
Nꞌgira̱nshin gura̱a̱ sha na nꞌana ta naa nda banshaun, ana ta naa makata butu wya̱ri na̱ butu wya̱ri, buꞌa̱ na̱a̱ a̱, ana ta naa sa̱a̱nha̱na̱a̱ agyama, ana ta naa ndaga ta̱be̱, anaa ta naa hyaan ta̱be̱ ta̱shi mahanda, ana ta naa nda ri ina ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ ta̱to̱n ta̱ba yanshin.
Ta̱ba ta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱ne̱e̱ kumazama mayata nama zumaa nama ta̱shapaciga nata̱ Hwe̱n. Ubwa mꞌpa̱ni ma bisa̱ga̱ muu. Uhwe̱n na shi naa rubara̱ka.
Bulusu gooji Hwe̱n na̱ ambishiri ndaabwa
Ga̱n gooji Ala̱masiihu Yeesu Butu O̱to̱ nda̱a̱tu naa mꞌpa̱ni ta̱kai. Ga̱n gooji buu na be̱ nꞌnda̱i mꞌmꞌbaa ahari na bina̱, be̱ nꞌta̱ masha bugyama nde̱e̱be̱.
Koo na ga̱n tanaa sa̱ manaa nda mazama nama hwashe̱ ku-Ala̱masiihu, ma kaka ana jwarigi buu ma nda gagu na̱ aba, ama be̱ hange̱ ambishiri nimi wana ga̱n tanaa nda wuun nꞌta̱yancin ga̱n ta tapa̱nciin gata.
Butu O̱to̱ nda̱a̱tu Ala̱masiihu Yeesu be̱ nꞌzóogi ta̱pana ꞌye̱n ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ ma̱ huku nii gata ta̱pana na̱ nꞌta̱ruba̱ wana ta̱maꞌunpa̱n ta̱niimi huku nii be̱.
<<Ala̱masiihu Yeesu jaa sa̱ra̱ri yana wana ta̱biha̱na̱ awyatu na pinsan.>> Maya̱nu mata mashi mazama nama mahanda nama shi koo buya̱ bwaa raa. Ga̱n ta nꞌshi bunaa hura̱gi ta̱sha naa bwa pinsan.
Ama Ala̱masiihu Yeesu nꞌndaaki ambishiri, bunaa hura̱gi hyo̱ pinsan, wana hyan bibisa̱a̱ akuri nde̱e̱be̱ na̱ hyo̱ iri na be̱ hiin nꞌndaaka, ushi iri na ta̱bisa̱a̱ kana ja̱a̱ pana nꞌgata waabe̱ ara̱a̱ bina̱ na mahwa.
xUhwe̱n ra̱a̱ hyo̱ ta̱shapaciga na̱ nꞌta̱pa hunrun ta̱naa na̱ mꞌmahwa mahwa. Bwa taa shi Bugwama naa ta̱gwama nata̱ za haru bunaa aba jaa ara ta̱ndaya, bunaa jaa ꞌwa̱ mahwa, bwa taa shi Hwe̱n bwaa ka̱. xMashi kunnu.
Iri na hyan Timooti nje̱
Timooti, be̱e̱ biniimi, nde̱e̱ iri na ga̱n maa bisa̱ga̱ na hyan u-nje̱, na ne̱e̱ re̱ na̱ mꞌmayaan mazama nama tabáni wana gaa kayaan cita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama. Tamanrinyan mꞌba mazama na̱ wana mashi haku ꞌwaa ndaa na na̱maa guna̱ gagu kugagu na Hwe̱n.
Sha̱a̱ ta̱pana bigata ndaabi ka̱ ki-Yeesu, na̱ iri na gaa makicihinaa nii gata na ne̱e̱ sabu. Awyatu ka̱ ga̱a̱ ta̱naa makicihinaa nii gata ndaaba ri na ne̱e̱ sabu ta aba kwane̱ ta̱panaa gata ndaaba.
Aka̱ ndaaba ta shi Himiniyusu na̱ Aleka̱zanda, ana ga̱n pa̱ sumo̱ wa̱tu, ga̱n tutumaa wyan ku-Shatan. Na̱nna ta nii bisa̱a̱ wyan ajaa gura̱a̱ cita̱ mazama nama hwashe̱ ku-Hwe̱n.

Haruwa na ta̱rupa Hwe̱n
Na hura̱gi bo̱do̱ hyo̱, ndaaka awyatu ro̱pe̱ hyo̱. Rupa Hwe̱n na hyan ubini wyan, ade̱be̱ ri na abaa wyanzan. U-gooji Hwe̱n na̱ wana ri na bwa ndaaki wyan.
Ndaaka nꞌgwama na̱ hyo̱ ana ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱gwama ro̱pe̱ wana ta̱nhunrana gumunu na̱ nꞌta̱fo̱n na̱ ahari na zumaa ana jabagu na Hwe̱n.
Uzumaa ta̱nda kunnu, ubwa nii caanhina Hwe̱n ame̱. Bunaa ta̱mbiha̱ni,
bunaa ribi koo buya̱a̱ xbuyansun mahanda bubini.
Na ta̱hyan Hwe̱n ka̱ ta ne̱e̱ na̱a̱ yaan buka̱ bunaa ne̱e̱ wyantancin na awyatu na̱ Hwe̱n, bwa taa shi butu wuma Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Bunaa tapana hyuhyu ndaabwa bwa ta̱nra̱a̱ wana koo buya̱ bude̱be̱ ta̱banana. Hwe̱n takáji buu na̱ ha̱ni na ta̱to̱n, na̱nna ta bisa̱a̱ hiku ta̱hyan uribi koo buya̱ xbubini.
Ta shani ubwa nꞌka̱shi ma sha butumashini bunaa nii bisa̱ga̱ ana shici Ayaahudiya mazama nama ta̱jwara̱ga nata̱ mahanda. Ga̱n jaa nda ta̱be̱, mahanda ga̱n cita̱ga̱ hiku.
Na̱ wana kunnu ga̱n ribi kope ha̱ni na awyatu wya̱ri aba mawuna̱ni, kanii nda ro̱pe̱ xaka̱cihini nꞌara ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱ ku-Hwe̱n na̱ nꞌgata na mꞌbure, shii na̱ nꞌgata ta̱guma, koo kuda̱ga.
Ga̱n ribi aꞌa̱ ashi ana ta̱a̱ni aꞌwana nata̱ ki, shii ana nii shaana aha̱nka̱ri ndaaba hiiki paaku ta̱hinje ta̱ndaaba ta̱ta sha nata̱ ne̱e̱ yaan iri goo na̱ ꞌwaa ndaaba na aba táani na yuwa haku nꞌshuwa na nꞌzinaari.
Na̱ kunnu ana shi ana pa̱ni nꞌgata ndaaba ku-Hwe̱n xabisa̱a̱ tuun kuꞌiri na zumaa na abaa nda.
xAꞌa̱ shi ana ra̱a̱ ta̱ga̱gaagana na̱ nꞌgata fo̱n na̱ hyuhyu ta̱pana hyo̱.
Ga̱n pa̱ncin aꞌa̱ ashi ana nii ga̱gaagana awyatu wya̱ri koo aꞌmꞌbaa ta̱kai nata̱ huri ta̱ndaaba, na̱ kunnu xaꞌa̱ shiraaga sa̱ fo̱n.
Wana Hwe̱n tanda Adamu na yigo naazhin bwa njé̱e̱ Hawaaꞌu.
Shii Adamu ta Bupira̱ bwa tapira̱. Buꞌa̱ ta aba ta pira̱, ta shani bwa tajwarigici mazama nama Hwe̱n.
Ama aꞌa̱ nii bina̱na̱ paaku ta̱mantaan mꞌmwaan, kanii ta ta̱hura̱ nii gata ta̱pana, aꞌmꞌbaa ta̱ruba̱, anaa sabu, na̱ hunranhunran fo̱n.

Awyatu o̱to̱ na awyatu na Yeesu
<<Kubutu naa ribi tasha butu o̱to̱ naa awyatu na Yeesu, tuma na bina̱ ta bwa wya̱nzhin.>> Maya̱nu mata mashi mazama nama mahanda.
Koo buya̱ butu o̱to̱ xbushi butu naa za yaan randa kaꞌuba̱ na wyatu. Bunaa mꞌbaa buꞌa̱ ka̱, bunaa ne̱e̱ fo̱n, bwa kota̱ni hyuhyu ndaabwa, bunaa aha̱nka̱ri. Bunaa ta raa agai nꞌara nꞌree, bunaa nii ara ta̱naa ga̱gaagana awyatu.
xButa sha naa gagu na̱ awyatu, xbuta sha busowa̱ koo bunaa tanaa wyanzan gagu ama xbushi naa tanaa maꞌiya shukuu, bunaa ma̱a̱ncin ta̱ruba̱ ayuwa.
Bunaa a̱ri ina ndaabwa ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱, bunaa mꞌmwaan nꞌndaabwa mꞌba ta cina̱na̱ mꞌba ta jwara̱ga mazama mandaabwa.
Kubutu shi naa a̱rici ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ ina ndaabwa, na bwa nii ara awyatu na Hwe̱n ta̱ha̱mba?
xBushi naa ta̱a̱ ke̱nye̱n nꞌta̱panaa gata ki-Yeesu, wana xbuta jaa shi bunaa ruwashi ajaa ndaaki be̱ ta̱suuga̱ haku Bupira̱.
xBushi bunaa awyatu aba cina̱ni koo ana pa̱ncin nꞌgata, na̱ wana xata jaa ga̱a̱ be̱, bumazha̱a̱ nꞌta̱ruma nata̱ Bupira̱.
Ana shi aguni awyatu na Yeesu
Ana shi aguni awyatu na Yeesu, xashi ana mꞌbaa suha̱nka̱ri, ana gii xacina̱ni wyan, xata sha ana ma̱a̱ ta̱swa ta̱ruba̱, xata sha ana ma̱a̱ ayuwa ta̱ruba̱.
xAshi ana ha̱mba̱gi ta̱ga̱gaagana ki nata̱ Hwe̱n bwa bisa̱a̱ wyan huku nii gata ta̱makicihinaa naa ne̱e̱ sabu.
xAshi ana aba hoo maanwyana, kiyaan ri za na nii yansan wyan, apa̱ni wyan bwa tuma.
Kunnu taa, aꞌa̱ ndaaba xashi ana gii xacina̱ni wyan, shici ana ta naa ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ ayaan ruzha̱a̱, xashi ana ne̱e̱ fo̱n, ana ta naa nda koya̱ ri to̱n.
Ana shi aguni ana pa̱ni nꞌgata, xaꞌmꞌbaaga aꞌa̱ ka̱a̱ ka̱a̱, ashi ana a̱ri ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ mꞌmwaan nꞌndaaba na̱ kwayaa na ne̱e̱ na̱ ina gumunu.
Kanii nda tuma ndaaba ki, anii da̱ba funa̱ ndaaba na ta̱cina̱na̱ paaka wyatu, aduwa̱ni bishita̱ naa ta̱ꞌisa hiku kiigata ta̱pana ku-Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Ashe̱re̱ ana mahanda kuta̱jwara̱ga ta̱nda̱a̱tu
Koo na ga̱mii ta̱a̱ga̱gi takaada na̱nna, ga̱n ribi ta̱jaa maa ndaya kunrun.
Ama kunja̱a̱ci na̱ ha̱ni, na̱nna takaada tanii bisa̱a̱ haruwa na awyatu na Hwe̱n abaa ara ta̱maha̱mba̱ga̱ na̱ wana ta̱shi ana jwarigi Hwe̱n na ne̱e̱ buwuma. Ga̱tu taa shi haku marodo nama ha̱mba̱gi ta̱ciba̱ mazama nama mahanda.
Buza naa nii hyan yaanyini kuharuwa na o̱to̱ na ashe̱re̱ na ta̱jwara̱ga ta̱nda̱a̱tu aba ne̱e̱:
Ala̱masiihu tabáni na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwaba nata̱ butu wuma,
Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n bisa̱a̱ mahanda bibáni paa Hwe̱n.
Atuma naa Hwe̱n aba nda̱i buu,
atabisa̱gi mazama mande̱e̱be̱ na̱ koya̱ ce̱nye̱n.
Aba ra̱a̱ buu kope na̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana,
Hwe̱n bwa sha̱pi buu zhagu ta̱ra̱ga̱da̱.

Mape̱e̱n kuta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ ta̱be̱
Bihwaanwun naa Hwe̱n cici da̱shi ta̱hyan, awyatu ka̱ nii gaa ta̱jwara̱ga mahanda na̱ nꞌhwe̱n yana na nꞌta̱makwaakaa, ajwara̱ga nꞌhwaanwun na nꞌwe̱ na̱ ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ awyatu na hira̱ na we̱.
Iri na ta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱ya̱nu ta̱báni paaka awyatu na za mahanda ana a̱ri ta̱be̱ ana ta̱makicihinaa nii gata ndaaba ta̱ba hoo ꞌwa̱ kiri na ne̱e̱ to̱n.
Ana nii ga̱gaagana wyatu xata zhaaga aꞌa̱, xata re̱ iyaan iri na shami. Ana pa̱ni nꞌgata kashi ana yan mahanda aba hwii ro̱pe̱ na ta̱gooda̱ Hwe̱n wana unje̱ koya̱ iri na shami xare̱ wuun.
xTa̱nra̱a̱ koya̱ ri na Hwe̱n bwa nje̱ na̱ nꞌta̱gooda̱, wana hyo̱ ishi na zumaa, za ri na hyan aga̱a̱,
wana ta̱hyan Hwe̱n shaani wuun ibe̱ ne̱e̱ sabu paaku ro̱pe̱ na̱ mazama mandaabwa.
Bugyama naa Ala̱masiihu Yeesu naa bina̱
Kuu-cici na̱nna ri paaka aya̱too na pa̱ni nꞌgata, bi-nii sha hiku bugyama naa bina̱ naa Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, bunaa mawaani na̱ mazama namaa gata ta̱pana na̱ ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ mahanda nata̱ gaa jwarigi.
Mahooshi na̱ kuda̱ga ta̱naa nda na̱ aca̱a̱sa̱ ca̱a̱sa̱ na shici na bina̱. Ama maya̱wa̱hini na̱ jabagu na Hwe̱n,
na̱ wana ta̱ya̱wa̱hina̱ ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱zumaa ama ta̱ya̱wa̱hina̱ na̱ jabagu na Hwe̱n bwa ribi ta̱huri na̱ koya̱ yo̱n, ta̱nii guna̱ butu niina nii ke̱nye̱n naa wuci.
Maya̱nu mata mashi ta̱cita̱ nata̱ mahanda, xta̱ra̱a̱ tuun nii gata ta̱pana.
Ta̱nii mapa dibi ma nda tuma o̱to̱ wana ta̱nshii nꞌgata nꞌnda̱a̱tu ku-Hwe̱n na ne̱e̱ buwuma, una shi na biha̱ni hyo̱ awyatu suta̱hyan maa hyo̱ ana pa̱ni nꞌgata na̱ bwa.
Ga̱gaagana wyan hyo̱ mazama maya̱nu u-shaani koo buya̱ buyansun muu.
xBuyaan butaa husana na̱ wana buta shi baa, ama sha iri na ta̱bisa̱a̱ paaka ana pa̱ni nꞌgata paaku mazama mandaabi, na̱ jabagu na gaa nda, na̱ nꞌta̱ruba̱ wyatu, na̱ nꞌta̱naa sabu nii gata.
Ta ga̱n wuco, pana bike̱nye̱n ndaabi na̱ kai ndaa na̱ nꞌta̱naa cita̱ga̱ atakaada na Hwe̱n da̱shi kawyatu, na̱ nꞌta̱naa bisa̱ga̱ wyan mazama nama zumaa, na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana.
Ta-gaa ta̱yansun nata̱a̱ Hwaanwun be̱e̱ pa̱ni nata̱ ne̱e̱ na̱ gaa, nata̱ gaa tada̱ba ha̱ni na awyatu o̱to̱ aba tacita̱a̱ga̱ Hwe̱n mazama mandaabi abaa ca̱guda̱a̱gi nꞌara.
Naa nda iri ya̱nu, u-pa̱ wuun zha̱munkun ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, wana hyan koo buya̱a̱ nda̱i bi-re̱ iyeebe.
Magwatani, ugura̱a̱ gwatana ta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱ndaabi. Ta kiigata macimi na̱ nꞌta̱naa nda iri ya̱nu, na̱ wana kuu-nje̱ wuun hyo̱, bi-nii bina̱na̱ buna buushiragi bwa nii bina̱na̱ taa.

Ri na ta̱ndaaka ana pa̱ni nꞌgata
