Ta-yinzhinkana butu naa hoo naa masha̱a̱, ama naa makusuma̱ na̱a̱ bwa u-sha̱pi be̱ haka baaba ndaa. Shapa Asa̱mba̱ri haka yamboo,
shapa aꞌa̱ ana hoo naa masha̱a̱ haka ada̱a̱doo ndaa, mꞌmwaan nꞌa̱ haka yamboo na a̱, na̱ nꞌta̱naa sabu nii gata.
Cina̱na̱ aꞌa̱ na suwya̱rugooba suba ꞌwa̱gi ana za naa nii gwatana wyan.
Kuubwa a̱ mꞌbaa mꞌmwaan, koo mꞌmwaan na nꞌayoo, too, iri na yigo na shi anje̱ xanaa ndaga ri na Hwe̱n bwa ribi ta shi xagwatani sushoo na̱ adaadoo ndaaba. Ta̱naa nda kunnu ta shi afuni wyan, wana uta caanhina Hwe̱n me̱.
Gwatana buꞌa̱ naa awya̱rugo aba ꞌwi, bunaa za naa nii gwatana be̱, buta sha̱a̱ bigata ndaabwa ku-Hwe̱n, ma rupa wuun gita na̱ hwe̱n xuguni be̱.
Ama buꞌa̱ naa awya̱rugo aba ꞌwi, bunaa pa̱ni hyuhyu ndaabwa kuna̱ ri na bwa ribi na masuunran, bushi naa hoo ꞌwa̱, koo buta ne̱e̱ buwuma.
Bisa̱ wyan maya̱nu mazama wana xbuyaan buta naa bunaa nii naa cwaagaga wyan.
Kuuyaan bune̱e̱ bunaa a̱cii gwatana diin ndaabwa, suta̱hyan ana shi awyatu na ina ndaabwa, buga̱a̱ ta iri na ta̱jwara̱ga ta̱nda̱a̱tu ta̱ba cici, buhuri ana pa̱ncin gata ta̱we̱.
xAta ta ruzha̱a̱ naru buꞌa̱ naa awya̱rugo aba ꞌwi bunaa wucici nꞌyo̱ kuje cininhin paaka azha̱a̱zha̱a̱ na aꞌa̱ na suwya̱rugooba suba ꞌwa̱gi. Bwaa a̱ xbushi naa tamashikana kawya̱rugo.
Bwaa a̱ xbushi naa awyatu ba cina̱ni wana tuma na gama na bwaa nda. Suta̱hyan buwaanhinai mꞌmwaan ndaabwa ki, bwa shi naa ta raa agai na̱ ina ndaabwa, bwa shi naa ta munsan hyuhyu ndaabwa kuta̱naa ndaaka ana pa̱ni nꞌgata tuma, bwa ta sha̱a̱ta̱na̱ ara paaka na ne̱e̱ na̱ ꞌwa̱, bwa ta pana hyuhyu ndaabwa paaku ta̱naa nda ri hwarapi na zumaa.
Aꞌa̱ na suwya̱rugooba suba ꞌwa̱gi ana ta shi mꞌmwaan, xata ta azha̱a̱zha̱a̱ ndaaba, wana ta̱hyan ha̱ni na ta̱ꞌwaba ta̱ndaaba ta̱ba ribi butu wya̱ri ushani wyan apa̱ni Ala̱masiihu baa, agura̱a̱ ruba̱ ta̱giya̱ga̱ ta̱wya̱ri.
Anii ndaaka wyan ta̱suuga̱ wana aciga̱hincin ala̱ka̱wa̱ri na aba tanda nii be̱.
Aba gura̱a̱ sha arinda ma ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱a̱ ha̱ni ndaaba paaku ta̱naa jabaga nꞌina nꞌina, iri na hura̱gi ta̱zumaancin ibe̱ ta shi ta̱naa wyasa mazama ma̱, ta̱naa ta̱na̱a̱ mazama nama shici mandaaba, ma cita̱ga̱ iri na shici xanaa cita̱ga̱.
Wana kunnu, ga̱n huri ta̱ruba̱, aꞌa̱ na suwya̱rugooba suba ꞌwa̱gi ana tashi mꞌmwaan agiya̱gi ta̱wya̱ri, ama̱nciin mꞌmwaan, aha̱mba̱ga̱ ina ndaaba ki, wana xata pa bunaa ta̱nribici ha̱ba̱ na hyan bunaa cita̱ga̱ mazama nama we̱ mandaaba.
Aka̱ hoo gaa ta̱jwara̱ga Hwe̱n ta aba jwarigi Shatan.
Koo buya̱ a̱ naa pa̱ni gata ki-Yeesu bunaa mꞌbaa aꞌa̱ ana suwya̱rugooba suba ꞌwa̱gi na̱ ina ndaabwa, xbugwatani wyan ki, wana xbuta sha̱a̱ga̱ kuꞌawyatu na Yeesu ayishe, na hyan aꞌa̱ri ta̱gwataga kana za butu.
Butu o̱to̱ naa awyatu na Yeesu naa nii nda tuma na zumaa, anii cina̱na̱ be̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, bunaa hura̱gi maa bwa taa shi bunaa nii ga̱gaagana wyatu bwaa bisa̱ga̱ wyan mazama nama zumaa.
Wana takaada na Hwe̱n hin, <<Ta-kadaga nu na binaa ha̱ni na gaa nda ta̱ga̱wa̱ nii be̱,>> na̱ <<Uzumaa butu naa tuma bura̱a̱ funa̱ ndaabwa.>>
Ta-shiraga mayaan mazama nama abaa íyaagi nama butu o̱to̱ nama gaa tahange̱ce̱ muu paaka wyatu reeko koo ataatu.
Ndaaka ana nje̱ pinsan gagu da̱shi wana hyan ana bwe̱ ahange̱ rukwanyan.
Na uba̱ na Hwe̱n na̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu na̱ atuma na Hwe̱n bwa ka̱shi, iita̱ tuma na̱nna hiku, jwara̱ga mazama nama ga̱n maa bisa̱ga̱ na za ta̱bisa̱a̱ ta̱hura̱ koo uhuri ta̱ruba̱a̱ yaan.
Ta-naa makwasa ta̱kasa butu o̱to̱ naa wyatu na Yeesu ta gaa ma̱a̱nwya̱nu bwa, wana ta-naa mata̱ha̱na̱a̱ na̱ pinsan na shici ndaa. Naa sabu nii gata.
Ta-swa kuma̱ni kumaba, ama swa ma̱ni nama ta̱ꞌwa̱ri nata̱ ꞌwe̱e̱ na iinabi ge̱ wana ta̱mba̱ra̱ ta̱guma na̱ ha̱ni na gaa hange̱ce̱ sa̱ sa̱.
Pinsan na awyatu ka̱ anii ndaya wuun da̱shi, ubwa nii naa iyeebe ndaaba paaku ta̱suuga̱, pinsan na awyatu ka̱ jaa insan niina kuhina iyeebe.
Kunnu taa, utuma na gama una awyatu ka̱ aba nje̱, unii naa da̱shi, koo una awyatu aba nda̱ci ujaa naa ta̱swee.

Awyatu ana shi agyama xapa̱ awyatu na ina ndaaba hunrun ta̱ꞌo̱to̱, na̱ wana xbuyaan buta husana mazama nama Hwe̱n na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱nda̱a̱tu.
Agyama ana awyatu na ina ndaaba aba pa̱ni nꞌgata ki-Yeesu, xata husana wyan wana ashi aya̱na̱ba. Na̱ kunnu xahuri ta̱naa ndaaka wyan tuma na zumaa, wana awyatu na nii naa re̱ funa̱ na tuma ndaaba ashi ana pa̱ni nꞌgata ana aba ribi.
Ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ ta̱be̱ na̱ ayuwa ta̱ruba̱
Ga̱gaagana ana pa̱ni nꞌgata, u-bisa̱gi wyan haruwa na ta̱nda na̱nna hyo̱.
Kwayaa na nii ga̱gaagana iri goo, bwa ribici mazama nama ta̱to̱n nama Butu O̱to̱ nda̱a̱tu Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, na̱ ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ ahari na Hwe̱n bwa ribi.
Buyancin ta, bwa shi naa ruwashi, bwa shi naa za gumunu bwaa wyanzan ta̱maga̱a̱ga̱nu na̱ kuda̱ga wana iri na mazama mꞌba hin. Una tahe̱e̱n uꞌwaan ta̱ribici yami na̱ ta̱mahoosa̱ga̱ga̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ buyaan ruzha̱a̱ na̱ nꞌta̱sha̱a̱ga̱ buyaan bushi naa we̱.
Awyatu ya̱nu ata naa nda kuda̱ga ji, paaka wyatu na sume̱ sundaaba suba ꞌwi na̱ ana a̱cii cita̱ mahanda. Aba shii ta̱hyan ta̱ga̱gaagana mazama nama Hwe̱n ta̱shi paaka hyan butu mꞌbaa funa̱ na ayuwa ma̱.
Ta̱mꞌmꞌbaa funa̱ ma̱ kuta̱nnje̱ ahari na Hwe̱n bwa ribi, ga̱tun shii iri na bwa ta̱mpa̱ni ita̱ngii.
Na ta̱hyan iba̱ ga̱tun jaa na̱ be̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana? Koori! Iba̱ ga̱tun shapa kusa̱ra̱ri yana? Koori!
Kuta̱mꞌmꞌbaa shami, ga̱tun mꞌbaa aꞌwana na ta̱taana, iya̱nu ta̱ngii.
Ana ribi aꞌmꞌbaa ri ma̱, ata mazwagana kuta̱maanwyana, azha̱a̱ wyan na̱ nꞌta̱ruma na̱ iri na uwa̱ na̱ nꞌta̱ruba̱ ta̱naa nda iri na zumaancin, na ja̱a̱ iya wyan kuta̱kuna̱ na̱ nꞌta̱mahanshinhina ta̱ꞌo̱to̱.
Ta̱ruba̱ ayuwa ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ta tashana ta̱naa nda iri hwarapi na we̱. Na̱ wana awyatu ka̱ huri ta̱ruba̱ xaꞌmꞌbaa iri ma̱, ta aba ka̱shi kuyo̱n na Hwe̱n, aba maꞌwaanyin ame̱ ta̱gura ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ ma̱.
Mazama nama ta̱makwaakaa ku-Timooti
Ama gaa, butu naa Hwe̱n, gaa iri ya̱nu na we̱ hyo̱. Jaga u-pa̱ni uba̱ kuta̱nda iri na ta̱to̱n, na̱ ahari na Hwe̱n bwa ribi, na̱ nꞌta̱panaa gata, na̱ nꞌta̱ruba̱, na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌisa hiku, na̱ nꞌta̱sha butu naa ta iya ri shukuu.
Maka̱nta̱ni na̱ nꞌfwaru namii gata ta̱pana na mꞌmahanda. Ha̱mba̱ga̱ ki ufuna̱ na bina̱ na mahwa, wana na̱nna ta Hwe̱n bwaa nꞌgani, na gaa cita̱gi ta̱pana gata ndaabi paaka wyatu hwarapi.
Iita̱ tuma na̱nna wana Hwe̱n na shani komba̱ri be̱ ne̱e̱ wuma na̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu na tacita̱ mahanda kuꞌaꞌuba̱ na Buntu Bilaatu,
nda hyo̱ iri na Hwe̱n bwaa hin nda ki na za randa kii ke̱nye̱n naa ta̱banrinyan nata̱ Butu O̱to̱ nda̱a̱tu Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Ta̱wuce ta̱nde̱e̱be̱ ta̱nii sha ha̱ni na Hwe̱n bwa ribi. Uhwe̱n ta shi naa rubara̱ka, bugwama naa mahya̱, Bugwama naa nꞌgwama na̱ Butu O̱to̱ naa awyatu o̱to̱.
Bwa taa shi bwaa ka̱ naa jaa ꞌwa̱ mahwa, bunaa hunrani paaku ta̱gwaan nata̱ buzaa na nii ara ta̱wuta̱ kaun. Buzaa naa hoo ndaya wuun, ubwa zaa naa nii ara wuun ta̱ndaya. xBushi naa baa pa hunrun naa hura̱gi ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ mahwa. xMashi kunnu.
Bisa̱ ana mꞌbaa iri na sa̱ra̱ri yana xata naa nda ruwashi na̱ be̱, xata sha̱a̱ nꞌgata kuna̱ ayuwa ndaaba wana ajaa naa ji. Na̱ kunnu xashii nꞌgata nꞌndaaba ku-Hwe̱n wana bwa taa shi naa ta pana koya̱ ri na hyan butu hange̱ gama.
Bisa̱ wyan xanje̱ ri na bure, anje̱ wuun ta̱ꞌo̱to̱ u-ta̱zhiga̱ni ara nꞌta̱naa pagana ana za.
Ta̱naa nda kunnu ji, anii masha̱a̱ga̱ ta iri kupa̱ri naka ta̱hiku nii ke̱nye̱n na wuci, na hyan amade̱e̱be̱ bina̱ na mahanda.
Gaa Timooti, ha̱mba ki iri na Hwe̱n bwaa pa̱ni ta̱nda. U-ga̱a̱ nꞌza̱zama na nꞌuwa̱ na nꞌawyatu ka̱ ana ga̱a̱ ta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱ndaabi aba masha̱pi ta̱hyan aba yan.
Na̱ nꞌta̱jwara̱ga nꞌza̱zama nꞌya̱nu awyatu ka̱ aba ka̱shi kuyo̱n na Hwe̱n.
Ta̱pana ꞌye̱n ku-Hwe̱n xta̱naa na̱ ga̱hin hyo̱.
TI - Pangu
Timooti
Tim
Timooti
Takaada na Bulusu bwa ta̱gi zhagu paaku Timooti na hin reenu
Takaada na Bulusu bwa ta̱gi zhagu paaku
Timooti
na hin reenu
Iri na ta̱yansun na yigo
Una̱nna takaada tashi na hin reenu na Bulusu bwa ta̱gi zhagu ku-Timooti, buyoo kutuma na Hwe̱n ta̱naa nda. Butataga takaada na̱nna ha̱ni na bwa ne̱e̱ na̱ zhaaro na̱ Rooma, do̱ko̱ nꞌta̱huwa̱ nata̱ tuma ndaabwa na̱ nꞌta̱ꞌwa̱ ta̱ndaabwa na̱ yo̱ na hin 67 koo 68 na̱ nꞌta̱mantan nata̱ Yeesu.
Na tashaana Bulusu bwa ta̱a̱ga̱gi bwa ubwa takaada tasha wana hyan buba̱shi Timooti bugura̱a̱ duwa̱na̱ bwa bishita̱ ta̱ta na hyan buꞌisa hiku na̱ koya̱ ngwan na jábani bwa kutuma ndaabwa. Mayaan, bugura̱a̱ re̱ iyeebe na̱ tuma na aba tanda da̱nda̱ una Ala̱masiihu.
Bulusu tabasa be̱ ta̱hyan xbugida̱ga̱ni ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ ta̱be̱, butaha̱nga rukwanyan naru ngwan, buꞌisa hiku nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ bwa de̱be̱ nata̱ ta̱to̱n. Bwa gura̱a̱ bisa̱ga̱ be̱ kuta̱huwa̱ nata̱ sa̱ra̱ri yana ta̱ba ja̱a̱ sha.
Butawanyan ta̱taga ta̱na̱nna na̱ ame̱ na tande̱ huku nꞌta̱sha̱a̱ bigata ta̱hyan Hwe̱n nii biha̱na̱ bwa hara̱ zhagu kuta̱gwama nata̱ Hwe̱n.
Iri na ne̱e̱ na̱ ame̱
Azumanu :1-2 Ta̱yaba na̱ nꞌta̱taa shita̱ :3--2:13Ta̱basa na̱ nꞌta̱pa mazama :14--4:5Ahari ana Bulusu bwa ne̱e̱ na̱ aba :6-18Mazama nama ta̱makwaakaa :19-22
Azumanu
Takaada na̱nna shi na báni kuga̱n Bulusu butumashini naa Ala̱masiihu Yeesu kuta̱sha̱a̱ nata̱ Hwe̱n. Biꞌnꞌka̱ji wana hyan ma bisa̱ga̱ awyatu haruwa na Hwe̱n bwa tanda ala̱ka̱wa̱ri na ta̱nda bina̱ na mahwa paaku ta̱panaa gata ku-Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Zhagu paa Timooti, baa buniimi kutuma na Hwe̱n bunaa ga̱n ribi.
Ta̱pana ꞌye̱n na̱ ambishiri na̱ hunranhunran na ta̱gumunu ku-Hwe̱n Ada na̱ Butu O̱to̱ nda̱a̱tu Ala̱masiihu Yeesu xta̱naa huku na̱ gaa.
Ta̱gooda̱ na̱ mazama ta̱pa
Timooti, ga̱n gooji Hwe̱n, una ga̱n ndaaka tuma nii gata ta̱makicihinaa binaa ta̱sabu, haruwa na adaadoo aba tandaga. Ga̱n ta gooda̱ wuun na ga̱n taa tamanrinyan koya̱ ha̱ni na̱ ro̱pe̱ nimi gita na̱ hwe̱n.
Ga̱n ta tamanrinyan maraba mandaabi nama ha̱ni na ga̱tu tamahoosa̱, ta ga̱n ribi maa ndaya vwainvwain, wana hyan ma ha̱nga gama ga̱tu gura̱a̱ mandaya.
Ga̱n ta tamanrinyan ta̱pana gata ndaabi nata̱ mahanda, ta̱panaa gata ta̱yata nata̱ ana̱a̱na̱ ndaa Loyisi na̱ ada̱a̱da̱ ndaa Afiniki nata̱ aba taꞌmꞌbaa. Nꞌshii bigata hiku gaa bi-mꞌbaa tuun taa.
Wana ya̱nu iita̱ma̱nriin ta̱hyan, hura̱ ta̱pana hyuhyu na̱ nꞌta̱yansun ta̱yata ji nata̱ Hwe̱n bwaa taapana ha̱ni na ga̱n taacagudaaga ara nimi.
Hwe̱n ta̱mpa̱ncin nꞌgata na nꞌrukwanyan, na̱ kunnu ta bwa ta̱mpa̱ni ta̱kai na̱ nꞌta̱ruba̱ na̱ nꞌta̱kota̱na̱ hyuhyu.
Ta-ha̱nga nꞌkogi na nꞌta̱nda sheeda na Butu O̱to̱ nda̱a̱tu Yeesu, koo ga̱mi, bunaa ne̱e̱ na̱ zhaaro wana Ala̱masiihu. Ama gaa taamaa naa huku na̱ ga̱mi, paaku ngwan taswa wana mazama nama zumaa. Hwe̱n ta bwaa pa̱ni ta̱kai nata̱ ta̱nda wuun.
Bwa ta̱mbiha̱ni, bwa ta̱nꞌnꞌgani wana xta̱nshi wyatu ndaabwa. Utanda kunnu shici wana yaanyini na ga̱tu nje̱ na bina̱, ama na̱ wana ta̱sha̱a̱ ta̱ndaabwa hasaa ta ubwa njiwo sa̱ra̱ri yana. Niina paaku Ala̱masiihu Yeesu ta Uhwe̱n bwa ta̱pa̱ni ta̱ba ta̱pana ꞌye̱n,
ta ubwa ta̱mbisa̱a̱ tuun paaku ta̱banrinyan nata̱ bunaa ta̱mbiha̱ni, Ala̱masiihu Yeesu. Bunaa hoo kuna kai na ta̱ꞌwa̱, bwa ta̱nbisa̱a̱ yo̱n na ta̱nda bina̱ na mahwa paaku mazama nama zumaa.
Na̱ wana mazama mayata nama zumaa ma ta ubwa nꞌka̱shi ga̱n shi butumashini na̱ biwya̱ra̱mi na hyan ma bisa̱ga̱ muu.
Na̱ wana kunnu ta ga̱n swa ngwan kuga̱n tanii swa wuun hara̱ ba̱re. Ama nꞌhange̱ce̱ nꞌkogi, wana nꞌyan bunaa ga̱n pa̱ni gata waabwa, ga̱n yan ga̱ga̱ga̱ buꞌmꞌbaa ta̱kai nata̱ ta̱ha̱mba iri na bwa mꞌpa̱ni ta̱sha̱a̱ kubwa hwe̱n na kuswa nde̱e̱be̱.
Ha̱mba̱ga̱ kami mazama nama ta̱to̱n nama ga̱mii ga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni, xma shi iri na gaa jwara̱ga, u-naa ji nii gata ta̱pana na̱ nꞌta̱ruba̱ nata̱ ga̱tu mꞌbaa na̱ nꞌta̱maꞌunpa̱n ta̱nda̱a̱tu na̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Paaku ta̱kai nata̱a̱ Hwaanwun naa Hwe̱n binaa ne̱e̱ ji na̱ nꞌga̱tu, ha̱mba iri na Hwe̱n bwaa pa̱ni ta̱sha̱a̱.
Bi-yan ta̱hyan awyatu hwarapi ana naawan na̱ gaa pita ana ne̱e̱ nꞌta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Aasiya ana̱ma nꞌgida̱ga̱ga̱na̱, huku na̱ Faijelusu na̱ Hamajenisu.
xUbutu O̱to̱ Yeesu ndaaki awyatu na Oniisimusu mbishiri wana buꞌnꞌduwa̱ni shita̱ ta̱ta paa bwa jábagi mahwarapi. Bwa hange̱ce̱ nꞌkogi na nꞌta̱hyan ga̱n ne̱e̱ na̱ zhaaro,
kuta̱naa wuce ta̱ndaabwa Rooma, bwa ke̱ne̱ wyanzun nimi sa̱i na bwa nda̱i paa ga̱n ne̱e̱.
xUbutu O̱to̱ Yeesu ndaaki be̱ mbishiri na̱ bwa hwe̱n ya̱nu! Gaa gura̱a̱ yansun haruwa na bwa nꞌndáaki iri hwarapi na bina̱ na̱ Afisa.

Sooja na ta̱hiku na Ala̱masiihu Yeesu
Baa buniimi, mashikitani na̱ kai paaku ta̱pana ꞌye̱n nata̱ shi ta̱nda̱a̱tu wana ta̱maꞌunpa̱n na̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Shapa ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ gaa hange̱ nꞌnii ga̱gaagana kawyatu hwarapi ana hange̱ tuun hiku. Ga̱gaagana tuun kawyatu ana shi na bina̱ ana ta̱hiku, ana nii ara ta̱ga̱gaagana ayaan taa.
Naa na̱ akuri huku na̱ ga̱mi na̱ nꞌta̱swa ngwan haku sooja na Ala̱masiihu Yeesu na ta̱hiku.
Koya̱ sooja na ta nda tuma o̱to̱ uta caanhina sooja na o̱to̱ na ta̱ wuun ame̱, bwa jaa gura̱a̱ yibaku tuma ndaabwa na̱ ana shici asooja.
Koya̱ butu naa umuntun na sumo̱ bujaa raa funa̱ na asumo̱, bwa jwarigici haruwa na nꞌgira̱nshin na nꞌsumo̱ mꞌba hin.
Buhwaanyan naa tamashikitaa na̱ cima ta̱hwan, bwa taa shi naa hyan bupa̱shi ta̱re̱ ꞌwaa na cima.
Naa makicihinaa ki na̱ iri na ga̱n cita̱ga̱, wana Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n nii shaana u-e̱nshe̱n muu ki hyo̱.
Naa matamanrinyaan Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, bunaa tahiika̱ kuꞌuya̱, bunaa báni kiikorogo naa Dawuda, haruwa na mꞌba ne̱e̱ kumazama nama zumaa nama ga̱n cita̱ga̱.
Wana ga̱n nii cita̱ga̱ mazama ma yata nama zumaa, ta ga̱n swa ta̱guma, aba nꞌka̱da̱gi na̱ zhaaro haku butu naa pinsan. Ama mazama nama Hwe̱n mꞌba za naa nii ara muu ta̱kadaga.
Wana kunnu ta ga̱n re̱ kuri na̱ ngwan hwarapi na ga̱n swa na̱ wana wyatu na Hwe̱n bwa takasa, wana aba taa maa ade̱be̱ ta̱biha̱na̱ nata̱ báni paaki Ala̱masiihu Yeesu nata̱ nii ta̱nꞌwaanyin ta̱shapaciga nata̱ mahwa.
Na̱nna ta shi ta̱cita̱ nata̱ mahanda,
<<Kuta̱nꞌwi huku nii be̱,
ta̱ja̱a̱ bina̱ huku nii be̱.
Kuta̱nre̱ iyeebe nꞌsukuri,
ta̱ja̱a̱ nꞌnda ta̱gwama huku nii be̱.
Kuta̱nga̱a̱ buu,
be̱ taa ma bija̱a̱ ta̱ngaa.
Kuta̱nshici ana bina̱ waabe̱,
be̱e̱ hoo sha naa bina̱,
wana bijaa mahiriga kiibe̱ hoo sha.>>
Atuma na Hwe̱n ana ta̱to̱n
Naa tamanrinyaan awyatu na Yeesu iri na̱nna, koota̱ wyan hiku na̱ aꞌuba̱ na Hwe̱n, xata naa nda gagu wana nꞌza̱zama. Izumaancin, ibe̱ nii foga̱hina̱ ana shiraagi.
Mashikitaa u-nje̱ haruwa na gaa ara ta̱nda u-de̱be̱ hiku ta̱raa kaꞌuba̱ na Hwe̱n hakuu tumaa naa za nꞌkogi na nꞌtuma ndaabwa, bunaa hyan bunaa bisa̱a̱ga̱ to̱n mazama nama Hwe̱n nama mahanda.
U-ga̱a̱ nꞌza̱zama na nꞌuwa̱ na nꞌshici na mꞌbina̱ na nii pa awyatu sumo̱ paaku Hwe̱n.
Nꞌya̱nu nꞌza̱zama ta nꞌshi haku suguma nasu ashukwa nasu nii re̱ pa̱ri. Awyatu reeko ana nii nda iri ya̱nu aba ta shi Himiniyusu na̱ Filitusu.
Aka̱shi kuyo̱n na mahanda abaa hanshihinaa nꞌgata ta̱pana na nꞌawyatu ka̱ ma hyaan ta̱hiika̱ nata̱ wyatu na Hwe̱n ana ꞌwa̱gi ta̱hoo nda.
Ta̱ma nata̱ Hwe̱n bwa hoo ciba̱ hiku nata̱ kai ta̱jaa zha̱a̱nta̱na̱, na̱ nꞌta̱ba ta aba ta̱gi mꞌba mazama ta̱hyan, <<Hwe̱n yan ana shi ndaabwa,>> na̱ <<Hyo̱ ana hin ashi ana Hwe̱n xaga̱a̱ ta̱naa nda iri na we̱.>>
Na̱ ina na mꞌbaa yuwa, shii kaꞌwana na zinaari na̱ azurufa ta ne̱e̱, hyo̱ na̱ ana ce̱nye̱n na̱ ana ꞌwe̱e̱ na shami ta̱re̱. Ana yuwa o̱to̱ anii nda tuma na̱ aba kuta̱mawuna̱na̱ nata̱ awyatu o̱to̱, aka̱ kuyaan tuma.
Wana kunnu koo buya̱ butu naa pe̱e̱n hyuhyu ndaabwa paaki iri ya̱nu na we̱, bunii sha ruꞌwana naru tuma naru zumaa naru gii ta̱cina̱na̱ kubutu naa ina ndaabwa. Koo buya̱ ne̱e̱ kunnu bunii magiya̱ butu naa ina ndaabwa nje̱ koya̱ tuma na zumaa na̱a̱ bwa.
Gida̱ga̱na̱ ta̱ruba̱ nata̱ iri na shi na uwa̱ ina ta̱njeke, u-pa̱ni uba̱ kuꞌiri na ta̱to̱n, bigata ta̱pana, ta̱ruba̱ wyatu, hunranhunran na ta̱gumunu, huku na̱ ana ta rupa Hwe̱n nii gata naa ta̱sabu.
Gaa kuda̱ga na ta̱guzha̱ni na̱ kuda̱ga na za yaan bina̱, bi-yan ta̱hyan uta huwa̱ kuna̱ gagu.
Bugyama naa Hwe̱n xbuta nda gagu, xbushi naa bina̱ kukoya̱ butu, bunaa a̱ri ta̱ga̱gaagana ki na̱ akuri,
shukuu bwa nii naa bisa̱ga̱ ana ribici mahanda, nii gata ta̱sha̱a̱ ta̱hyan Hwe̱n nii shana apa̱ni pinsan baa, ajwara̱ga yo̱n na mahanda.
Ha̱ni na aba e̱nshe̱n ki ajaa ba̱na̱ni nꞌta̱mazhaa nꞌta̱ruma nata̱ Bupira̱, bunaa hoo kota̱na̱ wyan xanje̱ hyo̱ ta̱sha̱a̱ ta̱ndaabwa.

Nꞌhwe̱n na nꞌta̱makwaakaa
Yansun ta̱hyan, nꞌhwe̱n na nꞌta̱makwaakaa ta nꞌja̱a̱ sha ha̱ni na da̱a̱rici.
Awyatu ja̱a̱ sha ana ribi suhyu sundaaba, ana ribi ayuwa o̱to̱, ana ruwashi, ana ta̱mashapaciga, ana hwashe̱ Hwe̱n, ana cina̱ncin sushoo, ana a̱cii gooda̱, ana wa̱shici Hwe̱n,
ana za suha̱nka̱ri, ana ta ha̱mba̱ga̱ butu nii gata, ana taha̱nsha̱nha̱na̱ butu ruzha̱a̱, ana mahumuncin hyuhyu, ana za ambishiri, ana ribici ri na bina̱,
ana ta banrinyan she̱re̱ na ayaan, ana tanaa nda ri ma̱, ana ta̱makumbura̱na̱, ana ribici Hwe̱n aba huri ta̱ruba̱ kiri na sa̱ra̱ri yana.
Paaka wyatu ane̱e̱ haka na jwarigi Hwe̱n ama aba ga̱a̱ ta̱kai nata̱ Hwe̱n paaku tuma ndaaba. Mape̱e̱n tutu paaka wyatu ya̱nu.
Iri ndaaba ta tanaa ta̱na̱a̱ nꞌina na nꞌawyatu, akota̱ni suhyu nasu aꞌa̱ na shici abe̱ce̱. Aya̱nu a̱ ana ndagi pinsan ubwa shaagi wyan ꞌwaa ta ta̱ruba̱ nata̱ iri na we̱ ta̱ba sha̱pi suha̱nka̱ri sundaaba,
atanaa nda koya̱ hwe̱n xayansun iri goo goo ama aba jaa insan mahanda.
Haki Yanisu na̱ Yambirisu ana tamaꞌunso̱ncin na̱ Muusa, kunnu taa nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nꞌya̱nu nꞌa̱cii maꞌunso̱n na̱ mꞌmahanda. Aba ta shi awyatu ana nꞌgata nꞌndaaba mꞌba ꞌwi, ta̱panaa gata ta̱ndaaba ta̱ba shi nata̱ ta̱be̱.
Ama aba jaa me̱ma, wana koo buya̱a̱ ja̱a̱ ndaya ta̱guzha̱ni guzha̱ni ta̱ndaaba. Ya̱nu ta shi iri na tanda na̱ Yanisu na̱ Yambirisu.
Iri na Bulusu bwa ribi Timooti nje̱
Gaa bi-hoo yansun ta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱niimi, ujabagu nimi, na̱ iri na shani ga̱n nda na̱nna. Gaa gura̱a̱ insan ta̱pana gata niimi, akuri nimi, ta̱ruba̱ nii gata niimi, ta̱ꞌisa hiku ta̱niimi,
iri na ta̱kaka na̱ ta̱guma nata̱ ga̱n taswa. Gaa yan hyo̱ iri na tanda na̱ ga̱mi na̱ Antiyaakiya, na̱ Ikooniya, na̱ Lisitira, na̱ nꞌta̱kaka nata̱ aba taꞌnꞌkaka, ga̱n re̱ kuri nꞌta̱ba. Ama hyo̱ maya̱nu Hwe̱n bwa mꞌbiha̱ni na̱ mꞌmaba.
Yansun ta̱hyan bunaa hiin nda jabagu na Hwe̱n bwa ribi na̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu anii kaka be̱ ta̱ꞌo̱to̱,
awyatu na we̱ na̱ apira̱ anii naa duwa̱na̱ kumaꞌwe̱n ta̱ꞌmꞌbaa, anaa pira̱ aka̱, anaa pira̱ga̱ wyan taa.
Ama gaa, ta ta̱hura̱ na̱ iri na abaa ga̱ga̱a̱ga̱ni na gaa hoo ara, gaa cori wuun nii gata. Gaa yan koo bwaa shi nꞌwya̱ra̱mi nꞌndaabi.
Mata̱ma̱nriin ta̱hyan ta na̱ nꞌta̱njeke ta̱ndaabi bi-tahoo yansun utakaada na Hwe̱n, ana nii ara ta̱a̱pana ta̱yansun nata̱ na̱maa iya kuta̱biha̱na̱ paakii gata ta̱pana ku-Ala̱masiihu Yeesu.
Hyo̱ mazama nama takaada na Hwe̱n mashi nama báni paa Hwe̱n, ubwa ta ta̱ndaaka tuma na bina̱ paaku ta̱ga̱gaagana mahanda, ushani ta̱ꞌinsan iri na zumaancin kujabagu. Bwa ta a̱sa̱ga̱na̱ paa ta̱wajigaa ta̱ba ne̱e̱, bwa ta ga̱gaagana ta̱nda iri na ne̱e̱ to̱n,
wana koya̱ butu naa nii ndaaka Hwe̱n tuma xbushi bunaa cigi ki ta̱sha bunaa ta̱nda koya̱ tuma na zumaa.

Na uba̱ na Hwe̱n na̱ Ala̱masiihu Yeesu, bunaa ja̱a̱ ndaaka awyatu na wuma na̱ ana ꞌwi ta̱suuga̱, wana bunii jaa bunje̱ ta̱gwama ta̱nde̱e̱be̱, iita̱ tuma na̱nna hiku,
bisa̱ga̱ wyatu mazama nama Hwe̱n, nda shiri na ta̱nda muu koo na̱ ha̱ni na zumaa koo na zumaancin, u-a̱ra̱ga̱ni wyan, u-ndaaki wyan gagu na̱ iri na zumaancin, u-ta̱ wyan bishita̱, u-naa ga̱gaagana wyan hyo̱ ya̱nu na̱ akuri.
Ha̱ni wuci na awyatu aba jaa shiraga ta̱ga̱gaagana nata̱ ta̱to̱n, ama ajwara̱ga kiri na aba ribi na̱ nꞌta̱mada̱a̱ba nꞌwya̱ra̱mi ndaaba ma̱ na nꞌnii naa bisa̱ga̱ wyan iri na aba ribi ta̱ha̱nga.
Aja̱a̱ pe̱e̱n ace̱be̱ ndaaba paaku mahanda mꞌba ne̱e̱, ahuri ta̱pana ha̱nka̱ri ndaaba paaku aca̱a̱sa̱.
Ama gaa, sha̱a̱ hyuhyu ndaa pa̱ri kaka̱ kukoya̱ ri naa jábani, u-re̱ kuri nꞌta̱guma ta̱swa, nda tuma na ta̱bisa̱ga̱ wyatu mazama nama zumaa, u-nje̱ tuma ndaa hyo̱ ki na Hwe̱n bwaa pa̱ni ta̱nda.
Kuga̱n, ahoo pana hyuhyu nimi haku ri na ta̱pana Hwe̱n, ha̱ni na ga̱n gaa sa̱ra̱ri yana goki.
Ga̱n hoo nda gagu na zumaa una ta̱panaa gata naa mahanda, ga̱n hoo huwa̱ tuma na Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwa mꞌpa̱ni, ga̱n jwarigi na̱ mꞌmahanda.
Niina ga̱n hambe̱ ye̱e̱ kufuna̱ na tuma na ta̱to̱n na ga̱n nje̱ una bwa nꞌsha̱a̱gi ga̱mi. Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bunaa ta̱suuga̱ nata̱ ta̱to̱n bwa nii mꞌpana hwe̱n na bwa kúshe̱. Ubwa jaa sha kuga̱mi, ama na̱ hyo̱ ana hambe̱ ji xbiwuce.
Mazama nama ta̱makwaakaa
Nda haruwa na gaa ara ta̱jaa wa̱ka̱mi na̱ ha̱ni.
Demasu nꞌga̱a̱ ta bwa huri Tasaloonika, wana ta̱ruba̱ nata̱ iri na sa̱ra̱ri yana. Karasaka be̱ huri ta̱ha̱mba̱ga̱ nata̱ Galaatiya, Taitusu bwa huri Dala̱maatiya.
Luka bwaa ka̱ ta naawan na̱ ga̱mi. Ha̱ni na gaa jaa wa̱ka̱mi, jaa huku na̱ Marukusu, wana bunii ara buꞌnꞌguni tuma na̱nna nimi.
Ga̱n káji Tikikusu xbujaa Afisa.
Kuu-ja̱a̱ jaa, u-nꞌsháapi da̱bi na ta̱hobi na ga̱n tagaa na̱ ara na Karupusu na̱ ce̱pe̱ na Toruwasu, shápi huku na̱ atakaada, ta-háasani ayata na aba nje̱ na̱ tutuu na ta̱ꞌyantan ta̱taga.
Aleka̱zanda buruma buꞌnꞌndáaki iri hwarapi na zumaancin, Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu nii pa be̱ funa̱ nge̱n na̱ iri na bwa nje̱.
Gaa taa maa nda ha̱nka̱ri na̱a̱ bwa, wana bwaa maꞌunso̱ncin mahwa na̱ nꞌta̱ga̱gaagana ta̱nda̱a̱tu.
Na yigo buza naa taꞌnꞌisaaga ha̱ni na ga̱n ne̱e̱ kuta̱suuga̱, kuga̱n ga̱n maba̱ha̱ni, hyo̱ aba nꞌga̱a̱. xUhwe̱n ta ha̱mba̱ga̱na̱ wyan muu nii gata ndaabwa.
Ama Butu O̱to̱ Yeesu bwa nꞌisaagi, bwa mꞌpa̱ni ta̱kai nata̱ ga̱n ta isa ga̱n a̱ri ta̱bisa̱ga̱ mazama nama zumaa hyo̱ kana shici Ayaahudiya hwarapi atibi, kabata bwa mꞌba̱ha̱ni nꞌta̱suuga̱ nata̱ ta̱ꞌnꞌkuna.
Bwa taa shi naa nii mꞌbiha̱na̱ paaku ta̱koya̱ ta̱we̱, buꞌnꞌye̱e̱ gumunu paaku ta̱gwama ta̱ndaabwa nꞌta̱ra̱ga̱da̱. xTa̱shapaciga ta̱naa waabwa na̱ mꞌmahwa mꞌmahwa. xMashi kunnu.
Azumanu na ta̱makwaakaa
Nꞌzumaanyin Birisikila na̱ awya̱rugo Akiila na̱ awyatu na ina na Oniisimusu.
Erasutusu tane̱e̱ na̱ Korinti, ga̱n tagáa Tarofimusu tapiree na̱ Militusu wana butahange̱ce̱ sa̱.
Nda haruwa na gaa ara ta̱nda u-jaa ta shuyo bwa wuco. Yubulusu, Pudenusu, Lainusu na̱ Kalaudiya na̱ hyo̱ awyatu na pa̱ni nꞌgata aazúmaani.
Butu O̱to̱ Hwe̱n xbunaawan huku nii hwaanwun ndaabi. Ta̱pana ꞌye̱n nata̱ Hwe̱n xta̱naa huku na̱ ga̱hin hyo̱.
